Yesu Kristo awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ Yesu Kristo Dawid ba he, Abraham ba he awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ.
Abraham woo Isak, na Isak woo Yakob, na Yakob woo Yuda ne ne nuanom; Yuda ne Tamar woo Peres ne Sera, na Peres woo Hesron, na Hesron woo Ram, Ram woo Aminadab, na Aminadab woo Nahson, na Nahson woo Salmon, na Salmon ne Rahab woo Boas, na Boas ne Rut woo Obed, na Obed woo Yisai, na Yisai woo Hene Dawid.
Na Dawid nso ne nea kane he na ɔyɛ Uria yerɛ he woo Salomo, na Salomo woo Rehoboam, na Rehoboam woo Abia, na Abia woo Asa, na Asa woo Yehosafat, na Yehosafat woo Yoram, na Yoram woo Usia, na Usia woo Yotam, na Yotam woo Ahas, na Ahas woo Hesekia, na Hesekia woo Manase, na Manase woo Amon, na Amon woo Yosia, na Yosia woo Yekonia ne ne nuanom, mmerɛ a Babilonfoɔ faa Yudafoɔ nommum kɔɔ Babel he.
Na mmerɛ a Babilonfoɔ faa bɛ nommum kɔɔ Babel akyi he, Yekonia woo Sealtiel, na Sealtiel woo Serubabel, na Serubabel woo Abihud, na Abihud woo Eliakim, na Eliakim woo Asor, na Asor woo Sadok, na Sadok woo Akim, na Akim woo Elihud, na Elihud woo Eleasa, na Eleasa woo Matan, na Matan woo Yakob, na Yakob woo Yosef, Maria kunu he.
Saa Maria yi ne woo Yesu a bɛfrɛ no Kristo he.
Nti ofiri Abraham so kosi Dawid so yɛ awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ dunnan; na ofiri Dawid so kosi mmerɛ a bɛfaa Yudafoɔ nommum kɔɔ Babel he so yɛ awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ dunnan; na ofiri berɛ a betu kɔtenaa Babel he kosi Kristo so nso yɛ awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ dunnan.
Yesu Kristo Awoɔ Afei kwane a bɛfaa so woo Yesu Kristo di: Berɛ a bɛde ne maame Maria maa Yosef sɛ asiwa, na bennya ntenaa sɛ awarefoɔ he, behuu sɛ Maria afa afuro a ofiri Honhom Kronkron.
Ɔnam sɛ na Yosef a ɔyɛ n'asiwa yerɛ he yɛ nipa tenenee na ɔmpɛ sɛ obegu Maria anim ase badwam nti, ɔbɔɔ ne tim pɔ sɛ obegyae no kokoam.
Nso berɛ a ɔyɔɔ sɛ obetu saa anammɔn he pɛ ne Nyankopɔn bɔfoɔ yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ no daeɛso mu, kaa sɛ, “Yosef, Dawid ba, nsuro sɛ wobɛfa Maria a ɔyɛ w'asiwa-yerɛ he akɔ wo fie, efiri sɛ, abɔfra a ɔnyem no he firi Honhom Kronkron.
Ɔbɛwo ba beema, na to ne dini Yesu, efiri sɛ ɔno ne bɛgye ne nkurofoɔ afiri bɛ bɔne mu.” Yei nyinaa siiɛ sɛdeɛ asɛm a Awurade nam diyifoɔ he so kaeɛ he bɛbam sɛ, “Hwɛ, babunu he bɛfa afuro na wawo ba beema, na bɛato ne dini sɛ Immanuel,” asekyerɛ ne sɛ, (Nyankopɔn ne yɛ ya hɔ).
Berɛ a Yosef nyane firii ne nna mu he, ɔyɔɔ sɛdeɛ Awurade bɔfoɔ he hyɛɛ no sɛ ɔnyɔ he; na ɔfaa Maria baa ne nkyɛne sɛ ne yerɛ, nso wamfa ne ho anka no kosii sɛ ɔwoo ba beema; na ɔtoo ne dini Yesu.
Nsoromma mu animdefoɔ bi kɔsraa Abɔfra Yesu Hene Herode berɛ so he, bɛwoo Yesu Betlehem a ɔya Yudea.
Na yei akyi he, nsoromma mu animdefoɔ bi firi apieeɛ baa Yerusalem, bebisaa sɛ, “Hefa ne Yudafoɔ hene a bɛawo no he ya?
Yɛahu ne nsoromma apieɛ, na yɛaba sɛ yɛɛbɛkoto no.” Berɛ a Herode a ɔyɛ hene he teeɛ he, ɔne Yerusalemfoɔ nyinaa akoma tuiɛ; na ɔfrɛɛ asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne mane he mu atwerɛfoɔ nyinaa bisaa bɛ baabi a ɔsɛ sɛ bɛwo Kristo he.
Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ɔsɛ sɛ bɛwo no Betlehem a ɔya Yudea, sɛnea adiyifoɔ he bɛatwerɛ ato hɔ sɛ: “Na wo, Betlehem a woya Yuda asaase so, wonyɛ kumaa Yuda amane mufoɔ mu, efiri sɛ wo mu ne bɛbɛfrɛ safohene afiri a ɔbɛyɛ dwanhwɛfoɔ ama me mane Israel.” Afei Herode frɛɛ nsoromma mu animdefoɔ he kokoam bisaa bɛ berɛ pɔtee a saa nsoromma he pieeɛ.
Na ɔsomaa bɛ Yerusalem, kaa sɛ, “Honkɔhwehwɛ abɔfra he yie; na sɛ hohu no a, hommɛka nkyerɛ me na me nso menkɔkoto no bi.” Na betiee hene he nsɛm he wieeɛ he, befirii hɔ; na hɔaa, nsoromma a opieeɛ he dii bɛ anim, kosii sɛ okogyinaa baabi a abɔfra he ya.
Behuu sɛ nsoromma he agyina he, bɛ ani gye boroo so.
Bewuraa fie a na abɔfra he yam he mu he, behuu ɔne ne maame Maria, na bɛkoto sɔree no.
Afei, bebiee bɛ kotokuo mu yii sikakɔkɔɔ, krobo, ne aduhwam de yɔɔ no ayɛ.
Na bɛbɔɔ bɛ kɔkɔ daeɛ mu sɛ bɛnnsane nkɔ Herode hɔ bio he, bɛfaa kwane foforɔ so kɔɔ bɛ kurom.
Yosef de abɔfra he dwane kɔɔ Misraim Na nsoromma mu animdifoɔ he firii hɔ he, Nyankopɔn bɔfoɔ yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ Yosef ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɔre, fa abɔfra he ne ne maame, na honnwane nkɔ Misraim, na hontena hɔ nkosi sɛ mɛka bibi akyerɛ ho bio ɔfa yei ho; efiri sɛ Herode ɔɔpɛ abɔfra he aku no.” Na Yosef sɔreeɛ, na ɔfaa abɔfra he ne ne maame anadwo he, na bɛkɔɔ Misraim, na bɛtenaa hɔ kosii sɛ Herode wuiɛ.
Yei maa deɛ Awurade nam diyifoɔ he so kaeɛ he baa mu sɛ, “Misraim ne mafrɛ me ba he afiri.” Bekuu mmɔfra Na Herode huu sɛ nsoromma mu animdefoɔ he adaadaa no he, ne bo fuu kɛse paa, na ɔsoma maa bekokuu mmɔfra mmeema a benni mmoroo mfie mmienu nyinaa a bɛya Yerusalem ne ne mpɔtamu, sɛnea berɛ a ohu firii nsoromma mu animudefoɔ he hɔ kyerɛ he.
Na diyifoɔ Yeremia asɛm he baam sɛ: “Bɛtee nne bi Rama, su ne adwotwa dendene, Rahel oosu ne mma, ɔmma kwane mma ne werɛ nkyekyere, efiri sɛ benni hɔ bio.” Yosef ne abɔfra he firii Misraim sane baeɛ Na Herode wuiɛ he, hwɛ, Awurade bɔfoɔ yii ne ho adi daeɛ mu kyerɛɛ Yosef Misraim na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɔre, fa abɔfra he ne ne maame, kɔ Israel mane mu, bɛ a bɛɛpɛ abɔfra he aku no he nyinaa awuwu.” Na Yosef sɔre faa abɔfra he ne ne maame, de bɛkɔɔ Israel asaase so.
Nso ɔtee sɛ Arkelao asi ne papa Herode anane mu oodi adeɛ Yudea he, osuroo sɛ ɔbɛkɔ hɔ.
Na afei, bɛbɔɔ no kɔkɔ daeɛ mu he, ɔkɔɔ Galilea mansinim.
Na ɔkɔtenaa baabi a bɛfrɛ hɔ Nasaret, nti deɛ diyifoɔ he kaeɛ he baam sɛ, “Bɛbɛfrɛ no Nasareni.”
Suboni Yohane asɛnka Saa nna he mu he, Suboni Yohane pae mu kaa no Yudea serɛ he so sɛ, “Honsakra ho adwene, na soro ahennie he abɛne.” Yei ne deɛ diyifoɔ Yesaia kaa ne ho asɛm sɛ, “Nea ɔɔteam serɛ so he dɛ, Siesie Awurade akwane, ma n’atempɔno ntene.” Na Yohane fira ntoma a bɛde yoma nwii ayɔ a nwoma aboomu bɔ n’asenem, na aduane a odi ne mmɛbɛ ne wuram woɔ.
Na Yerusalemfoɔ ne Yudeafoɔ nyinaa ɔne bɛ a bɛte Yordan agya nyinaa kɔɔ ne nkyɛne, na bɛba bɛkaa bɛ bɔne ma ɔbɔɔ bɛ asu Asubɔntene Yordan mu.
Nso ohuu Farisifoɔ ne Sadukifoɔ sɛ bɛɛba abɛbɔ asu he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho nankatia mma!
Hwane ne bɔɔ ho kɔkɔ sɛ honnwane mfiri abufuo a ɔɔba he ho?
Honso aba a ɔfata adwensakra.
Honnsusu nka ne ho adwene mu sɛ, ‘Yɛyɛ Abraham asefoɔ’; na meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, Nyankopɔn betumi anyane mma afiri boɔ yi mu ama Abraham sɛ mma.
Mpo seesei bɛde akuma ato dua he nhini ase; nti dua biaa a ɔnnso aba he bebetwa na bɛato atwene gya mu.
“Me deɛ mede nsuo ne bɔ asu kɔ adwensakram, na deɛ odi m’akyi ɔɔba he deɛ ɔkorɔn kyɛne me, na mensɛ mfata sɛ mekita ne mpaboa mpo.
Ɔno ne nea ɔde Honhom Kronkron ne gya bɛbɔ ho asu.
Okita ne huhuammoa ne nsam, na ɔbɛpra n’ayuporobea hɔ na woaboaboa n’ayuo ano akogu pata so; nso ntɛ he deɛ, ɔde gya a onnum da bɛhye ne nyinaa.” Yesu asubɔ Afei Yesu firii Galilea baa Yohane nkyɛne Yordan ho, sɛ Yohane mmɔ no asu.
Nso Yohane pɛɛ sɛ osi no kwane, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Me ne ɔsɛ sɛ wobɔ me asu, ne wo mmom wooba me nkyɛne yi?” Nso Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Ma ɔnyɛ saa, ɔyɛ ma yɛ sɛ yɛhyɛ tenenee nyinaa ma.” Na Yohane penee so maa no.
Na ɔbɔɔ Yesu asu wieeɛ he, na opie firii nsuo he mu a pɛ, amonom hɔaa ne soro bie maa no na ohuu sɛ Nyankopɔn Honhom oosiane sɛ abuburo ɔɔba ne so.
Na nne bi firi soro kaa sɛ, “Yei ne me dɔ Ba a ɔsɔ m’ani.”
Yesu sɔhwɛ Na afei Honhom he dii Yesu anim de no kɔɔ serɛ so sɛ Bronsam nkɔ sɔ no nhwɛ.
Odii mmuada adaduannan, awia ne anadwo, na yei akyi he kɔm dee no.
Na sɔhwɛfoɔ he ba bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ wo ne Nyankopɔn ba he a, hyɛ ma aboɔ yi nnane paanoo.” Nso ɔmaa no mmuaeɛ sɛ, “Bɛatwerɛ sɛ ɔnyɛ paanoo nkoaa so ne nipa nam benya nkwa, na mmom asɛm biaa ofiri Nyankopɔn anum nso.” Afei Bronsam de no kɔɔ kuro kronkron he mu de no kosii asɔredane he atifi, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ wo ne Nyankopɔn ba he a, to wo ho hwe fam; na bɛatwerɛ sɛ, Ɔbɛhyɛ n’abɔfoɔ ama wo na bɛbɛsɔ wo bɛ nsam, na wo nane ɔmpem boɔ.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Bɛatwerɛ bio sɛ, ‘Nsɔ Awurade wo Nyankopɔn nhwɛ.’ ” Afei nso, Bronsam faa no de no kosii bepɔ tentene bi atifi, na ɔkyerɛɛ no wiase ahennie ne mu afɛfɛdeɛ nyinaa, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ wobɛkoto asɔre me a, nka mede saa nnoɔma yi nyinaa bɛma wo.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ: Firi hɔ, Satan!
Na bɛatwerɛ sɛ: “Awurade wo Nyankopɔn nkoaa ne sɔre no, na ɔno nkoaa nso ne som no.” Yei akyi he, Bronsam gyaa no hɔ, na afei abɔfoɔ ba bɛsomm no.
Yesu kɔɔ Galilea Na afei Yesu tee sɛ bɛakye Yohane he, osiim kɔɔ Galilea.
Ofirii Nasaret na ɔkɔtenaa Kapernaum po he ho, Sebulon ne Naftali, mpɔtamu, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a nkɔmhyɛ a ɔnam diyifoɔ Yesaia so baeɛ he bɛba mu sɛ: “Sebulon asaase, Naftali asaase, po ho kwane so, Yordan agya amanamane mufoɔ Galilea— nkurofoɔ a na bɛte sum mu he bɛahu hann kɛseɛ, na bɛ a bɛte sum mu he, bɛahu hann kɛseɛ bi; na bɛ a bɛte wuo sunsum asaase so he, hann apie bɛ so.” Ofiri saa mmerɛ he ɔɔkɔ he, Yesu firii aseɛ pae mu kaa sɛ, “Honsakra ho adwene na soro ahennie he abɛne.” Yesu frɛɛ asuafoɔ nnan bi Na Yesu nam Galilea po ho he, ohuu anuanom mmienu, Simon, a bɛfrɛ no Petro, ɔne ne nua Andrea, sɛ beegu asau po he mu—efiri sɛ na bɛyɛ apofofoɔ.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honni m’akyi, na mɛma hoayɛ nnipa yifoɔ.” Amonom hɔaa begyaa bɛ asau he hɔ kodii n’akyi.
Na ofirii hɔ he, ohuu anuanom mmienu bi, Yakobo, Sebedeo ba ne ne nua Yohane, sɛ bɛ ne bɛ papa Sebedeo te kodoɔ mu a beesiesie bɛ asau, na ɔfrɛɛ bɛ.
Amonom hɔaa begyaa bɛ kodoɔ ne bɛ papa hɔ, na bekodii n’akyi.
Yesu kaa Nyankopɔn asɛm na ɔsaa yareɛ ya Galilea Yesu kyinkyinii Galilea nyinaa, kyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ hyia adane mu, na ɔpae mu kaa ahennie he ho asɛmpa na ɔsaa bɛ a bɛyare nyinaa yadeɛ.
Nti ne ho asɛm trɛɛ Siria nyinaa, na bɛde ayarefoɔ, bɛ a bɛyare yadeɛ ahodoɔ ne bɛ a bɛ honam tutu bɛ, ne bɛ a honhom fi ne twerɛ ya bɛ so, ɔne mmubuafoɔ nyinaa, baa ne nkyɛne.
Na ɔsaa bɛ nyinaa yadeɛ.
Na nkurofoɔ akuoakuo pii firi Galilea, Dekapoli, Yerusalem, Yudea, ne Yordan agya nyinaa dii n’akyi.
Bepɔ so asɛnka—Nhyirasɛm Berɛ a Yesu huu nnipadɔm he, ɔkɔɔ bepɔ he so; na ɔtenaa ase he, n’asuafoɔ baa ne nkyɛne.
Na afei obiee na no kasaeɛ, na ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ: “Nhyira ne bɛ a ahia bɛ honhom mu, efiri sɛ bɛ ne soro ahennie he yɛ bɛ dea.
Nhyira ne bɛ a bedi awerɛhoɔ, efiri sɛ bɛ ne bebenya awerɛkyekyerɛ.
Nhyira ne bɛ a bɛdwo, efiri sɛ bɛ ne bebedi asaase he so.
Nhyira ne bɛ a tenenee ho kɔm ne sukɔm de bɛ, efiri sɛ bɛ ne bɛbɛma bɛammee.
Nhyira ne bɛ a behu afoforɔ mmɔbɔ, efiri sɛ bɛ ne bebehu bɛ mmɔbɔ.
Nhyira ne bɛ a bɛ akoma mu te, efiri sɛ bɛ ne bebehu Nyankopɔn.
Nhyira ne bɛ a bɛhwehwɛ asomdwie, efiri sɛ bɛ ne bɛbɛfrɛ bɛ Nyankopɔn mma.
Nhyira ne bɛ a tenenee nti bɛtaa bɛ, efiri sɛ bɛ ne bebenya soro ahennie he.
Nhyira ne ho sɛ nnipa ka nsɛm gu ho so, na bɛtaa ho na bɛka nsɛmmɔne bebree fa ho ho, na me nti bedi torɔ gu ho so.
Homma ho ani nnye, efiri sɛ howɔ akatua kɛseɛ ya soro, na saa ne bɛtane adiyifoɔ a bedii ho anim kane he.
Mfantoho a ɔfa nkyene ne hann ho Hone asaase yi so nkyene; nso sɛ nkyene dɛ yera a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na ayɛ nkyene bio?
Bɛmmfa nnyɔ hwee bio, gye sɛ bɛto gu ma betiatia so.
Hoyɛ wiase hann.
Kuro a ɔda mmepɔ so ntumi nhinta.
Nipa biaa nsɔ kanea mmfa nnhyɛ atam ase, na mmom bɛde si kanea dua so, na ahyerɛn ama nnipa a bɛya fie hɔ nyinaa.
Ne saa nti homma ho kanea nhyerɛn mma nnipa nyinaa, na bɛahu ho nnwuma pa na bɛahyɛ ho Agya a ɔya soro he animuonyam.
Mmara he ho nkyerɛkyerɛ Honnwene sɛ maaba sɛ meebeyi mmara ne adiyifoɔ he hɔ; mamma sɛ meebeyi no hɔ, na mmom maaba sɛ meebɛma no aba mu pefee.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, kosi sɛ soro ne asaase betwam he, atwerɛdeɛ anaa nsensaneɛ ketewa baako mpo omfiri mmara he mu kosi sɛ ne nyinaa bɛba mu.
Ne saa nti, nipa biaa a obebu mmara nsɛm ketewa baako mpo so, na ɔbɛkyerɛkyerɛ binom ama bɛayɔ saa he, ɔbɛyɛ ketewa soro ahennie mu; nso deɛ odi so na ɔkyerɛkyerɛ ma nnipa di so he ɔbɛyɛ kɛseɛ soro ahennie mu.
Meeka akyerɛ ho, sɛ ho tenenee ammoro atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ bɛ deɛ so a, honnya soro ahennie mu kwane da.
Abufuo ho nkyerɛkyerɛ “Hoate sɛ bɛka kyerɛɛ tetefoɔ he sɛ, ‘Honni awu; na nea odi awu biaa bedi fɔ atemmuo mu.’ Na me deɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, sɛ wo bo fu wo nua a, wobedi fɔ atemmuo mu; wodi wo nua atɛm sɛ nipahunu a wobedi fɔ mpanyimfoɔ atitire he asɛniiɛ; na sɛ woka sɛ, ‘Woyɛ kwasea’ a, wobedi fɔ akɔ gya a onnum da mu.
Nti sɛ wode afɔrebɔdeɛ ba afɔrebokyia ho, na wokae sɛ wo nua wɔ bibi tia wo a, nea odi kane a ɔsɛ sɛ woyɔ ne sɛ, gya w’afɔrebɔdeɛ he afɔrebokyia he so na wo ne no nkobom, na ɔno akyi he woasane aba abɛbɔ w’afɔdeɛ.
Sɛ wo ne wo soboɔbɔni nam kwane so ɔɔkɔ asennibea a, yɛ ntɛm na wo ne no mmom ansa na wo ne no aduru asennibea hɔ, anyɛ saa a wo soboɔbɔni he de wo bɛhyɛ temufoɔ nsa, na temufoɔ he so de wo ahyɛ wɛmfoɔ nsa, na ɔde wo akɔto afiase.
Nɔkorɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho, wonnya kwane mmfiri kosi sɛ wobetua wo kaprɛ a aka wo nsam he ansa.” Awaresɛeɛ ho nkyerɛkyerɛ “Hoate sɛ bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Nsɛe awadeɛ.’ Na me deɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ biaa a ɔhwɛ baa akɔnnɔ so sɛ nka ɔpɛ sɛ ɔne no bɛda he afa no n’akomam dada.
Sɛ w’ani nifa to wo sintidua a, tu firi hɔ na to twene; ɔyɛ ma wo sɛ wobɛhwere akwaa baako kyɛne sɛ wode nipadua he nyinaa bɛto amanehunu gya mu.
Na sɛ wo nsa nifa to wo sintidua a, twa firi hɔ na to twene; ɔyɛ ma wo sɛ wobɛhwere akwaa baako kyɛne sɛ bɛde nipadua he nyinaa bɛto amanehunu gya mu.” Awaregyaeɛ ho nkyerɛkyerɛ “Afei nso, bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Biaa a obegyae ne yerɛ he, ɔmma no awaregyaeɛ krataa.’ Na me deɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, sɛ bi gyae ne yerɛ na ɔnyɛ adwamammɔ nti ne ogyae no a, obetumi ama baa he aseɛ awareɛ; na biaa a ɔbɛware baa a bɛagyae no he nso aseɛ awareɛ.
Ntanka ho nkyerɛkyerɛ “Bio, hoate sɛ bɛka kyerɛɛ tetefoɔ he sɛ, ‘Nka ntanhunu, nso fa wo ntankadeɛ ma Awurade.’ Na me deɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, Nka ntam koraa, mfa soro nka ntam, efiri sɛ ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn ahennwa, saa nso ne mfa asaase nka ntam, efiri sɛ ɔyɛ ne nane ntiasoɔ; mfa Yerusalem nso nka ntam, efiri sɛ ɔyɛ Hene kɛseɛ he ahenkuro.
Na nka wo ti ntam, efiri sɛ wontumi nnyɔ tinwii baako mpo fufuo anaa tuntum.
Na ma nea wobɛka sɛ ɔyɛ ‘ɛɛ, he, nyɛ ɛɛ’, na nea wobɛka sɛ ‘daabi, he nso nyɛ daabi’; yei akyi ade foforɔ biaa firi bɔne mu.
Awerɛtɔ ho nkyerɛkyerɛ “Hoate sɛ bɛkaa sɛ, ‘ani nsi ani ananem, na sẽ nso nsi sẽ ananem.’ Na me deɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, Ho ne bɔnefoɔ nni asie.
Nso sɛ bi pae w’aso nifa mu a, dane baako he nso ma no; sɛ bi pɛ sɛ ɔne wo di asɛm na ɔfa w’ataadeɛ ngusoɔ a, fa deɛ ɔhyɛ aseɛ he so ka no ho; na sɛ bi hyɛ wo sɛ wo ne no nkɔ borɔfo-kwansini baako a, kɔ borɔfo-kwansini mmienu.
Adeɛ biaa a bi bɛsrɛ afiri wo hɔ he, fa ma no, na deɛ ɔfɛm bibi firi wo hɔ biaa nkame no.
Dɔ w’atamfoɔ “Hoate sɛ bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Dɔ wo yɔnko na tane w’atamfoɔ.’ Na me deɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, Honnɔ ho atamfoɔ na hommɔ mpaeɛ mma bɛ a bɛtaa ho, saa ne bɛma ho ayɛ ho Agya a ɔya soro he mma; efiri sɛ ɔma awia pie abɔnefoɔ ne ateneneefoɔ so, na ɔtɔ nsuo gu ateneneefoɔ ne bɛ a bɛnnyɛ ateneneefoɔ so.
Na sɛ hodɔ bɛ a bɛdɔ ho a, mmɛ akatua ne hobenya?
Togyefoɔ mpo nnyɔ saa anaa?
Na sɛ ho kyea ho nuanom nkoaa a, mmɛ ne ho ayɔ akyɛne binom?
Amanamane mufoɔ mpo nnyɔ saa?
Honyɛ pɛ, efiri sɛ, ho Agya ɔya soro he yɛ pɛ.
Adɔeɛ ho nkyerɛkyerɛ “Honhwɛ yie na hoannyɔ ho tenenee nnipa anim sɛ bebehu ho; sɛ hoyɔ saa a hoonnya akatua ho Agya a ɔya soro he hɔ.
“Nti sɛ wooyɔ adɔeɛ adeɛ a, mmɔ dawuro nni w’anim, sɛnea nyaatwomfoɔ he yɔ no hyiadane mu ne mmɔntene so he, sɛdeɛ bebenya nipa anim animuonyam.
Nɔkorɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho, bɛanya ba akatua dada.
Na sɛ wooyɔ adɔeɛ a, mma wo nsa benkum nnhu deɛ wo nsa nifa ɔɔyɔ, saa nti w’adɔeɛ he bɛyɛ kokoam adeɛ; na w’Agya a ohu kokoam he betua wo ka (badwam).
Mpaebɔ ho nkyerɛkyerɛ “Na sɛ hoobɔ mpaeɛ a honnyɔ sɛ nyaatwomfoɔ he; efiri sɛ bɛpɛ sɛ begyina hyiadane mu ne mmɔntene ntweaso bɔ mpaeɛ, sɛ nnipa behu bɛ.
Nɔkorɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, bɛanya bɛ akatua dada.
Na wo deɛ, sɛ woobɔ mpaeɛ a, kɔhyɛ wo dane mu na to wo ho pono mu na bɔ mpaeɛ kyerɛ w’Agya a ɔya kokoam he; na w’Agya a ohu kokoam he betua wo ka.
“Sɛ woobɔ mpaeɛ a, nka nsɛm pii kwa sɛ abosonsomfoɔ he; efiri sɛ besusu sɛ bɛkasaa dodoɔ nti bebetie bɛ.
Na ho deɛ honnyɔ sɛ bɛ, efiri sɛ ho Agya nim deɛ ohia ho ansa na hoobisa no.
Nti hommɔ mpaeɛ sɛ: Yɛ Agya a woya soro, anidie nka wo dini, W’ahennie mmra.
Wopɛ nyɛ hɔ, asaase yi so sɛdeɛ ɔteɛ soro.
Ma yɛ aduane nnɛ nso, sɛnea wo de ma yɛ daa he.
Na fa yɛ ka kyɛ yɛ, sɛnea yɛ nso yɛde akyɛ bɛ a bɛde yɛ ka.
Na nnyae yɛ mma yɛnnkɔ nsɔhwɛ mu, na mmom gye yɛ firi bɔnefoɔ he nsam.
[Efiri sɛ ɔyɛ wo ne ahennie ne tumi ne animuonyam yɛ wo dea daa, Amen!]
Na sɛ hode bɛ a bɛfom ho he mfomsoɔ kyɛ bɛ a, ho Agya a ɔya soro he nso de ho mfomsoɔ bɛkyɛ ho; nso sɛ hoammfa afoforɔ bɛ mfomsoɔ ankyɛ bɛ a, ho Agya a ɔya soro he nso ɔmmfa ho mfomsoɔ nkyɛ ho.
Mmuadadie ho nkyerɛkyerɛ “Na sɛ hoodi mmuada a, honnyɔ ho anim bosaa sɛ nyaatwomfoɔ he, efiri sɛ bɛyɔ bɛ anim bosaa sɛ ɔbɛyɔ a nnipa behu bɛ sɛ beedi mmuada.
Nɔkorɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, bɛanya bɛ akatua dada.
Nso sɛ woodi mmuada a, sra wo tim, (nunu mu) na hohoro w’anim, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a nnipa onnhu sɛ woodi abuada gye sɛ w’Agya a ɔya kokoam he; na w’Agya a ohu kokoam he betua wo ka.
Soro Agyapadeɛ ho nkyerɛkyerɛ “Honnhyehyɛ agyapadeɛ asaase yi so, baabi a mfɔteɛ ne naakyee sɛe no na akorɔmfoɔ bubu kowia; na mmom honhyehyɛ ho agyapadeɛ soro baabi a mfɔteɛ anaa naakyee ntumi nsɛe no anaa akorɔmfoɔ ntumi mmubu nkowia, efiri sɛ baabi a w’agyapadeɛ ya he, hɔ ne w’akoma nso ya.
Akoma mu hann “Ani yɛ nipadua kanea.
Nti sɛ w’ani yɛ a, nipadua he nyinaa bɛyɛ hann; nso sɛ w’ani nyɛ a nipadua he nyinaa bɛyɛ sum.
Nti sɛ hann a ɔya ho mu he yɛ sum a, he deɛ sum he bɛyɛ kɛse paa!
Nyankopɔn ne ahonyadeɛ “Akoa biaa ntumi nsom awuranom mmienu; efiri sɛ ɔbɛtane baako na wadɔ baako, anaa ɔde ne ho bɛbata baako na waabu baako animtia.
Hontumi nsom Nyankopɔn ne ahonyadeɛ.” Honnwennwene Nti meeka akyerɛ ho, honnwennwene ho kra ho, deɛ hobedi anaa deɛ hobɛnom, anaa ho nipadua ho, ɔfa deɛ hobɛhyɛ ho.
Nkwa nsom bo nkyɛne aduane, na nipadua nkyɛne ntoma anaa?
Honhwɛ nnomaa a bɛya wiem; bennua, bentwa, na bɛmmoa hwee ano ngu pata so, nso ho Agya a ɔya soro he mma bɛ aduane di.
Honsom bo nkyɛne bɛ anaa?
Na ho mu bi betumi adwennwene de dɔnhwere baako mpo ato ne nkwa so anaa?
Mmɛ nti ne hodwene nea hobefira ho?
Honhwɛ wuram asukooko, sɛdeɛ benyini; bɛnnyɔ adwuma na bɛnnto asaawa, nso meeka akyerɛ ho, Salomo animuonyam nyinaa akyi he, wanhyehyɛ ne ho sɛ bɛ mu baako mpo.
Nso sɛ Nyankopɔn fira wura a, ɔya hɔ nnɛ na kyena onni hɔ na bɛatwa ato fononoo mu ahye no, ntoma a, he deɛ ontumi mfira ho ntoma mma no mmoro so anaa, ho a ho gyidie sua?
Ne saa nti honnwennwene sɛ, Mmɛ ne yebedi anaa Mmɛ ne yɛbɛnom anaa Ɛɛne ne yebefira?
Na ɔyɛ amanamane mufoɔ ne bɛpre yeinom nyinaa ho; na nɔkorɛ, ho Agya a ɔya soro he nim sɛ hohia yeinom nyinaa.
Nso honni kane nhwehwɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie ne ne tenenee, na ɔde yeinom nyinaa nso bɛka ho ho.
“Nti honnwene kyena ho, efiri sɛ haw a ɔya kyena mu he, dɔɔso ma kyena heaa.
Haw a ɔya da biaa mu he dɔɔso ma da heaa.”
Atenyie ho nkyerɛkyerɛ Hommmu atɛne, na bɛammu ho atɛne.
Na atɛne a hobu he ɔnoaa ne bɛde bebu ho, na deɛ wode susu he, ɔno ne bɛde besusu ama ho.
Mmɛ nti ne wohwɛ wo yɔnko ani ase mfrɛ, na wonnwene mpuna a ɔda w’ani so he ho?
Anaa mmɛ nti ne wotumi ka kyerɛ wo yɔnko sɛ, Mma menyi w’ani ase mfrɛ berɛ a mpuna da so da w’ani so?
Wo nyaatwomni, di kane yi mpuna a ɔda w’ani so he, na ɔbɛma woahu yie na woatumi ayi wo yɔnko ani ase mfrɛ.
Honngu ade kronkron ho fi Hommfa ade kronkron mma nkramane; na honnto ho nhwene pa ngu mma mprako, na bɛamfa bɛ nane antiatia so na bɛannane amma ho so ammɛseɛ ho.
Adesrɛ Hommisa, na bɛde bɛma ho; honhwehwɛ, na hobehu; hommom, na bebebie pono he ama ho.
Na biaa a obisa he, ne nsa ka, na biaa a ɔhwehwɛ he, ohu, na biaa a obom he bebie pono he ma no.
Ho mu hwane ne ne ba bisa no paanoo a ɔbɛma no boɔ?
Anaa ne ba bisa no adwene a ɔbɛma no wɔ?
Na afei sɛ ho a hoyɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ mpo de nnepa mma ho mma a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ ne ho Agya a ɔya soro he ɔmmfa nnoɔma pa mma bɛ a bebisa no!
Mmara titire Nti adeɛ biaa a hopɛ sɛ nnipa yɔ ma ho he, honyɔ saa mma bɛ; na yei ne nea mmara he ne adiyifoɔ he ka.
Akwane ahodoɔ mmienu Homfa pono teaa he mu nwuram; na kwane deɛ ɔkɔ sɛeɛ mu he pono trɛ na so fa ɔmmerɛ, na dodoɔ ne fa saa kwane he so.
Na pono teaa, ɔne kwane teaa he so fa ɔdene na ɔno ne kɔ nkwa mu, na nnipa kakraa bi ne hu saa pono ne kwane he.
Dua ne n’aba Honhwɛ yie atorɔ adiyifoɔ ho, bɛ a bɛfira dwane nwoma ba ho nkyɛne nso bɛ mu paa deɛ bɛyɛ mpataku.
Bɛ aduaba ne hode behu bɛ.
Bɛtete bobe nkasɛe so anaa bɛtete borɔdoma hwerɛmo so?
Saa nso ne dua pa biaa so aba pa, na dua bɔne so aba bɔne.
Dua pa ntumi nso aba bɔne, saa nso ne dua bɔne ntumi nso aba pa. Dua biaa a ɔnso aba pa he betwa to twene gya mu.
Nti bɛ aba ne hode behu bɛ.
Setie ho nkyerɛkyerɛ Ɔnyɛ biaa a ɔfrɛ me sɛ, Awurade, Awurade, ne bɛkɔ soro ahennie mu, na mmom deɛ ɔyɔ m’Agya a ɔya soro he apɛdeɛ.
Saa da he, bebree bebisa me sɛ, Awurade, Awurade, yɛamfa wo dini anhyɛ nkɔm, na yɛamfa wo dini antutu ahonhommɔne, na yɛamfa wo dini annyɔ tumideɛ pii anaa?
Na mɛpae mu aka akyerɛ bɛ sɛ, Mennim ho da; homfiri me so nkɔ, ho a hoyɔɔ nnebɔne.
Abotane ne anwea so dansie “Nipa biaa a otie me nsɛm yi na ɔyɔ bɛyɛ sɛ nyansani a osii ne dane abotane so.
Nsuo tɔeɛ, nsuhyiri baeɛ, na mframa bɔ bɛbɔɔ no, nso ammu angu, efiri sɛ otoo ne fapem he abotane so.
Nso nipa biaa a otie me nsɛm yi na ɔnnyɔ he bɛyɛ sɛ bi a onnim nyansa a osii ne dane anweam.
Nsuo tɔeɛ, nsuhyiri baeɛ, mframa bɔ bɛbɔɔ no, na obu guu fam tim bubuu pasaa!” Na afei, berɛ a Yesu kaa nsɛm yi wieeɛ he, nnipadɔm he ho dwirii bɛ ne nkyerɛkyerɛ he ho, efiri sɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ bi a ɔwɔ tumi, na ɔnyɛ sɛnea bɛ atwerɛfoɔ he kyerɛkyerɛ he.
Yesu saa kwatani bi yadeɛ Berɛ a Yesu siane firii mmepɔ he so he, nnipadɔm pii dii n’akyi.
Na hwɛ, kwatani bi baa ne hɔ bebuu nkotodwe n’anim, kaa sɛ, “Awurade, sɛ wopɛ a, wobetumi ama me ho afiri.” Na Yesu tenee ne nsa de kaa no, kaa sɛ, “Mepɛ.
Wo ho mfiri!” Amonom hɔaa ne kwata he firii ne ho.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Hwɛ na woanka ankyerɛ nipa biaa; afei kɔ, fa wo ho kɔkyerɛ sɔfo, na bɔ afɔdeɛ a Mose hyɛeɛ he, na ɔnyɛ adansedie mma bɛ.” Yesu saa asraafoɔ ha so panyini bi akoa yadeɛ Na oduruu Kapernaum he, asraafoɔ ha so panyini bi baa ne hɔ, srɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade, m’akoa abubu gu fie a ohu amane paa.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Mɛba abɛsa no yadeɛ.” Na asraafoɔ ha so panyini he buaa sɛ, “Owura, memfata sɛ wobɛba me fie; kasa kɛkɛ, na m’akoa he ho bɛtɔ no.
Na me nso meyɛ bi a me di tumi a asraafoɔ hyɛ m’ase; sɛ meka kyerɛ baako sɛ, “Kɔ a ɔkɔ,” na meka kyerɛ foforɔ nso sɛ, “Bra,” a ɔba, na mehyɛ m’akoa so sɛ, “Yɔ yei” a, ɔyɔ.” Na Yesu tee deɛ ɔkaeɛ he, ne ho dwirii no, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ a bedi n’akyi he sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, menhu biaa Israel mu a ɔwɔ gyidie sei.
Meeka akyerɛ ho, nnipa bebree firi apieeɛ ne atɔeɛ bɛba ne Abraham ne Isak ne Yakob abɛtena soro ahennie mu abedidi, na ahennie he mma paa deɛ bɛbɛto bɛ atwene sum kabii mu, baabi a suu ne benabɔ ya.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ asraafoɔ ha so panyini he sɛ, “Kɔ; ɔnyɔ hɔ ma wo sɛdeɛ wo gyidie teɛ.” Na akoa he ho tɔɔ no saa dɔnhwere heaa mu.
Yesu saa nnipa bebree yadeɛ ya Petro fie Na afei Yesu kɔɔ Petro fie, na abunu akye Petro ase baa da hɔ.
Yesu sɔɔ ne nsa, na abunu he gyaeɛ, na ɔsɔreeɛ, na ɔyɔɔ no ahɔhoyɛ.
Saa anwummerɛ he bɛde nnipa bebree a bɛwɔ ahohommɔne braa no; ɔde tumi a ɔya n’asɛm mu tutuu ahohommɔne he, na ɔsaa bɛ a bɛyare nyinaa yadeɛ.
Yei maa deɛ diyifoɔ Yesaia kaeɛ he baam sɛ, “Ɔfaa yɛ mmerɛyɛ na ɔsoaa yɛ yadeɛ.” Yesu daakye akyidifoɔ Afei Yesu huu nnipadɔm pii sɛ bɛatwa ne ho ahyia he, ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bentwa nkɔ fa nohoaa.
Twerɛfoɔ bi baa ne nkyɛne sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛni, medi w’akyi baabi a wobɛkɔ biaa.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sakramane wɔ bɔno, na nnomaa a bɛya wiem wɔ pirebuo; nso Nipa Ba he deɛ onni baabi a ɔde ne ti bɛto mpo.” Na suani foforɔ nso kaa sɛ, “Awurade, mma me kwane na menni kane nkosie me papa.” Nso Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Di m’akyi, na ma awufoɔ nsie bɛ awufoɔ.” Yesu brɛɛ ahum ase Na Yesu tenaa kodoɔ he mu he, n’asuafoɔ dii n’akyi.
Ahum kɛseɛ bi bɔ faa po he so, na ano dene nti asorɔkye he baa kodoɔ he mu; nso na Yesu ada.
Na asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bɛyanee no, sɛ, “Awurade, gye yɛ!
Yɛɛhwere yɛ nkwa!” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ntia ho suro yi, ho a ho gyidie sua?” Na ɔsɔreeɛ na ɔteateaa mframa ne po he; na bɛyɛɛ dinn koraa.
Na yei yɛɛ bɛ nwanwa, na bɛkaa sɛ, “Abɛ nipa di a, mframa ne po mpo yɔ setie ma no yi?” Yesu tutuu ahonhommɔne ya Gadarene Na Yesu duruu asuogya hɔ he, Gadarenefoɔ asaase so he, nnipa mmienu a bɛwɔ honhommɔne firi afunsieɛ behyiaa no.
Na bɛ ho hu nti, na nnipa biaa ntumi ntwam saa kwane he so.
Amonom hɔaa bɛteateam sɛ, Mmɛ ne wo ne yɛ wɔ yɔ, Nyankopɔn Ba?
Woaba ha sɛ wobɛha yɛ ansa na mmerɛ he aduru anaa?
Saa mmerɛ he na mprakokuo bebree bi oodidi nkyɛne hɔ.
Na ahohommɔne he srɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ wotutu yɛ a, ma yɛnkɔ mprakokuo yi mu.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔ!” Nti bɛkɔ kɔ wuraa mprakokuo he mu; na hɔaa, mprako he nyinaa bɔɔ bum sianee monku he mu koguu po he mu ma bɛ ase hyeeɛ.
Na bɛ a bɛɛhwɛ mprakokuo he dwane kɔɔ kurom hɔ, kaa deɛ asi fa bɛ a na bɛwɔ ahohommɔne he ho kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Na afei kuro mu he nyinaa ba behyiaa Yesu; na behuu no he, bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ommfiri bɛ mpɔtamu hɔ nkɔ.
Na ɔfaa kodoɔ twaa po he kɔɔ ɔnoaa ne kurom.
Yesu saa bubuani bi yadeɛ Na hwɛ, nnipa binom de bubuani bi a ɔda kɛtɛ so braa no.
Berɛ a Yesu huu bɛ gyidie he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bubuani he sɛ, “Ɔba, ma wo akoma ntɔ wo yam, bɛde wo bɔne akyɛ wo.” Na atwerɛfoɔ bi keka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Beema yi ɔɔka abususɛm.” Na Yesu huu bɛ adwene he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ho dwene bɔne ho akoma mu?
Na yei mu mɛneɛ ne ɔmmerɛ, sɛ wobɛka sɛ, ‘Bɛde wo bɔne akyɛ wo,’ anaa sɛ wobɛka sɛ, ‘Sɔre nante’?
Na sɛ hobehu sɛ Nipa Ba he wɔ tumi asaase so sɛ ɔde bɔne kyɛ nti a.” Na afei ɔka kyerɛɛ bubuani he sɛ, “Sɔre, fa wo kɛtɛ, na kɔ wo fie.” Na ɔsɔreeɛ na ɔkɔɔ ne fie.
Berɛ a nnipadɔm he huu yei he, bɛ ho dwirii bɛ, na bɛhyɛɛ Nyankopɔn a ɔde tumi a ɔte sei ama nnipa he animuonyam.
Yesu frɛɛ Mateo Na Yesu nam he, ohuu beema bi a bɛfrɛ no Mateo sɛ ɔte togyebea, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Di m’akyi.” Na ɔsɔre dii n’akyi.
Na Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ tenaa adidiiɛ fie hɔ he, hwɛ, atogyefoɔ ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ bebree nso bɛtenaa bɛ nkyɛne.
Berɛ a Farisifoɔ he huu yei he, bɛka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ho kyerɛkyerɛni yi ne atogyefoɔ ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ didi yi?” Na ɔtee yei he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Bɛ a bɛte apɔ he benhia yaresafoɔ, na mmom gye sɛ bɛ a bɛyare he ne hia yaresafoɔ.
Honkɔ nkosua nea Nyankopɔn kyerɛ, sɛ ‘Mepɛ mmɔborɔhunu, na nyɛ afɔrebɔ.’ Na mamma sɛ meebɛfrɛ ateneneefoɔ, na mmom mebaa sɛ meebɛfrɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ.” Akɔnkyene ho nkyerɛkyerɛ Afei Yohane asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bɛkaa sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne yɛ ne Farisifoɔ he taa kyene kɔm, na wo asuafoɔ yi deɛ nkyene kɔm?” Na Yesu ka kyerɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ayefohyia he ahɔhoɔ ntumi nni awerɛhoɔ berɛ a ayefokunu he ya bɛnkyɛne, ɔnte saa?
Nna bi bɛba a bɛbɛfa ayefokunu he afiri bɛnkyɛne, na afei bɛbɛkyene kɔm.
Biaa mfa ntoma mono sini ntɛ ataadeɛ dada mu, anyɛ saa a, ntɛmuu he bɛte afiri mu ama ne nteɛ he ayɛ kɛse paa.
Saa nso ne bɛmmfa bobesa foforɔ ngu nsakotokuo dadaa mu; anyɛ saa a, nsakotokuo he bɛpae ama bobesa he ahwie agu, na kotokuo he asɛe.
Na mmom bɛde bobesa foforɔ gu nsakotokuo mono mu, na ne mmienu nyinaa ansɛe.” Abaayaa bi baa nkwa mu bio na maame bi nso nyaa ayaresa Berɛ a Yesu gu so ɔɔka yeinom akyerɛ bɛ he, mpofiremuaa hyiadane mu panyini bi ba bebuu nkotodwe n’anim kaa sɛ, “Me ba baa awu seseiaa; na bra na fa wo nsa begu ne so na obenya nkwa.” Na Yesu sɔre ne n’asuafoɔ he dii hyiadane mu panyini he akyi.
Afei mpofiremuaa, baa bi a mogyaa atu no mfirinhyia dummienu firii Yesu akyi bɛsɔɔ n’ataadeɛ ano, efiri sɛ, ɔkaa ne ne tim sɛ, “Sɛ mesɔ n’ataadeɛ ano nkoaa mpo a, menya ayaresa.” Yesu danee ne ho, na ohuu no he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Babaa, ma w’akoma ntɔ wo yam, wo gyidie agye wo.” Na amonom hɔaa baa he nyaa ayaresa.
Berɛ a Yesu duruu panyini he fie na ohuu atɛntɛmmɛne hyɛnefoɔ ne nnipadɔm a bɛɛyɔ gyegyeegye he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Homfiri ha nkɔ; na abaayaa he nwuiɛ, na waada.” Na bɛseree no twee.
Na bɛmaa nnipadɔm he kɔɔ abɔntene he, ɔkɔɔ dane he mu na ɔsɔɔ ne nsa, na abaayaa he sɔreeɛ.
Na yei ho amanebɔ trɛɛ mansini mu hɔ nyinaa.
Yesu saa anifirafoɔ mmienu yadeɛ Na Yesu firii hɔ kɔeɛ he, anifirafoɔ mmienu dii n’akyi teateam dendene sɛ, “Hu yɛ mmɔbɔ, Dawid ba!” Berɛ a ɔkɔɔ fie hɔ he, anifirafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne, na Yesu bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Hogye di sɛ metumi ayɔ yei?” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ɛɛ, Awurade.” Afei ɔde ne nsa kaa bɛ ani, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Sɛdeɛ ho gyidie teɛ he, ɔnyɔ saa mma ho.” Na bɛ ani biebieɛ.
Afei Yesu bɔɔ bɛ kɔkɔ dendenndene sɛ, “Honhwɛ na biaa ante yei.” Nso befirii hɔ kɔeɛ a ne bɛde ne ho asɛm trɛɛ mansini he mu nyinaa.
Yesu saa mum bi yadeɛ Bɛkɔeɛ akyi he, bɛde mum bi a honhommɔne ya ne mu braa no.
Na berɛ a otuu honhommɔne he, mum he kasaeɛ; na nnipadɔm he ho dwirii bɛ, na bɛkaa sɛ, “Biaa nhuu bibiaa a ɔte sei Israel da.” Nso Farisifoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Ɔde ahonhommɔne panyini tumi ne tu ahonhommɔne he.” Twa adwuma he so, nso apaafoɔ he sua Afei Yesu kyinkyinii nkuro ne nkuraa nyinaa ase, kyerɛkyerɛ bɛ hyiadane mu, na ɔpae mu kaa ahennie he ho asɛmpa he, na ɔsaa yadeɛ ne ahoɔmmerɛ nyinaa.
Berɛ a ohuu nnipadɔm he, ohuu bɛ mmɔbɔ, efiri sɛ na bɛɛteetee a na bɛabrɛ nso, na begu hɔ sɛ nwane a benni hwɛfoɔ.
Na ɔka kyerɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Twa he so, nso apaafoɔ he sua; nti hommisa twawura he na ɔnsoma apaafoɔ nkɔ ne twa adwuma he mu.”
Yesu Asuafoɔ dummienu he Na Yesu frɛɛ n’asuafoɔ dummienu he na ɔmaa bɛ tumi sɛ bɛmfa ntutu ahonhom fi, na bɛnsa yadeɛ ahodoɔ ne honam mmerɛyɛ nyinaa.
Asomafoɔ dummienu he bɛ dini di: deɛ odi kane ne, Simon a bɛsane frɛ no Petro; bɛ a ne bɛka ho ne ɔnoaa ne nua Andrea; Sebedeo ba Yakobo, ɔne ne nua Yohane; Filipo ne Bartolomeo; Toma ne Mateo a na ɔyɛ togyeni; Alfeo ba Yakobo, ne Tadeo; Simon a ofiri Kana, ne Yuda Iskariot a oyii Yesu maeɛ he.
Asuafoɔ dummienu he dwumadie Saa nnipa dummienu yi ne Yesu somaa bɛ hyɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hommmane nkɔ Amanamane mufoɔ hɔ, na honnwura Samariafoɔ kuro biaa mu, na mmom honkɔ Israelfoɔ he mu, nwane a bɛayera he hɔ.
Sɛ hokɔ a, hompae mu nka asɛmpa he sɛ, ‘Soro ahennie he abɛne.’ Honsa yadeɛ, honyane awufoɔ, homma akwatafoɔ ho mfiri, hontutu ahohommɔne.
Honyaa no kwa; nti homfa mma kwa.
Hommfa sikakɔkɔɔ, anaa dwetɛ, anaa kɔɔbere ngu abɔsoɔ mu, hommfa akwantuo bɔtɔ, anaa ntaadeɛ mmienu, anaa mpaboa anaa poma; na mmom adwumayɔni akatua fata no.
Kuro anaa akuraa biaa a hobɛkɔ mu he, hommisa deɛ ɔfata a ɔya hɔ, na hontena hɔ kosi sɛ hobefiri hɔ.
Fie biaa a hobewura mu biaa honkyea.
Sɛ fie hɔfoɔ gye ho a, homma ho asomdwie mmra bɛ so; na sɛ bɛannye ho a, homma ho asomdwie nsane mmra ho nkyɛne.
Sɛ bi annye ho anaa wantie ho nsɛm a, hoofiri fie anaa kurom hɔ a homporoporo ho nane ase mfuturo ngu hɔ na ɔnyɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne sɛ ho apo bɛ.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, atemuda he Nyankopɔn behu Sodom ne Gomora mpo mmɔbɔ akyɛne saa kuro he.
Taa ho nkɔmhyɛ “Hwɛ, meesoma ho sɛ nnwane akɔ mpataku mfimfini; nti honya nyansa sɛ wɔ, na honyɛ nnipa a ho ho nni asɛm te sɛ mmuburo.
Honhwɛ ho ho yie bɛ ho, efiri sɛ bɛde ho bɛma badwafoɔ na bɛahwe ho bɛ hyia adane mu; na me nti bɛbɛtwe ho akɔ amradofoɔ ne ahemfo anim, na ayɛ adansedie ama bɛ ne Amanamane mufoɔ.
Sɛ beyi ho mma a, honnwene sɛnea hobɛkasa anaa deɛ hobɛka; efiri sɛ bɛde deɛ hobɛka he bɛma ho saa berɛ heaa mu; na nyɛ ho ne hobɛkasa, na mmom ɔyɛ ho Agya Honhom ne bɛfa ho mu akasa.
Nua beyi nua ama wuo, na agya ayi ne ba ama, na mma bɛsɔre atia awofoɔ ama bɛaku bɛ; na me dini nti nnipa nyinaa bɛtane ho.
Na nea obegyina akosi awieeɛ he, ɔno ne bɛbɛgye no nkwa.
Sɛ bɛtaa ho kuro baako so a, honwane nkɔ kuro foforɔ so; na nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, honnkɔ Israel nkuro nyinaa mu na Nipa Ba he aba.
“Suani nkyɛne ne kyerɛkyerɛni, saa ara nso ne akoa nkyɛne ne wura; ɔdɔɔso ma suani sɛ ɔbɛyɛ sɛ ne kyerɛkyerɛni, anaa akoa sɛ ne wura.
Sɛ bɛfrɛɛ fie he wura he Beelsebul a, mprɛ ahe ne bɛmfrɛ fie he mufoɔ saa bi!
Deɛ ɔsɛ sɛ besuro no “Nti honnsuro bɛ; na adeɛ biaa nni hɔ a so akata a bɛmmpa ho ntoma, anaa ahinta a ɔnna adi.
Deɛ meka kyerɛɛ ho kokoam he, honka no badwam; na deɛ meka guu ho asum he, honnyina adane atifi mmɔ no dawuro.
Honnsuro bɛ a beku honam nso bentumi nku kra; na mmom honsuro deɛ obetumi asɛe honhom ne honam bronsam gya mu.
Bɛnntɔno mpatuprɛ mmienu nnye kaprɛ anaa?
Nso bɛ mu baako mpo nkwati ho Agya ntɔ fam.
Na ho tinwii mpo bɛakane ne nyinaa.
Nti honnsuro; hosom bo sene mpatuprɛ koraa.
Saa nti biaa a ɔbɛgye me atum nnipa anim he, me nso mɛgye no atum m’Agya a ɔya soro he anim; nso deɛ ɔbɛpo me nipa anim he, me nso mɛpo no m’Agya a ɔya soro he anim.
Ko di asomdwie anim “Honnwenne sɛ mede asomdwie ne baa asaase so; mammfa asomdwie amma, na mmom mede sekane.
Na maaba sɛ mede mpaepaemu ɔɔbɛto babeema ne n’agya ntam, babaa ne ne maame ntam, na ase asɔre atia n’ase baa; na nipa fiefoɔ bɛyɛ n’atamfoɔ.
Biaa a ɔdɔ Agya anaa na kyɛne me he mfata sɛ ɔbɛyɛ me suani; na biaa a ɔdɔ babeema anaa babaa kyɛne me he nso mfata sɛ ɔbɛyɛ me suani; na biaa a ɔmmfa n’asennua he na onni m’akyi he mfata sɛ ɔbɛyɛ me suani.
Deɛ ne nsa aka ne kra he, obefiri ne nsa, na bɛ a me nti bɛbɛhwere bɛ kra he bɛ nsa bɛka.
Akatua “Biaa a ɔgye ho he gye me, na deɛ ɔgye me he gye deɛ ɔsomaa me he nso.
Deɛ ɔgye diyifoɔ ya diyifoɔ dini mu he benya diyifoɔ akatua; na deɛ ɔgye nipa tenenee ya nipa tenenee dini mu he benya nipa tenee akatua; na deɛ ɔbɛma nkumaa yi bi nsuo nnwunu kuruwaa baako mpo he suani dini mu he, nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ n’akatua ɔmmɔ no da.”
Suboni Yohane ahoyera Na berɛ a Yesu kasa kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ dummienu he wieeɛ he, ofirii hɔ kɔɔ bɛ nkuro he mu sɛ ɔɔkɔ kyerɛkyerɛ, na afei wapaem kaa n’asɛm he hɔ.
Asomafoɔ a bi firi Suboni Yohane hɔ baa Yesu nkyɛne Berɛ a Yohane da afiase a ɔtee deɛ Kristo ɔɔyɔ he, ɔsomaa n’asuafoɔ ma bɛ bebisaa Yesu sɛ, “Wone deɛ ɔɔba he, anaa yɛnhwɛ foforɔ kwane?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔ na honkɔka deɛ hoate ne deɛ hoahu nkyerɛ Yohane: anifirafoɔ hu adeɛ, mmubuafoɔ nante, akwatafoɔ ho firi, asotifoɔ te asɛm, awufoɔ nyane firi wuom, na bɛka asɛmpa he kyerɛ ahiafoɔ.
Nhyira ne deɛ mennto bɛ sintidua.” Yesu kamfõõ Suboni Yohane Na bɛɛkɔ he, Yesu firii aseɛ kaa Yohane ho asɛm kyerɛɛ nnipadɔm he sɛ: “Mmɛ ne hokɔɔ serɛ so kɔhwɛeɛ?
Nnɛm a mframa ohim no anaa?
Sɛ onte saa a ɛɛne ne hokɔhwɛeɛ?
Bi a ɔhyɛ ntaade pa?
Hwɛ, bɛ a bɛhyɛ ntaade pa he bɛya ahemfie.
Anaa abɛ koraa nti ne hofirii adi kɔhwɛeɛ?
Diyifoɔ?
Ɛɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho, sɛ ɔte saa; nso, ɔkyɛne diyifoɔ koraa.
Yei ne deɛ bɛatwerɛ ne ho asɛm sɛ, ‘Hwɛ, meesoma me bɔfoɔ adi w’anim, a obesiesie w’anim kwane.’ Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, nipa biaa nni hɔ a baa awo no a ɔyɛ kɛseɛ kyɛne Suboni Yohane; nso nea osua koraa soro ahennie mu he yɛ kɛseɛ kyɛne no.
Ofiri Suboni Yohane berɛ so besi nnɛ bɛyɔ soro ahennie he ho adeɛ anibereɛ so, na bɛ a bɛ ani abere he nso fa no aniɔdene so.
Na adiyifoɔ ne mmra he nyinaa hyɛɛ nkɔm de besii Yohane berɛ so; na sɛ hobɛgye adi a, ɔno ankasa ne Elia a otwa sɛ ɔba he.
Deɛ ɔwɔ aso he ntie!
“Nso hwane ho ne mede nemmafoɔ yi bɛtoto?
Bɛte sɛ mmɔfra a bɛɛteam frɛ bɛ mfɛfoɔ sɛ, ‘Yɛabɔ mmɛne amma ho, nso hoansa; yɛatwa adwo, nso hoannsu.’ Na Yohane baeɛ, na onnidi, na ɔnnom nso, na bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Ɔwɔ honhommɔne’; Nipa Ba he baeɛ a odidi na ɔnom, na hoka sɛ, “Ɔyɛ didifoɔ ne nsanomfoɔ, togyefoɔ ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ bɛ adamfo!’ Nso, bɛ a bɛde Nyankopɔn nyansa di dwuma he da no adi sɛ ne nyansa he yɛ papa.” Nkuro a bɛansakra bɛ adwene he nnue Afei ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ kaa nkuro a na waayɔ ne tumideɛ he mu fa kɛseɛ hɔ he anim, efiri sɛ bɛansakra bɛ adwene, “Korasin due!
Betsaida due!
Efiri sɛ, sɛ bɛyɔɔ tumideɛ a bɛayɔ no ho mu he, bɛyɔɔ no Tiro ne Sidon a, nka bɛasakra bɛ adwene afira ayitoma de nso apete bɛ tim de akyerɛ bɛ adwensakra dadaada.
Meeka akyerɛ ho, atemmuda he, bebehu Tiro ne Sidon mmɔbɔ akyɛne ho.
Na wo Kapernaum nso, bɛbɛpegya wo akɔ soro anaa?
Daabi da, bɛde wo bɛkɔ asamando.
Efiri sɛ, bɛyɔɔ tumideɛ a bɛayɔ no wo mu he Sodom a, nka Sodom kuro he ya hɔ de besi nnɛ.
Na meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, atemmuda he, bebehu Sodom asaase mmɔbɔ akyɛne ho.” Hommra me nkyɛne, na mɛma ho ahome Saa berɛ he, Yesu kaa sɛ, “Agya, soro ne asaase Wura, meda wo ase, efiri sɛ, wode nnoɔma yi ahinta anyansafoɔ ne mmadwemma, na woayi no adi akyerɛ mpapahwekwaa.
Ampa, Agya, saa ne sɔ w’ani.
M’Agya de nnoɔma nyinaa ahyɛ me nsa; na biaa nnim Ba he, gye Agya he; na biaa nnim Agya he nso, gye Ba he ne biaa a Ba he pɛ sɛ ɔbɛma n’ahu no.
Ho a hoabrɛ, na ho so nnesoa nyinaa, hommra me nkyɛne, na mɛma ho ahomee.
Homfa me konnua nto ho ho so, na honsua me, efiri sɛ medwo na mebrɛ me ho ase akoma mu, na hobenya homee ama ho kra.
Efiri sɛ, me konnua ɔmmerɛ na m’adesoa so mu ɔhare.”
Yesu asuafoɔ he buu homeda he so Saa berɛ he, Yesu kɔfaa aburofuom homeda; na kɔm de n’asuafoɔ he, na bɛhyɛɛ aseɛ pempanee aburo he bi weeɛ.
Na Farisifoɔ he huu bɛ he, bɛka kyerɛɛ Yesu sɛ, “Hwɛ, w’asuafoɔ he ɔɔyɔ deɛ mmara mma kwane mma bɛnnyɔ no homeda.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkenkanee deɛ Dawid yɔeɛ mmerɛ a kɔm dee ɔne ne nkurofoɔ he anaa?
Owuraa Nyankopɔn fie, na odii Kyerɛ Paanoo he a mmara mma kwane mma ɔno anaa ne nkurofoɔ he nso nni, gye sɛ asɔfoɔ nkoaa.
Anaa honkenkanee no mmara he mu sɛ homeda he, sɛ asɔfoɔ a bɛya asɔrefie he bu homeda he so a benni fɔ?
Meeka akyerɛ ho, deɛ ɔsõ kyɛne asɔrefie he ya ha.
Sɛ nka na honim Nyankopɔn asɛm a ɔdɛ ‘Mepɛ mmɔborɔhunu na nyɛ afɔrebɔ,’ ase a nka hoammu deɛ onni fɔ he fɔ.
Na Nipa Ba he yɛ homeda he so tumfoɔ.” Beema a ne nsa awu he Yesu firii hɔ kɔɔ bɛ hyiadane mu.
Na beema bi ya hɔ a ne nsa awu, na bebisaa no sɛ, “Ɔyɛ mmara sɛ bɛsa yadeɛ homeda?” Bebisaa no yei de pɛɛ kwane a bɛbɛfa so abɔ no kwaadu.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Fa ne sɛ ho mu bi wɔ dwane baako, na ɔtɔ abura mu homeda a, ɔnnsɔ ne mu nnyi no mmfiri mu anaa?
Nipa so nni mfasoɔ bebree nkyɛne dwane?
Mmara ma ho kwane sɛ bɛyɔ papa homeda.” Na afei ɔka kyerɛɛ beema he sɛ, “Tene wo nsa.” Ɔteneeɛ, na ɔyɛɛ yie sɛ baako heaa.
Na yei maa Farisifoɔ he firii adi kɔbɔɔ ne ti so pɔ, kwane a bɛbɛfa so aku no.
Nyankopɔn akoa a wayi no he Berɛ a Yesu huu saa he, ofirii hɔ.
Nnipa bebree dii n’akyi, na ɔsaa bɛ nyinaa yadeɛ, na ɔhyɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛmma biaa nhu ne nipa bane.
Yei maa deɛ diyifoɔ Yesaia kaeɛ he baam sɛ: “Yei ne m’akoa a mayi no, medɔ ba, ɔno ne me kra ani sɔ no.
Mehwie me Honhom agu ne so, na wapaem aka atɛntenenee akyerɛ Amanamane mufoɔ.
Ɔnnko na ɔnnteam, na biaa nso ɔnte ne nne abɔntene.
Ommu nnɛm a abuka he mu, na ntomabane a oofiri wisie he nso onnum no, kosi sɛ ɔde tenenee bɛkɔ nkunimdie mu.
Na ne dini mu ne Amanamane mufoɔ benya anidasoɔ.” Yesu ne Beelsebul Na bɛde bi a ɔwɔ honhommɔne a ɔyɛ nifirani na ɔsane yɛ mum braa no; na ɔsaa no yadeɛ, na deɛ na nka ɔyɛ mum he kasaeɛ na ohuu adeɛ.
Na nnipadɔm he nyinaa ho dwirii bɛ na bebisaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ Dawid Ba he di?” Nso Farisifoɔ he teeɛ he, bɛkaa sɛ, “Yei deɛ ɔnyɛ hwee sɛ Beelsebul tumi ne beema yi de tutu ahonhommɔne.” Na onim bɛ adwene, nti ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ahennie biaa a ɔne ne ho di asie he bɛsɛe, na kuro anaa fie biaa a ɔko tia ne ho he, onnyina.
Sɛ Satan tutu Satan a, sɛ na ɔne ne ho odi asie o?
Ɔba saa a ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na n’ahennie agyina?
Sɛ me de Beelsebul tumi tutu ahonhommɔne a, hwane tumi ne ho nkurofoɔ so de betutu ahonhommɔne?
Yei nti ho akyidifoɔ ne bebu ho atɛne.
Nso sɛ ɔnam Nyankopɔn Honhom so ne metutu ahonhommɔne a, hedeɛ na Nyankopɔn ahennie he anya aba ho so.
Anaa ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na bi atumi akɔ ahoɔdenfoɔ fie sɛ ɔɔkɔfom ne nnoɔma afa, berɛ a onni kane nkyekyere ahoɔdenfoɔ he?
Gye sɛ ɔkyekyere no ansa na watumi afa ne nnoɔma he.
Biaa a ɔnka me ho he sɔre tia me, na deɛ ɔne me mmoaboa ano he hwete mu.
Nti meka akyerɛ ho, bɛde bɔne ne abususɛm biaa a nipa bɛyɔ bɛkyɛ, nso abususɛm a bɛyɔ tia Honhom he deɛ bɛmmfa nkyɛ.
Deɛ ɔka asɛm bi tia Nipa Ba he bɛde bɛkyɛ no, nso deɛ ɔkasa tia Honhom Kronkron he deɛ bɛmmfa nkyɛ no, saa berɛ yi anaa berɛ a ɔbɛba akyire yi.
Dua ne n’aba “Homma dua he nyɛ dua pa, na n’aba nso ayɛ aba pa; na sɛ homma dua he nyɛ dua bɔne n’aba nso yɛ aba bɔne; na dua he aba ne yɛde hu dua korɔ a ɔyɛ.
Nankatia mma!
Ɔbɛ yɛ dɛ na hoaka nsɛm pa, berɛ a hoyɛ abɔnefoɔ?
Nea abu so akoma mu he ne ano ka.
Nipa pa de nnoɔma pa a waboaboa ano mu de nnoɔma pa ba, na nipa bɔne de nnoɔma bɔne a waboaboa ano de nnoɔma bɔne ba.
Meeka akyerɛ ho, atemmuda he hobebu asemhunu biaa a efiri ho anum ba ho akonta; efiri sɛ ho nsɛm so ne bɛnam bebu ho bem, na ho nsɛm nso so ne bɛnam bebu ho fɔ.” Bebisaa nsɛnkyerɛnne firii Yesu hɔ Na atwerɛfoɔ bi ne Farisifoɔ bi kaa sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, yɛpɛ sɛ yehu nsɛnkyerɛnne bi firi wo hɔ.” Nso obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Nemmafoɔ ho yɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ ne awaresɛefoɔ a hobisa nsɛnkyerɛnne, nso nsɛnkyerɛnne biaa nni hɔ sɛ diyifoɔ Yona nsɛnkyerɛnne.
Na sɛnea Yona dii bonsu yam nnansa, awia ne anadwo he, saa ara ne Nipa Ba he bedi nnansa asaase bunu mu.
Ninewefoɔ ne nemmafoɔ behyia atemmuo mu, na bebebu saa nemmafoɔ yi fɔ, efiri sɛ Ninewefoɔ he gyee Yona asɛnka diiɛ na bɛsakraa bɛ adwene, na hwɛ, deɛ ɔso kyɛne Yona ya ha.
Anafoɔ Hemaa ne nemmafoɔ behyia atemmuo mu, na obebu nemmafoɔ yi fɔ, efiri sɛ ofirii asaase ano nohoaa betiee Salomo nyansa, na hwɛ, deɛ ɔkyɛne Salomo ya ha!
Ahonhommɔne saneba “Sɛ honhommɔne tutu firi nipa mu kɔ a, okokyinikyini akwaweɛ so sɛ ɔɔpɛ homebea, na sɛ wannya bi a, afei ɔka sɛ, ‘Mɛsane akɔ me fie a mefirii mu he mu.’ Sɛ obeduru hɔ na sɛ obehu sɛ mu da hɔ mpan, na bɛaprapra mu kama asiesie mu a, ɔkɔ kɔfa ahonhommɔne ahodoɔ nson a bɛ tim ɔdene sene no, na bɛbɛtena mu; na ofiri saa mmerɛ he ɔɔkɔ he saa nipa he abrabɔ bɛyɛ tane akyɛne n’ahyɛaseɛ.
Saa na ɔbɛyɛ nemmafoɔ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ yi.” Yesu abusua kann Na ogu so ɔɔkasa kyerɛ nnipadɔm he, ne maame ne ne nuanom begyinaa abɔntene pɛɛ sɛ bɛ ne no kasa.
Na bi ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Hwɛ, wo maame ne wo nuanom gyina mfikyire pɛ sɛ bɛ ne wo kasa.” Na Yesu buaa deɛ ɔkaa saa he sɛ, “Hwane ne me maame, na hwane ne me nuanom?” Na ɔtenee ne nsa n’asuafoɔ he so sɛ, “Yeinom ne me maame ne me nuanom!
Na biaa a ɔyɔ m’Agya a ɔya soro he apɛdeɛ he ɔno ne yɛ me nuabeema, me nuabaa ne me maame.”
Mfantoho a ɔfa abaguo ho Saa da heaa, Yesu firii fie na ɔkɔtenaa mpoano.
Nnipadɔm pii kyeree ne so nti ɔkɔtenaa kodoɔ bi mu, maa nipakuo he gyinaa mpoano hɔ.
Na ɔyɔɔ mfantoho de kyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ nnoɔma bebree.
Na ɔkaa sɛ: “Hontie!
Gufoɔ bi firii adi sɛ okogu n’aba.
Na oguu aba he, aba he bi koguu kwankyɛne, na nnomaa bɛsosɔɔ ne nyinaa.
Aba he bi nso koguu abotane so, baabi a nɛteɛ nni papa, na ofifirii ntɛm, nso na nɛteɛ he mu nnɔ.
Na berɛ a awia pieeɛ he, esiane sɛ benni nhini nti, ne nyinaa twintwameeɛ, na ɔhyee koraa.
Na aba he bi nso koguu nkasɛe mu, na nkasɛe he nyiniiɛ he omiaa aba he.
Aba he bi nso koguu asaase pa mu na ɔsoo aba bebree, bi mmɔho ha, bi mmɔho aduosia, bi mmɔho aduasa.
Ma deɛ ɔwɔ aso he ntie!” Mfantoho he botae Na asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bebisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne wode mfantoho ne ɔɔkasa akyerɛ bɛ yi?” Obuaa sɛ, “Ho deɛ bɛde ama ho sɛ honte ahintasɛm a ɔfa soro ahennie he ho ase, nso bɛ deɛ bɛmfa maa bɛ.
Na bɛ a bɛwɔ ahennie he ho nteaseɛ he, bɛde nteaseɛ bebree bɛka bɛ ho ama bɛanya no mmorosoɔ, na bɛ a benni bi he, nteaseɛ ketewa bi a bɛwɔ he mpo befiri bɛ nsa.’ Deɛ ntia mede mfantoho ne ɔɔkasa akyerɛ ho ne sɛ ‘hu deɛ bebehu nso benhu no yie, te deɛ bɛbɛte nso bɛnte aseɛ.’ Ɔnam bɛ so ne diyifoɔ Yesaia nkɔmhyɛ he aba mu sɛ: Te deɛ hobɛte, nso hoɔnte aseɛ da na hobɛhwɛ paa, nso honnhu no yie da.
Efiri sɛ mane he akoma apirim, na bɛ asom oduru sɛ bɛbɛte, na bɛakata bɛ ani; sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bɛmfa bɛ ani mpo nhwɛ, na bɛmfa bɛ aso nso ntie, na bɛamfa bɛ akoma ante aseɛ ama bɛanane bɛ ho, na masa bɛ yadeɛ.’ Nso ho deɛ nhyira ne ho ani, sɛ ohu, ne ho aso, sɛ ɔte.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, adiyifoɔ ne ateneneefoɔ bebree pɛɛ sɛ behu deɛ hoahu yi, nso bɛanhu, na bɛte deɛ hoate yi, nso bɛante.
Mfantoho he asekyerɛ Afei hontie abaguo ho mfantoho he nkyerɛaseɛ.
Sɛ bi te ahennie he ho asɛm na ɔnnte aseɛ a, bɔnefoɔ he ba behwim deɛ bɛagu no na akomam he; yei ne deɛ beguu no kwankyɛne he.
Na deɛ beguu no abotane so he, ɔno ne nipa a ɔde anigyeɛ gye asɛm he ntɛntɛm; nso saa nipa he nni nyinasoɔ, nso ɔtena hɔ kakra, na sɛ asɛm he nti, sɛ amaneɛ anaa ɔtaa ba pɛ, ntɛmaa, saa nipa he sane n’akyi.
Na deɛ beguu no nkasɛe mu he, ɔno ne nipa a ɔte asɛm he a, wiase adwendwene ne ahonyadeɛ nnaadaa mia asɛm he, na ne saa nti, ontumi nso aba biaa.
Na deɛ beguu no asaase pa so he, ɔno ne nipa a ɔte asɛm he a ɔte aseɛ, na ɔsõ aba bebree, bi mmɔho ha, bi nso mmɔho aduosia, bi nso mmɔho aduasa.” Ayuo ne wuraa ho mfantoho Ɔmaa bɛ mfantoho foforɔ sɛ, “Yebetumi de soro ahennie he atoto nipa bi a oguu aba pa n’afuom ho; na berɛ a nnipa daeɛ he, tamfoɔ bi ba beguu wuraa fraa ayuo he mu, na ɔkɔeɛ.
Afei berɛ a ofifiriiɛ a na ɔɔso aba he, saa berɛ heaa ne wuraa he nso fifiriiɛ.
Na ne nkoa ba bebisaa no sɛ, ‘Owura, ɔnyɛ aba pa ne woduaa no w’afuo mu yi?
Na afei wuraa yi firi he?’ Obuaa sɛ, ‘Tamfoɔ bi ne ayɔ saa he o!’ Nkoa he bisaa no sɛ, ‘Nti wopɛ sɛ yekotutu firi mu anaa?’ Nso obuaa sɛ, ‘Daabi; sɛ hootutu wura he a hobetutu ayuo he afra.
“Homma ne nyinaa mmom nyini nkosi twaberɛ; na oduru twaberɛ a mɛka akyerɛ twafoɔ he sɛ, Honni kane nsesa wura he na honkyekyere no akuoakuo nkɔhye no, na ayuo he deɛ honsesa nkogu m’apata so.’ ” Sinapi aba ho Mfantoho Na ɔmaa bɛ mfantoho foforɔ bi sɛ, “Soro ahennie he te sɛ sinapi aba a bi koduaa no n’afuom; ɔyɛ ketewa paa aba nyinaa mu deɛ, nso sɛ onyini a, ɔbɛyɛ wuraa nyinaa mu kɛseɛ na ɔbɛyɛ dua kɛseɛ ma nnomaa a bɛya wiem bɛyɛ bɛ buo ne mmane so.” Mmɔreka ho mfantoho Na ɔmaa bɛ mfantoho foforɔ bi sɛ, “Soro ahennie te sɛ baa bi a ɔfaa mmɔreka na ɔde fraa sam susukuruwa mmeɛnsa kosii sɛ ne nyinaa tuiɛ.” Deɛ ntia Yesu de mfantoho kasa Yesu de mfantoho ne kaa yeinom nyinaa kyerɛɛ nnipadɔm he; wankwanti mfantoho ne bɛ ankasa.
Yei hyɛɛ deɛ diyifoɔ he kaeɛ he ma sɛ: “Mebie m’ano mfantoho mu; Mɛpae mu aka deɛ ahinta firi wiase ahyɛaseɛ.” Yesu kyerɛkyerɛ ayuo ne wuraa mfantoho he ase Afei ogyaa nnipakuo he hɔ, na ɔkɔɔ fie.
Na n’asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne, bɛkaa sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛ yɛ mfantoho a ɔfa wuraa a ɔya mfuom he ase.” Na obuaa sɛ, “Deɛ ogu aba pa he ne Nipa Ba he; afuo he ne wiase, na aba pa he ne ahennie he mma; wuraa he ne bɔnefoɔ he mma, na tamfoɔ a oduaa wuraa he ne Bronsam; twaberɛ he ne awieeɛ berɛ, na twafoɔ he ne abɔfoɔ.
Sɛnea bɛboaboa wuraa na bɛde gya hye he, saa ara na ɔbɛyɔ awieeɛ berɛ he nso.
Nipa Ba he bɛsoma n’abɔfoɔ, na bɛbɛboaboa bibi a ɔto sintidua ne abɔneyɛfoɔ nyinaa ano afiri n’ahennie mu, na bɛato bɛ atwene gya fononoo mu, hɔ ne bebesu na bɛatwerɛ bɛ sẽ Na teneneefoɔ he deɛ bɛbɛhyerɛn sɛ awia bɛ Agya ahennie mu.
Mma deɛ ɔwɔ aso he ntie!
Agyapadeɛ ho mfantoho “Soro ahennie he te sɛ agyapadeɛ a bɛde asie asaase bi so, na bi huiɛ na ɔkata so; na ɔde ho anigyeɛ kɔtɔnoo deɛ ɔwɔ nyinaa kɔtɔɔ asaase he.
Ahwene pa ho mfantoho “Bio, soro ahennie te sɛ dwadini bi a ɔɔhwehwɛ ahwene pa; na okohuu deɛ ne boɔ ɔdene paa he, ɔkɔtɔnoo deɛ ɔwɔ nyinaa de kɔtɔeɛ.
Asau ho mfantoho “Bio, soro ahennie te sɛ asau a bɛde guu po mu na benyaa nam ahodoɔ bebree; ɔyɛɛ ma he, bɛtwe baa kokoɔ so, tenaa ase, na bɛde papa he guu nkɛntɛne mu na bɛtoo deɛ ɔnyɛ he guiɛ.
Saa ara ne ɔbɛyɛ awieeɛ berɛ mu.
Abɔfoɔ he bɛba abɛfa abɔnefoɔ he afiri teneneefoɔ mu na bɛato bɛ agu gya fononoo he mu, baabi a suu ne setwerɛ ya.
Ahennie he ho mfantoho “Yesu bisaa bɛ sɛ, Hoate yei nyinaa ase?” Na bebuaa sɛ, “Ɛɛ.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Yei nti twerɛfoɔ biaa a bɛatete ne sɛ suani ma soro ahennie he te sɛ fiewura a oyi n’agyapadeɛ foforɔ ne dadaa nyinaa firi n’adekoradane mu.” Berɛ a Yesu wiee saa mfantoho yi, ofirii hɔ kɔeɛ.
Bɛpoo Yesu ya Nasaret Na afei Yesu baa ɔnoaa ne kurom, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ sɛ ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ nkurofoɔ he bɛ hyiadane mu hɔ, na bɛ ho dwirii bɛ maa bɛkaa sɛ, “He ne saa nipa yi konyaa nyansa ne tumi nnwuma a ɔte sei?
Ɔnyɛ duadwumfoɔ he ba he di?
Ɔnyɛ ne maame ne bɛfrɛ ne Maria he?
Ɔnyɛ ne nua mmeemmaanom ne Yakobo ne Yosef ne Simon ne Yuda?
Na ɔnyɛ yɛ ne ne nua mmaanom nso ne te yi?
Na afei he fa ne okonyaa yeinom nyinaa?” Na ɔyɛɛ sintidua maa bɛ.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Anidie mmɔ diyifoɔ biaa gye sɛ ne mane mu ne ne fie.” Na gye a bɛannye anni nti, wannyɔ tumi nnwuma bebree hɔ.
Suboni Yohane wuo Saa berɛ he Herode a na ɔyɛ mantam sodifoɔ he tee Yesu ho asɛm; na ɔka kyerɛɛ ne nkoa sɛ, “Yohane Suboni di; wanyane afiri awufoɔ mu, saa nti ne ahoɔdenneɛ nnwuma yi ɔɔda adi wɔ ne mu he.” Na Herode akye Yohane de no ato afiase, ne nua Filipo yerɛ, Herodia nti, efiri sɛ na Yohane taa ka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Mmara mma kwane sɛ wobɛware no.” Owom sɛ na Herode pɛ sɛ oku no deɛ, nso na osuro nkurofoɔ he, efiri sɛ bebu Yohane sɛ diyifoɔ.
Berɛ a Herode awoda duruu so he, Herodia babaa bɛsaa badwam hɔ, na ɔsɔɔ Herode aniaa kosii sɛ ɔhyɛɛ bɔ kaa ntam sɛ ɔbɛma no deɛ obebisa biaa.
Ogyinaa ne maame afotuo so, kaa sɛ, “Fa Suboni Yohane ti to apampaa so ma me ha yiaa.” Na hene he werɛ hoeɛ, nso ntam a ɔkaa ne badwafoɔ ne ahɔhoɔ he anim nti, ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa ma no.
Ɔsoma maa bɛkɔɔ afiase kotwaa Yohane ti.
Bɛde too apampaa so braa abaayaa he, na ɔde kɔmaa ne maame.
Yohane asuafoɔ bɛfaa n’amu he kosiee no; na bɛkɔ ka kyerɛɛ Yesu.
Yesu maa nnipa mpemnum aduane diiɛ Afei berɛ a Yesu teeɛ he, ɔtenaa kodoɔ mu firii nnipadɔm he nkyɛne kɔɔ baabi a biaa nni.
Nso nnipadɔm he teeɛ he, befirii nkuro so nam fam tii no.
Na osii fam he, ohuu nkurofoɔ bebree; ne yam hyehyɛɛ no maa bɛ, na ɔsaa bɛ mu ayarefoɔ he yadeɛ.
Nnwunu dwoeɛ he, n’asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bɛkaa sɛ, “Ha yɛ bea a biaa nni, adeɛ so asa; gya nkurofokuo he kwane ma bɛnkɔ nkuraa he ase nkɔtɔ aduane nni!” Nso Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ɔnsɛ sɛ bɛkɔ; homma bɛ bibi nni.” Bebuaa sɛ, “Yenni hwee sɛ paanoo num ne nkyenam mmienu.” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Homfa mmra me.” Afei ɔhyɛɛ nnipadɔm he sɛ bɛntenatena serɛ he so.
Ɔfaa paanoo nnum ne nkyenam mmienu he, ɔhwɛɛ soro, hyiraa so bubuu paanoo he, na ɔde maa asuafoɔ he, na asuafoɔ he de maa nkurofoɔ he.
Na biaa diiɛ na bɛmeeɛ; na bɛsesaa aseɛ mporoporowa nkɛntɛmma dummienu.
Sɛ yɛde mmaa ne mmɔfra si nkyɛne a, bɛ a bɛdiiɛ he bɛyɛ mmeema mpemnum.
Yesu nantee po so Amonom hɔaa Yesu maa asuafoɔ he kɔɔ kodoɔ he mu sɛ bentwa nni n’anim kane nkɔ asuogya nohoa, na onnya nnipadɔm he kwane.
Na ogyaa bɛ kwane wieeɛ he, ɔkɔɔ bepɔ he so kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ.
Nnwunu dwoeɛ he, na ɔno nkoaa ne ya hɔ.
Saa berɛ yi na kodoɔ he mmɛne asaase koraa, na na asorɔkye he ama nnoɔma mu ayɛ dene, efiri sɛ na mframa he bɔ tia bɛ.
Na ahemakye nnɔn mmeɛnsa ɔɔkɔ he, Yesu nantee po he so hyiaa bɛ.
Na berɛ a asuafoɔ he huu sɛ ɔnam po he so he, bɛ akoma tuiɛ, na bɛkaa sɛ, “Ɔyɛ samane!” Na bɛde hu teateam.
Nso amonom hɔaa Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Homa ho akoma ntɔ ho yam, ɔyɛ me a; honnsuro koraa.” Petro buaa no sɛ, “Awurade, sɛ ɔyɛ wo a, hyɛ me, na menante nsuo he so mmra wo nkyɛne.” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Bra!” Nti Petro si firii kodoɔ he mu, firii aseɛ nantee nsuo he so sɛ ɔɔkɔ Yesu nkyɛne.
Nso ohuu mframa dendene he, osuroeɛ, na ofirii aseɛ sɛ ɔɔmmem he, ɔteaam sɛ, “Awurade, gye me!” Na ntɛmaa Yesu tenee ne nsa sɔɔ ne mu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wo a wo gyidie sua, mmɛ nti ne wogyee akyinnye?” Berɛ a beduruu kodoɔ he mu he, mframa he gyaeɛ.
Na bɛ a bɛ ya kodoɔ he mu he koto sɔree Yesu, kaa sɛ, “Ampa, wo ne Nyankopɔn Ba he.” Yesu saa yadeɛ Genesaret Na betwaa nsuo he kɔɔ n’agya he, bebeduruu Genesaret asaase so.
Na asaase he sofoɔ huu no he, bɛde nkra kɔmaa bɛ a bɛtete mpɔtamu hɔ nyinaa ma bɛde ayarefoɔ a bɛya hɔ nyinaa braa no, na bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔma bɛmfa bɛ nsa nka n’ataadeɛ mmuano ano; na bɛ a bɛde bɛ nsa kaeɛ nyinaa nyaa ayaresa koraa.
Honhom mu ahoteɛ Na Farisifoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he firii Yerusalem baa Yesu nkyɛne bebisaa sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne w’asuafoɔ he bu mpanyimfoɔ atetesɛm so yi?
Bɛnnhohoro bɛ nsa ansa na bɛadidi.” Obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ho atetesɛm nti ho bu Nyankopɔn mmara so yi?
Nyankopɔn dɛ, ‘Di w’agya ne wo na nni,’ na ‘Biaa a ɔka asɛmmɔne fa ne n’agya anaa ne na ho he otwa sɛ owu.’ Nso hoka sɛ deɛ ɔka kyerɛ ne papa anaa ne maame sɛ, ‘Deɛ nka wobenya afiri me hɔ yɛ akyɛdeɛ a yɛde ma Nyankopɔn a onhia sɛ saa nipa he di ne papa ne maame nni.’ Nti hode ho atetesɛm sɛe Nyankopɔn asɛm.
Ho nyaatwomfoɔ!
Odi sɛ Yesaia hyɛɛ ho ho nkɔm sɛ: ‘Mane yi de bɛ ano fafa ne di me nni, nso bɛ akoma deɛ atwe afiri me ho kɔ akyirikyiri; bɛsom me kwa, bɛkyerɛkyerɛ nipa ahyɛdeɛ sɛ ɔyɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ pa.’ ” Nnoɔma a ogu nipa ho fi ankasa Na ɔfrɛɛ nkurofokuo he baa ne nkyɛne na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hontie na ho nteaseɛ: nyɛ deɛ ɔkɔ nipa anum ne gu nipa ho fi, na mmom deɛ ofiri anum ba ne gu nipa ho fi.” Na asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wonim sɛ Farisifoɔ he tee deɛ wokaeɛ yi ato bɛ sintidua?” Obuaa sɛ, “Dua biaa a ɔnyɛ m ‘Agya a ɔya soro he ne duaeɛ he bebetu.
Honnyae bɛ; bɛyɛ anifirafoɔ a bɛkyerɛ anifirafoɔ kwane.
Sɛ nifirani kyerɛ nifirani kwane a, bɛ mmienu he nyinaa bɛtɔ amena mu.” Petro tee yei he, ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛ yɛ saa bɛ yi ase.” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Ho nso honni nteaseɛ?
Honnim sɛ bibiaa a ɔkɔ anum he kɔ yafunum na opie kɔ yaaneem?
Na deɛ ofiri anum he firi akoma mu, na yei ne deɛ ogu nipa ho fi.
Na akoma mu ne adwemmɔne, awudie, ayerefasɛm, adwamane, korɔnobɔ, adansekunumu ne dinsɛeɛ firi ba.
Saa nnoɔma yi ne gu nipa ho fi, na mmom ɔnyɛ nsa a bi anhohoro ho na ode didi ne gu ne ho fi.” Kanaanni baa bi gyidie Na afei Yesu firii hɔ kɔɔ Tiro ne Sidon mantam mu.
Na amonom hɔaa, Kanaanni baa bi a ofiri mpɔtamu hɔ ba bɛteateam sɛ, “Hu me mmɔbɔ, Awurade, Dawid Ba; honhommɔne ɔɔha me babaa.” Nso wammua no koraa.
Na n’asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ, “Pam no ma no nkɔ, na ɔɔteateam gu yɛ so dodo.” Na obuaa sɛ, “Bɛansoma me baabiaa sɛ Israel mu nnwane a bɛayera he hɔ.” Nso baa he bebuu nkotodwe n’anim kaa sɛ, “Awurade, boa me.” Na Yesu buaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ fɛ sɛ bɛfa mma aduane to ma nkramane mma.” Na baa he kaa sɛ, “Awurade, ɔte saa deɛ, nso nkramane mma he di mporoporowa a ofiri bɛ wura pono so gu fam he.” Na Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Baa, wo gyidie so!
Ɔnyɔ hɔ mma wo sɛ deɛ wopɛ.” Amonom hɔaa ne ba he nyaa ayaresa.
Yesu saa nnipa bebree yadeɛ Afei Yesu firii hɔ bɛfaa Galilea po he ho, na ɔkɔɔ mmepɔ he so, ne ɔtenaa ase.
Nnipadɔm pii de mpakye, mmubuafoɔ, anifirafoɔ, mmum, ne afoforɔ bebree kaa bɛ ho baa ne nkyɛne.
Bɛde bɛ beguu ne nane ase, na ɔsaa bɛ yadeɛ, na ɔyɛɛ nnipadɔm he nwanwa berɛ a behuu nea na ɔyɛ mmum he sɛ ɔɔkasa, bɛ a na bɛyɛ mpakye ne mmubuafoɔ sɛ bɛnnante, na nea na ɔyɛ anifirani he huu sɛ afie deɛ ohu adeɛ.
Na bɛhyɛɛ Israel Nyankopɔn he animuonyam.
Yesu maa nnipa mpemnan aduane Na Yesu frɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne na ɔkaa sɛ, “Nnipadɔm yi yɛ me mmɔbɔ paa, efiri sɛ bɛatena me nkyɛne nnansa nso benni hwee a bebedi; na mempɛ sɛ mɛma bɛde kɔm akɔ, anyɛ saa a bebetumi atwa ato kwanem.” Na asuafoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “He fa ne yebenya paanoo a ɔbɛso nnipa bebree yi serɛ so ha?” Yesu bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Howɔ paanoo dodoɔ mmeɛhe?” Na bɛkaa sɛ, “Nson, ne nkyenam nketewa kakraa bi.” Na ɔhyɛɛ nkurofokuo he ma bɛtenaa ase, na afei ɔfaa paanoo nson ne nkyenam he; na ɔdaa ase wieeɛ he, obubuu mu mmaa asuafoɔ he, na asuafoɔ he nso de maa nnipadɔm he.
Na bɛ nyinaa di meeɛ; na bɛsesaa aseɛ mporoporowa nkɛntɛmma nson.
Sɛ yɛankane mmaa ne mmɔfra anka ho a, bɛ a bediiɛ he dodoɔ bɛyɛ mmeema mpemnan.
Berɛ a ogyaa nnipadɔm he kwane he, ɔfaa kodoɔ kɔɔ Magadan mpɔtamu.
Bebisaa nsɛnkyerɛnne firii Yesu hɔ Na Farisifoɔ ne Sadukifoɔ baa Yesu nkyɛne sɛ bɛbɛsɔ no ahwɛ.
Nti bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ ɔnyɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne bi a ofiri soro nkyerɛ bɛ.
Na obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ awia ɔkɔtɔ a, hoka sɛ, ‘Wiem bɛte, efiri sɛ anim ayɛ kɔkɔɔ.’ Na anɔpa, ‘Ahum betu, efiri sɛ anim ayɛ kɔkɔɔ ne kusuu.’ Honim sɛ deɛ bɛkyerɛ wiem tebea ase, nso honnim sɛnea bɛkyerɛ mmerɛ ho nsɛnkyerɛnne ase.
Ho nneemmafoɔ a hoyɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ ne adwamammɔfoɔ bisa nsɛnkyerɛnne, nso nsɛnkyerɛnne biaa nni hɔ a bɛde bɛma ho sɛ Yona nsɛnkyerɛnne.” Na ogyaa bɛ hɔ kɔeɛ.
Farisifoɔ ne Sadukifoɔ mmɔreka Berɛ a asuafoɔ he duruu asuogya nohoa he, bɛ werɛ firii sɛ bɛamfa paanoo biaa.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honhwɛ yie Farisifoɔ ne Sadukifoɔ mmɔreka ho.” Bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Sesɛɛ yɛamfa paanoo yi nti a.” Na Yesu huiɛ he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Ho a ho gyidie sua, mmɛ nti ne paanoo a hoammfa ho asɛm ne hooka?
Nti honni nteaseɛ?
Honnkae paanoo nnum a mede maa nnipa mpemnum, ne nkɛntɛmma dodoɔ a hosesaeɛ he?
Anaa paanoo nson a nnipa mpemnan diiɛ he, nkɛntɛmma meɛhe ne ho sesaeɛ?
Mmɛ nti ne ho nteaseɛ sɛ ɔnyɛ paanoo asɛm ne meeka?
Honhwɛ yie Farisifoɔ ne Sadukifoɔ mmɔreka ho!” Na bɛtee aseɛ sɛ ɔnyɛ mmɔreka paanoo ho ahwɛyie ho asɛm ne ɔɔka na mmom, Farisifoɔ ne Sadukifoɔ nkyerɛkyerɛ ho ahwɛyie.
Petro kyerɛɛ nipa ko a Yesu yɛ Afei Yesu baa Kaesare Filipi mpɔtamu, na obisaa n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Nkurofoɔ ka sɛ Nipa Ba he ne hwane?” Na bebuaa sɛ, “Binom dɛ ɔyɛ Yohane Suboni, binom so dɛ ɔyɛ Elia, na binom nso dɛ ɔyɛ Yeremia anaa adiyifoɔ he mu baako.” Obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Ho nso hodɛ me ne hwane?” Simon Petro buaa sɛ, “Wone Kristo he, Nyankopɔn teasefoɔ he Ba.” Na Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Nhyira ne wo, Simon, Yona ba!
Ɔnyɛ honam ne mogyaa ne yi kyerɛɛ wo, na mmom m’Agya a ɔya soro.
Na meeka akyerɛ wo, wo ne Petro, na botane yi so ne mesi m’asafo, na Asamando pono ontumi mmu mmfa so da.
Mɛma wo soro ahennie he safoa, na deɛ wobɛkyekyere no asaase yi so he na bɛakyekyere no soro dada, na deɛ wobɛsane no asaase so he na bɛasane no soro dada.” Na ɔhyɛɛ asuafoɔ he ketee sɛ bɛnnka nkyerɛ biaa sɛ ɔno ne Kristo he.
Yesu hyɛɛ ne wuo ne ne wusɔreɛ ho nkɔm Ofiri saa mmerɛ he ɔɔkɔ he, Yesu firii aseɛ kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ ɔsɛ sɛ ɔkɔ Yerusalem na okohu amane, mpanyimfoɔ ne asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ nsam na beku no, na ne nnansa so he ɔsɔre.
Na Petro de no gyinaa nkyɛne na ofirii aseɛ kaa n’anim sɛ, “Awurade!
Yei mpare wo.
Yei ntumi nto wo da!” Na ɔdanee ne ho ka kyerɛɛ Petro sɛ, “Firi me so kɔ, Satan!
Woyɛ sintidua ma me; efiri sɛ woamfa w’adwene ansi Nyankopɔn so na mmom honam nnwuma so.” Suaniyɛ ho asodie Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Sɛ bi pɛ sɛ odi m’akyi a, ma no mpa ne ho akyi na ɔmfa n’asennua na onni m’akyi.
Na bɛ a bɛpɛ sɛ bɛkora bɛ kra he, obefiri bɛ nsa, na bɛ a me nti bɛbɛhwere bɛ kra he, bɛ nsa bɛka.
Na sɛ bi nya wiase nyinaa na ohwere ne kra a mmɛ mfasoɔ ne obenya?
Anaa mmɛ ne bi bɛma de asesa ne kra?
“Na Nipa Ba he de n’abɔfoɔ bɛba n’Agya animuonyam mu, na obetua nipa biaa ka sɛdeɛ n’adwuma teɛ.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, binom gyina ha a, bennwu kosi sɛ bebehu sɛ Nipa Ba he firi n’ahennie mu ɔɔba.”
Yesu animuonyam hyerɛnn Nnansia akyi he, Yesu faa Petro ne Yakobo ne ne nua Yohane kaa ne ho kɔɔ bepɔ tentene bi so.
Na ɔsakraa bɛ ani so, na n’anim hyerɛnn te sɛ awia, na ne ntaadeɛ yɛɛ fitafita te sɛ hann.
Na hwɛ, Mose ne Elia yii bɛ ho adi, na bɛ ne no kasaeɛ.
Na Petro ka kyerɛɛ Yesu sɛ, “Awurade, ɔyɛ sɛ yɛya ha; sɛ wopɛ a, mɛbɔ apata mmeɛnsa, wo deɛ baako, Mose deɛ baako, na Elia so deɛ baako.” Berɛ a ogu so ɔɔkasa he, amonom hɔaa mununkum bi a ɔhyerɛn bɛkataa bɛ so, na nne bi firi mununkum he mu kaa sɛ, “Yei ne me Ba, deɛ medɔ no he; ɔno ne sɔ m’ani; hontie no!” Berɛ a asuafoɔ he tee saa he, bɛde bɛ ani butubutuu fam, na besuroeɛ paa.
Nso Yesu ba de ne nsa bɛkaa bɛ, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Honsɔre na honnsuro.” Na bɛmaa bɛ ani so he, bɛanhu biaa ka Yesu ho.
Befiri bepɔ he so oosiane he, Yesu hyɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honnka anisoadehunu yi ho asɛm nkyerɛ biaa kosi sɛ Nipa Ba he bɛsɔre afiri awufoɔ mu.” Na asuafoɔ he bisaa no sɛ, “Sɛ ɔte saa deɛ a mmɛ nti ne atwerɛfoɔ he ka sɛ ɔsɛ sɛ Elia ba ansa?” Oyii ano sɛ, “Ampa, Elia ɔɔba abɛtoto nnoɔma nyinaa yie; nso meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ Elia aba dada, na bɛanhu no, na bɛyɔɔ no deɛ bɛpɛ biaa.
Saa ara nso ne ɔnkyɛre biaa, Nipa Ba he nso behu amane bɛ nsam.” Na asuafoɔ he tee aseɛ sɛ Suboni Yohane ho asɛm ne ɔɔka akyerɛ bɛ he.
Yesu saa abranteɛ bi a na ɔwɔ honhommɔne yadeɛ Berɛ a bɛbaa nnipadɔm he nkyɛne he, beema bi baa ne nkyɛne bebuu nkotodwe n’anim, kaa sɛ, “Awurade, hu me ba yi mmɔbɔ, na ɔyare twerɛ, na oohu amane; na ɔtaa tɔ gya ne nsuo mu.
Na mede no braa w’asuafoɔ he, nso bɛantumi ansa no yadeɛ.” Yesu buaa sɛ, nneemmafoɔ a honni gyidie na hoamane, mentena ho nkyɛne nkosi da bɛ?
Onkosi da bɛ ne menya ho ho aboterɛ?
Homfa no mmra me.” Na Yesu teatea honhommɔne he, na ofirii ne mu, na abɔfra he nyaa ayaresa saa berɛ heaa.
Na asuafoɔ he baa Yesu nkyɛne kokoam bebisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti na yɛantumi antutu no yi?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho gyidie a osua nti a. Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, sɛ howɔ gyidie a ne kɛseɛ te sɛ sinapi aba a, nka hoka kyerɛ bepɔ yi sɛ, ‘Tu firi ha kɔ ha a,’ obetutu; na bibiaa nni hɔ a hoontumi nyɔ.” [Nso saa bibi yi deɛ gye sɛ mpaebɔ ne mmuadadie ne betumi atutu no.]
Yesu hyɛɛ ne wuo ne ne wusɔreɛ ho nkɔm Berɛ a bebehyiaa Galilea he, Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Bebeyi Nipa Ba he ahyɛ nnipa nsa, na bebeku no, na nnansa so he ɔbɛsɔre.” Na ɔyɛɛ bɛ awerɛhoɔ pii.
Yesu tuaa asɔrefie ho toɔ Beduruu Kapernaum he, bɛ a bɛgyegye asɔredane toɔ he baa Petro hɔ bebisaa no sɛ, “Nti wo kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ ntua asɔredane toɔ he bi anaa?” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Ɛɛ, otua.” Na Petro baa fie he, Yesu ne pagyaa ho asɛm baeɛ bisaa sɛ, “Simon, Wodwene ho sɛ?
Hefoɔ hɔ ne asaase yi so ahemfo gye adwadeɛ anaa toɔ?
Bɛgye no bɛ mma hɔ anaa afoforɔ hɔ?” Na Petro kaa sɛ, “Bɛgye firi afoforɔ hɔ,” he, Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Saa deɛ a, na mma he de bɛ ho.” Nso sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɔ na yɛnnto sintidua nti, kɔ po so koto doraa; na adwene a wobedi kane ayi no he bie n’anum a, na wobehu dwetɛ; fa kɔma bɛ sɛ me ne wo toɔ.”
Ahobrɛaseɛ ho nkyerɛkyerɛ Saa berɛ he asuafoɔ he baa Yesu nkyɛne bebisaa no sɛ, “Hwane ne yɛ kɛseɛ soro ahennie mu?” Na ɔfrɛɛ abɔfra bi, na ɔde no gyinaa bɛ ntam, na ɔkaa sɛ “Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, sɛ hoanyɔ ho ho sɛ mmɔfra a, hontumi nhyɛne soro ahennie mu.
Nipa biaa a ɔbrɛ ne ho ase sɛ abɔfra he, ɔno ne deɛ ɔyɛ kɛseɛ paa soro ahennie mu.
“Deɛ ɔgye abɔfra a ɔte sei baako me dini mu he, ɔgye me.
Sintiduatoɔ Sɛ ho mu bi to mmɔfra nketewa a bɛgye me di yi mu baako sintidua a, nsunsuansoɔ a ɔbɛba ne so he so kyɛne sɛ bɛde ayuyammoɔ bɛsɛne ne kɔno mu de no akɔto po bunu mu.
“Wiase nnue, sintidua nti!
Otwa sɛ sintidua toɔ ba, nso deɛ ɔnam ne so bɛba he, onnue!
Sɛ wo nsa anaa wo nane to wo sintidua a, twa firi hɔ, na to twene; ɔyɛ mma wo sɛ wode nsa sini anaa nane sini bɛkɔ nkwa mu sene sɛ wowɔ nsa mmienu anaa nane mmienu na bɛbɛto wo ato daa amanehunu gya mu.
Na sɛ w’ani to wo sintidua a, tu, na to twene; ɔyɛ sɛ wode ani baako bɛkɔ nkwam sene sɛ wowɔ ani mmienu na bɛbɛto wo atwene amanehunu gya mu.
Dwane a wayera ho mfantoho “Honhwɛ yie na hoammu nketewa yi baako mpo animtia; meeka akyerɛ ho, soro hɔ, bɛ abɔfoɔ hwɛ m’Agya a ɔya soro he anim daa.
[Na Nipa Ba he baeɛ sɛ ɔɔbɛgye bɛ a bɛayera.]
Hosusu yei ho sɛ?
Sɛ dwanhwɛfoɔ bi wɔ nnwane ha, na sɛ baako yera a, onnyae aduokro-nkron he mmepɔ he so nkɔnhwehwɛ baako a wayera he anaa?
Sɛ ohu no a, nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, n’ani gye ne ho kyɛne aduokro-nkron a bɛanyera he.
Saa ara nso ne ɔnyɛ ho Agya a ɔya soro he pɛ sɛ nketewa yi mu baako bɛyera.
Sɛdeɛ beyi bi a w’ayɛ bɔne atɛne “Sɛ wo nua fom wo a, kɔ na kɔka ne mfomsoɔ kyerɛ no, berɛ a ho mmienu nkoaa hoahyia.
Sɛ otie wo a, woanya wo nua.
Na sɛ wanntie wo a, fa nipa baako anaa mmienu ka wo ho, na asɛm he nyina adansefoɔ mmienu anaa mmeɛnsa so.
Sɛ saa nipa he anntie bɛ a, ka kyerɛ asafo he; na sɛ saa nipa he antie asafo he nso a, fa no sɛ bi a ɔnnyɛ gyidini, na mmom togyeni.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, deɛ hobɛkyekyere no asaase so he yɛ deɛ bɛakyekyere no soro, na deɛ hobɛsane no asaase so he yɛ deɛ bɛasane no soro.
Bio, nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, ho mu mmienu yɛ anokorɔ adeɛ biaa a hobebisa no asaase yi so a, m’Agya a ɔya soro he bɛyɔ ama ho.
Baabi a nnipa mmienu anaa mmeɛnsa ahyia me dini mu he, na meka bɛ ho.” Bɔnefakyɛ Na Petro baa ne nkyɛne bebisaa no sɛ, “Awurade, mprɛ dodoɔ sɛ ne me nua yɔ bɔne tia me a me mfa nkyɛ no?
Onkoduru mprɛ nson?” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Menka nkyerɛ wo sɛ, mprɛ nson, na mmom, onkosi mprɛ aduɔson mmɔho nson.
Akoa a onni bɔnefakyɛ he ho mfantoho “Ne saa nti bɛde soro ahennie he bɛtoto hene bi a ɔpɛɛ sɛ ɔne ne nkoa bu akonta ho.
Berɛ a ɔhyɛɛ nkotabuo ase he, bɛde bi a ɔde no ka a ɔboro paani mfie dunnum akatua begyinaa n’anim; esiane sɛ ontumi ntua nti, ne wura he hyɛɛ sɛ bɛntɔno ɔne ne yerɛ ne ne mma ne n’agyapadeɛ nyinaa metua ka he.
Ne saa nti akoa he buu nkotodwe hwee ase n’anim, srɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Nya aboterɛ ma me, na metua ne nyinaa.’ Na akoa he wura he nyaa tema maa no, na ogyaa no de ne ka he kyɛɛ no.
Nso saa akoa korɔ heaa firii hɔ kɔeɛ he, ɔkɔtoo ne yɔnko akoa baako a ɔno nso de no ka bɛyɛ paani bosome mmeɛnsa ne fa akatua; na ɔtintim no sɔɔ ne mene, na ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Tua ka a wode me he.’ Afei ne yɔnko akoa he de ne ho too fam srɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Nya aboterɛ ma me, na metua wo ka.’ Nso wampene; na ɔde no kɔtoo afiase sɛ ɔnna hɔ nkosi sɛ obetua ne ka he.
Berɛ a nkoaa a bɛka ne ho he huu deɛ asi he, bɛ werɛ hoo paa, na bɛkɔkaa deɛ asi nyinaa kyerɛɛ bɛ wura he.
Na ne wura he frɛɛ no ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Wo akoa timuɔdenfoɔ!
Mede wo ka a wo de me nyinaa kyɛɛ wo esiane sɛ wosrɛɛ me nti.
Ɔnsɛ sɛ nka wohu wo yɔnko akoa mmɔbɔ, sɛdeɛ mehuu wo mmɔbɔ he anaa?’ Na ne wura he de abufuo de no hyɛɛ ahohiahiafoɔ nsa, kosi sɛ obetua ne ka a ɔde no nyinaa.
Saa ne m’Agya a ɔya soro he so bɛyɔ ho mu bi a wamfiri n’akoma mu amfa ankyɛ ne nua.”
Awaregyaeɛ ho nkyerɛkyerɛ Yesu ka yeinom wiee he, ofirii Galilea kɔɔ Yudea mpɔtamu hɔ Yordan akyi.
Na nnipa nnipadɔm pii dii n’akyi, na ɔsaa bɛ yadeɛ hɔ.
Na Farisifoɔ baa ne nkyɛne bɛsɔɔ no hwɛeɛ, sɛ, “Mmara ma ho kwane sɛ asɛm bi nti beema bi gyae ne yerɛ anaa?” Obuaa sɛ, “Honkenkane sɛ, mfitiaseɛ he, beema ne baa ne Nyankopɔn bɔɔ bɛ na ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Yei nti ne beema begya ne papa ne ne maame, na ɔde ne ho akɔbata ne yerɛ, na bɛ mmienu ayɛ honam baako’?
Ne saa nti bɛnna so nyɛ mmienu bio, na mmom bɛyɛ honam korɔ.
Nti deɛ Nyankopɔn de abom he, ɔnsɛ sɛ biaa tete mu.” Afei bebisaa no sɛ, “Hedeɛ, mmɛ nti ne Mose hyɛɛ yɛ sɛ, bi betumi ama awaregyaeɛ krataa na wagyae baa he?” Ɔka kyerɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ɔyɛ ho akomadene nti ne Mose maa ho kwane sɛ honyae ho yerɛnom, na ofiri mfitiaseɛ he, na ɔnte saa.
Na meeka akyerɛ ho, sɛ ɔnyɛ adwamammɔ nti, na bi gyae ne yerɛ na ɔsane ware foforɔ a, wasɛe awareɛ.” N’asuafoɔ he ka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ saa ne beema ne ne yerɛ asɛm teɛ deɛ a, ɔnsɛ sɛ bi ware koraa.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ biaa ne betumi agye saa nkyerɛkyerɛ yi, gye sɛ bɛ a bɛde ho nteaseɛ ama bɛ nkoaa.
Na binom ya hɔ a bɛwoo bɛ he na bɛ ho nni hɔ, na binom nso ya hɔ a, nnipa ne ama bɛ ayɛ saa, na binom so ya hɔ a bɛ ankasa, ne soro ahennie he nti, bɛayɔ ama bɛ ho nni hɔ.
Deɛ obetumi agye yei he, ɔnye.” Yesu hyiraa mmɔfra Afei bɛde mmɔfra braa Yesu, sɛ ɔmfa ne nsa ngu bɛ so mmɔ mpaeɛ mma bɛ.
Na Asuafoɔ he kaa bɛ a bɛde bɛ baeɛ he anim; Nso Yesu kaa sɛ, “Homma mmɔfra he mmra me nkyɛne, na ho nsi bɛ kwane; na bɛ a bɛte saa ne soro ahennie he yɛ bɛ dea.” Na ɔde ne nsa guu bɛ so hyiraa bɛ na ɔkɔɔ ne kwane.
Daa nkwa Afei, nipa bi baa Yesu nkyɛne bebisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, mmɛ nwuma pa ne menyɔ na manya daa nkwa?” Na obisaa no sɛ, ‘Mmɛ nti ne wobisa me papa ho asɛm?
Baako pɛ ne yɛ papa.
Sɛ wopɛ sɛ wo nya nkwa a, di ahyɛdeɛ he so.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Mu deɛ ɔya he?” Na Yesu kaa sɛ, “Nni awu; Nsɛe awareɛ; Mmɔ korɔno; Nni adansekunumu; Di w’agya ne wo na nni; na afei, Dɔ wo yɔnko sɛ wo ho.” Abranteɛ he ka kyerɛɛ Yesu sɛ, “Maadi yeinom nyinaa so; mmɛ bio ne ɔsɛ sɛ meyɔ?” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ wo pɛ sɛ wo woyɛ pɛ a, kɔ, tɔno w’ahonyadeɛ, na fa sika he ma ahiafoɔ, na wobenya agyapadeɛ soro; na afei bra, bedi m’akyi.” Berɛ a abranteɛ he tee saa asɛm he, ɔde awerɛhoɔ firii hɔ kɔeɛ, efiri sɛ na ɔwɔ ahonyadeɛ pii.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, ɔbɛyɛ dene ama sikani sɛ ɔbɛkɔ soro ahennie mu.
Bio, meeka akyerɛ ho, ɔbɛyɛ mmerɛ ama yoma sɛ ɔbɛfa paneɛ tokuro mu sene sɛ sikani bɛkɔ Nyankopɔn ahennie mu.” Asuafoɔ he tee yei he, ɔyɛɛ bɛ nwanwa kɛse, na bɛkaa sɛ “Sei ne ɔteɛ deɛ a, hwane ne betumi anya nkwa?” Na Yesu hwɛɛ bɛ kaa sɛ, “Nnipa fam deɛ ɔnyɛ yie, nso Nyankopɔn fam deɛ bibiaa nni hɔ a ontumi nyɛ hɔ.” Na afei Petro yii ano sɛ, “Hwɛ, yɛagya nnoɔma nyinaa hɔ abedi w’akyi, mmɛ ne yebenya?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, sɛ Nipa Ba he tena n’animuonyam adwa so a, na nnoɔma nyinaa yɛ foforɔ a, ho a hoadi m’akyi yi nso ho bɛtena ahennwa dummienu so, abu Israel mmusuakuo dummienu he atɛne.
Na biaa a me dini nti, wagya afie anaa nuammeema anaa nuammaa, anaa papa anaa maame anaa mma, anaa nsaase hɔ he, obenya no mmɔho ha, na obenya daa nkwa nso.
Nso adikanfoɔ he mu pii bedi akyire, na akyikafoɔ mmom abedi kane.
Bobe turo mu adwumayɔfoɔ “Na soro ahennie he te sɛ afuowura bi a ɔkɔɔ abɔntene anɔpatutuutu sɛ ɔɔkɔpɛ apaafoɔ akɔ ne bobe turo mu.
Ɔne bɛ dii ano maa osii sɛ obetua paani da korɔ akatua ama he, ɔmaa bɛkɔɔ ne bobe turo mu.
Berɛ a ofirii abɔntene bɛyɛ nnɔn nkron he, ohuu apaafoɔ foforɔ dwaso sɛ begyina hɔ a bɛnnyɔ hwee.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, ‘Ho nso ho nkɔ bobe turo mu hɔ, na metua ho ka sɛdeɛ ɔsɛ.’ Nti bɛkɔeɛ.
Berɛ a ɔkɔɔ abɔntene bio bɛyɛ awigyina ne bɛyɛ nnɔn mmeɛnsa he, ɔyɔɔ saa.
Na ɔbɔɔ bɛyɛ nnɔn num he ɔkɔɔ abɔntene kohuu sɛ binom gyinagyina hɔ; na obisaa bɛ sɛ, ‘Mmɛ nti ne hogyina hɔ kwa da mu nyinaa?’ Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Nipa biaa mmɔ yɛ paa nti a.’ Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, ‘Ho nso honkɔ bobe turo mu hɔ.’ Nnwunu dwoeɛ he, bobe turo wura he ka kyerɛɛ ne hwɛsoni sɛ, ‘Frɛ apaafoɔ he na tua bɛ ka, firi deɛ otwa toɔ so kosi deɛ odi kane so.’ Ɔfrɛɛ apaafoɔ a ɔfaa bɛ nnɔn num he baeɛ, na ɔmaa bɛ mu biaa sɛnea paani dakorɔ akatua teɛ.
Afei bɛ a bedii kane baeɛ he, na benim sɛ bebenya bebree; nso bɛ mu biaa nyaa sɛnea paani dakorɔ akatua teɛ.
Na bɛ nsa kaeɛ he, benwinwini tiaa bobe turo wura he, kaa sɛ, ‘Yeinom a bɛbaa akyire yi yɔɔ adwuma dɔnhwere baako pɛ, nso woama yɛ a yɛayɔ adwuma da mũ nyinaa ama awia ahye yɛ ne bɛ nyinaa pɛ.’ Nso obuaa bɛ mu baako sɛ, ‘Damfo, wotee me aseɛ sɛ wobɛgye dakorɔ akatua; nti menyɔɔ wo bɔne biaa.
Fa wo akatua kɔ; ɔyɛ mepɛ sɛ mɛma bɛ a bɛbaa akyire yi sɛ wo.
Menni ho kwane sɛ mede m’agyapadeɛ yɔ deɛ meaa me pɛ?
Anaa m’ayamyɛ nti na w’ani abere yi?
Saa ne akyidifoɔ bedi kane, na adikanfoɔ mmom abedi akyire.” Yesu wuo ne ne wusɔreɛ ho nkɔmhyɛ a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa Berɛ a bɛɛkɔ Yerusalem he, Yesu frɛɛ asuafoɔ dummienu he gyinaa nkyɛne, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ kwane so sɛ, “Hwɛ, yɛɛkɔ Yerusalem, na bɛde Nipa Ba he bɛhyɛ asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he nsa, na bebebua no kumfɔ; na bɛde no ahyɛ Amanamane mufoɔ nsa ama bɛadi ne ho fɛw na bɛabɔ no mmaa, na bɛabɔ no asennuam, na da a ɔto so mmeɛnsa he Nyankopɔn anyane no afiri awufoɔ mu.” Ɔsɛ dikanfoɔ sɛ ɔyɛ somfoɔ Afei Sebedeo mma he ne bɛ maame baa Yesu hɔ.
Na bɛ maame he buu nkotodwe Yesu anim, na ɔsrɛɛ ne hɔ bibi.
Na obisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ ne woopɛ?” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Hyɛ sɛ w’ahennie mu hɔ me mma mmienu yi bɛtena wo nifa ne wo benkum so.” Nso Yesu buaa sɛ, “Wonnim deɛ woobisa he.
Hobetumi anom kuruwaa a mɛnom he bi?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Yebetumi.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Kuruwaa a mɛnom he deɛ ho nso hobɛnom, nso sɛ hobɛtena me nsa nifa ne benkum so deɛ, ɔnnyɛ me ne mede bɛma, na mmom, ɔya hɔ ma bɛ a m’ Agya asiesie de ama bɛ.” Berɛ a asuafoɔ du he tee yei he, bɛ bo fuu anuanom mmienu yi paa.
Nso Yesu frɛɛ bɛ baa ne nkyɛne kaa sɛ, “Honim sɛ wiase Amanamane sodifoɔ hyɛ bɛ nkurofoɔ so, na bɛ mu akɛsefoɔ he di bɛ so tumi.
Ɔnsɛ sɛ ho deɛ hoyɔ saa; na deɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔyɛ kɛseɛ ho mu he ɔsɛ sɛ ɔyɛ ho mu somfoɔ, na deɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔyɛ ho mu dikanfoɔ he, ɔsɛ sɛ ɔyɛ akoa ho mu; sɛdeɛ Nipa Ba he nso amma sɛ bɛnsom no na mmom ɔbɛsomeɛ na ɔde ne nkwa ayɛ agyedeɛ ama nipa bebree he.” Yesu saa mmeema anifirafoɔ mmienu bi yadeɛ Beefiri Yeriko he, nipadɔm pii tu dii n’akyi.
Na mmeema anifirafoɔ mmienu bi tete kwane nkyɛne.
Berɛ a bɛtee sɛ Yesu ootwam he, bɛteaam sɛ, “Awurade hu yɛ mmɔbɔ, Dawid Ba!” Nnipadɔm he hyɛɛ bɛ ketee sɛ bɛnyɔ komm; nso bɛteateam kɛse paa sɛ, “Hu yɛ mmɔbɔ, Awurade, Dawid Ba!” Yesu gyinaa hɔ dinn, na ɔfrɛɛ bɛ, bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne hopɛ sɛ menyɔ ma ho?” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade, ma yenhu adeɛ.” Yesu huu bɛ mmɔbɔ, na ɔde ne nsa kaa bɛ ani.
Amonom hɔaa behuu adeɛ bio na bedii n’akyi.
Yesu hyɛnee Yerusalem nkunimdie mu Berɛ a bɛbɛnee Yerusalem, na beduruu Betfage, Ngo Bepɔ so he, Yesu somaa asuafoɔ mmienu, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔ akuraa a ɔda ho anim yi mu, na hoduru hɔaa pɛ hobehu afunumu a bɛamantam no a ne ba ka ne ho; honsane bɛ na homfa bɛ mmra me.
Sɛ bi bisa ho asɛm a, ho deɛ honka sɛ, ‘Bɛ ho hia ma Awurade.’ Na ntɛmaa ɔbɛma ho de bɛ aba.” Yei nyinaa siiɛ maa deɛ diyifoɔ he kaeɛ he baam, sɛ, “Honka nkyerɛ Sion babaa, Hwɛ, wo hene ɔɔba wo nkyɛne, ɔdwo, na ɔte afunumu so, afunumu ba a ɔsoa nnoɔma so.” Na asuafoɔ he kɔ kɔyɔɔ sɛdeɛ Yesu kyerɛeɛ he; na bɛde afunumu he ne ne ba he baeɛ, na bɛde bɛ ntoma guguu bɛ so, na Yesu tenaa so.
Nnipadɔm he mu pii de bɛ ntoma sesɛɛ kwane mu, na afoforɔ so twaa nnua mmane sesɛɛ kwane he mu.
Na nnipadɔm a bedi n’anim ne bɛ a bedi n’akyi he teateam sɛ, “Hosiana, Dawid ba!
Nhyira ne deɛ ɔnam Awurade dini mu ɔɔba!
Hosiana ya sorosoro!” Berɛ a oduruu Yerusalem he, kuro mũ he nyinaa bɔɔ twi, bisaa sɛ, “Hwane di?” Nnipadɔm he kaa sɛ, “Yei ne Yesu, diyifoɔ a ofiri Nasaret a ɔya Galilea he.” Yesu siesie asɔredane mu Afei Yesu wuraa asɔredane mu hɔ na ɔpaamoo bɛ a bɛɛtɔno nnoɔma ne bɛ a bɛɛtɔ firii asɔredane he mu, na ɔkekaa sika sesafoɔ apono ne bɛ a bɛɛtɔno mmuburo nkonnwa butuiɛ.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Bɛ bɛfrɛ me fie mpaebɔfie’; nso hoadane no akrɔmfoɔ atenaeɛ.” Anifirafoɔ ne mmubuafoɔ baa ne nkyɛne asɔredane mu hɔ, na ɔsaa bɛ yadeɛ.
Nso berɛ a asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he huu anwanwadeɛ a ɔyɔeɛ he, na bɛtee sɛ mmɔfra ɔɔteam asɔredane mu hɔ sɛ, “Hosiana, Dawid Ba,” he bɛ bofuu paa na bebisaa no sɛ, “Nti wonte deɛ yeinom bɛɛka yi?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Ɛɛ!
honkenkanee no atwerɛ he mu sɛ, ‘Ofiri mmɔfra ne bɛ a betua nofoɔ ano na woasiesie ayeyie ama wo ho’?” Na afei ogyaa bɛ hɔ, firii hɔ kɔɔ Betania, na ɔdaa hɔ anadwo he.
Yesu domee borɔdoma dua bi Na adeɛ kyeeɛ he, berɛ a Yesu sane kɔɔ kurom hɔ he, kɔm dee no.
Ohuu borɔdoma dua bi kwane nkyɛne; na ɔkɔɔ ho sɛ ɔɔkɔ pɛ n’aba he bi, nso wanhu hwee dua he so sɛ ahahane nkoaa.
Na ɔdomee dua he sɛ, “Wonso aba bio da!” Na borɔdoma he wuu amonom hɔaa.
Berɛ a asuafoɔ he huiɛ he, ɔyɛɛ bɛ nwanwa na bɛkaa sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne borɔdoma dua he wuu amonom hɔaa yi?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, sɛ howɔ gyidie na honnye akyinnye a, nka nyɛ deɛ meyɔɔ borɔdoma dua yi nkoaa ne hobɛyɔ, na mmom sɛ hoka kyerɛ bepɔ yi sɛ, ‘Tutu kogu po mu a,’ ɔbɛyɔ hɔ.
Bibiaa a hode gyidie bɛsrɛ mpaebɔ mu he, ho nsa bɛka.” Bebisaa tumi a Yesu de di dwuma Na afei berɛ a Yesu wuraa asɔredane mu hɔ he, asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne mane he mu mpanyimfoɔ baa ne nkyɛne, berɛ a ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ he.
Na bebisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ tumi ne wode yɔ saa nnoɔma yi, na hwane ne maa wo saa tumi yi?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Me nso mebisa ho asɛm baako; sɛ homa me mmuaeɛ a, hedeɛ me nso mɛkyerɛ ho tumi a mede yɔ saa adwuma yi.
Na Yohane asubɔ he firi soro, anaa ofiri nnipa?” Na besusuu ho sɛ, “Sɛ yɛka sɛ, ‘Ofiri soro’ a, obebisa yɛ sɛ, ‘Mmɛ nti ne hoannye no anni?’ Nso sɛ yɛka sɛ, ‘Ofiri nnipa,’ a yesuro nea nnipadɔm he bɛyɔ; efiri sɛ bɛ nyinaa bebu Yohane sɛ diyifoɔ.” Saa nti bebuaa Yesu sɛ, “Yennim.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Saa ara ne me nso mennka tumi korɔ a mede yɔ yeinom nkyerɛ ho.” Setie ne asoɔdene ho asɛm Yesu bisaa sɛ, “Hodwene yei ho sɛ?
Beema bi wɔ mma mmienu; ɔkɔɔ deɛ odi kane he hɔ, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Me ba, kɔ na kɔyɔ bobe turo he mu adwuma nnɛ.’ Na obuaa no sɛ, ‘Mennkɔ’; nso akyire he ɔsesaa n’adwene na ɔkɔeɛ.
Papa he kɔɔ deɛ ɔtɔ so mmienu he hɔ kɔkaa asɛm korɔ heaa kyerɛɛ no; na ne ba he buaa sɛ, ‘Owura mɛkɔ’; nso woankɔ.
Hohwɛ a bɛ mmienu mu hwane ne yɔɔ ne papa he apɛdeɛ?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Deɛ odi kane he a.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, togyefoɔ ne adwamammɔfoɔ oodi ho anim kane Nyankopɔn ahennie mu, efiri sɛ Yohane baa ho nkyɛne tenenee kwane so, nso hoanye no anni, na togyefoɔ ne nwamanmɔfoɔ gyee no diiɛ; mpo akyire yi a hohuiɛ yɛ nso, hoannsesa ho adwene anye no anni.
Nhwɛsofoɔ bɔne he Afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hontie mfantoho foforɔ yi, afuowura bi yɔɔ bobe turo, too bane faa ho, tuu mu nsa-kyi-amena, na osii abane tentene.
Na ɔde hyɛɛ nhwɛsofoɔ nsa firii hɔ kɔɔ mane foforɔ so.
Berɛ a twaberɛ duruiɛ he, ɔsomaa ne nkoa kɔɔ nhwɛsofoɔ he hɔ sɛ bɛnkɔgye n’afudeɛ mmra no.
Nso nhwɛsofoɔ he kyee ne nkoa he, hwee baako, kuu foforɔ, na besii foforɔ nso aboɔ.
Na ɔsane somaa nkoa foforɔ a bɛ dɔɔso kyɛne kane deɛ he; na bɛde bɛfaa saa kwane heaa so.
Afei nea Afuowura he yɔ twaa toɔ ne sɛ, ɔsomaa ne ba nhwɛsofoɔ he hɔ, susuu sɛ, ‘Bɛbɛfɛre me ba yi.’ Nso berɛ a nhwɛsofoɔ he huu ne ba he, bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, ‘Yei ne nea obedi adeɛ he; homma yenku no na yɛmfa n’agyapadeɛ he.’ Nti bɛkyee no, twee no firii bobeturo he mu, na bekuu no.
Nti sɛ afuowura he ba a, mmɛ ne ɔde bɛyɔ saa nhwɛsofoɔ yi?” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ɔbɛsɛe saa nnipa bɔnefoɔ he pasaa, na ɔde bobe turo he ama nhwɛsofoɔ foforɔ a bɛde afudeɛ bɛbra no twaberɛ.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkenkanee no twerɛ nsɛm he mu pɛn sɛ: ‘Boɔ a abantofoɔ apo he; abɛyɛ tweaso tiboɔ titire; yei yɛ deɛ Awurade ayɔ, na ɔyɛ yɛ ani so nwanwa’ anaa?
Nti meeka akyerɛ ho, bɛbɛgye Nyankopɔn ahennie he afiri ho nsam na bɛde ama bɛ a bɛsõ ahennie he ho aba.” [Deɛ ɔbɛhwe saa boɔ yi so he mu bɛpaepae; na nea boɔ he bɛhwe ne so biaa nso ɔbɛyam no muhumuhu.]
Berɛ a asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he tee ne mfantoho he, behuu sɛ bɛ ho asɛm ne ɔɔka.
Na bɛpɛ sɛ bɛkye no, nso na besuro nnipadɔm he, efiri sɛ na nnipadɔm he gye no tom sɛ diyifoɔ.
Yesu de soro ahennie totoo ayefohyia ho Bio, Yesu de mfantoho bi kyerɛkyerɛ bɛ sɛ: “Soro ahennie he te sɛ hene bi a otoo ayefohyia pono maa ne ba.
Ɔsomaa ne nkoa sɛ bɛnkɔfrɛ bɛ a bɛtoo nsa frɛɛ bɛ ayefohyia he ase nyinaa, nso bɛampɛ sɛ bɛba.
Nti ɔsane somaa nkoa foforɔ, kaa sɛ, ‘Honka nkyerɛ bɛ a bɛato nsa afrɛ bɛ he sɛ: Hwɛ masiesie me nnuane, maaku m’anantwie ne mmoa a bɛadɔre sradeɛ, mawie nnoɔma nyinaa; hommra ayefohyia apontoɔ he ase.’ Nso bɛamfa n’asɛm he annyɛ hwee na bɛkɔɔ bɛ baabi, baako kɔɔ n’afuom, bi nso kɔɔ n’adwuma, binom nso kyee nkoa he, bɔɔ bɛ adapaa kukuu bɛ.
Na hene he bo fuiɛ.
Ɔsomaa ne dɔm maa bɛkɔsɛe saa wudifoɔ he hyee bɛ kuro.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ ne nkoa he sɛ, ‘Bɛasiesie ayefohyia apontoɔ he awie, nso bɛ a bɛtoo nsa frɛ bɛ he, amfata bɛ.
Nti honkɔ mmɔntene so, na homfrɛ biaa a hobehu no ma no mmra ayefohyia apontoɔ he ase.’ Nti nkoa he te sii mmɔntene so na bɛboaboa bɛ a behuu bɛ nyinaa ano, nnipa pa ne nnipa bɔne; yei maa ahɔhoɔ bɛhyɛɛ ayefohyia apontoɔ dane he ma.
“Nso berɛ a hene he behuu ahɔhoɔ he, ohuu beema bi a na ɔnhyɛ ayefohyia ataadeɛ he bi, na obisaa no sɛ, ‘Damfo, ɔyɛɛ dɛ na wonhyɛ ayefohyia ataadeɛ he bi, na nso wotumi bewuraa mu yi?’ Na akoa he tɔree mmum.
Na hene he ka kyerɛɛ asomfoɔ he sɛ, ‘Honkyekyere ne nsa ne ne nane, na honto no ntwene akyirikyiri sum kabii he mu, hɔ ne suu ne setwerɛ ya.’ Na bɛafrɛ bebree nso kakraa bi na bɛayi bɛ.” Toɔtua ho asɛmmisa Na afei Farisifoɔ he kotuu agyina sɛ bebesum Yesu fidie asɛm a ɔbɛka ho.
Nti bɛsomaa bɛ asuafoɔ ne Herodefoɔ kɔɔ ne nkyɛne, kaa sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, yenim sɛ woyɛ nɔkwafoɔ, wonam nɔkorɛ so kyerɛkyerɛ Nyankopɔn kwane, na wonsuro nipa biaa, saa nso ne wonhwɛ nnipa anim.
Kyerɛ yɛ nea wodwene fa yei ho.
Ɔsɛ sɛ yetua toɔ ma Kaesare, anaa sɛ ɔnsɛ yetua ma no?” Nso ɔnam sɛ na Yesu nim bɛ adwemmɔne nti, ɔkaa sɛ, “Ho nyaatwomfoɔ, mmɛ nti ne hoosɔ me ahwɛ?
Homfa dwetɛ deɛ yɛde tua toɔ he bi nkyerɛ me.” Na bɛde denare braa no.
Na afei obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Hwane ti ne ne abodini ne bɛakurukyire agu sika yi so yi?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Kaesare dea.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Saa deɛ a, homfa deɛ ɔyɛ Kaesare deɛ mma Kaesare, na homfa deɛ ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn deɛ mma Nyankopɔn.” Berɛ a bɛteeɛ he, bɛ ho dwirii bɛ; na begyaa ne hɔ kɔeɛ.
Wusɔreɛ ho asɛmmisa Saa da heaa Sadukifoɔ a bɛ gyidie ne sɛ wusɔreɛ biaa nni hɔ he mu bi baa Yesu nkyɛne; na bebisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, Mose kaa sɛ, ‘Sɛ beema bi ware na wanwo ba na owu a, ne nua nware kunafoɔ he, na wawo mma ama ne nua a waawu he.’ Na yɛ ne anuanom nson ne ya ha; nea odi kane he wareeɛ, na owuiɛ a wannya ba, yei maa ne nua waree kunafoɔ he.
Deɛ ɔtɔ so mmienu he nso wuiɛ a wannya ba.
Asɛm korɔ heaa too nea ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa ne bɛ a bɛaka he nyinaa kosii nea ɔtɔ so nson he so.
Na bɛ nyinaa bɛ akyi he, kunafoɔ he ankasa nso wuiɛ.
Sɛ ɔkɔ ba saa a wusɔreɛ he mu he, nnipa nson he mu mmɛneɛ ne baa he bɛyɛ ne yerɛ berɛ a bɛ nyinaa bɛaware no da he?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Nea hooka yi, te ne honte aseɛ yie, efiri sɛ honnim atwerɛeɛ he anaa Nyankopɔn tumi.
Na wusɔreɛ akyi he mmeema nware, na bɛmfa mma nso mma awareɛ, sɛnea abɔfoɔ a bɛya soro nware he, saa ara ne bɛ nso bɛnware.
Na awufoɔ sɔreeɛ ho he, honkenkanee deɛ Nyankopɔn ka kyerɛɛ ho sɛ, ‘Meyɛ Abraham Nyankopɔn, Isak Nyankopɔn, ne Yakob Nyankopɔn anaa’?
Ɔnnyɛ awufoɔ Nyankopɔn, na mmom ɔyɛ ateasefoɔ Nyankopɔn.” Na berɛ a nnipadɔm he tee saa he, ne nkyerɛkyerɛ he yɛɛ bɛ ahodwiri.
