Dɔ ne mmara he mu kɛseɛ paa Afei berɛ a Farisifoɔ he tee sɛ Yesu aka Sadukifoɔ he ano atum he, behyia faako.
Na bɛ mu baako a ɔyɛ mmaranimfoɔ paa de asemmisa sɔɔ no hwɛɛ sɛ “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, mmaransɛm he mu nea ɔya he ne yɛ kɛseɛ paa?” Obuaa no sɛ “Fa w’akoma nyinaa, wo kra nyinaa, ne w’adwene nyinaa dɔ Awurade wo Nyankopɔn.
Yei ne mmaransɛm he mu kɛseɛ paa ne deɛ odi kane.
Na deɛ ɔtɔ so mmienu a ɔte sɛ ɔno ne sɛ: ‘Dɔ wo yɔnko sɛ wo ho.’ Saa mmaransɛm mmienu yi so ne mmara ne adiyifoɔ he nyinaa gyina.” Dawid ba ho asɛmmisa Afei berɛ a Farisifoɔ he hyiaeɛ he, Yesu bisaa bɛ asɛm yi sɛ: “Ɛɛne ne hodwene fa Kristo he ho?
Ɔyɛ hwane ba?” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ɔyɛ Dawid ba.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Saa deɛ a mmɛ nti ne Dawid nam Honhom he so frɛ no Awurade, berɛ a ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Awurade ka kyerɛɛ m’Awurade sɛ, “Tena me nsa nifa so, kosi sɛ mede w’atamfoɔ bɛhyɛ wo nane ase” ’?
Sɛ Dawid frɛ no Awurade a, ɔyɛɛ dɛ na ɔyɛ ne ba?” Biaa antumi ammua no asɛm biaa, na ofiri saa da he biaa ammisa no asɛm biaa bio.
Kɔkɔbɔ a Yesu bɔ faa Atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ nkyerɛkyerɛ ho Afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ nnipadɔm he ne n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he atena Mose akonnwa so; Ne saa nti honyɔ deɛ bɛbɛkyerɛkyerɛ ho biaa na honni so.
Bɛkyekyere nnesoa duruduru a ne soa ɔdene, na bɛde ato afoforɔ mmati so; nso bɛ ankasa deɛ bɛmpɛ sɛ bɛde bɛ nsa teaa mpo ka nnesoa he.
Na bɛyɔ bɛ nnwuma nyinaa sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a nipa behu bɛ.
Na bɛyɔ bɛ nkaeɛ nwoma atɛtrɛtɛ, na bɛyɔ bɛ ntaadeɛ ano nso akɛseɛ.
Bɛpɛ tenabea a anidie ya mu ya apontoɔ ase, ɔne hyiadane mu nkonnwa pa, ne dwa so nkyea a anidie yam, ɔne sɛ nipa bɛfrɛ bɛ Rabi!
Nso ɔnsɛ sɛ bɛfrɛ ho Rabi, efiri sɛ ho kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ yɛ baako, na ho nyinaa hoyɛ asuafoɔ.
Na hommfrɛ biaa ho Agya asaase so, efiri sɛ, howɔ Agya baako, deɛ ɔya soro he.
Afei homma bɛmmfrɛ ho akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ nso, efiri sɛ, howɔ kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ baako, ɔno ne Kristo he.
Deɛ ɔyɛ kɛseɛ paa ho mu he bɛyɛ ho somfoɔ.
Biaa a ɔma ne ho so he bɛbrɛ no ase, na biaa a ɔbrɛ ne ho ase he bɛbɛma no so.
“Nso ho, atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ, nyaatwomfoɔ, honnue!
Efiri sɛ, hosi nipa kwane soro ahennie mu nipa anim, ho ankasa nso honkɔ mu, na sɛ binom ɔɔkɔ mu a, hosi bɛ kwane.
[Ho atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ, nyaatwomfoɔ honnue!
Hofa akunafoɔ nnoɔma na sɛdeɛ bebehu ho nti hobɔ mpaeɛ atentene; nti hobenya afobuo a mu oduru.]
Ho, atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ, nyaatwomfoɔ, honnue!
Efiri sɛ, hotware po ne asaase kɔ sɛ hokɔsakra nipa baako, na homa saa nipa he bɛyɛ ho fekuoni; na sɛ ɔyɛ a, homma ɔbɛfata brosamgyam amanehunu mprenu sɛ ho ankasa.
“Akwankyerɛfoɔ anifirafoɔ, honnue!
Ho a hoka sɛ, ‘Sɛ bi de hyiadane ka ntam a, ntam he nyɛ hwee, na mmom sɛ bi de hyiadane mu hɔ sikakɔkɔɔ ka ntam a ntam he kyekyere no.’ Ho anifirafoɔ ne nkwaseafoɔ!
Deɛ ɔya he ne sombo, sikakɔkɔɔ he anaa hyiadane he a woama sikakɔkɔɔ he ho ate he?
Na hoka sɛ, ‘Deɛ ɔde afɔrebokyia ka ntam he, hwee nkyekyere no, nso biaa a ɔde akyɛdeɛ a ɔda afɔrebokyia he so ka ntam he, ntam he kyekyere no.’ Ho ani afira paa!
Na deɛ ɔya he ne sombo, akyɛdeɛ he anaa afɔrebokyia a ɔma akyɛdeɛ he ho te he?
Nti biaa a ɔde afɔrebokyia ka ntam he ka ɔne deɛ ɔya so nyinaa ntam; na biaa a ɔde hyiadane he ka ntam he, ɔde ɔne deɛ ɔte mu he ne ka ntam; na biaa a ɔde soro ka ntam he, ka Nyankopɔn adwa ne deɛ ɔte so he ntam.
“Honnue, atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ, nyaatwomfoɔ!
Efiri sɛ, hoyi mmee ne nunum ne kumin mma ho ntotosoɔ du du, na hobu ho ani gu mmara he mu nnoɔma deɛ ohia kyɛne yeinom he so: atɛntenenee ne mmɔborɔhunu ne gyidie.
Yeinom a ohia kɛseɛ he ne nka ɔsɛ sɛ hoyɔ berɛ a hommu ho ani ngu deɛ aka he nso so.
Ho, akwankyerɛfoɔ anifirafoɔ!
Hosɔne anonneɛ so yi nwansena to twene nso homene yoma!
“Atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ, nyaatwomfoɔ honnue!
Efiri sɛ, hohohoro kuruwaa ne ayowa ho, nso mu deɛ, adufudepɛ ne pɛsɛmenkomenya ahyɛ ma.
Ho Farisifoɔ anifirafoɔ!
Honhohoro kuruwaa he mu kane na ho he nso afiri.
“Honnue, atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ, nyaatwomfoɔ!
Efiri sɛ, hote sɛ nna a bɛatwa ho fitafita a ɔyɛ fɛ abɔntene, nso mu deɛ funu nnompe ne fi ahodoɔ ahyɛ no ma.
Saa ne ho nso, afoforɔ hu ho ateneneefoɔ abɔntene, nso nyaatwom ne mmarato ahyɛ ho mu ma.
“Honnue, atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ, nyaatwomfoɔ!
Efiri sɛ, hoyɔ adiyifoɔ bɛ nna na hosiesie ateneneefoɔ adamena, na hoka sɛ, ‘Sɛ na nka yɛya hɔ yɛ nananom berɛ so a, nka yɛ ne bɛ ommom nhwie adiyifoɔ he mogyaa ngu.’ Nti hodi adanseɛ tia ho ho sɛ hoyɛ bɛ a bekuku adiyifoɔ he asefoɔ.
Saa deɛ a honwie deɛ ho agyanom hyɛɛ aseɛ he.
Awɔ, anankatia mma!
Hobɛyɛ dɛ adwane atemmuo a ɔde hobɛkɔ bronsam gya mu he?
Nti meesoma adiyifoɔ, anyansafoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ, na hobeku binom na hobɛtwa binom mmaa ho hyiadane mu na hoataa bɛ afiri kuro so akɔ kuro so, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a mogyaa a odi bem a bɛahwie agu asaase so nyinaa bɛba ho so, ofiri teneneeni Habel so de kosi Barakia ba Sakaria a hokuu no asɔredane ne afɔrebokyia ntam he.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, yei nyinaa bɛba nnɛ mma yi so.
Yerusalem ho kwadwom “Yerusalem, Yerusalem, kuro a oku adiyifoɔ na osi bɛ a bɛasoma bɛ ne nkyɛne aboɔ!
Hwɛ mprɛ dodoɔ a meepɛ sɛ mɛboaboa wo mma ano sɛdeɛ akokɔ baatane boaboa ne mma ano ne ntabane ase, nso hoampɛ!
Hwɛ, obegya wo fie ama no ada mpan.
Na meeka akyerɛ ho, honhu me bio de bɛkɔ akosi sɛ hobɛka sɛ, ‘Nhyira ne deɛ ɔɔba Awurade dini mu he.’ ”
Asɔrefie sɛeɛ ho nkɔmhyɛ Na Yesu firii asɔredane mu a na ɔɔkɔ he, n’asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bɛkyerɛɛ no asɔrefie he mu adane ahodoɔ.
Obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Hoahu yeinom nyinaa anaa?
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, bennya boɔ baako mpo mma ɔnka a benwiri ngu.” Awieeɛ mmerɛ ho nsɛnkyerɛnne Berɛ a ɔte Ngo Bepɔ so he, n’asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bebisaa no kokoam sɛ, “Ka kyerɛ yɛ, da bɛ ne yeinom besi, na mmɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne ne bɛda adi fa wo mmaeɛ ne awieeɛ berɛ he mu?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Honhwɛ yie na bi annaadaa ho.
Efiri sɛ bebree bɛba me dini mu, abɛka sɛ, ‘Me ne Kristo he,’ na bɛbɛdaadaa nnipa bebree.
Na hobɛte ko ne akosɛm; honhwɛ yie na ho akoma antu; efiri sɛ otwa sɛ yeinom nyinaa ba, nso na awieeɛ he nya mmaeɛ.
Na amane bɛsɔre atia amane, na ahennie bɛsɔre atia ahennie, kɔm bɛba na asaase wosoɔ nso bɛba baabi bebree.
Na yeinom nyinaa te sɛ awoko yea mfitiaseɛ.
Taa ho nkɔmhyɛ “Saa mmerɛ he bebeyi ho ama sɛ bɛmfa homfa ahohiahia mu, na bɛaku ho, na me dini nti amane nyinaa bɛtane ho.
Na bebree bɛpa bɛ gyidie, na bebeyiyi bɛ ho bɛ ho ama na bɛatentane bɛ ho bɛ ho.
Na atorɔ adiyifoɔ bebree bɛsɔre abɛdaadaa nnipa bebree.
Na ɔnam sɛ amumuyɔ bɛdɔɔso nti, bebree dɔ ano bɛdwo.
Na nipa a obegyina akosi awieeɛ he deɛ, bɛbɛgye no nkwa.
Na bɛbɛka ahennie yi ho asɛmpa ya amane nyinaa mu, de adi adanseɛ ama amanamane nyinaa; yei akyi ansa na awieeɛ he aba.
Akyiwadeɛ a ɔbɔ mane “Nti sɛ hohu sɛ akyiwadeɛ a ɔbɔ mane he gyina kronkronbea hɔ a, sɛdeɛ diyifoɔ Daniel kaeɛ he a (otwa sɛ deɛ ɔkenkane he te aseɛ), hedeɛ bɛ a bɛya Yudea he nnwane nkɔ bepɔ so; deɛ ɔya dane atifi he nnsiane nkɔfa bibi ne dane mu; deɛ ɔya afuom nsane mma fie mmɛfa ataadeɛ.
Bɛ a bɛafa afuro ne bɛ a bɛma mma nofoɔ nnue saa da he!
Hommɔ mpaeɛ sɛ saa da yi ɔmma awɔ anaa sutɔberɛ anaa homeda.
Saa berɛ he ahokyerɛ kɛseɛ a ofiri wiase mfitiaseɛ besi nnɛ bi mmaa da na bi nso ɔmma bio bɛba.
Sɛ bɛantwa saa nna he so a, biaa nni hɔ a obenya nkwa; nso bɛ a bɛayi bɛ he nti bebetwa nna he so tia.
Na sɛ bi ka kyerɛ ho sɛ, ‘Hwɛ, Kristo he di!’ Anaa ‘Ɔya ha a!’ Honnnye nnni.
Na kristo-atorɔfoɔ ne atorɔ adiyifoɔ bebree bɛba abɛyɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne ne anwanwadeɛ akɛseɛ, de adaadaa binom, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ yie a bɛ a bɛayi bɛ he mpo nka bɛbɛdadaa bɛ.
Honhyɛ no nso sɛ maaka akyerɛ ho dada.
Nti, sɛ bɛka kyerɛ ho sɛ, ‘Hwɛ!
Ɔya serɛ so a,’ honnkɔ.
Sɛ bɛka sɛ, ‘Hwɛ!
Ɔya piem a,’ honnye nnni.
Na sɛdeɛ anyinam pae firi apieɛ kɔ atɔeɛ he, saa ne ɔbɛyɛ Nipa Ba he maeɛ mu.
Baabi a funu ya he hɔ ne mpɛtɛ boa bɛ ano.
Nipa Ba he mmaeɛ “Saa ahohiahia nna he akyi pɛ awia bɛyɛ sum, na bosome ɔnhyerɛn; na nsoromma betutu afiri soro agu, na soro ahoɔdenneɛ bɛwoso.
Na Nipa Ba he ho nsɛnkyerɛnne bɛda adi soro, na asaase so mmusuakuo nyinaa besu, na bebehu ‘Nipa Ba he sɛ ɔde tumi ne animuonyam kɛseɛ nam soro mununkum mu ɔɔba.’ Na ɔbɛsoma n’abɔfoɔ ama bɛde totorobɛnto nyegyeɛ a ano ɔdene aba; na bɛbɛboaboa bɛ a bɛayi bɛ he ano afiri wiase mframa nnan he mu, firi soro ano akosi ano.
Borɔdoma ho adesua “Honsua bibi mfiri borɔdoma ho: Sɛ ne mmane nya yɛ frɔmfrɔm na ooyiyi ahahane a, na honim sɛ ahuhuro berɛ abɛne.
Saa ara nso ne sɛ hohu yeinom nyinaa a, honhu sɛ Kristo mmaeɛ he abɛne, ogyina pono ano.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, awoɔntoatoasoɔ yi ontwam ansa na yeinom abam.
Soro ne asaase betwam, nso me nsɛm deɛ, ontwam da.
Honwɛne “Nso saa da ne dɔnhwere he deɛ biaa nnim, soro abɔfoɔ, anaa Ɔba he mpo nnim, gye sɛ Agya he nkoaa.
Na sɛdeɛ Noa nna he yɛeɛ he, saa ne Nipa Ba he so maeɛ bɛ yɛ.
Saa mmerɛ he, ansa na nsuhyiri he ɔɔba he, nnipa didiiɛ, na bɛnomeeɛ, mmeema wareeɛ na bɛde maa maa awareɛ, kosii sɛ Noa wuraa adaka he mu.
Na bɛanhu hwee kosi sɛ nsuhyiri he baeɛ bɛfaa bɛ nyinaa kɔeɛ.
Na sɛdeɛ ɔyɛeɛ he, saa ne ɔbɛyɛ Nipa Ba he mmaeɛ mu.
Ɔte sɛ nnipa mmienu ya afuom; bɛbɛfa baako na bɛagya baako hɔ.
Saa ara nso ne ɔte sɛ mmaa mmienu ɔɔyam wiyammoɔ so a; bɛbɛfa baako na bɛagya baako hɔ.
Saa nti ho nkɔ so nwɛne, efiri sɛ honnim da korɔ a ho Wura bɛba.
Honte aseɛ: Sɛ nka fiewura nim berɛ pɔtee dasuom a korɔmfoɔ bɛba a, nka ɔbɛnwɛne, na korɔmfoɔ annya kwane ammebu ne dane anwura mu.
Nti ho nso honna ho ho so, efiri sɛ dɔnhwere a ho ani nna so mu na Nipa Ba he bɛba.
Akoa nɔkwafoɔ ne akoa a onni nɔkorɛ “Afei, hwane ne akoa nɔkwafoɔ ne nyansafoɔ a, ne wura de no asi ne fie so, sɛ ɔma nkoa a bɛhyɛ n’ase aduane ne berɛ mu?
Nhyira ne akoa a ne wura bɛba abehu no sɛ ɔɔyɔ saa.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, ɔbɛma saa akoa he adi n’agyapadeɛ nyinaa so.
Nso sɛ akoa timɔdenfoɔ he ka no ne tim sɛ, ‘Me wura akyɛre,’ na ofiri aseɛ boro nkoa a bɛhyɛ n’ase na ɔne nsaborofoɔ didi na bɛnom nsa a, ne wura he bɛba da korɔ a n’ani nna so ne dɔnhwere a onnim mu.
Obetwitwa ne mu na ɔde no aka nyaatwomfoɔ ho ya baabi a suu ne setwerɛ ya.
Yesu de soro ahennie he totoo Mmabaa bi ho Yesu kaa sɛ, “Afei nso soro ahennie he bɛyɛ sɛ mmabaa du bi a bɛfaa bɛ nkanea sɛ beekohyia ayefokunu.
Na bɛ mu nnum yɛ mmadwemma, na nnum nso nyɛ mmadwemma.
Berɛ a bɛ a bɛnyɛ mmadwemma he faa bɛ nkanea he bɛamfa ngo anka ho; nso mmadwemma he deɛ bɛfaa ngo kaa bɛ nkanea he ho.
Ɔkyɛreɛ a ayefokunu he mmaeɛ he, bɛ nyinaa bɛ ani kumiiɛ na bɛdedaeɛ.
Nso anadwo dasuom bɛtee nteamu, ‘Hwɛ, ayefokunu he di!
Hommra mmehyia no.’ Nti mmabaa he nyinaa sɔre sosɔɔ bɛ nkanea he.
Bɛ a bɛnyɛ mmadwemma he ka kyerɛɛ mmadwemma he sɛ, ‘Homma yɛ ho ngo yi bi, na yɛ nkanea he oodumdum.’ Nso mmadwemma he buaa bɛ sɛ, ‘Daabi, ɔnso yɛ ne ho; honkɔ adetɔnfoɔ hɔ nkɔtɔ bi.’ Na bɛkɔɔ sɛ bɛɛkɔtɔ bi he, ayefokunu he baeɛ, na bɛ a bɛasiesie bɛ ho he ne no kɔɔ ayefohyia he ase; na bɛtoo pono he mu.
Yei akyi he, mmabaa a bɛnyɛ mmadwemma he nso baeɛ, na bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Owura, owura, bie yɛ.’ Nso obuaa sɛ, ‘Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, mennim ho.’ Saa nti honwɛne, efiri sɛ honnim da anaa dɔnhwere korɔ he a (Nipa Ba he bɛba.)
Akontabuo ho mfantoho “Na ɔte sɛ beema bi a ootu kwane, na ɔfrɛɛ ne nkoa na ɔde n’agyapadeɛ hyɛɛ bɛ nsa; ɔmaa baako sika dwetire mmɔho nnum, na foforɔ so mmɔho mmienu na foforɔ so baako, sɛdeɛ biaa ahoɔdene teɛ.
Na ɔkɔɔ ne kwane.
Deɛ onyaa sika dwetire nnum he ntɛmaa ɔde kodii dwa, na ɔnyaa sika dwetire mmɔho nnum kaa ho.
Saa ne deɛ onyaa mmienu he nso nyaa mmienu kaa ho.
Nso deɛ onyaa baako he kɔ kotutuu fam na ɔde ne wura sika he siee hɔ.
Mmerɛ tentene bi akyi he, nkoa he wura he baeɛ na ɔne bɛ bebuu akonta.
Na deɛ onyaa sika dwetire mmɔho nnum he baa anim, de sika dwetire mmɔho nnum foforɔ baeɛ, ɔkaa sɛ ‘Owura, womaa me sika dwetire mmɔho nnum; hwɛ mede nnum abɛka ho.’ Ne wura he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Mo ne yɔ, akoa pa ne nɔkwafoɔ; woadi kakra yi ho nɔkorɛ, mede nnoɔma bebree bɛhyɛ wo nsa; nya wo wura anigye he bi.’ Na nea ɔnyaa sika dwetire mmɔho mmienu he so baeɛ, bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Owura, womaa me sika dwetire mmɔho mmienu; hwɛ manya mmɔho mmienu aka ho.’ Ne wura he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Mo ne yɔ, akoa pa nɔkwafoɔ; woadi kakra yi ho nɔkorɛ, mede nnoɔma bebree bɛhyɛ wo nsa; nya wo wura anigye he bi.’ Afei deɛ onyaa sika dwetire baako he nso baeɛ, bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Owura, menim sɛ woyɛ bi a wo asɛm ɔdene, wotwa aba firi baabi a wonnuaeɛ, na woboaboa ano baabi wonto aba mpeteeɛ; nti mesuroeɛ, na mede wo sika he kosiee fam.
W’adeɛ di, gye.’ Nso ne wura he buaa sɛ, ‘Wo akoa bɔne ne anihafoɔ!
Wonnim sɛ metwa baabi a mennguiɛ, na meboaboa ano baabi a memmfa mmpeteɛ?
Saa deɛ a nka ɔsɛ sɛ wode me sika he kɔto sika korabea, na mesane ba a, manya me sika he ne ho ba.
Afei honye mfiri ne nsam, homfa mma nea ɔnyaa dwetire du he.
Na bɛ a bɛanya bi aka nea bɛde ama bɛ ho he, bɛde bebree bɛka bɛ ho, na bɛanya ama no abu so; na bɛ a bɛanya hwee anka nea bɛde ama bɛ ho he deɛ, kakra a bɛwɔ he mpo, bɛbɛgye afiri bɛ nsam.
Akoa a ne so nni mfasoɔ yi deɛ, homfa ne nto sum kabii mu, baabi a suu ne setwerɛ ya.’ Atemmuda kɛseɛ he “Sɛ Nipa Ba he ba n’animuonyam mu a, na abɔfoɔ nyinaa ka ne ho a, ɔbɛtena n’animuonyam adwa so.
Amane nyinaa bɛboaboa bɛ ano n’anim, na ɔbɛpaepae nnipa mu sɛ dwanhwɛfoɔ paepae nnwane firi mmirekyie mu, na ɔde nnwane he begyina ne nsa nifa so na mmirekyie he nso ɔde bɛ agyina ne nsa benkum so.
Na hene he bɛka akyerɛ bɛ a bɛya ne nifa so he sɛ, ‘Hommra, ho a m’Agya ahyira ho, hommɛfa ahennie a bɛasiesie ama ho firi wiase mfitiaseɛ he nni; efiri sɛ kɔm dee me na homaa me aduane diiɛ, nsukɔm dee me na homaa me nsuo nomeeɛ, meyɛɛ hɔhoɔ na hode me kɔɔ fie, medaa adagya na hofiraa me ntoma, meyareeɛ, na hohwɛɛ me, mekɔdaa afiase na hobɛsraa me.’ Na teneneefoɔ he bebua sɛ, ‘Awurade, da bɛ ne yehuu sɛ kɔm de wo na yɛmaa wo aduane diiɛ, anaa nsukɔm de wo na yɛmaa wo nsuo nomeeɛ?
Na da bɛ ne yehuu sɛ woyɛ hɔhoɔ na yɛfaa wo kɔɔ fie, anaa woda adagya na yefiraa wo ntoma?
Na da bɛ ne yehuu sɛ woyare anaa woda afiase na yɛbaa wo nkyɛne?’ Na hene bebua bɛ sɛ, ‘Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, sɛ hoyɔ maa me nuanom nkumaa yi mu baako he, hoayɔ ama me nso.’ Na ɔbɛka akyerɛ bɛ a bɛya ne nsa benkum so he sɛ, ‘Ho a bɛadome ho, homfiri me so nkɔ daa gya a bɛasiesie ama Bronsam ne n’abɔfoɔ he mu; efiri sɛ kɔm dee me nso hoamma me aduane, nsukɔm dee me, nso hoamma me hwee annom, meyɛɛ hɔhoɔ nso hoamfa me ankɔ fie, medaa adagya nso hoamfira me ntoma, meyareeɛ na mekɔdaa afiase nso hoammɛsra me.’ Hɔ ne bɛ so bɛbɛka sɛ, ‘Awurade, da bɛ na yehuu sɛ kɔm de wo anaa sukɔm de wo, anaa woyɛɛ hɔhoɔ anaa wodaa adagya anaa woyareɛ anaa wokɔdaa afiase, na yɛannyɔ wo yie?’ Na obebua bɛ sɛ, ‘Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, sɛdeɛ hoannyɔ amma nkumaa yi mu baako he, saa ne hoannyɔ amma me nso.’ Na yeinom befiri hɔ akɔ daa asotwe mu, na ateneneefoɔ he bɛkɔ daa nkwa mu.”
Bɛbɔɔ pɔ faa Yesu ku ho Na Yesu kaa yeinom nyinaa wieeɛ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Honim sɛ, aaka nnanu na Twam afahyɛ he aduru, na bebeyi Nipa Ba he ama, na bɛabɔ no asennua mu.” Afei asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne nnipa he so mpanyimfoɔ he hyiaam sɔfo panyini a bɛfrɛ no Kaiafa fie hɔ, na bɛbɔɔ pɔ sɛ bɛbɛfa nyansa kwane so akye Yesu aku no.
Nso bɛkaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ afahyɛ berɛ he mu ne ɔsɛ sɛ bɛyɔ saa, anyɛ saa basabasa bɛba mane he mu.” Bɛsraa Yesu ngo ya Betania Na berɛ a Yesu ya Betania, Simon kwatani he fie he, baa bi de toa bi a aduhwam bi a ne boɔ ɔdene gu mu baa hɔ, na ohwie guu Yesu ti mu, berɛ a ɔte adidiiɛ he.
Nso asuafoɔ he huiɛ he, bɛ bo fuiɛ, na bɛkaa sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne woasɛe aduhwam yi sei?
Nka bebetumi atɔno agye sika kɛseɛ, na bɛde sika he ama ahiafoɔ.” Na Yesu huu yɛ he, obisaa sɛ, “Ɛɛne nti ne hooha baa he?
Waayɔ adwuma pa ama me.
Na howɔ ahiafoɔ ya ho nkyɛne daa, na me deɛ hoonya me daa.
Aduhwam a ohwie guu me so he, ɔde asiesie me ama me sie.
Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem, wiase baabi a bɛ bɛpae mu aka asɛmpa yi, bɛbɛka deɛ baa yi ayɔ yi de akae no.” Yuda Iskariot gye tomm sɛ obeyi Yesu ama Na dummienu he mu baako a bɛfrɛ no Yuda Iskariot kɔɔ asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he hɔ na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ meyi no ma ho a, mmɛ ne hode bɛma me?” Betuaa dwetɛbena aduasa maa no.
Na ofiri saa berɛ he, ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ hwehwɛɛ akwannya bi a ɔde beyi Yesu ama.
Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he dii Twam Afahyɛ he Da a odi twam, kyerɛ sɛ afahyɛ a bedi Paanoo a Mmɔreka nni mu, kane he, asuafoɔ he baa Yesu nkyɛne bebisaa sɛ, “Hefa ne wopɛ sɛ yesiesie ma wodi Twam aduane he?” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Hokɔ kuro he mu a, hobehu beema bi, honka nkyerɛ no sɛ, ‘Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he dɛ, Me berɛ abɛne; na me ne m’asuafoɔ he bedi twam aduane he wo fie.’ ” Nti asuafoɔ he yɔɔ deɛ Yesu kaeɛ he, na besiesie Twam aduane he.
Awurade adidie Afei nwunu dwoeɛ he, ɔne n’asuafoɔ dummienu he tenaa ase; na beedidi he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorɛ mu sɛ, ho mu baako beyi me ama.” Yei maa bɛyɛɛ basaa paa, na bɛhyɛɛ aseɛ bisaa no sɛ, “Awurade, ɔyɛ me anaa?” Obuaa sɛ, “Deɛ ɔne me to nsa didi ayowa baako mu he ɔno ne beyi me ama.’ Nipa Ba he ɔɔkɔ sɛdeɛ bɛahyɛ ato hɔ ama no deɛ, nso nea ɔnam ne so beyi no ama he nnue!
Sɛ bɛanwo saa nipa he mpo a nka ɔyɛ.” Yuda, deɛ oyi no maeɛ he kaa sɛ, “Rabi, ɔyɛ me anaa?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Ɛɛ, ɔno ne woaka he.” Awurade adidi nhyehyɛeɛ Berɛ a beedidi he, Yesu faa paanoo, ohyiraa so wieeɛ he, obubu de maa asuafoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Honnye, honni; me nipadua di.” Na ɔfaa kuruwaa, na ɔdaa ase wieeɛ he, ɔde maa bɛ kaa sɛ, “Ho nyinaa honnom bi; na yei ne me mogyaa a ɔyɛ apam he mogyaa a, nnipa bebree nti beehwie agu ama bɔne fakyɛ.
Meeka akyerɛ ho, mennom saa bobesa yi bi bio kosi da a me ne ho bɛnom no kwane foforɔ so m’ Agya ahennie mu.” Na bɛtoo ayeyie nnwom wieeɛ he, befiri adi kɔ Ngo Bepɔ he so.
Yesu hyɛɛ pa a Petro bɛpa no he ho nkɔm Afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Anadwo yi, deɛ ɔbɛba me so he bɛto ho nyinaa sintidua; efiri sɛ bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Mɛbɔ dwanhwɛfoɔ he, na nnwane he bɛhwete.’ Na sɛ mesɔre firi awufoɔ mu a, medi ho anim kane akɔ Galilea.” Petro ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛdeɛ ɔbɛba wo so he bɛto biaa sintidua a, me deɛ ɔnto me sintidua koraa.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ wo nɔkorem, anadwo yi, ansa na akokɔ bɛbɔno he, na woapa me mprɛnsa.” Petro ka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ otwa sɛ me ne wo wu mpo a, mempa wo da.” Na saa ne asuafoɔ he nyinaa nso kaeɛ.
Yesu bɔɔ mpaeɛ ya Getsemane Afei Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he kɔɔ bea bi a bɛfrɛ hɔ Getsemane; na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hontena ha, na menkɔ nohoa nkɔbɔ mpaeɛ.” Ɔfaa Petro ne Sebedeo mma mmeema mmienu he kaa ne ho, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ dii awerɛhoɔ na ne ho yera no.
Na ɔka kyerɛ bɛ sɛ, “Awerɛhoɔ ahyɛ me kra so de ɔɔkɔ wuo mu; hontwɛne ha na ho ne me nwɛne.” Na ɔkɔɔ anim kakra he, ɔde n’anim kobutuu fam bɔɔ mpaeɛ sɛ, “M’Agya sɛ obetumi a, ma kuruwaa yi ntwam me ho, nso ɔnyɛ deɛ mepɛ na mmom deɛ wopɛ (ne nyɛ hɔ).” Afei ɔsane baa asuafoɔ he nkyɛne behuu sɛ bɛɛda; na ɔka kyerɛɛ Petro sɛ, “Nti wantumi ne me anwɛne dɔnhwere baako mpo?
Honwɛne na hommɔ mpaeɛ na hoankɔ sɔhwɛ mu; honhom he pɛ deɛ nso honam he ɔmmerɛ.” Na ofirii hɔ kɔɔ ne mprenu so na ɔkɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ sɛ, “M’Agya, sɛ yei ntumi ntwa me ho na otwa sɛ menom a, ma wopɛ nyɛ hɔ.” Bio, ɔba behuu sɛ bɛɛda, efiri sɛ na bɛ ani kum yie.
Nti ogyaa bɛ hɔ bio he, ɔkɔ kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ ne mprɛnsa so na ɔkaa asɛm korɔ heaa.
Na afei ɔbaa asuafoɔ he nkyɛne bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nti hogu so ɔɔda gye ho ahome?
Hwɛ, berɛ he abɛne, sɛ bebeyi Nipa Ba he ahyɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ nsa.
Honsɔre, mma yɛnkɔ.
Hwɛ, deɛ obeyi me ama he abɛne.” Yuda Iskariot de asraafoɔ baa Turom hɔ Na ogu so ɔɔkasa he, Yuda a ɔyɛ dummienu he mu baako beduru hɔ, na nnipadɔm pii ka ne ho a bekitakita asekane ne mmaa a na asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne nnipa he so mpanyimfoɔ na asoma bɛ.
Na deɛ obeyi no ama he maa bɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Deɛ mɛfe n’ano he, ɔno ne nipa a hoohwehwɛ no he, honkye no.” Prɛko pɛ, Yuda baa Yesu nkyɛne bɛkaa sɛ, “Rabi, Mekyea wo,” na ɔfee n’ano.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Damfo, yɔ deɛ wobaa ha sɛ woobɛyɔ he ntɛm.” Na afei bɛba bɛsɔɔ Yesu mu na bɛkyee no.
Amonom hɔaa, bɛ a bɛka Yesu ho he mu baako twee ne sekane twaa sɔfo panyini he akoa aso.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Fa sekane he hyɛ bɔha he mu; na bɛ a bɛtwe sekane he nyinaa bewu sekane ano.
Anaa wodwene sɛ mentumi nsrɛ m’agya, ma ɔnsoma abɔfoɔ bɛboro dɔm dummienu mmra me seeseiaa anaa?
Na nka ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na atwerɛ a ɔka sɛ otwa sɛ ɔba saa he abam?” Afei, Yesu bisaa nnipadɔm he sɛ, “Hode sekane ne mmaa ne ɔɔbɛkye me, te sɛ nea meyɛ korɔmfoɔ?
Da biaa mete asɔredane mu kyerɛkyerɛ he, hoankye me.
Nso yei nyinaa asi, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a adiyifoɔ he atwerɛ he bɛba mu.” Afei asuafoɔ he nyinaa gyaa no hɔ dwaneeɛ.
Bɛde Yesu kogyinaa sɔfo panyini anim Afei bɛ a bɛkyee Yesu he de no kɔmaa Kaiafa, sɔfo panyini a na atwerɛfoɔ he ne mpanyimfoɔ he ahyiam ne fie.
Na Petro dii n’akyi akyirikyiri de koduruu sɔfo panyini he abane mu hɔ, na ɔkɔɔ mu he ɔne asraafoɔ he tenaa ase sɛ ɔɔbɛhwɛ deɛ obesi.
Afei asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne badwa he nyinaa hwehwɛɛ Yesu ho adansekunumu, na bɛagyina so de aku no, nso bɛannya bi, owom sɛ adansekunumufoɔ bebree baeɛ.
Na akyire yi mmienu bi baeɛ na bɛbɛkaa sɛ, “Akoa yei kaa sɛ, ‘Metumi de dakorɔ abubu asɔredane he na mede nnansa asi.’ ” Na sɔfo panyini he sɔre bisaa no sɛ, ‘Wonni anoyie biaa?
Mmɛ adanseɛ ne beedi tia wo yi?” Nso Yesu yɔɔ komm.
Afei sɔfo panyini he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Meka Nyankopɔn teasefoɔ he ntam gu wo so sɛ, sɛ wo ne Kristo, Nyankopɔn Ba he a, ka kyerɛ yɛ!” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Woaa woaka, Na meeka akyerɛ ho, Ofiri nnɛ ɔɔkɔ yi, hobehu Nipa Ba he sɛ ɔte Nyankopɔn Tumfoɔ nifa so na ɔte soro mununkum so ɔɔba asaase so.” Na afei sɔfo panyini he sunsuanee n’ataadeɛ mu kaa sɛ, “Woaka abususɛm!
Ɛɛne nti ne yɛda so hia adansefoɔ?
Afei hoate n’abususɛm he.
Ho adwene ne sɛ?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Ɔfata wuo.” Na bɛtoo ntasuo guu n’anim na bɛbobɔɔ no, na binom bɔɔ n’asum, kaa sɛ, “Kristo, hyɛ yɛ nkɔm!
Hwane ne bɔɔ wo yi?” Petro paa Yesu Berɛ a yeinom ɔɔkɔ so he na Petro te fie he adihɔ.
Abaawa bi baa ne nkyɛne bɛkaa sɛ, “Wo nso na woka Yesu a ofiri Galilea he ho.” Na ɔsanee bɛ nyinaa bɛ anim kaa sɛ, “Mennim deɛ wooka ho asɛm yi.” Petro pie kɔɔ abranaa he so he, abaawa foforɔ huu no, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ a begyina hɔ he sɛ, “Na beema yi ka Nasareni Yesu ho.” Bio, ɔkaa ntam de sanee ne ti sɛ, “Mennim beema he.” Mmerɛ kakra akyi he, bɛ a begyina hɔ he bi baa ne nkyɛne bɛka kyerɛɛ Petro sɛ, “Nɔkwasɛm, wo nso woka bɛ ho, na wo kasaa kyerɛ saa.” Na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ dii nse kaa ntam sɛ, “Mennim beema he!” Saa berɛ he, akokɔ bɔneeɛ.
Na Petro kae Yesu asɛm a ɔkaa sɛ: “Ansa na akokɔ bɛbɔno he na woapa me mprɛnsa.” Na ofirii adi kosuu yayaaya.
Bɛde Yesu baa Pilato anim Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne mane he mu mpanyimfoɔ he nyinaa tuu agyinaa hwehwɛɛ kwane a bɛbɛfa so aku no.
Bɛkyekyere no, na befirii adi de no kɔhyɛɛ Pilato a na ɔyɛ amrado he nsa.
Yuda Iskariot nuu ne ho Berɛ a Yuda a oyii no maeɛ he huu sɛ bɛabua Yesu kumfɔ he, onuu ne ho, na ɔde dwetebena aduasa he sane braa asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne mane mpanyimfoɔ he.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Maayɔ bɔne sɛ maayi nipa a onni fɔ ama.” Nso bɛkaa sɛ, “Ɔfa yɛ ho bɛ?
Ɔyɛ woaa w’asɛm.” Na ɔtoo dwetɛbena aduasa he guu asɔredane he mu he, ofiri hɔ kɔsɛne ne ho.
Na asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he sesaa dwetɛbena aduasa he, kaa sɛ, “Mmara mma kwane sɛ bɛde begu fotoɔ he mu, efiri sɛ ɔyɛ nipa bi nkwa ano boɔ.” Bɛde beti sɛɛ ho he, bɛde kɔtɔɔ kukuo nwomfoɔ asaase he de yɔɔ amanfrafoɔ amusieɛ.
Yei nti bɛfrɛ saa asaase he Mogyaa Asaase de besi nnɛ.
Na deɛ diyifoɔ Yeremia kaeɛ he baam sɛ, “Bɛfaa dwetɛbena aduasa he a ɔyɛ boɔ a betwa too nipa he ti so, nea Israel mma binom twaa boɔ too ne ti so he, na bɛde tɔɔ kukuo nwomfoɔ asaase he, sɛdeɛ Awurade hyɛɛ me he.” Pilato bisaa Yesu nsɛm Afei Yesu begyinaa amrado he anim; na amrado he bisaa no sɛ, “Wone Yudafoɔ Hene he?” Na Yesu kaa sɛ, “Ɔne ne woaka he.” Nso asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne mane mpanyimfoɔ he bɔɔ no kwaadu he, woankasa.
Na Pilato bisaa no sɛ, “Wonte kwaadu bebree a bɛɛbɔ wo yi?” Nso wamma no mmuaeɛ biaa, wammua kwaadu baako koraa, na ɔyɛɛ amrado he nwanwa kɛse.
Bebuaa Yesu kumfɔ Na afei afahyɛ berɛ he, na amrado he taa yi deduani bi firi afiase ma nnipadɔm he, deɛ bɛpɛ no biaa.
Na saa berɛ he na bɛwɔ deduani mammɔfoɔ bi a bɛfrɛ no Baraba.
Nti behyia wieeɛ he, Pilato bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Hwane ne hopɛ sɛ meyi no ma ho, Baraba, anaa Yesu a bɛfrɛ no Kristo he?” Obisaa yei efiri sɛ, ohuu sɛ anibereɛ nti ne bɛde Yesu bɛhyɛɛ ne nsa.
Berɛ a na ɔte atemmuo adwa he so he, ne yerɛ soma maa bɛbɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nyɔ bibiaa ntia saa beema a onni fɔ yi, na nnɛ maabrɛ papaapa, ɔnam daeɛ bi a m’aso afa ne ho nti.” Afei asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne mane mpanyimfoɔ he bɔɔ nnipadɔm he aso sɛ bɛmma bennyae Baraba, na benku Yesu mmom.
Amrado he bisaa bɛ bio sɛ, “Nnipa mmienu he mu mmɛneɛ ne hopɛ sɛ megyae no?” Na bɛkaa sɛ, “Baraba.” Pilato bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne memfa nyɔ Yesu a bɛfrɛ no Kristo he?” Bɛ nyinaa bɛkaa sɛ, “Ma bɛmmɔ no asennuam!” Na obisaa sɛ, “Mmɛ ntia, abɛ bɔne ne waayɔ?’ Nso bɛkɔɔ so teateam dendenndene sɛ, “Ma bɛmmɔ no asennuam!” Pilato maa bɛbɔɔ Yesu asennuam Nti Pilato huu sɛ ontumi nyɔ bibiaa bio, na afei basabasa bi ɔɔhyɛ aseɛ he, ɔfaa nsuo bi hohoro ne nsa nipakuo he anim, kaa sɛ, “Menni beema yi mogyaa ho fɔ; honyɔ deɛ hopɛ.” Na afei nnipa he nyinaa bom kaa sɛ, “Ne mogyaa mmra yɛ ne yɛ mma so!” Nti ogyae Baraba sedeɛ bɛsrɛɛ no he; na bɛhwee Yesu wieeɛ he, ɔde no maa bɛ sɛ bɛnkɔbɔ no asennuam.
Asraafoɔ he dii Yesu ho fɛw Afei amrado asraafoɔ he faa Yesu kɔɔ amrado he abane mu, na bɛboaboa kuo he nyinaa ano twaa ne ho hyiaeɛ.
Bɛpaa ne ho, na bɛde ataadeɛ kɔkɔɔ bi hyɛɛ no, na bɛkyimkyim nkasɛe bi maa bɛde yɔɔ ahenkyɛ de hyɛɛ ne ti.
Bɛde demmire hyɛɛ ne nsa nifa mu na bebuu nkotodwe n’anim dii ne ho fɛw sɛ, “Hommɔ Yudafoɔ Hene he se!” Bɛtoo ntasuo guu ne so, na bɛgyee demmire he de hwee n’apampam.
Bɛbɔɔ Yesu asennua mu Bedii ne ho fɛw wieeɛ he, beyii ataadeɛ kɔkɔɔ he firii ne ho, na bɛde ɔnoaa n’ataadeɛ hyɛɛ no.
Na afei bɛde no firi hɔ kɔbɔɔ no asennua mu.
Befirii adi ɔɔkɔ he, bɛtoo Kireneni beema bi a bɛfrɛ no Simon; ɔno ne bɛhyɛɛ no maa no soaa Yesu asennua he.
Na beduruu faako a bɛfrɛ hɔ Golgota (asekyerɛ ne sɛ Ti Nkankuro Bea), bɛmaa no nsa a bɛde bɔnwoma afra, nso ɔka hwɛeɛ he, wannom.
Na bɛbɔɔ no asennuam wieeɛ he, bɛtwee ntonto kyɛɛ n’ataadeɛ maa bɛ ho bɛ ho; na bɛtenaa hɔ hwɛɛ ne so.
Bɛtwerɛɛ asɛm a begyinaa so bɔɔ no asennuam he sɛ, “Yei ne Yesu, Yudafoɔ Hene he”, na bɛde bɔɔ n’atifi.
Na bɛbɔɔ akorɔmfoɔ mmienu asennuam kaa ne ho, baako ya ne nifa ne baako nso ya ne benkum.
Bɛ a betwaa mu hɔ he dii ne ho fɛw, wosoo bɛ ti na bɛkaa sɛ, “Wo a wodwiri asɔredane na wode nnansa si, gye wo ho ɛ!
Sɛ woyɛ Nyankopɔn ba a, si firi asennua he so.” Saa ara nso ne asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne atwerɛfoɔ ne mane mpanyimfoɔ he dii ne ho fɛw kaa sɛ, “Ɔgyee afoforɔ; nso ontumi nnye ne ho.
Sɛ ɔyɛ Israel Hene a, ma no mfiri asennua he so nsi fam, na yɛbɛgye no adi.
Ɔde ne ho too Nyankopɔn so, sɛ Nyankopɔn pɛ sɛ ɔgye no a ma no nye no seeseiaa, efiri sɛ, ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Meyɛ Nyankopɔn Ba.’ ” Akorɔmfoɔ a bɛbɔɔ bɛ asennuam kaa ne ho he nso dii ne ho fɛw saa ara.
Yesu wuiɛ Na ofiri awigyina ɔɔkɔ he, sum baa asaase he nyinaa so kosii awia nɔn mmeɛnsa.
Na bɛyɛ awia nnɔn mmeɛnsa berɛ mu he, Yesu teaam dendenndene sɛ, “Eli, Eli lama sabaktani?” asekyerɛ ne sɛ, “Me Nyankopɔn, me Nyankopɔn, ɛɛne nti ne woapa me?” Berɛ a bɛ a bɛgyingyina hɔ he mu bi teeɛ he, bɛkaa sɛ, “Beema yi ɔɔfrɛ Elia.” Prɛko pɛ, bɛ mu baako de mmirika kɔfaa sapɔ de bɔɔ nsa kekakeka mu de hyɛɛ dua so, na ɔde maa no sɛ ɔnom.
Na bɛ a bɛ aka he nso kaa sɛ, “Hontwɛne ma yɛnhwɛ sɛ Elia bɛba abɛgye no anaa.” Yesu de nne dendene teaam bio, na ogyae ne honhom mu.
Saa berɛ he, ntoma a otwa asɔredane he mu he tee mmienu firi soro de kosii fam, na asaase wosoeɛ, na abotane paepaeɛ.
Na adamena nso biebieɛ, na ahoteefoɔ a bɛawuwu he bebree nyanenyaneɛ, na befirii bɛ adamena mu.
Na Yesu wusɔreɛ akyi he, befirii bɛ adamenam kɔɔ Yerusalem, Yudafoɔ kuro kronkron he mu koyiyii bɛ ho adi kyerɛkyerɛɛ nnipa bebree.
Na asraafoɔ ha so panyini ne bɛ a bɛka ne ho ɔɔwɛne Yesu he huu asaasewosoɔ ne nnoɔma a ɔsisiiɛ he, besuroo pii, kaa sɛ, “Ampa, Nyankopɔn Ba di!” Na mmaa bebree ya hɔ a begyina akyirikyiri ɔɔhwɛ nea ɔɔkɔ so he; bɛ ne bedii Yesu akyi firii Galilea maa no deɛ ohia.
Bɛ mu binom ne Maria Magdalene ne Maria a ɔyɛ Yakobo ne Yosef maame, ne Sebedeo yerɛ.
Besiee Yesu Na nwunu dwoeɛ he, sikani bi a ofiri Arimatea a bɛfrɛ no Yosef a ɔno nso yɛ Yesu suani baeɛ; ɔno ne kɔɔ Pilato nkyɛne kɔsrɛɛ Yesu amu he.
Na Pilato hyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa amu he mma no.
Na Yosef faa amu he de nwera fitaa kyekyeree ho de kɔtoo ɔno ankasa ne damena foforɔ a watwa no abotane mu mu.
Na omunii boɔ kɛseɛ bi too nna he ano, na ofirii hɔ kɔeɛ.
Na Maria Magdalene ne Maria a ɔyɛ Yakobo ne Yosef maame he ya hɔ tete baabi a ɔne da he di animhwɛ.
Na adeɛ kyeeɛ a ɔyɛ da a odi ahosiesie da he akyi he, asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ behyiaa Pilato anim.
Na bɛkaa sɛ, “Owura, yɛkae sɛ daadaafoɔ he te ase he ɔkaa sɛ ‘Nnansa akyi he menyane.’ Nti ma bɛnkɔwɛne da he na asuafoɔ he ammewia no, na bɛanka ankyerɛ mane he sɛ, ‘Wanyane afiri awufoɔ mu’; na ama nnaadaa a ɔbɛba akyire he ansene kane deɛ he.” Pilato ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Howɔ asraafoɔ, homfa bɛ nkɔwɛne sɛdeɛ hobetumi biaa.” Na bɛkataa boɔ he ano, de nsɔano hyɛɛ no nso maa awɛmfoɔ he wɛne Yesu damena he.
Yesu wusɔreɛ Na homeda twaa mu he, nnawɔtwe he da a odi kane ahemakye, Maria Magdalene ne Maria foforɔ he baa sɛ bɛbɛhwɛ da he.
Na mpofirem, asaasewosoɔ kɛseɛ siiɛ, na Awurade bɔfoɔ firi soro siane baeɛ, beminii boɔ he firii da he ano, na ɔtenaa so.
Na ne ho te sɛ anyinam, na n’ataadeɛ yɛ fitaa sɛ asukɔtwea.
Na ne ho hu nti, awɛmfoɔ he ho popoeɛ, na bɛyɛɛ sɛ nea bɛawuwu.
Nso bɔfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ mmaa he sɛ, “Honnsuro!
Na menim sɛ hoohwehwɛ Yesu a bɛbɔɔ no asennua mu he.
Onni ha, na wanyane sɛdeɛ ɔkaeɛ he.
Hommra mmɛhwɛ baabi a na ɔda!
Na honkɔ ntɛm nkɔka nkyerɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, ‘Wanyane afiri awufoɔ mu.
Na hwɛ, oodi ho anim kane akɔ Galilea, hɔ ne hobehu no.’ Hwɛ, maka akyerɛ ho.” Nti befirii damena he so ntɛmaa de suro ne anigye kɛseɛ tutuu mmirika sɛ bɛɛkɔka akyerɛ n’asuafoɔ he.
Na ntɛmaa, Yesu hyiaa bɛ kaa sɛ, “Asomdwie nka ho!” Na bɛbaa ne nkyɛne bɛsɔɔ ne nane koto sɔree no.
Afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honnsuro; honkɔ nkɔbɔ me nuanom amaneɛ sɛ bɛnkɔ Galilea; na bebehu me hɔ.” Awɛmfoɔ he amanebɔ Bere a bɛnam kwane so ɔɔkɔ he, hwɛ, awɛmfoɔ he bi kɔɔ kuro he mu kɔkaa deɛ asi nyinaa kyerɛɛ asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ he.
Na berɛ a bɛ ne mpanyimfoɔ he hyiaeɛ he betuu agyina bɔɔ pɔ maa awɛmfoɔ he sika kɛseɛ ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ “Honka sɛ, ‘Anadwo a na yɛadeda he ne n’asuafoɔ he bewiaa no.’ Na sɛ Amrado he te yei a, yɛbɛkyerɛ no mu na ho ho anka adwaam.” Nti bɛgyee sika he, ne bɛkɔyɔɔ sɛdeɛ bɛhyɛɛ bɛ he.
Na asɛm yi atrɛ Yudafoɔ mu de besi nnɛ.
Asɛmpatrɛ adwuma ho ahyɛdeɛ Afei asuafoɔ dubaako he kɔɔ, bepɔ bi a ɔya Galilea a na Yesu akyerɛ bɛ he so.
Behuu no he, bɛkoto sɔree no, nso binom gyee akyinnye.
Na Yesu ba bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Bɛde soro ne asaase so tumi nyinaa ama me.
Nti honkɔyɛ amane nyinaa m’asuafoɔ, na hommɔ bɛ asu nhyɛ Agya he, Ɔba he ne Honhom Kronkron he dini mu, na honkyerɛkyerɛ bɛ sɛ benni deɛ mahyɛ ho nyinaa so.
Na hwɛ, me ne ho ya hɔ nna nyinaa de kosi wiase awieeɛ.”
NNIANIMU Asɛmpa a Marko twerɛ maeɛ he, asɛm a ɔde hyɛɛ aseɛ ne sɛ, “Yesu Kristo, Nyankopɔn Ba he ho asɛmpa he.” Mfonyini a Marko twa fa Yesu ho ne sɛ ɔyɛ nipa a ɔbɔ ne ho mmɔdene paa na ɔwɔ tumi nso.
Ne tumi da adi ne nkyerɛkyeremu, na ɔda adi nso ahonhommɔne so, ne bɔne a otumi de kyɛ mu.
Marko asɛmpa mu he, Yesu da ne ho adi sɛ Nipa Ba he a ɔde ne nkwa maeɛ de gyee nnipa firii bɛ bɔne mu.
Marko bɔ Yesu ho asɛm he tɔfa, na ɔkasa pii fa nnoɔma a Yesu yɔeɛ ho kyɛne nsɛm a Yesu kaeɛ ne ne nkyerɛkyerɛɛ he.
Ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ kaa Suboni Yohane ho asɛm, Yesu asubɔ, ne sɔhwɛ ɔne Yesu dwumadie a ɔfa ayaresa ne nkyerɛkyerɛ ho.
Ti a otwa toɔ he ka nsɛm a osisiiɛ Yesu amanehunu nnawɔtwe ne titire ne wuo.
Ti a otwa toɔ yiaa nso kasa fa ne wusɔreɛ ho.
Asɛmpa he awie yɛ mmienu, nea ɔya nkahyemdeɛ adeɛ mmienu mu he , nnipa bebree adwene ne sɛ, nipa foforɔ bi ne twerɛeɛ na mmom ɔnyɛ Marko ne twerɛeɛ.
MU NSƐM Asɛmpa he mfitiaseɛ :- Yesu som adwuma ya Galilea abɔntene so :—: Yesu firi Galilea ɔɔkɔ Yerusalem :- Yesu bɛnee Yerusalem ne nnanwɔtwe a odi akyire a odii ya hɔ :—: Yesu wusɔreɛ he :- Awurade a wasɔre he ahoyie ne ne sorokɔ :-
Suboni Yohane Asɛnka Yesu Kristo, Nyankopɔn Ba he asɛmpa mfitiaseɛ.
Sɛnea diyifoɔ Yesaia atwerɛ he, “Hwɛ, meesoma me bɔfoɔ adi w’anim, asiesie wo kwane.
Nea ɔɔteam serɛ so he dɛ, ‘Siesie Awurade kwane, ma N’akwane ntene.’ ” Suboni Yohane baa serɛ he so a, na ɔpaee mu kaa adwensakra ho asubɔ a ɔde kɔ bɔne fakyɛ mu.
Na Yuda asaase sofoɔ ne Yerusalemfoɔ nyinaa kɔɔ ne nkyɛne, na bɛkaa bɛ bɔne ma ɔbɔɔ bɛ asu asubɔntene Yordan mu.
Na Yohane hyɛ ataadeɛ a bɛde yoma ho nwii ayɔ, na ɔde aboomu a bɛde aboa nwoma ayɔ abɔ n’asene, na n’aduane a odi ne mmɛbɛ ne wuram woɔ.
Ɔpaem kaa sɛ, “Nea ɔwɔ tumi kyɛne me di m’akyi a ɔɔba.
Memfata sɛ mɛkoto asane ne mpaboa ahoma mpo.
Me deɛ mede nsuo ne abɔ ho asu; na ɔno deɛ, ɔde Honhom Kronkron ne bɛbɔ ho asu.” Yohane Bɔɔ Yesu Asu Saa nna he mu he, Yesu firi Nasaret a ɔya Galilea baeɛ, na Yohane bɔɔ no asu Yordan mu.
Na oofiri nsuo he mu apie heaa, ohuu soro sɛ abie a na Honhom he oosiane sɛ abuburo ɔɔba ne so.
Na nne bi firi soro kaa sɛ, “Wone me dɔba he; wo ne wosɔ m’ani!” Bronsam Sɔɔ Yesu Hwɛeɛ Na amonom hɔaa, Honhom he hwimm no kɔɔ serɛ he so.
Odii adaduannan serɛ he so, Satan sɔɔ no hwɛeɛ; ɔne wuram mmoa tenaeɛ; na abɔfoɔ som no.
Dwumadie a Yesu dii no Galilea he Mfitiaseɛ Afei berɛ a bɛkyee Yohane akyi he, Yesu baa Galilea, na ɔpaem kaa asɛmpa a ofiri Nyankopɔn he sɛ, “Berɛ he awie duru, na Nyankopɔn ahennie he abɛne; honsakra ho adwene na honye asɛmpa he nni.” Yesu Frɛɛ N’asuafoɔ a Bedi kane he Na Yesu nam Galilea po ho he, ohuu Simon ne Andreo a ɔyɛ Simon nua sɛ beegu asau po he mu efiri sɛ na bɛyɛ apofofoɔ.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honni m’akyi na mɛma hoayɛ nnipayifoɔ.” Na amonom hɔaa begyaa bɛ asau hɔ dii n’akyi.
Na ɔkɔɔ animu kakra he, ohuu Sebedeo ba Yakubu ne ne nua Yohane, na bɛ te bɛ kodoɔ mu a bɛɛkora bɛ asau.
Amonom hɔaa, ɔfrɛɛ bɛ, na begyaa bɛ papa Sebedeo ne apaafoɔ he ne kodoɔ he hɔ bedii n’akyi.
Beema bi a na Honhommɔne ya ne mu Na bekoduru Kapernaum kurom.
Na homeda duruiɛ he, ntɛmaa Yesu kɔɔ hyiadane he mu kɔkyerɛkyerɛeɛ.
Ne nkyerɛkyerɛ he yɛɛ bɛ nwanwa, esiane sɛ ɔde tumi paa ne kasaeɛ, na wankasa sɛ atwerɛfoɔ he.
Saa berɛ heaa na beema bi a ɔwɔ honhom fi ya hyiadane he mu, na ɔteaam sɛ, “Ɛɛne ne yɛne wo wɔ yɔ, Nasareni Yesu?
Wobaa sɛ woobɛsɛe yɛ anaa?
Menim wo, Nyankopɔn Kronkronni.” Na Yesu teateaa no kaa sɛ, “Ka wo ano tom, na firi ne mu kɔ!” Na honhom fi he maa no senseneeɛ, na ɔde nne kɛseɛ teaam, na ofirii ne mu kɔeɛ.
Na yei yɛɛ bɛ nyinaa ahodwiri ma bebisabisaa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ: “Abɛ di?
Nkyerɛkyerɛ foforɔ a tumi yam!
Ɔhyɛ ahonhom fi mpo na betie no.” Na ne ho asɛm firii hɔ trɛɛ ntɛm kɔɔ nsaase a atwa Galilea ho ahyia nyinaa so.
Yesu saa nnipa bebree yadeɛ Simon fie Na befirii hyiadane he muaa pɛ, bɛ ne Yakobo ne Yohane kɔɔ Simon ne Andreo fie.
Na Simon asebaa yare abunu da hɔ.
Na ntɛmaa bɛkaa ne ho asɛm kyerɛɛ Yesu.
Na ɔba bɛsɔɔ ne nsa maa no so, na abunu he gyaeɛ, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ yɔɔ bɛ ahohoyɛ.
Na saa da he anwummerɛ berɛ a awia kɔtɔeɛ he, bɛde bɛ a bɛyare anaa bɛwɔ ahonhommɔne nyinaa braa no.
Na kuro mũ he nyinaa behyiaa pono he ano.
Na ɔsaa nnipa bebree a bɛyare nyarewa ahodoɔ yadeɛ, na otutuu ahonhommɔne pii; na wamma ahonhommɔne he kwane amma bɛnkasa, efiri sɛ na benim no.
Yesu asɛnka dwumadie a odii no Galilea Anɔpa a animu nteteeɛ he, Yesu sɔre kɔhyɛɛ kokoam baabi, na ɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ hɔ.
Na Simon ne ne nnamfonom tii no.
Behuu no he, bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Biaa ɔɔhwehwɛ wo.” Obuaa sɛ, “Homma yɛnkɔ nkuro a ɔbembɛne yi mu na menkɔka asɛmpa he hɔ nso; na ɔno ne adwuma a mebaa sɛ meebɛyɔ.” Na ɔkɔɔ Galilea nyinaa kɔkaa asɛmpa he ya bɛ hyiadane ahodoɔ mu, na otutuu ahonhommɔne.
Yesu saa Kwatani bi Yadeɛ Kwatani bi baa ne nkyɛne bebuu nkotodwe srɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ wopɛ a, wobetumi ama me ho afiri.” Na Yesu nyaa tema maa no, na ɔtenee ne nsa kaa no, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Mepɛ, wo ho mfiri.” Amonom hɔaa, kwata he kɔeɛ, na ne ho firiiɛ.
Na ogyaa no kwane ntɛm so braa no keteee ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Hwɛ na woanka hwee ankyerɛ biaa, na mmom kɔ na fa wo ho kɔkyerɛ sɔfo, na tua w’ahofire aboadeɛ a Mose hyɛeɛ he, na ɔnyɛ adanseɛ mma bɛ.” Nso ofirii adi, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ kekaa ho asɛm, ma ɔtrɛɛ maa afei deɛ Yesu antumi anyi n’anim ankɔ kuro biaa mu bio, na ɔtenaa nkuro agya, na nnipa firii mmeammea baa ne nkyɛne.
Yesu Saa Bubuani bi Yadeɛ Na nna bi akyi he, Yesu sane kɔɔ Kapernaum; na benyaa nkra sɛ ɔya fie.
Nti nnipa bebree behyiaam kyeree so kosii kwane he ano nyinaa, na ɔɔka asɛm he akyerɛ bɛ.
Na nnipa binom baeɛ a na mu nnan so bubuani.
Na bɛde no braa no.
Na berɛ a nnipa he nti bɛantumi amfa no amma Yesu nkyɛne he, bɛpaa dane he so, tuu tokuro dane he atifi, na begyeegyaa kɛtɛ he a bubuani he da so he mu besii fam.
Na Yesu huu bɛ gyidie he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bubuani he sɛ, “Ɔba, bɛde wo bɔne akyɛ wo.” Ɔkaa saa he, atwerɛfoɔ he binom te hɔ a bebisaa bɛ mu sɛ, “Ɛɛne nti ne ɔkasa saa?
Ɔyɛ abususɛm!
Hwane ne tumi de bɔne kyɛ ka Nyankopɔn ho?” Amonom hɔaa, Yesu nyaa atenka ne honhom mu sɛ bɛɛdwene asemmisa yi ho.
Na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ho dwene saa asemmisa yi ho ho mu?
Yei mu deɛhe ne ɔmmerɛ, sɛ bɛbɛka akyerɛ bubuani yi sɛ, ‘Bɛde wo bɔne akyɛ wo, anaa, Sɔre na fa wo kɛtɛ nante’?
Na sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a hobehu sɛ Nipa Ba he wɔ tumi asaase so sɛ ɔde bɔne kyɛ nti ɔka kyerɛɛ bubuani he sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ wo, sɔre, fa wo kɛtɛ, na kɔ wo fie.” Na ɔsɔreeɛ, na ɔfaa ne kɛtɛ ntɛm pa so, na ofirii bɛ nyinaa bɛ anim hɔ kɔeɛ ma bɛ nyinaa bɛ ho dwirii bɛ na bɛhyɛɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam kaa sɛ, “Yenhuu bibiaa sei da.” Yesu Frɛɛ Lewi Yesu firii adi kɔɔ po he ho bio; dɔm he nyinaa betwaa ne ho hyiaeɛ, na ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ.
Na ɔnam he, ohuu Alfeo ba Lewi sɛ ɔte togyebea, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Di m’akyi.” Na ɔsɔre dii n’akyi.
Na akyire he, ɔbaa sɛ berɛ a Yesu te didipono ho ya Lewi fie he, na ɔne atogyefoɔ ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ bebree ne n’asuafoɔ ne te hɔ; na nnipa foforɔ bebree nso ka ne ho.
Na Farisifoɔ he mu atwerɛfoɔ he huu sɛ ɔne atogyefoɔ ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ oodidi he, bebisaa n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ɔne atogyefoɔ ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ didi yi?” Yesu tee yei he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Bɛ a bɛnyare he, benhia yaresafoɔ, gye sɛ bɛ a bɛyare.
Mamma sɛ meebɛfrɛ ateneneefoɔ na mmom nnebɔnyɛfoɔ.” Akɔnkyene ho Asemmisa Afei, na Yohane asuafoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he ɔɔkyene kɔm; na nnipa binom bebisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne Yohane asuafoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he ɔɔkyene kɔm, na w’asuafoɔ deɛ, bɛnkyene kɔm?” Yesu bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Nnipa a bɛkɔ ayefohyia ntumi nkyene kɔm berɛ a ayefokunu he ya bɛ nkyɛne, ɔnte saa’?
Mmerɛ tentene a ayefokunu he ne bɛya hɔ he, ɔnsɛ sɛ bɛkyene kɔm.
Nso nna bi bɛba a bɛbɛfa ayefokunu he afiri bɛ nkyɛne, na afei bɛbɛkyene kɔm.
“Bɛmmfa ntoma mono sini ntɛ ataadeɛ dada mu; anyɛ saa a, ntemu he bɛte afiri mu, kyerɛ sɛ, ntemu mono he befiri dada he mu, na nteɛ he bɛyɛ kɛse paa.
Saa ara nso ne bɛmmfa bobesa foforɔ nngu nsakotokuo dada mu, anyɛ saa a, nsa foforɔ he bɛpae kotokuo he na nsa he ahwie agu, na kotokuo he nso bɛsɛe; na mmom bɛde bobesa foforɔ gu nsakotokuo foforɔ mu.” Homeda He Ho Asɛnka Na ɔbaa sɛ homeda bi na Yesu nam aburofuo bi mu, na bɛɛkɔ he, n’asuafoɔ he hyɛɛ aseɛ pempanee aburo mmɛtem he bi.
Yei maa Farisifoɔ he bisaa no sɛ, “Hwɛ, mmɛ nti ne bɛɛyɔ deɛ otia mmara homeda?” Na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Honnkenkanee deɛ Dawid yɔeɛ berɛ a na kɔm de ɔne ne nkurofoɔ na bɛɛpɛ aduane adi he?
Owuraa Awurade fie, berɛ a na Abiata yɛ sɔfopanyini he, na odii Kyerɛ Paanoo a na mmara mma ho kwane mma biaa nni gye asɔfoɔ nkoaa, na ɔde bi nso maa ne nkurofoɔ he ma bediiɛ.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nnipa nti ne bɛyɔɔ homeda he, na ɔnyɛ homeda nti ne bɛyɔɔ nnipa; nti Nipa Ba he yɛ homeda he so tumfoɔ.”
Beema bi a na ne Nsa Adwodwo Na afei, Yesu kɔɔ hyiadane he mu, na beema bi ya hɔ a na ne nsa adwodwo.
Na bɛhwɛɛ sɛ ɔbɛsa no yadeɛ homeda he anaa, na bɛde abu no fɔ.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ nea ne nsa adwodwo he sɛ, “Bra ha!” Na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne nipa wɔ ho kwane sɛ ɔyɔ no homeda, adepa anaa adebɔne, sɛ ɔbɛgye bi kra nkwa anaa ɔbɛma na asɛe?” Na biaa yɔɔ komm.
Na ɔde abufuo hwɛɛ bɛ nyinaa hyiaeɛ; na ne werɛ hoeɛ bɛ akoma dene he nti, na ɔka kyerɛɛ beema he sɛ, “Tene wo nsa.” Ɔteneeɛ, na ahoɔdene baa ne nsa he mu bio.
Na Farisifoɔ he firii abɔntene a pɛ, bɛ ne Herodefoɔ bɔɔ pɔ hwehwɛɛ kwane a bɛbɛfa so aku no.
Nnipadɔm Bebree ya Mpoano Na afei Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he twee bɛ ho kɔɔ mpoano, na nnipadɔm bebree firi Galilea ne Yudea dii n’akyi.
Bɛtee nea wayɔ nyinaa he, nnipadɔm firi Yerusalem, Idumea, Yordan agya, ɔne Tiro ne Sidon mantam mu baeɛ.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ dɔm he nti bensiesie kodoɔ mma no sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bemmu mfa ne so.
Esiane sɛ na wasa bebree yadeɛ nti, bɛ a bɛwɔ yadeɛ nyinaa ba bɛkyere ne so sɛ bɛbɛsɔ ne mu.
Berɛ biaa a ahonhom fi behu no he, bɛhwe ase n’anim teaam sɛ, “Wone Nyame Ba he!” Na ɔhyɛɛ bɛ ketee sɛ bɛnna no adi nkyerɛ biaa.
Yesu yii Dummienu he Yesu kɔɔ bepɔ he so, na ɔtoo ne nsa frɛɛ bɛ a ohia bɛ ma bɛbaa ne nkyɛne.
Na oyii dummienu a ɔmaa bɛ abodini sɛ “Asomafoɔ” a bɛbɛka ne ho akɔ ka asɛmpa he, na bɛanya tumi atu ahonhommɔne.
Nnipa dummienu bɛ he ne: Simon (ɔtoo no dini Petro), Sebedeo ba Yakubu ɔne Yohane a ɔyɛ Yakubu nua (bɛ ne ɔmaa bɛ dini Bo-anerges, asekyerɛ ne Apranaa mma); ne Andreo, ne Filipo, ne Bartolomeo, ne Mateo, ne Toma, ne Afeos ba Yakubu, ne Tadeo, ɔne Kanani Simon, ne Yuda Iskariot a oyii Yesu mmaeɛ he.
Yesu ne Beelsebul Na Yesu kɔɔ fie, na nnipadɔm he sane behyiaa mu a na bennya aduane mpo nni.
N’abusuafoɔ teeɛ he, bɛkɔɔ sɛ beekosi no kwane, efiri sɛ na nkurofoɔ ɔɔka sɛ, “Ne ti nni hɔ”.
Na atwerɛfoɔ he a befiri Yerusalem baeɛ he kaa sɛ, “Ɔwɔ Beelsebul, na ɔde ahonhommɔne panyini he tumidie ne tutu ahonhom fi.” Na ɔfrɛɛ bɛ baa ne nkyɛne na ɔyɔɔ saa mfantoho yi kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na Satan atutu Satan?
Sɛ ahennie bi ne ne ho di asie a, ahennie he ntumi nnyina.
Na sɛ mpaepaemu ya fie bi mu a, saa fie he ntumi nnyina.
Na sɛ Satan asɔre atia ne ho na ne mu akyekyɛ a, ontumi nnyina, na mmom n’awieeɛ ne aba.
Na bi ntumi nkɔ ahoɔdenfoɔ fie nkɔfom ne nnoɔma gye sɛ waakyekyere ahoɔdenfoɔ he, ansa na wafom fie hɔ nnoɔma.
Nɔkorɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, ɔde nipa bɔne ne abususɛm biaa a ɔbɛka bɛkyɛ no, nso deɛ ɔka abususɛm tia Honhom Kronkron he deɛ onnya bɔne fakyɛ, na daa afobuo da ne so.” Ɔkaa yei sɛ efiri sɛ na bɛɛkeka sɛ, “Ɔwɔ honhom fi.” Yesu Abusua kann Na afei Yesu maame ne ne nuanom baeɛ, na begyinaa abɔntene somaa sɛ bɛnkɔfrɛ no mmara.
Na nnipa atwa ne ho ahyia; na bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Hwɛ, wo maame ne wo nua mmeema ne wo nua mmaa gyina abɔntene a bɛɛfrɛ wo.” Na obuaa sɛ, “Me maame ne me nuanom ne hefoɔ?” Na ɔhwɛɛ bɛ a bɛtete ne nkyɛne he kaa sɛ, “Yeinom ne me maame ne me nuanom.
Nea ɔyɔ Nyankopɔn apɛdeɛ biaa yɛ me nua beema ne me nua baa ne me maame.”
Mfantoho a ɔfa abaguo ho Na afei nso, Yesu hyɛɛ aseɛ maa nkyerɛkyerɛ po he ho.
Nnipadɔm betwaa ne ho hyiaeɛ ma ɔkɔforoo kodoɔ bi po he so na ɔtenaa mu, berɛ a na nnipadɔm he tete po he ano.
Ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ de mfantoho kyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ nnoɔma pii, ne nkyerɛkyerɛ he mu he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hontie!
Gufoɔ bi koguu aba.
Na oogu he, aba he bi koguu kwane nkyɛne, na nnomaa bediiɛ.
Aba he bi nso koguu abotane so, baabi a nɛteɛ nni papa, esiane sɛ nɛteɛ he mu nnɔ nti ofifirii ntɛm.
Na awia bɔeɛ he, ɔhyee no; na ɔnam sɛ onni nhini nti otwintwameeɛ.
Na aba he bi koguu nkasɛem, na nkasɛe he nyiniiɛ he, omiaa no, na anso aba biaa.
Afei, aba he bi nso koguu asaase pa mu, na ɔsoo aba, onyiniiɛ, yɛɛ akɛseɛ, na ofirii aseɛ sõõ aba mmɔho aduasa, aduosia ne mmɔho ha.” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Ma nea ɔwɔ aso betie biaa ntie.” Mfantoho he Nkyerɛaseɛ Berɛ a Yesu nkoaa ya hɔ he, bɛ a na bɛya ne nkyɛne he ne n’asuafoɔ dummienu he bisaa no mfantoho he ho asɛm.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho deɛ, bɛde Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho ahintasɛm ama ho, na bɛ a bɛya wiase he deɛ, bɛde bibiaa ama bɛ mfantoho mu; sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a, ‘bɛbɛhwɛ paa deɛ nso benhu, na bɛatie paa nso bɛnte aseɛ; na bɛansakra annya bɔne fakyɛ.’ ” Na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Honnte mfantoho yi ase?
Na ɔbɛyɛ na ho ate mfantoho a aka he nyinaa ase.
Gufoɔ he guu asɛm he.
Na aba a oguu kwane nkyɛne he gyina hɔ ma nnipa a bɛte asɛm he a, ɔnkyerɛ na Satan abeyi asɛm a bɛagu ne bɛ mu he kɔ.
Na yeinom ne nea beguu ne abotane mu he: bɛne nnipa a sɛ bɛte asɛm he a, bɛde anigye gye no ntɛm so.
Nso ɔnam sɛ benni nhini nti, begyina kakra bi, na sɛ haw anaa taa ba bɛ so ɔnam asɛm he nti a, bɛhwe ase ntɛm so.
Na aba a oguu nkasɛe mu he gyina hɔ ma nnipa a sɛ bɛte asɛm he a, wiase mu dadwene ne ahonya ho nnadaa ne nnoɔma a aka ho akɔnnɔ ba bemia asɛm he, na ɔmma no nso aba biaa.
Na nea beguu no asaase pa mu he gyina hɔ ma nnipa a bɛte asɛm he a bɛgye na bɛsõ aba mmɔho aduasa ne aduosia ne mmɔho ha.” Kanea a ɔhyɛ Atam Ase Hohwɛeɛ yi, bɛde kanea ba sɛ bɛ ɔɔbɛhyɛ atam anaa mpa ase, a ɔnyɛ kanea dua so ne bɛde oobisi?
Na bibiaa nni hɔ a ahinta a bemmie so, anaa bibiaa nni hɔ a ahinta a ɔmma hann mu.
Ma deɛ ɔwɔ aso a bɛde tie he ntie!” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honhwɛ nea hote yie, sɛnea wobesusu de ama he, saa ne wobenya, na mpo bɛde bi bɛka ho ama wo.
Na nea ɔde bi ma he bɛbɛma no bebree aka ho, na nea ɔmma hwee he, deɛ ɔwɔ he mpo bɛbɛgye afiri ne nsam.” Aba ɔnoaa fifiri ho Mfantoho Ɔkaa bio sɛ, “Soro ahennie te sɛ bi a wakogu aba asaase so, na ɔkɔda anadwo sɔre anɔpa, na aba he fifiri na onyini a onnim kwane a ɔfa so yɔ saa.
Asaase heaa ma onyini, nea odi kane ne dua he, na afei tire he, ansa na aburoo he ankasa.
Nso aburoo he nyini wie a, ntɛmaa ɔde ne twa-sekane kɔ mu efiri sɛ twaberɛ aduru.” Sinapi aba ho Mfantoho Ɔkaa bio sɛ, “Mmɛ ne yebetumi de atoto Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho, anaa mmɛ mfantoho ne yɛbɛyɔ afa ahennie he ho?
Ɔte sɛ sinapi aba a sɛ bedua ne asaase mu a, ɔno ne aba a osua paa asaase so aba nyinaa mu; nso sɛ bedua a, onyini bɛyɛ nnua mu dua kɛseɛ paa, na ɔnya mmane akɛseɛ bebree, na wiem nnomaa atumi ayɛ prebuo ne nwunum.” Mfantoho he ho asekyerɛ Ɔde mfantoho bebree maa bɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ, sɛnea na bebetumi ate aseɛ.
Wankasa ankyerɛ bɛ a na mfantoho nka ho; na ɔka ɔne n’asuafoɔ he nkoaa a, ɔkyerɛkyerɛ bibiaa mu kyerɛ bɛ.
Yesu aaa po mframa yɛɛ dinn Saa da he, berɛ a na nnwunu adwo he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Homma yentware nkɔ fa nohoaa.” Nti begyaa nnipadɔm he kwane wieeɛ he, bɛde Yesu tenaa kodoɔ he mu kɔeɛ; na akodoɔ foforɔ nso ka ho.
Na akodoɔ binom ka ne ho.
Nsuframa kɛseɛ bi bɔeɛ; na mframa he bɔ baa kodoɔ he mu maa nsuo begyinaa kodoɔ he mu.
Nso na Yesu ada summiiɛ so ya kodoɔ he mu; na benyanee no bisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, yɛɛyera yi, ɔmfa wo ho?” Onyaneeɛ, na ɔkaa mframa he anim ka kyerɛɛ po he sɛ, “Gyae, yɛ dinn!” Na mframa he ano brɛɛ ase, na ɔyɛɛ dinn.
Obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Ɛɛne nti ne hosuro?
Nti obesi nnɛ yi honni gyidie?” Na bɛ ho dwirii bɛ kɛse na bɛkeka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Abɛ nipa koraa di a mframa ne po mpo tie no yi?”
Yesu Saa bi a ɔwɔ honhommɔne yadeɛ ya Gerasene Na afei bɛbaa po he agya, Gerasefoɔ asaase so.
Na ofirii kodoɔ he muaa pɛ, beema bi a ɔwɔ honhom fi firii afunsieɛ hyiaa no.
Na ɔte afunsieɛ hɔ, na biaa ntumi mpoa no, bɛde nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn mpo gu no a, bentumi mpoa no; efiri sɛ na bɛtaa de mpokyerɛ ne nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn kyekyere no, nso ɔtete mpokyerɛ he na wabubu nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn he mu asisinasini, na biaa nni ahoɔdene a ɔde bɛbrɛ no ase.
Na daa, awia ne anadwo, ɔteateaam, de aboɔ twitwa ne ho afunsieɛ hɔ mmepɔ he so.
Na ohuu Yesu akyirekyire he, ɔde mmirika kɔkotoo n’anim; na ɔteaam kɛse sɛ, “Abɛ ne wo ne me wɔ yɔ, Yesu, Sorosoro Nyankopɔn Ba?
Mede Nyankopɔn dini srɛ wo, nha me.” Nea nti a beema he kaa saa ne sɛ, na Yesus aka akyerɛ no sɛ “Honhom fi, firi beema he mu firi!” Afei, Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Wo dini de sɛ’?” Oyi ano sɛ, “Me de Dodoɔ, efiri sɛ yɛ dɔɔso.” Ɔsrɛɛ no anibereɛ so sɛ ɔmmpamo bemmfiri asaase he so.
Afei, na mprako binom oodidi bepɔ he so hɔ, na ahonhom fi he srɛɛ no sɛ, “Ma yɛnkɔhyɛ mprako he mu.” Nti ɔmaa bɛ kwane.
Na ahonhom fi he firi kɔhyɛɛ mprako he mu; na mmoa bɛyɛ mpem mmienu he nyinaa gyee twi siane koguu po he mu maa po he faa bɛ.
Mprakohwɛfoɔ he tuu mmirika kɔbɔɔ amaneɛ kuro he ne mane he mu.
Na nnipa ba bɛhwɛɛ deɛ asi.
Na bɛbaa Yesu hɔ, na bebehuu nea kane he na ɔwɔ ahonhommɔne a na bɛfrɛ no Dɔm he sɛ ɔte hɔ fira ntoma na n’adwene mu ate.
Na besuroeɛ.
Bɛ a na bɛahu nea na ato nea ɔwɔ honhom fi he ne mprako he kaa ho asɛm.
Na bɛhyɛɛ aseɛ srɛɛ Yesu sɛ omfiri bɛ mpɔtamu hɔ nkɔ.
Na ɔɔbɛforo kodoɔ he, beema a na honhom fi ya ne mu he srɛɛ no sɛ ɔne no bɛkɔ.
Nso Yesu amma no kwane, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kɔ fie, wo nnamfonom nkyɛne, na ka nea Awurade ayɔ ama wo, ɔne mmɔborɔhunu a wayi no adi akyerɛ wo.” Na ɔkɔeɛ, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ paem kaa nea Yesu ayɔ ama no he ya Dekapoli, na biaa ho dwirii no.
Yairo ba baa byane ne baa a na mogyaa ootu no he ayaresa Na afei berɛ a Yesu tware po he bio sane ba n’agya he, nnipadɔm kɛseɛ twaa ne ho hyiaeɛ, na ɔya po he ho.
Na hyiadane he mu mpanyimfoɔ he mu baako a bɛfrɛ no Yaaro baeɛ, na ohuu no he, ɔhwee ne nane ase na ɔsrɛɛ no pii sɛ, “Meba baa oowu.
Bra na fa wo nsa begu ne so, na ne ho nyɛ no dene, na onya nkwa.” Nti ɔne no kɔeɛ.
Na nnipadɔm kɛseɛ dii n’akyi, na bɛkyeree ne so.
Afei, na baa bi ya hɔ a na mogyaa atu no mfenhyia dummienu.
Na waafa ahokyerɛ pii mu ayaresafoɔ bebree nsam, na waahwere deɛ ɔwɔ nyinaa, nso na ne ho ntɔɔ no a yadeɛ he ayɛ kɛse mpo.
Na waate Yesu ho asɛm, na ofirii n’akyi nnipadɔm he mu bɛkaa n’ataadeɛ ano, efiri sɛ ɔkaa sɛ, “Sɛ mede me nsa ka n’ataadeɛ nkoaa mpo a, menya ayaresa.” ‘Amonom hɔaa mogyaa he twaeɛ; na ɔtee no ne nipadua mu sɛ waanya ayaresa.
Na ntɛmaa, Yesu huu sɛ tumi bi afiri ne mu.
Na ɔdanee ne ho nnipadɔm he mu bisaa sɛ, “Hwane ne kaa m’ataadeɛ yi?” Na n’asuafoɔ he bisaa no sɛ, “Woaa wonim sɛ nnipa yi kyere wo so, na afei mmɛ nti ne woobisa sɛ, ‘Hwane kaa me?’ ” Na ɔhwehwɛɛ hɔ nyinaa sɛ obehu nea ɔyɔɔ saa he.
Na ɔnam sɛ baa he nim nea wayɔ nti, ɔde suro ne ahopopoɔ bɛhwee n’anim, na ɔkaa nɔkorɛ he nyinaa.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ba baa, wo gyidie asa wo yadeɛ, fa asomdwie kɔ, na wo yadeɛ he nkɔ.” Na ogu so ɔɔkasa he, nnipa bi firi hyiadane mu panyini he fie bɛkaa sɛ, “Wo ba baa he awu, mmɛ nti ne woda so ɔɔha kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he?” Na Yesu tee nea bɛkaeɛ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ hyiadane mu panyini he sɛ, “Nsuro, gye nkoaa ne gye di” Wamma biaa anni n’akyi gye Petro, Yakubu ne Yohane, Yakubu nua he.
Bɛbaa hyiadane mu panyini he fie hɔ he, ohuu sɛ hɔ yɛ gyegyeegye a nnipa oosu, na bɛde anibereɛ ootwa adwo dendenndene.
Na owuraa fie hɔ he, obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne hooyɔ gyegyeegye na hoosu yi?
Akwadaa he nwuiɛ, na waada.” Na bɛseree no.
Na ɔmaa bɛ nyinaa kɔɔ abɔntene, na ɔfaa akwadaa he papa ne ne maame ne bɛ a bɛka ne ho he, na ɔkɔɔ baabi a akwadaa he ya he.
Ɔsɔɔ ne nsa ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Talita kumm,” a ɔkyerɛ sɛ, “Abaayaa kumaa, sɔre!” Na amonom hɔaa abaayaa he sɔreeɛ, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ nanteeɛ (na waadi mfie dummienu).
Yei nti bɛ ho dwirii bɛ kɛse.
Na ɔhyɛɛ bɛ ketee sɛ bɛmma biaa nte yei, na afei ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, bɛmma akwadaa he bibi nni.
Bɛpoo Yesu Nasaret Na afei Yesu firii hɔ baa ne kurom, na n’asuafoɔ he dii n’akyi.
Homeda he, ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ kyerɛkyerɛɛ hyiadane mu, na dodoɔ a bɛtee ne nkyerɛkyerɛɛ he nyinaa ho dwirii bɛ.
Bebisaa sɛ, “Hefa ne beema yi nyaa yeinom nyinaa?
Mmɛ nyansa ne bɛde ama no yi?
Mmɛ tumi-nnwuma ne ne nsa ɔɔyɔ yi!
Aa!
Ɔnyɛ yei ne dua dwumfoɔ he, Maria ba ne Yakubu ne Yose ne Yuda ne Simon nua he, na ne nua mmaa nni yɛ nkyɛne ha?” Na bɛde abufuo buu no animtia.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Anidie mmɔ adiyifoɔ gye sɛ bɛ kurom, ne bɛaa bɛ nkurofoɔ mu, ne bɛaa bɛ fie.” Na wantumi anyɔ tumideɛ biaa hɔ gye nnipa kakraa bi a ɔde ne nsa guu bɛ so saa bɛ yadeɛ.
Na ɔyɛɛ no nwanwa sɛ bɛannye anni.
Dummienu he Dwumadie Na okyinkyini nkuraase kyerɛkyerɛeɛ.
Ɔfrɛɛ dummienu he na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ somaa bɛ kɔ abɔntene mmienu mmienu, na ɔmaa bɛ ahonhom fi so tumi.
Ɔhyɛɛ bɛ sɛ, bɛmmfa hwee ntu kwane he ka poma ho; bɛmmfa aduane, bɔtɔ; saa ara nso ne bɛmfa sika nhyɛ bɛ abɔsoɔ mu; na bɛnhyɛ mpaboa, bɛnnhyɛ ntaadeɛ mmienu mmienu nso.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ hokɔ fie bi mu a, hontena hɔ nkosi sɛ hobefiri kurom hɔ.
Baabi a hobɛkɔ a bɛannye ho he, na bɛantie ho he, sɛ hoofiri hɔ a, homporoporo ho nane ase mfuturo ngu hɔ, na ɔnyɛ adanseɛ ntia bɛ.” Nti bɛkɔ kɔpaem kaa sɛ biaa nsakra n’adwene.
Betutuu ahonhommɔne bebree, na bɛsraa bɛ a bɛyare bebree ngo na bɛsaa bɛ yadeɛ.
Suboni Yohane wuo Hene Herode teeɛ, efiri sɛ na Yesu dini ahyeta hɔ nyinaa.
Na binom ɔɔka sɛ, “Bɛanyane Yohane Suboni afiri awufoɔ mu, saa nti ne tumideɛyɔ yi ɔɔkɔ so ne mu.” Na binom kaa sɛ, “Ɔyɛ Elia.” Na binom nso kaa sɛ, “Ɔyɛ diyifoɔ te sɛ tete adiyifoɔ he bi.” Na Herode teeɛ he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Eei!
Yohane a metwaa ne ti he anyane?” Nea na asi ne sɛ, na Herode asoma mmeema ama bɛakɔkye Yohane, akyekyere no de no ato afiase, Herodia a ɔyɛ ne nua Filipo yerɛ he ho nti, efiri sɛ na Herode agye no afiri Filipo nsam aware no.
Ɔne sɛ, na Yohane taa ka kyerɛ Herode sɛ, “Mmara mma kwane sɛ wobɛware wo nua yerɛ.” Ne saa nti na Herodia wɔ meneasepɔ tia Yohane, na ɔpɛɛ sɛ oku no, nso wantumi, efiri sɛ, na Herode suro Yohane, esiane sɛ onim sɛ ɔyɛ teneneeni ne kronkronni, nti ɔbɔɔ ne ho bane.
Sɛ otie no a, na waayɛ basaa nso na ɔpɛ sɛ otie no.
Na akwannya bi baa Herode awoda, berɛ a ɔtoo pono maa n’atitire ne n’asafohene ne Galilea mpanyimfoɔ.
Berɛ a Herodia ba baa baa apontoɔ he ase bɛsaeɛ he, ɔsɔɔ Herode ne n’ahɔhoɔ ani na hene he ka kyerɛɛ abaayaa he sɛ, “Bisa me nea wopɛ biaa, na mede bɛma wo.” Na ɔkaa ntam kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nea wobebisa biaa, sɛ oduru m’ahennie mu fa mpo a, mede bɛma wo.” Abaayaa he firii adi, na obisaa ne maame sɛ, “Ɛɛne ne memmisa?” Obuaa no sɛ, “Ka sɛ wopɛ Suboni Yohane ti.” Ntɛmaa, ɔsane kɔɔ hene he hɔ, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Mepɛ sɛ wode Suboni Yohane ti to apampaa so ma me seeseiaa.” Hene he werɛ hoo kɛse, nso ntam a ɔkaeɛ ne n’ahɔhoɔ he anim fɛreɛ nti, wampɛ sɛ ɔbɛkame no.
Ntɛmaa, hene he somaa abammɔfoɔ he mu sraani baako sɛ ɔmfa Suboni Yohane ti mmara.
Nti okotwaa ne ti afiase hɔ, na ɔde to apampaa so baeɛ, na ɔde maa abaayaa he.
Afei abaayaa he de maa ne maame.
Na Yohane asuafoɔ he tee asɛm he, bɛba bɛfaa n’amu he na bɛkɔpɛɛ no koraberɛ bodane bi mu.
Yesu maa Nnipa Mpem Nnum Aduane Afei asomafoɔ he twaa Yesu ho hyiaeɛ, na bɛkaa nea bɛayɔ ne nea bɛakyerɛkyerɛ nyinaa kyerɛɛ no.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hommra baabi a biaa nni mmɛhome kakra,” efiri sɛ na nnipa bebree oodi akɔ ne aba a na ɔmma benya kwane nnidi mpo.
Na bɛ ankasa bɛde kodoɔ he firii hɔ kɔɔ baabi a biaa nni.
Na nnipa bebree huu sɛ Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he ɔɔkɔ, na benim bɛ, na bɛyɛɛ ntɛm firii nkuro he nyinaa mu nante dii bɛ anim kane koduruu baabi a na Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he ɔɔkɔ he.
Ɔɔkɔ po he ano he, ohuu nnipadɔm kɛseɛ bi, na onyaa tema maa bɛ, efiri sɛ, ná bɛte sɛ nwane a benni hwɛfoɔ, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ kyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ nnoɔma bebree.
Berɛ a adeɛ saeɛ he, n’asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bɛkaa sɛ, “Ha yɛ baabi a biaa nni, na adeɛ nso asa, ma bɛnkɔ nkuro a atwa ahyia ha he bi mu nkɔtɔ bibi nni.” Nso obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Homma bɛ bibi nni.” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nti wosusu sɛ yebitumi akɔtɔ paanoo bebree a ne boɔ bɛyɛ paani abosome nsia akatua de ama nnipa yi nyinaa adi anaa?” Na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Paanoo meɛhe ne ho wɔ?
Honkɔ hwɛ,” na behuiɛ he bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Paanoo num ne nkyenam mmienu.” Na ɔhyɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛmma nnipa he nyinaa mmara na bɛntena nsensane he so akuo akuo.
Na bɛtenaa akuo akuo, ha ha ne aduonum aduonum.
Na ɔfaa paanoo num ne nkyenam mmienu he, ɔhwɛɛ soro, na ohyiraa so wieeɛ he obubuu paanoo he mu de maa n’asuafoɔ he sɛ bɛmfa mma nkurofoɔ he, na ɔkyɛɛ nkyenam mmienu he maa bɛ nyinaa.
Na biaa didi mmeeɛ.
Na bɛsesaa paanoo ne nkyenam mproprowa nkɛntɛne du mmienu ma ma.
Nnipa a bedii paanoo he na bɛ dodoɔ yɛ mmeema mpem num.
Yesu Nantee Nsuo so Amonom hɔaa, ɔmaa n’asuafoɔ he tenaa kodoɔ he mu dii kane kɔɔ Betsaida fam hɔ baabi ya asuogya, na ɔmaa nkurofoɔ he kɔeɛ.
Ogyaa bɛ kwane wieeɛ he, ɔkɔɔ bepɔ he so kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ.
Afei nwunu dwoeɛ a na kodoɔ he akoduru po he mfimfini he, na ɔno nkoaa ne ya fam hɔ.
Na ohuu sɛ mframa dendene ɔɔbɔ hyia bɛ na ama hare ayɛ dene ama bɛ he, ɔbaa bɛnkyɛne anɔpa tutuutu, na ɔɔnante po he so.
Ɔyɔɔ n’adwene sɛ ɔbetwam bɛ ho.
Nso behuu sɛ ɔɔnante po so he, bɛdwenee sɛ ɔyɛ samane na bɛteateam, efiri sɛ, bɛ nyinaa behuu no he, besuroeɛ.
Nso amonom hɔaa ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Homma ho akoma ntɔ ho yam, ɔyɛ me a; honnsuro.” Na ɔne bɛ kɔɔ kodoɔ he mu, na mframa he gyaeɛ.
Na yei yɛɛ bɛ nwanwa paa.
Afei nso, bɛante paanoo ho asɛm he ase, ɔnam bɛ akomapirim nti.
Yesu Saa Yadeɛ Genesaret Na betwaree nsuo he, bebeduruu Genesaret asaase so, na bɛtwee kosii po he ano.
Na befirii kodoɔ he mu sii fam he, nnipa huu no ntɛm so, na bɛyɔɔ ntɛm de ayarefoɔ firi mpɔtamu hɔ nyinaa totoo kɛtɛ so braa no baabi a bɛtee sɛ na ɔya biaa.
Na baabi a ɔkɔeɛ biaa, sɛ ɔyɛ nkuraase oo, nkurom oo, mfuom oo, bɛde ayarefoɔ beguu dwam hɔ, na bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ bɛbɛkaa n’ataadeɛ ano; na bɛ a bɛkaeɛ he nyinaa nyaa ayaresa.
Mpanyimfoɔ he Atetesɛm Na afei Farisifoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ bi a na befiri Yerusalem aba he twaa ne ho hyiaeɛ, behuu sɛ n’asuafoɔ he bi de nsa a ho agu fi oodi paanoo, ɔne sɛ bɛanhohoro bɛ nsa ho.
Nti Farisifoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he bisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne w’asuafoɔ nni mpanyimfoɔ atetesɛm he so yi, na bɛde nsa a ho agu fi ne didi yi?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Odi sɛ Yesaia hyɛɛ ho nyaatwomfoɔ ho nkɔm sɛ, ‘Nnipa yi de bɛ ano ne di me ni nso bɛ akoma deɛ ya akyirikyiri bɛsom me kwa, bɛkyerɛkyerɛ nipa ahyɛdeɛ sɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ pa.’ Hopo Nyankopɔn mmara na hokura nnipa atetesɛm.” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honam nyansakwane so po Nyankopɔn mmara sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a hobetumi adi ho atetesɛm so!
Na Mose kaa sɛ, ‘Di wo agya ne wo na ni,’ na ‘biaa a ɔbɛka asɛm bɔne afa n’agya anaa ne na ho he, ɔsɛ sɛ owu.’ Nso hoka sɛ, sɛ bi ka kyerɛ n’agya anaa ne na sɛ, ‘Mfasoɔ a nka wobenya afiri me so nyinaa yɛ Korban’ (ɔne sɛ afɔreɛ ma Nyankopɔn) a, hedeɛ na onni ho kwane sɛ ɔyɔ bibiaa ma n’agya anaa ne na.
Yei nti honam ho atetesɛm a hode agya nkyiremma so ato Nyankopɔn asɛm atwene.
Na hoyɔ nnoɔma a ɔte sei bebree.” Afei ɔfrɛɛ nnipadɔm he bio ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho nyinaa hontie me na honte aseɛ: Adeɛ biaa nni hɔ a ɔkɔ nipa mu a otumi gu ne ho fi; ɔyɛ deɛ ofiri nipa mu ba mmom ne tumi gu ne ho fi.” [Ma deɛ ɔwɔ aso he ntie.]
Berɛ a ogyaa nnipakuo he hɔ kɔ fie he, n’asuafoɔ he bisaa no asɛm a ɔkaeɛ he mu nkyeremu.
Na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Ho nso honte aseɛ?
Nti honnim sɛ adeɛ biaa nni hɔ a ɔkɔ nipa mu a otumi gu ne ho fi?
Nea nti a ɔte saa ne sɛ ɔnkɔ akoma he mu, na mmom yafunu mu, na apie akɔ yaanee mu.” (Na ɔkaa yei de tee aduane nyinaa ho.)
Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Nea ofiri nipa bi mu pie ne gu ne ho fi.
Na nipa mu, nipa akomam ne adwemmɔne firi ba: adwamammɔ, korɔno, awudie, awaresɛeɛ, aniberebereɛ, amumuyɔ, nnaadaa, honam akɔnnɔ, ahoɔyea, abususɛnka, ahomasoɔ, nkwaseasɛm.
Saa nnoɔma bɔne yi nyinaa firi nipa mu, na yeinom gu ne ho fi.” Siro-Foinikeni Baa he Gyidie Yesu firii hɔ he, osiim kɔɔ Tiro.
Ɔkɔɔ fie bi mu, na wampɛ sɛ biaa behu sɛ ɔya hɔ.
Nso wantumi amfa ne ho ansie.
Na ankyɛre biaa ne baa bi a honhom fi te ne ba baa mu tee ne nka, na ɔba bɛkotoo ne nane ase.
Na baa he yɛ Helani a ofiri Siro-Foinike.
Ɔsrɛɛ Yesu sɛ ontu honhom fi he mfiri ne ba baa he mu.
Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ baa he sɛ, “Ma mma nnidi nwie, na ɔnyɛ sɛ woto mma aduane ma nkramane.” Nso baa he maa no muaeɛ sɛ, “Owura, mpo nkramane a bɛda pono he ase he di mma he aduane ase mproprowa.” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Dea waka he nti kɔ—honhom fi he afiri wo ba baa he mu.” Nti ɔkɔɔ fie, na ohuu sɛ ne ba baa he da kɛtɛ so a honhom fi he afiri ne mu ampa.
Yesu Saa Beema bi a N’aso asi Yadeɛ Afei Yesu firii Tiro kuro mu baeɛ, na ɔfaa Sidon kɔ Galilea po ho Dekapoli mpɔtamu hɔ.
Na bɛde beema bi a n’aso asi a ɔwɔ haw ne kasaa mu braa no, na bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔmfa ne nsa nto ne so.
Ɔde no firii dɔm he nkyɛne kɔɔ kokoam baabi, na ɔde ne nsateaa hyehyɛɛ n’asum, afei ɔtoo ntasuo guu ne nsateaa so, na ɔde kaa beema kɛtrɛma.
Na ɔhwɛɛ soro, guu ahome na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Effata!” Asekyerɛ ne sɛ, “Ma no mmie.” Na amonom hɔaa n’aso bieeɛ, na ne kɛtrɛma mu nso goeɛ, na ɔkasaa kama.
Na Yesu hyɛɛ bɛ ketee sɛ bɛnnka nkyerɛ biaa, na mprɛ dodoɔ a ɔhyɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛnnka he, saa mprɛ dodoɔ heaa ne bɛde anigyeɛ bɔɔ asɛm he dawuro.
Ɔyɛɛ bɛ nwanwa boro so na bɛkaa sɛ, “Waayɔ nnoɔma nyinaa yie, ɔma deɛ n’aso asi mpo te asɛm na mum nso kasa.”
Ɔmaa Nnipa Mpem nnan Aduane Afei da foforɔ bi nso a ɔkɔ baa sɛ na nnipadɔm he nni hwee a bebedi he, Yesu frɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nnipadɔm yi ne me atena nnansa di, na seesei deɛ bɛyɛ me mmɔbɔ efiri sɛ bibiaa nni hɔ a aka a bebedi.
Sɛ mema bɛde kɔm kɔ a, bebetwa ahwe kwane so, binom nso firi akyirikyiri ne baeɛ.” N’asuafoɔ he bisaa no sɛ, “Ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na bi atumi anya aduane ama nnipadɔm yi serɛ yi so?” Obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Paanoo mmeɛhe ne howɔ?” Bɛkaa sɛ, “Nson.” Na ɔhyɛɛ nnipadɔm he maa bɛtenaa fam, na ɔfaa paanoo nson he na ɔdaa ase wieeɛ he, obubuu mu na ɔde maa n’asuafoɔ he sɛ bɛnkyɛ, na bɛkyɛ maa nnipadɔm he.
Na bɛwɔ nkyenam kakra bi nso, na ohyiraa so wieeɛ he, ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛnkyɛ ɔno nso.
Bedi mmeeɛ, na bɛsesaa aseɛ mproprowa nkɛntɛne nson ma ma.
Na nnipa he bɛyɛ mpem nnan.
Na ogyaa bɛ kwane maa bɛkɔeɛ.
Na amonom hɔaa ɔne n’asuafoɔ he tenaa kodoɔ he mu na bɛkɔɔ Damanuta mansinim.
Soro nsɛnkyerɛnne Afei Farisifoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne ne no bɛgyee akyinnye, bisaa no nsɛnkyerɛnne a ofiri soro, de sɔɔ no hwɛeɛ.
Na oguu ahome ne honhom mu bisaa sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne nneemmafoɔ bisa nsɛnkyerɛnne?
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, bɛmmfa nsɛnkyerɛnne biaa mma nneemmafoɔ.” Na ogyaa bɛ hɔ, na ɔtenaa kodoɔ he mu bio, tware kɔɔ nsuo he agya.
Farisifoɔ ne Herode Mmɔreka Na asuafoɔ he werɛ firii sɛ bɛbɛfa paanoo, na paanoo baako pɛ ne ya bɛ nkyɛne kodoɔ he mu.
Na ɔbɔɔ bɛ kɔkɔ sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Honya ahweyie Farisifoɔ mmɔreka ne Herode mmɔreka ho.” Bebisabisaa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Yenni paanoo he nti ne ɔɔka yei anaa?” Na Yesu huu saa he, obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne hooka sɛ honni paanoo?
Nti obesi nnɛ yi honhuu anaa hontee aseɛ?
Hoapirim ho akoma?
Howɔ ani, nso honnhu adeɛ?
Howɔ aso, nso honte asɛm?
Na honkae?
Berɛ a mebubuu paanoo num maa nnipa mpem num he, paanoo mproprowa nkɛntɛmma meɛhe ne hosesaeɛ?” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nkɛntemma dummienu.” Na paanoo nson a mede maa nnipa mpem nnan he, mproprowa nkɛntɛmma meɛhe ne hosesaeɛ?” Na bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nkɛntɛmma nson.” Afei obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Nti honnya ntee aseɛ?” Yesu Saa Nifirani Beema bi Yadeɛ Betsaida Na afie bɛbaa Betsaida.
Na nnipa binom de nifirani braa no, na bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔmfa ne nsa nka no.
Ɔsɔɔ nifirani he nsa, na odii n’anim de no firii akuraa he ase; na ɔde ntasuo kaa n’ani, na ɔde ne nsa guu ne so bisaa no sɛ, “Wohu bibi anaa?” Na beema he hwɛɛ soro kaa sɛ, “Mehu nnipa a bɛnenam hɔ, nso mehu bɛ sɛ nnua.” Afei Yesu de ne nsa guu n’ani he so bio; na ɔhwɛɛ adeɛ gyee, na ohuu adeɛ yie, na ne ho tɔɔ no.
Na Yesu gyaa beema he kwane maa ɔkɔɔ ne fie.
Na ɔɔkɔ he Yesu ka kyerɛɛ sɛ, “Nkɔ akuraa he ase seesei.” Nea Petro pae mu ka faa Yesu ho Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he toaa so kɔɔ Kaesarea Filipi nkuraa he ase; na bɛɛkɔ he, obisaa n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Nkurofoɔ dɛ meyɛ hwane?” Na bebuaa no sɛ, binom dɛ woyɛ “Yohane Suboni, binom nso dɛ woyɛ Elia, na binom nso ka sɛ, woyɛ adiyifoɔ he mu baako.” Obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Na ho nso hoka sɛ meyɛ hwane?” Petro yii ano sɛ, “Woyɛ Kristo he.” Na ɔhyɛɛ bɛ ketee sɛ bɛnnka ne ho asɛm nkyerɛ biaa.
Yesu hyɛɛ ne wuo ne ne wusɔreeɛ ho nkɔm Afei Yesu hyɛɛ aseɛ kyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, ɔsɛ sɛ Nipa Ba he fa amanehunu pii mu, na mpanyimfoɔ, asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he po no na beku no, na nnansa akyi he wasɔre bio.
Ɔkaa yeinom nyinaa maa mu daa hɔ pefee.
Na Petro de no kɔɔ nkyɛne, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ kaa n’anim.
Na ɔdanee n’ani hwɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he, na ɔkaa Petro anim sɛ, “Firi me so, Satan!
Efiri wonnwene Nyankopɔn adwene, na mmom nipa deɛ.” Ɔfrɛɛ nnipadɔm he ne n’asuafoɔ he, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ bi pɛ sɛ odi m’akyi a, ma ɔmpa ne ho akyi, na ɔmfa n’asennua, na onni m’akyi.
Na bɛ a bɛpɛ sɛ bɛbɔ bɛ nkwa ho bane he, bɛbɛhwere bɛ nkwa he, na bɛ a bɛbɛhwere bɛ nkwa me ne asɛmpa he nti he, bebenya nkwa.
Na sɛ benya wiase nyinaa na ɔhwere ne nkwa a, mmɛ mfasoɔ ne obenya?
Na mmɛ koraa ne bebetumi de ne nkwa so ka?
Na biaa a ɔbɛma n’ani awu me ne me nsɛm ho ya nnɛ mma, awaresɛefoɔ ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ mu he, ɔno nso ho bɛyɛ Nipa Ba he animuwo berɛ a ɔbɛba n’Agya animuonyam mu a abɔfoɔ kronkron he ka ne ho he.”
Afei nso ɔtoaa so ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem sɛ, binom gyina ha a bennwu kosi sɛ bebehu sɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie he aba tumi mu.” Yesu Sakraa ya Asuafoɔ he Anim Nna nsia akyi he, Yesu faa Petro ne Yakobo ne Yohane kaa ne ho, na odii bɛ anim foro kɔɔ bepɔ tentene bi so baabi a biaa nni.
Na ɔsakraeɛ bɛ anim, na ne ntaadeɛ hyerɛnn fitafita sene deɛ asaase so ntomasifoɔ biaa betumi ama no ayɛ.
Na Elia ne Mose yii bɛ ho adi kyerɛɛ bɛ, na bɛ ne Yesu ɔɔkasa.
Afei Petro ka kyerɛɛ Yesu sɛ, “Rabi, ɔyɛ sɛ yɛbɛtena ha; ma yɛnyɔ tenabea mmeɛnsa, wo deɛ baako, Mose deɛ baako na Elia nso deɛ baako.” Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ na onhu asɛm a ɔnka, efiri sɛ, bɛ ho dwirii bɛ paa.
Na afei mununkum bi bɛkataa bɛ so, na nne bi firi mununkum he mu kaa sɛ, “Yei ne me Dɔ Ba korɔ he; hontie no!” Na mpofirem bɛhwehwɛɛ hɔ he bɛanhu biaa, gye Yesu nkoaa.
Elia Mmaeɛ Na afei berɛ a beesiane afiri bepɔ he so asi fam he, ɔhyɛɛ bɛ ketee sɛ bɛnnka nea bɛahu he nkyerɛ biaa kosi sɛ Nipa Ba he benyane afiri awufoɔ mu.
Nti bɛde asɛm he hyɛɛ bɛ ho.
Na beebisabisa nea awufoɔ sɔreeɛ he kyerɛ.
Na afei bebisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne atwerɛfoɔ he ka sɛ ɔsɛ sɛ Elia di kane ba?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Elia bedi kane aba ampa abɛtoto nnoɔma nyinaa; na ɔyɛɛ dɛ ne bɛatwerɛ Nipa Ba he ho asɛm sɛ, otwa sɛ ohu amane pii na bebu no animtia?
Nso meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, Elia aba, bɛde nea bɛpɛ biaa ayɔ no, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ afa ne ho he.” Abɔfra bi a ɔwɔ honhommɔne nyaa ayaresa Bɛbaa asuafoɔ a aka he nkyɛne he, behuu nnipadɔm pii sɛ bɛne bɛ ya hɔ, na atwerɛfoɔ binom ne bɛ ɔɔgye akyinnye.
Na nnipadɔm he nyinaa huu no he, ntɛmaa, bɛ ho dwirii bɛ, na betuu mmirika kɔɔ n’anim kɔkyeaa no.
Obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne ho ne bɛ ɔɔgye ho akyinnye yi?” Nipa bi a ɔya nnipakuo he mu buaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, mede me ba beema braa wo; honhom bi ya ne so a ɔmma no ntumi nkasa, na berɛ biaa a ɔbɛba ne so he, ɔde no hwe fam, na n’ano twa ahuro, na ɔtwerɛ ne sẽ, na wasensene.
Na meka kyerɛɛ w’asuafoɔ he sɛ, bentu mfiri ne mu, nso bɛantumi.” Obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Ho nnemafoɔ a honni gyidie, me ne ho ntena nkosi da bɛ na ho anya gyidie?
Menya ho ho abotrɛ nkosi da bɛ’?
Homfa no mmra me.” Na bɛde abeemaa he braa no.
Na honhom he huu no he, ntɛmaa, soro kaa abeemaa he, na ɔhwee fam munimuniɛ, na ahuro betuaa n’ano.
Yesu bisaa ne papa he sɛ, “Mprɛ mmeɛhe ne yei ato no.” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Ofiri ne mmɔfrase.
Ɔtaa de no kɔto gya ne nsuo mu, sɛ ɔbɛsɛe no; nso sɛ wobetumi ayɛ bibi a, hu yɛ mmɔbɔ, na boa yɛ.” Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne wooka sɛ: Sɛ wobetumi a!
Te aseɛ sɛ bibiaa betumi ayɛ hɔ ama nea ɔgye di.” Ntɛmaa abɔfra he papa teaam sɛ, “Mewɔ gyidie, na baabi a mehia gyidie he boa me!” Berɛ a Yesu huu sɛ nnipadɔm bi abom de mmirika ɔɔba he, ɔkaa honhom he anim, ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wo honhom a womma abeemaa yi ntumi nkasa, na ɔnte asɛm, mehyɛ wo sɛ, firi ne mu firi kɔ, na mankɔhyɛ ne mu bio.” Na ɔteaam, na soro kaa abeemaa he kɛse paa wieeɛ he honhommɔne he firri ne mu, na ɔyɔɔ sɛnea wawu, nti nnipa he bi kaa sɛ, “Waawu.” Na Yesu sɔɔ ne nsa pagyaa no, na otumi gyinaa hɔ.
Ɔkɔɔ fie he, n’asuafoɔ he bisaa no kokoam sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne yɛantumi antutu honhom fi he?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ ɔnyɛ mpaebɔ ne [akɔnkyena] a, bibiaa nni hɔ a obetumi atutu no.” Yesu sane hyɛɛ ne Wuo ne ne Sɔreeɛ ho Nkɔm Befirii hɔ kɔeɛ, na bɛfaa Galilea.
Na ɔmpɛ sɛ biaa behu sɛ ɔɔkɔ; efiri sɛ ná ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Bebeyi Nipa Ba he ama de no ahyɛ nnipa nsa, na bebeku no, na nnansa akyi he waasɔre bio.” Bɛante nea ɔɔka he ase, nso ná besuro sɛ bebebisa no.
Hwane ne Kɛseɛ?
Afei bɛbaa Kapernaum; na ɔya fie he, obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne ná hoogye ho akyinnye berɛ a ná yɛnam kwane so he?” Nso bɛyɛɛ komm, efiri sɛ, bɛnam kwane so ɔɔba he bɛgyee bɛ ho bɛ ho akyinnye faa nea ɔyɛ kɛseɛ paa ho.
Ɔtenaa ase, frɛɛ dummienu he ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nea ɔpɛ sɛ ɔyɛ kannifoɔ he, ɔsɛ sɛ ɔto ne ho mpan, na ɔnsom biaa.” Afei ɔde akwadaa ketewa bi begyinaa bɛ mfimfini; na ɔfaa no sii ne basa so he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nea ɔgye nkumaa yi mu baako me dini mu he gye me, na nea ɔgye me he, ɔnnyɛ me ne ɔgye me na mmom ɔgye nea ɔsomaa me he nso.” Nipa foforɔ bi a Otu Ahonhommɔne Yohane ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, yehuu sɛ bi de wo dini ootu ahonhommɔne, na yɛbɔɔ mmɔdene sɛ yebesi no kwane, efiri sɛ ɔnnka yɛ ho.” Nso Yesu kaa sɛ, “Honnsi no kwane; na biaa nni hɔ a ɔyɔ tumidwuma me dini mu a ɔno akyi heaa obetumi aka me ho asɛm bɔne.
Nea ɔnko ntia yɛ he ya yɛ afa.
Na nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, biaa a ɔbɛma ho nsuo kuruwa baako mpo anom, sɛ hokura Kristo dini nti he, n’akatua ɔmmɔ no da.” Sɔhwɛ a ɔde bɔne mu “Sɛ ho mu bi to nkumaa yi a bɛgye me di yi mu baako sintidua a, afanyinam sɛ bɛde boɔ keseɛ paa ato no kɔno mu, na bɛato mo atwene po mu.
Sɛ wo nsa to wo sintidua a, twa twene; ɔyɛ ma wo sɛ wode nsa sini bɛkɔ nkwa mu sene sɛ wode wo nsa mmienu bɛkɔ Gehenna, gya a onnum da he mu, [faako a bɛ a bɛya hɔ he mu nnokommoa nwu na hɔ gya he nnum da.]
Na sɛ wo nane to wo sintidua a, twa twene; ɔyɛ sɛ wode nansini bɛkɔ nkwa mu sene sɛ wowɔ nane mmienu na bɛbɛto wo ato Gehenna gya mu, [faako a bɛ a bɛya hɔ he mu nnokommoa nwu na hɔ gya he nnum da.]
Na sɛ w’ani to wo sintidua a, tu firi hɔ; ɔyɛ ma wo sɛ, wode ani baako bɛkɔ nkwa mu sene sɛ wowɔ ani mmienu na bɛbɛto wo atwene Gehenna gya mu, faako a bɛ a bɛya hɔ he mu nnokommoa nwu na hɔ gya he nnum da.
“Na gya ne bɛde bɛhyɛ biaa nkyene.
Nkyene yɛ; nso sɛ nkyene dɛ firi mu a, wobɛyɛ dɛ ahyɛ no nkyene?
Honnya nkyene ho mu, na ho ne ho ho ntena asomdwie mu.”
Awaregyaeɛ ho Nkyerɛkyerɛ Afei Yesu firii saa bea hɔ kɔɔ Yudea mpɔtamu hɔ Yordan akyi.
Na nnipadɔm pii betwaa ne ho hyiaa bio; na sɛdeɛ na ɔtaa yɔ he, ɔkyerɛkyerɛeɛ.
Farisifoɔ bi baeɛ, na bebisa de sɔɔ ne hwɛeɛ sɛ, “Mmara ma kwane sɛ beema bi gyae ne yerɛ?” Obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne Mose hyɛɛ ho?” Bɛkaa sɛ, “Mose maa ho kwane sɛ betumi twerɛ awaregyaeɛ krataa de gyae baa he.” Nso Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho akoma pirim nti ne ɔtwerɛɛ saa ahyɛdeɛ yi maa ho.
Na ofiri adebɔ mfitiaseɛ he, ‘Nyankopɔn yɔɔ beema ne baa.’ ‘Yei nti, beema begya n’agya ne ne na hɔ, na ɔne ne yerɛ aka abom, na bɛ mmienu he ayɛ honam baako.’ Ɔba saa a bɛnna so nyɛ mmienu, na mmom bɛyɛ honam baako.
Nti nea Nyankopɔn aka abom he, mma nipa biaa ntetem.” Afei bɛ ya fie he, asuafoɔ he bisaa yei ho asɛm bio.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ bi gyae ne yerɛ, na ɔware foforɔ a, na wasɛe awareɛ ɔnam baa he a ogyae no he nti; na sɛ baa he nso gyae ne kunu na ɔware foforɔ a wasɛe awareɛ.” Yesu hyiraa Mmɔfra Nketewa Na nnipa bebree de mmɔfra nketewa ɔɔbra no sɛ ɔde ne nsa bɛka bɛ; na asuafoɔ he kaa bɛ anim dendenndene.
Afei Yesu huiɛ he, n’ani annye ho, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Homma mmɔfra he mmara me nkyɛne; honnsi bɛ kwane; na bɛ a bɛte sei ne Nyankopɔn ahennie he yɛ bɛ dea.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho, nea ɔnnye Nyankopɔn ahennie he sɛ abɔfra he nkɔ mu da.” Na ɔmaa bɛ so kɔɔ soro de ne nsa guu bɛ so, na ohyiraa bɛ.
Defoɔ he Na osiim sɛ ɔɔkɔ baabi he, beema bi de mmirika bebuu nkotodwe n’anim, na obisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ pa, mmɛ ne menyɔ na manya daa nkwa?” Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Ɛɛne nti ne wofrɛ me papa?
Biaa nyɛ papa, gye Nyankopɔn nkoaa.
Wonim ahyɛdeɛ he, ‘Nni awu; Nsɛe awareɛ; Mmɔ korɔno; Nni adansekunumu; Nsisi biaa; Di w’agya ne wo na ni.’ ” Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, mefiri me mmɔfra ase adi yei nyinaa so.” Na Yesu hwɛɛ no he, ɔdɔɔ no, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Aaka wo adeɛ baako; kɔ, kɔtɔno nea wowɔ, na fa sika he ma ahiafoɔ, na wobenya agyapadeɛ soro; na afei bra bedi m’akyi.” Ɔtee yei he, ne ho dwirii no, na ɔde awerɛhoɔ kɔeɛ, efiri sɛ, na ɔwɔ ahonyadeɛ pii.
Na Yesu too n’ani hwɛɛ nnipa a na bɛya hɔ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Hwɛ dene a ɔbɛyɛ ama adefoɔ sɛ bɛbɛkɔ Nyankopɔn ahennie he mu!” Na nsɛm yi haa asuafoɔ he adwene.
Nso Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ bio sɛ, “Mmɔfra, honhwɛ dene a ɔyɛ sɛ bi bɛkɔ Nyankopɔn ahennie he mu!
Ɔmmerɛ ma yoma sɛ obewura paneɛ tokuro mu sene sɛ sikani bɛkɔ Nyankopɔn ahennie mu.” Asɛm yi yɛɛ bɛ nwanwa kɛse, na bɛkaa sɛ, “Sɛ saa ne ɔteɛ dea, hwane ne obetumi anya nkwa?” Yesu hwɛɛ bɛ, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Nnipa fam deɛ, ontumi nyɛ hɔ, na ɔnyɛ Nyankopɔn fam; na Nyankopɔn fam deɛ bibiaa betumi ayɛ hɔ.” Petro fitii aseɛ ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Hwɛ, yɛagya bibiaa hɔ abedi w’akyi.” Yesu kaa sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem, biaa nni hɔ a wagya fie anaa nua mmeema, anaa nua mmaa, anaa maame, anaa papa, anaa mma ne nsaase, ɔnam me ne asɛmpa he nti, na onya no mmɔho ha, saa wiase yi mu a, fie, nua mmeema, nua mmaa, nanom, ne mma, anaa nsaase, na taa nso ka ho, ne nna a ɔbɛba he mu daa nkwa.
Nso adikanfoɔ bebree bɛka akyi, na akyikafoɔ bedi kane.” Yesu hyɛɛ ne Wuo ne ne Sɔreeɛ ho Nkɔm Mprɛnsa so Na bɛnam kwantempɔno he so ɔɔkɔ Yerusalem, na Yesu adi bɛ anim kane; ɔyɛɛ bɛ nwanwa, na bɛ a bedi akyire he suroeɛ.
Ɔde dummienu he kɔɔ nkyɛne bio, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ kaa nea ɔbɛto no, sɛ, “Honhwɛ, yɛɛkɔ Yerusalem, na bɛde Nipa Ba he bɛhyɛ asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he nsa, na bebebua no kumfɔ; na afei bɛde no ahyɛ Amanamane mufoɔ nsa; bebedi ne ho fɛw, na bɛato ntasuo agu ne so na bɛatwa no mmaa, na bɛaku no, na nnansa akyi wasɔre bio.” Yakubu ne Yohane Adesrɛ Yakubu ne Yohane, Sebedeo mma he baa ne nkyɛne bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, yɛpɛ sɛ nea yebebisa wo biaa woyɔ ma yɛ.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne hopɛ sɛ meyɔ ma ho?” Na bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ma yɛ mu baako ntena wo nifa, na baako ntena wo benkum w’animuonyam mu.” Nso Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honnim nea hoobisa he.
Hobetumi anom kuruwa a menom he, anaa hobetumi abɔ asu a bɛde bɔ me he?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Yebetumi.” Afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Kuruwa a menom he, hobɛnom; na asubɔ a bɛde bɔ me he, bɛde bɛbɔ ho; nso sɛ hobɛtena me nifa anaa me benkum deɛ, ɔnyɛ me ne mede ma, na ɔya bɛ a bɛasiesie ama bɛ deɛ.” Na du he tee yei he, bɛ bo hyɛɛ aseɛ fuu Yakobo ne Yohane.
Nti Yesu frɛɛ bɛ ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honim sɛ Amanamane mufoɔ he mu deɛ, bɛ a bebu bɛ sɛ bɛ sodifoɔ he hyɛ bɛ so, na bɛ akɛsefoɔ he yɛ bɛ so ka-a-nka-bi.
Nso ɔsɛ sɛ ɔba saa ho mu; na biaa a ɔpɛ sɛ ɔyɔ kɛseɛ ho mu he, otwa sɛ ɔyɔ ho akoa, na nea ɔpɛ sɛ ɔdi kane ho mu biaa he, otwa sɛ ɔyɔ ho nyinaa ho akoa, na Nipa Ba he amma sɛ bɛnsom no, na mmom ɔbɛsomeeɛ, na ɔde ne nkwa ayɛ agyedeɛ ama nnipa bebree.” Nifirani Bartimeo Ayaresa Bɛbaa Yeriko.
Na ɔne n’asuafoɔ he ne nnipadɔm bi oofiri Yɛriko he, na Timeo ba Bartimeo, nifirani adesrɛfoɔ he te kwane nkyɛne.
Na ɔtee sɛ ɔyɛ Yesu Nasareni he ne ootwam he, ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ teaam kaa sɛ, “Yesu, Dawid ba, hu me mmɔbɔ!” Nnipa bebree teateaa no sɛ ɔnyɔ komm; nso ɔteateaam kɛse sɛ, “Dawid Ba, hu me mmɔbɔ!” Yesu gyinaa hɔ dinn kaa sɛ, “Homfrɛ no mmra ha.” Na bɛka kyerɛɛ nifirani he sɛ, “Ma w’akoma ntɔ wo yam; sɔre, ɔɔfrɛ wo.” Nti ɔtoo n’ataadeɛ guiɛ, ohuru gyinaeɛ, na ɔkɔɔ Yesu nkyɛne.
Afei Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ ne wopɛ sɛ meyɔ ma wo?” Nifirani he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Me Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, ma menhu adeɛ bio.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kɔ, wo gyidie asa wo yadeɛ.” Amonom hɔaa, ohuu adeɛ, na odii n’akyi kwane he so.
Yesu Wuraa Yerusalem Nkunimdie so Berɛ a bɛɛbɛne Yerusalem he, na beduruu Betfage ne Betania he, baabi a hɔ bɛne Ngo Bepɔ he, ɔsomaa n’asuafoɔ he mu mmienu na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔ akuraa a ɔya ho anim he mu, na howura kuro he mu pɛ, hobehu sɛ bɛamantam afunumu ba bi a biaa ntenaa ne so da ya hɔ, honsane no, na homfa no mmra.
Sɛ bi bisa ho sɛ, ‘Ɛɛne nti ne hooyɔ yei a,’ honka sɛ, ‘Awurade hia no, hoka saa a ɔntwentwɛne ne nane ase koraa na wama hode no aba ha.’ ” Befiri hɔ kɔeɛ, na bekohuu afunumu ba a bɛde no abɔ pono bi nkyɛne ya abɔntene, kwane he mu.
Na beesane no he, bɛ a begyina hɔ he bi bisaa bɛ sɛ, “ ‘Ɛɛne ne nti ne hoosane afunumu ba yi?” Bɛkaa nea Yesu dɛ bɛnka he, na bɛmaa bɛ kwane ma bɛfaa no kɔeɛ.
Afei bɛde afunumu he braa Yesu, na bɛtoo bɛ ntaadeɛ guu afunumu he so, na Yesu tenaa ne so.
Nnipa bebree de bɛ ntaadeɛ sesɛɛ kwane he so, na binom nso twitwaa nwura de sesɛɛ kwane he mu.
Na afei bɛ a bedi kane ne bɛ a bedi akyire he teateaam sɛ, “Hosiana!
Nhyira ne nea ɔɔba Awurade dini mu!
Nhyira ne yɛ nana Dawid ahennie a ɔɔba he!
Nhyira nka sorosoro Nyankopɔn.” Yesu domee borɔdoma dua he Na owuraa Yerusalem, na ɔkɔɔ asɔrefie hɔ; na ɔhwɛɛ nnoɔma a ɔya hɔ he nyinaa hyiaeɛ he, na adeɛ asa nti ɔne dummienu he kɔɔ Betania.
Adeɛ kyeeɛ a befirii Betania ɔɔba he, na kɔm de Yesu.
Yesu too n’ani, na ohuu brɔdoma dua bi a ahahane ya so sɛ ɔya akyirikyiri; na ɔkɔ kɔhwɛɛ sɛ ebia aduaba bi ya so a. Oduruu ho he, wanhu hwee, gye ahahane nkoaa, efiri sɛ na berɛ a borɔdoma so nya nnuruiɛ.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wonnso aba bio na bi anya bi adi.” Na n’asuafoɔ he teeɛ.
Yesu dwiraa asɔredane he mu Afei bɛbaa Yerusalem.
Na ɔkɔɔ asɔrefie hɔ na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ pamoo bɛ a bɛɛtɔno ne bɛ a bɛɛtɔ nnoɔma asɔrefie hɔ, na ɔdanee sika sesafoɔ apono, ɔne bɛ a bɛtɔno mmorɔnoma he nkonnwa butubutuiɛ.
Na wamma biaa kwane amma wansoa adeɛ antwam asɔrefie hɔ.
Ná ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ sɛ, “Bɛntwerɛɛ sɛ, ‘Bɛbɛfrɛ me fie mpaebɔ fie ama amane nyinaa’?
Nso hode ayɛ akorɔmfoɔ bɔno.” Na asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ he ne atwerɛfoɔ he teeɛ he, bɛkɔɔ so hwehwɛ kwane a bɛbɛfa so aku no nso, na besuro no, efiri sɛ, ne nkyerɛkyerɛ he twee nnipakuo he nyinaa adwene.
Na nnwunu dwoeɛ he, Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he firii kuro he mu.
Borɔdoma dua he ho adesua Adeɛ kyeeɛ a na Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ ootwam he, behuu borɔdoma dua he sɛ atwintwam firi ne soro kosi ne ne nhini so.
Na Petro kaeɛ, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Rabi, hwɛ!
Borɔdoma dua he a wodomee no he atwintwam.” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Honnya gyidie Nyankopɔn mu.
Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem sɛ, sɛ hoka kyerɛ bepɔ yi sɛ, ‘Tutu kɔ soro na kɔhwe po mu,’ na sɛ hoannye akyinnye ho akoma mu, na mmom hogye di sɛ nea hoaka he bɛyɔ hɔ a, ɔbɛyɔ hɔ ama ho.
Nti meeka akyerɛ ho, nea hobebisa no mpaebɔ mu biaa, honnye nni sɛ hoanya na ɔbɛyɛ ho deɛ.” “Berɛ biaa a hobɛsɔre sɛ hoobɔ mpaeɛ he, homfa bɛ a howɔ bibi tia bɛ bɔne nkyɛ bɛ, na ho soro Agya nso de ho mfomsoɔ akyɛ ho.” [Na sɛ hoamfa ankyɛ a, ho Agya a ɔya soro nso mfa ho mfomsoɔ nkyɛ ho.]
Bebisaa Yesu Tumi a ɔde yɔ Nsɛnkyerɛnne ho Asɛm Na afei Yesu baa Yerusalem bio.
Na ɔnenam asɔrefie hɔ he, asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ, atwerɛfoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne na bebisaa no sɛ, “Tumi a wode yɔ yeinom firi he?
Hwane ne maa wo saa tumi yi sɛ fa yɔ saa?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Mebisa ho asɛm baako; honnyi me ano, na mɛkyerɛ ho tumi korɔ a mede yɔ yei.
Yohane asubɔ he, na ofiri soro anaa ofiri nipa?
Honnyi ano.” Bɛgyee bɛ ho bɛ ho akyinnye sɛ, “Sɛ yɛka sɛ, ‘Ofiri soro a,’ ɔbɛka sɛ, ‘Mmɛ nti ne hoannye no anni?’ Na yɛnam he ne kɔka sɛ, ‘Ofiri nipa’?” Na besuro nnipadɔm he efiri sɛ na bɛ nyinaa bebu Yohane sɛ ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ diyifoɔ.
Nti bebuaa Yesu sɛ, “Yennim.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Saa deɛ a me nso menka tumi korɔ a mede ɔɔyɔ yeinom nkyerɛ ho.”
Mfantoho a ɔfa hwɛsofoɔ timɔdenfoɔ binom ho Afei Yesu firii aseɛ de mfantoho kasa kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Beema bi yɔɔ bobe turo, gyee ho hyiaeɛ, tuu nsa-kyi-amena, na osii awɛmfoɔ dane; afei ɔde turo he hyɛɛ ahwɛfoɔ nsa, na otuu kwane kɔɔ kuro foforɔ so.
Afei twaberɛ duruiɛ he, ɔsomaa akoa bi kɔɔ ahwɛfoɔ he hɔ sɛ, ɔnkɔgyegye ne kyɛfa a ɔya bobe turo he mu nnɔbae he mmra.
Nso bɛkyee no boroo no, na bɛpamoo no maa ɔkɔɔ nsapan.
Na ɔsomaa akoa foforɔ kɔɔ bɛ nkyɛne; yei nso bɛbobɔɔ ne ti ho piraa no, na bedidii no atɛm.
Na ɔsomaa foforɔ, na ɔno nso bekuu no.
Saa ne ɔsomaa afoforɔ bebree; na bɛboroo binom na bekuu binom nso.
Na aaka nipa baako a na ɔyɛ ne dɔ ba.
Ɔno ne nea otwa toɔ a ɔsomaa no kɔɔ bɛ nkyɛne kaa sɛ, ‘Bɛde anidie bɛma me ba beema yi.’ Nso ahwɛfoɔ he keka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, ‘Ehẽẽ!
Deɛ obedidi adeɛ he di; hommra ma yenku no, na agyapadeɛ he abɛyɛ yɛ deɛ.’ Nti bɛkyee no, kuu no, na bɛtoo no twenee bobe turo he akyi.
Nea bɛayɔ yi hosusu sɛ mmɛ ne bobe turo wura he de bɛyɔ bɛ?
Ɔbɛba abɛsɛe ahwɛfoɔ he, na ɔde bobe turo he ahyɛ nnipa foforɔ nsa.
Nti, honnkenkanee atwerɛ yi da: ‘Boɔ a adansifoɔ he poeɛ he abɛyɛ tweasotiboɔ titire; Awurade ne ayɔ ne saa na ɔyɛ yɛ ani so nwanwa’?” Berɛ a behuu sɛ ɔyɔɔ saa mfantoho yi tiaa bɛ he, bɛpɛɛ sɛ bɛbɛkye no, nso na besuro nnipadɔm he.
Nti bɛgyae no, na bɛkɔeɛ.
Toɔ tua ho asemmisa Na afei bɛsomaa Farisifoɔ ne Herodefoɔ bi ne nkyɛne sɛ benkosum no fidie ne kasaa mu.
Na bɛba bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, yenim sɛ woka nɔkorɛ, na wonyɛ nyiyimu, efiri sɛ, wonhwɛ nnipa anim mmu ntɛnkyea, na mmom wokyerɛkyerɛ Nyankopɔn kwane nɔkorem.
Ɔyɛ sɛ yetua toɔ ma Kaesare anaa ɔnyɛ?
Yentua anaa yenntua?” Na onim bɛ nyaatwom nti ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne hoosɔ me ahwɛ?
