Hommra me denare baako na menhwɛ.” Na bɛde baako baeɛ.
Na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Hwane ti ne da so yi, na hwane abodini ne da so yi?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Kaesare deɛ.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hommfa nea ɔyɛ Kaesare deɛ mma Kaesare, na hommfa nea ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn deɛ mma Nyankopɔn.” Na ne ho yɛɛ bɛ nwanwa paa.
Wusɔreɛ ho asemmisa Sadukifoɔ a bɛ gyidie kyerɛ bɛ sɛ wusɔreɛ nni hɔ he mu binom baa Yesu nkyɛne bebisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, Mose twerɛ maa yɛ sɛ, ‘sɛ beema bi nua wu gya ne yerɛ, ná onni ba a, beema he nware kunafoɔ he ná ɔnwo mma mma ne nua he.’ Anuanom nson bi tenaa ase; nea odi kane he wareeɛ na owuiɛ he na onni mma.
Na afei nea ɔtɔ so mmienu he waree baa he, na owuiɛ a na ɔno nso nni mma; na nea ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he nso saa.
Nnipa nson he nyinaa waree no, na wannya mma.
Awieeɛ koraa he, baa he ankasa nso wuiɛ.
Sɛ ɔkɔ ba saa a, wusɔreɛ he mu he, baa he bɛyɛ hwane yerɛ?
Efiri sɛ nnipa nson he nyinaa aware no.” Yesu bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Nea hooka yi te ne honte aseɛ yie.
Honnim atwerɛ he, na honnim Nyankopɔn tumi nso; efiri sɛ, wusɔreɛ akyi he nnipa ɔnware, na bɛmmfa biaa mma awareɛ, na mmom nnipa ɔnware, sɛnea soro abɔfoɔ nso nware he.
Na ɔfa awufoɔ sɔreeɛ ho he, honnkenkaneɛ ya Mose nwoma he mu, asɛm a ofiri nkyɛkyerɛ he mu baaa Mose nkyɛne a Nyankopɔn ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Mene Abraham Nyankopɔn, Isak Nyankopɔn, ne Yakobo Nyankopɔn’?
Ɔnyɛ awufoɔ Nyankopɔn na mmom ateasefoɔ Nyankopɔn; hoamane koraa.” Ahyɛdeɛ a odi kane Atwerɛfoɔ he mu baako twe bɛnee hɔ, na ɔtee sɛ bɛɛgye bɛ ho bɛ ho akyinnye, na ohuu sɛ wabua bɛ yie he, obisaa no sɛ, “Ahyɛdeɛ mɛneɛ ne di ne nyinaa kane?” Na Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Nea odi kane ne sɛ, ‘Tie, O Israel; Awurade yɛ yɛ Nyankopɔn, Awurade yɛ baako, fa w’akoma nyinaa, ne wo kra nyinaa, ne w’adwene nyinaa, ne w’ahoɔdene nyinaa dɔ Awurade wo Nyankopɔn.’ Nea ɔtɔ so mmienu ne sɛ, ‘Dɔ wo yɔnko sɛ wo ho.’ Ahyɛdeɛ biaa nni hɔ a ɔkyɛne yeinom.” Na atwerɛfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wabua no yie, Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, woaka no nɔkorem sɛ, ‘Awurade yɛ baako, na n’akyi biaa nni hɔ’; ɔne sɛ yɛde yɛ akoma nyinaa, ne yɛ adwene nyinaa, ne yɛ ahoɔdene nyinaa bɛdɔ Awurade, na afei nso bi bɛdɔ ne yɔnko sɛ ne ho—yei ho hia kyɛne hyeɛ afɔdeɛ ne afɔdeɛ ahodoɔ nyinaa.” Berɛ a Yesu huu sɛ wabua no yie he, ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wo ne Nyankopɔn ahennie he mu ntwe koraa.” Yei akyi he, biaa antumi ammisa no asɛm biaa bio.
Asemmisa a ɔfa Dawid ba ho Berɛ a Yesu ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ asɔredane mu hɔ he, obisaa sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne atwerɛfoɔ he kaa sɛ Kristo he yɛ Dawid ba?
Dawid heaa nam Honhom Kronkron so paem kaa sɛ, ‘Awurade ka kyerɛɛ m’Awurade sɛ, “Tena me nsa nifa so, kosi sɛ mede w’atamfoɔ bɛhyɛ wo nane ase.” ’ Sɛ Dawid he ankasa frɛɛ no Awurade a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na wayɛ ne ba?” Na nnipadɔm he de anigyeɛ tiee no.
Atwerɛfoɔ ho Kɔkɔbɔ Ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ he ɔkaa sɛ, “Honhwɛ ho ho yie atwerɛfoɔ he ho, bɛ a bɛpɛ sɛ bɛde ntaadeɛ atentene nenam, sɛ bɛde anidie bɛkyea bɛ dwa so, na bɛbɛtena nkonnwa papa so hyia adane mu, ne nkonnwa a ɔya anim ne mpanyini tenabea ya apontoɔ ase!
Bɛde apoobɔ fa akunafoɔ agyapadeɛ nyinaa, na bɛbɔ mpaeɛ tentene sɛ nnipa behu bɛ.
Yei nti, bebenya afobuo kɛseɛ.” Baa Kunafoɔ Hiani he Afɔrebɔ Ɔtenaa ase baabi a na n’ani hwɛ fotobea hɔ, na ɔhwɛɛ nnipadɔm he sɛ bɛde sika oogu fotoɔ he mu.
Adefoɔ bebree de sika pii guu mu.
Nso baa kunafoɔ hiani bi deɛ ɔde nkaprɛ mma mmienu a ɔnsom bo biaa beguu mu.
Afei ɔfrɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorɛ mu sɛ, baa kunani hiani yi de nea ɔkyɛne biaa deɛ ne abɛto fotoɔ yi mu, efiri sɛ, nnipa yi nyinaa firi nea bɛanya ama abu so mu ne ayi bi aba, na ɔno deɛ, ofiri ne hia mu de nea ɔwɔ nyinaa, n’asetenadeɛ nyinaa, abegu mu.”
Asɔrefie he sɛeɛ ho nkɔmhyɛ Na afei Yesu firii asɔredane he mu firiiɛ he, n’asuafoɔ he mu baako ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, hwɛ aboɔ akɛseɛ ne adane nwanwasono yi!” Afei Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Woahu adane nwanwasono yi?
Boɔ baako mpo ɔnka boɔ foforɔ so ha; bebedwiri ne nyinaa agu fam.” Berɛ a na ɔte Ngo Bepɔ so, faako a ɔne hyiadane he di animhwɛ he, Petro, Yakobo, Yohane ne Andreo bisaa no kokoam sɛ, “Ka kyerɛ yɛ, mmɛ berɛ ne yei bɛyɔ hɔ, na mmɛ ne bɛyɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne sɛ saa nnoɔma yi nyinaa ɔɔbɛba mu?” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honhwɛ yie na biaa amma hoanyera.
Nnipa bebree de me dini bɛba abɛka sɛ, ‘Mene no!’ Na bɛbɛma nnipa bebree amane afiri kwane he ho.
Sɛ hote ko ne akosɛm a, hommma ho akoma ntu; ɔsɛ sɛ ɔba saa, nso na awieeɛ he nnuruiɛ.
Na amane bɛsɔre atia amane, na ahennie asɔre atia ahennie; asaasewosoɔ bɛba mmeammea; kɔm bɛba.
Yei yɛ awoko yeyaa mfitiaseɛ.
Yesu hyɛɛ Taa ho Nkɔm “Ho deɛ, honhwɛ ho ho yie, efiri sɛ bebeyi ho ama abadwafoɔ; na bɛbɛhwe ho hyia adane mu; na me nti, hobegyina amradofoɔ ne ahemfo anim, de ayɛ adanseɛ ama bɛ.
Na otwa sɛ bɛpae mu ka asɛmpa he kyerɛ amane nyinaa kane.
Sɛ bɛde ho kɔ sɛ beekodi ho asɛm ayi ho ama a, honnwennwene deɛ hobɛka ho; na deɛ bɛde bɛma ho saa berɛ he ɔnoaa ne honka, efiri sɛ, ɔnyɛ ho ne hokasa, na mmom ɔyɛ Honhom Kronkron ne bɛkasa afa ho mu.
Na afei nua beyi nua ama na bɛaku no; na agya ayi ne ba ama, na mma bɛsɔre atia awofoɔ, na bɛama bɛaku awofoɔ he.
Na me dini nti nnipa nyinaa bɛtane ho.
Nso nea obegyina akosi awieeɛ he ne benya nkwa.
Akyiwadeɛ a ɔbɔ Mane “Nso berɛ a hobehu sɛ bɛde akyiwadeɛ a ɔma mane da mpan he asi baabi a ɔnsɛ sɛ osi he (ma nea ɔɔkenkane he nte aseɛ), hedeɛ ma bɛ a bɛya Yudea nwane nkɔ mmepɔ so; Mmma nea ɔya dane atifi he nsi fam, saa ara nso ne ɔnsɛ sɛ osi kɔ fie hɔ kɔfa bibi firi hɔ; nea ɔya afuom nsane nnkɔfa ataadeɛ ngusoɔ.
Na saa da he apemfoɔ ne bɛ a bɛma mmɔfra nofoɔ nnue!
Nti hommɔ mpaeɛ na amma awɔ berɛ.
Na nna he mu, amanehunu a ofiri Nyankopɔn adebɔ ahyɛaseɛ de besi nnɛ bi mmaa da, na bi nso ɔmma bio bɛba.
Na sɛ Awurade antwa nna he so tia a, nipa biaa onya nkwa; nso bɛ a bɛapa bɛ he na bɛayi bɛ he nti, bɛatwa nna he so tia.
Na sɛ biaa ka kyerɛ ho da he sɛ, ‘Hwɛ!
Kristo he di!’ Anaa ‘Hwɛ, Ɔya do a,’ honye nni, Kristo atorɔfoɔ ne adiyifoɔ atorɔfoɔ bɛba na bɛayɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne ne anwanwadeɛ, na sɛ obetumi a, nka bɛde adaadaa bɛ a bɛayi bɛ he.
Nso honyɛ krado; maadi kane aka ne nyinaa akyerɛ ho.
Nipa Ba he mmaeɛ Na nna he mu, amanehunu he akyi, Awia beduru sum, na bosome ɔnhyerɛn na nsoromma bɛtete afiri soro agu na soro tumi bɛwoso.
Na afei bebehu Nipa Ba he sɛ osiane mununkum mu tumi ne animuonyam kɛseɛ mu.
Afei ɔbɛsoma abɔfoɔ he, na bɛakɔboaboa bɛ a bɛayi bɛ afiri atifi kɔpem anaafoɔ, apieeɛ kɔpem atɔeɛ, ofiri asaase ano de kosi soro ano.
Borɔdoma dua ho adesua Honsua bibi mfiri borɔdoma dua he ho mfantoho he mu: Sɛ ne mmane he yɛ frɔmfrɔm na oyi n’ahahane he a, na hoahu sɛ pɛ berɛ abɛne.
Saa ne sɛ ho nso hohu sɛ saa nnoɔma yinom oosisi a, hoahu sɛ waabɛne, na ɔya pono ano pɛɛ.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, saa awoɔntoatoasoɔ yi ontwam, gye sɛ yei nyinaa sisi ansa.
Soro ne asaase betwam, nso me nsɛm deɛ ontwam da.
Hia a ohia sɛ yɛnwɛne “Na ɔfa da he ne dɔnhwere he ho deɛ, biaa nnim, soro abɔfoɔ oo, Ba he oo, biaa nnim, gye Agya he nkoaa.
Honhwɛ yie, homma ho ani nna hɔ; efiri sɛ, honnim da a saa berɛ he bɛba.
Ɔte sɛ beema bi a ootu kwane, na oofiri fie he, ɔde ne nkoa sisii nnwuma ahodoɔ ano, na ɔhyɛɛ ponohwɛfoɔ sɛ ɔnwɛne.
Nti homma ho ani nna hɔ, efiri sɛ honnim berɛ a fiewura he bɛba, sɛ ɔbɛba anwummerɛ oo, dasuom oo, dasuom akokɔbɔmmereɛ oo, anaa ahemakye oo, honnim.
Saa nti sɛ hoamma ho ani anna hɔ a, ɔbɛba mpofirem abɛto ho sɛ hoadeda.
Na deɛ meeka akyerɛ ho he, meeka akyerɛ biaa: Homma ho ani nna hɔ.”
Bɛbɔɔ Yesu ti so pɔ sɛ bebeku no Na aka nnaanu na Twam ne Apiti afahyɛ he aduru.
Na asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he ɔɔpɛ nyansa kwane bi afa so akye Yesu, na bɛaku no; na bɛkaa sɛ, “Yɛnnyɔ yei afahyɛ berɛ yi mu, anyɛ saa a, basabasa bɛsɔre nnipa he mu.” Baa bi sraa Yesu ngo ya Betania Berɛ a Yesu ya Betania, Simon kwatani he fie he, na ɔte adidiiɛ he, baa bi de aduhwam a ne boɔ ɔdene a ogu kɔntoa mu baeɛ, na obie so hwiee aduhwam he guu Yesu ti mu.
Na nnipa a bɛya hɔ he mu binom de abufuo keka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ɔsɛe aduhwam he sei berɛ a nka bebetumi atɔno aduhwam yi anya sika a ɔboro paani bosome du akatua, na bɛde sika he ama ahiafoɔ?” Na benwinwii tia baa he.
Na Yesu kaa sɛ, “Honnyae no; mmɛ nti ne hooha no yi?
Nea waayɔ yi yɛ ma me.
Na ahiafoɔ deɛ bɛya ho nkyɛne daa, na hobetumi ayɔ bɛ papa berɛ biaa a hopɛ, na me deɛ menntena ho nkyɛne daa.
Waayɔ deɛ obetumi; wasra me nipadua de ɔɔtwɛne me sie da.
Nɔkorɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho, wiase baabi a bɛbɛpaem aka asɛmpa he, bɛbɛka deɛ waayɔ yi de akae no.” Yuda gye tomm sɛ obeyi Yesu ama Afei Yuda Iskariot a ɔyɛ dummienu he mu baako, kɔɔ asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he nkyɛne ne bɛ kɔ kasaa sɛ obeyi Yesu ama bɛ.
Bɛteeɛ he, bɛ ani gyee paa, na bɛhyɛɛ no bɔ sɛ bɛbɛma no sika.
Nti ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ hwehwɛɛ kwane a ɔbɛfa so ayi no ama.
Yesu ne asuafoɔ he dii Twam Afahyɛ Afei da a odi kane a bedi paanoo a mmɔreka nnim he, berɛ a beku Twam dwane he, Yesu asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne bebisaa no sɛ, “Hefa ne wopɛ sɛ yekosiesie ma wodi Twam he?” Nti ɔsomaa n’asuafoɔ he mu mmienu, ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔ kuro he mu, na beema bi behyia ho a ɔsõ asuhina; honni n’akyi, na baabi a obewura biaa, honka nkyerɛ fiewura he sɛ, ‘Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he dɛ yemmisa sɛ, Hefa ne m’ahɔhodane a me ne m’asuafoɔ bedi Twam he ya?’ Ɔbɛkyerɛ ho dane kɛseɛ bi abrosane he so a bɛasiesie mu ayɛ no krado.
Honnyɔ ahosiesie mma yɛ hɔ.” Nti asuafoɔ he firii adi kɔɔ kuro he mu, na bibiaa siiɛ sɛdeɛ na waaka akyerɛ bɛ he, na besiesie Twam aduane he.
Adidie a otwa toɔ Nnwunu dwoeɛ he, Yesu ne dummienu he baeɛ.
Na bɛtenaa ase a beedidi he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho, ho a ho ne me oodidi he mu baako beyi me ama.” Na bɛyɛɛ basaa, na bebisaa no mmaako mmaako sɛ, “Ɔyɛ me a’?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ɔyɛ dummienu yi mu baako, nea ɔne me de paanoo ɔɔbɔ ayowa baako mu he a, na Nipa Ba he ɔɔkɔ deɛ, sɛdeɛ bɛatwerɛ afa ne ho he, nso deɛ ɔnam ne so beyi no ama he nnue!
Nka ɔyɛ ma no sɛ bɛanwo no mpo.” Awurade Adidie ahyɛaseɛ Na beedidi he, Yesu faa paanoo, na ohyiraa so he, obuu mu de maa bɛ kaa sɛ, “Honye, yei ne me nnipadua.” Afei ɔfaa kuruwaa, na ɔdaa ase he, ɔde maa bɛ, na bɛ nyinaa bɛnom mu.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Yei ne me mogyaa a ɔyɛ apam foforɔ he mogyaa a nnipa bebree nti beehwie agu.
Nɔkorɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, mennom bobe aba bio de kosi da a mɛnom no foforɔ Nyankopɔn ahennie he mu.” Yesu hyɛɛ Nkɔm sɛ Petro bɛpa no Bɛtoo ayeyie dwom, na ɔno akyi he befirii adi kɔɔ Ngo Bepɔ so.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho nyinaa hobeyi me ama; na bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Mɛbɔ dwanhwɛfoɔ he, na nwantene he ahwete.’ Na me wusɔreɛ akyi he, medi ho anim akɔ Galilea.” Petro ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ biaa pa wo mpo a, me deɛ mempa wo.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ.
“Meeka akyerɛ wo nɔkorem nnɛ sɛ, anadwo yiaa, ansa na akokɔ bɛ bɔne mprenu he na woayi me ama mprɛnsa.” Na Petro kaa no anibereɛ so sɛ, “Sɛ otwa sɛ me ne wo wu koraa a, mempa wo.” Na bɛ nyinaa bɛkekaa saa.
Yesu bɔ Mpaeɛ Getsemane Bɛkɔɔ bea bi a bɛfrɛ no Getsemane; na ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Hontena ha na menkɔbɔ mpaeɛ.” Ɔfaa Petro ne Yakubu ne Yohane kaa ne ho, na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ teeteeɛ na odii awerɛhoɔ.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Me werɛ aho kɛse de ɔɔkɔ wuo mu mpo; honnka ha, na honnwɛne.” Na ɔkɔɔ animu kakra he, ɔde ne ho too fam na ɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ sɛ, sɛ obetumi a nka berɛ he ntwa ne ho nkɔ.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Abba, Agya, bibiaa nso wo yɔ; yi kuruwaa yi firi me so; nso nyɛ deɛ mepɛ na mmom deɛ wopɛ.” Na ɔba behuu sɛ bɛadeda; na obisaa Petro sɛ, “Ei!
Simon, wada?
Nti woantumi anwɛne dɔnhwere baako mpo?
Honnwɛne na hommɔ mpaeɛ na hoankɔ sɔhwɛ mu.
Honhom he pɛ paa deɛ, nso honam he ɔmmerɛ.” Na bio, ofiri hɔ kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ korɔ heaa.
Na ɔsane behuu bɛ sɛ bɛadeda bio, efiri sɛ, na bɛ ani kum kɛse, nti bɛanhu muaeɛ a bɛmfa mma no.
Na afei ɔbaa ne mprɛnsa so bebisaa bɛ sɛ, “Hogu so ɔɔda dwodwo ho ho?
Aayɛ yie!
Berɛ he aso sɛ bɛde Nipa Ba he hyɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ nsa.
Honnsɔre ma yɛnkɔ.
Honhwɛ, deɛ obeyi me ama he abɛne.” Yesu Yima ne ne Kyeɛ Amonom hɔaa, ogu so ɔɔkasa he, Yuda, dummienu he mu baako beduruiɛ; na nnipadɔm a bekitakita asekane ne mmaa a befiri asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ he mu ne no ne baeɛ.
Afei na deɛ oobeyi no ama he akyerɛ bɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne bi sɛ, “Deɛ mɛfe n’ano he, ɔno a, honnkye no, mfa no mfiri hɔ nkɔ, honhwɛ yie na wammfiri ho nsa.” Nti ɔbaeɛ he, ɔkɔɔ ne nkyɛne ntɛm so kaa sɛ, “Rabi!” Na ɔfee n’ano.
Afei bɛsɔɔ ne mu, na bɛkyee no.
Na bɛ a na begyina bɛnkyɛne hɔ he mu baako twee ne sekane na otwaa sɔfo panyini akoa he aso.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hode asekane ne mmaa ne afiri adi ɔɔbɛkye me te sɛ nea meyɛ korɔmfoɔ?
Daa na me ne ho ya asɔrefie a meekyerɛkyerɛ, nso hoankye me.
Nso aaba saa sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a twerɛsɛm he bɛbam.” Bɛ nyinaa begyaa no hɔ dwaneeɛ.
Na abranteɛ bi di n’akyi a ɔde nwera nkoaa ne akata n’adagya so.
Bɛsɔɔ ne mu a nka bɛɛpɛ no akye no, na ogyaa ne nwera he hɔ de ne ho kwaterekwa dwane kɔeɛ.
Bɛde Yesu kogyinaa Abadwafoɔ he Anim Bɛde Yesu kɔmaa sɔfo panyini; na asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he, mane he mu mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he ahyia.
Na Petro dii n’akyi akyirikyiri koduruu sɔfo panyini he adi hɔ; na ɔne abammɔfoɔ he tenaa gya ho toeɛ.
Afei asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne badwa he nyinaa hwehwɛɛ adanseɛ tia Yesu na bɛagyina so aku no; nso bɛanya bi.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, nnipa bebree dii adansekunumu tia no, nso bɛ adanseɛ he ankɔ bɛnkorɔ mu.
Binom sɔre dii adanseɛ tiaa no sɛ, “Yɛtee sɛ ɔɔka sɛ, ‘Mɛsɛe asɔredane a bɛde nsa ayɔ yi, na nnansa so, mesi deɛ bɛamfa nsa anyɔ.’ ” Nso asɛm yei ho mpo, bɛ adanseɛ he anhyia.
Na sɔfo panyini he sɔre gyinaa bɛ anim bisaa Yesu sɛ, “Wonni mmuaeɛ biaa?
Ɛɛne ho ne beedi adanseɛ atia wo yi?” Nso ɔyɛɛ komm na wammua.
Bio, sɔfo panyini he bisaa no sɛ, “Wone Kristo he, Nhyira Wura Ba he anaa?” Yesu kaa sɛ, “Me a; na ‘hobehu Nipa Ba he sɛ ɔte Tumfoɔ he nsa nifa’ na ‘ɔnam soro mununkum mu ɔɔba.’ ” Afei sɔfo panyini he tetee n’ataadeɛ mu, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne yɛda so hia adansefoɔ?
Hoate n’abususɛm he!
Hoadwene ne sɛ?” Bɛ nyinaa bebuu no fɔ sɛ ɔfata wuo.
Binom hyɛɛ aseɛ totoo ntasuo guu ne so, kyekyeree n’ani, na bɛbobɔɔ no ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Hyɛ nkɔm!” Abammɔfoɔ he nso bɛfaa no kɔeɛ, na bɛkɔhwee no.
Petro paa Yesu Afei berɛ a na Petro ya aseɛ hɔ he, sɔfo panyini he mmaawa he mu baako baa hɔ.
Na ohuu Petro sɛ ɔɔto gya he, ɔhwɛɛ no gyee kaa sɛ, “Wo nso na woka Nasareni Yesu he ho.” Nso wannye antom, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Mennim na mente deɛ wooka yi ase.” Na ofirii adi, kogyinaa aboboɔ ano hɔ.
Na akokɔ bɔnooɛ.
Abaawa he huu no bio he, ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ ka kyerɛɛ bɛ a begyina hɔ he sɛ, “Beema yei yɛ bɛ mu baako.” Saa berɛ yi nso, Petro annye antom.
Na ɔyɛɛ kakra he, bɛ a begyina hɔ he ka kyerɛɛ Petro sɛ, “Woka bɛ ho ampa, na woyɛ Galileani.” Na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ domeeɛ, na ɔkaa ntam sɛ, “Mennim beema a hooka n’asɛm yi.” Saa berɛ he akokɔ bɔno mprenu so.
Na Petro kae sɛ Yesu aka akyerɛ no sɛ, “Ansa na akokɔ bɛbɔno mprenu he na woapa me mprɛnsa.” Nti ne werɛ hoeɛ, na osuiɛ.
Bɛde Yesu kogyinaa Pilato anim Na afei, adeɛ kyee anɔpa tutuutu he, asɔfoɔ mpayimfoɔ, mane he mu mpanyimfoɔ, atwerɛfoɔ ne abadwafoɔ he nyinaa tuu agyina.
Bɛkyekyeree Yesu de no kɔeɛ na bɛde no kɔhyɛɛ Pilato nsa.
Pilato bisaa no sɛ, “Wone Yudafoɔ hene he?” Oyii no ano sɛ, “Yoo!
Wone wooka.” Na asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he de nsɛm bebree too Yesu so.
Pilato bisaa no bio sɛ, “Wonni anoyie biaa’?
Hwɛ nsɛm ahodoɔ a bɛde ɔɔto wo so.” Nso Yesu amma mmuaeɛ biaa, na yei yɛɛ Pilato nwanwa.
Pilato de Yesu maa sɛ bɛmmɔ no asennuam Na oduru afahyɛ so a Pilato yi deduani a bebebisa no de no ma bɛ.
Na beema bi a bɛfrɛ no Baraba ne amammɔfoɔ a bɛnam atuateɛ so dii awu gu afiase hɔ.
Nti nnipadɔm he baeɛ, na bɛka kyerɛɛ Pilato sɛ ɔnyɛ mma bɛ sɛdeɛ daa ɔyɔ he.
Na Pilato bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Hopɛ sɛ megyaa Yudafoɔ hene he ma ho anaa?” Ná onim sɛ ahoɔyea nti ne asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ de yii no maeɛ.
Nso asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he tutu guu nnipadɔm he asom sɛ onyi Baraba mmom.
Pilato bisaa bɛ bio sɛ, “Hedeɛ mmɛ ne hopɛ sɛ memfa nyɔ beema he a hofrɛ no Yudafoɔ hene he?” Bɛteaam sɛ, “Bɔ no asennua mu!” Pilato bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Abɛ bɔne ne waayɔ?” Na bɛteaam kɛse paa sɛ, “Bɔ no asennua mu!” Na ɔnam sɛ na Pilato pɛ sɛ ɔyɛ nea nnipadɔm he pɛ nti, oyii Baraba maa bɛ, na bɛhwee Yesu wieeɛ he ɔde no maa bɛ sɛ bɛmɔ no asennua mu.
Asraafoɔ he dii Yesu ho fɛw Afei asraafoɔ he de no firii hɔ kɔɔ adi hɔ (Ammrado abankɛseɛ mu hɔ), na bɛfrɛɛ asrafokuo he nyinaa hyiaeɛ.
Na bɛde ataade kɔkɔɔ hyɛɛ no, na bɛde nkasɛe yɔɔ kyɛ hyɛɛ no.
Na befirii aseɛ kyeaa no sɛ, “Yudafoɔ hene yɛma wo amo!” Bɛde demmire hwee ne tim, too ntasuo guu ne so, na bebuu nkotodwe kotõõ no.
Bedii ne ho fɛw wieeɛ he, bɛworɔɔ ataadeɛ kɔkɔɔ he de ɔnoaa n’ataadeɛ hyɛɛ no.
Na bɛde no kɔɔ sɛ bɛɛkɔbɔ no asennuam.
Bɛbɔɔ Yesu Asennuam Na bɛhyɛɛ Simon, Kireneni bi a ofiri baabi ootwam, a ɔyɛ Aleksandro ne Rufo papa, sɛ ɔnsoa n’asennua he.
Afei bɛde Yesu baa bea bi a bɛfrɛ no Golgota (a asekyerɛ ne Tikankuro).
Na bɛde bobesa a bɛde aduhwam afra mu maa no; nso wannom.
Na bɛbɔɔ no asennuam, na bɛkyekyɛɛ ne ntoma mu, na bɛtwee so ntonto de huu nea otwa sɛ biaa nya.
Afei berɛ a na aabɔ anɔpa nnɔn nkron he bɛbɔɔ no asennuam.
Na bɛatwerɛɛ ne soboɔ bɔɔ n’atifi sɛ, “Yudafoɔ hene” Na bɛbɔɔ ɔne akwamukafoɔ mmienu asennuam, baako ya ne nifa ne baako ya ne benkum.
[Na twerɛ he baa mu sɛ, “Bɛkanee no fraa mmaratofoɔ.]
Na bɛwosoo bɛ ti kaa sɛ, “Mhõõ!
Wo a wosɛe asɔredane na wode nnansa si, gye wo ho na si firi asennua he so ɛ!” Saa ne asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ he ne atwerɛfoɔ dii ne ho fɛw kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Ɔgye afoforɔ, nso ontumi nnye ne ho.
Ma Kristo he, Israel Hene he nsiane mfiri asennua he so sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɔ a yebehu na yɛagye adi.” Bɛ a bɛbɔɔ bɛ ne no asennua mu he nso huruu no.
Yesu wuo Na oduruu awigyina he, sum duruu asaase nyinaa so, kosii nnɔn mmeɛnsa.
Nnɔn mmeɛnsa duruiɛ he, Yesu de nne kɛseɛ teaam sɛ, “Eli, Eli, lama sabaktani?” Asekyerɛ ne, “Me Nyankopɔn, me Nyankopɔn, mmɛ nti ne woapo me?” Bɛ a begyina hɔ he bi teeɛ he, bɛkaa sɛ, “Hontie, ɔɔfrɛ Elia.” Afei bi tuu mmirika de sapɔ kɔbɔɔ nsa kekakeka mu, de hyɛɛ abaa so de maa no sɛ ɔnnom, kaa sɛ, “Hontwɛne mma yɛnhwɛ sɛ Elia bɛba abeyi no asi fam a.” Afei Yesu teaam dendenndene, na ogyaam.
Na asɔredane he mu ntwamtam he tee mmienu firii soro kosii aseɛ.
Afei berɛ a asraafoɔ ha so panyini a na ogyina hɔ a na n’ani tua no he, huu kwane a ɔfaa so gyaam he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Nɔkwasɛm di, nipa yi yɛ Nyankopɔn Ba!” Ná mmaa bi nso gyina akyirikyiri ɔɔhwɛ, bemu bi ne Maria Magdalene ne Yakoko a ɔyɛ kumaa ne Yose maame Maria Salome.
Berɛ a na ɔya Galilea he, na saa nnipa yi taa di n’akyi som no, afei nso na mmaa foforɔ binom gyina hɔ ɔɔhwɛ nea ɔɔkɔ so he a na bedi Yesu akyi aba Yerusalem.
Besiee Yesu amu Afei nwunu dwoeɛ, na esiane sɛ na saa da he yɛ ahosiesie da, kyerɛ sɛ, ɔyɛ da a odi homeda anim nti, Yosef a ofiri Arimatea, na odi mu badwa he mu a na ɔno nso ɔɔhwɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie he kwane, de akokoɔduro kɔɔ Pilato anim kɔsrɛɛ no Yesu amu he.
Na Pilato adwene mu yɛɛ no naa sɛ waawu anaa, nti ɔkɔfrɛɛ sraani panyini he, bisaa no sɛ waawu dada anaa.
Na afei ɔte firii sraani panyini he hɔ sɛ waawu he, ɔde amu he ma Yosef.
Na Yosef kɔtɔɔ nwera pa, na oyii no too hɔ de nwera pa he kyekyeree no, na ɔde no too nna a bɛatwa no botane he mu.
Na afei omunii boɔ de too nna he ano.
Nso Maria Magdalene ne Yose maame Maria kɔɔ so hwɛɛ faako a bɛde no toeɛ.
Yesu wusɔreɛ Na homeda twaam he, Maria Magdalene ne Yakubu maame Maria ne Salome kɔtɔɔ aduhwam sɛ bɛde ɔɔkɔsra Yesu.
Na nnawɔtwe da a odi kane anɔpatutuutu he, berɛ na awia oopieɛ he, bɛkɔɔ nna he so.
Na bebisabisaa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Hwane ne bemini boɔ he afiri nna he so ama yɛ?” Bɛhwɛeɛ he, behuu sɛ boɔ kɛseɛ a ɔda adamena he ano he amini afiri hɔ.
Beewura nna he mu he, behuu abeemaa bi a ɔhyɛ ataadeɛ tentene fitaa te nifa so hɔ, na bɛ akoma tuiɛ.
Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hommma ho akoma ntu, hoohwehwɛ Nasareni Yesu nea bɛbɔɔ no asennua mu he.
Wanyane, na onni ha.
Hwɛ, baabi a bɛde no toeɛ.
Na honkɔ, nkɔka nkyerɛ n’asuafoɔ ne Petro sɛ oodi ho anim kane Galilea, hɔ ne ho behu no, sɛdeɛ ɔka kyerɛɛ ho he.” Bepieeɛ, na bedwane firii adamena he mu efiri sɛ na hu ne suro ahyɛ bɛ so, na bɛanka hwee ankyerɛ biaa, efiri sɛ na besuro.
Marko Asɛmpa awieeɛ a odikane [Na deɛ na wahyɛ bɛ nyinaa bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ a bɛ ne Petro ya hɔ he.
Na akyire yi Yesu ankasa de somaa bɛ, firi apieeɛ kosii atɔeɛ sɛ bɛmpae mu nka daa nkwa nsɛm a ɔyɛ kronkron na ɔnsɛe da he.]
MARKO ASƐMPA AWIE A ƆTƆ SO MMIENU Yesu yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ Maria Magdalene [Na afei berɛ a Yesu sɔre firii awufoɔ mu nnawɔtwe da a odi kane he, anɔpa tututuutu he, odii kane yii ne ho kyerɛɛ Maria Magdalene, nea otuu ahonhommɔne nson firi ne mu he.
Nti ɔkɔ kɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ a na bɛ ne no ya hɔ he, berɛ a na beesu di awerɛhoɔ he.
Nso bɛtee sɛ ɔte ase na waahu no he, bɛannye anni.
Yesu yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ mmienu bi Yei akyi he, Yesu yii ne ho adi tebea foforɔ mu kyerɛɛ bemu mmienu, berɛ a na bɛnam ɔɔkɔ kuro he mu.
Na bɛsane kɔɔ kuro he mu kɔka kyerɛɛ nkaeɛ he, nso bɛangye anni.
Yesu maa Asuafoɔ he Ahyɛdeɛ Akyire yi oyii ne ho kyerɛɛ dubaako he berɛ a na bɛte adidi pono ho, na ɔkaa bɛ anim ɔnam gye a bɛannye anni ne bakoma dene nti, efiri sɛ bɛannye bɛ a bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ waasɔre he anni.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔ wiase nkɔbɔ asɛmpa he dawuro nkyerɛ abɔdeɛ nyinaa.
Nea ɔbɛgye adi na hobɛbɔ no asu he benya nkwa, na nea wannye anni he bebebu no fɔ.
Na nsɛnkyerɛnne yeinom bedi bɛ a bɛbɛgye adi he akyi, bɛde me dini betutu ahonhommɔne, bɛbɛka kasa foforɔ.
Bɛde bɛ nsa bɛfa awɔ, na sɛ bɛnom awuduro mpo a, ɔnyɔ bɛ hwee, bɛde bɛ nsa begu ayarefoɔ so, na bebenya ayaresa.” Yesu Soro kɔ Na afei Awurade Yesu ne bɛ kasa wieeɛ he, Nyankopɔn maa no so kɔɔ soro kɔtenaa ne nsa nifa so.
Na bɛkɔɔ abɔntene kɔbɔɔ asɛm he dawuro baabiaa, na Awurade de bɛ yɔɔ adwuma na ɔde nsɛnkyerɛnne a odi akyire hyɛɛ asɛm he dene.]
NNIANIMU Luka Asɛmpa he ma yehu Yesu sɛ Israel Agyenkwa ne adasamma nyinaa Agyenkwa a bɛhyɛɛ ne ho bɔ he.
Luka atwerɛ sɛ, Awurade Honhom afrɛ Yesu sɛ “ɔmɛka asɛmpa he nkyerɛ ahiafoɔ” ; nea ɔya Asɛmpa he mu titire ne adwenpa a ɔda adi fa ahiafoɔ ho.
Anigyesɛm di akotene paa, ne titire nwoma he ahyɛaseɛ a ɔbɔ Yesu ba ho dawuro, na okowie Yesu sorokɔ ho ne n’awieeɛ a ɔkasa fa ne sorokɔ ho.
Twerɛfoɔ he kasa fa Kristosom gyidie ho.
Nea ɔyɔeɛ a som he mu trɛeɛ, na afei Yesu sorokɔ akyi he, nea ɔyɔeɛ a onyiniiɛ.
Twerɛfoɔ korɔ heaa ka saa nsɛm yi nso ya Asomafoɔ He Nnwuma he mu.
Nwoma yi wɔ afa ahodoɔ mmienu , na okura nsɛm bi a Luka Asɛmpa he mu nkoaa ne ɔya a bi ne abɔfoɔ nnwom a bɛtoeɛ, ne nnwanhwɛfoɔ he nsra a bɛkɔsraa Yesu berɛ a bɛwoo no he, kɔ a abeemaa Yesu kɔɔ asɔrefie, mfatoho asɛm a ɔka faa Samariani a ɔyɛ yɔnko pa he ho, ne agya he dɔ a ɔdaa no adi kyerɛɛ ne ba kohwini he ho.
Asɛmpa he mu baabiaa, besi mpaebɔ, Honhom Kronkron, mmaa kyɛfa ya Yesu som adwuma mu, ne Nyankopɔn bɔne fakyɛ so dua.
MU NSƐM Nnianimu :- Suboni Yohane ne Yesu awoɔ ho asɛm :—: Suboni Yohane dwumadie :- Yesu asubɔ ne ne sɔhwɛ :—: Yesu badwam dwumadie a odii no Galilea abɔntene so :—: Yesu firii Galilea kɔɔ Yerusalem :—: Nnawɔtwe a otwa toɔ ya Yerusalem ne nkuro a ɔbɛne hɔ :—: Awurade wusɔreɛ, n’ahoyie, ne ne sorokɔ he :-
Luka twerɛɛ Nwoma he maa Teofilo Esiane sɛ nnipa bebree afa ato bɛ ho so sɛ bɛbɛkyerɛ nsɛm a abam yɛ ntam he nnidisoɔ nnidisoɔ, sɛnea bɛ a befiri mfitiaseɛ de bɛ ani huiɛ na bɛyɛɛ asɛm he ho asomfoɔ he de abra yɛ he nti, Nimuonyamfoɔ Teofilo, me nso maabɔ me tim pɔ sɛ nea meaa mahwehwɛ mu defedefe firi ahyɛaseɛ he, meetwerɛ no nnidisoɔ nnidisoɔ de ama wo, na woahu nɔkorɛ a ɔfa nnoɔma a bɛakyerɛkyerɛ wo he ho.
Suboni Yohane awofoɔ Yudea hene Herode berɛ so he, na sɔfo bi ya hɔ a bɛfrɛ no Sakaria a ofiri Abia asɔfokuo he mu, na ne yerɛ yɛ Aaron mma mmaa he mu baako a ne dini de Elisabet.
Na bɛ mmienu nyinaa tene Nyankopɔn anim di Awurade mmara ne n’atemmudeɛ ne n’atenenedeɛ nyinaa so pɛpɛɛpɛ a asɛm biaa nni bɛ ho.
Na benni ba, efiri sɛ, na Elisabet yɛ bonyini, na bɛ mmienu nyinaa nso anyinyini paa.
Suboni Yohane awoɔ ho nkɔmhyɛ Berɛ a oduruu Sakaria asɔfokuo so sɛ bɛne bɛyɔ asɔfodwuma he, na Sakaria ɔɔyɔ n’asɔfodwuma Nyankopɔn anim he, na sɛnea asɔfodwuma ho amanneɛ teɛ he, bɛtwee ntonto yii no sɛ ɔno ne nkɔ Awurade kronkronbea hɔ nkɔhye aduhwam.
Na berɛ a ɔɔhye aduhwam he, na nnipadɔm he nyinaa ya adihɔ ɔɔbɔ mpaeɛ.
Awurade bɔfoɔ begyinaa aduhwam afɔrebokyia he nifa yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ no.
Berɛ a Sakaria huu no he, ne ho yeraa no na ɔbɔɔ hu.
Nso bɔfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ.
“Nsuro, Sakaria, efiri sɛ bɛatie w’adesrɛ, na wo yerɛ Elisabet bɛwo babeema ama wo, na woato ne dini Yohane.
W’ani bɛgye na woadi ahurusie, na nnipa pii hobɛsɛpɛ bɛ, ɔnam n’awoɔ he nti; efiri sɛ, ɔbɛyɛ kɛseɛ Awurade anim.
Nso ɔnsɛ sɛ ɔnom bobesa ne nsãdene biaa, na Honhom Kronkron bɛhyɛ no mã firi ne maame yam; na ɔbɛdane Israel mma pii asane aba Awurade bɛ Nyankopɔn nkyɛne.
Na ɔde Elia honhom ne tumi bedi Awurade anim na wadane agyanom akoma aba bɛ mma so asoɔdenfoɔ akɔ teneneefoɔ adwene ho, na wasiesie mane he ama Awurade.” Afei Sakaria bisaa bɔfoɔ he sɛ.
“Maabɔ akɔkora na me yerɛ nso mfie kɔ animu paa.
Afei ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na nea wooka yi abam?” Bɔfoɔ he buaa no sɛ, “Mene Gabriel, Nyankopɔn somfo a wasoma me sɛ me ne wo mmɛkasa na menka nnoɔma yi ho asɛmpa nkyerɛ wo.
Hwɛ!
Wobɛtɔre mum, wontumi nkasa kosi da a yeinom bɛba mu, efiri sɛ, woannye me nsɛm a ɔbɛba mu berɛ a bɛahyɛ mu he anni.” Saa berɛ he nyinaa na nkurofoɔ he ɔɔtwɛne Sakaria, na ɔyɛɛ bɛ nwanwa sɛ wakyɛre kronkronbea hɔ saa.
Nso ɔbaeɛ he wantumi ne bɛ ankasa, na behuu sɛ wakohu bibi kronkronbea hɔ, na ɔde ni ti ne ne nsa yɔɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne kyerɛɛ bɛ efiri sɛ wantumi ankasa.
Afei nna a Sakaria de ɔɔsom he baa awieeɛ he, ofirii hɔ kɔɔ ne fie.
Nna yi akyi he, ne yerɛ Elisabet nyinsɛneeɛ; na ɔde ne ho siee abosome nnum, na ɔkaa sɛ: “Yei ne kwane a Awurade afa so ne me adi berɛ a wabɛhwɛ me sɛ oobeyi m’ahohora nnipa anim afiri hɔ he mu.” Yesu awoɔ ho nkɔmhyɛ Na Elisabet anyinsɛne mu bosome a ɔtoɔ so nsia he, Nyankopɔn somaa bɔfoɔ Gabriel kɔɔ Galilea kuro a bɛfrɛ no Nasaret mu, babunu bi a bɛde no ama beema bi a bɛfrɛ no Yosef a ofiri Dawid fie asiwa he nkyɛne; na babunu he dini ne Maria.
Ɔkɔɔ ne nkyɛne he, ɔkyea no kaa sɛ, “Asomdwie nka wo, wo a bɛadom wo, Awurade ka wo ho.” Na asɛm he maa Maria ho dwirii no yie, na ɔdwendwenee ho sɛ, “Mmɛ nkyea di?” Nti bɔfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ: “Nsuro Maria, na woanya Nyankopɔn anim adom; na hwɛ, wobenyinsɛne na woawo babeema, na woato no dini Yesu.
Ɔno ne bɛyɛ kɛse, na bɛbɛfrɛ no Sorosoroni he Ba; na Awurade Nyankopɔn de n’agya Dawid ahennwa bɛma no, na obedi Yakob fie so hene afebɔɔ, na n’ahennie ɔmma awieeɛ da.” Maria bisaa bɔfoɔ he sɛ, “Ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na yei aba mu berɛ a me ne beema nnaa da?” Afei bɔfoɔ he buaa no sɛ, “Honhom Kronkron bɛba wo so, na Sorosoroni he tumi bɛkata wo so.
Yei nti ne bɛbɛfrɛ nea wobɛwo no he Kronkron, Nyankopɔn Ba.
Hwɛ!
Wo busuani Elisabet nso anyinsɛne babeema ne mmerewaberɛ mu, na ɔno a bɛfrɛ no bonyini he anyinsɛne bosome nsia di; efiri sɛ, Nyankopɔn fam deɛ, bibiaa nni hɔ a ontumi mma mu.” Afei Maria kaa sɛ.
“Hwɛ!
Meyɛ Awurade afenaa!
Ɔmmra mu sɛdeɛ waka he.” Na bɔfoɔ he firii ne nkyɛne kɔeɛ.
Maria kɔsraa Elisabet Afei Maria sɔree saa nna he mu de ahoɔhare kɔɔ Yuda kuro bi a ɔda bepɔ so mu, ɔkɔɔ Sakaria fie, na ɔkyeaa Elisabet.
Na Elisabet tee Maria nkyea heaa pɛ, akokoa a ɔhyɛ ne yafunu mu he huruiɛ; na Honhom Kronkron hyɛɛ Elisabet mã, na ɔde nne kɛseɛ teaam sɛ, “Bɛahyira wo mmaa nyinaa mu, na bɛahyira wo yafunu mu aba!
Mmɛ akwannya ne manya sɛ m’Awurade maame aba me nkyɛne yi?
Hwɛ!
Wo nkyea twaa m’asomaa pɛ ne akokoa a ɔya me yam he de anigyeɛ kɛseɛ huruiɛ.
Na nhyira nso ne nea wagye adi, efiri sɛ nea ofiri Awurade hɔ a bɛabɛka akyerɛ no he biaa bɛyɛ hɔ.” Maria kaa sɛ.
“Me kra kamfo Awurade, na m’Agyenkwa Nyankopɔn ho ne me honhom di ahurusie; Efiri sɛ waahwɛ n’afenaa hianiwaa.
Nɔkorɛ, efiri nnɛ ɔɔkɔ yi, awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ nyinaa bɛfrɛ me nhyira; efiri sɛ Nea ɔwɔ tumi he ayɔ adeɛ kɛseɛ ama me, na ne dini ne Kronkron; efiri awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ so kosi awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ so he, ohu bɛ a besuro no he mmɔbɔ.
Ɔde ne basa ayɔ ahoɔdenneɛ, waabɔ bɛ a bedi ahantansɛm bɛ akomam apansam: Waatu atumfoɔ afiri bɛ nhennwa so na waama mmɔborɔfoɔ so; waama nnepa amee bɛ a kɔm de bɛ na waama bɛ a bɛwɔ ahodeɛ de nsapan kɔ.
Wabɛhwɛ n’akoa Israel, na wakaeɛ ne mmɔborɔhunu daa sɛnea ɔka kyerɛɛ yɛ agyanom, Abraham ne n’asefoɔ he.” Na Maria tenaa ne nkyɛne bɛyɛ abosome mmeɛnsa, na ɔsane kɔɔ ne fie.
Suboni Yohane awoɔ Na Elisabet awoɔ duruu so he, ɔwoo babeema.
Na mpɔtamu hɔfoɔ ne n’abusuafoɔ tee sɛ Awurade mmɔborɔhunu adɔɔso ne so he, bɛ ne no dii ahurusie.
Na da a ɔtɔ so nwɔtwe he, bɛbaa sɛ beebetwa abɔfra kumaa he twetia, na nka bɛde no ɔɔto ne papa Sakaria.
Nso ne maame kaa sɛ, “Daabi!
Bɛbɛfrɛ no Yohane.” Afei bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Biaa nni w’abusua mu a ne dini de saa.” Nti bɛde nsɛnkyerɛnne bisaa ne papa sɛnea ɔpɛ sɛ bɛfrɛ no.
Afei ɔgyee boɔ twerɛ-pono twerɛɛ so sɛ, “Ne dini ne Yohane.” Na ɔyɛɛ bɛ nyinaa nwanwa.
Mpofirem hɔaa Sakaria ano bieeɛ na ne kɛtrɛma saneeɛ na ofirii aseɛ kasaeɛ, na ohyiraa Nyankopɔn.
Hu kaa bɛ a bɛte mpɔtamu hɔ nyinaa; na befirii aseɛ kaa yeinom nyinaa ho asɛm Yudea nkuro a ɔdeda mmepɔ so he nyinaa mu, na bɛ a bɛteeɛ nyinaa de siee bɛ akoma mu, na bebisaa sɛ, “Ɛɛne koraa ne abɔfra kumaa yi bɛyɔ?” Nea nti a bɛkaa saa ne sɛ, na bennim sɛ Awurade nsa ya abɔfra he so ampa.
Sakaria nhyira dwom Na Honhom Kronkron hyɛɛ ne papa Sakaria ma, na ɔhyɛɛ nkɔm sɛ: “Nhyira nka Awurade, Israel Nyankopɔn, sɛ wama n’ani aba ne nkurofoɔ so na wagye bɛ.
Waama nkwagyeɛ abɛne n’akoa Dawid fie ama yɛ, sɛnea ɔnam n’adiyifoɔ kronkron a bɛtenaa ase tete he anum asɛ so aka sɛ ɔbɛgye yɛ afiri yɛ atamfoɔ ne bɛ a bɛmpɛ yɛ asɛm nyinaa nsam he; waahu yɛ agyanom mmɔbɔ de akaeɛ n’apam kronkron he, ntam a ɔka kyerɛɛ yɛ agya Abraham sɛ onya gye yɛ firi atamfoɔ nsam a, ɔbɛma yɛ ho kwane de asom no a yensuro, ahoteɛ ne tenenee mu n’anim, yɛ nna nyinaa.
Na wo abɔfra kumaa yi, bɛbɛfrɛ wo Sorosoroni he diyifoɔ, efiri sɛ wobedi Awurade anim akosiesie n’akwane, na waama ne nkurofoɔ anya nkwagyeɛ a ɔnam bɛ bɔne fakyɛ so ba he ho nimdeɛ, yɛ Nyankopɔn mmɔborɔhunu nti.
Saa mmɔborɔhunu yi nti adekyeɛ hann firi soro bepie yɛ so, ama bɛ a bɛtete sum ne wuo sunsum ase he anya hann, na wagye yɛ taataa akɔ asomdwie kwane so.” Na abɔfra kumaa he nyini yɛɛ dene honhom mu, na ɔtenaa serɛ so kosii da a oyii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ Israel.
Yesu awoɔ Na nna he mu he, Kaesare Augusto hyɛɛ mmara sɛ bɛntwerɛ nnipa a bɛya n’ahennie mu nyinaa dini.
Yei ne nnipa-kane na odi kane; na ɔkɔɔ so berɛ a na Kirenio yɛ Siria amrado he.
Na nnipa nyinaa tuu kwane kɔɔ bɛ kurom kɔtwerɛɛ bɛ dini.
Yosef nso firii Nasaret a ɔya Galilea kɔɔ Yudea, na esiane sɛ ofiri Dawid fie ne Dawid abusua mu nti, ɔkɔɔ Dawid kuro a bɛfrɛ no Betlehem mu sɛ ɔɔkɔtwerɛ ɔne Maria a na waasi no asiwa he dini; saa berɛ he na Maria ɔɔgye nna awo.
Na ɔbaa sɛ bɛya hɔ he, awoɔ kaa Maria.
Na ɔwoo n’abakane beema, na ɔde ntoma kyekyeree ne ho de no too mmoa adididaka mu, efiri sɛ bɛannya kwane ahɔhodane he mu.
Saa berɛ he, na nnwanhwɛfoɔ bi nso ya wuram ɔɔwɛne bɛ nwane anadwo.
Amonom hɔaa Awurade bɔfoɔ begyinaa bɛ nkyɛne, na Awurade animuonyam hyerɛn twaa bɛ ho hyiaeɛ, na hu kaa bɛ yie.
Na bɔfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honnsuro, hwɛ, mede asɛmpa a ɔfa anigyeɛ pii a nnipa nyinaa benya he ho ɔɔbra ho, efiri sɛ bɛawo Agyenkwa a ɔne Awurade Kristo he ama ho nnɛ Dawid kurom.
Na yei bɛyɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne ama ho.
Hobehu akokoa a bɛde ntoma akyekyere ne ho sɛ ɔda mmoa adididaka mu.” Na amonom hɔaa, soro asafodɔm bɛkaa bɔfoɔ he ho yii Nyankopɔn ayɛ sɛ, “Animuonyam nka Nyankopɔn sorosoro, na asomdwie nka nnipa a bɛsɔ n’ani asaase so.” Nti berɛ a abɔfoɔ he gyaa bɛ hɔ kɔɔ soro he, nnwanhwɛfoɔ he keka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Homma yɛnkɔ Betlehem nkɔhwɛ nea asi a Awurade ayi no adi akyerɛ yɛ yi.” Na bɛyɔɔ ntɛm kɔeɛ, na bekohuu Maria ne Yosef, ne akokoa he sɛ ɔda mmoa adididaka mu.
Na behuu no he, bɛkaa nsɛm a bɛaka akyerɛ bɛ afa abɔfra he ho kyerɛɛ Yosef ne Maria.
Na nea nnwanhwɛfoɔ he kaeɛ he yɛɛ bɛ a bɛteeɛ nyinaa nnwanwa, na Maria de nsɛm yi nyinaa sieeɛ ne tim, na ɔdwendwenee ho.
Na nnwanhwɛfoɔ he sane kɔeɛ, na ɔnam sɛ nea abɔfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ bɛ he, bɛkɔteeɛ na behuiɛ nti, bɛɛhyɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam na beeyi no ayɛ.
Afei nnawɔtwe duruiɛ a betwaa no twetia he, bɛtoo ne dini sɛ Yesu, dini a bɔfoɔ he bɔeɛ ansa na beenyinsɛne no he.
Bɛde abɔfra kɔɔ Yerusalem Bio nso, berɛ a nna a bɛde dwira bɛ ho sɛnea Mose mmara he kyerɛ he baa awieeɛ he, bɛde no baa Yerusalem sɛ bɛde no ɔɔbra Awurade, (sɛnea bɛatwerɛ no Awurade mmara mu sɛ.
“Bɛbɛfrɛ beema biaa a ɔyɛ abakane sɛ Awurade ade kronkron he), na afei bɛbɔɔ afɔdeɛ sɛnea bɛaka no Awurade mmara mu sɛ, “Mmuburo mmienu anaa mmorɔnoma nkumaa mmienu ne bɛmfa mmɔ afɔdeɛ.” Simeon huu Agyenkwa he Na afei na beema bi ya Yerusalem a bɛfrɛ no Simeon a na ɔyɛ nipa tenennee a nyamesuro ya ne mu a ɔɔtwɛne Israel awerɛkyekyerɛ, na Honhom Kronkron ya no so.
Bio nso, na Honhom Kronkron ayi akyerɛ no sɛ onwu gye sɛ waahu Kristo a ɔyɛ Awurade deɛ he ansa.
Honhom he de no kɔɔ asɔrefie hɔ; na berɛ a awofoɔ he de abɔfra Yesu baa sɛ bɛɛbɛyɔ nea mmara he mu amanneɛ kyerɛ sɛ bɛnyɔ mma no he, ɔgyee no too ne nsa so hyiraa Nyankopɔn sɛ, “Awurade, afei woogya w’akoa kwane asomdwie mu sɛnea w’asɛm teɛ; efiri sɛ m’ani ahu nea wonam so bɛgye nkwa a woasiesie amane nyinaa anim he, kanea a wonam so beyi nea ɔkata Amanamane he so na ama ahyɛ wo mane Israel animuonyam.” Na nea ɔka faa ne ho he yɛɛ ne papa ne ne maame nwanwa.
Afei Simeon hyiraa bɛ, na ɔka kyerɛɛ ne maame Maria sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Yei ne bɛayi no ama Israelfoɔ bebree sɛ ɔnam ne so nti bɛbɛhwe ase na bebree nso bɛsɔre.
Na ɔno nso ne bɛyɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne a bɛbɛkasa atia, na ama nnipa bebree akoma mu nsusuiɛ ada adi, na wo deɛ wo ahohera bɛyɛ te sɛ deɛ (bɛde sekane ɔɔwowɔ w’akoma mu nso).” Hana huu Agyenkwa hu Afei na diyifoɔ baa bi ya hɔ a bɛfrɛ no Hana, Fanuel babaa a ofiri Aser abusuakuo mu a na ne mfie kɔ anim paa.
Na ɔwaree ne mmabunu berɛ mu ne ne kunu tenaeɛ mfie nson.
Nso seesei deɛ ɔyɛ kunafoɔ a wadi mfie aduɔwɔtwe nnan, na ɔmpa asɔrefie hɔ da, ɔde mmuadadie ne nkotosrɛ som Nyankopɔn, awia ne anadwo.
Na dɔno heaa mu he, Hana baa hɔ bɛdaa Nyankopɔn ase kaa abɔfra he ho asɛm kyerɛɛ bɛ a bɛɛtwɛne gye a bɛbɛgye Yerusalem he nyinaa.
Bɛyɛɛ nea Awurade mmara hwehwɛ nyinaa wieeɛ he, bɛsane kɔɔ bɛ kuro Nasaret a ɔya Galilea mu.
Na abɔfra he kɔɔ so nyini yɛɛ dene, nyansa hyɛɛ no mã, na Nyankopɔn adom ya ne so.
Yesu ya asɔrefie Afe biaa na n’awofoɔ kɔ Yerusalem kodi Twam afahyɛ he.
Na berɛ a odii mfie dummienu he, bɛkɔeɛ sɛnea afahyɛ he ho amanneɛ teɛ, na bɛtenaa hɔ kosii nna he awieeɛ.
Nso berɛ a bɛɛsane aba he, abɔfra Yesu kaa Yerusalem a n’awofoɔ anhu.
Bɛdwenee sɛ wafra nnipadɔm he mu kɔ, nti betwaa bɛyɛ nkwansini dunnum kosi aduonu.
Na afei befirii aseɛ kyini hwehwɛɛ no abusuafoɔ ne manifoɔ mu.
Ɔbaa sɛ bɛanhu no he, bɛsane kɔɔ Yerusalem kɔhwehwɛɛ no anibereɛ so.
Na nnansa akyi he, behuu no asɔrefie hɔ sɛ ɔte akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he mfinimfini ootie bɛ na oobisabisa bɛ nsɛm.
Na sɛnea n’adwene mu dɔ na oyi nsɛm ano he nti, bɛ a beetie no he ho dwirii bɛ.
Afei behuu no he, ɔyɛɛ bɛ nwanwa, na ne maame ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ: “Me ba, ɛɛne nti ne woyɔɔ yɛ saa?
Hwɛ, me ne wo agya de ahodwiri ahwehwɛ wo.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ɔsɛ sɛ hokyini hwehwɛ me?
Nti honnim sɛ otwa sɛ metena m’Agya fie anaa?” Nso bɛante asɛm a ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ he ase.
Yesu setie ne ne nyini Na ɔne bɛ kɔɔ Nasaret, na ɔkɔɔ so brɛɛ ne ho ase hyɛɛ bɛ ase.
Ne maame nso de nsɛm yi nyinaa siee n’akoma mu.
Na Yesu nyini nyansa ne honam mu, na onyaa Nyankopɔn ne nnipa anim adom.
Suboni Yohane asɛnka Tiberio Kaesare ahennie afe a ɔtɔ so dunnum mu, berɛ a na Pontio Pilato yɛ Yudea amrado he, na Herode nso di Galilea mantam so, na ne nua Filipo nso di Iturea ne Trakoniti amantam so, saa ara nso ne na Lisaneia di Abilene, mantam so.
Asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ Anas ne Kaiafa nna he mu he, Nyankopɔn asɛm baa Sakaria ba Yohane nkyɛne ya serɛ he so.
Nti ɔkɔɔ nkuro a atwa Yordan ho ahyia nyinaa mu pae mu kaa adwensakra ho asubɔ a ɔde kɔ bɔne fakyɛ mu he ho asɛm, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ no diyifoɔ Yesaia nwoma mu sɛ, “Bi ɔɔteam serɛ so sɛ: ‘Honsiesie Awurade kwane, homma n’akwane ntene.
Homma bonhwa nyinaa nyɛ mã, na honnwiri mmepɔ ne nkokoɔ nyinaa ngu fam, na nea akyea he, homma ɔntene na mmonkyimmɔnka nnane akwane tromtrom, na nnipa nyinaa behu Nyankopɔn nkwagyeɛ he.’ ” Na Yohane ka kyerɛɛ nnipadɔm a bɛbaa sɛ ɔmmɔ bɛ asu he sɛ, “Nankatia mma, hwane ne ka kyerɛɛ ho sɛ honwane mfiri abufuo a ɔɔba he ho?
Honso aba a ɔkyerɛ adwensakra.
Na honnka no ho mu sɛ, ‘Yɛ agya ne Abraham.’ Na meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ Nyankopɔn betumi ama Abraham anya mma afiri aboɔ yi mu.
Nɔkorɛ, bɛde akuma he ato nnua he nhini ho dada; nti dua biaa a ɔnso aba pa he bebetwa de agu gya mu.
Na nnipadɔm he bisaa no sɛ, “Saa dea, mmɛ ne yɛnyɔ?” Na obuaa bɛ sɛ.
“Nea ɔwɔ ntaadeɛ mmienu he mma nea onni bi he baako, na nea ɔwɔ bibi di nso mma deɛ onni bi he bi.” Na atogyefoɔ nso baa sɛ ɔmmɔ bɛ asu, na bebisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, abɛ ne yɛnyɔ?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honnye mmmoro toɔ a bɛatwa ato hɔ he.” Asraafoɔ nso bisaa no sɛ, “Ɛɛne ne yɛ nso yɛnyɔ?” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honnwodwoo biaa, na hommfa asɛm nto biaa so, na homma ho ani nsɔ ho akatua.” Kristo ba ne n’adwuma ho nkɔmhyɛ Berɛ a na nnipa he ɔɔhwɛ kwane, na bɛ nyinaa susuu no bɛ akoma mu sɛ, gyama Yohane ne Kristo he, Yohane buaa bɛ sɛ, “Me deɛ, mede nsuo ne bɔ ho asu, na nea ɔwɔ tumi sene me ɔɔba a ne mpaboa ahoma mpo memfata sɛ mesane.
Ɔno ankasa ne de Honhom Kronkron ne gya bɛbɔ ho asu.
Okita ne nhuhusoɔ apampaa ne nsam a ɔde bɛpra n’ayuporobea fitafita, na waboaboa ayuo he ano agu ne pata so, na ntɛ he deɛ, ɔde gya a onnum da bɛhye.” Yohane afiaseda Nti Yohane nam afotuo bebree so pae mu kaa asɛmpa kyerɛɛ nkurofoɔ he.
Nso esiane sɛ Herode a ɔyɛ mantam sodifoɔ he ntene, na Yohane aka n’anim ne nua yerɛ Herodia ho ne nnoɔma bɔne a Herode ayɔ nyinaa ho nti, nea ɔyɔ kaa yeinom nyinaa ho ne sɛ, ɔde Yohane too afiase.
Yesu asubɔ Berɛ a ɔbɔɔ nnipa he nyinaa asu he, ɔbɔɔ Yesu nso asu, na ɔɔbɔ mpaeɛ he, soro bieeɛ, na Honhom Kronkron sianee honam tebea mu te sɛ abuburo baa ne so, na nne bi fi soro kaa sɛ.
“Wone me dɔba, wo ne wo sɔ m’ani.” Yesu awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ Afei berɛ a Yesu hyɛɛ n’adwuma ase he, na waadi bɛyɛ mfie aduasa, na behuu no sɛ Yosef ba, Eli ba, Mattat ba, Lewi ba, Melki ba, Yanai ba, Yosef ba, Matatia ba, Amos ba, Nahum ba, Hesli ba, Nagai ba, Mahat ba, Matatia ba, Semein ba, Yosek ba, Yoda ba, Yohanan ba, Resa ba, Serubabel ba, Sealtiel ba, Neri ba, Melki ba, Adi ba, Kosam ba, Elmadam ba, Er ba, Yosua ba, Eliesa ba, Yorim ba, Matat ba, Lewi ba, Simeon ba, Yuda ba, Yosef ba, Yonam ba, Eliakim ba, Melea ba, Mena ba, Matata ba, Natan ba, Dawid ba, Yisai ba, Obed ba, Boas ba, Sala ba, Nahson ba, Aminadab ba, Admin ba, Arni ba, Hesron ba, Peres ba, Yuda ba, Yakob ba, Isak ba, Abraham ba, Tera ba, Nahor ba, Serug ba, Reu ba, Peleg ba, Eber ba, Sela ba, Kainan ba, Arfaksad ba, Sem ba, Noa ba, Lamek ba, Metusela ba, Henok ba, Yared ba, Mahalaleel ba, Kainan ba, Enos ba, Set ba, Adam ba, Nyankopɔn ba.
Yesu sɔhwɛ Na Yesu a Honhom Kronkron ahyɛ no mã he danee ne ho firii Yordan ho, na Honhom he de no kɔɔ serɛ so adaduannan, na Bronsam sɔɔ no hwɛeɛ.
Afei nso, wanni hwee saa nna he mu, na nna he baa awieeɛ he, na kɔm de no.
Na Bronsam ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ.
“Sɛ woyɛ Nyankopɔn Ba a, kasa kyerɛ boɔ yi ma ɔnane paanoo.” Nso Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Ɔnyɛ paanoo nkoaa so ne nipa nam bɛtena ase.’ ” Na Bronsam de no kɔ baabi a hɔ krɔnn kɔkyerɛɛ no asaase so ahennie nyinaa prɛko; na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Mede tumi yi nyinaa ne mu animuonyam bɛma wo, efiri sɛ bɛde ama me, na biaa a mepɛ he mede ma no.
Nti sɛ wobɛkoto asom me a, ne nyinaa bɛyɛ wo dea.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Awurade wo Nyankopɔn ne ɔsɛ sɛ wokoto no, na ɔno nkoaa ne ɔsɛ sɛ wosom no.’ ” Afei ɔde no kɔɔ Yerusalem kogyinaa asɔredane he atifi ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ woyɛ Nyankopɔn Ba a, gyaa wo ho kɔhwe fam; efiri sɛ bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Wo nti ɔbɛhyɛ n’abɔfoɔ sɛ bɛmmɔ wo ho bane,’ na ‘Bɛmmɛsoa wo bɛ nsa so, na bɛamfa wo nane ampem boɔ biaa.’ ” Ne Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Bɛaka sɛ, ‘Nsɔ Awurade wo Nyankopɔn nhwɛ.’ ” Nti Bronsam wiee sɔhwɛ he nyinaa he, ogyaa Yesu hɔ kɔɔ kakra (sɛ onkosi sɛ obenya ne ho kwane bio.)
Yesu asɛnka mfitiaseɛ Afei Yesu a na Honhom he tumi ahyɛ no ma he sane kɔɔ Galilea.
Na ne ho asɛm hyetaa nkuro a atwa hɔ ahyia he nyinaa mu.
Ofirii aseɛ kyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ hyia adane mu nso, na bɛ nyinaa bɛ kamfõõ no.
Yesu Nasaret asɛnka Na ɔkɔɔ Nasaret, baabi a bɛtetee no he; na sɛnea ɔtaa yɔ homeda he, ɔkɔɔ hyiadane mu, na ɔsɔre gyinaa hɔ sɛ ɔɔbɛkenkane, nti bɛmaa no diyifoɔ Yesaia nwoma a na bɛabobɔ he, na obiee nwoma mmobɔeɛ he mu, na ɔkenkanee faako a bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Awurade Honhom ya me so, efiri sɛ wasra me sɛ memmɛka asɛmpa nkyerɛ ahiafoɔ, wasoma me sɛ memmɛka gyeɛ ho asɛm nkyerɛ bɛ a bɛafa bɛ nommum na memma anifirafoɔ nhu adeɛ, sɛ memma bɛ a binom hyɛ bɛ so nya fahodie, na mempae mu nka berɛ a ɔsɔ Awurade ani nkyerɛ.” Na afei ɔbobɔɔ nwoma mmobɔeɛ he sane de maa somfo he na ɔtenaa ase; na bɛ a bɛya hyiadane he mu nyinaa hwɛɛ no too.
Afei ofirii aseɛ ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nnɛ ne twerɛsɛm a hotee no seeseiaa yi abam.” Na bɛ nyinaa bedii ne ho adanse-pa, na adom nsɛm a ɔkaeɛ he maa bɛ ho dwirii bɛ, na bebisaa sɛ, “Nyɛ Yosef ba yi di?” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ampa hobebu me bɛ yi sɛ, ‘Yaresafoɔ, sa wo ho yadeɛ, yɔ nnoɔma a yɛtee sɛ ɔkɔɔ so Kapernaum he bi woaa wo kurom ha nso.’ ” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ diyifoɔ biaa nni hɔ a bɛgye no tom ne kurom.
Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem sɛ, Elia nna he mu he, na akunafoɔ bebree ya Israel berɛ a nsuo antɔ mfie mmeɛnsa ne abosome nsia maa kɔm kɛseɛ baa asaase he nyinaa so he, nso bɛansoma Elia ankɔ mmaa yi mu biaa hɔ gye sɛ kunafoɔ bi a na ɔya Sidon kuro Serepta mu hɔ.
Bio nso, diyifoɔ Elisa berɛ so he, na akwatafoɔ bebree ya Israel, nso bɛamma bɛ mu biaa ho amfiri gye Siriani Naaman.” Yesu nkurofoɔ pɛɛ sɛ beku no Afei bɛ a bɛya hyiadane he mu nyinaa tee saa nsɛm he, bɛ bo fuiɛ; na bɛsɔre piapiaa no firii kuro he mu, na bɛde no kɔɔ bepɔ a bɛ kuro he gu so he ano sɛ beekosum no ahwe fam.
Nso ɔfaa bɛ mfimfini kɔeɛ.
Yesu sa bi a ɔwɔ honhommɔne yadeɛ Afei Yesu kɔɔ Kapernaum, Galilea kuro bi mu.
Na homeda duruiɛ he, ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ; na kwane a ɔfaa so kyerɛkyerɛeɛ he yɛɛ bɛ nwanwa, efiri sɛ na tumi ya ne nsɛm he mu.
Na beema bi ya hyiadane he mu a ɔwɔ honhommɔne, honhom fi, na ɔde nne kɛseɛ teaam sɛ, “Aa!
Nha yɛ adwene!
Nasareni Yesu, mmɛ ne yɛ ne wo wɔ yɔ?
Nti wobaa sɛ woobɛsɛe yɛ?
Menim onii ko a woyɛ ankasa, wone Kronkronni a ofiri Nyankopɔn hɔ he.” Yesu kaa n’anim hyɛɛ no sɛ, “Yɛ komm, na firi ne mu kɔ!” Nti honhommɔne he maa beema he twa hwee bɛ mfimfini, na ofirii ne mu kɔeɛ a wanyɔ beema he hwee.
Yei yɛɛ bɛ nyinaa nwanwa, na bɛkeka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Ei!
Abɛ asɛm di?
Ɔde tumi ne ahoɔdene hyɛ ahonhom fĩ ma befiri adi!” Nti ne ho asɛm trɛ kɔɔ nkuro a atwa ahyia hɔ he nyinaa mu.
Petro ase baa ayaresa Yesu sɔre firii hyiadane he mu he, ɔkɔɔ Simon fie.
Na abunu akye Simon asebaa, na bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔnhwɛ no.
Nti ogyinaa n’atifi hyɛɛ abunu he sɛ omfiri ne so nkɔ, na abunu he firii ne so kɔeɛ.
Mpofiremaa ɔsɔre firii aseɛ som bɛ.
Yesu saa nyarewa ahodoɔ bebree Na awia ɔɔkɔtɔ he, bɛ a bɛwɔ nkurofoɔ a nyarewa ahodoɔ ayɛ bɛ he de bɛ braa no.
Ɔde ne nsa guu bɛ mu biaa so saa bɛ yadeɛ.
Na ahonhommɔne nso firii bɛ mu pii mu teateam sɛ, “Wone Nyankopɔn Ba he.” Nso, ɔkaa bɛ anim, na wamma bɛ kwane sɛ bɛnkasa, efiri sɛ na benim no sɛ ɔno ne Kristo he.
Yesu Yudea asɛnka Na adeɛ kyeeɛ he, Yesu firii adi kɔɔ baabi a biaa nni.
Nso nnipadɔm he hwehwɛɛ no baa faako a ɔya he, na bɛbɔɔ mmɔdene sɛ bebesi no kwane, na wamfiri bɛ nkyɛne ankɔ.
Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ.
“Ɔsɛ sɛ mekɔ nkuro foforɔ mu nso kɔka Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho asɛmpa he, efiri sɛ yei nti ne bɛsomaa me.” Nti ɔtoaa so kaa asɛm Yudea hyia adane mu.
Asuafoɔ he frɛ Berɛ bi, ɔbaa sɛ na nnipakuo he akyere Yesu so a na beetie Nyankopɔn asɛm.
Na ogyina Genesaret tadeɛ he ho.
Na ohuu akodoɔ mmienu sɛ osisi tadeɛ he ho, nso na apofofoɔ he asisi afiri mu a bɛɛhohoro bɛ asau.
Yesu kɔforoo akodoɔ he mu baako a na ɔyɛ Simon deɛ, na ɔsrɛɛ Simon sɛ ompia mfiri asaase so nkɔ akyire kakra.
Afei ɔtenaa mu, firii aseɛ kyerɛkyerɛɛ nnipakuo he.
Berɛ a ogyae kasa he, ɔka kyerɛɛ Simon sɛ.
“Pia kɔ nea hɔ dɔ, na hongu ho asau he nyi nam.” Na Simon buaa sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, yɛayɔ adwuma anadwo mũ nyinaa na yɛannya hwee, nso w’anum asɛm nti megu asau he.” Na bɛyɔɔ saa he, bɛ asau he bumaa mpataa pii ma no hyɛɛ aseɛ teteeɛ.
Nti benyam bɛ mfɛfoɔ a bɛya kodoɔ baako he mu sɛ bɛmmɛboa bɛ; na bɛbaeɛ ma bɛhyɛɛ akodoɔ mmienu he mama, na ofirii aseɛ sɛ ɔɔmem.
Berɛ a Simon Petro huu yei he, ɔkotoo Yesu nane ase kaa sɛ, “Awurade, firi me nkyɛne kɔ, na meyɛ debɔneyɛni!” Mpataa a beyiiɛ he maa Petro ne bɛ a bɛka ne ho he nyinaa ho dwirii bɛ, na Sebedeo mma Yakobo ne Yohane, a bɛyɛ Simon yɔnko adwumayɔfoɔ he nso ho dwirii bɛ.
Nso Yesu ka kyerɛɛ Simon sɛ, “Nsuro, efiri saa berɛ yi ɔɔkɔ yi, wobeyi nnipa.” Nti bɛsane de akodoɔ he baa asaase so, na begyaa bibiaa hɔ dii n’akyi.
Kwatani bi ayaresa Berɛ foforɔ bi a na Yesu ya nkuro he baako mu he, hwɛ!
Ohuu beema bi a kwata adware no.
Berɛ a n’ani bɔɔ Yesu so he, ɔbɛhwee n’anim srɛɛ no anibereɛ so sɛ, “Awurade, sɛ wopɛ nkoaa a, wobetumi ama me ho afiri.” Nti, Yesu tenee ne nsa kaa no kaa sɛ, “Mepɛ.
Wo ho mfiri.” Na amonom hɔaa kwata he tu yeraeɛ.
Afei ɔhyɛɛ beema he sɛ ɔnnka nkyerɛ biaa.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kɔ na fa wo ho kɔkyerɛ sɔfo, na bɔ w’ahofire ho afɔdeɛ sɛnea Mose hyɛeɛ he, na ɔnyɛ adanseɛ mma bɛ.” Nso ne ho asɛm trɛɛ pii, na nnipakuo pii baeɛ sɛ beebetie no na wasa bɛ yadeɛ afiri bɛ nyarewa ahodoɔ nyinaa mu.
Nso, ɔtwee ne ho kɔhyɛɛ serɛ so baabi kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ.
Bubuani bi ayaresa Da koro bi, Yesu gu so ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ he, na Farisifoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ a befiri nkuraa a ɔya Galilea ne Yudea ne Yerusalem ase aba he nyinaa tete hɔ, na Awurade tumi ya ne so a ɔde bɛsa yadeɛ.
Na hwɛ!
Na mmeema bi sõ bubuani bi a ɔda kɛtɛ so, na bɛɛhwehwɛ kwane a bɛbɛfa so de no abɛto n’anim.
Nti, berɛ a bɛannya kwane amfa no amma esiane nnipadɔm he nti he, bɛkɔɔ dane he atifi kogyaagyaa ɔne kɛtɛ he mu faa dane he soro bɛtoo Yesu anim ne nnipadɔm he mfinfini.
Na ohuu bɛ gyidie he, ɔkaa sɛ.
“Beema, bɛde wo bɔne akyɛ wo.” Hɔaa ne atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he firii aseɛ dwenee ho sɛ, “Hwane di a ɔka abususɛm sei?
Hwane ne betumi de bɔne akyɛ ka Nyankopɔn ho?” Na Yesu huu bɛ nsusuiɛ he, obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne hoodwene ho ho akoma mu yi?
Nea ɔya he ne ɔmmerɛ, sɛ bɛbɛka sɛ, ‘Bɛde wo bɔne akyɛ wo,’ anaa bɛbɛka sɛ, ‘Sɔre na nante’?
Nso sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na hobehu sɛ Nipa Ba he wɔ tumi ya asaase so sɛ ɔde bɔne kyɛ nti, Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bubuafoɔ he sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ wo sɛ, sɔre fa wo kɛtɛ na kɔ wo fie!” Na amonom hɔaa ɔsɔre gyinaa bɛ anim, faa nea ɔda so he firii hɔ kɔɔ ne fie a, na ɔɔhyɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam.
Afei ɔyɛɛ bɛ mu biaa nwanwa, na befirii aseɛ hyɛɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam, na hu kaa bɛ ma bɛkaa sɛ, “Nnɛ deɛ, yɛahu anwanwadeɛ!” Yesu frɛɛ Lewi Yeinom akyi he, Yesu firii adi kohuu sɛ togyeni bi a bɛfrɛ no Lewi te togyebea, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Bedi m’akyi.” Na ogyaa bibiaa hɔ sɔre dii n’akyi.
Afei nso, Lewi too pono kɛseɛ bi ne fie maa no; na atogyefoɔ bebree ne nnipa foforɔ bɛtenatenaa adidiiɛ hɔ.
Nti Farisifoɔ ne Atwerɛfoɔ he nwiinwii kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ho ne togyefoɔ ne nnebɔneyɛfoɔ didi nom yi?” Yesu buaa sɛ.
“Bɛ a bɛte apɔ he nhia yaresafoɔ, na bɛ a bɛyare he mmom ne behia yaresafoɔ.
Mamma sɛ meebɛfrɛ ateneneefoɔ, na mmom maaba sɛ meebɛfrɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ de bɛ akɔ adwensakra mu.” Mmuadadie ho asɛm Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ.
“Yohane asuafoɔ he di mmuada mprɛ pii na bɛbɔ mpaeɛ, na Farisifoɔ nso yɔ saa, nso wo deɛ, w’asuafoɔ he didi na bɛnom!
Yesu bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Nti hobetumi ama ayefokunu he ahɔhoɔ adi mmuada berɛ a ayefokunu he ya bɛ nkyɛne yi?
Nso nna bi bɛba a bɛbɛfa ayefokunu he afiri bɛ nkyɛne; saa nna he mu ne bebedi mmuada.” Afei, ɔtoaa so maa bɛ mfantoho bi sɛ, “Biaa mmfa ntoma mono sini ntɛ ataadeɛ dadaa mu; anyɛ saa a, ntoma foforɔ he bɛte afiri ataadeɛ he mu, efiri sɛ deɛ otwa firii foforɔ he mu he ne dada he nsɛ.
Bio nso, biaa mfa bobesa mono ngu nsa kotokuo dadaa mu; anyɛ saa a, nsa mono he bɛpaapae nsa kotokuo he, na nsa he betu agu na kotoku he asɛe.
Mmom ɔsɛ sɛ bɛde bobesa mono gu nsa kotokuo foforɔ mu.
Biaa a wanom nsa dadaa awie he mpɛ nsa mono; na mmom ɔka sɛ, ‘dadaa he yɛ paa.’ ”
Homeda sɛeɛ Na homeda bi duruiɛ he ɔkɔfaa aburofuo bi mu, na n’asuafoɔ he pempanee aburo mmɛtem he bi, posaa no bɛ nsam weeɛ.
Na Farisifoɔ he bi kaa sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne hooyɔ nea mmara mma kwane sɛ bɛyɔ no homeda yi?” Nso Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Honkenkanee nea Dawid yɔeɛ berɛ a kɔm dee ɔne mmeema a bɛka ne ho he?
Sɛnea ɔkɔɔ Nyankopɔn fie kɔgyee Kyerɛɛ Paanoo a mmara mma kwane sɛ biaa di, gye asɔfoɔ nkoaa, na odiiɛ de bi maa mmeema a bɛka ne ho he?” Na ɔtoaa so ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nipa Ba he ne homeda he so tumfoɔ.” Beema bi a ne nsa adwodwo he Homeda foforɔ duruiɛ he Yesu kɔɔ hyiadane mu, na ofirii aseɛ kyerɛkyerɛeɛ.
Na beema bi ya hɔ a na ne nsa nifa adwodwo.
Nti na atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he ɔɔhwɛ no komm sɛ ebia ɔbɛsa yadeɛ homeda na bɛanya kwane bi afa so abɔ no soboɔ.
Ewom sɛ na onim bɛ adwene deɛ, nso ɔka kyerɛɛ beema a ne nsa adwodwo he sɛ, “Sɔre gyina mfimfini ha.” Na ɔsɔre gyinaa hɔ.
Afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Meebisa ho, nti mmɛ ne nipa wɔ ho kwane sɛ ɔyɔ no homeda, adepa anaa adebɔne, sɛ ɔbɛgye bi kra nkwa anaa ɔbɛma na asɛe?” Na ɔhwɛɛ bɛ nyinaa hyiaeɛ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ beema he sɛ, “Tene wo nsa.” Beema he yɔɔ saa, na ahoɔdene baa ne nsa he mu.
Na yei maa bɛ ani beree dendenndene, na betuu Yesu ho agyina hwɛɛ nea bɛde bɛyɔ no.
Asuafoɔ dummienu he yie Saa nna he mu he Yesu kɔɔ bepɔ so kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ, na ɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ anadwo mũ he nyinaa.
Na adeɛ kyeeɛ he, ɔfrɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne, na ɔpaa bɛ mu dummienu frɛɛ bɛ asomafoɔ; Bɛne Simon, a ɔsane frɛɛ no Petro, ne ne nua Andreo, ne Yakobo ne Yohane, ne Filipo ne Bartolomeo, ne Mateo ne Toma, ne Alfeo ba Yakobo, ne Simon a bɛfrɛ no Selote, Yakobo ba Yuda, ne Yuda Iskariot a ɔbɛyɛɛ bi a oyii Yesu maeɛ he.
Yesu kyerɛkyerɛeɛ, na ɔsaa nyarewa Na ɔne bɛ sane begyinaa baabi a hɔ da so, na n’asuafoɔ pii, ne nnipadɔm a befiri Yudea ne Yerusalem, ne Tiro ne Sidon mpoano nyinaa baa sɛ beebetie no na wasa bɛ yadeɛ.
Ɔsaa bɛ a honhom fĩ ha bɛ yadeɛ.
Na nnipadɔm he nyinaa hwehwɛɛ sɛ bɛde bɛ nsa bɛka no, efiri sɛ na tumi firi ne mu ba, na ɔsaa bɛ nyinaa yadeɛ.
Serɛ so asɛnka Na Yesu maa n’ani so kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he firii aseɛ kaa sɛ.
“Nhyira ne ho ahiafoɔ, efiri sɛ ho ne Nyankopɔn ahennie he yɛ ho dea.
“Nhyira ne ho a saa berɛ yi kɔm de ho, efiri sɛ bɛbɛma hoamee.
“Nhyira ne ho a saa berɛ yi hoosu, efiri sɛ hobɛsere.
“Nhyira ne ho sɛ nnipa tane ho, na beyi ho firi nnipa mu, na bɛbɔ ho ahohora, na Nipa Ba he nti, bɛmmɔ ho dini nka asɛm te sɛnea ho dini yɛ akyiwadeɛ.
Homma ho ani nnye na honni ahurusie saa da he, na hwɛ!
Howɔ akatua ya soro, efiri sɛ saa adekoro yiaa ne bɛ agyanom de yɔɔ adiyifoɔ he.
“Nso ho adefoɔ honnue, efiri sɛ hoanya ho awerɛkyekyerɛ nyinaa dada.
“Honnue, ho a sesieaa hoamee, efiri sɛ kɔm bɛde ho.” “Honnue, ho a sesieaa hoosere, efiri sɛ ho werɛ bɛho na hoasu.
“Sɛ nnipa nyinaa ka ho ho asɛmpa a, honnue, efiri sɛ saa ne bɛ agyanom kaa nsɛmpa faa atorɔ adiyifoɔ he ho.
Honnɔ ho atamfoɔ!
“Nso meeka akyerɛ ho a hootie yi sɛ, honkɔ so nnɔ ho atamfoɔ, na honyɔ bɛ a bɛtane ho he papa, na honhyira bɛ a bɛdome ho, na hommɔ mpaeɛ mma bɛ a bɛha ho!
Nea ɔbɔ w’aso fa mu he, dane fã a aaka he nso ma no; na nea ɔfa w’ataadeɛ ngugusoɔ he, mfa ataadeɛ nhyɛaseɛ he nso nkame no.
Na biaa a obisa wo bibi he, ma no, na nea ɔfa wo nnoɔma he, mmisa no ho asɛm.
“Afei nso, sɛnea hopɛ sɛ nnipa yɛ ma ho he, honyɔ saa mma afoforɔ nso.
“Na sɛ hodɔ bɛ a bɛdɔ ho a, abɛ mfasoɔ ne ɔya so ma ho?
Abɔnefoɔ mpo dɔ bɛ a bɛdɔ bɛ.
Na sɛ hoyɔ papa ma bɛ a bɛyɔ ho papa a, mmɛ mfasoɔ koraa ne ya so ma ho?
Abɔnefoɔ mpo yɔ saa.
Afei nso, sɛ homa bɛ a howɔ anidasoɔ sɛ hobenya bibi afiri bɛ nkyɛne he bosea a, mmɛ mfasoɔ ne ɔya so ma ho?
Abɔnefoɔ mpo ma bɛ nuanom abɔnefoɔ bosea na ama bɛanya pii afiri bɛ hɔ.
Mmom, honnɔ ho atamfoɔ na honyɔ bɛ papa na homma afoforɔ bosea a ho ani nna so sɛ hobenya bibi akyire yi; na ho akatua bɛyɛ kɛseɛ, na hobɛyɛ Sorosoroni he mma, efiri sɛ ne yam yɛ ma boniayɛfoɔ ne abɔnefoɔ.
Nti honhu biaa mmɔbɔ sɛnea ho Agya hu biaa mmɔbɔ he.
Atenyie bɔne “Bio nso, hommu atɛne na bɛammu ho atɛne; na hommu fɔ na bɛammu ho fɔ.
Homfa nkyɛ na bɛde akyɛ ho.
Homma na bɛama ho.
Susukuruwa pa a bɛamia so, awoso no ama abu so ne bɛde begu ho ntoma mu.
Na susukuruwa a hode susu ma nkurofoɔ he, ɔnoaa ne bɛde besusu ama ho.” Afei nso ɔmaa bɛ mfantoho bi sɛ.
“Nti nifirani betumi akyerɛ nifirani kwane?
Sɛ ɔba saa a bɛ mmienu nyinaa bɛnkɔtɔ amena mu anaa?
Suani nsene ne kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, nso biaa a wasua bibi ahu he bɛyɛ sɛ ne kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ.
Sɛ ɔte saa a, mmɛ nti ne wohwɛ mfrɛ a ɔda wo nua ani so, na wunhu mpuna a ɔda w’ankasa w’ani so mmom?
Ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na woatumi aka akyerɛ wo nua sɛ, ‘Me nua, ma menyi mfrɛ a ɔda w’ani so yi mma wo,’ berɛ a wonhu mpuna a ɔda w’ankasa w’ani so he mpo?
Nyaatwomni!
Di kane yi w’ankasa w’ani so mpuna he, na wobehu sɛnea wobeyi mfrɛ a ɔda wo nua ani so he.
“Na dua pa biaa nso aba bɔne; saa ara nso ne dua bɔne biaa nso aba pa. Na dua biaa aba ne bɛde hu dua pɔtee a ɔyɛ.
Bɛntete borɔdoma mfiri nkasɛe so, na bentwa bobe mfiri nwerɛ so.
Nipa pa firi adepa a wakora no n’akoma mu ne oyi adepa adi, nso bɔnefoɔ firi nnebɔne a wakora no n’akoma mu ne oyi adebɔne adi; efiri sɛ nea ayɛ akoma mã aboro so he ne ano ka.
Fapem ahodoɔ mmienu he “Mmɛ nti ne hofrɛ me ‘Awurade, Awurade,’ nso honyɔ nea meka yi?
Biaa a ɔba me nkyɛne na ɔte me nsɛm na ɔyɔ he, mɛkyerɛ ho sɛnea ɔteɛ.
Ɔte sɛ beema bi a oosi dane, a otutuu fam kɔɔ akyire na ɔtoo fapem botane so.
Nti, berɛ a nsuo hyiriiɛ he, ɔbɛbɔɔ dane he, nso antumi anwoso no, efiri sɛ besii no yie.
Nso, nea ɔte me nsɛm na ɔnyɔ he, ɔte sɛ beema bi a osii ne dane sii asaase so a wanto fapem.
Na nsuo hyiri bɛbɔɔ no, na dane he bubuu ntɛmaa, na ɔsɛe koraa.”
Akoa bi ayaresa Berɛ a Yesu kaa ne nsɛm he nyinaa kyerɛɛ nkurofoɔ he wieeɛ he, ɔkɔɔ Kapernaum.
Na sraani panyini bi akoa a ɔsombo ma no paa yare a oowu.
Berɛ a ɔtee Yesu nka he, ɔsomaa Yudafoɔ mpanyimfoɔ sɛ bɛnkɔsrɛ no na ɔmmɛsa n’akoa he yadeɛ.
Bɛbaa Yesu nkyɛne he, bɛsrɛɛ no anibrɛ so sɛ, “Ɔfata sɛ woyɛ yei ma sraani panyini he, efiri sɛ ɔdɔ yɛ mane yi, na ɔno ankasa ne sii hyiadane maa yɛ.” Nti Yesu ne bɛ siim kɔeɛ.
Nso ɔɔyɛ aduru fie hɔ he, na sraani panyini he asoma ne nnamfoɔ dada sɛ bɛmmɛka nkyerɛ no sɛ, “Owura, nha wo ho, na memfata sɛ wobɛba me fie.
Nti mammu me ho sɛ mefata sɛ mɛba wo nkyɛne.
Na wo deɛ ka bibi kɛkɛ na m’akoa he ho nyɛ no dene, efiri sɛ me nso mehyɛ bi ase, na mewɔ asraafoɔ nso hyɛ m’ase, na meka kyerɛ bɛ mu bi sɛ, ‘Kɔ ha a!’ Ɔkɔ.
Na meka kyerɛ foforɔ nso sɛ ‘Bra a!’ Ɔba.
Na meka kyerɛ m’akoa sɛ, ‘Yɔ yei a!’ Ɔyɔ.” Berɛ a Yesu tee yei he, ne ho dwirii no, na ɔdanee n’ani kyerɛɛ nnipakuo a bedi n’akyi he kaa sɛ.
“Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, menhuu gyidie a ɔsõ sei Israel mu mpo.” Na bɛ a bɛasoma bɛ he sane bɛ akyi kɔɔ fie he, bekohuu akoa he sɛ ne ho ayɛ no dene.
Nain kunafoɔ he ba he Ankyɛre biaa ne Yesu tuu kwane kɔɔ kuro bi a bɛfrɛ no Nain mu, na n’asuafoɔ he ne nnipadɔm pii ka ne ho.
Berɛ a ɔbɛnee kuro he pono ano he, hwɛ, na bɛsõ beema bi a ne maame di no bakorɔ a wawu de no oofiri adi.
Na baa he yɛ kunafoɔ nso.
Na nnipadɔm pii a befiri kuro he mu nso ka ne ho.
Berɛ a Awurade ani bɔɔ baa he so he, ɔyɛɛ no mmɔbɔ, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Gyae su.” Afei ɔbɛnee funnaka he de ne nsa kɔsɔɔ mu, na bɛ a bekitakita mu he gyinaeɛ, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Abeemaa, meeka akyerɛ wo sɛ, sɔre!” Na abeemaa a wawu he sɔre tenaa ase, na ofirii aseɛ kasaeɛ, na ɔde no maa ne maame.
Afei hu kaa bɛ nyinaa, na befirii aseɛ hyɛɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam sɛ, “Bɛama diyifoɔ kɛseɛ bi so ya yɛ mu,” na “Nyankopɔn ama n’ani aba ne nkurofoɔ so!” Na Yesu ho asɛm yi trɛ kɔɔ Yudea nyinaa ne nkuro a atwa ho ahyia nyinaa mu.
Suboni Yohane ahoyera Afei Yohane asuafoɔ he kɔkaa yeinom nyinaa kyerɛɛ no.
Nti Yohane frɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he mu mmienu somaa bɛ Awurade nkyɛne sɛ benkobisa no sɛ, “Nti wone nea ɔɔba he anaa yɛnhwɛ foforɔ kwane?” Berɛ a mmeema he koduruu Yesu nkyɛne he bɛkaa sɛ, “Suboni Yohane asoma yɛ sɛ yemmebisa wo sɛ, ‘Wone nea ɔɔba he anaa yɛnhwɛ foforɔ kwane?’ ” Dɔno heaa mu, Yesu saa nnipa bebree a bɛnte apɔ, ne bɛ a bɛ yadeɛ mu ɔdene ne bɛ a bɛwɔ ahonhommɔne nyinaa yadeɛ, na ɔmaa anifirafoɔ bebree huu adeɛ.
Nti obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔ nkɔka nea hoahu na hoate yi nkyerɛ Yohane sɛ, anifirafoɔ hu adeɛ, mmubuafoɔ nante, akwatafoɔ ho firi, asotifoɔ te asɛm, awufoɔ nyane, na bɛka asɛmpa kyerɛ ahiafoɔ.
Na nhyira ne biaa a menyɛ sintidua mma no.” Yesu dii Yohane ho adanseɛ Berɛ a bɛ a Yohane somaa bɛ he kɔeɛ he, ofirii aseɛ kaa Yohane ho asɛm kyerɛɛ nnipakuo he sɛ.
“Mmɛ ne hokɔɔ serɛ so kɔhwɛeɛ?
Demmire a mframa ɔɔwoso no anaa?
Sɛ ɔnte saa a, mmɛ ne hofirii adi kɔhwɛeɛ?
Beema a ɔhyɛ ntaade-pa?
Hwɛ, bɛ a bɛhyɛ ntaade-pa ne bedi dɛ he bɛya ahemfie.
Nti mmɛ koraa ne hofirii adi kɔhwɛeɛ?
Diyifoɔ?
Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ ɔte saa, na ɔsene diyifoɔ koraa.
Yei ne nea bɛatwerɛ ne ho asɛm sɛ, ‘Hwɛ, meesoma me bɔfoɔ adi w’anim, a obesiesie wo kwane adi w’anim.’ Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, bɛ a mmaa awo bɛ mu biaa nni hɔ a ɔyɛ kɛseɛ kyɛne Yohane; nso nea osua koraa Nyankopɔn ahennie mu he yɛ kɛseɛ kyɛne no.” “Nti, mmɛ ho ne mede nnemafoɔ bɛtoto, na bɛte sɛ hefoɔ?
Bɛte sɛ mmɔfra a bɛtete dwa so ɔɔteateam frɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, ‘Yɛhyɛne abɛne maa ho, nso hoansa; yɛbɔɔ bena, nso hoansu.’ Saa nso ne Yohane Suboni baeɛ he, wannidi na wannom nsa, nso hoka sɛ, ‘Ɔwɔ honhommɔne.’ Nipa Ba he aba, odidi na ɔnom, nso hoka sɛ, ‘Hwɛ!
Beema didifoɔ ne nsanomfoɔ, togyefoɔ ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ adamfo di!’ Nso, bɛ a bɛde Nyankopɔn nyansa di dwuma he da no adi sɛ ne nyansa he yɛ papa.” Baa debɔneyɛni Afei Farisini bi kɔɔ so srɛɛ no sɛ ɔne no mmedidi.
Nti ɔkɔɔ Farisini he fie kɔtenaa didipono ho.
Na hwɛ, baa bi a benim no kuro he mu sɛ debɔneyɛni tee sɛ ɔte adidiiɛ Farisini he fie he ɔde kɔntoa a ngo hwamhwam gu mu baeɛ, na obegyinaa n’akyi kotoo ne nane ase suiɛ, na ofirii aseɛ de ne nisuo foaa ne nane ho, na ɔde ne ti nwi popaeɛ.
Afei, ofee ne nane ho de ngo hwamhwam he srasraa ho.
Na Farisini a ɔtoo nsa frɛɛ no he huiɛ he, ɔkaa no ne tim sɛ, “Sɛ beema yi yɛ diyifoɔ a, nka obehu onii ne baa ko a ɔde ne nsa ɔɔka no he sɛ ɔyɛ debɔneyɛni.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Simon, mewɔ asɛm bi ka kyerɛ wo.” Simon kaa sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, kasa!” Na Yesu kaa sɛ, “Na mmeema mmienu de defɛmfoɔ bi ka; baako de no ka bɛyɛ paani abosome dunson akatua, na baako nso ka bɛyɛ paani bosome baako ne fa akatua.
Berɛ a benni hwee a bɛde betua he, ogyae ka he mu de kyɛɛ bɛ mmienu.
Nti, bɛ mu deɛ ɔya he ne bɛdɔ nea ɔde bɛ ka kyɛɛ bɛ he kɛse?” Simon buaa no sɛ, “Mesusu sɛ nea ɔde ka pii kyɛɛ no he a.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ.
“Woabua no yie.” Nti ɔhwɛɛ baa he ka kyerɛɛ Simon sɛ, “Woahu baa yi?
Mebaa wo fie; woamma me nsuo anhohoro me nane ho.
Nso baa yi de ne nisuo afoa me nane ho na ɔde ne ti nwii apopa.
Woamfe m’ano; nso baa yi deɛ, efiri dɔno a mebaeɛ mu he, onnyae me nane ho fe.
Woamfa ngo ansra me ti mu; nso baa yi de ngo hwamhwam asrasra me nane ho.
Yei nti, meeka akyerɛ wo sɛ, ewom sɛ ne bɔne dɔɔso deɛ, nso bɛde akyɛ no, efiri sɛ ɔdɔɔ pii; nso nea bɛde kakraa bi akyɛ no he dɔ kakraa bi.” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ baa he sɛ, “Bɛde wo bɔne akyɛ wo.” Nti bɛ a bɛ ne no te adidiiɛ he firii aseɛ kekaa no bɛ mu sɛ.
“Hwane di a ɔde bɔne mpo kyɛ yi?” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ baa he sɛ, “Wo gyidie agye wo; fa asomdwie kɔ.”
Asɛnka Yei akyi berɛ tiaa bi mu he, Yesu tutuu akwane kɔɔ nkuro mu ne nkuraa ase kɔ pae mu kaa Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho asɛmpa.
Na dummienu he ka ne ho.
Na mmaa bi a wasa bɛ yadeɛ atutu ahonhommɔne afiri bɛ mu, Maria a bɛfrɛ no Magdalene, a ahonhommɔne nson firii ne mu kɔeɛ he, ne Herode fie so panyini Kusa yerɛ Yohana, ne Susana ne mmaa foforɔ bebree nso ka ne ho; na bɛde bɛ ahodeɛ bi somm no.
Mfantoho a ɔfa abaguo ho Afei berɛ a nnipakuo kɛseɛ bi bɛkaa bɛ a bɛ ne no kokɔɔ nkuro nkuro so he ho he, ɔyɔɔ mfantoho bi kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Gufoɔ bi firii adi sɛ ookogu n’aba.
Na oogu aba he, bi koguu kwane nkyɛne ma betiatiaa so, na wiem nnomaa bɛsosɔeɛ.
Bi nso koguu abotane so, na ofifiriiɛ akyi he, owuiɛ esiane nsuo a wannya nti.
Bi nso koguu nkasɛe mu, na nkasɛe he nyini miaa no.
Bi nso guu asaase pa mu, na ofifiri soo aba mmɔho ha.” Berɛ a ɔkaa yeinom he, ɔmaa ne nne so kaa sɛ, “Ma nea ɔwɔ aso a ɔde betie he ntie.” Abaguo ho mfantoho he asekyerɛ Nso n’asuafoɔ he firii aseɛ bisaa no nea mfantoho yi kyerɛ.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Ho ne bɛde ama ho sɛ honte Nyankopɔn ahennie ho ahintasɛm he ase, na bɛ a bɛ aka he deɛ, bɛde mfantoho ne ka ho asɛm kyerɛ bɛ, na nti bɛbɛhwɛ deɛ, nso bɛbɛhwɛ no kwa, na bɛbɛte deɛ, nso bɛnte aseɛ.
“Afei bɛ he asekyerɛ di.
Aba he ne Nyankopɔn asɛm: Nea oguu kwane nkyɛne he ne bɛ a bɛteeɛ, na Bronsam beyii asɛm he firii bɛ akoma mu na bɛannye anni annya nkwa.
Nea oguu abotane so he gyna hɔ ma bɛ a bɛte asɛm he a bɛde anigye gye, nso yeinom nni nhini; bɛgyidi berɛ tiaa bi mu, nso oduru sɔhwɛ berɛ a, na bɛawae.
Na nea oguu nkasɛe mu he ne bɛ a bɛte asɛm he, nso asetena yi mu dadwene ne ahonya ne anigyeɛ twetwe bɛ, na emia bɛ koraa ma nti sɛ bɛso aba mpo a aba he nyini nwie.
Nea oguu asaase pa mu he, yɛ bɛ a bɛde akoma pa tie asɛm he wie a, bekura mu na bɛde boasetɔ so aba.
Kanea adwuma “Biaa nni hɔ a ɔsɔ kanea a, ɔde adeɛ bɛkata so anaa ɔde besi mpa ase, na mmom ɔde si kaneadua so, na ama bɛ a bɛba mu he ahu hann he.
Bibiaa nni hɔ a ahinta a ɔɔnna adi, na bibiaa nni hɔ a bɛakata so a benhu na ɔɔmma petee mu.
Nti, honhwɛ yie sɛnea hote asɛm he fa; na biaa a ɔwɔ he, bɛbɛma no pii, na nea onni he deɛ, nea osusuu sɛ ɔwɔ he mpo, bɛbɛgye afiri ne nsam.” Yesu abusuafoɔ kann Afei Yesu maame ne ne nuanom baa baabi a ɔya he, nso nnipakuo he nti, bɛantumi annuru ne nkyɛne.
Na bɛbɔɔ no amaneɛ sɛ, “Wo maame ne wo nuanom gyina abɔntene pɛ sɛ behu wo.” Na obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Me maame ne me nuanom ne nnipa a bɛte Nyankopɔn asɛm na bɛyɔ.” Ahum asebrɛ Da koro bi, Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he kɔtenaa kodoɔ bi mu, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ.
“Homma yentwa nkɔ tadeɛ he agya nohoa.” Nti besiim kɔeɛ.
Na bɛya nsuo he so he, ɔdaeɛ.
Afei mframa kɛseɛ bi bɔ baa tadeɛ he so, na nsuo he firii aseɛ bu faa bɛ so a na ayɛ hu ama bɛ.
Afei bɛkɔɔ ne nkyɛne konyanee no kaa sɛ.
“Owura, Owura, yeebewuwu!” Onyaneeɛ he, ɔteateaa mframa he ne nsuo a abu afa so he, na ano brɛɛ ase, na ɔyɛɛ dinn.
Afei obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Ho gyidie ya he?” Nso hu kaa bɛ, na bɛde ahodwiri keka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Hwane koraa di a otumi hyɛ mframa ne nsuo mpo ma bɛyɛ setie ma no yi?” Ahonhommɔne tuo Na bekoduruu Gerasefoɔ asaase a ɔne Galilea di animhwɛ so.
Na osii fam he, beema bi a ɔwɔ honhommɔne a ofiri kuro he mu behyiaa no.
Na berɛ tentene di a na omfiraa ntoma, na ɔnte dane biaa mu, na mmom amusieɛ ne ɔte.
Ohuu Yesu he, ɔteaam dendenndene hwee n’anim de nne kɛseɛ kaa sɛ.
“Ɛɛne ne me ne wo wɔ yɔ, Yesu, Sorosoroni Nyankopɔn he Ba?
Mesrɛ wo, nha me!” (Na ɔɔhyɛ Honhom fĩ he sɛ omfiri beema he mu.
Na waanya no so tumi berɛ tentene di, na bɛtaa de nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn ne mpokyerɛ gu no wɛne no, nso ɔtete mpokyerɛ he mu na honhom fĩ he twe no kɔ baabi a biaa nni.)
Na Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Wo dini de sɛ?” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Mene dodoɔ” efiri sɛ na honhommɔne pii ahyɛ ne mu.
Na bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔnnhyɛ bɛ mmma bemfiri ne mu nkɔ bunu he mu.
Na mprako pii oodidi bepɔ he so; nti bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔmma bɛ kwane ma bɛnkɔhyɛ bɛ mu.
Na ɔmaa bɛ kwane.
Nti honhommɔne he firii beema he mu kɔhyɛɛ mprako he mu, na mprako he bɔɔ twi firii bepɔ he so koguu tadeɛ he mu wuwuiɛ.
Berɛ a bɛ a bɛɛhwɛ mmoa he huu nea asi he, bedwane kɔbɔɔ amaneɛ kuro he mu ne nkuraa ase.
Afei nkurofoɔ baa sɛ bɛbɛhwɛ nea asi, na bɛbaa Yesu nkyɛne behuu beema a bɛatu honhommɔne afiri ne mu he sɛ ɔhyɛ ataadeɛ te Yesu nane ase, a n’dwene mu ate; na bɛ ho dwirii bɛ.
Bɛ a behuiɛ he kaa sɛnea ɔyɛɛ a beema a ɔwɔ honhommɔne he ho tɔɔ no he kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Nti nnipadɔm a befiri Gerasefoɔ nsaase a atwa hɔ ahyia he nyinaa ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ omfiri bɛ nkyɛne nkɔ, efiri sɛ na hu kɛseɛ aka bɛ.
Afei ɔtenaa kodoɔ he mu siim sɛ ɔɔkɔ.
Na beema a honhommɔne firii ne mu he kɔɔ so srɛɛ noaa sɛ ɔne no bɛkɔ; nso Yesu gyaa ne kwane kaa sɛ, “Sane kɔ fie, na kɔka nea Nyankopɔn ayɛ ama wo he kyerɛ.” Nti ofirii hɔ kɔeɛ, pae mu kaa nea Yesu ayɛ ama no he kuro he mu nyinaa.
Yairo babaa Berɛ a Yesu sane baeɛ he, nnipakuo he gyee no fɛ so, efiri sɛ na bɛ nyinaa bɛɛhwɛ no kwane.
Saa berɛ heaa beema bi a ne dini de Yairo a ɔyɛ hyiadane mu panyini baeɛ.
Na ɔbɛhwee Yesu nane ase srɛɛ no sɛ ɔmmra ne fie, efiri sɛ na ɔwɔ babaa korɔ pɛ a wadi bɛyɛ mfie dummienu a ɔda awusu.
Berɛ a ɔɔkɔ he, nnipadɔm he kyere ne so.
Baa bi ayaresa Na baa bi a mogyaa atu no mfie dummienu, a biaa ntumi nsaa no yadeɛ, kɔfaa Yesu n’akyi de ne nsa bɛkaa n’ataadeɛ ngugusoɔ ano, na amonom hɔaa mogyaa he twaeɛ.
Nti Yesu bisaa sɛ, “Hwane ne de ne nsa kaa me he?” Berɛ a bɛ nyinaa bɛkaa sɛ ɔnyɛ bɛ he, Petro kaa sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, nnipadɔm yi afum wo ho na bɛakyere wo so.” Nso Yesu kaa sɛ, “Bi de ne nsa aka me, maahu sɛ tumi bi afiri me mu kɔ.” Berɛ a baa he huu sɛ wahu no he, ɔde ahopopoɔ bɛhwee n’anim kaa deɛ nti a ɔde ne nsa kaa no ne sɛnea ne ho tɔɔ no amonom hɔaa he nnipa he nyinaa anim.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ.
“Babaa, wo gyidie agye wo nkwa; fa asomdwie kɔ.” Yairo babaa wunyane Na ogu so ɔɔkasa he, bi firi hyiadane mu panyini he fie bɛka kyerɛɛ Yairo sɛ, “Wo babaa he awu; nha kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he bio.” Berɛ a Yesu teeɛ he, obuaa no sɛ, “Nsuro, wo deɛ, gyidie nkoaa ne hia, na obenya nkwa.” Berɛ a Yesu duruu fie hɔ he, wamma biaa ne no ankɔ mu gye Petro ne Yohane ne Yakobo ne abaayaa he papa ne ne maame nkoaa.
Nso na nkurofoɔ oosu twa agyaadwoɔ.
Nti ɔkaa sɛ, “Honnyae su, onwuiɛ na mmom waada.” Yei nti bɛsree no, efiri sɛ na benim sɛ waawu.
Na ɔsɔɔ ne nsa maa no so frɛɛ no sɛ.
“Abaayaa, sɔre!” Na abaayaa he honhom sane baeɛ, na ɔsɔree ntɛmaa, na ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛmma no bibi nni.
Na n’awofoɔ he ho dwirii bɛ; nso ɔhyɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛnka nea asi he nkyerɛ biaa.
Yesu somaa asuafoɔ dummienu he Afei Yesu frɛɛ dummienu he nyinaa maa bɛ ahoɔdene ne tumi a bɛde betutu ahonhommɔne nyinaa na bɛde bɛsa yadeɛ nso.
Na ɔsomaa bɛ sɛ bɛnkɔ pae mu nka Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho asɛm na bɛnsa yadeɛ, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hommfa hwee ntu kwane he, hommfa poma anaa bɔtɔ, paanoo anaa sika; hommfa ntaadeɛ nhyɛaseɛ mmienu nso.
Na fie biaa a hobɛhyɛne mu he, hontena hɔ kosi sɛ hobefiri hɔ akɔ.
Na baabiaa a nnipa annye ho he, sɛ hoofiri kuro he mu akɔ a, homporoporo ho nane ase mfuturo ngu hɔ ma ɔnyɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne sɛ hoapo bɛ.” Yei akyi he, besiim kɔɔ nkuraa ase, kaa asɛmpa he na bɛsaa nyarewa baabiaa.
Herode pɛɛ sɛ ohu Yesu Na Herode a ɔyɛ mantam sodifoɔ he tee nnoɔma a ɔɔkɔ so he nyinaa, na ne tim yɛɛ no kesenenee, efiri sɛ na binom ɔɔkeka sɛ bɛanyane Yohane afiri awufoɔ mu, na binom nso dɛ Elia aba, na afoforɔ nso dɛ tete adiyifoɔ he mu bi asɔre.
Herode kaa sɛ.
“Maatwa Yohane ti.
Afei hwane ne meetete ne ho asɛm sei yi?” Nti ɔhwehwɛɛ sɛ obehu no.
Yesu maa nnipa mpemnum aduane Na berɛ a asomafoɔ he sane baeɛ he, bɛkaa nnoɔma a bɛayɔ he kyerɛɛ Yesu.
Nti ɔne bɛ twee bɛ ho kɔhyɛɛ kokoam baabi, kuro bi a bɛfrɛ no Betsaida mu.
Nso berɛ a nnipadɔm he huiɛ he, bedii n’akyi.
Na ɔgyee bɛ fɛ so firii aseɛ kaa Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho asɛm kyerɛɛ bɛ, na ɔsaa bɛ a bɛyare he yadeɛ.
Afei na adeɛ ɔɔsa.
Na dummienu he ba bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Gya nnipadɔm yi kwane na ama bɛatumi akɔ nkuraa-nkuraa a atwa ahyia he ase akɔpɛ daberɛ ne nnoɔma a behia, efiri sɛ baabi a yɛya yi mmɛne fie.” Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Homma bɛ bibi nni.” Bɛkaa sɛ, “Yenni hwee sɛ paanoo num ne nkyenam mmienu, gye sɛ ebia yɛ ankasa yɛkɔtɔ aduane bra nnipa yi nyinaa.” Na bɛbɛyɛ mmeema mpemnum.
Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Homma bɛtenatena ase akuoakuo bɛyɛ aduonum aduonum.” Na bɛyɔɔ saa maa bɛ nyinaa bɛtenatenaa ase.
Afei Yesu faa paanoo num ne nkyenam mmienu he, ɔhwɛɛ soro hyiraa so bubuu mu de maa asuafoɔ he sɛ bɛmfa nsisi nnipa akuoakuo he anim.
Nti bɛ nyinaa bedidi meeɛ, na berɛ a bɛsesaa aseɛ mproprowa he, benyaa nkɛntɛne dummienu ma ma.
Petro paee mu kaa sɛ Yesu yɛ Nyankopɔn Ba Afei berɛ a na Yesu nkoaa hyɛ baabi ɔɔbɔ mpaeɛ he, asuafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne, na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Nnipakuo he, bɛdɛ me ne hwane?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Binom dɛ woyɛ Yohane Suboni; na binom dɛ woyɛ Elia, na binom nso dɛ woyɛ tete adiyifoɔ he mu baako a wasɔre.” Afei obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Na ho nso hodɛ me ne hwane?” Petro buaa sɛ, “Wone Kristo a ofiri Nyankopɔn nkyɛne he.” Yesu hyɛɛ ne wuo ne ne wusɔreɛ ho nkɔm Na Yesu braa bɛ ketee sɛ bɛnnka nkyerɛ biaa, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Otwa sɛ Nipa Ba he hu amaneɛ pii na mpanyimfoɔ ne asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he po no, na beku no, na da a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he Nyankopɔn anyane no afiri awufoɔ mu.” Ahopakyie Afei ɔtoaa so ka kyerɛɛ bɛ nyinaa sɛ, “Sɛ bi pɛ sɛ odi m’akyi a, ma ɔmpa ne ho akyi, ɔmfa n’asennua na onni m’akyi daa.
Na biaa a ɔpɛ sɛ ne nsa ka ne kra he, ne kra bɛhwere no; nso biaa a me nti ɔbɛhwere ne kra he, bɛbɛgye no nkwa.
Sɛ nipa nya wiase nyinaa na ɔhwere ne nkwa a abɛ mfasoɔ koraa ne ya so?
Na biaa a ɔbɛma n’ani awu me ne m’asɛm ho he, ɔno nso ho bɛyɛ nipa Ba he aniwuo berɛ a mede m’Agya animuonyam bɛba, a abɔfoɔ kronkron ka me ho he.
Nɔkwasɛm, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, bɛ a begyina ha yi mu bi ya hɔ a bɛnka wuo nhwɛ da kosi sɛ bebehu Nyankopɔn ahennie he.” Yesu animuonyam hyerɛn Na afei, nsɛm yi akyi bɛyɛ nnanwɔtwe he, Yesu faa Petro ne Yohane ne Yakobo kaa ne ho foro kɔɔ bepɔ so kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ.
Na ogu so ɔɔbɔ mpaeɛ he, n’anim tebea sakraeɛ na n’ataadeɛ yɛɛ fitaa hyerɛnhyerɛn.
Na afei hwɛ, mmeema mmienu ne no bɛkasaeɛ.
Saa mmeemaa mmienu yi ne Mose ne Elia.
Yeinom yii bɛ ho adi animuonyam mu, na bɛkaa ne wuo a otwa sɛ owu Yerusalem he ho asɛm.
Na aaka Petro ne bɛ a bɛka ne ho he; na berɛ a bɛ ani so tetee bɛ he, behuu n’animuonyam he ne mmeema mmienu a bɛ ne no gyina hɔ he.
Na berɛ a yeinom oogya ne hɔ akɔ he, Petro ka kyerɛɛ Yesu sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, ɔyɛ sɛ yɛya ha, nti ma yensi apata mmeɛnsa, wo deɛ baako, Mose deɛ baako, Elia nso deɛ baako,” na ɔno deɛ na onnim nea ɔɔka.
Na berɛ a ɔɔkasa he, mununkum bi ba bɛkataa bɛ so.
Berɛ a bɛhyɛ mununkum he mu he, besuroeɛ.
Na nne bi firi mununkum he mu kaa sɛ.
“Yei ne me Ba, nea m’ayi no he, hontie no.” Na nne he baeɛ akyi he, behuu Yesu nkoaa.
Nso bɛyɛɛ komm a bɛanka nea behuiɛ yi mu biaa ho asɛm ankyerɛ biaa saa nna he mu.
Abɔfra twafoɔ bi ayaresa Na ɔbaa sɛ adeɛ kyeeɛ he, berɛ a befiri bepɔ he so sianeeɛ he, nnipadɔm bi behyiaa no.
Na hwɛ, beema bi firi nnipadɔm he mu teaam sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, mesrɛ wo hwɛ me ba yi, efiri sɛ ɔyɛ me ba koro pɛ, na hwɛ, honhom bi ba ne so, na ɔteaam prɛko pɛ, na otwa no hwe fam sensene no ma n’ano pu ahuro, na obu fa so, na ɔha no kyɛre paa ansa na wafiri ne so.
Na mesrɛɛ w’asuafoɔ he sɛ bentu honhom he mfiri ne so, nso bɛantumi.” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Ho saa awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ kontonkyi a honni gyidie, me ne ho ntena na mennya ho ho aboterɛ nkosi da bɛne?
Fa wo ba he bra ha.” Na abeemaa he ɔɔbɛne Yesu he, honhommɔne he ma otwa hwee fam na ɔsensenee dendenndene.
Nso Yesu kaa honhom fĩ he anim, na ɔsaa abeemaa he yadeɛ de no maa ne papa.
Yesu hyɛɛ ne yima ne ne wuo ho nkɔm Afei bɛ nyinaa bɛho dwirii bɛ Nyankopɔn tumi kɛseɛ he ho.
Na berɛ a nnoɔma a ɔyɔeɛ he nyinaa yɛɛ bɛ nyinaa ahodwiri he, ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ: “Honwɛne ho aso ntie saa nsɛm yi, na otwa sɛ beyi Nipa Ba he hyɛ adasamma nsa.” Nso bɛante saa asɛm yi ase, efiri sɛ na bɛde ahinta bɛ na bɛanhu mu, nso na besuro sɛ bebebisa no asɛm yi ho nkyerɛmu.
Ahobrɛaseɛ ne nuadɔ Afei akyinyegyeɛ bi sɔree asuafoɔ he mu a na ɔfa deɛ ɔbɛyɛ bɛ mu kɛseɛ ho.
Berɛ a Yesu huu bɛ akoma mu nsusuiɛ he, ɔfaa abɔfra kumaa bi de no gyinaa ne nkyɛne; na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Biaa a ɔbɛgye abɔfra yi me dini mu he, na waagye me nso, na biaa a ɔbɛgye me he, na waagye nea ɔsomaa me he nso.
Na nea ɔyɛ ne ho kumaa ya ho nyinaa mu he, ɔno ne bɛyɛ kɛseɛ paa.” Yohane buaa sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, yehuu bi a na ɔde wo dini ootu ahonhommɔne na yɛbɔɔ mmɔdene sɛ yebesi no kwane, efiri sɛ ɔnyɛ wo kyidifoɔ.” Nso Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Honnsi no kwane, efiri sɛ nea ɔnsɔre ntia ho he ya ho afã.” Samariafoɔ atimuɔdenfoɔ Berɛ a nna he ɔɔbɛne ama bɛafa Yesu akɔ soro he, ɔde sii n’ani so dendenndene sɛ ɔbɛkɔ Yerusalem.
Nti otuu abɔfoɔ dii n’anim.
Na besii kwane so kɔɔ Samariafoɔ akuraa bi ase sɛ beekosiesie hɔ ama no; nso bɛannye no, efiri sɛ na n’ani kyerɛ Yerusalem.
Berɛ a Yakobo ne Yohane a bɛ nso bɛyɛ Yesu asuafoɔ he huu yei he bebisaa sɛ, “Awurade, wopɛ sɛ yɛhyɛ ma gya firi soro bɛtɔre bɛ ase?” Nso ɔdane n’ani kaa bɛ anim.
Afei bɛkɔɔ akuraa foforɔ ase.
Bɛ a bɛɛpɛ bibi ayɔ ansa na bɛadi Kristo akyi Berɛ a bɛnam kwane so he, bi ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Medi w’akyi akɔ baabiaa a wobɛkɔ biaa.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sakramane wɔ bɔno, na wiem nnomaa wɔ pirebuo, nso Nipa Ba he nni baabi a ɔde ne ti bɛto.” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ foforɔ sɛ, “Di m’akyi.” Beema he kaa sɛ, “Ma me kwane ma menkosie me papa ansa.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ma awufoɔ nsie bɛ awufoɔ, na wo deɛ, kɔka Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho asɛm.” Na foforɔ nso kaa sɛ, “Awurade, medi w’akyi; nso ma me kwane ma menkɔkra me fiefoɔ ansa.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Biaa nni hɔ a ɔde ne nsa akɔsɔ funtumdadeɛ mu na ɔhwɛ nnoɔma a ɔya n’akyi a ɔfata Nyankopɔn ahennie he.”
Asɛmpakafoɔ aduɔson he Yeinom akyi he, Awurade yii nnipa foforɔ aduɔson somaa bɛ mmienu mmienu dii n’anim kɔɔ kuro biaa ne baabiaa a na ɔno ankasa ɔɔbɛkɔ hɔ.
Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Twa adwuma he sõ, nso adwumayɔfoɔ he sua.
Nti honsrɛ twa he Wura he na ɔnsoma adwumayɔfoɔ mmra ne twa he mu.
Honkɔ.
Hwɛ, meesoma ho sɛ nwammaa akɔ mpataku mu.
Hommfa sika bɔtɔ, aduane bɔtɔ, anaa mpaboa, sɛ honam kwane so ɔɔkɔ a homma nkyea mfa ho mmerɛ bebree.
Baabiaa a hobɛhyɛne fie bi mu he, honni kane nka sɛ, ‘Asomdwie mmra fie yi mu!’ Na sɛ nipa bi ya hɔ a ɔɔhwehwɛ asomdwie a, ho asomdwie bɛkɔ no so.
Nso sɛ bi nni hɔ saa a, ho asomdwie bɛsane aba ho so.
Nti hontena saa fie he mu, na honni na honnom nea bɛde bɛma ho he, efiri sɛ dwumayɔni fata sɛ onya akatua.
Honntu mmfiri fie baako mu nkɔ foforɔ mu kɔpem sɛ hobewie adwuma hooyɔ kuro he mu he.
“Afei nso, berɛ biaa a hobɛhyɛne kuro bi mu na bɛbɛgye ho he, honni nea bɛde besi ho anim he, na honsa mu ayarefoɔ yadeɛ, na honka nkyerɛ bɛ sɛ, ‘Nyankopɔn ahennie he abɛne ho.’ Nso berɛ biaa a hobɛhyɛne kuro bi mu a bɛannye ho he, homfiri adi nkɔ n’atempɔno so na honka sɛ, ‘Ho kuro yi mu mfuturo mpo a oguu yɛ nane ho he, yɛ aporoporo agu ho so.
Nso, homma ɔntena ho adwene mu sɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie he abɛne.’ Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ atemmuda da he, Nyankopɔn behu Sodom mmɔbɔ asene saa kuro he.
Korasin, Betsaida ne Kapernaum “Korasin, due!
Betsaida, due!
Efiri sɛ ahoɔdenneɛ a bɛayɔ no ho mu yi, sɛ bɛyɔɔ no Tiro ne Sidon a, nka bɛsakra bɛ adwene ntɛm so firaa ayitoma de nsõ guguu bɛ tim.
Nti Nyankopɔn behu Tiro ne Sidon mmɔbɔ atemmuo he mu akyɛne ho.
Na wo Kapernaum, bɛbɛma wo so akɔ soro anaa?
Daabi!
Asamando ne wobɛsiane akɔ!
“Nea otie ho he tie me nso.
Na nea obu ho animtia he bu me nso animtia.
Afei nso, nea obu me animtia he bu nea ɔsomaa me he nso animtia.” Aduɔson he saneba Na nnipa aduɔson he de anigye sane baeɛ bɛkaa sɛ, “Awurade, wo dini a yɛde yɔɔ adwuma nti ahohommɔne mpo brɛɛ bɛ ho ase maa yɛ!” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Maahu sɛ Satan firi soro ahwe ase sɛ anyinam.
Hwɛ, maama ho tumi a hode betiatia awɔ ne naanantwi so, ne nea hode bedi tamfoɔ he tumi nyinaa so, na bɔne biaa ɔnto ho da.
Nso honnni yei ho ahurusie, sɛ ahonhom abrɛ bɛ ho ase ama ho, na mmom honni ahurusie sɛ bɛatwerɛ ho dini soro.” Yesu aseda mpaebɔ Saa dɔno heaa mu he, anigye hyɛɛ Yesu mã Honhom Kronkron mu, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Agya, soro ne asaase Wura, meyi wo ayɛ, efiri sɛ yeinom ahinta anyansafoɔ ne animdefoɔ, na woayi no adi akyerɛ mpapahwekwaa.
Ɔyɛ ampa, Agya, efiri sɛ ɔyɛ wo pɛ sɛ ɔba saa.
M’Agya de nnoɔma nyinaa ahyɛ me nsa, na biaa nnim onii ko a Ba he yɛ, gye Agya he; na biaa nnim onii a Agya he yɛ, gye Ba he ne nea Ba he pɛ sɛ ɔda no adi kyerɛ no nkoaa.” Afei ɔdanee ne ho kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Nhyira ne ani a ohu nnoɔma a hohu yi!
Na meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, adiyifoɔ ne ahemfo bebree pɛɛ sɛ behu nnoɔma a hohu yi nso bɛanhu, bɛpɛɛ sɛ bɛte nsɛm a hote yi nso bɛante.” Hwane ne me yɔnkɔ paa?
Afei, hwɛ, beema bi a onim Mmara he sɔree sɛ ɔɔsɔ no ahwɛ, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, abɛ paa ne sɛ meyɔ a, menya daa nkwa?” Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Ɛɛne ne bɛatwerɛ Mmara he mu?
Mmɛ ne wokenkane firii Mmara he mu?” Obuaa sɛ, “Ɔsɛ sɛ wode wo akoma nyinaa, ne wo kra nyinaa, ne wo ahoɔdene nyinaa, ne w’adwene nyinaa dɔ Awurade wo Nyankopɔn, na wodɔ wo yɔnko sɛ wo ho.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Woabua no yei; kɔ so yɔ yei na wobenya nkwa.” Nso, beema he pɛɛ sɛ obu ne ho bem nti, obisaa Yesu sɛ, “Na hwane ne me yɔnko?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Na beema bi firi Yerusalem oosiane akɔ Yeriko, na ɔkɔtɔɔ akwamukafoɔ mu ma bɛworɔɔ ne ho ntaadeɛ bobɔɔ no, gyaa no hɔ kɔeɛ a na watɔ baha.
Afei, ɔbaa sɛ na sɔfo bi ootwam saa kwane he so, nso berɛ a ohuu no he, ɔfaa kwane he fã baabi kɔeɛ.
Saa nso ne berɛ a Lewini bi nso duruu hɔ a ohuu no he, ɔfaa kwane he fã baabi kɔeɛ.
Yei akyi he, Samariani bi a ɔnam kwane he so ootu kwane bɛtoo no, na ohuu no he, ɔyɛɛ no mmɔbɔ.
Nti ɔkɔɔ ne nkyɛne de aduro kekaa n’akuro he mu kyekyeree so.
Afei ɔde no tenaa n’ankasa aboa so de no kɔɔ ahɔhodane mu kɔhwɛɛ no.
Na adeɛ kyeeɛ he, oyii sika a ne dodoɔ bɛyɛ paani nnaanu akatua de maa ahɔhodane sohwɛfoɔ he kaa sɛ, ‘Hwɛ no, na ka biaa a wobɛbɔ yei akyi he, mesane ba a, metua ama wo.’ Saa nnipa mmeɛnsa yi mu deɛ ɔya he ne wosusu sɛ wada ne ho adi sɛ beema a ɔkɔtɔɔ akwamukafoɔ mu he yɔnko paa?” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Nea ohuu no mmɔbɔ he a.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kɔ na wo nso kɔyɔ saa.” Marta ne Maria Afei berɛ a bɛɛkɔ he, ɔkɔɔ akuraa bi ase.
Ha ne baa bi a bɛfrɛ no Marta gyee no kɔɔ fie sɛ hɔhoɔ.
Na saa baa yi wɔ nuabaa bi a bɛfrɛ no Maria, na ɔno deɛ ɔtenaa Awurade nane ase tiee asɛm a na ɔɔka he.
Nso Marta deɛ, na nnwuma bebree agye n’adwene.
Nti ɔba bɛkaa sɛ, “Awurade, wonhu sɛ me nuabaa he agya me hɔ a me nkoaa ne meeyɔ adeɛ nyinaa?
Nti ka kyerɛ no na ɔmmɛboa me.” Nso Awurade buaa no sɛ, “Marta, Marta, wodwendwene bebree na wode nnoɔma pii ha wo ho.
Nso, adeɛ baako pɛ ne hia.
Maria deɛ, waayi nea ɔyɛ he, ɔno ne bɛnnye mfiri ne nsam.”
Awurade mpaebɔ Na afei na Yesu ya baabi ɔɔbɔ mpaeɛ.
Na owiee mpaebɔ he, n’asuafoɔ he mu baako ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade, kyerɛ yɛ sɛnea bɛbɔ mpaeɛ, sɛnea Yohane nso kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he.” Nti ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Berɛ biaa a hobɛbɔ mpaeɛ he, honka sɛ, “Agya, anidie nka wo dini.
W’ahennie mmra.
Ma yɛ aduane nnɛ nso, sɛnea wode ma yɛ daa he.
Na fa yɛ bɔne kyɛ yɛ, sɛnea yɛ ankasa nso yɛde akyɛ bɛ a bɛde yɛ ka.
Na nnyae yɛ mma yɛnkɔ sɔhwɛ mu.” Mpaebɔ ho nsiyɛ Bio nso, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho mu hwane ne wɔ adamfoɔ a ɔbɛkɔ ne nkyɛne dasuom akɔka akyerɛ no sɛ, ‘Damfo, fɛm me paanoo mmeɛnsa, na m’adamfoɔ bi firi kwane so aba me nkyɛne, na menni hwee a mede bɛma no adi.’ Na n’adamfoɔ he bebua sɛ, ‘Nha m’adwene.
Yɛato pono he mu dada, na me ne mma ada; mentumi nsɔre mmɛma wo hwee.’ Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, sɛ ɔkaa sɛ ɔyɛ n’adamfoɔ nkoaa deɛ a, nka ɔnsɔre mmɛma no hwee, nso esiane sɛ odwane ne ho nti ɔbɛsɔre abɛma no nea ohia.
Bɔhyɛ ahodoɔ mmeɛnsa Nti meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, hommisa, na bɛde bɛma ho; honhwehwɛ, na hobehu; hommom na bebebie ho.
Na biaa a obisa he onya, na biaa a ɔhwehwɛ he ohu, na biaa a obom he bebebie no.
Ho mu hwane koraa ne ɔyɛ agya a sɛ ne ba bisa no adwene a, ɔde wɔ bɛma no na ɔmma no adwene?
Anaa sɛ obisa kosua nso a, ɔde naanantwi bɛma no?
Nti, sɛ ho a hoyɛ abɔnefoɔ mpo nim sɛnea hode akyɛdeɛ pa ma ho mma a, mprɛ dodoɔ sɛ ne ho Agya a ɔya soro he mfa Honhom Kronkron mma bɛ a bebisa no?” Nkɔnkɔnsa bi ho mmuaeɛ Afei na Yesu ootu honhommɔne afiri mum bi mu.
Honhommɔne he firiiɛ he, beema a ɔyɛ mum he kasaeɛ.
Na ɔyɛɛ nnipadɔm he nwanwa.
Nso bɛ mu binom kaa sɛ, “Ɔnam ahonhommɔne panyini Beelsebul so ne ootu ahonhommɔne.” Nso, binom a na bɛpɛ sɛ bɛsɔ no hwɛ firii aseɛ hwehwɛɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne a ofiri soro firii ne hɔ.
Na ohuu bɛ nsusuiɛ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ.
“Ahennie biaa a ɔne ne ho di asie he dane amamfõõ, na fie a mpaapaemu yam he nso bɔ.
Na sɛ Satan nso ne ne ho di asie a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na n’ahennie agyina?
Meeka yei, efiri sɛ hodɛ menam Beelsebul so ne metu ahonhommɔne.
Sɛ menam Beelsebul so ne metu ahonhommɔne a, ɔnam hwane so ne ho nkurofoɔ nso tu bɛ?
Yei nti hoaa ho nkurofoɔ he bebu ho atɛne.
Na sɛ menam Nyankopɔn tumi so ne metu ahonhommɔne a, hedeɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie ayi ne ho adi akyerɛ ho.
Bronsam tumi so nkunimdie Sɛ beema hoɔdenfoɔ bi hyehyɛ ne ho wɛne n’aban a, n’agyapadeɛ nya ahobammɔ.
