Nso sɛ bi a ne ho ɔdene sene no bɛto hyɛ no so di no so a, ɔgye n’akodeɛ a ɔde ne ho to so he nyinaa, na ɔkyɛ nnoɔma a ɔfa firi ne nkyɛne he nyinaa.
Nea onni m’afa he ko tia me, na nea ɔne me mmoaboa ano he nso hwete nea m’aboaboa ano he mu.
Honhom fĩ akyisane “Sɛ Honhom fĩ bi firi nipa mu a, okokyinkyini akwaweɛ so kɔhwehwɛ homebea, na sɛ wannya bi a, ɔka sɛ ‘Mɛsane akɔ me fie a metu firii mu he mu.’ Na ɔba a, obehu sɛ bɛaprapra mu kama de nnoɔma asiesie mu.
Nti ɔsane kɔ kɔfa Honhom nson foforɔ a bɛyɛ werɛmfoɔ sene no ka he ho, na bɛba mu bɛtena hɔ; na saa nipa he awieeɛ sɛe sene kane he.” Setie Na Yesu gu so ɔɔka yeinom he, baa bi firi nnipakuo he mu teaam ka sɛ, “Nhyira ne yafunu a ɔnyinsɛne wo ne nofoɔ a wonomeeɛ!” Nso ɔkaa sɛ, “Daabi, mmom, nhyira ne bɛ a betie Nyankopɔn asɛm na bedi so!” Yudafoɔ fɔdie kyɛne amanamane mufoɔ deɛ Berɛ a nnipakuo he ɔɔboaboa bɛ ho ano he, ofirii aseɛ kaa sɛ, “Awoɔ ntoatoaso yi yɛ awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ bɔne; bɛhwehwɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne.
Nso bɛmma bɛ sɛnkyerɛnne biaa ka Yona nsɛnkyerɛnne he ho.
Na sɛnea Yona bɛyɛɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne maa Ninewefoɔ he, saa ne nipa Ba he nso bɛyɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne ama awo ntoatoaso yi.
Bebenyane anafoɔ fam hemmaa he ne saa awo ntoatoasoɔ yi mu nnipa atemmuo he mu na obebu bɛ fɔ; efiri sɛ ofiri asaase ano betiee Salomo nyansa, nso hwɛ, nea ɔsene Salomo ya ha.
Bebenyane Ninewefoɔ ne awo ntoatoaso yi atemmuo mu; na bebebu ntoatoaso yi fɔ, efiri sɛ Ninewefoɔ he sakraa bɛ adwene berɛ a Yona bɔɔ bɛ kɔkɔ he; nso, hwɛ, nea ɔsene Yona ya ha.
Kanea adwuma “Sɛ bi sɔ kanea a, ɔmfa nsi kokoam, saa ara nso ne ɔmfa nhyɛ kodoɔ ase, na mmom ɔde si kaneadua so, sɛnea bɛ a bɛba mu he behu hann he.
Nipadua he kanea ne ani.
Nti sɛ w’ani yɛ a, wo nipadua nyinaa nso hyerɛn; na sɛ ɔnyɛ a, wo nipadua nso bɛyɛ kusuu.
Nti, homma ho ani nna hɔ; na hann a ɔya ho mu he annane sum.
Nti, sɛ wo nipadua nyinaa hyerɛn na baabiaa nyɛ sum a, ne nyinaa bɛhyerɛn te sɛ nea kanea hyerɛn ma benya hann he.” Farisini bi fie adidie Berɛ a Yesu kaa yei he, Farisini bi srɛɛ no sɛ ɔne no mmedidi.
Nti ɔkɔɔ hɔ kɔtenaa adidipono ho.
Nso, berɛ a Farisini no huu sɛ wanni kane anhohoro ne nsa ansa na oodidi he, ɔyɛɛ no nwanwa.
Na Awurade ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ho Farisifoɔ, ho hohoro kuruwa ne ayowa ho, na ho mu deɛ, amim ne nnebɔne ahyɛ mã: Nnipa a honni adwene!
Ɔnyɛ nea ɔyɔɔ akyi heaa ne yɔɔ mu he nso?
Nso, homfa nea ɔya mu he nyɔ adɔeɛ, na hwɛ, nnoɔma a aka nyinaa ho ate ho fam.
“Na ho Farisifoɔ deɛ, honnue, efiri sɛ hoyi mẽẽ, nunum ne kumin nyinaa so ntotosoɔ du du, nso hototo atɛntenenee ne Nyankopɔn dɔ ase!
Saa nnoɔma yi ne ɔsɛ sɛ nka hoyɔ, na nea aka he nso ɔnsɛ sɛ hoyi firi mu.
Honnue, ho Farisifoɔ, efiri sɛ hopɛ hyia adane mu nkonnwa a osisi animu ne dwa so nkyea!
Honnue, efiri sɛ hote sɛ adamena a ahinta na nnipa nante so a bennim!” Afei mmarakyerɛfoɔ he mu baako buaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, sɛ woka saa a yɛ nso woadidi yɛ atɛm.” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Ho nso Honnue, ho a honim mmara he, efiri sɛ hode nnesoa a mu oduru soa nnipa, nso ho ankasa hommfa ho nsateaa baako mpo nka nnesoa he!
“Honnue sɛ hoto adiyifoɔ a ho agyanom ne kuu bɛ nna so!
Nɔkorem he, hoyɛ ho agyanom nnwuma ho adansefoɔ, nso hofoa bɛ so, efiri sɛ yeinom ne bekuu adiyifoɔ he, na ho ne hooto bɛ nna so.
Yei nti na Nyankopɔn nyansa nso kaa sɛ, ‘Mɛsoma adiyifoɔ ne asomafoɔ akɔ bɛ nkyɛne, na bebeku bɛ mu binom ataa binom.
Nti ne bebebisa adiyifoɔ he nyinaa mogyaa a bɛahwie agu firi wiase ahyaseɛ afiri awo ntoatoaso yi hɔ, efiri Habel mogyaa so kosi Sakaria a bekuu no afɔrebokyia he ntomadane he ntam he mogyaa so.’ Ɛɛ, meka akyerɛ ho sɛ bebebisa afiri awo ntoatoaso yi hɔ.
“Honnue, ho mmarakyerɛfoɔ, efiri sɛ hoagye nimdeɛ safoa he, nso ho ankasa hoankɔ mu, na bɛ a bɛɛkɔ mu he nso hosi bɛ kwane!” Nti ofirii hɔ he, Atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he befumm ne ho na bebisabisaa no nsɛm foforɔ pii de hyɛɛ no abufuo na bɛtɛɛ no hwɛɛ sɛ bebenya asɛm bi afiri n’anum anaa.
Nyaatwom ho kɔkɔbɔ Afei, berɛ a nnipakuo mpempem pii he dɔɔso ama bɛakyere so ama beetiatia bɛ ho bɛ ho he, Yesu dii kane ka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ.
“Honhwɛ yei Farisifoɔ mmɔreka a ɔyɛ nyaatwom he ho.
Na bibiaa nni hɔ a bɛakata so a ɔnna adi, anaa ahinta a benhu.
Nti bibiaa a hoaka no sum mu he bɛbɛte no hann mu, na nea hoaka agu aso mu kokoam he, bɛbɛpae mu aka no badwam.
Nnipa suro ho kɔkɔbɔ Bio nso, me nnamfonom, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, honnsuro bɛ a beku nipadua na ɔno akyi he bentumi nyɛ no hwee bio.
Na mmom mɛkyerɛ ho nea honsuro no.
Honsuro nea oku wie a ɔwɔ tumi sɛ ɔbɛto agu Gehenna (amanehunu kurom).
Ampa!
Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ: Ɔno ne honsuro no.
Bɛtɔno akasanoma nnum gye nkaprɛ mma mmienu, ɔnyɛ saa?
Nso bɛ mu baako mpo nni hɔ a Nyankopɔn werɛ firi no.
Na ho ti nwii mpo bɛakane ne nyinaa.
Nti honnsuro; hosom bo paa kyɛne nkasanoma bebree.
Ɔnsɛ sɛ yɛpa Kristo “Nti, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, biaa a ɔgye me tom nnipa anim he, Nipa Ba he nso bɛgye no atom Nyankopɔn abɔfoɔ anim.
Na nea ɔpa me nnipa anim he, Nipa Ba he nso bɛpa no Nyankopɔn abɔfoɔ anim.
Honhom Kronkron ne n’akwankyerɛ Na biaa a ɔbɛka asɛm bi atia Nipa Ba he, bɛde bɛkyɛ no; na nea ɔbɛka abususɛm atia Honhom Kronkron he deɛ, bɛmfa nkyɛ no.
Na sɛ bɛde ho kɔ hyia adane mu, mpanyimfoɔ ne atumfoɔ anim a, honnwennwene nea hode beyi ho ho ano anaa nea hobɛka ho; na dɔno heaa mu Honhom Kronkron bɛkyerɛ ho nnoɔma a ɔsɛ sɛ hoka.” Yesu mpɛ sɛ oyi atɛne Afei bi firi nnipakuo he mu ka kyerɛɛ Yesu sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, ka kyerɛ me nua na ɔne me nkyɛ awunnyadeɛ he.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Beema!
Hwane ne de me sii ho so temmufoɔ anaa dekyɛfoɔ?” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Homma ho ani nna hɔ na honhwɛ yie anibereɛ nyinaa ho, efiri sɛ, sɛ nipa nya ne ho ma obu so mpo a, ɔnyɛ nnoɔma a ɔwɔ he mu ne ne obenya ne nkwa.” Adufudepɛ Yei nti, ɔmaa bɛ mfantoho bi sɛ, “Defoɔ bi asaase soo aba pii.
Nti osusuu ne mu sɛ, ‘Ɛɛne ne menyɔ?
Efiri sɛ, menni baabi a mede me nnɔbae besie.’ Nti ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Nea meyɔ di.
Medwiri m’apata agu na masisi akɛseɛ, na hɔ ne mɛboaboa m’ayuo ne me nnoɔma pa nyinaa ano agu; na mɛka akyerɛ me kra sɛ, “ ‘Me kra, wowɔ nnoɔma pa pii a bɛaboa ano ama mfie pii, dwodwo wo ho, didi, nom, na gye w’ani.” ’ Nso Nyankopɔn ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Kwasea, anadwo yiaa bɛbɛgye wo kra afiri wo nsam.
Na ɔba saa a, hwane ne nnoɔma a wode asie he bɛyɛ ne dea?’ Saa ne nipa a ɔhyehyɛ agyapadeɛ fa nso ɔnyɛ defoɔ Nyankopɔn fam he teɛ.” Suro ne akyinnyegyeɛ Afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Yei nti, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, honnwennwene ho kra ho, nea hobedi anaa ho nipadua anaa nea hobɛhyɛ ho, efiri sɛ kra he som bo pii sene aduane, na nipadua he nso sombo sene ataadeɛ.
Honhwɛ sɛ nkwããkwããdabi a bennua aba biaa na bentwa, na benni adekoradane anaa pata, nso Nyankopɔn ma bɛ aduane.
Honnsom bo beberee nsene nnomaa anaa?
Ho mu hwane ne betumi adwendwene de dɔnhwere baako ato ne nkwa so?
Nti sɛ hontumi nyɔ nnoɔma nketewa a ɔte sei a, mmɛ nti ne hodwendwene nnoɔma a aka he ho?
Honhwɛ sɛnea asukooko nyini; ɔnyɛ adwuma na ɔnto asaawa; nso meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, Salomo animuonyam nyinaa mu mpo he, wanhyehyɛ ne ho kamakama sɛ yeinom mu baako mpo.
Nti sɛ Nyankopɔn fira wuram nhahane a ɔya hɔ nnɛ na kyena bɛtwa de agu fononoo mu ahye no he ntoma saa a, mmɛ nti ne ommfira ho mmom a ho ho hia he ntoma?
Oo!
ho a ho gyidie sua!
Nti, honnhwehwɛ nea hobedi ne nea hobɛnom, na honnwennwene nnha ho ho; efiri sɛ yeinom nyinaa ne nnoɔma a amane a ɔya wiase he di akyi dendenndene, na ho Agya nim sɛ hohia saa nnoɔma yi.
Na mmom honhwehwɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie, na bɛde yeinom nyinaa bɛka ho ho.
Soro ahonyadeɛ “Honnsuro!
Nwankuo ketewa, efiri sɛ ɔsɔ ho Agya ani sɛ ɔde ahennie he bɛma ho.
Hontɔno nnoɔma a howɔ na homfa nyɔ adɔeɛ.
Honyɔ sika nkotokuo a ɔnsɛe mfa, na hompɛ agyapadeɛ a ɔya soro, baabi a akorɔmfoɔ ntumi nkowia na nwewemmoa nsɛe no, na baabi a ho agyapadeɛ ya he, hɔ ne ho akoma nso ya.
Honwɛne ntwɛne ho wura sanba “Hommɔ abɔsoɔ, na homma ho nkanea nnɛre, na honyɛ ho ho sɛ nnipa a bɛɛtwɛne bɛ wura a ofiri awaregyeɛ ase ɔɔba, na sɛ obeduru na ɔbɔ mu a, bɛabie no ntɛmntɛm.
Nhyira ne nkoa a bɛ wura he bɛba abehu bɛ sɛ begu so ɔɔwɛne!
Nɔkorɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, ɔbɛbɔ n’abɔsoɔ, na wama bɛatenatena didipono ho na waba abɛsom bɛ.
Na sɛ ɔba anadwo dasuom anaa nhemadeakyeɛ na ɔbɛto bɛ saa a, nhyira ne bɛ!
Nso honhu yei sɛ, sɛ fiewura nim dɔno korɔ a korɔmfoɔ bɛba a, nka wamma no ammetu ne dane ase ammewura mu.
Ho nso honsiesie ho ho, efiri sɛ dɔno a honsusu koraa mu ne Nipa Ba he bɛba.” Afei Petro bisaa sɛ, “Awurade, wode mfantoho yi ɔɔma yɛ anaa wode ɔɔma bɛ nyinaa nso?” Na Awurade buaa sɛ, Hwane koraa ne fiepanyini nɔkwafoɔ ne badwemma a ne wura de no bedi ne fiefoɔ so, sɛ ɔmma bɛ bɛ aduane berɛ a ɔsɛ mu?
Nhyira ne saa akoa he a ne wura bɛba abehu no sɛ ɔɔyɔ saa!
Nɔkorem, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, ɔde saa akoa he besi nea ɔwɔ nyinaa so.
Nso sɛ ɔkɔba sɛ akoa he ka no n’akoma mu sɛ, ‘Me wura akyɛre ba, na ofiri aseɛ boro nkoa ne mmaawa he, na odidi nom, na ɔboro a, saa akoa he wura bɛba da a ɔnhwɛ no kwane ne dɔno a onnim sɛ ɔbɛba mu, na ɔbɛtwe n’aso dendenndene na ɔde no afra bɛ a bɛnnye nni mu.
Nti akoa he a onim nea ne wura pɛ nso wansiesie ne ho anaa wanyɔ nea ɔpɛ he, bɛbɛbɔ no mmaa pii.
Nso nea onnim a ɔyɔɔ nnoɔma a ɔsɛ hweɛ he bɛbɛhwe no kakraa bi.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, biaa a bɛma no pii he, bebebisa pii afiri ne hɔ, na nea bɛde pii hyɛ ne nsa he, ɔno ne bebebisa pii nso afiri ne hɔ.
Akodie ho nkɔmhyɛ “Mebaa sɛ meebɛma gya asɔ asaase so, na sɛ asɔ dada a, mmɛ ne meehwehwɛ kyɛne yei?
Nɔkorɛ di, mewɔ asubɔ bi da m’anim, na hwɛ sɛnea me ho yera me kosi sɛ bebewie!
Hosusu sɛ mede asomdwie ne aba asaase so anaa?
Ɔnte saa, na mmom mpaepaemu ne mede aba.
Na ofiri nnɛ, fie baako mu nnipa mmienu bedi mpaepaemu, na mmeɛnsa ne mmienu anya, na mmienu ne mmeɛnsa anya.
Bebedi mpaepaemu, agya bɛsɔre atia ne ba na ba asɔre atia n’agya, na na bɛsɔre atia ne babaa na babaa asɔre atia ne na, asebaa bɛsɔre atia n’ase, na ase nso asɔre atia n’asebaa.” Afei Yesu toaa so ka kyerɛɛ nnipakuo he nso sɛ, “Sɛ hohu sɛ nsuo amuna atɔeɛ fam a, hoka ntɛmaa sɛ, ‘Nsuo ɔɔbɛtɔ’; na ɔba saa.
Na sɛ hohu sɛ anafoɔ fam mframa ɔɔbɔ a, hoka sɛ, ‘Ahuhuro ɔɔbɛba,’ na ɔbam.
Nyaatwomfoɔ, honim sɛnea bɛkyerɛ asaase ne wiem nsɛnkyerɛnne ase, afei, mmɛ nti ne honnim sɛnea bɛkyerɛ saa mmerɛ yi mu?
“Afei, ɛɛne nti ne ho ankasa honntumi nhu nea ɔfata sɛ hoyɔ?
Sɛ wo ne wo nkurobɔfoɔ ookodi asɛm tumfoɔ bi hɔ a, honam kwane so ɔɔkɔ he, bɔ mmɔdene sɛ wobesiesie wo ne no ntam, na wantwe wo ankɔ temmufoɔ he anim, na temmufoɔ he amfa woanhyɛ asennibea sohwɛfoɔ nsa, na asennibea sohwɛfoɔ he amfa wo ankɔto afiase.
Meeka akyerɛ wo sɛ, womfiri hɔ nkɔ gye sɛ woatua ka biaa a ɔsɛ sɛ wo tua ansa.”
Asotwe ho asɛnka Saa berɛ heaa, nnipa bi a bɛya hɔ kaa sɛnea Pilato de Galileafoɔ bi mogyaa fraa bɛ afɔrebɔ mu he ho asɛm kyerɛɛ no.
Nti obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Nti hosusu sɛ na saa Galileafoɔ yi yɛ abɔnefoɔ kyɛne Galileafoɔ a aka nyinaa esiane saa amaneɛ a behuiɛ yi nti anaa?
Nɔkorem, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ ɔnte saa koraa; nso sɛ hoansakra a, saa ne bebekuku ho nyinaa nso.
Anaa nnipa dunwɔtwe a Siloa abrosane he bu guu bɛ so kuku bɛ he, nti hosusu sɛ na bɛyɛ abɔnefoɔ kyɛne nnipa a bɛtete Yerusalem nyinaa anaa?
Nɔkorem, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ ɔnte saa; nso sɛ hoansakra a, bebekuku ho nyinaa saa nso.” Borɔdoma a ɔnso aba Afei ɔtoaa so maa mfantoho yi sɛ, “Na beema bi wɔ borɔdoma si ne bobe turom, na ɔbaa sɛ ɔɔbɛhwɛ sɛ aduaba ya so a, nso wannya bi.
Nti ɔka kyerɛɛ bobeturo hwɛfoɔ he sɛ, hwɛ, ‘Oo!
Mfie mmeɛnsa di ne maba abɛhwehwɛ aduaba borɔdoma yi so, nso mannya bi.
Twa twene!
Ɛɛne koraa nti ne ɔsɛ sɛ ɔgye asaase he kɛntɛne so?’ Obuaa no sɛ, ‘Owura, gyae no afe yi nso, na memfuntum aseɛ na memfa sumina ngu aseɛ.
Na sɛ ɔsõ aba afe sesɛɛ a ɔyɛ asɛmpa, na mmom sɛ anso a, hedeɛ wobetumi atwa atwene.’ ” Yesu saa baa bi yadeɛ Homeda bi Afei na Yesu ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ hyia adane he baako mu homeda bi.
Saa berɛ he, na baa bi a honhom bi ama no ayare mfie dunwɔtwe ama ne mu akuntunu a na ontumi mmae ne mu.
Berɛ a Yesu huu no he, ɔfrɛɛ no ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Baa, bɛayi wo afiri wo w’ahoɔmmerɛ mu.” Na ɔde ne nsa guu ne so; na amonom hɔaa ne mu teneeɛ, na ofirii aseɛ hyɛɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam.
Hyiadane he mu panyini ani bereeɛ sɛ Yesu asa yadeɛ homeda he.
Nti ɔka kyerɛɛ nnipakuo he sɛ, “Nnansia ne ɔsɛ sɛ bɛde yɔ adwuma, ɔno mu ne ɔsɛ sɛ ho ba na bɛsa ho yadeɛ, na ɔnyɛ homeda ne ɔsɛ sɛ ho ba.” Nso, Awurade buaa no sɛ, “Nyaatwomfoɔ, nti ho mu biaa nsane ne nantwie anaa n’afunumu mfiri buom homeda nkɔma no nsuo nnom?
Ɔmfata sɛ baa yi a ɔyɛ Abraham babaa a Satan akyekyere no mfie dunwɔtwe he, bɛsane no firi mpokyerɛ yi mu homeda anaa?” Na ɔkaa yeinom he, n’atamfoɔ he nyinaa ani wuiɛ; nso nnipakuo he nyinaa firii aseɛ dii ahurusie anwanwadeɛ a ɔyɔeɛ he nyinaa ho.
Sinapi aba ne mmɔreka ho mfantoho Afei Yesu toaa so sɛ, “Sɛ ne Nyankopɔn ahennie teɛ?
Na ɛɛne ho ne mede bɛto?
Na ɔmaa mfantoho yi sɛ: Nyankopɔn ahennie he te sɛ sinapi aba a bi duaa no ne turom, na onyini bɛyɛɛ dua, na soro nnomaa tenatenaa ne mmane so.” Na ɔkaa bio sɛ, “Mmɛ ho ne mede Nyankopɔn ahennie bɛto?
Ɔte sɛ mmɔreka a baa bi de fraa siam susukuruwaa akɛseɛ mmeɛnsa mu kosii sɛ ne nyinaa tuiɛ.” Pono teateaa he Na Yesu tutuu akwane kɔɔ nkuro mu ne nkuraa ase kyerɛkyerɛeɛ na ɔtoaa n’akwantuo he so kɔɔ Yerusalem.
Afei bi bisaa no sɛ, “Awurade, bɛ a wobegye bɛ nkwa he yɛ kakraa bi anaa?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honyere ho ho dendenndene nwura pono teateaa he mu, na meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ nnipa beberee bɛhwehwɛ sɛ bewura mu nso bentumi.
Na sɛ fiewura he nya sɔre to pono he mu a, afei hobegyina abɔntene abɔ pono he mu aka sɛ, ‘Owura, bie yɛ.’ Nso obebua ho sɛ, ‘Mennim baabi a hofiri.’ Na hobefiri aseɛ aka sɛ, ‘Yɛ ne wo didi nomeeɛ, na womaa nkyerɛkyerɛ yɛ mmɔntene so.’ Nso obebie n’ano aka akyerɛ ho sɛ, ‘Mennim baabi a hofiri.
Homfiri me so nkɔ, ho a hoyɔ nea ɔntene nyinaa!’ Saa berɛ he hobesu na hoatwɛre ho sẽ, berɛ a hobehu Abraham ne Isak ne Yakob ne adiyifoɔ he nyinaa sɛ bɛya Nyankopɔn ahennie mu, na ho deɛ, bɛapam ho kɔ abɔntene he.
Bio nso, nkurofoɔ befiri apieɛ fam ne atɔeɛ fam, atifi fam ne anafoɔ fam aba, na bɛbɛtenatena adidiiɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie mu.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, binom aka akyi nso bebedi kane, saa nso ne binom adi kane nso bɛbɛka akyi.” Herode Antipa Dɔno heaa mu he Farisifoɔ bi ba bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Firi ha kɔ, efiri sɛ Herode pɛ sɛ oku wo.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔka nkyerɛ saa dadaafoɔ he sɛ, ‘Hwɛ, meetu ahonhommɔne na masa yadeɛ nnɛ ne kyena, na n’adekyeɛ he mawie.
Yesu twa Yerusalem ho adwo Nso, otwa sɛ menante nnɛ ne kyena ne adekyeeɛ, efiri sɛ ɔnsɛ sɛ beku diyifoɔ bi baabi foforɔ biaa gye Yerusalem.’ Yerusalem!
Yerusalem!
Wo a woku adiyifoɔ na wosi bɛ a bɛasoma bɛ wo nkyɛne aboɔ; hwɛ mprɛ dodoɔ a mepɛɛ sɛ meboaboa wo manfoɔ ano sɛnea akokɔbaatane boaboa ne mma ano hyɛ ne ntabane ase, nso woampene so!
Hwɛ!
Bɛagyaa ho fie fituo ama ho.
Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, honhu me bio kosi sɛ hobɛka sɛ, ‘Nhyira ne nea ɔba Awurade dini mu!’ ”
Yesu sa bi a ɔyare sasaborɔ yadeɛ Homeda Afei homeda bi, Yesu kɔɔ Farisifoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he mu baako fie sɛ ookodidi he, na nkurofoɔ he ɔɔtetɛ no.
Saa berɛ heaa na bi ya n’anim a wahonhono.
Nti Yesu bisaa Mmaranimfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he sɛ, “Mmara ma kwane sɛ bɛsa yadeɛ homeda anaa ɔmma kwane?” Nso bɛyɛɛ komm.
Nti Yesu sɔɔ ne mu saa no yadeɛ na ɔmaa no kɔeɛ.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho mu hwane ne sɛ ne ba anaa ne nantwie tɔ abura mu homeda a, onnyi no mfiri mu ntɛmaa homeda he?” Bɛantumi anyi saa asɛm yi ano.
Ahobrɛaseɛ Afei ɔtoaa so maa mfantoho bi kyerɛɛ nnipa a bɛato nsa afrɛ bɛ he, berɛ a ohuu sɛnea na bɛɛhwehwɛ mu ayi mpanyini tenabea he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ bi to nsa frɛ wo ayefohyia ase a, ntena mpanyini tenabea, ebia na waato nsa afrɛ bi a odi mu kyɛne wo, na nea ɔtoo nsa frɛɛ wo ne no he bɛba abɛka akyerɛ wo sɛ, ‘Ma nipa yi ntena ha.’ Afei wode aniwuo befiri hɔ akɔtena baabi a onni mu sɛ kane tenabea he.
Na mmom sɛ bɛto nsa frɛ wo a, kɔ na kɔtena baabi a ɔya fam koraa, na sɛ nea wato nsa afrɛ wo he ba a, waka akyerɛ wo sɛ, ‘Damfo, foro kɔ soro.’ Ɔno bɛma woanya anidie wo mfɛfoɔ a bɛahyia he nyinaa anim.
Na biaa a ɔma ne ho so he bɛbɛbrɛ no ase, na nea ɔbrɛ ne ho ase he bɛbɛma no so.” Ahiafoɔ adidifrɛ Na ɔka kyerɛɛ beema a ɔtoo nsa frɛɛ no he nso sɛ, “Sɛ woto pono, mfrɛ wo nnamfo anaa wo nuanom anaa w’abusuafoɔ anaa wo mfɛfoɔ adefoɔ nkoaa, ɔnam sɛ wodwene sɛ bɛ nso da bi bɛbɛto nsa afrɛ wo bɛ apontoɔ asɛ de atua wo ka nti.
Na mmom, sɛ wo to pono a, to nsa frɛ ahiafoɔ, mmubuafoɔ, mpakye, ne anifirafoɔ nso, na wobenya nhyira, efiri sɛ bɛ deɛ benni bibiaa a bɛde betua wo so ka.
Na wobenya akatua ateneneefoɔ wusɔreɛ he mu.” Apontoɔ kɛseɛ he Berɛ a bɛ a bɛ ne no tete adidiiɛ hɔ he mu baako tee nsɛm yi he, ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nhyira ne nea obedidi Nyankopɔn ahennie mu!” Na afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nipa bi too pono kɛseɛ anwummerɛ bi, na ɔtoo nsa frɛɛ nnipa bebree.
Na dɔno a bɛde bedi aduane he duruiɛ he, ɔsomaa n’akoa kɔɔ bɛ a ɔtoo nsa frɛɛ bɛ he hɔ sɛ, ‘Hommra na afei bɛasiesie bibiaa awie.’ Nso bɛ nyinaa befiri aseɛ yiyii bɛ ho ano.
Nea odi kane he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Maatɔ asaase na ehia sɛ mekɔhwɛ; mesrɛ wo, yi me firi mu.’ Na foforɔ nso kaa sɛ, ‘Maatɔ anantwie mpamho nnum na meehwɛ sɛnea bɛteɛ; mesrɛ wo, yi me firi mu.’ Na foforɔ nso kaa sɛ, “Mewareɛ nkyereeɛ, nti mentumi mma.
Nti akoa he bɛkaa nsɛm yi kyerɛɛ ne wura he.
Na fiewura he bo fuiɛ na ɔka kyerɛɛ n’akoa he sɛ, ‘Yɔ ntɛm kɔ kuro he akwane ne mmorɔnoo so kɔfa ahiafoɔ ne mmubuafoɔ ne anifirafoɔ ne mpakye bra.’ Akoa he yɔɔ saa wieeeɛ he, ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Me wura, maayɔ nea wo hyɛɛ me he, nso kwane da so ya hɔ.’ Na ne wura he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Kɔ akwane ne mmɔntene so na hyɛ amanfoɔ ma bɛ mmra mu, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na fie ha bɛyɛ ma.
Na meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, nnipa a (bedii kane) too nsa frɛɛ bɛ he mu biaa nni hɔ a m’aduane he bi bɛka n’ano.’ ” Kristo frɛ a ɔfrɛ nnipa Afei na nnipadɔm pii bi ne no nam, na ɔdanee ne ho ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ bi ba me nkyɛne na w’annɔ me asene ne papa ne ne maame ne ne yerɛ ne ne mma ne ne nuammeemanom ne ne nuammaanom ne n’ankasa mpo kra a, ontumi nyɛ me suani.
Biaa a ɔnsoa n’asennua na onni m’akyi he ntumi nyɛ me suani.
Nkontabuo Na ho mu hwane ne ɔpɛ sɛ osi abrosane a onni kane nsese ne boɔ nhwɛ sɛ sika a ɔwɔ he betumi asi ansa na wahyɛ aseɛ?
Sɛ wanni kane anyɔ saa a, ɔbɛto fapem he nso ontumi nwie, na bɛ a bɛhwɛ nyinaa befiri aseɛ atweetwe no aka sɛ, ‘Nipa yi firii aseɛ siiɛ nso wantumi anwie.’ Anaa hene hwane ne ɔne hene foforɔ ɔɔkɔko a, onni kane ntena ase ntu agyina na ɔnhwɛ sɛ obetumi de asraafoɔ mpem du akohyia nea ɔde mpem aduonu ɔɔba no so he?
Sɛ ontumi nyɔ saa a, hedeɛ berɛ a baako he ya akyiri nohoa he, ɔbɛsoma binom ma bɛkɔsrɛ sɛ benni no asomdwie mu.
Nti, honhu sɛ, ho mu biaa a onnya n’ahodeɛ nyinaa hɔ he ntumi nyɛ me suani.
Nkyene ho asɛm “Ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ sɛ nkyene yɛ.
Nso sɛ nkyene dɛ firi mu a, mmɛ ne bɛde bɛhyɛ nkyene bio?
Ɔnnyɛ mma asaase anaa sumina.
Bɛto gu.
Ma nea ɔwɔ aso he ntie.”
Dwane a wayera ho mfantoho Na togyefoɔ ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ nyinaa twi bɛnee Yesu sɛ beebetie no.
Nti Farisifoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he nyinaa nwiinwii kaa sɛ, “Nipa yi gye nnebɔnyɛfoɔ na ɔne bɛ didi.” Nti ɔyɔɔ mfantoho bi kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ: “Ho mu hwane ne wɔ nwane ha, na mu baako yera a, onnya aduɔkron nkron he serɛ so nkɔhwehwɛ nea wayera he nkosi sɛ obehu no?
Na berɛ a wahu no he, ɔde no bɔ ne kɔno ho na odi ahurusie.
Na oduru fie a ɔfrɛfrɛ ne nnamfonom ne ne mpɔtamfoɔ boa ano ka kyerɛ bɛ sɛ, ‘Ho ne me nni ahurusie, efiri sɛ mahu me dwane a ɔyeraeɛ he.’ Nti meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ anigye pii bɛba soro debɔneyɛfoɔ baako a wasakra ho kyɛne ateneneefoɔ aduɔkron nkron a benhia adwensakra.
Dwetɛbena a ayera he ho mfantoho “Anaa baa hwane ne wɔ dwetɛbena du na sɛ dwetɛbena baako yera a, ɔnsɔ kanea mpra ne fie na ɔnhwehwɛ no yie nkosi sɛ obehu?
Na sɛ ohu a, ɔfrɛfrɛ ne nnamfoɔ mmaa ne n’afipamfoɔ boa ano ka sɛ, ‘Ho ne me nni ahurusie, efiri sɛ mahu me dwetɛbena a ɔyeraeɛ he.’ Nti, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, Nyankopɔn abɔfoɔ anigye debɔneyɛni baako a wasakra ho.” Agya a ɔdɔ ne ba ho mfantoho Afei ɔkaa sɛ, “Na beema bi wɔ mma mmienu.
Na bɛ mu kumaa he ka kyerɛɛ ne papa sɛ, ‘Papa, fa w’agyapadeɛ he fã a ɔyɛ me deɛ ma me.’ Nti ɔkyɛɛ n’asetenadeɛ mu maa bɛ.
Na nna kakraa bi akyi he, ba kumaa he boaboaa nnoɔma he nyinaa ano na otuu kwane kɔɔ akyirikyiri mane bi so, na okobuu akohwibra de sɛee n’agyapadeɛ he nyinaa.
Berɛ a ɔhweree ne nyinaa he, kɔm kɛseɛ bi sii mane he mu baabiaa, na ne ho firii aseɛ kyere no.
Afei ɔde ne ho kɔdanee mane he muni baako, na ɔde no kɔɔ n’asaase so sɛ ɔnkɔhwɛ ne mprako.
Na ne kɔno dɔɔ sɛ ɔde aduane a mprako di he bi bɛhyɛ ne yafunu mã, nso biaa amma no hwee.
“Berɛ a n’ani baa ne ho so he, ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Me papa apaafoɔ he mu deɛ ɔya he ne nnya aduane mma ne mmu so a mete ha yi a kɔm ooku me yi!
Mɛsɔre akɔ me papa nkyɛne akɔka akyerɛ no sɛ, “Papa, maayɔ soro ne wo anim bɔne.
Memfata sɛ wofrɛ me wo ba bio.
Yɛ me w’apaafoɔ he mu baako.” ’ Nti ɔsɔre sii kwane so sɛ ɔɔkɔ ne papa nkyɛne.
Berɛ a ɔda soaa ya akyirikyiri he, ne papa huu no, na ne yam hyehyee no maa ne ba he, na otuu mmirika kɔsɔɔ ne mu yɔɔ no atuu.
Afei ne ba he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Papa, maayɔ soro ne wo anim bɔne.
Memfata sɛ wofrɛ me wo ba bio.
Na papa he ka kyerɛɛ ne nkoa he sɛ, ‘Honyɔ ntɛm, mfa ataadeɛ a odi mu mmra mmɛhyɛ no, na homfa petea nhyɛ ne nsa na homfa mpaboa nhyɛ no.
Na homfa nantwie kumaa a wadɔre sradeɛ mmra mmeku no mma yenni na yɛnnye yɛ ani, efiri sɛ me ba yi wuiɛ na wasane aba nkwa mu; ɔyeraeɛ na maahu no.’ Na befirii aseɛ gyee bɛ ani.
“Saa berɛ yi na ne ba panyini he ya mfuom; na ɔɔba a ɔbɛne fie he ɔtee sɛ nnwom ne asa ɔɔkɔ so.
Nti ɔfrɛɛ nkoa he mu baako na obisaa no nea ɔɔkɔ so.
Akoa he buaa no sɛ, ‘Wo nua kumaa he aba, na wo papa aku nantwie kumaa a wadɔre sradeɛ, efiri sɛ ne nsa aka no bio a ɔwɔ nkwa mu.’ Na ne bo fuu paa, na wampɛ sɛ ɔkɔ fie.
Afei ne papa pie bɛkorɔkrɔɔ no.
Obuaa ne papa sɛ, ‘Maasom wo mfie bebree, na memmuu wo mmara so da, nso wommaa me abirekyie ba mpo sɛ me ne me nnamfonom mfa nnye yɛ ani da.
Nso wo ba yi a ɔne nwamanfoɔ adi wo ahodeɛ baeɛaa pɛ, woaku nantwie ba a wadɔre sradeɛ ama no.’ Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Me ba, woya me nkyɛne berɛ nyinaa, na nea mewɔ nyinaa yɛ wo deɛ; nso ɔsɛ sɛ yɛma yɛ ani gye na yedi ahurusie, efiri sɛ wo nua yi wuiɛ na waaba nkwa mu bio, ɔyeraeɛ na yɛahu no.’ ”
Fiepanyini nitefoɔ he ho bɛ Afei Yesu toaa so ka kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Na defoɔ bi ya hɔ a ɔwɔ fiehwɛfoɔ bi, na bɛkaa ne ho asɛm kyerɛɛ no sɛ ɔɔyɔ n’agyapadeɛ basabasa.
Nti defoɔ he frɛɛ n’akoa he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘mmɛ ne mete fa wo ho yi?
Bebu wo fiehwɛ adwuma he ho akonta kyerɛ me, efiri sɛ wontumi nhwɛ fie he so bio.’ Afei fiehwɛfoɔ he kaa no ne tim sɛ, ‘Mmɛ ne menyɔ, berɛ a me wura ɔɔbɛgye me fiehwɛ adwuma afiri me nsam yi?
Me ho nyɛ dene pii sɛ metutu fam, mefɛre nso sɛ mɛsrɛsrɛ adeɛ.
Ehẽẽ!
Menim nea mɛyɔ a sɛ oyi me adi firi fiehwɛ adwuma he mu a, nkurofoɔ bɛgye me akɔ bɛ fie.’ Saa nti ɔfrɛɛ bɛ a bɛde ne wura ka he mu biaa baa ne nkyɛne bisaa nea odi kane he sɛ, ‘Wode me wura ka mmeɛhe?’ Ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Ngo susuhina ha.’ Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Gye wo nhyehyɛeɛ nwoma he na tena ase twerɛ aduonum ntɛm.’ Afei, fiehwɛfoɔ he bisaa foforɔ sɛ, ‘Wo nso, wode ka mmeɛhe?’ Ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Ayuo mmɔtɔ ha.’ Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Gye wo nhyehyɛeɛ nwoma he na twerɛ aduowɔtwe.’ Na fiewura he kamfõõ fiehwɛfoɔ nitefoɔ he, efiri sɛ ɔde n’adwene yɔɔ adwuma; yei mpo kyerɛ sɛ, wiase yi mu mma yɛ anitefoɔ sene hann mma bɛ mfɛfoɔ mu.
Ahonyadeɛ ho kwane pa “Bio nso, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, homfa ahonyadeɛ a ɔntene so nnya nnamfoɔ, na sɛ ɔsa a, bɛagye ho akɔ daa tenabea mu.
“Nipa a odi adeɛ ketewa mu nɔkorɛ he di pii mu nɔkorɛ nso, na nipa a ɔntene adeɛ ketewa mu he ntene pii mu nso.
Nti sɛ hoanni nɔkorɛ ahonyadeɛ a ɔntene mu a, hwane ne de ahonyadeɛ pa bɛhyɛ ho nsa?
Na sɛ hoanni nɔkorɛ afoforɔ deɛ mu a, hwane ne de ho ankasa ho deɛ bɛma ho?
Som afaanu Akoa biaa nni hɔ a obetumi asom awuranom mmienu; efiri sɛ obebu baako animtia na ɔde anidie ama baako, anaa ɔbɛbata baako ho na watwe ne ho afiri baako ho.
Hontumi nsom Nyankopɔn ne ahonyadeɛ.” Yesu kaa Farisifoɔ anim Afei nso Farisifoɔ a bɛyɛ sikaniberɛ he tee yeinom nyinaa, na befirii aseɛ tweetwee no.
Nti ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho ne hobu ho ho bem nnipa anim, nso Nyankopɔn nim ho akomam; efiri sɛ nea ɔsombo nnipa ani so he yɛ akyiwadeɛ Nyankopɔn ani so.
“Mmara he ne adiyifoɔ he tenaa hɔ besii Yohane so; efiri hɔ he, bɛpae mu ka Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho asɛmpa, na nipa biaa bɔ mmɔdene sɛ obewura mu.
Nso, ɔmmerɛ sɛ soro ne asaase betwam akɔ kyɛne sɛ mmara he mu ntwerɛdeɛ he bi ho nsensaneɛ baako mpo bɛtɔ fam.
“Biaa a obegyaa ne yerɛ na waware foforɔ he asɛe awareɛ, na nea ɔbɛware baa a ne kunu agyaa no he nso asɛe awareɛ.
Defoɔ ne hiani he “Na nipa bi yɛ defoɔ, na ɔtaa hyɛ ataadeɛ pa ne nwera, na da biaa ɔde asetena afɛfɛdeɛ gye n’ani.
Na hiani bi a bɛfrɛ no Lasaro a ne ho nyinaa atutu akuro taa kɔtena n’aboboano, na ne kɔno dɔɔ sɛ ɔde mporoporowa a ofiri defoɔ he didipono so gu fam he hyɛ ne yafunu mã, nso ɔba saa a, nkramane bɛtaferee n’akuro mu.
Na berɛ bi akyi he, hiani he wuiɛ na abɔfoɔ faa no kɔɔ Abraham kokom.
“Defoɔ he nso wuiɛ ma besiee no.
Na sakani he maa n’ani so he, na ɔya Asamando, na ɔya ahoyera mu, na ohuu sɛ Abraham ya akyirikyiri a Lasaro ya ne kokom.
Nti ɔfrɛɛ no kaa sɛ, ‘Agya Abraham, hu me mmɔbɔ na soma Lasaro ma ɔmfa ne nsateaa ano mmɔ nsuom na ɔmfa mmɛdwodwo me kɛtrɛma, efiri sɛ me ho yera me gyaframa yi mu.’ Na Abraham kaa sɛ, ‘Me ba, kae sɛ wote ase he, wonyaa nnoɔma pa a wopɛ nyinaa, na Lasaro deɛ, ohuu amane, na afei ne wanya awerɛkyekyerɛ ne wo nso woohu amane.
Na yeinom nyinaa akyi he, bɛde kuu kɛseɛ ato yɛ ne ho ntam, nti bɛ a bɛpɛ sɛ befiri ha ba ho nkyɛne he ntumi, na bɛ a bɛpɛ sɛ befiri hɔ ba yɛ nkyɛne he nso ntumi.’ Na ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Hedeɛ mesrɛ wo, Agya, soma no ma ɔnkɔ me papa fie, na mewɔ anuanom nnum, na onkodi adanseɛ nkyerɛ bɛ, na ɔmmɔ bɛ kɔkɔ na bɛamma saa ahoyera yi mu bi.’ Na Abraham kaa sɛ, ‘Bɛwɔ Mose ne adiyifoɔ he; ma bentie bɛ.’ Afei ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Daabi, agya Abraham, sɛ bi firi awufoɔ mu kɔ bɛ nkyɛne mmom a ne bɛbɛsakra.’ Na ɔka kyerɛɛ defoɔ he sɛ, ‘Sɛ bɛantie Mose ne adiyifoɔ he a, saa ne sɛ bi sɔre firi awufoɔ mu kɔ bɛ nkyɛne mpo a, bɛnnye no nni.’ ”
Sintiduatoɔ Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ.
“Nea ɔbɛyɛ biaa sintiduatoɔ he bɛba.
Nso nea ɔnam no so bɛba he nnue!
Nka ɔyɛ ma no sɛ bɛde ayuyammoɔ bɛsɛne ne kɔno mu akɔto no ato po mu, sene sɛ ɔbɛto nketewa yi mu baako sintidua.
Bɔne fakyɛ Homma ho ani mmra ho ho so.
Sɛ wo nua yɛ bɔne bi a ka n’anim, na sɛ onu ne ho a fakyɛ no.
Sɛ bi yɛ wo bɔne mprɛ nson da koro na ɔsane ba wo nkyɛne mprɛ nson ka sɛ, ‘Maanu me ho a,’ fakyɛ no.” Na asomafoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ Awurade sɛ, “Ma yɛ gyidie nyɛ kɛseɛ.” Gyidie mu tumi Na Awurade kaa sɛ, “Sɛ howɔ gyidie a ne kɛseɛ te sɛ sinapi aba mpo a, nka hobɛka akyerɛ saa akyee dua yi sɛ, ‘Tutu na kosi po mu!’ Na nka obetie ho.
Nɔkorɛdie “Ho mu hwane ne ɔwɔ akoa a oofuntum asaase anaa ɔɔhwɛ mmoa, na sɛ ofiri afuom ba a ɔbɛka akyerɛ no sɛ, ‘Yɔ ntɛm bra bɛtena didipono ho’; na ɔnnka nkyerɛ no sɛ, ‘Siesie bibi ma menni anwummerɛ yi, na bɔ wo ho so som me kosi sɛ medidi anom awie, na ɔno akyi he wobetumi adidi anom?’ Ɔbɛda akoa he ase sɛ wayɔ nea wahyɛ no he anaa?
Nti ho nso, sɛ hoyɔ nea bɛahyɛ ho nyinaa wie a, honka sɛ, ‘Yɛyɛ nkoa a yɛnsɛ hwee.
Nea ɔsɛ sɛ yɛyɔaa ne yɛayɔ yi.’ ” Akwatafoɔ du he ayaresa Na Yesu ɔɔkɔ Yerusalem he ɔfaa Samaria ne Galilea ntam.
Na ɔɔyɛ aduru akuraa bi ase he, mmeema akwatafoɔ du huu no, nso bɛsɔre gyinaa akyirikyiri.
Na bɛmaa bɛ nne so kaa sɛ.
“Owura Yesu hu yɛ mmɔbɔ!” Na ohuu bɛ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔ na homfa ho ho nkɔkyerɛ asɔfoɔ he.” Na berɛ a bɛɛkɔ he bɛ ho firiiɛ.
Berɛ a bɛ mu baako huu sɛ ne ho afiri he, ɔsane baeɛ de nne kɛseɛ hyɛɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam: Na ɔde n’anim butu Yesu nane ase daa no ase; na ɔyɛ Samariani.
Afei Yesu buaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ du ne bɛ ho firiiɛ?
Na nkron a bɛaka he ya he?
Nti bɛanhu bɛ mu biaa a wasane n’akyi ammfa animuonyam ammra Nyankopɔn ka beema a ɔyɛ manfrani yi ho?” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɔre kɔ; wo gyidie agye wo.” Nyankopɔn ahennie he mmaeɛ Berɛ bi Farisifoɔ he bisaa Yesu berɛ korɔ a Nyankopɔn ahennie he bɛba, obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Nyankopɔn ahennie he ɔɔmma sɛ adeɛ a behu no pefee; na bɛnka nso sɛ ‘Hwɛ, ɔya ha’ anaa ‘ɔya hɔ,’ efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie he ya ho mfimfini.” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Nna bi ɔɔba a hobɛpɛ sɛ hohu Nipa Ba he nna he mu baako nso hoonhu.
Na nnipa bɛka akyerɛ ho sɛ, ‘Honhwɛ hɔ,’ anaa ‘Honhwɛ ha!’ Nso honnkɔ na honnni bɛ akyi nso.
Na sɛnea anyinam ma ne hann hyerɛn firi soro ase fã bi kɔ soro aseɛ fã foforɔ he, saa ne nipa Ba he bɛyɛ ne nna he mu.
Nso nea odi kane he, ɔsɛ sɛ Nipa Ba he hu amaneɛ bebree na nneemmafoɔ po no.
Noa ne Lot nna ho mfatoho Bio nso, sɛnea ɔyɛɛ Noa nna he mu he, saa ne ɔbɛyɛ nipa Ba he nna he nso mu.
Bedidiiɛ, nomeeɛ, mmeema warewareeɛ, bɛde mmaa memaa awareɛ, kosii da a Noa kɔhyɛnee adaka he mu na nsuhyiri he ba bɛsɛee bɛ nyinaa he.
Saa ne ɔyɛɛ Lot nna he mu, bedidiiɛ, nomeeɛ, bɛtɔeɛ, bɛtɔnooɛ, beduaeɛ, besisii adane.
Na da a Lot firii Sodom he, gya ne sɔɔfee tɔ firii soro bɛsɛee bɛ nyinaa.
Saa ne ɔbɛyɛ da a bebeyi nipa Ba he adi he.
“Saa da he, mma nipa a ɔya dane atifi a ne nnoɔma ya fie hɔ he nsi fam mmɛfa, na nipa a ɔya afuom he, mma ɔno nso nsane mmɛfa nnoɔma a ɔya akyi he.
Honkaeɛ Lot yerɛ he.
Biaa a ɔhwehwɛ sɛ ɔbɛkora ne kra he, ɔbɛhwere, na biaa a ɔbɛhwere ne kra he benya nkwa.
Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, saa anadwo he, ɔte sɛ nnipa mmienu da mpa baako so, na bɛafa baako kɔ na bɛagya nea ɔka ne ho he hɔ.
Saa ara nso ne sɛ mmaa mmienu ɔɔyam adeɛ ayuyammoɔ korɔ so na bɛafa baako kɔ na bɛagya nea ɔka ne ho he hɔ.” [Ɔte sɛ mmeema mmienu te afuom; na bɛafa baako, na bɛagya baako hɔ.]
Nti bebisaa no sɛ, “Awurade, he fa?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nea afunu ya he, hɔ ne pɛtɛ bɛboaboa bɛ ho ano.”
Temmufoɔ a ɔntene he ho mfantoho Afei ɔtoaa so maa bɛ mfantoho bi de kyerɛɛ sɛnea ohia sɛ bɛbɔ mpaeɛ daa a bɛmpa aba.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Na temmufoɔ bi ya kuro bi mu a onsuro Nyankopɔn na ommu nipa biaa, na na kunafoɔ bi ya saa kuro he mu a ɔtaa kɔ ne nkyɛne kɔka sɛ, ‘Hwɛ sɛ wobebu atɛntenenee me ne me nkurobɔfoɔ ntam.’ Ɔtwentwɛnee ne nane ase kakra, nso akyire yi ɔkaa no ne tim sɛ, ‘Ewom sɛ mensuro Nyankopɔn na memmu nnipa deɛ, nso, sɛnea kunafoɔ yi kɔ so ha me nti, mɛhwɛ na mabu atɛntenenee, na wamma ammɛdwane me ho bio.’ ” Afei Awurade kaa sɛ, “Hontie nea temmufoɔ a ɔntene he mpo kaeɛ!
Nɔkwasɛm di, ewom sɛ Nyankopɔn ma ne bo dwo kyɛre ma ho deɛ, nso ommu atɛntenenee mma bɛ a wayi bɛ a besu frɛ no awia ne anadwo he anaa?
Nti, ɔbɛtwentwɛne ne nane ase bɛ ho anaa?
Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, obebu atɛntenenee ama bɛ ntɛm so.
Nso sɛ Nipa Ba he ba a, obehu gyidie ankasa asaase so anaa?” Farisini ne togyeni he Na ɔde mfantoho yi nso maa binom a bɛgye bɛ ho di sɛ bɛyɛ ateneneefoɔ na bemmu bɛ a bɛaka he koraa he sɛ, “Nnipa mmienu kɔɔ asɔre fie kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ, na baako yɛ Farisini, na nea ɔka ne ho he yɛ togyeni.
Farisini he sɔre gyinaeɛ, na ofirii aseɛ bɔɔ mpaeɛ ne tim sɛ, ‘Nyankopɔn, meda wo ase sɛ mente sɛ nnipa a aka he, apoobɔfoɔ, bɛ a bɛntene, awaresɛefoɔ, anaa togyeni yei mpo.
Medi mmuada mprenu nnawɔtwe, meyi nea menya nyinaa so ntotosoɔ du du.’ Na togyeni he a ogyina fã nohoa he ampɛ sɛ ɔma n’ani so hwɛ soro mpo, na mmom ɔde ne nsa guu ne koko so kaa sɛ, ‘Nyankopɔn, hu me debɔneyɛni mmɔbɔ.’ Meka kyerɛ ho sɛ, togyeni he de bembuo sane kɔɔ ne fie sene Farisini he, efiri sɛ, biaa a ɔma ne ho so he bɛbɛbrɛ no ase, na nea ɔbrɛ ne ho ase he bɛbɛma no so.” Yesu hyira mmɔfra Afei nkurofoɔ firii aseɛ de bɛ mma nkokoa brɛɛ no sɛ ɔmfa ne nsa nka bɛ; na n’asuafoɔ he huiɛ he bɛkaa bɛ anim.
Nso, Yesu frɛɛ mmɔfra he baa ne nkyɛne kaa sɛ, “Homma mmɔfra he mmra me nkyɛne, na honsi bɛ kwane, efiri sɛ bɛ a bɛte saa ne Nyankopɔn ahennie he yɛ bɛ dea.
Nɔkorem, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, biaa a onnye Nyankopɔn ahennie sɛ abɔfra kumaa he, kwane biaa so ɔnkɔ mu koraa.” Daa nkwa Na tumfoɔ bi bisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ pa, ɛɛne ne meyɔ a menya daa nkwa?” Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne wofrɛ me papa?
Biaa nyɛ papa gye baako pɛ, ɔno ne Nyankopɔn.
Wonim mmara he, ‘Nsɛe awareɛ, Nni awu, Mmɔ korɔno, Nni adansekunumu, di w’agya ne wo na ni.’ ” Afei ɔkaa sɛ, “Maadi yeinom nyinaa so firi me mmɔfrase.” Yesu tee yei he, ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nso aka wo adeɛ baako: kɔtɔno nea wowɔ nyinaa na kyekyɛ ma ahiafoɔ, na wobenya agyapadeɛ soro; na bra bedi m’akyi.” Berɛ a temmufoɔ he tee yei he, ne werɛ hoo paa, efiri sɛ, na ɔyɛ defoɔ ankasa.
Ahonyadeɛ mu asiane Yesu hwɛɛ no kaa sɛ, “Sɛ hoahu dene a ɔyɛ ma asikafoɔ ne adefoɔ sɛ bɛbɛkɔ Nyankopɔn ahennie mu!
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, ɔmmerɛ ma yoma sɛ ɔbɛfa paneɛ tokuro mu kyɛne sɛ defoɔ bɛkɔ Nyankopɔn ahennie mu.” Bɛ a bɛtee yei he kaa sɛ, “Hedeɛ hwane ne betumi anya nkwa?” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Nea ontumi nyɛ hɔ nnipa fam he betumi ayɛ hɔ Nyankopɔn fam.” Ahopakyie so akatua Na Petro kaa sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Yɛagya yɛ nnoɔma nyinaa hɔ abedi w’akyi.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nɔkorem meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, biaa nni hɔ a wagya fie anaa yerɛ anaa anuanom anaa awofoɔ anaa mma, Nyankopɔn ahennie nti, a onnya ho mmɔho pii saa berɛ yi, ne daa nkwa, wiase a ɔɔba he mu.” Yesu wuo ne ne wusɔreɛ ho nkɔmhyɛ a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa Afei ɔde dummienu he kɔɔ nkyɛne kɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Yɛɛkɔ Yerusalem, na nnoɔma a adiyifoɔ he atwerɛ afa Nipa ba he ho nyinaa bɛba mu.
Na bebeyi no ahyɛ amanamane mufoɔ nsa, na bɛagoro ne ho, na bɛabɔ no adapaa, na bɛatete ntasuo agu ne so, na bɛhwe no wie a, bebeku no, na da a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he obenyane.” Nso, bɛante nnoɔma yi mu biaa ase; na nsɛm yi ahinta bɛ, na bɛante nea ɔkaeɛ he ase.
Yesu maa nifirani bi huu adeɛ Na berɛ a ɔɔbɛne Yeriko he, na nifirani bi te kwankyɛne ɔɔsrɛsrɛ adeɛ.
Esiane sɛ ɔtee sɛ nnipakuo bi ootwam nti, ofirii aseɛ bisabisaa nea yei kyerɛ.
Bɛbɔɔ no amaneɛ sɛ, “Yesu, Nasareni he ne ootwam!” Afei ɔteaa mu sɛ, “Yesu, Dawid Ba, hu me mmɔbɔ!” Na bɛ a bedi kane he teateaa no sɛ ɔnyɛ komm, nso ɔkɔɔ so teateaa mu dendenndene sɛ, “Dawid Ba, hu me mmɔbɔ!” Afei Yesu gyinaeɛ na ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa beema he mmra ne nkyɛne.
Oduruu Yesu nkyɛne he, Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Ɛɛne ne wopɛ sɛ meyɔ ma wo?” Ɔkaa sɛ “Awurade, ma menhu adeɛ.” Nti Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Hu adeɛ; wo gyidie agye wo.” Na amonom hɔaa ohuu adeɛ, na ofirii aseɛ dii n’akyi a ɔɔhyɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam.
Na afei, berɛ a nkurofoɔ he nyinaa huu no he, beyii Nyankopɔn ayɛ.
Yesu ne Sakeo Na Yesu hyɛnee Yeriko sɛ ootwam akɔ.
Na beema bi ya hɔ a ne dini de Sakeo; na ɔyɛ togyeni panyini a ɔyɛ defoɔ.
Na ɔɔhwehwɛ sɛ obehu nipa korɔ a Yesu yɛ, nso nnipadɔm he nti na ontumi, efiri sɛ na ɔyɛ akwatia.
Nti otutuu mmirika dii kane kɔɔ animu kɔforoo akyee dua bi sɛnea obehu no, efiri sɛ na Yesu oobetwam afa saa kwane he so.
Berɛ a Yesu duruu hɔ he, ɔmaa n’ani so hwɛɛ soro ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sakeo, yɛ ntɛm si fam na nnɛ ɔsɛ sɛ metena wo fie.” Ɔno nti, ɔyɔɔ ntɛm sii fam na ɔde anigyeɛ gyee no.
Na behuiɛ he, bɛ nyinaa nwiinwii kaa sɛ.
“Beema debɔneyɛfoɔ yi ne ɔɔkɔsoɛ no yi.” Na Sakeo sɔre gyinaeɛ ka kyerɛɛ Awurade sɛ, “Oo!
Awurade, mede m’ahodeɛ fã ma ahiafoɔ na adeɛ biaa mede nkontompo agye afiri bi hɔ he, mɛbɔ adekorɔ he ho mprɛ nnan ama oni korɔ he.” Na afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ampa, Nnɛ da yi nkwagyeɛ aba fie ha, efiri sɛ ɔno nso yɛ Abraham ba.
Na Nipa Ba he baa sɛ ɔɔbɛhwehwɛ na wagye bɛ a bɛ ayera.” Akontabuo ho mfantoho Berɛ a ɔɔbɛne Yerusalem he, nnipa a bɛtee nea ɔkaeɛ he susuu sɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie oobeyi ne ho adi amonom hɔaa.
Nti ɔmaa bɛ mfantoho bi.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Dehyeɛ bi tuu kwane kɔɔ asaase bi so akyirikyiri sɛ ɔɔkɔgye ahennie tumi aba.
Na ɔfrɛɛ ne nkoa mu du maa bɛ sika a ne dodoɔ bɛyɛ bosome mmeɛnsa akatua.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, ‘Homfa nyɔ adwuma nkosi sɛ mɛba.’ Nso na ne manfoɔ he tane no na betuu abɔfoɔ kɔkaa sɛ, ‘Yɛmpɛ sɛ beema yi di yɛ so hene.’ Berɛ a onyaa ahennie tumi he a afei ɔsane baeɛ he, ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfrɛ nkoa a wama bɛ sika he mmra na bɛmmɛkyerɛ mfasoɔ a bɛanya afiri adwuma a bɛde sika he yɔeɛ he so.
Afei nea odi kane he bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Owura, wo sika he awo mmɔho du.’ Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Mo, akoa pa!
Esiane sɛ woadi adeɛ ketewa mu nɔkorɛ nti, di nkuro du so tumi.’ Afei nea ɔto so mmienu he bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Owura, wo sika he awo mmɔho nnum.’ Ɔka kyerɛɛ yei nso sɛ, ‘Wo nso, di nkuro num so.’ Na foforɔ bɛkaa sɛ, ‘Owura, wo sika he di.
Mede siee ntoma mu.
Wonim bibi!
Na mesuro wo efiri sɛ woyɛ nipa a w’asɛm ɔdene; wofa nea womfa nsieɛ, na wotwa nea wonguiɛ.’ Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Akoa bɔne, wo ankasa w’anum asɛm so ne mebu wo atɛne.
Sɛ wonim sɛ meyɛ nipa a m’asɛm ɔdene, mefa nea memfa nsieɛ na metwa nea menguiɛ a hedeɛ ɛɛne nti na woamfa me sika he ankɔto sikakorabea na nka maba yi magye nsihoo aka ho?’ Nti ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ a begyinagyina hɔ he sɛ, ‘Honye sika he mfiri ne nsam mfa mma nea ɔwɔ mmɔho du he.’ (Na bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Owura, ɔwɔ mmɔho du o!’) ‘Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, biaa a ɔwɔ bi he, bɛbɛma no bi aka ho; na nea wannya bi anka ne deɛ ho he, ketewa a ɔwɔ he mpo bɛbɛgye afiri ne nsam: Bio nso, homfa m’atamfoɔ a bɛampɛ sɛ medi bɛ so hene he mmra ha na hommekuku bɛ m’anim.’ ” Nti, Yesu kaa yeinom akyi he, osiim sɛ ɔɔkɔ Yerusalem.
Yesu fɛm afunumu ba bi Na berɛ a ɔbɛne Betfage ne Betania a ɔya bepɔ a bɛfrɛ no Ngo Bepɔ he so he, ɔsomaa n’asuafoɔ he mu mmienu, sɛ, “Honkɔ akuraa a hohu yi ase, na hohyɛne mu a, hobehu afunumu ba bi a bɛamantam no a nipa biaa ntenaa no so da.
Honsane no mfa no mmra.
Na sɛ bi bisa ho sɛ, ‘Mmɛ nti ne hoosane no a,’ honka sɛ, ‘Awurade hia no.’ ” Nti bɛ a ɔsomaa bɛ he firii hɔ kɔeɛ na bekohuu nea ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ he pɛpɛɛpɛ.
Na berɛ a beesane afunumu he, ne wuranom bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Ɛɛne nti ne hoosane afunumu ba he?” Na bɛkaa sɛ, “Awurade hia no.” Yesu hyɛne Yerusalem Na afei bɛde no kɔmaa Yesu, na bɛtotoo bɛ ntaadeɛ ngugusoɔ guu afunumu he so na bɛde Yesu tenaa so.
Berɛ a ɔɔba he, bɛde bɛ ntaadeɛ ngugusoɔ sesɛɛ kwane he mu.
Ɔɔyɛ aduru kwane a osiane firi Ngo Bepɔ so he so pɛ, asuafodɔm he nyinaa firii aseɛ dii ahurusie na beyii Nyankopɔn ayɛ, tumideɛ a bɛahu he nyinaa ho, sɛ, “Nhyira ne Hene ɔɔba sɛ hene Awurade dini mu!
Asomdwie ya soro, na animuonyam ya sorosoro nohoa!” Nso, Farisifoɔ bi a bɛya nnipakuo he mu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, ka w’asuafoɔ he anim.” Na obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, sɛ yeinom mua bɛ ano a, aboɔ yi mpo bɛteaam.” Yesu su gu kuro he so Na ɔbɛne hɔ he, ɔhwɛɛ kuro he suiɛ kaa sɛ, “Sɛ wo, nnɛ nka wonim nea ɔfa asomdwie ho a, nka ɔyɛ, nso bɛde ahinta wo seesei; efiri sɛ nna bi bɛba a w’atamfoɔ de nnua a ano yɛ mfeamfea bɛto bane atwa wo ho ahyia, na bɛaka wo ahyem ama wo ho ahiahia wo afã nyinaa.
Na bɛde wo ne wo mma a bɛya wo mu bɛhwehwe fam, na bennya boɔ mma ɔnka boɔ so wo mu, efiri sɛ woanhu berɛ a bɛbɛhwɛɛ wo he.” Yesu pamoo adwadifoɔ firii asɔrefie Na ɔkɔɔ asɔrefie hɔ kɔpamoo bɛ a bɛɛtɔno nnoɔma he ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Me fie bɛyɛ mpaebɔ fie,’ nso hode ayɔ dwotwafoɔ atenaeɛ.” Bio nso, ɔkɔɔ so maa nkyerɛkyerɛ asɔre fie hɔ da biaa, na asɔfoɔ mpanyini he ne atwerɛfoɔ ne nnipa he mu atitire he ɔɔhwehwɛ sɛ bebeku no; nso bɛannya kwampa a bɛbɛfa so ayɔ, efiri sɛ nnipa he nyinaa tu taree no tiee no.
Mane mpanyimfoɔ he animguaseɛ Na ɔbaa sɛ da koro bi a na Yesu ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ nkurofoɔ asɔrefie hɔ na ɔɔka asɛmpa he, asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne atwerɛfoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne, na bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ka tumi korɔ a wode yɔ yeinom kyerɛ yɛ, anaa nea ɔde saa tumi yi maa wo he.” Obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Me nso meebisa ho asɛm bi, na honyi me ano.
Tumi a Yohane de bɔɔ asu he firi soro anaa ofiri nnipa?” Afei besusuu ho sɛ, “Sɛ yɛka sɛ, ‘Ofiri soro’ a ɔbɛka sɛ, ‘Mmɛ nti ne hoannye no anni?’ Nso sɛ yɛka sɛ, ‘Ofiri nnipa’ a, nkurofoɔ he nyinaa besi yɛ aboɔ, efiri sɛ bɛgye tom sɛ Yohane yɛ diyifoɔ.” Nti bebuaa sɛ bennim baabi a tumi he firi.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hedeɛ me nso mennka tumi a mede yɛ yeinom nkyerɛ ho.” Nhwɛsofoɔ bɔne bi ho mfantoho Afei ɔyɔɔ mfantoho yi kyerɛɛ nkurofoɔ he sɛ, “Beema bi yɔɔ bobe turo bi de gyaa nhwɛsofoɔ, na otuu kwane kɔɔ mane foforɔ so kodii berɛ tentene.
Afei twaberɛ duruiɛ he, ɔsomaa akoa bi kɔɔ nhwɛsofoɔ he nkyɛne sɛ bɛmma no bobe turo he mu aba he bi.
Nso nhwɛsofoɔ he hwee no, pamoo no ma ɔde nsapan kɔeɛ.
Na ɔsane somaa akoa foforɔ kɔɔ bɛ nkyɛne.
Ɔno nso, bɛhwee no guu n’anim ase ma ɔde nsapan kɔeɛ.
Afei ɔsane somaa nea ɔto so mmeɛnsa.
Yei nso bepirapiraa no sane pamoo no.
Nti bobeturo wura he kaa sɛ, ‘Abɛ ne menyɔ?
Mɛsoma me ba a medɔ no he.
Yei deɛ, ebia bɛbɛfɛre no.’ Berɛ a nhwɛsofoɔ he ani bɔɔ no so he, befirii aseɛ susuu ho sɛ, ‘Mhõõ!
Yei ne diadefoɔ he; homma yenku no, na agyapadeɛ he abɛyɛ yɛ deɛ.’ Nti bɛpamoo no firii bobe turo he mu kokuu no.
Afei, hosusu sɛ mmɛ ne bobeturo wura he de bɛyɔ bɛ?
Ɔbɛba abɛsɛe nhwɛsofoɔ yi na ɔde bobe turo he ama nnipa foforɔ.” Bɛtee yei he bɛkaa sɛ, “Nyankopɔn mpa ngu!” Na ɔhwɛɛ bɛ kaa sɛ, “Hedeɛ nea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Boɔ a adansifoɔ he poeɛ he, ɔno ne abɛyɛ tweasotiboɔ, yi kyerɛ sɛ’?
Biaa a ɔbɛhwe boɔ he so he bebubu pasapasa.
Na biaa a boɔ he bɛhwe no so he, ɔbɛyam no muhumuhu.” Dɔno heaa mu he, atwerɛfoɔ ne asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he pɛɛ sɛ bɛkye no, nso na besuro nkurofoɔ he; behuu sɛ ɔmaa saa mfantoho yi tiaa bɛ.
Toɔ tua ho asɛmmisa Na bɛhwɛɛ no dinn he, bɛbɔɔ nnipa bi paa kokoam sɛ bɛnyɔ bɛ ho sɛ bɛyɛ anɔkwafoɔ, na ama bɛafa nsɛm a ɔkaeɛ he so anya no, na bɛde no ahyɛ abane ne amrado nsa.
Na bebisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, yenim sɛ wo nsɛm ne wo nkyerɛkyerɛ yɛ nɔkorɛ na wonyɛ nyiyimu, na wokyerɛkyerɛ Nyankopɔn kwane nɔkorɛ mu.
Nti, mmara ma ho kwane sɛ yetua toɔ ma Kaesare anaa mmara mma kwane?” Na ohuu bɛ nnaadaasɛm he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Homfa denare mmɛkyerɛ me.
Hwane mfonyini ne ne ntwerɛeɛ ne bɛakurukyire agu so yi?” Bɛkaa sɛ, “Kaesare deɛ.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hedeɛ, homfa Kaesare deɛ mma Kaesare na homfa Nyankopɔn deɛ mma Nyankopɔn.” Na bɛannya soboɔ biaa amfa ammɔ no asɛm yi ho nkurofoɔ he anim, na mmom ne mmuaeɛ he maa bɛ ho dwirii bɛ ma bɛyɛɛ dinn.
Wusɔreɛ ho asɛmmisa Afei Sadukifoɔ a bɛka sɛ wusɔreɛ nni hɔ he mu bi ba bebisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, Mose twerɛ maa yɛ sɛ, ‘Sɛ beema bi nua wɔ yerɛ na owu, na ɔne no anwo ba a, ne nua nware ne yerɛ he na ɔne no nwo mma ma ne nua a wawu he.’ Na anuanom nson bi ya hɔ; nea odi kane he wareeɛ na owuiɛ a wanwo ba.
Nti nea ɔto so mmienu he ne nea ɔto so mmeɛnsa he waree baa he.
Nnipa nson he nyinaa yɔɔ saa wuwuiɛ a bɛannya mma bɛ akyi.
Awieeɛ koraa he, baa he nso wuiɛ.
Nti, wusɔre mu he, bɛ mu hwane ne baa he bɛyɛ ne yerɛ, berɛ a nnipa nson he nyinaa waree no?” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Wiase yi mma deɛ, bɛware na bɛde bɛ ma awareɛ, nso bɛ a bɛabu bɛ sɛ bɛfata sɛ benya wiase foforɔ he ne awufoɔ mu sɔreeɛ hedeɛ, bɛnware na bɛmfa bɛ mma awareɛ.
Nɔkorem he, bentumi nwu bio, efiri sɛ bɛte sɛ abɔfoɔ a bɛnnware, na esiane sɛ bɛyɛ wusɔreɛ mma nti, bɛyɛ Nyankopɔn mma.
Na ɔfa awufoɔ sɔreɛ ho deɛ, Mose nso kyerɛɛ no wuraa he mu nsɛm he mu berɛ a ɔfrɛɛ Awurade sɛ, Abraham Nyankopɔn ne Isak Nyankopɔn ne Yakob Nyankopɔn.’ Ne saa nti, ɔnyɛ awufoɔ Nyankopɔn, na mmom ɔyɛ ateasefoɔ Nyankopɔn, efiri sɛ bɛ nyinaa bɛte ase ma no.” Atwerɛfoɔ he mu bi buaa sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, woaka no yie.” Na bɛannya akokoɔduro ammisa no asɛm biaa bio.
Dawid ba he ne Dawid wura Afei obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne bɛka sɛ Kristo he yɛ Dawid ba?
Efiri sɛ Dawid ankasa ka no Nnwom nwoma he mu sɛ, ‘Awurade ka kyerɛɛ m’Awurade sɛ, “Tena me nsa nifa kosi sɛ mede w’atamfoɔ bɛyɛ wo nane ase ntiasoɔ.” ’ Nti, sɛ Dawid frɛɛ no ‘Awurade’ a, hedeɛ ɔyɛɛ dɛ ne ɔyɛ ne ba?” Atwerɛfoɔ ho kɔkɔbɔ Afei, berɛ a nnipa he nyinaa ootie no he, ɔka kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Honhwɛ yie atwerɛfoɔ he ho; bɛ ne bɛpɛ sɛ bɛhyɛ ntaadeɛ atentene, kyinkyini na bɛpɛ badwa mu nkyea ne hyiadane mu nkonnwa a ɔya animu ne mpanyini tenabea apontoɔ ase, na bɛbɔ akunafoɔ apoo, na nyaatwom nti, bɛbɔ mpaeɛ atentene.
Yeinom benya fobuo kɛseɛ.”
Baa kunafoɔ he afɔrebɔdeɛ Na Yesu maa n’ani so he, ohuu sɛ adefoɔ he de bɛ afɔrebɔdeɛ oogu sika nnaka he mu.
Afei ohuu sɛ kunafoɔ hiani bi de nkaprɛ mma mmienu a ɔnsom bo biaa abegu mu.
Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Nɔkorem meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, ewom sɛ kunafoɔ yi yɛ hiani deɛ, nso nea ɔde agu mu he so kyɛne bɛ nyinaa bɛ deɛ, efiri sɛ afɔrebɔdeɛ a nnipa yi nyinaa de abegu mu he firi nea bɛanya ama no aboro so mu, na baa yi deɛ, ofiri ne hia mu de n’asetenadeɛ a ɔwɔ nyinaa abegu mu.” Asɔrefie sɛeɛ ho nkɔmhyɛ Na afei berɛ a binom ɔɔka asɔre fie he ho asɛm sɛnea bɛde abo-pa ne nnoɔma a bɛahyira so ahyehyɛ he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Nnoɔma a hohu yi, nna bi ɔɔba a bennya boɔ mma ɔnka boɔ so a bennwiri ngu fam.” Nsɛm a odi sɛeɛ yi anim Afei bebisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, mmɛ berɛ koraa ne yeinom bɛba mu, na mmɛ ne ɔbɛyɛ berɛ a otwa sɛ nnoɔma yi ba he ho nsɛnkyerɛnne?” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Honhwɛ yie na bɛannaadaa ho, efiri sɛ nnipa bebree de me dini bɛba abɛka sɛ, ‘Mene no,’ na ‘Berɛ a bɛahyɛ he abɛne!’ Honnni bɛ akyi.
Bio nso, sɛ hote kõ ne sakasaka a, hommma ɔmɔ ho hu.
Na otwa sɛ yeinom di kane sisi, nso awieeɛ he ɔmma hɔaa.” Akodie ne asaasewosoɔ Afei ɔtoaa so ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mane bɛsɔre atia mane na ahennie atia ahennie; na asaasewosoɔ kɛseɛ bɛba, na yaredɔm ne kɔm bɛba mmeammea; na nnoɔma a ohu ne nsɛnkyerɛnne akɛseɛ afiri soro aba.
Taa “Nso, ansa na yeinom nyinaa bɛba he, nkurofoɔ bɛkye ho, na bɛataa ho, de ho akɔ hyia adane mu ne afiase, atwe ho akɔ ahemfo ne amradofoɔ anim, me dini nti.
Gyeɛ Yei bɛma ho kwane ama hoadi adanseɛ.
Nti homfa nto ho tim sɛ, sɛ ɔba saa a, ɔnsɛ sɛ hodwene deɛ hodebeyi ho ho ano ansa, efiri sɛ mɛma ho ano ne nyansa a bɛ a bɛsɔre tia ho nyinaa ntumi nnyina ano anaa bɛmmɔ ngu.
Afei nso, awofoɔ ne anuanom ne abusuafoɔ ne nnamfonom mpo beyi ho ama, na bɛaku ho mu binom; na me dini nti nnipa nyinaa bɛtane ho.
Nso ho tinwi baako mpo ɔnnyera da.
Sɛ honya boasetɔ a, hobenya ho kra.
Yerusalem sɛeɛ ho nkɔmhyɛ “Afei nso, sɛ hohu sɛ asrafodɔm atwa Yerusalem ho ahyia a, hedeɛ honhu sɛ ne sɛeɛ abɛne.
Afei homma bɛ a bɛya Yudea mfiri aseɛ nwane nkɔ mmepɔ he so, na homma bɛ a bɛya kuro he mu he mfiri mu nkɔ, na hommma bɛ a bɛya nkuraase he nkɔ kuro he mu; efiri sɛ yei yɛ aweretɔ nna, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a nea bɛatwerɛ he nyinaa bɛba mu.
Kuro he sɛeɛ Nna he mu he, mmaa a bɛanyinsɛne ne bɛ a bɛma mmɔfra nofoɔ nnue!
Na ahohia kɛseɛ bɛba asaase he so na abufuo aba nkurofoɔ yi so; na bɛbɛtotɔ sekane ano na bɛafa bɛ nommum akɔ amanamane nyinaa mu; na amanamane he bɛsɛe Yerusalem kosi sɛ amanamane he mmerɛ a bɛahyɛ he bɛ duru.
Nipa ba no mmaeɛ “Bio nso, nsɛnkyerɛnne bɛba awia ne bosome ne nsoromma mu, na amanamane ho ayera bɛ asaase so a benhu nea bɛbɛyɔ esiane po a oohuru na oobu fa so nti, na hu ne nnoɔma a ɔɔba asaase so he bɛma nnipa atotɔ piti, efiri sɛ bɛbɛwoso soro ahoɔdene.
Na afei hobehu sɛ Nipa Ba he nam mununkum mu de tumi ne animuonyam kɛseɛ ɔɔba.
Na sɛ nnoɔma yi firi aseɛ sɛ oosisi a, honsɔre nnyina na homma ho ti so, efiri sɛ na hogyeɛ he abɛne.” Borɔdoma ho adesua Nti, ɔmaa mfantoho bi sɛ, “Honhwɛ borɔdoma dua ne nnua a aka nyinaa.
Sɛ onya fefɛ na hohwɛ a, hohu sɛ ahuhuro berɛ abɛne.
Saa ara ne ho nso, sɛ hohu sɛ nnoɔma a mekaa ho asɛm he oosisi a, honhu sɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie he abɛne.
Nɔkorem, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ saa awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ yi ontwam da gye sɛ nnoɔma nyinaa bɛba mu ansa.
Soro ne asaase betwam, nso me nsɛm deɛ, onntwam da.
Yesu bɔɔ asuafoɔ he kɔkɔ sɛ bɛnwɛne “Na honhwɛ ho ho so yie, na adidi mmorosoɔ ne nsaborɔ ne asetena mu dadwene anhyɛ ho akoma so, na da he ammɛto ho mpofirem te sɛ fidie, na sɛ ɔbɛba nnipa a bɛtete asaase ani nyinaa so.
Nti, honwɛne, na honsrɛ berɛ nyinaa na hoatumi agyina nnoɔma a otwa sɛ osisi yi nyinaa ano, na hoatumi agyina Nipa Ba he anim akokoɔduro so.” Na Yesu kyerɛkyerɛ asɔrefie hɔ dabiaa, na oduru anadwo a, ofiri kɔtena Ngo Bepɔ he so.
Na nkurofoɔ he nyinaa ba ne nkyɛne asɔrefie hɔ anɔpahema betie no.
Bɛbɔɔ Yesu ti so pɔ Afei na paanoo a mmɔreka nnim Afahyɛ a bɛfrɛ no Twam he ɔɔbɛne.
Na asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he nso ɔɔhwehwɛ kwane a bɛbɛfa so aku Yesu, efiri sɛ na besuro nkurofoɔ he.
Yuda gye toom sɛ obeyi Yesu ama Na Satan wuraa Yuda a bɛfrɛ no Iskariot, a na ɔyɛ dummienu he mu baako he mu; na Yuda ne asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne asɔrefie ahwɛfoɔ he kɔkaa kwane a ɔbɛfa so ayi no ama bɛ he ho asɛm: Nti bɛ ani gyeɛ na bɛpenee so sɛ bɛbɛma no sika bi.
Nti ɔgye toom, na ofirii aseɛ hwehwɛɛ kwane a ɔde beyi no ama bɛ berɛ a nnipa bebree nni hɔ.
Twam Afahyɛ ho ahosiesie Na da a bedi paanoo a mmɔreka nnim afahyɛ duruiɛ he, na ɔsɛ sɛ bɛde twam dwane he bɔ afɔdeɛ.
Nti Yesu somaa Petro ne Yohane ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honkɔ na honkosiesie Twam aduane he mma yemmedi.” Bebisaa no sɛ, “Hefa ne wopɛ sɛ yekosiesie?” Obuaa sɛ, “Hontie!
Sɛ howura kuro he mu a, beema bi a ɔsõ ahina a nsuo yam behyia ho.
Honni n’akyi nkɔ fie a ɔbɛkɔ mu he mu.
Na hommisa fiewura he sɛ, ‘Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he dɛ, “Hefa ne ahɔhodane a me ne m’asuafoɔ bedi twam afahyɛ ya mu he ya?” ’ Na beema he bɛkyerɛ ho dane kɛseɛ bi a ɔya abansoro a bɛasiesie mu.
Honyɔ ahosiesie he hɔ.” Nti befirii hɔ kɔeɛ, na behuu bibiaa sɛnea ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ he pɛpɛɛpɛ, na besiesiee Twam aduane he.
Adidie a otwa toɔ Berɛ he duruiɛ he, ɔkɔtenaa didipono ho a na asomafoɔ he ka ne ho.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mepɛ paa sɛ me ne ho bedi twam yi ansa na mahu amane; na meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, menni bio kosi da a ne nkyerɛaseɛ paa he bɛbam Nyankopɔn ahennie mu.” Na afei ɔfaa kuruwa daa ase kaa sɛ, “Honye yei na honkyɛ nom; na meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, efiri nnɛ ɔɔkɔ yi, mennom bobesa he bio kosi sɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie he bɛba.” Awurade Adidie he asehyɛ Afei nso, ɔfaa paanoo daa ase, bubuu mu de maa bɛ kaa sɛ, “Yei ne me honam a bɛde bɛma, esiane ho nti.
Honyɔ yei mfa nkae me.” Saa ara nso ne berɛ a bedii anwummerɛduane he wieeɛ he, ɔfaa kuruwa he na ɔdaa ase de maa bɛ kaa sɛ, “Kuruwaa yi ne me mogyaa, apam foforɔ he mogyaa, a ho nti, beehwie agu.
“Na honhu sɛ, nea obeyi me ama he ne me te didipono yi ho, ɔyam sɛ Nipa Ba he ɔɔkɔ sɛnea bɛahyɛ ato hɔ he deɛ; nso, nipa a obeyi no ama he nnue!” Nti befirii aseɛ bisabisaa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ bɛ mu hwane ne bɛyɔ yei.
Yesu kasa tiaa ahomasoɔ Na akasakasaa bi nso sɔree asuafoɔ he ntam fa bɛ mu nea ɔyɛ kɛseɛ ho.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ.
“Amanamane ahene di bɛ so akokorokosɛm, na bɛfrɛ bɛ a bedi bɛ so tumi he adɛɛfoɔ.
Na ho deɛ, ɔnsɛ sɛ hoyɔ saa.
Na mmom homma nea ɔyɛ ho mu kɛseɛ he nyɛ te sɛ kumaa koraa, na kandifoɔ he nsom.
Na hwane ne yɛ kɛseɛ, nea ɔte adidipono ho anaa nea ɔɔsom?
Ɔnyɛ nea ɔte adidipono ho he a?
Me mmom deɛ, meya ho mu sɛ somfo.
“Ho ne hoda so bata me ho me sɔhwɛ brɛ mu.
Na me nso sɛnea m’agya ayi me sɛ menni ahennie so he, saa ara ne me nso meeyi ho sɛ ahennie sodifoɔ, na hoadidi anom me pono so m’ahennie mu, na hoatena nhennwa so abu Israel mmusuakuo dummienu he atɛne.
Petro pa ho nkɔmhyɛ “Simon, Simon, hwɛ!
Satan pɛ sɛ onya kwane na ohuhu ho so sɛ aburo.
Nso masrɛ ama wo, na wo ampa wo gyidie; na wo deɛ sɛ daakye wo sane gyina a, hyɛ wo nuanom dene.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade, masiesie me ho sɛ me ne wo bɛkɔ afiase ne wuo mu mpo.” Nso Yesu kaa sɛ, “Petro, meeka akyerɛ wo sɛ, ansa na akokɔ bɛbɔno nnɛ he, na woasane mprɛnsa sɛ wonnim me.” Kɔkɔbɔ bi Afei Yesu bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Berɛ a mesomaa ho a hoamfa sika kotokuo ne akwantuo bɔtɔ ne mpaboa he, bibi hiaa ho anaa?” Bɛkaa sɛ, “Daabi!” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ.
“Seesei deɛ, homma nea ɔpɛ sika kotokuo he mfa, na nea ɔpɛ akwantuo bɔtɔ he nso nyɔ saa; na ma nea onni sekane he ntɔno n’ataadeɛ ngugusoɔ na ɔntɔ bi.
Na meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, otwa sɛ nea bɛatwerɛ yi bam fa me ho sɛ, ‘Bɛkane no fraa mmaratofoɔ.’ Na nea ɔfa me ho he anya abam.” Na bɛkaa sɛ, “Awurade, hwɛ, sekane mmienu di.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ.
“Ɔyɛ.” Yesu dii waerɛhoɔ ya Getsemane Befirii adi he, Yesu kɔɔ Ngo Bepɔ he so sɛnea na ɔtaa yɔ he; na asuafoɔ he nso dii n’akyi.
Beduruu hɔ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hommɔ mpaeɛ na hoankɔ sɔhwɛ mu.” Afei ɔtwee ne ho firii bɛ ho kɔɔ bea bi a hɔ bɛne; na obuu nkotodwe firii ase bɔɔ mpaeɛ sɛ, “Agya, sɛ wopɛ a, yi kuruwa yi firi me so.
Nso, ɔnyɛ me pɛ, na mmom ma wo pɛ ne nyɛ hɔ.” [Na bɔfoɔ bi firi soro yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ no hyɛɛ no dene.
Na berɛ a ne ho yera no he, ɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ dendenndene; na ne ho mfifire yɛɛ sɛ mogyaa a ɔɔsosɔ gu fam.]
Na ɔsɔre firii mpaebɔ mu he, ɔkɔɔ asuafoɔ he nkyɛne kohuu sɛ awerɛhoɔ nti bɛadeda.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ɛɛne nti ne hoadeda yi?
Honsɔre na hommɔ mpaeɛ, na hoankɔ nsɔhwɛ mu.” Bɛkyee Yesu Yesu gu so ɔɔkasa he, mpofirem, nnipakuo bi baeɛ a na dummienu he mu baako a bɛfrɛ no Yuda di bɛ anim; na ɔbaa Yesu nkyɛne bɛfee n’ano.
Na Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Yuda, wode mfeano ooyi Nipa Ba he ama?” Berɛ a bɛ a bɛka ne ho he huu nea oobesi he, bebisaa sɛ, “Awurade, yɛntwe sekane nkɔ bɛ so anaa?” Bɛ mu baako mpo twee sɔfo panyini akoa he so sekane twaa n’aso nifa firii hɔ.
Na Yesu kaa sɛ, “Homma no nso ha yiaa!” Na ɔde ne nsa kaa aso he maa ne ho tɔɔ no.
Afei Yesu bisaa asɔfoɔ mpanyini ne asɔrefie ahwɛfoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ a bɛaba ɔɔbɛkye no he sɛ.
“Hode sekane ne nkontimaa aba me so te sɛ meyɛ dwotwafoɔ?
Berɛ a na me ne ho ya asɔrefie hɔ daa he, hoantene ho nsa me so.
Nso yei ne ho berɛ ne sum mu tumi.” Petro paa Yesu Afei bɛkyee Yesu de no kɔeɛ, na bɛde no kɔɔ sɔfo panyini he fie, na Petro di bɛ akyi ya akyirikyiri.
Berɛ a bɛsɔɔ gya adihɔ tenatenaa ho he, na Petro te bɛ mu bi.
Na abaawa bi huu no sɛ ɔte gya he ho; na ɔhwɛɛ no gyee kaa sɛ, “Na beema yei nso ka ne ho.” Nso Petro sanee sɛ, “Baa, mennim no.” Na berɛ tiaa bi akyi he, nnipa foforɔ bi huu no kaa sɛ, “Wo nso woka bɛ ho.” Na Petro kaa sɛ.
“Beema, menka bɛ ho.” Na bɛyɛ dɔnhwere baako akyi he, nipa foforɔ nso bɛkaa asɛm korɔ heaa sɛ, “Ampa na yei nso ka ne ho; nɔkwasɛm di, ɔyɛ Galileani!” Nso Petro kaa sɛ, “Damfo, mennim nea wooka he.” Na hɔaa, berɛ a ogu so ɔɔkasa he, akokɔ bɔneeɛ.
Na Awurade danee n’ani hwɛɛ Petro, na Petro kae asɛm a Awurade ka kyerɛɛ no he sɛ, “Ansa na akokɔ bɛbɔno nnɛ he, na woapo me mprɛnsa.” Na ofirii adi de awerɛhoɔ kosuu yayaaya.
Yesu ho agodie Afei mmeema a na bekita ne mu he firii aseɛ dii ne ho agorɔ bobɔɔ no; na bɛde adeɛ kataa n’anim kɔɔ so bisaa no sɛ, “Hyɛ nkɔm!
Hwane ne bɔɔ wo yi?” Na bɛkɔɔ so kekaa abususɛm bebree tiaa no.
Na adeɛ kyeeɛ he, mane he mpanyimfoɔ abadwakuo he, asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he nyinaa ka boom, na bɛde no kogyinaa bɛ asennibea kaa sɛ.
“Sɛ wone Kristo he a, ka kyerɛ yɛ.” Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ meka kyerɛ ho mpo a, ɔnyɛ adeɛ a hobɛgye adi.
Afei nso, sɛ mebisa ho asɛm a, hommua me nso.
Nso, efiri sesɛɛ ɔɔkɔ he nipa Ba he bɛtena Nyankopɔn nsa nifa a tumi yam he so.” Na bɛ nyinaa bebisaa no sɛ, “Nti, wone Nyankopɔn Ba he?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hoaa ne hooka sɛ mene no.” Bɛkaa sɛ, “Abɛ adanseɛ bio ne yehia?
Yɛate afiri ɔno ankasa n’anum.”
Bɛde Yesu begyinaa Pilato anim Nti nnipadɔm he nyinaa sɔreeɛ, na bɛde Yesu kɔmaa Pilato.
Afei befirii aseɛ bɔɔ no soboɔ sɛ, “Yɛakye beema yi sɛ ɔɔsɛe yɛ mane, na ɔbra sɛ bentua toɔ mma Kaesare na ɔka sɛ ɔno ne hene Kristo he.” Afei Pilato bisaa no sɛ, “Wone Yudafoɔ hene he ampa?” Na obuaa no sɛ, “W’ankasa ne wooka.” Afei Pilato ka kyerɛɛ asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne nnipakuo he sɛ, “Menhu bɔne biaa beema yi ho.” Nso bɛkaa no dendenndene sɛ, “Ɔkyerɛkyerɛ Yudea nyinaa de hwanyane mane he mu, ofirii aseɛ mpo firii Galilea ne ɔde abeduru ha yi.” Berɛ a Pilato teeɛ he, obisaa sɛ beema he yɛ Galileani anaa?
Bɛde Yesu kɔmaa Herode Na ohuu sɛ Yesu hyɛ Herode tumi ase he, ɔma bɛde no kɔmaa Herode a nna he mu na n’ankasa ya Yerusalem he.
Berɛ a Herode huu Yesu he n’ani gyee yie, efiri sɛ na ofiri mmerɛ tentene apɛ sɛ ohu no esiane ne ho asɛm a waate nti, na na ɔpɛ sɛ ɔyɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne bi ma ohu.
Afei ofirii aseɛ bisaa no nsɛm bebree; nso Yesu ammua no.
Na asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne atwerɛfoɔ he kɔɔ so sɔre gyinaeɛ de abufuɔ bɔɔ no soboɔ aniberɛ so.
Afei Herode ne n’asraafoɔ he bɔɔ no adapaa, goroo ne ho, na bɛhyɛɛ no ahentaadeɛ bi de no kɔmaa Pilato bio.
Afei Herode ne Pilato bɛyɛɛ nnamfoɔ saa da heaa; kane he, na nka bɛyɛ atamfoɔ.
Pilato di maa Yesu Afei Pilato frɛɛ asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he, mane sodifoɔ he ne ne manfoɔ he hyiaa mu na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hode nipa yi braa me sɛ bi a ɔma nkurofoɔ te atua, na hwɛ, mehwehwɛɛ n’asɛm mu ho anim ha yiaa, nso manhu nnyinasoɔ biaa a hode bɔɔ no soboɔ.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, Herode nso anhu bi, na ɔsane de no braa yɛ; na hwɛ, ɔnyɔɔ bibiaa a ɔsɛ sɛ beku no.
Nti mɛtwe n’aso na magyaa no.” [Nso ɔsɛ Pilato sɛ daa, afahyɛ he mu, ogyaa deduani baako ma bɛ.]
Na nnipadɔm he nyinaa teaam kaa sɛ, “Fa yei kɔ, na gyaa Baraba ma yɛ!” (Saa nipa yi, ɔnam sakasaka bi a ɔkɔyɔɔ no kuro mu hɔ ne awudie bi a odiiɛ nti ne bɛde no kɔtoo afiase.)
Pilato buaa Yesu kumfɔ Pilato maa ne nne so ne nnipadɔm he kasaa bio, efiri sɛ na ɔpɛ sɛ ogyaa Yesu.
Na befirii aseɛ teateam sɛ.
“Bɔ no asennua mu!
Bɔ no asennua mu!” Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ ne mprɛnsa so sɛ.
“Abɛ bɔne ne nipa yi ayɔ?
Menhu bibiaa a ɔya ne ho a ɔsɛ sɛ owu.
Nti mɛtwe n’aso na magyaa no.” Afei bɛde nne kɛseɛ kaa no dendenndene sɛ ɔmmɔ no asennua mu; na bɛ nne bunkamm ne deɛ so.
Nti Pilato buu atɛne sɛnea bɛɛhwehwɛ he.
Na ogyaa deɛ sakasaka ne awudie nti bɛde no kɔtoo afiase maa bɛ sɛnea bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔnyɔ he; nso oyii Yesu maeɛ sɛdeɛ na bɛɛpɛ he.
Yerusalem mmaa Na bɛde no ɔɔkɔ he, bɛsɔɔ Simon, Kireneni bi a na ofiri akuraa bi ase ɔɔba kurom, na bɛde asennua he soaa no dii Yesu akyi.
Na dɔm kɛseɛ bi a befiri mane he mu ne mmaa a beedi abooboo na beesu dii n’akyi.
Yesu danee ne ho kyerɛɛ mmaa he kaa sɛ, “Yerusalem mmaa, honnsu mmma me; na mmom honsu mma ho ho ne ho mma!
Na hwɛ, nna bi ɔɔba a nkurofoɔ bɛka sɛ, ‘Nhyira ne bonyini ne yafunu a ɔnwoo da ne nofoɔ a bɛnnom ano da!’ Afei bebefiri aseɛ aka akyerɛ mmepɔ sɛ, ‘Hommegu yɛ so,’ ne nkokoɔ sɛ, ‘honkata yɛ so!’ Na sɛ bɛde yei ɔɔyɔ dua mono a, mmɛ ne bɛde bɛyɔ dua wuiɛ?” Na bɛde nnebɔnyɛfoɔ mmienu bi nso aka ne ho a beekoku bɛ.
Golgota Berɛ a beduruu baabi a bɛfrɛ hɔ Golgota he, bɛbɔɔ Yesu ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ he asennua mu, baako ya ne nifa, ne baako nso ya ne benkum.
Na Yesu kaa sɛ, “Agya fa kyɛ bɛ efiri sɛ bennim nea bɛɛyɔ.” Bio nso, bɛtwee ntonto kyɛɛ ne ntaadeɛ faeɛ.
Na nkurofoɔ he gyina hɔ ɔɔhwɛ.
Na atumfoɔ he dii ne ho agorɔ kaa sɛ, “Ɔgyee binom; sɛ yei ne Kristo a Nyankopɔn ayi no he a, ma onnye ne ho ɛ!” Yesu ho agodie Asraafoɔ he mpo dii ne ho agorɔ, na bɛbaa ne nkyɛne de nsa kekakeka maa no kaa sɛ, “Sɛ wone Yudafoɔ hene he a, gye wo ho!” Bɛde ntwerɛeɛ bi nso bɔɔ n’atifi sɛ, “Yei ne Yudafoɔ hene he.” Wudini a ɔsakraa n’adwene he Na nnebɔnyɛfoɔ a bɛasɛne bɛ he mu baako firii aseɛ kasa tiaa Yesu sɛ, “Wone Kristo he, anaa ɔnyɛ wo a?
Gye wo ho, na gye yɛ nso.” Na nea ɔka ho he buaa no kaa n’anim sɛ, “Nti wonsuro Nyankopɔn koraa berɛ a woya afobuo korɔ yiaa mu yi?
Yɛ deɛ, wuo fata yɛ, efiri sɛ nea yɛ yɔeɛ so akatua ne yɛ nsa aka yi, na yei deɛ, ɔnyɔɔ mfomsoɔ biaa.” Na ɔtoaa so kaa sɛ, “Yesu, sɛ woba w’ahennie mu a, kae me.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nɔkorem meeka akyerɛ wo sɛ, nnɛ wobɛka me ho Paradise hɔ.” Yesu wuo Na aabɔ bɛyɛ awia dummienu, afei sum baa asaase nyinaa so kosii awie nnɔnmmeɛnsa, na awia duruu sum; afei asɔredane he mu ntoma a otwa mfimfini he mu tee mmienu.
Na Yesu de nne kɛseɛ teaam sɛ, “Agya, wo nsam ne mede me honhom hyɛ.” Ɔkaa yei he ogyaa mu.
Yesu wuo ho hu kaa nkurofokuo he Na sraani panyini he huu nea asi he, ɔhyɛɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam sɛ, “Ampa, na nipa yi yɛ teneneeni.” Na berɛ a nnipakuo a bɛahyiam ɔɔhwɛ nea ɔɔkɔ so he nyinaa huu nea asi he, bɛde bɛ nsa bobɔɔ bɛ koko so firii hɔ kɔeɛ.
Bio nso, na bɛ a benim no he nyinaa gyinagyina akyiri.
Na mmaa a bedii n’akyi firii Galilea he nso gyinagyina hɔ ɔɔhwɛ yeinom.
Yesu sie Na hwɛ, na beema bi ya hɔ a bɛfrɛ no Yosef a ɔyɛ badwani na ɔyɛ nipa pa na ɔtene nso.
Ɔno deɛ, wampene bɛ agyina ne bɛ nneyɔeɛ he so.
Ofiri Yudafoɔ kuro Arimatea mu, na ɔnoaa nso ɔɔtwɛne Nyankopɔn ahennie he.
Saa beema yi kɔɔ Pilato nkyɛne kɔsrɛɛ no Yesu amu he.
Na okoyii amu he kyekyeree no nwera mu, na ɔde kɔtoo da a bɛatwa no boɔ mu a bensie nipa biaa mu da mu.
Na da he yɛ ahoboaboa da ma homeda a na ɔɔba he.
Na mmaa he nso a bɛne no firi Galilea baeɛ he dii akyire kɔhwɛɛ da he ne sɛdeɛ bɛde n’amu he too hɔ faeɛ.
Na bɛsane besiesiee nnuro ne ngo hwamhwam.
Na homeda he, bɛhomeeɛ sɛnea mmara he teɛ he.
Yesu sɔre firii awufoɔ mu Na nnawɔtwe he da a odi kane he, bɛyɔɔ ntɛm de aduhwam a bɛasiesie he kɔɔ nna he so.
Nso behuu sɛ bɛamini boɔ a na ɔda nna he ano he afiri hɔ, na berɛ a bɛkɔɔ mu he, bɛanhu Awurade Yesu amu he.
Berɛ a bɛ tirim ayɛ bɛ kesenenee he, hwɛ, mmeema mmienu a bɛhyehyɛ ntaadeɛ nahanaha begyinaa bɛ nkyɛne.
Berɛ a hu aka mmaa he na bɛasisi bɛ ti aseɛ he, mmeema he ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ.
“Mmɛ nti ne hoohwehwɛ teasefoɔ awufoɔ mu yi?
Onni ha, na mmom wasɔre.
Honkae nea ɔka kyerɛɛ ho berɛ a na ɔda so ya Galilea he, sɛ otwa sɛ beyi Nipa Ba he hyɛ abɔnefoɔ nsa na bɛbɔ no asennua mu na da a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he wasɔre.” Nti bɛkae ne nsɛm he, na bɛsane firii da he so de nea asi he nyinaa ho amaneɛ kɔbɔɔ dubaako he ne bɛ a bɛaka he nyinaa.
Na ɔyɛ Maria Magdalene, ne Yohana, ne Yakobo maame Maria.
Afei nso, mmaa a aka a bɛka bɛ ho he kaa yeinom kyerɛɛ asomafoɔ he.
Nso, nsɛm yi yɛɛ bɛ sɛ nsenhunu bi, na bɛannye mmaa he anni.
[Na Petro sɔre tutuu mmirika kɔɔ da he so, na ɔbɔɔ ne mu ase he, ohuu nwera a bedekyekyeree Yesu amu he nkoaa.
Nti ofirii hɔ kɔɔ fie, na nea asi he maa ne ho dwirii no.]
Yesu ne asuafoɔ bino kɔɔ Emaus Na hwɛ, da heaa na bɛ mu mmienu ɔɔkɔ Emaus a ɔyɛ akuraa bi a ofiri hɔ kɔ Yerusalem bɛyɛ akwansini nson, na bɛɛbɔ nea asi he nyinaa ho nkɔmmɔ.
Berɛ a bɛɛbɔ nkɔmmɔ na beesusu ho he, Yesu ankasa bɛtoo bɛ na ɔne bɛ bɔɔ anane nanteeɛ, nso bɛanhu sɛ ɔyɛ ɔno a. Obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Abɛ asɛm ne honam kwane so oosusu ho yi?” Na begyinaeɛ a na bɛ anim ayɛ bosaa.
Bɛ mu baako a ne dini de Kleopa buaa no sɛ, “Nti wo nkoaa ne wote Yerusalem a woyɛ hɔhoɔ a nti wonnim asɛm a asi hɔ nnansa yi?” Na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ asɛm ne asi?” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nea ɔfa Nasareni Yesu, a ɔyɛ diyifoɔ a ɔwɔ tumi, nnwuma ne kasa mu, Nyankopɔn ne mane he nyinaa anim he ho he, ne sɛnea yɛ asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne atumfoɔ he yii no maeɛ ma bebuu no kumfɔ na bɛbɔɔ no asennua mu he.
Na yɛ deɛ, yɛ ani daa so sɛ nka ɔno ne ɔɔbɛgye Israel.
Nso yei nyinaa akyi he, nnansa ni a nsɛm yi siiɛ.
Bio nso, mmaa bi a befiri yɛ mu maa yɛ ho dwirii yɛ, efiri sɛ bɛyɔɔ ntɛm kɔɔ da he so nso bɛanhu n’amu he, na bɛbɛkaa sɛ abɔfoɔ yii bɛ ho adi kyerɛɛ bɛ ma bɛkaa sɛ ɔte ase.
Afei, bɛ a bɛne yɛ ya hɔ he binom kɔɔ da he so; na bekohuu sɛ ɔte saa, sɛnea mmaa he bɛkaeɛ he pɛpɛɛpɛ, nso bɛ deɛ bɛanhu no.” Nti ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “O adwenharefoɔ a hoyɛ nyaa ho akoma mu sɛ hobɛgye deɛ adiyifoɔ he aka nyinaa adi!
Nti na ɔnsɛ sɛ Kristo he hu amaneɛ yi nyinaa na ɔkɔ n’Animuonyam mu anaa?” Na ɔde firi Mose ne Adiyifoɔ he nyinaa so kyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ nsɛm a ɔfa ne ho a ɔya Twerɛsɛm he nyinaa mu.
Awieeɛ koraa he, bɛbɛnee akuraa a na bɛɛkɔ aseɛ he, na ɔyɔɔ te sɛ nea ɔɔtoa so akɔ n’anim: Nso bɛhyɛɛ no dendenndene sɛ “Tena yɛ nkyɛne, efiri sɛ nwunu adwo, na adeɛ anya asa.” Nti ɔkɔtenaa bɛ nkyɛne.
Na ɔne bɛ te adidiiɛ he ɔfaa paanoo hyiraa so bubuiɛ, na ofirii aseɛ de maa bɛ.
Afei bɛ ani biebie koraa ma behuu sɛ ɔyɛ ɔno a; na ɔyera firii bɛ nkyɛne.
Na bɛbisabisa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Berɛ a ɔne yɛ ɔɔkasa kwane so na ɔɔkyerɛ Twerɛsɛm he mu kyerɛ yɛ he, ampusu yɛ akoma anaa?” Asuafoɔ mmienu he sane kɔ Yerusalem Na dɔno heaa mu he, bɛsɔre sane kɔɔ Yerusalem, na bekohuu dubaako he ne bɛ a bɛka bɛ ho he sɛ bɛahyiam, ɔɔka sɛ “Ampa, Awurade anyane, na waayi ne ho adi akyerɛ Simon!” Afei bɛ ankasa nso bɛkaa nsɛm a osii kwane so ne sɛdeɛ behuu no paanoobubuo mu he kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Yesu yi ne ho kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he Na bɛɛkasa saa he, ɔno ankasa begyinaa bɛ mfimfini ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Asomdwie nka ho.” Nso esiane sɛ na hu aka bɛ, na besuro nti, besusuu sɛ bɛahu samane bi.
Nti ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ɛɛne nti ne ho akoma tutu, na mmɛ nti ne ho adwene yɛ ho naa yi?
Honhwɛ me nsa ne me nane, na hoahu sɛ ɔyɛ meaa; homfa ho nsa nso me mu nhwɛ, na samane nni honam ne nnompe sɛnea hohu sɛ mewɔ yi.” Na ɔkaa yei he, ɔde ne nsa ne ne nane kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Yesu didii asuafoɔ he anim Nso berɛ a anigyeɛ nti bɛda so nnye nni na asɛm he yɛ bɛ nwanwa he, obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Howɔ aduane bi ya hɔ anaa?” Na bɛmaa no apataa sini bi a bɛatoto; ɔgyeeɛ, na odii no bɛ anim.
Yesu kyerɛkyerɛ anyamesɛm ase Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Yei ne me nsɛm a meka kyerɛɛ ho berɛ a na meda so ka ho ho he, sɛ otwa sɛ nea bɛatwerɛ afa me ho ya Mose mmara ne Adiyifoɔ he ne Nnwom he mu nyinaa ba mu.” Afei obiee bɛ adwene mu yie ma bɛtee Twerɛsɛm he ase, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Saa kwane yi so ne bɛatwerɛ sɛ Kristo he behu amaneɛ na da a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he wasɔre afiri awufoɔ mu, na ne dini so ne bebegyina aka adwensakra ne bɔne fakyɛ ho asɛm amansa nyinaa mu, na bɛbɛhyɛ aseɛ afiri Yerusalem.
Hobɛyɛ nnoɔma yi ho adansefoɔ.
Na hwɛ, meesoma nea m’Agya ahyɛ ho bɔ he aba ho so.
Ho deɛ, hontena kuro he mu nkosi sɛ bɛbɛma ho ahoɔdene a ofiri soro.” Yesu sorokɔ Na ɔde bɛ firii adi dii bɛ anim kɔɔ Betania, na ɔmaa ne nsa so hyiraa bɛ.
Na oohyira bɛ he ɔne bɛ ntam teteɛ na bɛmaa no so kɔɔ soro.
Na bɛkotoo no sane de anigye kɛseɛ baa Yerusalem.
Na bɛtenaa asɔre fie hɔ daa yii Nyankopɔn ayɛ.
NNIANIMU Yohane Asɛmpa he yi Yesu Kristo kyerɛ sɛ Nyankopɔn Asɛm a ɔya hɔ daa: “Na Asɛm he bɛyɛɛ honam bɛtenaa yɛ mu” .
Sɛdeɛ nwoma heaa ka he, bɛatwerɛ saa Asɛmpa yi sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a akenkanfoɔ bɛgye Yesu adi sɛ ɔno ne Agyenkwa he, Nyankopɔn Ba he, nea bɛahyɛ ne ho bɔ sɛ bɛnam ne mu gyidie so benya nkwa .
Asɛmpa he fa a odi kane he ka Yesu nsɛnkyerɛnne ahodoɔ a ɔyɔ de kyerɛɛ sɛ ɔno ne Agyenkwa a bɛahyɛ ne ho bɔ he, Nyankopɔn Ba he.
Afei, ɔkyerɛkyerɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne ahodoɔ he mu.
Saa fa yi ma yehu sɛnea binom gyee Yesu diiɛ na bɛbɛyɛɛ n’asuafoɔ.
Bio, ɔkasa fa binom nso a bɛko tiaa no na bɛannye no anni.
Ti - kyerɛ ayɔnkofa soronko a ɔbɛdaa Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he ntam anadwo a bɛkyee no, ne awerɛkyekyerɛ ne ahosiesie nsɛm a ɔde gyaa bɛ anadwo a adeɛ ɔɔbɛkye ama bɛabɔ no asennuam he.
Ti a otwa toɔ he ka Yesu kyeɛ, gyina a bɛde no kogyinaa asennibea, n’asennua so wuo, ne wuo ne ne wusɔreɛ, ne n’ahoyie a oyi kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ berɛ a ɔsɔre firii awufuom he ho asɛm.
Yohane si daa nkwa a ɔya Kristo mu he so dua, akyɛdeɛ a ɔde ma n’akyidifoɔ, sɛ ɔno ne kwane he, nɔkorɛ he ne nkwa he.
Nea ɔda adi pefee ya Yohane Asɛmpa he ho ne sɛnea ɔde nnoɔma a yɛtaa hu no yɛ daa asetena mu toto honhom mu nnoɔma ho, nnoɔma bi te sɛ nsuo, paanoo, hann, dwanhwɛfoɔ he ne ne nnwane, bobe ne n’aduaba.
MU NSƐM Ahyɛaseɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ mu :- Suboni Yohane ne Yesu asuafoɔ a bedi kane he :- Yesu abɔntene so asɛnka :—: Yesu nna a otwa toɔ odii no Yerusalem ne ne mpɔtamu :—: Awurade wusɔreɛ ne n’ahoyie he :- Awieeɛ nsɛm: Yesu yii ne ho adi bio ya Galilea :-
Asɛm he bɛyɛɛ honam Mfitiaseɛ he na Asɛm he ya hɔ, na Asɛm he ne Nyankopɔn ne bɛya hɔ, na Asɛm he ankasa nso yɛ Nyankopɔn.
Ɔnoaa ne mfitiaseɛ he na ɔne Nyankopɔn ya hɔ.
Nnoɔma nyinaa nam ne so ne baeɛ, na bɛankwati no annyɔ bibiaa a bɛyɔeɛ.
Ne mu ne nkwa ya, na nkwa he ne nnipa hann.
Na hann he hyerɛn sum mu, na sum he ntumi mmunkam mfa ne so.
Nipa bi ya hɔ a Nyankopɔn somaa no a na ne dini de Yohane.
Ɔbaa sɛ oobedi hann he ho adanseɛ, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a nnipa nyinaa nam hann he so bɛgye adi.
Ɔnyɛ ɔno ne hann he, na mmom ɔbaa sɛ oobedi hann he ho adanseɛ.
Saa berɛ he, na hann trodoo a ɔhyerɛn ma nnipa nyinaa he ɔɔba wiase.
Na ɔya wiase deɛ, na ɔnam ne so ne bɛbɔɔ wiase, nso wiase anhu no.
Ɔbaa ɔno ankasa ne deɛ mu, nso ne deɛ annye no antom.
Na dodoɔ a bɛgyee no he―meekyerɛ, bɛ a bɛgyee no dini diiɛ he―ɔmaa bɛ akwannya sɛ bɛnyɛ Nyankopɔn mma.
Yeinom yɛ mma a omfiri mogyaa anaa nea honam pɛ anaa nea beema pɛ so ne awo bɛ, na mmom Nyankopɔn pɛ so ne ɔnam a bɛawo bɛ.
Na Asɛm he bɛyɛɛ honam bɛtenaa yɛ mu, na yɛahu n’animuonyam sɛ Agya he Ba a ɔwoo no koro maa yɛ, adom ne nɔkorɛ ahyɛ no ma.
(Yohane dii ne ho adanseɛ na ɔteaam sɛ, “Yei ne mekaa ne ho asɛm sɛ, ‘Nea odi m’akyi he so kyɛne me, efiri sɛ ɔya hɔ ansa na meeba.’ ”) Ɔnam sɛ adom ahyɛ no ma nti, yɛ nyinaa yɛanya adom aka adom ho.
Mmara he deɛ, bɛnam Mose so ne de maeɛ, na adom ne nɔkorɛ he deɛ nam Yesu Kristo so ne baeɛ.
Biaa nni hɔ a wahu Nyankopɔn da.
Nyankopɔn a ɔyɛ Ba koro he, nea ɔya Agya he kokom he, ɔno ne wada no adi.
Suboni Yohane adanseɛ a odi faa Yesu ho Na yei ne adanseɛ a Yohane diiɛ berɛ a Yudafoɔ he somaa asɔfoɔ ne Lewifoɔ firi Yerusalem baa ne nkyɛne bebisaa no sɛ, “Wone hwane?” Ɔpaem kaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ mene Kristo he.” Na bebisaa no sɛ, “Wone Elia anaa?” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Daabi, menyɛ Elia.” “Wone diyifoɔ he?” Obuaa sɛ, “Daabi.” Nti bebisaa no sɛ, “Hedeɛ, wone hwane?
Ma yɛ mmuaeɛ nkɔ ma bɛ a bɛsomaa yɛ he.
Ɛɛne ne yɛnka mfa wo ho nkyerɛ bɛ?” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Me ne deɛ ɔya serɛ he so a ɔɔteam sɛ, ‘Homma Awurade kwane he ntene,’ sɛnea diyifoɔ Yesaia kaeɛ he.” Na bɛasoma bɛ firi Farisifoɔ mu.
Na bebisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne wonyɛ Kristo he, Elia anaa diyifoɔ he, nso wobɔ asu yi?” Yohane buaa bɛ sɛ, “Mede nsuo ne bɔ asu.
Nso bi gyina ho mu a honnim no a odi m’akyi; memfata sɛ mesane ne mpaboa ahoma mpo.” Yei siiɛ ya Betania a ɔya Yordan agya, baabi a na Yohane bɔ asu he.
Nyankopɔn Adwamaa Na adeɛ kyeɛ he, Yohane huu sɛ Yesu ɔɔba, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Nyankopɔn adwamaa a oyi wiase bɔne kɔ he di!
Yei ne nea mekaa no ho asɛm sɛ, ‘Nipa bi di m’akyi a ɔɔba a ɔkyɛne me, efiri sɛ ɔya hɔ ansa na meeba.’ Me deɛ, na mennim no; nso mede nsuo bɛbɔɔ asu sɛ ɔbɛda no adi akyerɛ Israel.” Na Yohane dii adanseɛ sɛ, “Mehuu Honhom he sɛ ofiri soro ɔɔba sɛ abuburo abesi ne so Me deɛ na mennim no, nso nea ɔsomaa me maa mede nsuo bɔɔ asu he ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, ‘Nea wobehu sɛ Honhom he abesi ne so he, ɔno ne de Honhom Kronkron bɔ asu he.’ Na meaa maahu na maadi ho adanseɛ sɛ ɔno ne Nyankopɔn Ba he.” Yesu Asuafoɔ a Bedi kane Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, na Yohane ne n’asuafoɔ mmienu gyina hɔ, na ohuu Yesu sɛ ɔɔkɔ he, ɔteaam sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Nyankopɔn adwamaa he di!” Na asuafoɔ mmienu he tee sɛ ɔɔka yei he, bedii Yesu akyi Yesu danee ne ho a ohuu sɛ bedi n’akyi he, obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne hoopɛ?” Bebisaa no sɛ, “Rabuni” (asekyerɛ ne kyerɛkyerɛni), “Wote he?” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hommra mmɛhwɛ.” Bɛba behuu baabi a na ɔte, na bɛ ne no tenaa hɔ saa da he.
Na aabɔ bɛyɛ awia nɔnnan.
Simon Petro nua Andrea yɛ nnipa mmienu a bɛtee nea Yohane kaeɛ na bedii Yesu akyi he mu baako Ohuu ɔnoaa ne nua Simon Petro kane, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Yɛahu Mesaia he” (nea bɛasra no ngo he).
Ɔde Simon baa Yesu nkyɛne, na Yesu hwɛɛ no kaa sɛ, “Wone Simon, Yohane ba.
Bɛbɛfrɛ wo Kefa” (asekyerɛ ne Petro).
Yesu frɛɛ Filipo ne Natanael Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, Yesu yɔɔ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛkɔ Galilea.
Ohuu Filipo, na ɔka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Di m’akyi.” Na Filipo firi Bɛtesaida, kuro a Andrea ne Petro firi mu he.
Filipo huu Natanael, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Yɛahu nea Mose kaa ne ho asɛm ya mmara he mu na adiyifoɔ he nso kaa ne ho asɛm he, Yesu, Yosef ba a ofiri Nasaret he.” Natanael kaa sɛ, “Nti, adepa bi betumi afiri Nasaret aba?” Filipo ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Bra bɛhwɛ.” Berɛ a Yesu huu sɛ Natanael ɔɔba he, ɔka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Israelni ankasa a nnaadaa biaa nni ne mu di!” Natanael bisaa no sɛ, “Wonim me he?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Mehuu wo sɛ woya borɔdoma dua he ase ansa na Filipo ɔɔfrɛ wo mpo.” Natanael kaa sɛ, “Ampa, Rabuni, wone Nyankopɔn Ba he!
Wone Israelfoɔ Hene he!” Yesu kaa sɛ, “Meka kyerɛ wo sɛ mehuu wo borɔdoma dua he ase ne wogyedi yi?
Wobehu nnoɔma akɛseɛ a ɔkyɛne yeinom.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nɔkwasɛm di, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, hobehu soro sɛ abie na Nyankopɔn abɔfoɔ oodi aforosiane Nipa Ba he so.”
Kana Ayefohyia Yei akyi da a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he, na ayefohyia bi ɔɔkɔ so Kana a ɔya Galilea.
Na Yesu maame ya hɔ.
Na bɛtoo nsa frɛɛ Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he nso sɛ bɛmmra ayefohyia he ase.
Na nsa he saeɛ he, Yesu maame ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Bɛ nsa asa.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ “Maame, mmɛ ne wo pɛ sɛ meyɔ?
Me berɛ nnya nnuruiɛ.” Na ne maame ka kyerɛɛ asomfo he sɛ, “Honnyɔ nea ɔbɛka akyerɛ ho biaa.” Na nsuhina nsia a bɛde aboɔ ayɔ sisi hɔ sɛnea Yudafoɔ ahodwira ho nhyehyɛeɛ teɛ he.
Na mu biaa betumi afa galɔn aduonu anaa aduasa.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Homfa nsuo nhyehyɛ nhina yi mama.” Nti bɛde nsuo guguu nhina he mu na ne ɔyɛɛ ma tɛntɛm.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Afei honsesa bi nkɔ ma adidieɛhwɛfoɔ panyini he.” Nti bɛsesaa bi kɔeɛ.
Adidieɛhwɛfoɔ panyini he kaa nsuo a na adane nsa he bi hwɛeɛ he na onhu baabi a nsa he firi (na asomfoɔ he deɛ na benim nea asi).
Ɔfrɛɛ ayefokunu he na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Biaa de nsa pa ma n’ahɔhoɔ kane, na sɛ bɛnom pii wie a ɔde nea ɔnyɛ papa he nso ama bɛ.
Na wo deɛ wode nsa pa he asie abesi sesɛɛ.” Yesu yɔɔ yei Kana a ɔya Galilea.
Yei ne nsɛnkyerɛnne a odi kane, na ɔdaa n’animuonyam adi; na n’asuafoɔ he gyee no diiɛ.
Yei akyi he Yesu ne ne maame, ne ne nuanom ne n’asuafoɔ he sane kɔɔ Kapernaum kodii nna kakra.
Yesu pamoo adwadifoɔ firii asɔredane he mu Yudafoɔ Twam Afahyɛ he bɛneeɛ he, Yesu kɔɔ Yerusalem.
Ohuu binom sɛ bɛɛtɔno anantwie, nnwane ne mmorɔnoma, na sika sesafoɔ nso te bɛ pono ho ya asɔrefie hɔ.
Ɔde nhoma yɔɔ mmaa de pamoo bɛ nyinaa, nnwane ne anantwie he firi asɔredane mu hɔ, na ohwiee sikasesafoɔ he sika guiɛ, na ɔkaa bɛ apono he nso butubutuiɛ.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ a bɛɛtɔno mmorɔnoma he sɛ, “Homfa yeinom mfiri ha, honnyɛ m’Agya fie dwadibea.” Na n’asuafoɔ he kae sɛ bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Wofie ho mmɔdenmmɔ bɛhyɛ me ma.” Afei Yudafoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Mmɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne ne wode kyerɛ yɛ a nti wooyɔ yei yi?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Honnwiri asɔredane yi ngu, na mede nnansa besi no bio.” Na Yudafoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Ei!
Mfenhyia aduannan nsia ne bɛde sii asɔredane yi oo, ne wo deɛ wooka sɛ wode nnansa bɛma so asi hɔ yi?” Nea ɔteɛ ne sɛ, ɔno mmom deɛ, na ɔyɛ ne nipadua asɔredane ho asɛm na ɔɔka.
Ɔsɔre firii awufoɔ mu he, n’asuafoɔ he kae sɛ na ɔtaa ka saa; na bɛgyee twerɛsɛm he ne asɛm a Yesu kaeɛ he diiɛ.
Na berɛ a ɔya Yerusalem Twam afahyɛ ase he, nnipa bebree a behuu nsɛnkyerɛnne a ɔyɔeɛ he gyee no diiɛ.
Nso, Yesu deɛ wamfa ne ho anto bɛ so, efiri sɛ na onim bɛ nyinaa.
Afei nso na onhia sɛ biaa di nipa ho adanseɛ kyerɛ no, efiri sɛ na ɔno ankasa nim nea ɔya nipa mu.
Nikodemo kɔsraa Yesu Na afei na nipa bi ya hɔ a na ɔka Farisifoɔ he ho a na bɛfrɛ no Nikodemo, a na ɔyɛ Yudafoɔ panyini.
Ɔbaa Yesu hɔ anadwo bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Rabuni, yenim sɛ woyɛ kyerɛkyerɛni a wofiri Nyankopɔn nkyɛne ne aba, na bi ntumi nyɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne a woyɔ yi, gye sɛ Nyankopɔn ka ne ho.” Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Meeka nɔkwasɛm paa akyerɛ wo sɛ, bɛamfiri soro anwo bi a ontumi nnya kyɛfa biaa Nyankopɔn ahennie he mu.” Nikodemo bisaa no sɛ, “Ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na nipa a woanyini he, bɛatumi awo no bio?
Obetumi akɔ ne maame yam ama bɛ awo no bio anaa?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ wo sɛ, bɛamfa nsuo ne honhom anwo bi a ontumi nkɔ Nyankopɔn ahennie mu.
Nea befiri honam mu awo no he yɛ honam, na nea befiri Honhom mu awo no he yɛ honhom.
Mma no nyɛ wo nwanwa sɛ meeka akyerɛ wo sɛ, ɔsɛ sɛ befiri soro wo ho.
Mframa bɔ kɔ baabi a ɔpɛ, na hote sɛ ɔɔbɔ, nso honnim baabi a ofiri ne baabi a ɔɔkɔ.
Saa ne bi a bɛawo no honhom mu he teɛ.” Nikodemo buaa sɛ, “Ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na yeinom atumi aba mu?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Nti wo a woyɛ Israel kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he, wonnim yeinom?” Meeka akyerɛ wo nɔkorem paa sɛ, “Nea yenim ne yɛka, na nea yɛani ahu ne yedi ho adanseɛ, nso honnye yɛ adanseɛ he nni.
Sɛ maaka asaase so nsɛm akyerɛ ho na honnye nni a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na meka soro nsɛm kyerɛ ho a hoagye adi?
Nipa biaa mforo nkɔɔ soro gye sɛ nea wasiane afiri soro, Nipa Ba he.
Na sɛnea Mose maa wɔ he so serɛ so he, saa ne otwa sɛ bɛma Nipa Ba he so, na biaa ɔbɛgye no adi he, benya daa nkwa.” Na sɛnea Nyankopɔn dɔɔ wiase di, sɛ ɔde ne Ba ɔwoo no koro he maeɛ, na biaa a ɔbɛgye no adi he anyera, na mmom wanya daa nkwa.
Na Nyankopɔn ansoma ne Ba he amma wiase sɛ ommebu wiase atɛne, na mmom sɛ bɛmfa no so nnye wiase nkwa.
Nea ɔgye Nyankopɔn Ba he di he, bemmu no atɛne, na nea ɔnnye no nni he, bɛabu no atɛne dada efiri sɛ wannye Nyankopɔn Ba koro pɛ he anni.
Na yei ne atemmuo he, sɛ hann he aba wiase na nnipa dɔ sum kyɛne hann he, efiri sɛ bɛ nnwuma yɛ bɔne.
Biaa a ɔyɔ bɔne he tane hann he, na ɔmma hann he ho, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a ne nnwuma he onna adi.
Na nea ɔyɔ setie ma nɔkorɛ he ba hann he ho sɛ ne nnwuma mmɛda adi, efiri sɛ ɔyɔ no Nyankopɔn mu.
Yesu ne Suboni Yohane Yeinom akyi he, Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he kɔɔ Yudea asaase so.
Ɔne bɛ tenaa hɔ kakra na ɔbɔɔ nkurofoɔ asu.
Na Yohane nso ɔɔbɔ asu nsuo Ainon a ɔbɛne Salim efiri sɛ na asuasu pii ya hɔ, na nnipa kɔɔ so baa hɔ maa no bɔɔ bɛ asu.
Na bennya mfaa Yohane nkɔtoo afiase.
Na akyinnyegyeɛ bi a ɔfa ahodwira ho sɔree Yohane asuafoɔ ne Yudani bi ntam.
Nti bɛbaa Yohane nkyɛne bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, beema a na ɔne woya Yordan agya a wodii ne ho adanseɛ he, ɔɔbɔ asu ha, na nnipa nyinaa ɔɔkɔ ne nkyɛne.” Yohane buaa sɛ, “Nipa ntumi nya bibi gye sɛ bɛde firi soro ama no.
Ho ankasa hodi adanseɛ sɛ mekaa sɛ, ‘Ɔnyɛ mene Kristo he, na mmom bɛsomaa me dii n’anim.’ Nea ayeforɔ he wɔ no he ne ayefokunu.
Na ayefokunu adamfo a ogyina hɔ na otie ayefokunu he deɛ, n’ani gye paa.
Nti m’anigyeɛ awie pɛyɛ.
Ɔno deɛ, otwa sɛ ɔkɔ so yɛ kɛse, na me deɛ, me so hwane.” Nea Ofiri Soro ba Nea ofiri soro ba he boro biaa so.
Ampa nea ofiri asaase so he firi asaase so, na ɔka asaase so nsɛm.
Nea ofiri soro ba he boro biaa so.
Odi nea wahu na wate ho adanseɛ, nso biaa nnye n’adanseɛ he ntom.
Nea ɔgye n’adanseɛ he tom he asɔ ano sɛ Nyankopɔn yɛ nɔkwafoɔ.
Na nea Nyankopɔn asoma no he ka Nyankopɔn asɛm, na Nyankopɔn nsusu Honhom ansa na ɔde ama.
Agya he dɔ Ba he, na ɔde nnoɔma nyinaa ahyɛ ne nsa.
Nea ɔgye ba he di he wɔ daa nkwa, na nea ontie ba he onhu nkwa, na Nyankopɔn abufuo ya ne so.
Yesu ne Samariani baa he Na Awurade huu sɛ Farisifoɔ he ate sɛ, “Oonya asuafoɔ bebree, na ɔɔbɔ nnipa bebree asu kyɛne Yohane.” Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, Yesu ankasa ammɔ asu, na n’asuafoɔ he ne ɔmaa bɛbɔeɛ.
Ofirii Yudea na ɔsane n’akyi baa Galilea.
Nso na otwa sɛ ɔfa Samaria.
Nti ɔbaa Samaria kuro bi a bɛfrɛ no Sikar, baabi a ɔbɛne asaase a Yakobo de maa ne ba Yosef he.
Na Yakobo abura he ya hɔ.
Esiane sɛ na Yesu abrɛ nti, ɔtenaa Yakobo abura he so sɛ ɔɔhome.
Na aabɔ bɛyɛ awia dummienu.
Na Samariani baa bi baa sɛ ɔɔbɛsa nsuo.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ma me nsuo he bi nnom.” (Na Yesu asuafoɔ he kɔ kuro he mu sɛ bɛɛkɔtɔ aduane.)
Samariani baa he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne wo a woyɛ Yudani woobisa me Samariani baa nsuo?” (Na Yudafoɔ ne Samariafoɔ nni twaka biaa.)
Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Sɛ wonim Nyankopɔn akyɛdeɛ ne nea oobisa wo sɛ, ‘Ma me nsuo he bi nnom’ a nka wobebisa no na wama wo nkwa nsuo.” Na baa he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Owura, wonni adeɛ a bɛde sa nsuo mpo, na abura he nso mu dɔ, nti hefa ne woya nkwa nsuo yi firi?
Woyɛ kɛseɛ kyɛne yɛ nana Yakobo a ɔde abura he maa yɛ na ɔno ankasa ne ne mma ne ne mmoa nom bi he anaa?” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Biaa a ɔnom saa nsuo yi bi he, sukɔm bɛde no bio, na nea ɔbɛbɛnom nsuo a mede bɛma no he, sukɔm ɔnne no da.
Na mmom nsuo a mede bɛma no he, bɛyɛ abura a ofifiri ne mu kɔ daa nkwam.” Na baa he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Owura, ma me saa nsuo yi bi nnom, na sukɔm anne me bio, na mankɔ so amma ha ammɛsa nsuo.” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ baa he sɛ, “Kɔfrɛ wo kunu, na hommra ha.” Na baa he kaa sɛ, “Menni kunu.” Na Yesu kaa sɛ, “Woaka no yie sɛ, ‘Menni kunu’; efiri sɛ woaware kununom num, na nea wo ne no wɔ hɔ seesei mpo, ɔnyɛ wo kunu.
Nea woaka he yɛ nɔkorɛ.” Na baa he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Owura, afei maahu sɛ woyɛ diyifoɔ.
Yɛ nananom som bepɔ yi so, nso ho deɛ hoka sɛ Yerusalem ne baabi a ɔsɛ sɛ bɛsom.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Baa, gye me di, berɛ bi ɔɔba a honnsom Agya he bepɔ so anaa Yerusalem.
Hosom nea honnim no, na yɛ deɛ yɛsom nea yenim no, efiri sɛ nkwagyeɛ firi Yuda.
Na berɛ he ɔɔba, na anya aba sɛ nɔkorɛ asomfoɔ bɛsom Agya he honhom ne nɔkorem, efiri sɛ nnipa saa ne Agya he ɔɔhwehwɛ.
Nyankopɔn yɛ honhom, na ɔsɛ sɛ bɛ a bɛsom no he som no honhom ne nɔkorem.” Na baa he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Menim sɛ Mesaia he ɔɔba” (nea bɛfrɛ no Kristo he).
“Sɛ ɔba a, ɔbɛka yei nyinaa akyerɛ yɛ.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Me a meekasa akyerɛ wo yi, mene no.” Saa berɛ heaa ne n’asuafoɔ he baeɛ, na ɔyɛɛ bɛ nwanwa sɛ ɔne baa he bɛɛkasa.
Nso biaa anka sɛ “Mmɛ ne woohwehwɛ?” Anaa “Mmɛ nti ne wo ne no ɔɔkasa?” Na afei baa he gyaa n’asuhina hɔ kɔɔ kuro he mu kɔka kyerɛɛ nnipa he sɛ, “Hommra mmɛhwɛ beema bi a waka m’asumasɛm nyinaa akyerɛ me!
Ɔnyɛ yei ne Kristo he anaa?” Befirii kuro he mu baa ne nkyɛne.
Saa berɛ he na n’asuafoɔ he gu so ɔɔka sɛ, “Rabuni, didi.” Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mewɔ aduane bi di a honnim.” Nti asuafoɔ he bisaa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Bi abra no bibi adi anaa?” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “M’aduane ne sɛ mɛyɔ nea ɔsomaa me he apɛdeɛ, na mawie n’adwuma.
Ɔyɛ a honka sɛ, ‘Aaka bosome nnan, na twaberɛ aduru’?
Hwɛ, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ homma ho ani so nhwɛ mfuo he sɛ aho sɛ betwa.
Nea otwa he ɔɔgye akatua dada na ɔɔboaboa aba ano akɔ daa nkwam; na nea oduaeɛ ne nea otwaeɛ nyinaa ani agye abom.
Na yei ma asɛm he yɛ nɔkorɛ sɛ, ‘Bi dua, na bi twa.’ Mesomaa ho sɛ ho nkotwa nea hoanyɔ ho adwuma.
