Binom ayɔ adwuma, na ho ne hoanya bɛ adwuma he ho mfasoɔ.” Ɔnam baa he adanseɛ sɛ, “Ɔkaa m’asumasɛm nyinaa kyerɛɛ me” nti, Samariafoɔ bebree a na bɛya saa kuro he mu gyee Yesu diiɛ.
Nti berɛ a Samariafoɔ he baa ne nkyɛne he, bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔntena bɛ nkyɛne nnaanu.
Na nnipa bebree a bɛboro kane nnipa he gye diiɛ, ɔnam nea baa he kaeɛ nti.
Bɛka kyerɛɛ baa he sɛ, “Afei, ɔnyɛ nea wokaeɛ he nti ne yɛagye adi, efiri sɛ yɛ ankasa yɛate na yɛahu sɛ nipa yi ne wiase Agyenkwa he ampa.” Yesu sane baa Galilea Na nnanu akyi he, ofirii hɔ kɔɔ Galilea (efiri sɛ Yesu ankasa dii adanseɛ sɛ diyifoɔ nni anidie ɔno ankasa ne kurom.)
Berɛ a ɔbaa Galilea he, Galileafoɔ he gyee no efiri sɛ bɛkɔɔ afahyɛ he ase bi, na behuu nea ɔyɔeɛ he.
Yesu saa Ahenkwaa Panyini bi ba Yadeɛ Afei Yesu sane baa Kana a ɔya Galilea, baabi a ɔdanee nsuo nsa he bio.
Na ahenkwaa panyini bi ya hɔ a ne ba yare ya Kapernaum.
Berɛ a beema he tee sɛ Yesu firi Yudea aba Galilea he, ɔkɔɔ ne nkyɛne kɔsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔmɛsa ne ba yadeɛ, efiri sɛ na ɔda wusu.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ho deɛ, hoanhu nsɛnkyerɛnne ne anwanwadeɛ a honnye nni.” Ahenkwaa panyini he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Owura, bra na me ba he anwu ansa.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ “Kɔ, wo ba he ate apɔ!” Na nipa he gyee asɛm a Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no he diiɛ, na ɔkɔeɛ.
Na ɔɔkɔ he, ne nkoa behyiaa no, na bɛkaa sɛ, “Wo ba he ate apɔ!” Na obisaa bɛ berɛ pɔtee a ne ho yɛɛ no dene he, na bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nnora bɛyɛ awia dummienu ne abunu he kɔeɛ.” Na papa he huu sɛ ɔyɛ saa berɛ heaa ne Yesu kaa sɛ, “Wo ba he onnwu.” Nti ɔne n’abusuafoɔ nyinaa gye diiɛ.
Yei nso ne nsɛnkyerɛnne a ɔtɔ so mmienu a Yesu firi Yudea baa Galilea he, ɔyɔeɛ.
Yesu saa Yadeɛ Homeda Yei akyi he na Yudafoɔ ɔɔhyɛ fa, na Yesu kɔɔ Yerusalem.
Na tadeɛ bi ya Yerusalem “Nnwantene Pono” kɛseɛ he ho a bɛfrɛ no Hebri kasa mu sɛ Betesda a ɔwɔ abranaa num.
Ha ne ayarefoɔ pii—anifrafoɔ, mpakye, ne bɛ a bɛ fa adwodwo deda.
[Nea ɔteɛ ne sɛ, sɛ Awurade bɔfoɔ he hono nsuo he wie a, yarefoɔ a obedi kane akɔtɔ nsuo he mu he nya ayaresa.]
Na abranteɛ bi ya hɔ a wayare mfie aduasa-nwɔtwe.
Berɛ a Yesu huu beema he sɛ ɔda hɔ he, na onim sɛ wayare akyɛre he, obisaa no sɛ, “Wopɛ sɛ wo ho yɛ wo dene?” Yarefoɔ he buaa no sɛ, “Owura, menni nipa biaa a sɛ nsuo he hono a ɔde me bɛkɔ akɔtɔ mu, na sɛ meyɛ sɛ meekɔtɔ mu a na bi adi m’anim kane akɔtɔ mu.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɔre fa wo kɛtɛ na nante.” Amonom hɔaa beema he ho yɛɛ no dene, na ɔfaa ne kɛtɛ firi aseɛ nanteeɛ.
Nso na saa da he yɛ homeda.
Nti Yudafoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ beema a Yesu saa no yadeɛ he sɛ, “Ɔyɛ homeda, na mmara mma kwane sɛ wobɛsoa wo kɛtɛ.” Na obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Nea ɔsaa me yadeɛ heaa ne ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, ‘Fa wo kɛtɛ na nante.’ ” Bebisaa no sɛ, “Nipa hwane ne ka kyerɛɛ wo sɛ, ‘Fa wo kɛtɛ na nante?’ ” Nso na nea ne ho ayɛ no dene he nnim nipa korɔ a ɔsaa no yadeɛ he, efiri sɛ na Yesu atwe ne ho kɔ, ɔnam nnipakuo a na bɛya hɔ nti.
Yei akyi he, Yesu huu no asɔredane he mu, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Hwɛ, wo ho ayɛ dene, nyɔ bɔne bio na nea ɔkyɛne yei amma wo so.” Beema he kɔka kyerɛɛ Yudafoɔ he sɛ, Yesu ne saa no yadeɛ.
Yei nti Yudafoɔ he hyɛɛ aseɛ sɛ bɛɛtaa Yesu, efiri sɛ ɔyɔɔ yeinom homeda.
Na Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “M’Agya gu so ɔɔyɔ adwuma besi sesɛɛ, na me nso meeyɔ adwuma.” Na yei nti afei Yudafoɔ he hwehwɛɛ sɛ bebeku no, efiri sɛ ɔnyɛ homeda nkoaa ne wabu so, na mmom ɔfrɛ Nyankopɔn sɛ ɔno ankasa n’Agya, de yɛ ne ho sɛ ɔne Nyankopɔn yɛ pɛ.
Tumi a Ba he wɔ Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, Ba he ankasa ntumi mmɔ ne ti mu nyɔ hwee, gye sɛ nea ohu sɛ Agya he yɔ, efiri sɛ bibiaa Agya he yɔ he, ɔno ne Ba he nso yɔ.
Agya he dɔ Ba he, na ɔbɛkyerɛ no nnoɔma a ɔno ankasa yɔ nyinaa.
Na ɔbɛkyerɛ no nnwuma akɛseɛ asene yeinom na ayɛ ho nwanwa.
Na sɛnea Agya he nyane awufoɔ na ɔma bɛ nkwa he, saa ne Ba he nso de nkwa ma bɛ a ɔno ankasa pɛ.
Na Agya he mmu biaa atɛne, na mmom ɔde atemmuo nyinaa ahyɛ Ba he nsa, na ama biaa adi Ba he ni sɛnea bedi Agya he ni heaa.
Nea onni Ba he ni he, onni Agya a ɔsomaa no he nso ni.
Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, nea otie m’asɛm na ɔgye nea ɔsomaa me he di he wɔ daa nkwa, na ɔmma atemmuom, na mmom waafiri wuom aba nkwam.
“Nɔkorɛ meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, berɛ he ɔɔba, na anya aduru, sɛ awufoɔ bɛte Nyankopɔn Ba he nne, na bɛ a bebetie no he benya nkwa.
Na sɛnea Agya he wɔ nkwa ɔnoaa ne mu he, saa na ɔde ama Ba he nso sɛ onya nkwa ɔno ankasa ne mu.
Na waama no tumi sɛ ommu atɛne nso, efiri sɛ ɔno ne Nipa Ba he.
Hommma yei nyɔ ho nwanwa, efiri sɛ berɛ he ɔɔba a bɛ a bɛya adakamenam nyinaa bɛte ne nne, na bɛafiri adi, na bɛ a bɛayɔ papa he bɛkɔ nkwa wusɔreɛ mu, na bɛ a bɛayɔ bɔne he bɛkɔ fobuo wusɔreɛ mu.
Yesu ho Adansedie “M’ankasa mentumi mmɔ me tim nyɔ hwee.
Nea mete heaa ne megyina so bu atɛne, na atɛne a mebu he tene, efiri sɛ menhwehwɛ nea m’ankasa mepɛ, na mmom nea ɔsomaa me he apɛdeɛ.
“Sɛ m’ankasa medi me ho adanseɛ a, m’adanseɛ he nyɛ nɔkorɛ.
Bi ya hɔ a odi me ho adanseɛ na menim sɛ adanseɛ a odi fa me ho he yɛ nɔkorɛ.
Hosomaa binom kɔɔ Yohane nkyɛne, na odii nɔkorɛ adanseɛ, na me deɛ, mennye adanseɛ nipa biaa nkyɛne, na meeka yeinom na hoanya nkwa.
Na ɔyɛ kanea a ɔdɛre na ɔhyerɛn, na ho deɛ, na hopɛ sɛ ho ani gye mmerɛ kakra ne hann mu.
Nso mewɔ adanseɛ a ɔkyɛne Yohane deɛ he, efiri sɛ nnwuma a m’Agya de ahyɛ me nsa sɛ menyɔ he, nnwuma a meeyɔ heaa di me ho adanseɛ sɛ Agya heaa ne asoma me.
Na Agya he a ɔsomaa me he ankasa di me ho adanseɛ.
Hontee ne nne, na honhuu ne su nso, na n’asɛm nni ho mu, efiri sɛ nea ɔsomaa me he mpo honnye no nni.
“Hohwehwɛ twerɛsɛm he mu, efiri sɛ hogye di sɛ ɔno ne bɛma ho nkwa, na ɔnoaa nso ne di me ho adanseɛ.
Nso, hommpɛ sɛ ho ba me nkyɛne na hoanya nkwa.
Mennye animuonyam mfiri nnipa nkyɛne.
Na menim yie sɛ honni Nyankopɔn dɔ ya ho mu.
Maaba m’Agya dini mu, nso honnye me, sɛ foforɔ ba ɔno anakasa ne dini mu a, ɔno ne hobɛgye no.
Hobɛyɔ dɛ na hoagye adi berɛ a hogye animuonyam firi hoaa ho ho, na honnye animuonyam mfiri Nyankopɔn korɔ he nkyɛne?
Honnsusu sɛ mɛbɔ ho soboɔ akyerɛ Agya he, na nea ɔbɔ ho soboɔ he ya hɔ, ɔno ne Mose a hode ho ani ato ne so he.
Sɛ hogye Mose di a, hobegye me nso adi, efiri sɛ Mose twerɛɛ me ho asɛm.
Na sɛ honnye asɛm a ɔtwerɛɛ he nni a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na hoagye me nsɛm adi?”
Nnipa Mpem Num Aduanema Yeinom akyi he, Yesu kɔɔ Galilea po, nea bɛsane frɛ no Tiberia po, he agya.
Na nnipakuo kɛseɛ kɔɔ so dii n’akyi, efiri sɛ behuu nsɛnkyerɛnne a na ɔɔyɔ ma ayarefoɔ.
Yesu kɔɔ bepɔ he so na ɔne n’asuafoɔ he tenaa hɔ.
Nso na Yudafoɔ Twam Afahyɛ he abɛne.
Afei Yesu maa n’ani so na ohuu sɛ nnipakuo kɛseɛ ɔɔba ne nkyɛne he, obisaa Filipo sɛ, “Hefa na yɛbɛtɔ paanoo ama nnipa yi adi?” Obisaa yei de sɔɔ no hwɛeɛ, efiri sɛ na ɔno ankasa nim nea ɔɔbɛyɔ.
Filipo buaa sɛ, “Paanoo a ne boɔ bɛyɛ paani bosome nsia akatua mpo ɔnso bɛ sɛ bɛ mu biaa benya bi adi.” Na asuafoɔ he mu baako, Andrea, Simon Petro nua beema, ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Abeemaa bi ya ha a ɔwɔ atokoɔ paanoo nnum ne nkyenam nketewa mmienu.
Nso yei bɛyɛ nnipadɔm yi dɛ?” Na Yesu kaa sɛ, “Homma nnipa he ntenatena ase!” Nso na serɛ pii ya hɔ.
Nti mmeema a bɛ dodoɔ bɛyɛ mpem num tenatenaa ase.
Na Yesu faa paanoo ne nkyenam he, na ɔdaa ase he, ɔkyɛ maa bɛ a bɛtete hɔ he; saa nso ne ɔmaa bɛ nkyenam he dodoɔ a biaa hia.
Na bɛmemeeɛ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Hommoaboa mproprowa he ano, na bi anyera.” Nti bɛboaboa ano, na atokoɔ paanoo mproprowa he yɛɛ nkɛntɛne dummienu ma ma.
Afei nnipa he huu nsɛnkyerɛnne a Yesu yɔeɛ he, bɛkaa sɛ, “Nɔkwasɛm, diyifoɔ a ɔɔba wiase he di.” Afei berɛ a Yesu huu sɛ bɛpɛ sɛ bɛkye no si no hene he, ɔno ankasa twee ne ho kɔɔ bepɔ he so bio.
Yesu nantee Nsuo so Na nwunu doeɛ he, n’asuafoɔ he kɔɔ mpoano, na bɛforo tenaa kodoɔ bi mu sɛ beetwa po he akɔ Kapernaum.
Saa berɛ he na sum ahyɛ dada, na Yesu nnya mmaa bɛ nkyɛne.
Na mframa kɛseɛ bɔ maa po he huruiɛ.
Afei berɛ a bɛharee bɛyɛ nkwansini nnan he, behuu sɛ Yesu nam po he so ɔɔba kodoɔ he ho, na besuroeɛ.
Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ɔyɛ me a, honnsuro.” Afei deɛ na bɛpɛ sɛ ɔbɛtena kodoɔ he mu, na ankyɛre koraa ne kodoɔ he duruu asaase a bɛɛkɔ so he so.
Paanoo a ofiri Soro baeɛ Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, nnipakuo a na begyina po he agya he huu sɛ kodoɔ biaa nni hɔ gye sɛ baako a n’asuafoɔ he kɔɔ mu he, nso Yesu ne bɛ ankɔ kodoɔ he mu, na n’asuafoɔ he nkoaa ne bɛkɔeɛ.
Na afei akodoɔ firi Tiberia baa baabi a Awurade daa ase, na bedii paanoo he.
Na nnipakuo he huu sɛ Yesu ne n’asuafoɔ he mu biaa nni hɔ he, bɛkɔtenatenaa kodoɔ nketewa mu baa Kapernaum bɛhwehwɛɛ Yesu.
Na berɛ a behuu no po he agya he, bebisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, mmɛ berɛ ne wobaa ha?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Nɔkwasɛm a ɔyam ne sɛ, ɔnyɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne a hohuiɛ nti ne hoohwehwɛ me, na mmom paanoo a hodi meeɛ he nti a. Honnyɔ aduane a ɔsɛe ho adwuma, na mmom honyɔ aduane a ɔtena hɔ de kɔ daa nkwam a Nipa Ba he de bɛma ho he ho adwuma, efiri sɛ, ɔno ne Agya Nyankopɔn ankasa de ne nsɔano agye no atom.” Nti bebisaa no sɛ, “Ɛɛne ne ɔsɛ sɛ yɛ yɔ na yɛayɔ Nyankopɔn nnwuma?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Nyankopɔn adwuma ne sɛ hobɛgye nea ɔsomaa no he adi.” Nti bebisaa no sɛ, “Abɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne ne wobɛyɔ na yɛagye wo adi?
Mmɛ adwuma ne wooyɔ?
Yɛ nananom dii mana serɛ he so sɛnea bɛatwerɛ he, ‘Ɔmaa bɛ paanoo a ofiri soro ma bediiɛ.’ ” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem paa sɛ, ɔnyɛ Mose ne maa ho paanoo a ofiri soro he, na mmom m’Agya ne maa ho paanoo kann a ofiri soro he.
Na Nyankopɔn paanoo ne nea osiane firi soro ba na ɔma wiase nkwa he.” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Owura, ma yɛ paanoo he bi da biaa.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mene nkwa paanoo he.
Nea ɔba menkyɛne he kɔm ɔnne no da, na nea ɔgye me di he, sukɔm ɔnne no da.
Nso maka akyerɛ ho sɛ, hoahu me nso honnye nni.
Bibiaa a Agya he de bɛma me he bɛba me nkyɛne, na nea ɔba me nkyɛne he, mempam no da, efiri sɛ mefiri soro ne aba sɛ hobɛyɔ nea ɔsomaa me he apɛdeɛ, na ɔnyɛ m’ankasa me deɛ.
Nea ɔsomaa me he apɛdeɛ ne sɛ memma nea ɔde ama me he mu biaa nyera, na mmom sɛ menyane no da a odi akyi he.
Na m’Agya apɛdeɛ ne sɛ biaa a ohu Ba he na ɔgye no di he benya daa nkwa, na menyane no da a odi akyi he.” Afei Yudafoɔ he firi aseɛ nwiinwii sɛ waka sɛ, “Mene paanoo a osiane firii soro he.” Na bɛkaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ yei ne Yesu, Yosef ba, nea yenim ne papa ne ne maame he?
Ɔyɛɛ dɛ ne afei deɛ ɔdɛ, ‘Mene paanoo a osiane firii soro he’?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Honwiinwii ho mu.
Biaa ntumi mma me nkyɛne gye sɛ Agya a ɔsomaa me he twe no ba; na menyane no nna odi akyire he.
Bɛatwerɛ ya adiyifoɔ he mu sɛ, ‘Nyankopɔn bɛkyerɛkyerɛ bɛ nyinaa.’ Biaa a wate bibi afiri Agya he nkyɛne na wasua he ne ba me nkyɛne.
Biaa nhuu Agya he, gye sɛ nea ofiri Nyankopɔn hɔ he; ɔno ne wahu Agya he.
Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem sɛ, biaa a ɔgye di he benya daa nkwa.
Mene nkwa paanoo he.
Ho nananom dii mana serɛ he so, na bewuwuiɛ.
Yei ne paanoo a osiane firi soro he, sɛ biaa nni na wanwu.
Mene paanoo a nkwa yam a mesiane firi soro baeɛ he, sɛ bi di paanoo yi bi a, ɔbɛtena ase daa.
Na paanoo a mede bɛma wiase nkwa he ne me honam.” Na afei Yudafoɔ he firi aseɛ kasakasaa bɛ mu sɛ, “Ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na saa beema yi de ne honam ama yɛ adi?” Nti Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem sɛ, sɛ hoanni Nipa Ba he honam na hoannom ne mogyaa a, honnya nkwa ya ho mu.
Bɛ a bedi me honam na bɛnom me mogyaa he wɔ daa nkwa, na menyane bɛ nna odi akyire he, efiri sɛ me honam yɛ aduane ampa na me mogyaa yɛ anonneɛ ampa.
Bɛ a bedi me honam na bɛnom me mogyaa tena me mu, na me nso metena bɛ mu.
Sɛnea Agya a ɔte ase he somaa me he, na Agya he nti mete ase he, saa ara nso ne nea odi me honam he, me nti ɔbɛtena ase.
Yei ne paanoo a osiane firii soro baeɛ a ɔnte sɛ nea ho nananom diiɛ na bewuiɛ he; nea odi paanoo yi bɛtena ase daa.” Ɔkaa saa nsɛm yi berɛ a na ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ Kapernaum hyiadane mu.
Daa Nkwa Nsɛm Nti berɛ a n’asuafoɔ he mu bebree tee yei he, bɛkaa sɛ, “Asɛm yi ano ɔdene, hwane ne betumi agye?” Nso esiane sɛ na Yesu nim sɛ n’asuafoɔ he nwiinwii yei ho nti, obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Yei to ho sintidua anaa?
Na afei, sɛ hohu Nipa Ba he sɛ ɔɔkɔ soro, baabi a na ɔya kane he nso ɛ?
Honhom ne ma nkwa; honam deɛ nka hwee koraa.
Nsɛm a maka akyerɛ ho yi yɛ honhom ne nkwa.
Nso ho mu binom nnye nni.” Na ofiri mfitiaseɛ he na Yesu nnim bɛ a bɛnnye nni ne nea obeyi no ama he.
Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Yei nti ne meka kyerɛ ho sɛ biaa ntumi mma me nkyɛne gye sɛ Agya he ama no kwane.” Yei nti n’asuafoɔ he bebree sane kɔɔ bɛ akyi, na bɛne no annante bio.
Nti Yesu bisaa dummienu he sɛ, “Ho nso hopɛ sɛ ho kɔ anaa?” Simon Petro buaa sɛ, “Awurade, hwane nkyɛne ne yɛbɛkɔ?
Wo nkoaa ne wowɔ daa nkwa nsɛm.
Na yɛagye adi, na yɛahu sɛ wone Kronkronni a wofiri Nyankopɔn hɔ he.” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Nyɛ mene maayi ho nnipa dummienu yi?
Nso ho mu baako yɛ bronsam.” Na ɔɔka Yuda Iskariot, Simon ba he ho asɛm.
Ewom sɛ na ɔyɛ dummienu he mu baako deɛ, nso na oobeyi Yesu ama.
Yesu nuanom annyeannie Yei akyi he, Yesu kɔɔ Galilea.
Na ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔbɛkɔ Yudea efiri sɛ na Yudafoɔ he ɔɔhwehwɛ kwane bi afa so aku no.
Afei na Yudafoɔ Apata Afahyɛ he abɛne.
Nti ne nuanom ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Firi ha kɔ Yudea sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na w’asuafoɔ he nso behu nnwuma a wooyɔ, efiri sɛ biaa a ɔpɛ sɛ nnipa bebree behu no he nni dwuma kokoam.
Sɛ hoyɔ saa nnoɔma yi a, homfa ho ho nkyerɛ wiase.” (Na ne nua mmeemanom mpo nnye no nni.)
Nti Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Me berɛ nnuruiɛ, na ho deɛ, berɛ biaa yɛ ma ho.
Wiase nni nnyinasoɔ biaa de tane ho, na me deɛ ɔtane me, efiri sɛ medi ne ho adanseɛ sɛ ne nnwuma yɛ bɔne.
Honkɔ afahyɛ he ase, me deɛ mennya nkɔɔ afahyɛ yi ase, efiri sɛ berɛ he nnuruiɛ.” Na ɔkaa yeinom wieeɛ he, ɔtenaa Galilea.
Yesu kɔɔ afahyɛ he ase Na ne nuammeemanom kɔɔ afahyɛ he ase he, ɔno nso kɔeɛ a wannyi ne ho adi na mmom ɔde ne ho sieeɛ.
Na Yudafoɔ ɔɔhwehwɛ no afahyɛ he ase; na bebisaa sɛ, “Ɔya he?” Na bɛyɛɛ ne ho huhuhuhu pii nnipadɔm he mu.
Binom kaa sɛ.
“Ɔyɛ nipa pa.” Binom nso kaa sɛ, “Daabi, ɔɔdaadaa nkurofoɔ he.” Nso, Yudafoɔ he ho hu nti, biaa anyi n’anim anka ne ho asɛm.
Afei berɛ a afahyɛ he duruu mfimfini he, Yesu kɔɔ asɔredane he mu, na ofirii aseɛ kyerɛkyerɛeɛ.
Na yei yɛɛ Yudafoɔ he nwanwa ma bɛkaa sɛ, “Ɔyɛɛ dɛ ne nipa a onsuaa nwoma biaa yi nim nwoma saa?” Na Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Nea me kyerɛkyerɛ he nyɛ me dea, na mmom ɔyɛ nea ɔsomaa me he dea.” Sɛ bi pɛ sɛ ɔyɛ n’apɛdeɛ a, obehu sɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ he firi Nyankopɔn hɔ anaa m’ankasa ne mebɔ me tim kasa.
Bɛ a bɛbɔ betim kasa he hwehwɛ bɛ ankasa bɛ animuonyam; na nea ɔhwehwɛ nea ɔsomaa no he animuonyam he yɛ nɔkwafoɔ a nea ɔntene biaa nni ne mu.
“Ɔnyɛ Mose ne maa ho mmara he?
Nso ho mu baako mpo nni mmara he so.
Ɛɛne nti ne hoopɛ kwane afa so aku me?” Nnipa he buaa sɛ, “Wowɔ honhommɔne; hwane ne ɔɔhwehwɛ wo aku wo?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Maayɔ adwuma baako, na yei yɛ ho nyinaa nwanwa.
Mose maa ho twetiatwa (ɔnyɛ sɛ ofiri Mose hɔ, na mmom ofiri agyanom hɔ), na ho twa nipa twetia homeda.
Sɛ hotumi twa nipa twetia homeda sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a ɔnto Mose mmara he a, ɛɛne nti ne ho bo afu me sɛ mama bi ho ayɛ ne dene homeda?
Hommfa nea hohu mmmu atɛne, na hommu atɛntenenee.” Kristo he di?
Afei Yerusalemfoɔ he binom kaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ beema yi ne bɛɛpɛ no aku no yi?
Nso, hwɛ ɔɔkasa peteem, nso bɛnka hwee nkyerɛ no.
Nti mpanyimfoɔ he ahu sɛ ɔno ne Kristo he anaa?
Yei deɛ yenim nea ofiri, nso Kristo he deɛ sɛ ɔba a, biaa onhu baabi a ofiri.” Nti berɛ a Yesu ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ asɔredane mu hɔ he, ɔteaam sɛ, “Honim me, na honim baabi a mefiri nso.
Na ɔnyɛ m’ankasa mepɛ so na me baeɛ, na nea ɔsomaa me he yɛ nɔkwafoɔ a honnim no.
Menim no efiri sɛ, mefiri ne nkyɛne ne baeɛ, na ɔno ne somaa me.” Nti bɛhwehwɛɛ kwane a bɛbɛfa so akye no nso biaa amfa ne nsa anka no, efiri sɛ na berɛ he nnuruiɛ.
Na nnipakuo he mu pii gyee no diiɛ, na bebisaa sɛ, “Sɛ Kristo he ba a, ɔbɛyɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne asene nea nipa yi ayɔ yi anaa?” Bɛsomaa Mpanyimfoɔ sɛ bɛnkɔ kye Yesu Farisifoɔ he tee sɛ nnipakuo he oonwinwii keka yeinom fa ne ho, na Farisifoɔ ne asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he somaa asɔrefie awɛmfoɔ sɛ bɛnkɔ kye no.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Meya ho nkyɛne berɛ tiaa bi, na meebɛkɔ nea ɔsomaa me he nkyɛne.
Hobɛhwehwɛ me, na honhu me, na nea meya he, hontumi mma hɔ.” Yudafoɔ he bisaa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Hefa ne nipa yi pɛ sɛ ɔkɔ a nti yenhu no?
Ɔpɛ sɛ ɔkɔ Yudafoɔ a bɛahwete Helafoɔ mu he nkyɛne na ɔkɔkyerɛkyerɛ Helafoɔ he anaa?
Abɛ asɛm ne ɔɔka yi sɛ, ‘Hobɛhwehwɛ me, na honhu me, na nea meya he, hontumi mma hɔ’?” Nkwa Nsuo Da a otwa toɔ afahyɛ he mu he, Yesu gyinaa hɔ teaam sɛ, “Nea sukɔm de no he mmra me nkyɛne mɛnom nsuo.
Sɛnea twerɛsɛm he aka he, ‘Nea ɔgye me di he, nkwa asubɔntene bɛtene afiri n’akomam.’ ” Nso ɔkaa yei faa Honhom a na bɛ a bɛbɛgye no adi he benya he ho, saa berɛ he na Honhom he nnya mmaeɛ, efiri sɛ na bennya nhyɛɛ Yesu animuonyam.
Nnipa he mu ntete mu Na bɛtee saa nsɛm yi he, nnipa bi firi nnipakuo he mu kaa sɛ, “Diyifoɔ he di ampa.” Na binom nso kaa sɛ, “Kristo he di.” Na binom nso bisaa sɛ, “Kristo he befiri Galilea anaa?” Twerɛsɛm he nkaa sɛ Kristo he befiri Dawid ase ne Betlehem, akuraa a na Dawid te mu he ne bɛba?” Afei Yesu nti nnipakuo he mu kyekyɛeɛ.
Na bemu binom pɛɛ sɛ bɛkye no, nso biaa amfa ne nsa anka no.
Mpanyimfoɔ he Annyeanie Nti awɛmfoɔ he sane kɔɔ asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he hɔ, na bebisaa awɛmfoɔ he sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne hoankye no?” Awɛmfoɔ he buaa sɛ, “Nipa biaa nkasaa sɛ beema yi da!” Afei Farisifoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Wadaadaa ho nso anaa?
Mpanyimfoɔ he bi anaa Farisifoɔ he bi agye no atom anaa?
Na nnipakuo yi a bennim mmara he—bɛadome bɛ!” Nikodemo a ɔbaa Yesu nkyɛne dabi he a na ɔyɛ bemu baako bisaa sɛ, “Sɛ wonnii kane ntiee bi anum asɛm nhuu nea ɔɔyɔ a, nti yɛ mmara he tumi bu no atɛne?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Womfiri Galilea, anaa wofiri hɔ?
Hwehwɛ mu hwɛ na wobehu sɛ diyifoɔ biaa nni hɔ a obefiri Galilea asɔre.” Baa he a bɛkyee no adwammammɔ mu he [Nti biaa kɔɔ fie.
Na Yesu kɔɔ Ngo Bepɔ he so.
Na anɔpa tutuutu he ɔsane baa asɔredane he mu.
Na mane mũ he nyinaa baa ne nkyɛne na ɔtenaa ase kyerɛkyerɛ bɛ.
Afei atwerɛfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ de baa bi a bɛakye no adwamammɔ mu baeɛ, na bɛde no begyinaa mfimfini.
Na bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, bɛakye baa yi adwamammɔ so pɛɛ.
Mose hyɛɛ yɛ mmara he mu sɛ, yensi mmaa a bɛ te saa he aboɔ.
Na wo nso ɛɛne ne wooka?” Bɛkaa yei de sɔɔ no hwɛeɛ, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na bebenya soboɔ bi abɔ no.
Na Yesu bɔɔ ne mu ase de ne nsateaa twerɛtwerɛɛ fam.
Na bɛkɔɔ soaa bisaa no he, ɔmaa ne mu so ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho mu nea ɔnyɔɔ bɔne da he nni kane nto boɔ mmɔ no.” Na ɔsane bɔɔ ne mu ase bio de ne nsateaa twerɛtwerɛɛ fam.
Na bɛtee yei he, (bɛ tiboa buu bɛ fɔ), nti befirii adi mmaako mmaako firi mpanyimfoɔ so.
Na ɔkaa Yesu ne baa he nkoaa a ogyina mfinfini hɔ.
Yesu maa ne mu so bisaa baa he sɛ, “Baa, bɛya he?
Biaa ammu wo fɔ?” Na baa he kaa sɛ, “Me wura, daabi.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Me nso memmu wo fɔ, kɔ na nkɔyɔ bɔne bio.”] Yesu ne wiase hann Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ bio sɛ, “Mene wiase hann.
Nea odi m’akyi he nnante sum mu da, na obenya nkwa hann he.” Afei Farisifoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wo deɛ wodi w’ankasa wo ho adanseɛ; w’adanseɛ he nyɛ nɔkorɛ.” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Mpo sɛ medi meaa me ho adanseɛ a, m’adanseɛ he yɛ nɔkorɛ, efiri sɛ, menim baabi a mefiri baeɛ ne baabi a meekɔ.
Na ho deɛ honnim baabi a mefiri ne baabi a meekɔ.
Ho deɛ hobu atɛne honam mu, na me deɛ memmu biaa atɛne.
Na sɛ mebu atɛne mpo a, m’atemmuo he yɛ nɔkorɛ efiri sɛ nyɛ me nkoaa ne mebu atɛne, na mmom me ne Agya a ɔsomaa me he ne bu atɛne.
Bɛatwerɛ no ho mmara he mu sɛ, “Nnipa mmienu adanseɛ yɛ nɔkorɛ.” Mene medi me ho adanseɛ, na Agya a ɔsomaa me he nso di me ho adanseɛ.” Na bebisaa no sɛ, “W’Agya ya he?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Honnim me, na honnim m’Agya nso; sɛ honim me a, nka honim m’Agya nso.” Ɔkaa nsɛm yi berɛ a na ɔɔma nkyerɛkyerɛ ya asɔrefie sikakorabea hɔ; na biaa ankye no, efiri sɛ na ne mmerɛ nya nnuruiɛ.
Yesu hyɛɛ ne Wuo ho Nkɔm Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ bio sɛ, “Me deɛ, meekɔ, na hobɛhwehwɛ me, na hobewu ho bɔne mu; na baabi a meekɔ he, ho deɛ, hontumi mma hɔ.” Nti Yudafoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Oobeku ne ho anaa?
Nti na ɔdɛ, ‘Baabi a meekɔ he, honntumi mma hɔ yi’?” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho deɛ hofiri fam, na me deɛ, mefiri soro.
Hofiri wiase; na me deɛ, memmfiri wiase yi mu.
Meka kyerɛɛ ho sɛ hobewu ho bɔne mu, na sɛ hoannye anni sɛ mene no a, hobewu ho bɔne mu.” Bebisaa no sɛ, “Hwane ne wo”?
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mene nipa korɔ a maka sɛ meyɛ ofiri me dwumadie ahyɛaseɛ he.
Mewɔ ho ho nsɛm pii a mɛka, na mabu atɛne, na nea ɔsomaa me he yɛ nɔkwafoɔ.
Na nea mate afiri ne hɔ ne meka kyerɛ wiase.” Bɛante aseɛ sɛ Agya he ho asɛm ne ɔɔka kyerɛ bɛ.
Nti Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ honya ma nipa ba he so a, saa berɛ he ne hobehu sɛ mene no, na memmɔ m’ankasa me tim nyɔ bibiaa, na nea Agya he kyerɛkyerɛ me he, ɔno ne meka.
Na nea ɔsomaa me he ka me ho, na onnyae me nko, efiri sɛ meyɔ nea ɔsɔ n’ani daa.” Na ɔɔka saa nsɛm yi he, nnipa bebree gyee no diiɛ.
Asuafoɔ kann Na afei Yesu ka kyerɛɛ Yudafoɔ a bɛagye adi he sɛ, “Sɛ hotena m’asɛm mu a, hoyɛ m’asuafoɔ ampa; na hobehu nɔkorɛ he, na nɔkorɛ he ama ho ayɛ adehyeɛ.” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Yɛ yɛ Abraham asefoɔ, na yɛ nyɛɛ bi nkoa da.
Ɛɛne nti ne wooka sɛ, ‘Hobenya adehyeɛ’?” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem sɛ, biaa a ɔyɔ bɔne he yɛ bɔne akoa.
Afei nso akoa ntena fie daa, na ba deɛ ɔtena fie hɔ daa.
Nti sɛ Ba he ma ho fahodie a hobɛyɛ adehyeɛ ampa.
Menim sɛ hoyɛ Abraham asefoɔ, nso hopɛ sɛ hoku me, efiri sɛ m’asɛm nsene ho mu.
Nea mahu no Agya he nkyɛne ne meka, na ho deɛ honyɔ nea hoate firi Agya he nkyɛne.” Yesu ne Abraham Bebuaa no sɛ, “Yɛ Agya ne Abraham.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ ho Agya ne Abraham a, nka hobɛyɔ nea Abraham yɔeɛ, nso seesei hopɛ sɛ hoku me, nipa a maaka nɔkorɛ a mete firi Agya he nkyɛne akyerɛ ho he.
Nso Abraham deɛ wanyɔ saa adeɛ yi.
Hoyɔ nea ho agya yɔ ampa.” Na bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Bɛanwo yɛ adwamammɔ mu, yɛwɔ Agya baako, ɔno ne Nyankopɔn.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ Nyankopɔn yɛ ho Agya a nka hobɛdɔ me, efiri sɛ mefiri Nyankopɔn hɔ ne baeɛ.
Ɔnyɛ mene mede mepɛ baeɛ na mmom ɔno ne somaa me.
Mmɛ nti ne ho nte nea meka he ase yi?
Efiri sɛ hontumi ntie m’asɛm.
Hofiri ho agya bronsam hɔ, na hopɛ sɛ hoyɔ ho Agya he apɛdeɛ.
Ɔyɛ wudini firi mfitiaseɛ, na wannyina nɔkorɛ he mu efiri sɛ nɔkorɛ nni ne mu.
Sɛ odi torɔ a, ofiri ɔno ankasa ne mu ne ba, efiri sɛ ɔyɛ torɔfoɔ ne atorɔ agya.
Na esiane sɛ mekaa nɔkorɛ kyerɛ ho nti, honnye me nni.
Ho mu hwane ne bu me bɔne bi ho atɛne?
Sɛ meka nɔkorɛ a, mmɛ nti ne honnye me nni?
Nea ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn deɛ biaa tie Nyankopɔn asɛm.
Nea nti a hontie ne sɛ, ho nyɛ Nyankopɔn deɛ.” Yudafoɔ he buaa no sɛ, “Sɛ yɛka sɛ woyɛ Samariani na wowɔ honhommɔne a, ɔnyɛ nɔkorɛ?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Menni honhommɔne, na mmom medi m’Agya ni, na ho deɛ honni me ni.
Nso menhwehwɛ animuonyam mma me ho, bi ya hɔ a ɔhwehwɛ na obu atɛne.
Meeka nɔkwasɛm paa akyerɛ ho sɛ, biaa a obedi me nsɛm so he, onwu da.” Yudafoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Afei deɛ yɛahu sɛ wowɔ honhommɔne.
Abraham wuiɛ, na adiyifoɔ he nso wuiɛ.
Nso wo dɛ, ‘Biaa a obedi me nsɛm so he, onwu da.’ Wo so kyɛne yɛ agya Abraham a owuiɛ he anaa?
Adiyifoɔ he nso wuiɛ.
Afei wo dɛ wo ne hwane?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Sɛ m’ankasa mehyɛ me ho animuonyam a, m’animuonyam he nyɛ hwee.
M’Agya a hoka sɛ ɔyɛ ho Nyankopɔn he ne hyɛ me animuonyam nso honnim no.
Na me deɛ menim no.
Na sɛ meka sɛ mennim no a, na meyɛ torɔfoɔ te sɛ ho.
Menim no na medi n’asɛm so.
Ho agya Abraham dii ahurusie ɔnam anidasoɔ a onyaa sɛ obehu me nti, na ɔte sɛ deɛ ohuu me, nti n’ani gyeeɛ.” Na afei Yudafoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wonnii mfie aduonum mpo na woahu Abraham yi?” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem paa sɛ, Abraham nnya mmaeɛ he, ne meya hɔ.” Yei nti bɛsesaa aboɔ sɛ bɛɛbɛtoto abɔ no, nso Yesu de ne ho sieeɛ, na ofirii asɔrefie hɔ kɔeɛ.
Beema bi a bɛwoo no anifira mu nyaa n’ayaresa Na afei Yesu ootwam baabi he, ohuu beema bi a bɛwoo no he na n’ani afira.
N’asuafoɔ he bisaa no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, hwane ne yɔɔ bɔne, beema yi anaa n’awofoɔ, sɛ bɛwoo no a na n’ani afira yi?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ beema yi anaa n’awofoɔ ne yɔɔ bɔne, na mmom bɛwoo no anifra mu senea ɔbɛyɛ a Nyankopɔn nnwuma bɛda adi ne mu.
Adekyeɛ ya hɔ yi ɔsɛ sɛ yɛyɔ nea ɔsomaa yɛ he nnwuma; anadwo ɔɔba a biaa ntumi nnyɔ adwuma.
Berɛ a meya wiase yi, mene wiase hann.” Ɔkaa saa he, ɔtoo ntasuo too fam, na ɔde ntasuo he fraa nnɛteɛ, na ɔde nnɛteɛ he faa nifirani he ani so.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kɔhohoro so ya tadeɛ Siloa (asekyerɛ ne nea bɛasoma no) mu.” Na ɔkɔhohoroo so, na ɔbaeɛ he na ohu adeɛ.
Ne mpɔtamufoɔ ne bɛ a na benim no sɛ na ɔyɛ srɛsrɛfoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ beema a na ɔte hɔ srɛsrɛ adeɛ he di?” Afei binom kaa sɛ, “Ɔyɛ ɔno a.” Na binom nso kaa sɛ, “Ɔsɛ no.” Na ɔnoaa deɛ, ɔkaa sɛ, “Ɔyɛ me a.” Na bebisaa no sɛ: Ɔyɛɛ dɛ ne w’ani abie yi?
Obuaa sɛ, “Nipa bi a bɛfrɛ no Yesu ne potɔɔ nnɛteɛ de sraa m’ani so, na ɔka kyerɛ me sɛ, ‘Kɔ tadeɛ Siloa mu kɔ hohoro so.’ Na mekɔ hohoroo so he, mehuu adeɛ.” Na bebisaa no sɛ, “Ɔya he?” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Mennim.” Farisifoɔ he hwehwɛɛ Ayaresa he mu Bɛde nea nka ɔyɛ nifirani he kɔɔ Farisifoɔ nkyɛne.
Na nea na ɔteɛ ne sɛ, na saa da a Yesu potɔɔ nnɛteɛ de biee n’ani he yɛ homeda.
Na Farisifoɔ he nso bisaa no bio sɛnea ɔyɔeɛ a ohuu adeɛ.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Nnɛteɛ ne ɔde sraa m’ani so a, mekɔ hohoroo so a, mehuu adeɛ yi.” Na Farisifoɔ he mu bi kaa sɛ, “Nipa yi mfiri Nyankopɔn nkyɛne, efiri sɛ onni homeda.” Nso binom bisaa sɛ, “Ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na nipa debɔneyɛni atumi ayɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne a ɔte sɛ yi?” Afei mpaepaemu baa bɛ mu.
Nti bɛsane bisaa nea na ɔyɛ nifirani he sɛ, “Wone wabie w’ani, na wo nso mmɛ ne wowɔ ka fa ne ho?” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Ɔyɛ diyifoɔ.” Nso na Yudafoɔ he nnye ne ho nsɛm he nni, sɛ na nka ɔyɛ nifirani na seesei ohu adeɛ, kosii sɛ bɛfrɛɛ deɛ ohuu adeɛ he awofoɔ, na bebisaa bɛ sɛ, “Ho ba a hoka sɛ howoo no nifirani he di?
Afei ɔyɛɛ dɛ ne ohuu adeɛ yi?” N’awofoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Yenim sɛ yɛba di, na yɛwoo no nifirani; na sɛnea ɔyɔeɛ a ohuu adeɛ yi deɛ yennim.
Afei nso nipa korɔ a obiee n’ani he, yɛdeɛ, yennim no; waanyini, hommisa no, na ɔno ankasa betumi ayi ano.” Deɛ nti a n’awofoɔ kaa saa ne sɛ, na besuro Yudafoɔ he; efiri sɛ, na Yudafoɔ he apam dada sɛ, sɛ bi paem ka sɛ Yesu ne Kristo he a, bebetu no afiri hyiadane he mu.
Yei ne maa n’awofoɔ kaa sɛ, “Wɔanyini hommisa no.” Na bɛfrɛɛ nipa a na nka ɔyɛ nifirani he ne mprenu so ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Fa animuonyam ma Nyankopɔn!
Yɛ deɛ, yenim sɛ nipa yi yɛ debɔnyɛni.” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Sɛ ɔyɛ debɔnyɛni a, mennim; adeɛ baako pɛ ne menim, na nka meyɛ nifirani, na afei deɛ maahu adeɛ.” Na bebisaa no sɛ: Mmɛ ne ɔyɔ maa wo?
Obiee w’ani he sɛ?
Ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Maaka akyerɛ ho dada, na hoantie?
Ɛɛne ne hopɛ sɛ hote bio?
Ho nso hopɛ sɛ hoyɛ n’asuafoɔ anaa?” Bɛyeyaa no, na bɛkaa sɛ, “Wone woyɛ ne suani; na yɛ deɛ, yɛyɛ Mose asuafoɔ.” Yenim sɛ Nyankopɔn kasa kyerɛɛ Mose; na yei deɛ, yennim baabi a ofiri.
Beema he buaa sɛ, “Yei ne ɔnwanwa he, sɛ honnim faako a ofiri, nso wabie m’ani.
Yenim sɛ Nyankopɔn ntie abɔnefoɔ, na otie bɛ a bɛsom no ne bedi n’apɛdeɛ so.
Ofiri tete de besi nnɛ yɛntee sɛ bi abie bi a bɛwoo no nifirani ani da.
Sɛ beema yi mfiri Nyankopɔn hɔ a, nka ontumi nyɔ hwee.” Bebuaa no sɛ, “Wo a bɔne mu ne bɛwoo wo yi ne wookyerɛkyerɛ yɛ yi?” Na bɛpamoo no firi hɔ.
Honhom mu Anifira Yesu tee sɛ bɛapam no, na ohuu no he, obisaa no sɛ, “Wogye Nipa Ba he di?” Obuaa sɛ, “Owura, ɔno ne hwane?
Ka kyerɛ me na mennye no nni.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Woahu no, na ɔnoaa ne ɔne wo ɔɔkasa yi.” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Awurade, megye no di.” Na ɔsɔree no.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Atemmuo nti ne mebaa wiase, na bɛ a benhu adeɛ he ahu adeɛ, na bɛ a behu adeɛ he bɛadane anifirafoɔ.” Na Farisifoɔ he mu bi a na bɛ ne no ya hɔ tee asɛm yi, na bebisaa no sɛ, “Yɛ nso yɛyɛ anifirafoɔ anaa?” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ honyɛ anifirafoɔ a nka bɔne nni ho ho.
Na afei ho dɛ, ‘Yehu adeɛ.’ Ho bɔne he aka hɔ.”
Yesu ne dwanhwɛfoɔ pa he “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem paa sɛ, biaa a ɔmfa pono ano nkɔ nnwammuom na mmom ɔforo fa baabi foforɔ he, yɛ korɔmfoɔ ne dwotwafoɔ.
Nea ɔfa pono he ano ba mu he ne nwane he hwɛfoɔ.
Pono ano nwɛmfoɔ he bie no, na nnwane he tie ne nne.
Na ɔbɔ ne nnwane he dini frɛ bɛ, na ɔde bɛ firi adi.
Sɛ ɔde ne deɛ nyinaa firi adi a, odi bɛ anim ma bedi n’akyi efiri sɛ benim ne nne.
Benni hɔhoɔ biaa akyi, na mmom bebedwane afiri ne nkyɛne efiri sɛ bennim ahɔhoɔ he nne.” Yesu kaa saa kasakoa yi kyerɛɛ bɛ, nso bɛante nea na ɔɔka kyerɛ bɛ he ase.
Nti Yesu kaa bio sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem paa sɛ, mene nnwammuo he ano pono ma nnwane he.
Bɛ a bɛde me dini aba nyinaa yɛ akorɔmfoɔ ne dwotwafoɔ; nso nnwane he antie bɛ.
Mene pono he, biaa a ɔfa me so kɔ mu he, bɛbɛgye no nkwa, na ɔbɛba mu, na wafiri adi, na wanya adidibea.
Korɔmfoɔ mma, gye sɛ oobewia, adi awu, na waseɛ adeɛ.
Na me deɛ, mebaa sɛ hobenya nkwa na hoanya no mmorosoɔ.
“Mene dwanhwɛfoɔ pa he.
Dwanhwɛfoɔ pa he de ne nkwa to hɔ ma nnwane he.
Na nipa a bɛabɔ no paa sɛ ɔnhwɛ nnwane he, na nnwane he nyɛ ɔno ankasa ne deɛ he hu pataku sɛ ɔɔba a, ogya nnwane he hɔ dwane ma pataku he bɛkye bɛ, na wabɔ bɛ ahwete.
Paani he dwane efiri sɛ ɔyɛ paani, na ɔnnwene nnwane he ho.
Mene dwanhwɛfoɔ pa he, menim me deɛ, na me deɛ nso nim me, sɛnea Agya he nim me na me nso menim Agya he.
Na mede me nkwa to hɔ ma nnwane he.
Mewɔ nnwane foforɔ a bemfiri bane yi mu.
Ɔsɛ sɛ mede bɛ nso ba na bebetie me nne, na ayɛ kuo baako a ɔwɔ hwɛfoɔ baako.
Yei nti ne Agya he dɔ me, efiri sɛ mede me nkwa to hɔ na mefa bio.
Biaa nnye mfiri me nsam, na m’ankasa ne mefiri mepɛ mu de to hɔ.
Mewɔ tumi sɛ mede to hɔ, na mewɔ tumi sɛ mesane fa bio.
Menyaa yei ho ahyɛdeɛ firii m’Agya nkyɛne.” Na nsɛm yi nti mpapaemu baa Yudafoɔ he mu bio.
Na bɛ mu pii kaa sɛ, “Ɔwɔ honhommɔne na waabɔ dam.
Mmɛ nti ne hotie no?” Na binom nso kaa sɛ, “Nsɛm yi nyɛ nea ɔwɔ honhommɔne nsɛm.
Honhommɔne betumi abie nifirani ani anaa?” Yudafoɔ he poo Yesu Saa berɛ he na ahodwira afahyɛ aduru so ya Yerusalem.
Na ɔyɛ awɔ berɛ.
Na Yesu nenam asɔrefie hɔ, Salomo abranaa he so.
Nti Yudafoɔ he twa hyiaa ne ho bisaa no sɛ, “Wobɛma yɛatwɛne akosi da bɛ?
Sɛ wone Kristo he a, pae mu ka kyerɛɛ yɛ pefee.” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Maka akyerɛ ho, na honnye nni.
Nnwuma a meyɔ no m’Agya dini mu heaa di me ho adanseɛ; nso honnye nni, efiri sɛ honka me nnwane he ho.
Me nnwane te me nne.
Menim bɛ, na bedi m’akyi.
Mema bɛ daa nkwa, na bɛnyera da.
Na biaa ntumi nhwim bɛ mfiri me nsam.
Nea m’Agya de ama me he so kyɛne bibiaa, na biaa ntumi nhwim mfiri Agya he nsam.
Mene Agya he yɛ baako.” Na Yudafoɔ he sesaa aboɔ bio sɛ bɛɛbɛtoto abɔ no.
Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Maada nnwumapa pii adi akyerɛ ho a efiri Agya he nkyɛne.
Nnwuma yi mu nea ɔya he nti ne hoobesi me aboɔ yi?” Yudafoɔ he buaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ nnwumapa bi nti ne yeebesi wo aboɔ, na mmom abususɛm ntia, efiri sɛ wo a woyɛ nipa he woyɛ wo ho sɛ Nyankopɔn.” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Bɛntwerɛɛ wɔ ho mmara mu sɛ, ‘Mekaa sɛ, hoyɛ anyame’?
Sɛ bɛfrɛ bɛ a Nyankopɔn asɛm baa bɛ nkyɛne he anyame na bentumi nsɛe twerɛ he a, hoka kyerɛ me a Agya he ate me ho asoma me aba wiase he sɛ, ‘Woaka abususɛm’ esiane sɛ mekaa sɛ ‘Meyɛ Nyankopɔn Ba nti’?
Sɛ ɔnyɛ m’Agya adwuma ne meeyɔ a, hedeɛ honnye me nni.
Na sɛ m’Agya adwuma ne meeyɔ deɛ a, hedeɛ sɛ mene honnye me nni a, honye nnwuma he nni na hoahu na ho ate aseɛ sɛ Agya he ya me mu na me nso meya ne mu.” Na bɛbɔɔ mmɔdene sɛ bɛbɛkye no, nso ofiri bɛ nsa kɔeɛ.
Nti osiim bio kotwaa Yordan kɔɔ baabi a na kane he Yohane bɔ asu he, na ɔtenaa hɔ.
Na nnipa bebree baa ne nkyɛne, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Yohane anyɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne baako pɛ mpo, nso nea Yohane ka faa saa nipa yi ho he nyinaa yɛ nɔkorɛ.” Na pii gyee no dii hɔ.
Lasaro wuo Afei na beema bi ya hɔ a ɔyare a bɛfrɛ no Lasaro a ofiri Betania, akura a na Maria ne ne nua baa Marta firi he.
Lasaro a na ɔyare he yɛ Maria a ɔde ngo hwamhwam guu Awurade nane ase na ɔde ne tinwii popaeɛ he nua beema.
Nti ne nuamaanom too Yesu nkra sɛ, “Awurade, nea wodɔ no he yare.” Na Yesu teeɛ he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Saa yadeɛ yi nyɛ wuyareɛ; na mmom Nyankopɔn animuonyam ntia, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na bɛnam so bɛhyɛ Nyankopɔn Ba he animuonyam.” Ewom sɛ na Yesu dɔ Marta, ne ne nuabaa ne Lasaro deɛ, nso ɔtee sɛ ɔyare he ɔtenaa baabi a na ɔya heaa nnaanu.
Na ɔno akyi he ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Homma yɛnkɔ Yudea bio.” Asuafoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, ɔnyɛ nnaano yiaa ne Yudafoɔ yi pɛɛ sɛ besi wo aboɔ, ne woobɛkɔ hɔ bio yi?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ nnɔnhwere dummienu ne ya adekyeɛ mu?
Bɛ a bɛnante awia berɛ he nsonti bibiaa, efiri sɛ behu wiase hann.
Nso bɛ a bɛnante anadwo he sonti, efiri sɛ benni hann mu.” Ɔkaa yei wieeɛ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Yɛ adamfo Lasaro ada, na meekɔ hɔ akonyane no.” Asuafoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade, sɛ waada deɛ a, ɔbɛsɔre.” Yesu deɛ na Lazuro wuo ho asɛm ne ɔɔka, nso asuafoɔ he susuu sɛ ɔyɛ nna ho asɛm ne ɔɔka.
Nti afei deɛ, Yesu kaa no pefee sɛ, “Lasaro awu.
Na ho nti ɔyɛ me anigye sɛ na menni hɔ, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na hobɛgye adi.
Nso ho mma yɛnkɔ ne nkyɛne.” Toma a na bɛfrɛ no Ata he ka kyerɛɛ ne mfɛfoɔ asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Homma yɛ nso yɛnkɔ na yɛ ne no nkowu.” Yesu yɛ Wusɔreɛ ne Nkwa Berɛ a Yesu duruu hɔ he, ohuu sɛ Lasaro adi nnanan adamena mu.
Na Betania bɛne Yerusalem bɛyɛ nkwansini mmienu ne fa, na Yudafoɔ bebree aba Marta ne Maria nkyɛne ɔɔbɛkyekyere bɛ werɛ, bɛ nua he nti.
Afei Marta tee sɛ Yesu ɔɔba he, okohyiaa no; na Maria deɛ ɔtenaa fie.
Marta ka kyerɛɛ Yesu sɛ, “Awurade, sɛ na woya ha a, nka me nua beema yi anwu.
Na seesei mpo menim sɛ adeɛ biaa a wobebisa Nyankopɔn he, ɔbɛyɔ ama wo.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wo nua beema he bɛsɔre bio.” Marta ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Menim sɛ wusɔreɛ a ɔbɛba da a odi akyire he mu he, ɔbɛsɔre.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Me ne wusɔreɛ ne nkwa.
Bɛ a bɛgye me di he, bewu mpo a bebenya nkwa.
Na biaa a ɔte ase na ɔgye me di he onwu da.
Wogye yei di anaa?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ɛɛ, Awurade, megye di sɛ wo ne Kristo, Nyankopɔn Ba a ɔɔba wiase mu he.” Yesu suiɛ Ɔkaa yei wieeɛ he, Marta kɔfrɛɛ ne Maria kokoam ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he aba ha, na ɔɔfrɛ wo.” Na ɔtee yei he, ɔsɔree ntɛm siim kɔɔ ne nkyɛne.
Nso saa berɛ he nyinaa na Yesu nnya nnuruu kuro he mu, na mmom na ɔda so ya baabi a Marta behyiaa no he.
Afei berɛ a Yudafoɔ a na bɛ ne Marta ya fie hɔ ɔɔkyekyere ne were he huu sɛ Maria asɔre ntɛm afiri adi he, bedii n’akyi susuu sɛ ɔɔkɔ nna he so akosu.
Na Maria duruu baabi a na Yesu ya he na n’ani bɔɔ ne so he, obuu nkotodwe ne nane ase, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade, sɛ na woya ha a, nka me nua beema yi anwu.” Yesu huu sɛ oosu he, na Yudafoɔ a bɛ ne no baeɛ nso beesu he, osii apinie ya ne honhom mu na ne ho nso yera no.
Obisaa sɛ, “Hefa ne hode no toeɛ?” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade, bra na bɛhwɛ.” Yesu suiɛ.
Nti Yudafoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Honhwɛ sɛnea na osi dɔ no fa!” Nso binom kaa sɛ, “Yei ne bie nifirani ani he; nka ontumi nsi yei wuo yi ho kwane anaa?” Yesu nyanee Lasaro firii Wuom Afei Yesu a na oosi apinie bio he, baa nna he so.
Na ɔyɛ abodane, na boɔ twere ano.
Yesu kaa sɛ, “Honyi boɔ he.” Marta a na ne nua aka baabi he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sesɛɛ deɛ, ɔbɔno, efiri sɛ waadi nnanan.” Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Menka nkyerɛɛ wo sɛ, sɛ wogye di a, hobehu Nyankopɔn animuonyam?” Nti beyii boɔ he hɔ.
Na Yesu hwɛɛ soro, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Agya, meda wo ase sɛ woatie me.
Menim sɛ wotie me daa, nso nnipakuo a begyina ha he nti ne maka saa na ama bɛagye adi sɛ wone wosomaa me.” Ɔkaa saa he, ɔde nne kɛseɛ teaam sɛ, “Lasaro, firi bra!” Afei beema a na wawu he firi baeɛ a na bɛde ntoma akyekyere ne nane ne ne nsa, na bɛde ntoma nteantea akyekyere n’anim.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honsane no na homma no nkɔ.” Bɛbɔɔ Yesu ho pɔ sɛ bebeku no Nti Yudafoɔ a na bɛaba Maria nkyɛne a behuu deɛ Yesu yɔeɛ he mu bebree gye diiɛ, nso bɛ mu bi kɔɔ Farisifoɔ he hɔ kɔkaa deɛ Yesu yɔeɛ he kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Nti asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he maa bekohyiaa abadwafoɔ he, na bɛkaa sɛ, “Mmɛ ne yɛbɛyɔ efiri sɛ nipa yi ɔɔyɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne pii?
Sɛ yɛma no kɔ so saa a, biaa bɛgye no adi, na Romafoɔ he bɛba abɛsɛe yɛ kronkron bea ne yɛ mane yi.” Na bɛ mu baako, Kaiafa a na ɔyɛ sɔfo panyini saa afe he, ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honnim hwee koraa, na honnwene nso sɛ ɔyɛ ma ho sɛ nipa baako bewu ama manfoɔ na mane mũ he nyinaa ansɛe.” Nso, omfiri n’ankasa ne tim ne ɔkaa yei; na mmom esiane sɛ na ɔyɛ sɔfo panyini saa afe he nti, ɔhyɛɛ nkɔm sɛ otwa sɛ Yesu wu ma mane he, na ɔnyɛ mane he nko, na mmom sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ na Nyankopɔn bɛka ne mma a bɛabɔ bɛ ahwete he abom ayɛ baako.
Nti ofiri saa da he bɛbɔɔ pɔ sɛ bebeku no.
Saa nti afei Yesu annante badwam bio wɔ Yudafoɔ he mu, na ofirii hɔ kɔɔ asaase a ɔbɛne serɛ so, kuro bi a bɛfrɛ no Efraim mu, na ɔne n’asuafoɔ he tenaa hɔ.
Saa berɛ he na Yudafoɔ Twam he abɛne, na nnipa bebree firi nkurase baa Yerusalem ansa na Twam afahyɛ he ooduru so sɛnea bebedwira bɛ ho.
Na bɛɛhwehwɛ Yesu, na berɛ a begyinagyina asɔrefie hɔ he, bɛ bisabisa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Hodwene ho sɛ?
Nti ɔmma afahyɛ he ase koraa anaa?” Na asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he ahyɛ sɛ, sɛ bi nim baabi a ɔya a, ɔmmɛkyerɛ, na bɛnkɔ kye no.
Maria sraa Yesu Ngo Afei aka nnansia na Twam he aduru he, Yesu baa Betania, baabi a na Lasaro a Yesu nyane no firii awufoɔ mu he te he.
Bɛtoo Yesu pono hɔ.
Marta someeɛ, na Lasaro deɛ na ɔka bɛ a na bɛ ne no te adidipono he ho.
Na Maria faa ngo hwamhwam krɔgyee a na ne boɔ bɛyɛ nkariboɔ baako de bɛsraa Yesu nane ase, na ɔde ne tinwii popaeɛ.
Na ne hwam hyɛɛ fie hɔ ma.
Nso, Yuda Iskariot, asuafoɔ he mu baako a na oobeyi no ama he kaa sɛ, “Ɛɛne nti ne bɛantɔno saa ngo hwamhwam yi annye sika a ɔbɛyɛ afe baako akatua amfa amma ahiafoɔ?” (Nso ɔnyɛ sɛ ɔdwene ahiafoɔ ho nti ne ɔkaa saa, na mmom na ɔyɛ korɔmfoɔ, na sika adaka he ya ne nkyɛne, na ɔtaa yi sika a bɛde gu mu he bi.)
Yesu kaa sɛ, “Honyaa no, na ɔde yei asie ama me sie da.
Ahiafoɔ deɛ, bɛya ho nkyɛne daa, na me deɛ honnya me daa.” Bɛbɔɔ Lasaro ho pɔ sɛ bebeku no Na afei Yudafoɔ nnipakuo kɛseɛ bi huu sɛ ɔya hɔ, na bɛbaa hɔ.
Ɔnyɛ Yesu nko nti, na mmom bɛbaa sɛ bɛɛbɛpɛ Lasaro a wanyane afiri wuom he ahwɛ.
Nti asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he bɔɔ pɔ sɛ bebeku Lasaro nso, efiri sɛ ɔno nti ne Yudafoɔ bebree kɔɔ hɔ na bɛgyee Yesu diiɛ.
Yesu wuraa Yerusalem Nkunimdie so Adeɛ kyeɛ he, nnipakuo pii a na bɛaba afahyɛ he asɛ he tee sɛ Yesu ɔɔba Yerusalem he, bɛfaa berɛɛ, na befiri adi sɛ beekohyia no, na bɛteaam sɛ, “Hosiana!
Nhyira ne deɛ ɔɔba Awurade dini mu— Israel hene he!” Na berɛ a Yesu huu afunumu ba bi he, ɔtenaa ne so, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ: “Sion babaa, nsuro.
Hwɛ, wo hene ɔɔba, ɔte afunumu ba so!” Nso n’asuafoɔ he ante yeinom ase saa berɛ he; na Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ Yesu animuonyam akyi he ne bɛkae sɛ bɛatwerɛ yeinom afa ne ho, na bɛayɔ nea bɛatwerɛ he nyinaa ama no.
Na nnipakuo a na bɛya hɔ berɛ a ɔfrɛɛ Lasaro firii adakamena mu na onyane no firi wuom he kɔɔ so dii adanseɛ.
Ɔnam sɛ bɛtee sɛ wayɔ saa nsɛnkyerɛnne yi nti, nnipakuo he kohyiaa no.
Farisifoɔ he keka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, Honhu sɛ hontumi nyɔ no hwee.
Hwɛ!
Wiase atu di n’akyi.
Helafoɔ pɛɛ sɛ bebehu Yesu Na Helafoɔ bi ka bɛ a bɛbaa sɛ bɛɛbɛsom afahyɛ he ase he ho.
Nti yeinom baa Filipo a na ofiri Betsaida a ɔya Galilea he nkyɛne, na befirii aseɛ srɛɛ no sɛ, “Owura, yɛpɛ sɛ yehu Yesu.” Filipo kɔka kyerɛɛ Andreo, na Andreo ne Filipo kɔka kyerɛɛ Yesu.
Yesu buaa sɛ, “Berɛ he aduru sɛ bɛhyɛ Nipa Ba he animuonyam.
Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem paa sɛ, sɛ ayuo ba baako antɔ fam anwu a, ɔdasoaa yɛ ba baako; nso sɛ owu a ɔsõ mma bebree.
Deɛ ɔdɔ ne nkwa he, obefiri ne nsa; na deɛ ɔtane ne nkwa wiase ha yi bɛkora no akɔ daa nkwam.
Sɛ bi yɛ me somfoɔ a ma no nni m’akyi, na baabi a meya he, hɔ ne me somfoɔ bɛba; na sɛ bi som me a, m’Agya bedi no ni.
Yesu kaa ne wuo ho asɛm “Afei me kra ho yera no.
Na mmɛ ne menka?
‘Agya, gye mefiri dɔno yi mu’?
Daabi!
Yei nti ne saa mmerɛ yi ato me.
Agya, hyɛ wo dini animuonyam.” Na afei nne bi firi soro baeɛ sɛ, “Maahyɛ no animuonyam dada, na mɛhyɛ no animuonyam bio.” Na nnipakuo a begyina hɔ na bɛteeɛ he kaa sɛ, “Agradaa abom.” Binom nso kaa sɛ, “Bɔfoɔ akasa akyerɛ no.” Yesu kaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ me nti ne nne yi baeɛ, na mmom ho ntia.
Afei ne beebebu wiase atɛne; afei ne beebetu wiase sodifoɔ afiri hɔ.
Na me deɛ, sɛ bɛma me so firi wiase a, mɛtwe nnipa bebree aba me nkyɛne.” Ɔkaa yei de kyerɛɛ wuo ko a na oobewu.
Nti nnipakuo he buaa no sɛ, “Yɛte firi mmara he mu sɛ, Kristo he ya hɔ daa.
Afei mmɛ nti ne wooka sɛ otwa sɛ bɛma Nipa Ba he so?
Hwane ne Nipa Ba he?” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hann he bɛtena ho nkyɛne kakra.
Howɔ hann he, honante na sum anni ho so.
Na deɛ ɔnante sum mu he nnim baabi a meekɔ.
Howɔ hann he yi, honye hann he nni, na hoayɛ hann he mma.” Nnipa he annyeanie Na Yesu kaa yei wieeɛ he, ofirii hɔ kohintaeɛ.
Ewom sɛ na waayɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne pii bɛ anim deɛ, nso bɛannye no anni.
Yei siiɛ sɛ asɛm a diyifoɔ Yesaia kaeɛ he bɛbam sɛ: “Awurade, hwane ne agye yɛ asɛm adi, na hwane ne bɛayi Awurade abasa akyerɛ no?” Deɛ ntia bɛantumi annye anni ne sɛ Yesaia kaa bio sɛ, “Wafira bɛ ani na waama bɛ akoma ayɛ dene, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ na bɛmmfa bɛ ani nnhu, na bɛ akoma ante aseɛ na bɛansakra na mansa bɛ yadeɛ.” Yesaia kaa yeinom, efiri sɛ ohuu n’animuonyam, na ɔkaa ne ho asɛm.
Yei nyinaa akyi he, mpanyimfoɔ he mu pii nso gyee no diiɛ; nso Farisifoɔ he nti bɛanka sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ na bentu bɛ mfiri hyiadane he mu, efiri sɛ bɛpɛ nnipa animuonyam kyɛne Nyankopɔn animuonyam mpo.
Yesu Nkyerɛkyerɛ Tɔfabɔ Afei Yesu teaam dendene sɛ, “Deɛ ɔgye me di he, ɔnyɛ menko ne ɔgye me di, na mmom nea ɔsomaa me he nso.
Na nea ohu me he hu deɛ ɔsomaa me he nso.
Maaba wiase sɛ hann, na biaa a ɔgye me di he antena sum mu.
Na sɛ bi te m’asɛm na onni so a, me deɛ memmu no atɛne efiri sɛ mamma sɛ meebebu wiase atɛne, na mmom mebaa sɛ meebɛgye wiase nkwa.
Nea ɔpo me na ɔnnye me nsɛm he wɔ temmufoɔ baako.
Nsɛm a maka heaa ne bebu no atɛne da a odi akyire he mu, efiri sɛ me deɛ ɔnyɛ mene mehyɛɛ me ho kasaeɛ, na Agya he a ɔsomaa me he ne hyɛɛ me nea menka ne sɛnea menkasa.
Na menim sɛ n’ahyɛdeɛ yɛ daa nkwa.
Nti deɛ maka he, sɛnea Agya he aka akyerɛ me he, saa ne meka.”
Yesu hohoroo n’asuafoɔ he nane ase Na afei Twam afahyɛ he oobeduru he, na Yesu nim sɛ berɛ he aduru sɛ oobefiri wiase akɔ Agya he nkyɛne.
Na ɔdɔɔ ɔnoaa ne deɛ a na bɛya wiase he, na ɔdɔɔ bɛ de kosii awieeɛ.
Nti berɛ a na beebedi anwummerɛduane he, na bronsam de ahyɛ Simon ba Yuda Iskariot akomam dada sɛ onyi no ma.
Na esiane sɛ na Yesu nim sɛ Agya he de nnoɔma nyinaa ahyɛ ne nsa, na ofiri Nyankopɔn nkyɛne, na ɔɔkɔ Nyankopɔn hɔ nti, ɔsɔre firii aduane he ho yii n’ataadeɛ ngusoɔ guu hɔ.
Afei ɔfaa bɔɔdoa de bɔɔ n’asenem.
Ɔno akyi he ohwiee nsuo guu dwaresɛn mu, na ofiri aseɛ hohoroo asuafoɔ he nane ho.
Na ɔde bɔɔdoa a ɔde bɔɔ n’asenem he popaa ho.
Na oduruu Simon Petro so he, obisaa Yesu sɛ, “Awurade, wo ne woobɛhohoro me nane ase yi?
Na Yesu buaa sɛ, “Nea meeyɔ yi wonte aseɛ seesei na akyire he wobɛte aseɛ.” Petro ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Aa!
Awurade, memma wonhohoro me nane ase.” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Sɛ manhohoro wo nane ase a wonni kyɛfa biaa me mu.” Simon Petro ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ ɔte deɛ a, Awurade, ɔnyɛ me nane ase nkoaa, na me nsa ne meti nso ka ho!” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nea woadware he nhia sɛ ɔbɛhohoro bio, na mmom ohia sɛ ohohoro ne nane ase, efiri sɛ, ne ho nyinaa afiri.
Ho ho afiri nso ɔnyɛ ho nyinaa.” Na onim nipa korɔ a obeyi no ama he, nti ne ɔkaa sɛ “Ɔnyɛ ho nyinaa ne ho ho afiri he.” Afei berɛ a ɔhohoroo bɛ nane ase wieeɛ a ɔhyɛɛ n’ataadeɛ ngusoɔ, na ɔkɔtenaa pono he ho bio he, obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Hoahu nea maayɔ ho yi?
Hofrɛ me Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ ne Awurade, na ɔyɛ ne kwane so sɛ hoka saa, efiri sɛ meyɛ saa.
Na sɛ me a meyɛ Awurade ne Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ ahohoro ho nane ase a, hedeɛ na ɔsɛ sɛ ho nso ho mu biaa hohoro ne yɔnko nane ase.
Na maama ho nhwɛsoɔ sɛnea mayɔ ho he, ho nso honyɔ saa.
Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem paa sɛ, akoa nsene ne wura, na saa ne somafoɔ nso nsene onii a ɔsomaa no he.
Sɛ honim yeinom na hoyɔ a, hoyɛ nhyira.
Ɔnyɛ ho nyinaa ho asɛm ne meeka yi, me deɛ menim bɛ a maayi bɛ.
Na mmom sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a twerɛsɛm he bɛbam sɛ, ‘Nea me ne no bɔ kosua tafere he, ayi me ama ntia.’ Afei meeka akyerɛ ho nnɛ ansa na aba, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ na sɛ onya ba a, hobɛgye adi sɛ mene no.
Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem paa sɛ, nea ɔgye biaa a mesoma no he gye me nso.
Saa nso ne nea ɔgye me nso gye nea ɔsomaa me he nso.” Yesu hyɛɛ ne Wuo ho Nkɔm Na Yesu kaa yei wieeɛ he, ne ho yeraa no ne honhom mu, na ɔpaem kaa sɛ, “Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem paa sɛ, ho mu baako beyi me ama.” Na asuafoɔ he hwehwɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho anim a na benhu onii korɔ a ɔɔka ne ho asɛm he.
Na asuafoɔ he mu baako a Yesu dɔ no he twere Yesu kokom na Simon Petro bɔɔ n’ani kyerɛɛ no sɛ, omisa onii korɔ a ɔɔka ne ho asɛm he.
Nti ɔpa tweree Yesu kokom bisaa no sɛ, “Awurade, ɔyɛ hwane a?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Ɔno ne mede paanoo sini bɛbɔ ayowa mu ama no he.” Nti ɔde paanoo sini bɔɔ ayowa mu de kɔmaa Yuda, Simon Iskariot ba he.
Ɔgyee paanoo sini he wieeɛ he, Satan bɛhyɛɛ ne mu.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nea woobɛyɔ he, yɔ no ntɛntɛm.” Nso na bɛ a bɛte pono he ho he biaa nnim nea nti a ɔkaa saa kyerɛɛ no he.
Esiane sɛ na Yuda ne kura bɛ sika adaka he nti, binom susuu sɛ na Yesu ɔɔka akyerɛ no sɛ, “Kɔtotɔ nnoɔma a yehia ma afahyɛ he” anaa ɔmfa bibi mma ahiafoɔ.
Afei ɔgyee paanoo sini he, ntɛmaa na ofiri adi.
Na ɔyɛ anadwo.
Ahyɛdeɛ foforɔ Nti ofirii adi he, Yesu kaa sɛ, “Afei bɛahyɛ Nipa Ba he animuonyam, na ɔno nti bɛahyɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam.
Na Nyankopɔn ankasa bɛhyɛ no animuonyam, na ɔbɛhyɛ no animuonyam ntɛm.
Mma nkumaa, mene ho ya hɔ mmerɛ tiaa bi.
Hobɛhwehwɛ me, na sɛnea maka akyerɛ Yudafoɔ he sɛ, ‘Baabi a meekɔ hontumi mma hɔ he, saa ne seesei meeka akyerɛ ho nso.’ Ahyɛdeɛ foforɔ ne mede ɔɔma ho sɛ, honnodɔ ho ho sɛnea medɔɔ ho he, saa ne ho nso honnodɔ ho ho ho ho.
Sɛ hododɔ ho ho ho ho a, ɔno ne bɛma nnipa nyinaa ahu sɛ hoyɛ m’asuafoɔ ampa.” Yesu hyɛɛ nkɔm sɛ Petro bɛpa no Simon Petro bisaa no sɛ, “Awurade, hefa ne wookɔ?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Baabi a meekɔ he wontumi nni m’akyi seesei, nso akyire yi wobedi m’akyi aba hɔ.” Petro ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade, mmɛ nti ne mentumi nni w’akyi seesei?
Mede me nkwa bɛto hɔ ama wo.” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Wode wo nkwa bɛto hɔ ama me?
Meeka akyerɛ wo nɔkorem paa sɛ, ansa na akokɔ bɛbɔno he, na woapa me mprɛnsa.
Yesu ne kwane a ɔkɔ Agya he nkyɛne “Hommma ho akoma ntutu!
Honye Nyankopɔn nni, na me nso honye me nni.
Tenabea pii ya m’Agya fie.
Sɛ ɔnte saa a, nka mɛka akyerɛ ho sɛ, meekosiesie baabi ama ho?
Na sɛ mekosiesei baabi ma ho a, mɛba bio, na mabɛfa ho akɔ me nkyɛne, na nea meya he ho nso hoaba hɔ.
Honnim kwane a ɔkɔ baabi a meekɔ he.” Toma bisaa no sɛ, “Awurade, yennim baabi a wookɔ, na ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na yɛatumi ahu kwane he?” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Mene kwane he, nɔkorɛ he ne nkwa he, bi nkɔ Agya he nkyɛne gye sɛ ɔfa me so.
Sɛ honim me a hobehu Agya he nso.
Ofiri saa berɛ yi, ho nim no, na hoahu no.” Filipo ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade kyerɛ yɛ Agya he, na ɔnoaa yɛ ma yɛ.” Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Filipo, me ne hoya hɔ dadaada yi, honhuu me anaa?
Biaa a w’ahu me he ahu Agya he nso.
Afei mmɛ nti ne wooka sɛ, ‘Kyerɛ yɛ Agya he’?
Wonnye nni sɛ meya Agya he mu, na Agya he nso ya me mu anaa?
Nsɛm a meka kyerɛ ho he, omfiri meaa me tim ne meka, na Agya a ɔte me mu he ne yɔ ne nnwuma.
Honye me nni sɛ meya Agya he mu, na Agya he nso ya me mu, na sɛ ɔnte saa nnwuma heaa nti honye nni.
Meeka akyerɛ ho nɔkorem paa sɛ, nea ɔgye me di he, nnwuma a meyɔ he ɔno nso bɛyɔ bi, na ɔbɛyɔ nnwuma bebree asene yeinom, efiri sɛ, me deɛ meekɔ Agya he nkyɛne.
Na bibiaa a hobɛsrɛ me dini mu he ɔno ne mɛyɔ na Agya he anya animuonyam Ba he mu.
Sɛ hosrɛ bibi me dini mu a, mɛyɔ.” Honhom Kronkron he ho bɔhyɛ “Hodɔ me a hobedi m’ahyɛdeɛ so.” Na m’ankasa mebisa Agya he na wama ho Kyigyinafoɔ foforɔ, na ɔne ho abɛtena daa, Nɔkorɛ Honhom a wiase ntumi nnye no he, efiri sɛ, onhu no, na onnim no nso.
Na ho deɛ honim no, efiri sɛ ɔya ho nkyɛne, na ɔbɛtena ho mu.
“Mennyae ho nyanka, na mɛba honkyɛne.
Aaka kakra na wiase nhu me bio, na ho deɛ hobehu me efiri sɛ, mete ase, nti ho nso hobɛtena ase.
Da heaa, hobehu sɛ meya m’Agya mu, na hoya me mu.
Nea ɔwɔ m’ahyɛdeɛ na odi so he, ɔno ne nea ɔdɔ me, na nea ɔdɔ me he m’Agya bɛdɔ no, na me nso mɛdɔ no, na mayi me ho akyerɛ no.” Yuda (ɔnyɛ Iskariot) bisaa no sɛ, “Awurade ɔyɛɛ dɛ na wobeyi wo ho akyerɛ yɛ yi, na ɔnyɛ wiase?” Yesu buaa no sɛ, “Sɛ bi dɔ me a obedi m’asɛm so, na m’Agya bɛdɔ no, na yɛbɛba ne nkyɛne na yɛ ne no abɛtena.
Nea ɔnnɔ me he nni me nsɛm so, na nsɛm a hoate he nyɛ me deɛ na ɔyɛ Agya a ɔsomaa me he deɛ.
“Meya ho nkyɛne yi, ne meeka yeinom.
Na Kyigyinafoɔ a ɔno ne Honhom Kronkron a m’Agya bɛsoma no me dini mu he, ɔno ne bɛkyerɛkyerɛ ho nnoɔma nyinaa na ɔbɛkae ho nea maka akyerɛ ho nyinaa.
Asomdwie ne mede oogya ho, m’asomdwie ne mede ɔɔma ho, nyɛ sɛnea wiase de ma ho he ne mede ɔɔma ho.
Hommma ho akoma ntutu, na hommɔ hu nso.
Hoate sɛ meka kyerɛɛ ho sɛ, ‘Meekɔ na mɛba ho nkyɛne.’ Sɛ hodɔ me a nka ho ani bɛgye sɛ meekɔ Agya he nkyɛne efiri sɛ m’Agya he yɛ keseɛ kyɛne me.
Afei maka akyerɛ ho ansa na aba mu, na sɛ onya ba mu a hoagye adi.
Me ne ho nkasa pii bio, na wiase sodifoɔ he ɔɔba, na onni tumi biaa me so nso meeyɔ sɛnea Agya he hyɛ me he, na wiase ahu sɛ me dɔ Agya he.
Honsɔre ma yemfiri ha nkɔ.
Yesu ne bobe trodoo he “Mene bobe trodoo he, m’Agya ne kuafoɔ he.
Mmane biaa ɔnso aba he, oyi firi ho; na nea ɔsõ aba he oyiyi ho ma ne so bebree.
Asɛm a maka akyerɛ ho nti, ho ho afiri dada.
Hontena me mu na me nso mentena ho mu.
Sɛnea mmane bi ankasa ntumi nso aba gye sɛ ɔtena bobe he mu he, saa nso ne hontumi nso aba gye sɛ hotena me mu.
Mene bobe he, ho ne mmane he.
Nea ɔtena me mu na me nso metena ne mu he, ɔsõ aba bebree; na ho kwati me a hontumi nyɔ hwee.
Sɛ bi antena me mu a, betwa no twene sɛ mmabaa a mfasoɔ nni so; na bɛboaboa ano de kogu gya mu ma ɔhye.
Sɛ hotena me mu na me nsɛm tena ho mu a, hommisa bibiaa a hopɛ na ɔbɛyɛ hɔ ama ho.
Nea ɔhyɛ m’Agya animuonyam ne sɛ hobɛkɔ so aso aba bebree na hoada ho ho adi sɛ m’asuafoɔ.
Sɛnea Agya he adɔ me na me nso madɔ ho he, hontena me dɔ mu.
Sɛ hodi m’ahyɛdeɛ so a, hobɛtena me dɔ mu, sɛnea madi m’Agya ahyɛdeɛ so na mete ne dɔ mu he.
Maaka nsɛm yei akyerɛ ho sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ na m’anigyeɛ bɛtena ho mu, na ama ho anigyeɛ awie pɛyɛ.” “Yei ne m’ahyɛdeɛ, sɛ honnodɔ ho ho sɛnea medɔɔ ho he.
Biaa nni dɔ a ɔkyɛne yei, sɛ bi de ne nkwa bɛto hɔ ama ne nnamfo.
Sɛ hoyɔ nea mehyɛ ho he a, hedeɛ hoyɛ me nnamfo.
Memmfrɛ ho nkoa bio, efiri sɛ akoa nnim nea ne wura yɔ.
Na mmom maafrɛ ho me nnamfo, efiri sɛ maada bibiaa a mate afiri m’Agya hɔ adi akyerɛ ho.
Ɔnyɛ ho na hoayi me, na mmom mene maayi ho.
Na maayi ho sɛ honkɔso aba, na hoaba he atena hɔ, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a nea hobebisa Agya he me dini mu biaa ɔde bɛma ho.
Yei ne meehyɛ ho na ama hoadodɔ ho ho.” Tane a wiase betane ho “Sɛ wiase tane ho a, honhu sɛ ɔtane me ansa na ɔɔtane ho.
Sɛ howɔ wiase afa a, wiase bɛdɔ ho sɛ ɔnoaa ne deɛ.
Na esiane sɛ honni wiase afa, na mmom maayi ho afiri wiase nti, wiase tane ho.
Honkae asɛm a maka akyerɛ ho yi, ‘Akoa nkyɛne ne wura.’ Sɛ bɛtane me a, bɛbɛtane ho nso, sɛ bedi me nsɛm so a, bebedi ho deɛ nso so.
Na bɛbɛyɔ yei nyinaa atia ho ɔnam me dini nti, efiri sɛ bennim nea ɔsomaa me he.
Sɛ mamma ammɛkasa ankyerɛ bɛ a, nka bɛnnyɔɔ bɔne; na seesei deɛ benni bɛ bɔne ho anoyie biaa.
Nea ɔtane me he tane m’Agya nso.
Sɛ mannyɔ nnwuma a biaa nyɔɔ bi da bɛ mu a, nka bɛnnyɔɔ bɔne.
Na afei deɛ bɛahu, nso bɛatane me ne m’Agya nyinaa.
Na ɔno ne ɔbɛma asɛm a bɛatwerɛ bɛ mmara he mu aba mu sɛ, ‘Bɛtane me tane hunu.’ “Sɛ Kyigyinafoɔ a mɛsoma no afiri Agya he nkyɛne aba ho hɔ he, Nɔkorɛ Honhom a ofiri Agya nkyɛne he nya ba a, ɔno ne bedi me ho adanseɛ.
Ho nso ɔsɛ sɛ hodi adanseɛ efiri sɛ ho ne me atena ase firi mfitiaseɛ he.
“Maaka yei nyinaa akyerɛ ho sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bibiaa nto ho sintidua.” Bɛbɛpam ho afiri hyia adane mu.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, berɛ bi ɔɔba a biaa a obeku ho he bɛdwene sɛ ɔɔyɔ saa Nyankopɔn dini mu.
Na bɛbɛyɔ yei, efiri sɛ, bennim Agya he anaa me.
Na maaka yei nyinaa akyerɛ ho na saa berɛ he duru a, hoakae sɛ maaka akyerɛ ho dada.
Honhom he Dwumadie “Na manka saa nsɛm yi ankyerɛ ho mfitiaseɛ he, efiri sɛ na meya ho nkyɛne.
Na afei deɛ meekɔ nea ɔsomaa me he nkyɛne, nso ho mu biaa mmisa me sɛ, ‘He ne wookɔ?’ Na esiane sɛ maka yei akyerɛ ho nti, awerɛhoɔ ahyɛ ho akoma ma.
Nso meeka nɔkorɛ akyerɛ ho sɛ, ɔyɛ ma ho sɛ mɛkɔ, efiri sɛ, sɛ mankɔ a, Kyigyinafoɔ he ɔmma ho nkyɛne.
Na sɛ mekɔ a, mɛsoma no ama no aba ho nkyɛne.
Na sɛ ɔba a, obeyi wiase atɛne afa bɔne ne tenenee ne atemmuo ho: Bɔne ho, efiri sɛ bɛnnye me nni; tenenee ho, efiri sɛ meekɔ Agya he nkyɛne, na honhu me bio; atemmuo ho, efiri sɛ nea odi wiase yi so he bɛabu no fɔ.
“Mewɔ nsɛm pii ka kyerɛɛ ho, nso hontumi nnye ne nyinaa seesei.
Na sɛ Nɔkorɛ Honhom he ba a, ɔbɛkyerɛ ho kwane akɔ nɔkorɛ he nyinaa mu, efiri sɛ omfiri ɔno ankasa ne mu ne bɛkasa, na mmom bibiaa ɔbɛte he ɔno ne ɔbɛka.
Na ɔbɛkyerɛ ho nnoɔma a ɔɔba.
Ɔno ne bɛhyɛ m’animuonyam; efiri sɛ ɔbɛfa nea ɔyɛ me deɛ he bi na wapaem aka akyerɛ ho.
Nea Agya he wɔ nyinaa yɛ me dea.
Saa nti ne mekaa sɛ nɔkorɛ Honhom he bɛfa nea ɔyɛ me deɛ na wapaem aka akyerɛ ho he.
Awerɛhoɔ bɛdane Anigyeɛ “Aaka kakraa bi na honhu me, na bio aaka kakraa bi hobehu me.” Afei n’asuafoɔ he binom bisaa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Asɛm a ɔɔka kyerɛ yɛ yi kyerɛ sɛ, “Aaka kakraa bi na honhu me, na bio aaka kakraa bi hobehu me; ne sɛ ‘Efiri sɛ meekɔ Agya he nkyɛne’?” Bɛkaa sɛ, “ ‘Aaka kakraa bi’ he kyerɛ sɛ?
Yennim nea ɔka ho asɛm yi.” Na Yesu huu sɛ bɛpɛ sɛ bebisa no nea ɔkaeɛ he asekyerɛ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Asɛm a mekaa sɛ ‘Aaka kakraa bi na honhu me, na bio aaka kakraa bi hobehu me’ he ne hoobisabisa ho ho asekyerɛ yi?” Nɔkwasɛm paa ne sɛ, hobesu atwa agyaadwoɔ, nso wiase ani bɛgye.
Hobedi awerɛhoɔ nso ho awerɛhoɔ he bɛdane anigyeɛ.
Sɛ baa ɔɔwo a, ɔte yeyaa efiri sɛ ne berɛ aduru.
Na sɛ ɔwo ne ba he a, ɔnkae ne yeyaa he bio esiane anigyeɛ a wanya sɛ wawo nipa aba wiase nti.
Ho nso, seesei deɛ howɔ awerɛhoɔ mu, nso mehu ho bio he, na ho ani agye ho akoma mu, na biaa ntumi nnye ho anigyeɛ he mfiri ho nsam.
Saa da he, hommmisa me asɛm biaa.
Nɔkwasɛm paa ne meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, hobisa bibiaa firi Agya he hɔ ya me dini mu a, ɔde bɛma ho.
Obesi sesɛɛ hommisaa bibiaa a me dini mu.
Hommisa, na ho nsa bɛka, na ho anigyeɛ awie pɛyɛ.
Asuafoɔ he asomdwie “Menam mfantoho so aka yeinom akyerɛ ho.
Berɛ he ɔɔba a memmfa mfantoho ne bɛkasa ho ho bio, na mmom mɛka Agya he ho asɛm akyerɛ ho pefee.
Saa da he me dini mu ne hobebisa.
Nso menka nkyerɛ ho sɛ mebisa Agya he ama ho.
Na Agya he ankasa dɔ ho, efiri sɛ hodɔ me na hoagye adi sɛ mefiri Nyankopɔn nkyɛne ne aba.
Mefiri Agya he nkyɛne ne aba wiase.
Afei deɛ meefiri wiase akɔ Agya he nkyɛne.” N’asuafoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Afei wookasa pefee, ɔnyɛ mfantoho so!
Afei deɛ yɛahu sɛ wonim bibiaa, na onhia sɛ biaa bebisa wo hwee.
Yei nti yɛagye adi sɛ wofiri Nyankopɔn hɔ ne baeɛ.” Yesu bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Afei hogye di anaa?” Berɛ he ɔɔba, na anya aba awie sɛ ho nyinaa hobɛhwete akɔ ho nkurom, na hoagya me nkoaa.
Nso ɔnka me nkoaa efiri sɛ Agya he ka me ho.
Maaka yeinom nyinaa akyerɛ ho sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a hobenya asomdwie me mu.
Hobehyia taa wiase mu.
Nso homma ho bo ntɔ ho yam; na maadi wiase so nkunim dada!
Yesu bɔɔ mpaeɛ maa asuafoɔ he Yesu kaa nsɛm yeinom wieeɛ he, ɔhwɛɛ soro kaa sɛ, “Agya, berɛ he anya aduru, hyɛ wo ba animuonyam na Ba he nso ahyɛ wo animuonyam sɛnea woama no nnipa nyinaa so tumi, sɛ biaa a wode ama no he ɔmma bɛ daa nkwa.
Na yei ne daa nkwa sɛ bebehu wo, wo a aoyɛ Nyankopɔn kann koro he, ne Yesu Kristo nea wasoma no he.
Mawie adwuma a wode ama me sɛ menyɔ he de ahyɛ wo animuonyam asaase so.
Na afei, Agya, fa animuonyam a na mewɔ no wo nkyɛne ansa na wiase ɔɔba he hyɛ me bio woaa wo nkyɛne.
“Maada wo dini adi akyerɛ bɛ a wode befiri wiase ama me he.
Bɛyɛ wo deɛ ne wode bɛ ama me.
Na bɛadi w’asɛm so.
Afei bɛahu sɛ adeɛ biaa a wode ama me he nyinaa firi wo nkyɛne; efiri sɛ nsɛm a wode maa me he mede ama bɛ; na bɛ nso bɛagye; na bɛahu ampa sɛ, mefiri wo nkyɛne ne baeɛ, na bɛagye adi sɛ wone wosomaa me.
Meebisa ama bɛ; memmisa mma wiase na mmom mebisa ma bɛ a wode bɛ ama me he, efiri sɛ bɛyɛ wo deɛ.
Nea mewɔ nyinaa yɛ wo dea, na wo deɛ nyinaa nso yɛ me deɛ, na maanya animuonyam yam.
Na afei nso, menni wiase bio, na mmom bɛ deɛ bɛya wiase, na meeba wo nkyɛne.
Agya Kronkron, bɔ bɛ a wode bɛ ama me he ho bane wo dini mu na bɛayɛ baako sɛ yɛyɛ baako he.
Meya bɛ nkyɛne he, mede bɛ siee wo dini mu.
Mekoraa bɛ yie na bɛ mu baako pɛ mpo annyera gye sɛ yera ba he, na ama twerɛsɛm he aba mu.
Na afei meeba wo nkyɛne, na meeka yeinom wiase na ama bɛanya m’anigyeɛ, na awie pɛyɛ bɛ mu.
Mede w’asɛm ama bɛ, na wiase atane bɛ efiri sɛ bɛnyɛ wiase deɛ sɛnea me nso menyɛ wiase deɛ he.
Mensrɛ sɛ yi befiri wiase, na mmom mesrɛ sɛ bɔ bɛ ho bane firi sɛefoɔ he ho.
Bemfiri wiase sɛnea me nso memfiri wiase he.
Fa nɔkorɛ he te bɛ ho, w’asɛm yɛ nɔkorɛ, sɛnea woasoma me wiase he, saa ne me nso meesoma bɛ wiase.
Meyɔɔ me kronkron maa bɛ, na bɛ nso bɛ ho ate nɔkorɛ mu.
“Mensrɛ mma yeinom nkoaa, na mmom mesrɛ ma bɛ a bɛnam bɛ asɛm so bɛgye me adi nso sɛ bɛ nyinaa bɛbɛyɛ baako, sɛnea wo, Agya, woya me mu, na meya wo mu; sɛ bɛ nso bɛnyɛ baako yɛ mu, na ama wiase agye adi sɛ wone wosomaa me.
Animuonyam a wode maa me he mede ama bɛ, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na bɛbɛyɛ baako sɛnea yɛyɛ baako he.
Meya bɛ mu, na woya me mu, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bebewie pɛyɛ baakoyɛ mu, na wiase ahu sɛ wone woasoma me na wodɔ bɛ sɛnea wodɔ me he.
Agya mepɛ sɛ bɛ a wode bɛ ama me he ba baabi a meya he.
Bɛmmɛka me ho na benhu m’animuonyam a wode ama me he, efiri sɛ wodɔɔ me ansa na wohyɛɛ wiase fapem ase.
“Oo!
Agya Teneneeni, wiase nnim wo, nso menim wo, na yeinom nim sɛ woasoma me.
Maada wo dini adi akyerɛ bɛ, na mɛda no adi akyerɛ, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a dɔ a wode adɔ me he bɛtena bɛ mu, na matena bɛ mu.”
Yesu yima ne ne kyeɛ Na Yesu kaa nsɛm yei nyinaa wieeɛ he, ɔne n’asuafoɔ he firii adi kotwaree Nsuo Kidron kɔɔ turo bi mu.
Na Yuda a oyii no maeɛ nso nim hɔ, efiri sɛ na Yesu taa hyia n’asuafoɔ he hɔ.
Nti Yuda de asrafokuo ne awɛmfoɔ a befiri asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne Farisifoɔ he nkyɛne baa hɔ a na bekitakita ntanii ne nkanea ne akodeɛ.
Afei, Yesu a na onim nea ɔbɛto no nyinaa he, pinii anim na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Hwane ne hoohwehwɛ no?” Bebuaa no sɛ, “Yesu, Nasareni he.” Yesu buaa bɛ sɛ, “Ɔyɛ me a.” Saa berɛ he na Yuda a oyii no maeɛ he ne bɛ ne gyina hɔ.
Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ “Ɔyɛ me a.” Na bɛpimpinii bɛ akyi na bɛhwehwee ase.
Na obisaa bɛ bio sɛ, “Hwane ne hoohwehwɛ no?” Na bɛkaa sɛ, “Yesu, Nasareni he a.” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Maka akyerɛ ho sɛ ɔyɛ me a.” Nti sɛ me ne hoohwehwɛ me deɛ a, homma saa mmeema yi nkɔ!
Yei maa asɛm a bɛkaeɛ he baam sɛ, “Mamma bɛ a wode bɛ maa me he mu baako koraa anyera.” Na Simon Petro twee sekane twaa sɔfopanyini he akoa aso nifa.
Na akoa he de Malko.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ Petro sɛ, “Fa sekane he hyɛ bɔha he mu.
Nti ɔnsɛ sɛ mennom kuruwa a Agya he de ama me he anaa?” Bɛde Yesu kogyina sɔfopanyini anim Afei asrafokuo he ne bɛ safohene ne Yudafoɔ awɛmfoɔ he kyee Yesu, na bɛkyekyeree no.
Bedii kane de no kɔɔ Anas hɔ.
Na Anas yɛ Kaiafa a na ɔyɛ sɔfopanyini saa afe he ase.
Kaiafa yɛ bi a otuu Yudafoɔ he fo sɛ ɔyɛ sɛ nipa baako bewu ama mane he.
Petro yii Yesu mmaeɛ Na Simon Petro ne suani foforɔ bi dii Yesu akyi.
Saa suani he yɛ bi a na sɔfopanyini he nim no, na ɔne Yesu kɔɔ sɔfopanyini he abane mu hɔ, nso Petro deɛ na ogyina aboboa he ano abɔntene hɔ.
Nti suani foforɔ a na sɔfopanyini he nim no he baa abɔntene.
Na ɔne baa a na ɔyɛ aboboa he ano hwɛfoɔ he kɔkasae.
Na ɔde Petro baa mu.
Na baa he bisaa Petro sɛ, “Wo nso woyɛ beema yi asuafoɔ he mu baako, ɔnte saa?” Petro kaa sɛ, “Daabi menka ho.” Na esiane sɛ na awɔ yam nti, na nkoa ne awɛmfoɔ he de bidie asɔ gya gyinagyina ho ɔɔto.
Na Petro nso ne begyina hɔ ɔɔto gya he bi.
Sɔfopanyini he totoo Yesu Ano Na afei sɔfopanyini he bisaa Yesu asɛm faa n’asuafoɔ ne ne nkyerɛkyerɛ ho.
Yesu buaa sɛ, “Me deɛ makasa akyerɛ wiase badwam; mekyerɛkyerɛɛ hyia adane ne asɔredane mu daa, baabi a Yudafoɔ nyinaa hyia he.
Menkaa bibiaa kokoam.
Mmɛ nti ne wobisa me?
Bisa bɛ a bɛtee nea meka kyerɛɛ bɛ he; benim nea mekaeɛ.” Na ɔkaa yei he, awɛmfoɔ he mu baako a na ogyina hɔ bɔɔ Yesu asom, kaa sɛ “Nti, sɛnea wobuaa sɔfopanyini di?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Sɛ maaka asɛmmɔne a, di bɔne he ho adanseɛ, na sɛ nea mekaeɛ he yɛ a, ɛɛne nti ne wobɔ me?” Na Anas maa bɛkyekyeree Yesu de no kɔmaa sɔfopanyini Kaiafa.
Petro yii Yesu mmaa bio Saa berɛ yi na Simon Petro gyina hɔ ɔɔto gya.
Bebisaa no sɛ, “Wo nso woyɛ beema yi asuafoɔ he mu baako, ɔnte saa?” Ɔsanee sɛ, “Daabi menka ho.” Na sɔfopanyini he akoa a Petro twaa n’aso he busuani kaa sɛ, “Manhu wo ne no turom hɔ?” Petro sanee bio sɛ ɔnte saa, na amonom hɔaa akokɔ bɔneeɛ.
Bɛde Yesu kogyinaa Pilato anim Na bɛde Yesu firii Kaiafa hɔ kɔɔ amrado Pilato abane mu.
Na ɔyɛ anɔpatutuutu.
Na Yudafoɔ he ankasa ankɔ amrado abane he mu sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a bengu bɛ ho fi na bɛatumi adi Twam he bi.
Nti Pilato kɔɔ bɛ nkyɛne abɔntene bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ soboɔ ne hode ɔɔbɔ saa beema yi?” Bɛkaa sɛ, “Sɛ beema yi nyɛ nipa bɔnefoɔ a, nka yɛamfa no ammrɛ wo.” Pilato ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho ankasa homfa no nkobu no atɛne sɛnea ho mmara teɛ.” Yudafoɔ he buaa sɛ, “Mmara mma yɛ kwane mma yenku biaa.” (Yei maa asɛm a Yesu ka faa wuo korɔ a na oobewu he ho he baa mu.)
Nti Pilato kɔɔ amrado abane he mu hɔ bio, na ɔfrɛɛ Yesu bisaa no sɛ, “Wo ne Yudafoɔ hene he?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “W’ankasa na woabɔ wo tim ɔɔka yei anaa nipa bi ne kaa me ho asɛm kyerɛɛ wo?” Pilato buaa sɛ, “Menyɛ Yudani, anaa meyɛ bi?
Wo ankasa wo manfoɔ ne asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he ne de wo ahyɛ me nsa.
Mmɛ adeɛ ne woayɔ?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “M’ahennie mfiri wiase yi mu.
Sɛ nka ofiri wiase yi mu a, nka m’asomfoɔ bɛko na bɛamfa me anhyɛ Yudafoɔ he nsa.
Nso m’ahennie mfiri ha.” Pilato bisaa no sɛ, “Nti woyɛ hene?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Wone wooka sɛ meyɛ hene.
Me deɛ yei nti ne bɛwoo me, na mebaa wiase sɛ meebedi nɔkorɛ he ho adanseɛ.
Biaa a ofiri nɔkorɛ he tie me nne.” Pilato bisaa no sɛ, “Ɛɛne ne nɔkorɛ?” Bebuaa Yesu Kumfɔ Ɔkaa yei wieeɛ he, ɔsane firi kɔɔ Yudafoɔ he hɔ kɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Mennhuu mfomsoɔ biaa ne ho.
Nso howɔ amanneɛ bi sɛ, sɛ Twam duru a megyae nipa baako ma ho.
Nti hopɛ sɛ megyae Yudafoɔ hene he ma ho anaa?” Bɛteaam kaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ yie, na mmom Baraba!” Na Baraba yɛ dwotwafoɔ.
Afei Pilato faa Yesu, na ɔmaa bɛbɔɔ no mmaa.
Na asraafoɔ he de nkasɛe yɔɔ kyɛ de hyɛɛ ne ti, na bɛde ataadeɛ ngugusoɔ kɔkɔɔ bi hyɛɛ no.
Na bɛkɔɔ so baa ne nkyɛne bɛkaa sɛ, “Yudafoɔ hene, mo oo mo!” Na bɛbobɔɔ no asotorɔ.
Pilato kɔɔ abɔntene bio kɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Mede no oofiri adi abra ho na hoahu sɛ menhuu ne ho mfomsoɔ biaa.” Nti Yesu firii adi baeɛ a na nkasɛe kyɛ hyɛ no na ataadeɛ ngugusoɔ kɔkɔɔ bi nso hyɛ no.
Pilato ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Beema he di!” Berɛ a asɔfoɔ ne awɛmfoɔ he huu Yesu he, bɛteateaam sɛ, “Bɔ no asennua mu!
Bɔ no asennua mu!” Pilato ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho ankasa homfa no na hommɔ no asennua mu.
Menhu mfomsoɔ biaa ne ho.” Yudafoɔ he buaa no sɛ, “Yɛwɔ mmara, na sɛnea mmara he kyerɛ he ɔsɛ sɛ owu efiri sɛ ɔyɛ ne ho sɛ Nyankopɔn Ba.” Afei berɛ a Pilato tee yei he, osuroo paa.
Ɔkɔɔ n’abane mu bio, na obisaa Yesu sɛ, “Wofiri he?” Na Yesu ammua no.
Na Pilato ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wommua me?
Wonnim sɛ mewɔ tumi sɛ megyae wo anaa mebɔ wo asennua mu?” Yesu buaa sɛ, “Sɛ bɛamfa amfiri soro amma wo a wonnya me so tumi biaa.
Ɔno nti nea oyii me maa wo he bɔne so paa.” Ofiri saa berɛ he Pilato kɔɔ so hwehwɛɛ kwane a ɔbɛfa so agyae Yesu, nso Yudafoɔ he teaam kaa sɛ, “Sɛ wogyae beema yi a na wonyɛ Kaesare adamfo.
Nipa biaa a ɔyɛ ne ho sɛ hene he kasa tia Kaesare.” Na Pilato tee nsɛm yi, ɔde Yesu pie baa abɔntene na ɔtenaa atemmuo adwa so baabi a bɛfrɛ hɔ Aboɔ-nsɛeɛ, na Hebri kasa mu bɛfrɛ no Gabata.
Saa berɛ he na bɛɛboaboa bɛ ho ama Twam he, na aabɔ bɛyɛ awia dummienu.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ Yudafoɔ he sɛ, “Hwɛ, ho hene di!” Bɛteaam sɛ, “Fa no kɔ!
Fa no kɔ!
Bɔ no asennua mu!” Pilato bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Memmɔ ho Hene he asennua mu?” Asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he buaa sɛ, “Yenni hene biaa ka Kaesare ho.” Na ɔde Yesu maa bɛ sɛ bɛnkɔ bɔ no asennua mu.
Bɛbɔɔ Yesu asennua mu Nti bɛfaa Yesu kɔeɛ berɛ a na ɔno ankasa so n’asennua.
Ofirii adi kɔɔ baabi a bɛfrɛ hɔ Tikankuro (anaa Golgota Hebri kasa mu).
Hɔ ne bɛbɔɔ ɔne nnipa mmienu asennua mu.
Na nnipa mmienu he mu baako ya Yesu nifa ne baako nso ya ne benkum.
Pilato twerɛɛ asɛm bi bɔɔ asennua he atifi.
Ɔtwerɛɛ sɛ, “Yesu Nasareni, Yudafoɔ hene he.” Yudafoɔ bebree kane saa ntwerɛeɛ yi efiri sɛ na baabi a bɛbɔɔ Yesu asennua he bɛne kuro he.
Bɛtwerɛɛ asɛm yi Hebri ne Roma ne Hela kasa mu.
Na Yuda asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ Pilato sɛ, “Ntwerɛ sɛ, ‘Yudafoɔ hene,’ na mmom twerɛ sɛ ‘Saa beema yi dɛ, mene Yudafoɔ hene.’ ” Pilato kaa sɛ, “Nea matwerɛ he na matwerɛ.” Na asraafoɔ he bɔɔ Yesu asennua mu wieeɛ he, bɛfaa n’ataadeɛ ngugusoɔ he kyɛɛ mu nnan maa sraani biaa nyaa baako, ɔne n’ataadeɛ nhyɛaseɛ.
Nso na ataadeɛ nhyɛaseɛ he nni mpameeɛ, bɛnwene firi soro besii fam.
Nti bɛkeka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Hommma yɛ ntete mu, na mmom yɛntwe so ntonto nhwɛ nea ɔbɛyɛ ne deɛ.” Na yei ma twerɛ he baa mu sɛ, “Bɛkyekyɛɛ me ngusoɔ mu faeɛ, na bɛ twee m’ataadeɛ nso so ntonto.” Na yei ne nea asraafoɔ he yɔeɛ.
Saa berɛ heaa na Yesu maame, ne maame nua baa, Maria a ɔyɛ Klopa yerɛ ne Maria Magdalene gyina Yesu asennua he ho.
Na Yesu huu ne maame ne suani a ɔdɔ no he sɛ ogyina ne maame nkyɛne he, ɔka kyerɛɛ ne maame sɛ, “Baa, hwɛ, wo ba beema di.” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ suani he sɛ, “Hwɛ, wo nso wo maame di.” Na efiri saa berɛ he suani he de Maria kɔɔ ɔno ankasa ne fie.
Yei akyi a Yesu huu sɛ woanya awie nnoɔma nyinaa he (sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ na twerɛ he aba mu nti), ɔkaa sɛ, “Sukɔm de me.” Na adeɛ bi si hɔ a nsa kekakeka ahyɛ no ma.
Nti bɛde nsa he bi hyɛɛ sapɔ ma de hyɛɛ dua so de kaa n’ano.
Na Yesu gyee nsa he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Mawie!” Osii ne ti ase, na ogyaam.
Bɛde pea wɔɔ Yesu mfe Na saa da he yɛ ahosiesie da.
Na sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a homeda he beduru na amu he nsɛne asennua he so nti, Yudafoɔ he bɛsrɛɛ Pilato sɛ ɔmma bemmubu bɛ a bɛabɔ bɛ asennua he nane mu, na benyi amu he mfiri hɔ.
Na asraafoɔ he ba bebubuu nipa a odi kane ne nea ɔka ho he nane mu.
Na beduruu Yesu nkyɛne a behuu sɛ wawu dada he, bɛammubu ne nane mu.
Na asraafoɔ he mu baako de pea wɔɔ ne mfe, na mogyaa ne nsuo firii mu baeɛ amonom hɔaa.
(Na nea ohuiɛ he adi adanseɛ yi sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a wo nso wobɛgye adi.
N’adanseɛ he yɛ nɔkorɛ, na onim sɛ nea ɔɔka he yɛ nɔkorɛ.)
Yei siiɛ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na twerɛsɛm he aba mu sɛ, “Bemmmu ne dompe biaa mu,” Na bio twerɛsɛm foforɔ dɛ, “Bɛbɛhwɛ nea bɛde pea awɔ no he.” Yesu amu sie Na yeinom akyi he, Yosef a ofiri Arimatea a ɔyɛ Yesu suani nso Yudafoɔ ho hu nti, na ɔyɛ no kokoam he, bɛsrɛɛ Pilato sɛ ɔmma no mfa Yesu amu he nkɔ; na Pilato maa ne kwane na ɔbɛfa kɔeɛ.
Nikodemo a dabi ɔbaa Yesu nkyɛne anadwo he nso baeɛ, na ɔde korobo ne pɛprɛ mfrafrae a mu duru bɛyɛ nkariboɔ ha baeɛ.
Afei bɛfaa Yesu amu he, na bɛde nwera a aduhwam yam kyekyere ne ho, sɛnea Yudafoɔ sie bɛ amu he.
Na turo bi ya baabi a bɛbɔɔ no asennua mu he, na nna bi ya turom hɔ a ɔyɛ foforɔ a bensie biaa mu da.
Na hɔ ne Yudafoɔ ahosiesie da he nti, bɛde Yesu kɔtoeɛ, efiri sɛ saa nna he a na bɛde boɔ ayɔ he na na ɔbɛne.
Yesu wusɔreɛ Afei nnawɔtwe da a odi kane he, Maria Magdalene kɔɔ da he so anɔpatutuutu na ohuu sɛ boɔ he nna nna he ano.
Nti ɔde mmirika kɔɔ Petro ne suani foforɔ a Awurade pɛ n’asɛm he nkyɛne kɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Bɛafa Awurade afiri nna he mu, na yennim baabi a bɛde no akɔto.” Na Petro ne suani foforɔ he firii adi baa nna he ho.
Na bɛ mmienu ne beetu mmirika boom nso suani baako he de mmirika tɛntɛ dii Petro anim, na oduruu nna he ho kane.
Na ɔbɔɔ ne mu ase hwɛɛ nna he mu, nso wankɔ mu.
Na Simon Petro dii n’akyi baeɛ, na ɔkɔɔ nna he mu na ohuu nwera he sɛ ogu hɔ, na afei ntoma a bɛde bɔɔ ne ti he nso bɛabobɔ gu nkyɛne baabi a ɔnka nwere he ho.
Na afei suani foforɔ he a oduruu nna he ho kane he nso kɔɔ mu, na ohuuiɛ, na ɔgye diiɛ.
Saa berɛ he na ɔntee twerɛsɛm he ase sɛ otwa sɛ onyane firi awufoɔ mu.
Nti asuafoɔ he sane kɔɔ bɛ afie mu.
Yesu yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ Maria Magdalene Maria deɛ, na ɔda soaa gyina da he nkyɛne baabi a oosu.
Na oguso oosu he, ɔbɔɔ ne mu ase hwɛɛ da he mu.
Na ohuu abɔfoɔ mmienu bi a bɛhyɛ ntaadeɛ fitaa a na bɛtete baabi a na Yesu amu da he; na baako te baabi a na Yesu amu he da he atifi na baako nso te anafoɔ.
Bebisaa no sɛ, “Baa, ɛɛne nti ne woosu yi?” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Bɛafa m’Awurade amu kɔ na mennim baabi a a bɛde no akɔto.” Na ɔkaa yei wieeɛ he ɔdane ne ho na ohuu Yesu sɛ ogyina hɔ, nso wanhu sɛ ɔyɛ Yesu a. Yesu bisaa no sɛ “Baa, Mmɛ nti ne woosu yi?
Hwane ne woohwehwɛ no?” Maria deɛ na osusu sɛ ɔyɛ turom hɔ hwɛfoɔ nti ɔkaa sɛ, “Owura, sɛ wone wafa no afiri ha a, kyɛrɛ me baabi a wode no akɔto.” Na Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Maria!” Na ɔdanee ne hoka kyerɛɛ no Hebri kasa mu sɛ “Rabuni” (asekyerɛ ne sɛ “Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ!”) Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Mfa wo nsa nka me, efiri sɛ menya nkɔɔ soro, m’Agya nkyɛne.
Na kɔ me nuanom nkyɛne kɔka kyerɛ bɛ sɛ, ‘Meekɔ soro, m’Agya ne ho Agya ne me Nyankopɔn ne ho Nyankopɔn nkyɛne.’ ” Na Maria Magdalene bɛkaa nea asi he kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he sɛ, “Maahu Awurade”, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ Awurade aka yeinom akyerɛ no.
Yesu yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ Asuafoɔ he Na saa da he yɛ nnawɔtwe he da a odi kane.
Na nwunu dwoeɛ he, ewom sɛ na Yudafoɔ ho hu nti asuafoɔ he atoto apono mu baabi a na bɛya he deɛ, nso Yesu ba begyinaa bɛ mfimfini, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Asomdwie nka ho!” Na ɔkaa saa he, ɔde ne nsa ne ne mfem kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he.
Na asuafoɔ he ani gyee sɛ bɛahu Awurade.
Na Yesu sane ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Asomdwie nka ho!
Sɛnea Agya he asoma me he, saa are ne me nso meesoma ho.” Ɔkaa yei wieeɛ he, ɔhome guu bɛ so, kaa sɛ, “Honye Honhom Kronkron.
Na biaa a hode ne bɔne bɛkyɛ no he, na bɛde akyɛ no dada.
Na biaa a hoammfa ne bɔne akyɛ no he, bɛmmfa nkyɛɛ no.” Yesu ne Toma Na berɛ a Yesu baeɛ he na Toma, Yesu asuafoɔ dummienu he mu baako a bɛfrɛ no Ata he, nka ho.
Nti asuafoɔ a aka he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Yɛahu Awurade.” Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ manhu ne nsam nnadewa twa na mamfa me nsa teaa anka dadewa he twa he a mennye nni.” Ne nnawɔtwe akyi he, na asuafoɔ he ya dane mu bio a na Toma nso ka ho.
Ewom sɛ na bɛatoto apono he mu deɛ, nso Yesu ba begyinaa bɛ mfinfini, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Asomdwie nka ho!” Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ Toma sɛ, “Fa wo nsa tea ka ha na bɛhwɛ me nsam, na fa wo nsa bɛka me mfem, na nyɛ akyinnyegyefoɔ.” Toma buaa no sɛ, “M’Awurade ne me Nyankopɔn!” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Woahu me nti ne woagye adi?
Nhyira ne bɛ a benhuiɛ nso bɛagye adi.” Nwoma yi Botaeɛ Na afei nsɛnkyerɛnne pii nso ya hɔ a Yesu yɔɔ n’asuafoɔ he anim a bɛantwerɛ no nwoma yi mu.
Nso bɛatwerɛ yei ato hɔ na ama hoagye adi sɛ Yesu ne Kristo he, Nyankopɔn Ba, na hogye di a, hoanya nkwa ne dini mu.
Yesu yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ Asuafoɔ nson Yei akyi he, Yesu yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he bio Tiberia po ho.
Na oyii ne ho adi saa kwane yi so.
Na Simon Petro, Toma a bɛfrɛ no Ata, Natanael a ofiri Kana a ɔya Galilea, Sebedeo mma mmeema he ne asuafoɔ he mu mmienu nso ya hɔ.
Simon Petro ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Meekoyi nam.” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Yɛ ne wo bɛkɔ.” Bɛkɔtenaa kodoɔ he mu, na anadwo he nyinaa bɛanyi nam biaa.
Na adeɛ ɔɔyɛ akye he, Yesu begyinaa po he ano, nso asuafoɔ he ahu sɛ ɔyɛ ɔno a. Yesu bisaa bɛ sɛ, “Mma nkumaa, hoanya nam?” Na bebuaa sɛ, “Daabi.” Na ɔka kyerɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honto asau he ngu kodoɔ he nifa na hobenya bi.” Nti bɛtoo asau he na adwene dodoɔ a benyaeɛ nti na bentumi ntwe asau he.
Na suani a Yesu dɔ no he ka kyerɛɛ Petro sɛ, “Ɔyɛ Awurade!” Petro tee sɛ ɔyɛ Awurade he, ɔde n’ataadeɛ kyekyeree ne ho, efiri sɛ na ɔda adagya, na ohuri kɔhwee po he mu.
Na asuafoɔ nkaeɛ he baa kodoɔ he mu bɛtwee asau a na adwene ahyɛ no ma he, saa berɛ he na bɛne asaase ntam bɛyɛ basafa ha.
Na bebeduru kokoɔ so he, behuu gyabidie a bɛasɔ a nam ne paanoo gu so.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Homfa adwene a hoayi he bi mmra.” Nti Simon Petro kɔtwee asau a adwene akɛseɛ ha aduonum mmeɛnsa ahyɛ no ma he baa kokoɔ so.
Na ɔdɔɔso deɛ, nso asau he ante.
Yesu ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Hommra mmedidi.” Nso asuafoɔ he mu biaa antumi ammisa sɛ, “Woyɛ hwane?” Na benim sɛ ɔyɛ Awurade.
Yesu ba bɛfaa paanoo he na ode maa bɛ, na ɔfaa nam he nso yɔɔ saa.
Yei ne ne mprɛnsa so a Yesu nyane firii awufoɔ mu he, oyii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ asuafoɔ he.
Yesu ne Petro Na bedidi wieeɛ he, Yesu bisaa Simon Petro sɛ, “Simon, Yohane ba, wodɔ me kyɛne yeinom nyinaa?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ɛɛ, Awurade, wonim sɛ medɔ wo.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ma me nnwane he aduane nni.” Obisaa no mprenu so sɛ, “Simon, Yohane ba, wodɔ me?” Ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Ɛɛ, Awurade, wonim sɛ medɔ wo.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Yɛne me nnwane.” Obisaa no mprɛnsa so sɛ, “Simon, Yohane ba, wodɔ me anaa?” Petro werɛ hoo sɛ oobisa no mprɛnsa so sɛ “wodɔ me?” Na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade, wonim bibiaa, wonim sɛ medɔ wo.” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nyɛne me nnwane he.” Nɔkwasɛm paa ne sɛ, woyɛ abranteɛ he na wode abɔsoɔ bɔ wo mu nante kɔ baabiaa a w’ankasa wopɛ.
Nso sɛ wobɔ akɔkora a, wobɛtene wo nsa na bi de abɔsoɔ abɔ wo mu, na ɔde wo akɔ baabi a wompɛ sɛ wokɔ.
(Ɔkaa yei de kyerɛɛ wuo korɔ a obewu de ahyɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam.)
Yei akyi he ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Di m’akyi.” Yesu ne suani a ɔdɔ no he Petro danee ne ho he, ohuu suani a Yesu dɔ no he sɛ odi n’akyi, nea na ɔtweree Yesu kokom adidie he ase a obisaa sɛ, “Awurade, hwane ne beyi wo ama he.” Na Petro huu no he, obisaa Yesu sɛ, “Awurade, na yei nso ɛ?” Yesu ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɛ ɔyɛ mepɛ sɛ ɔtena hɔ kosi sɛ mɛba a, ɔfa wo ho bɛ?” Wo deɛ, kɔ soaa na di m’akyi.
Nti asɛm yi trɛɛ anuanom he mu sɛ saa suani he onwu; nso Yesu anka sɛ suani he onwu, na mmom ɔkaa sɛ, “Sɛ mepɛ sɛ ɔbɛtena hɔ akosi sɛ mɛba a, ɔfa wo ho bɛ?” Yei ne suani a oodi nnoɔma yi ho adanseɛ na watwerɛ yeinom, na yenim sɛ adanseɛ a odi he yɛ nɔkorɛ.
Na nnoɔma bebree ya hɔ nso a Yesu yɔeɛ a, sɛ bɛtwerɛɛ ne nyinaa a, nka mesusu sɛ, nwoma a bɛbɛtwerɛ he nkɔ wiase mu mpo.
NNIANIMU Asomafoɔ He Nnwuma yɛ Luka Asɛmpa he ntoasoɔ.
Ne botaeɛ titire paa ne sɛ ɔbɛka sɛdeɛ Honhom Kronkron dii Yesu akyidifoɔ a bedii kane he akyi, ma bɛkaa ne ho Asɛmpa he ya Yerusalem, Yudea ne Samaria mu de kosii asaase ano nohoa .
Nwoma yi yɛ nsɛm a ɔfa Kristofoɔ anammɔntuo ho sɛdeɛ ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ ya Yudafoɔ mu na ɔkɔɔ soaa bɛyɛɛ wiase nyinaa gyidie.
Twerɛfoɔ he botaeɛ ne sɛ ɔbɛma n’akenkanfoɔ ate aseɛ sɛ na Akristofoɔ he nyɛ amammɔfoɔ ya Romafoɔ ahemmane he mu.
Ɔdaa no adi sɛ akristofoɔ gyidie he yɛ deɛ ɔbɛhyɛ Yudasom he ma.
Asomafoɔ he Nnwuma he wɔ nkyekyɛmu ahodoɔ mmeɛnsa: Kristofoɔ anammɔntuo a ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ Yerusalem, Yesu sorokɔ akyiri; Bɛtrɛɛ asɛmpa he mu kɔɔ Palestina; Bɛsane trɛɛ mu kɔɔ wiase fa a ɔwɔ po agya, de koduruu Roma.
Adeɛ a ho hia baako ya Asomafoɔ He Nnwuma mu ne Honhom Kronkron dwumadie a ɔde tumi baa agyidifoɔ he so ya Yerusalem berɛ a Pentekoste da he duruiɛ he.
Honhom Kronkron kɔɔ soaa hyɛɛ Asafo he ne n’akannifoɔ nkrunee.
Ɔbɔ Akristofoɔ a bedii kane he nsɛm mua ya asɛnka ahodoɔ mu, na nsɛm a bɛatwerɛ ya Asomafoɔ He Nnwuma mu he de kyerɛ tumi a ɔya nsɛm yi mu agyidifoɔ abrabɔ ne Asafo he ayɔnkofa mu.
MU NSƐM Adansedie ho ahosiesie :- .
Yesu ahyɛdeɛ ne bɔhyɛ a odi akyire :- .
Yuda anamusini :- Adansefoɔ ya Yerusalem :—: Adansedie ya Yudea ne Samaria :—: Paulo som adwuma :—: .
N’asɛnka akwantuo a odi kane :—: .
Yerusalem nhyiamu he :- .
N’asɛnka akwantuo a ɔtɔ so mmienu :—: .
N’asɛnka akwantuo a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa :—: .
Paulo yɛ deduani ya Yerusalem, Kaesarea ne Roma :—:
Teofilo, nwoma a odi kane a metwerɛeɛ he fa nnoɔma a Yesu firii aseɛ yɔeɛ na ɔkyerɛkyerɛeɛ nyinaa de besi da a ɔnam Honhom Kronkron so maa asomafoɔ a oyii bɛ he ahyɛdeɛ, na ɔno akyi he bɛfaa no kɔɔ soro.
N’amanehunu akyi he, ɔnam adanseɛ pii so yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ ɔte ase maa behuu no adaduannan ntam.
Na ɔkaa Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho asɛm.
Na ɔne bɛ hyiaeɛ he, ɔhyɛɛ bɛ sɛ: “Hommfiri Yerusalem nkɔ, na mmom hontwɛne nea Agya he ahyɛ ho bɔ a, hotee sɛ mekaa ho asɛm sɛ, Yohane deɛ, ɔde nsuo ne bɔɔ asu, na ho deɛ, nna yi mu, ɔnkyɛre bɛbɛbɔ ho asu Honhom Kronkron mu.” Berɛ a behyiaeɛ he, bebisaa no sɛ, “Awurade, berɛ yi mu ne bɛbɛsane de ahennie he ama Israel anaa?” Afei obuaa bɛ sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ ho asɛm sɛ hobehu berɛ anaa nna a Agya he ankansa de ne tumi ahyɛ ato hɔ, na mmom sɛ Honhom Kronkron he nya ba ho so a, hobenya ahoɔdene, na hoayɛ m’adansefoɔ ya Yerusalem, Yudea ne Samaria de akɔpem asaase ano nohoa.” Na ɔkaa yeinom wieeɛ a na bɛɛhwɛ no he, bɛmaa no so, na mununkum bɛkataa no so a afei na benhu no bio.
Na ɔɔkɔ na asuafoɔ he ɔɔhwɛ soro haa he, mpofiremuaa nnipa mmienu bi a bɛhyɛ ntaadeɛ fitaa begyinaa ne nkyɛne.
Na bɛkaa sɛ, “Galilea mmeema, ɛɛne nti na hogyina ha ɔɔhwɛ soro haa yi?
Yesu yi a bɛafa no ho nkyɛne kɔ soro yi, ɔbɛba saa, sɛnea hohu no sɛ ɔɔkɔ soro yi.” Na yei akyi he, asuafoɔ he firii Ngo Bepɔ a ɔbɛne Yerusalem bɛyɛ borɔfo kwansini fa he so sane kɔɔ Yerusalem.
Na beduruu hɔ he, bɛforo kɔɔ abrosane so kowuraa dane bi a na Petro ne Yohane ne Yakobo ne Andrea, Filipo ne Toma, Bartolomeo ne Mateo, Alfeo ba Yakobo ne Simon Selote ne Yakobo ba Yuda te mu he mu.
Na bɛ nyinaa bɛde akoma korɔ tuu bɛ ho sii hɔ maa mpaebɔ, a na mmaa a bɛne Yesu nanteeɛ he ne Yesu maame Maria ne Yesu nuanom nso ka ho.
Na nna he mu he Petro sɔre gyinaa agyidifoɔ he mfinimfini.
Na nnipakuo a bɛahyia faako he bɛyɛ nnipa ha aduonu.
Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Anuanom, otwa sɛ twerɛsɛm a Honhom Kronkron nam Dawid so ka faa Yuda a ɔkyerɛɛ bɛ a bɛkyee Yesu he kwane maa bɛkyee no he ba mu.
Na ɔka yɛ ho, na onyaa som yi kyɛfa bi someeɛ.
“Na bɛatwerɛ no Nnwom nwoma he mu sɛ, ‘Ma ne tenabea nnane amanfõõ, na mma biaa ntena hɔ’; na ‘Ne hwɛfoɔ adwuma he, ma bi foforɔ nyɔ.’ Nti otwa sɛ mmeema a bɛ ne yɛ nateeɛ berɛ a Awurade Yesu ne yɛ dii akɔneaba he nyinaa ofiri Yohane asubɔ so de besi da a bɛfaa no firii yɛ nkyɛne kɔɔ soro he mu baako ne yɛ yɛ ne sɔreɛ ho adansefoɔ.” Nti besusuu nnipa mmienu, Yosef a bɛfrɛ no Barsaba a bɛtoo ne dini Yusto, ɔne Matia.
Na bɛbɔɔ mpaeɛ sɛ, “Awurade, wonim nnipa nyinaa akomam, kyerɛ mmienu yi baako a woayi no sɛ ɔmfa som yi, ne asomfodwuma a Yuda firii mu gya too hɔ, faa ɔno ankasa kwane so he!” Na bɛtwee bɛ so ntonto; na ntonto he bɔɔ Matia, na bɛde no kaa asomafoɔ dubaako he ho.
Na Pentekoste da he duruiɛ he, na bɛ nyinaa ahyia faako.
Na mpofiremuaa, dede bi a ɔte sɛ mframa a ɔɔbɔ dendenndene firi soro baeɛ, na ɔbɛhyɛɛ fie a na bɛte mu he ma.
Na behuu bibi te sɛ gya a ɔɔdɛre a atwetwe sɛ kɛtrɛma, na obesisii bɛ atifi mmaako mmaako.
Na Honhom Kronkron bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nyinaa ma ma, na befiri aseɛ sɛ kaa kasa foforɔ, sɛnea Honhom he de maa bɛ sɛ bɛnka.
Afei na Yudafoɔ bi a bɛyɛ nyamesurofoɔ a befiri wiase amane nyinaa mu te Yerusalem.
Na dede he baeɛ he, nnipa pii behyiaeɛ, na bɛ adwene mu yɛɛ bɛ naa sɛ biaa tee nea bɛɛka he ne kurom kasa mu.
Na ɔyɛɛ bɛ nyinaa ahodwiri ne nwanwa, na bebisaa sɛ, “Aa!
Bɛ a bɛɛkasa yi nyinaa nyɛ Galileafoɔ?
Na afei ɔyɛɛ dɛ ne yɛ nyinaa yɛte nea bɛɛka yi yɛ ankasa yɛ kurom kasa mu yi?
Ye mu binom firi Partia, Media, Elam, Mesopotamia, Yudea, Kapadokia, Ponto, Asia, Frigia Pamfilia, Misraim ne Libia fa a ɔfa Kirene; afei binom nso yɛ ahɔhoɔ a befiri Roma, binom nso yɛ Yudafoɔ ne amanamane mufoɔ a bɛabɛdɔm Yudafoɔ som he, Kretefoɔ ne Arabiafoɔ; na yɛte no yɛ kasa mu sɛ bɛɛka Nyankopɔn tumi ne ne nnwuma akɛseɛ ho asɛm.” Na ɔyɛɛ bɛ nyinaa ahodwiri ne nwanwa, na bebisabisaa bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Yei kyerɛ sɛ?” Na binom nso dii bɛ ho fɛw sɛ “Nsa dɔkɔdɔkɔ aboro bɛ.” Na Petro ne dubaako he sɔre gyinaeɛ; afei Petro teaam ka kyerɛɛ nnipa a bɛya hɔ he sɛ, “Yudafoɔ ne ho a hote Yerusalem nyinaa, honyɛ aso ntie nea meebɛka yi!
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, yeinom mmoro nsa, sɛnea hosusu he, na afei mpo ne abɔ anɔpa nnɔn nkron.
Na deɛ asi yi yɛ nea diyifoɔ Yoel kaa ho asɛm sɛ, Nyankopɔn dɛ: ‘Nna a odi akyire he mu he, mehwie me Honhom agu honam nyinaa so, na ho mma mmeema ne ho mma mmaa ahyɛ nkɔm, na mmabunu anya anisoadehunu, na ho mpanyini asõsõ adaeɛ.
Na me nkoa ne me mfena so ne, nna he mu, mehwie me Honhom agu, na bɛahyɛ nkɔm.
Na mɛma anwanwadeɛ aba soro na nsɛnkyerɛnne aba asaase so, fam, mogyaa ne gya ne wisie kumoo.
Awia beduru sum, na bosome nso adane sɛ mogyaa, ansa na Awurade da kɛseɛ a ɔhyerɛn he aba.
Na biaa ɔbɛbɔ Awurade dini he bɛbɛgye no nkwa.’ “Israelfoɔ, hontie nea meeka yi: Yesu, Nasareni he, beema a Nyankopɔn de anwanwadeɛ ne nsɛnkyerɛnne a ɔno Nyankopɔn he ankasa nam ne so yɔɔ no ho mu yii no adi kyerɛ ho pefee, sɛnea hoaa honim he; ɔnoaa ne ɔnam Nyankopɔn nhyehyɛeɛ ne ne nim a onim dada so yii no maeɛ he, na hofaa no, nam bɛ a benni mmara nsa so bɔɔ no asennua mu kuu no.
Nyankopɔn anyane no afiri wuom, na waayi wuo-yeyaa afiri ne so, efiri sɛ ontumi mma sɛ ɔbɛkɔ so ahu wuo amaneɛ.
Na Dawid kaa ne ho asɛm sɛ, ‘Mehu Awurade m’anim da biaa, ɔya me nifa nti menhinhim da; Yei nti m’akoma tɔɔ me yam, na me kɛtrɛma ho sanee no; afei nso me nipadua mpo bɛtena anidasoɔ mu, efiri sɛ wonnya me kra Asamando, na womma wo Kronkronni he nipadua mporɔ.
