Woama mahu nkwa kwane; esiane sɛ wo ne me ya hɔ nti, m’anigyeɛ awie pɛyɛ.’ “Anuanom, homma me kwane na menka nana Dawid ho asɛm pefee menkyerɛ ho, sɛ owuiɛ, na besiee no, na n’adamena ya yɛ nkyɛne ha de besi nnɛ.
Ɔnam sɛ ɔyɛ diyifoɔ, na onim sɛ Nyankopɔn de ntam aka akyerɛ no sɛ n’asenemfoɔ he mu baako bɛtena n’ahennwa so nti, ohuu yei sieeɛ na ɔkaa Kristo ho asɛm sɛ bɛannya no Asamando, saa ara nso ne ne honam amporɔ.
Yesu yiaa ne Nyankopɔn anyane no; yɛ nyinaa yɛyɛ ho adansefoɔ.
Afei bɛmaa no so kɔɔ Nyankopɔn nifa, na onyaa Agya he nkyɛne Honhom bɔhyɛ he nti ne wahwie nea hohu na hote yi agu.
Na Dawid amforo ankɔ soro, nso ɔno ankasa kaa sɛ, ‘Awurade ka kyerɛɛ m’Awurade sɛ, Tena me nsa nifa, kosi sɛ mede w’atamfoɔ bɛhyɛ wo nane ase.’ Nti ma Israel fie nyinaa nhu ampa sɛ Nyankopɔn ayɔ Yesu yi a hobɔɔ no asennua mu he Awurade ne Kristo.” Na bɛteeɛ he, asɛm he wowɔɔ bɛ akoma mu, na bebisaa Petro ne Asomafoɔ a bɛaka he sɛ, “Anuanom, ɛɛne ne yɛnyɔ?” Afei Petro ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Honsakra ho adwene, na ho nyinaa homma bɛmmɔ ho asu Yesu Kristo dini mu, na hoanya bɔne fakyɛ, na hobenya akyɛdeɛ a ɔyɛ Honhom Kronkron he.
Na bɔhyɛ yi ya hɔ ma ho ne ho mma ne bɛ a bɛya akyirikyiri, a Awurade yɛ Nyankopɔn bɛfrɛ bɛ aba ne nkyɛne nyinaa.” Na ɔde nsɛm foforɔ pii dii adanseɛ, na otuu bɛ fo sɛ, “Homma bɛnnye ho mfiri awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ porɔeɛ yi mu.” Na bɛ a bɛde anigyeɛ gyee n’asɛm he maa bɛbɔɔ bɛ asu, na saa da he akra bɛyɛ mpem mmeɛnsa nso bɛyɛɛ asuafoɔ.
Na betuu bɛ ho sii hɔ maa asomafoɔ he nkyerɛkyerɛ ne ayɔnkofa, paanoo bubuo ne mpaebɔ.
Na hu tɔɔ akra nyinaa so, efiri sɛ Asomafoɔ he yɔɔ anwanwadeɛ ne nsɛnkyerɛnne pii.
Na bɛ a bɛgye diiɛ nyinaa hyiaa faako, na bɛ nnoɔma nyinaa yɛɛ kwasafodeɛ.
Na bɛtɔno nea bɛwɔ ne bɛ agyapadeɛ kyekyɛɛ nea benyaeɛ maa bɛ ho bɛ ho, sɛnea biaa ahiadeɛ teɛ.
Da biaa na behyiam asɔrefie hɔ, na bebubu paanoo afie mu, de anigyeɛ ne akoma a mu te didi bom yi Nyankopɔn ayɛ.
Na benyaa nnipa he nyinaa anim adom.
Na Awurade de bɛ a ɔgyee bɛ he kaa asafo he ho da biaa.
Da koro bi, ɔɔkɔ bɔ awia nnɔn mmeɛnsa, mpaebɔ berɛ he, Petro ne Yohane siim sɛ bɛɛkɔ asɔrefie.
Na nkurofoɔ so beema bi a bɛwoo no he na ɔyɛ bubuani; na daa bɛde no ba asɔrefie pono a bɛfrɛ no Pono Fɛɛfɛ he ano ma no bɛsrɛ bɛ a bɛɛkɔ asɔrefie hɔ he hɔ sika.
Berɛ a ohuu Petro ne Yohane sɛ bɛɛkɔ asɔrefie hɔ he, ɔsrɛɛ sɛ bɛnkyɛ no sika.
Nso Petro ne Yohane hwɛɛ no gyee; na Petro kaa sɛ “Hwɛ yɛ.” Nti ɔhwɛɛ bɛ susuu sɛ obenya bibi afiri bɛnkyɛne.
Nso Petro kaa sɛ, “Sika anaa dwetɛ deɛ menni bi, na mmom nea mewɔ ne mede ma wo yi; sɔre nante Yesu Kristo, Nasareni he, dini mu.” Nti ɔsɔɔ ne nsa nifa maa no so.
Na amonom hɔaa ne nane ne ne nanpɔ so yɛɛ dene.
Ohuri gyinaeɛ, na ofirii aseɛ nanteeɛ, na ɔne bɛ kɔɔ asɔrefie hɔ a na oohurihuri na ooyi Nyankopɔn ayɛ.
Nnipa he nyinaa huu no sɛ ɔɔnante na ooyi Nyankopɔn ayɛ, na behuu sɛ ɔyɛ ɔno ne na ɔtena Pono Fɛɛfɛ he ano srɛsrɛ sika he, na nea asi he yɛɛ bɛ nwanwa ne ahodwiri.
Berɛ a beema he kita Petro ne Yohane mu he, nnipa a bɛya hɔ he nyinaa de ahodwiri tuu mmirika kɔɔ bɛ nkyɛne bea bi a bɛfrɛ hɔ Salomo abranaa so.
Na Petro huu yei he, ɔka kyerɛɛ nkurofokuo he sɛ, “Israel mmeema, ɛɛne nti ne yei yɛ ho nwanwa, mmɛ nti ne hoohwɛ yɛ haa te sɛ nea yɛnam yɛ ankasa yɛ tumi anaa yɛ tenenee so ne ama beema yi anante yi?
Abraham Nyankopɔn ne Isak Nyankopɔn ne Yakobo Nyankopɔn, yɛ nananom Nyankopɔn ahyɛ n’akoa Yesu animuonyam, nea ho deɛ, hoyii no maeɛ, na hopaa no Pilato anim, berɛ a Pilato sii gyinaeɛ sɛ obegyaa no he.
Na hopoo Kronkronni ne Hoteeni he, na hosrɛɛ sɛ bennyae wudini he ma ɔnkɔ.
Na hokuu nkwa Farebae he, nea Nyankopɔn nyanee no firii awufuom he.
Yɛyɛ yei ho adansefoɔ.
Nti gyidie a yɛwɔ ya ne dini mu ne ama beema a hohu no na honim no yi anya ahoɔdene, na Yesu mu gyidie ne ama beema yi ho atɔ no korakora ya ho nyinaa ho anim yi.
“Afei anuanom, menim sɛ nim a honnim nti ne hoyɔɔ sɛnea ho atumfoɔ yɔɔeɛ he.
Nso Nyankopɔn nam saa kwane yi so ama nnoɔma a ɔnam adiyifoɔ he so kaeɛ he aba mu sɛ, ne Kristo he behu amane.
Nti ho nsakra ho adwene, na hommra Nyankopɔn nkyɛne na wapopa ho bɔne, na ayɛ ahotɔ nna afiri Awurade nkyɛne aba, na wasoma nea bɛayi no asi hɔ ama ho dada he, Yesu, Kristo he a ɔsɛ sɛ ɔtena soro kosi berɛ a bebesiesie nnoɔma nyinaa sɛnea Nyankopɔn nam n’adiyifoɔ kronkron he so firi teteete aka he.
Mose kaa sɛ, ‘Awurade ho Nyankopɔn beyi diyifoɔ a ɔte sɛ me afiri ho nuanom mu ama ho.
Ɔsɛ sɛ hotie nea ɔbɛka akyerɛ ho nyinaa.
Na ɔbɛba sɛ, biaa a ontie saa diyifoɔ he, bɛbɛsɛe no koraa afiri mane he mu.’ Na adiyifoɔ a bɛakasa he, ofiri Samuel ne bɛ a bɛbaa n’akyi, nso hyɛɛ saa nna yi ho nkɔm.
Hoyɛ adiyifoɔ he ne apam a Nyankopɔn ne ho agyanom pameeɛ he mma, sɛnea ɔka kyerɛɛ Abraham sɛ, ‘W’aseni so ne bɛbɛfa ahyira asaase so mmusua nyinaa he.’ Berɛ a Nyankopɔn somaa n’Akoa he, ho nkyɛne ne ɔmaa no baa kane sɛ ɔmmɛdane ho nyinaa mfiri ho nneyɔeɛ bɔne ho na onhyira ho.”
Afei berɛ a Petro ne Yohane ɔɔkasa akyerɛ nkurofoɔ he, asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne asɔrefie hwɛfoɔ he ne Sadukifoɔ he baa bɛ so, na bɛ bo afu sɛ asuafoɔ he nam Yesu wusɔreɛ he ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ nkurofoɔ he wusɔreɛ ho asɛm.
Nti bɛkyee bɛ kɔtoo afiase ma adeɛ kyeeɛ, efiri sɛ na adeɛ asa dada.
Na bɛ a bɛtee asɛm a Petro ne Yohane kaeɛ he mu bebree gye diiɛ, na bɛ dodoɔ bɛyɛ mpemnum.
Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, bɛ atumfoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ ne atwerɛfoɔ he hyiaam Yerusalem, a na sɔfo panyini Anas, ne Kaiafa, ne Yohane ne Aleksandro, ne bɛ mu pii a na bɛyɛ sɔfo panyini he abusuafoɔ nso ka ho.
Na bɛde Petro ne Yohane begyinaa bɛ mfimfini firi aseɛ bisabisaa bɛ sɛ: “Mmɛ tumi ne hode yɔɔ yei anaa hwane dini mu ne hoyɔɔ saa?” Na Petro a Honhom Kronkron he ahyɛ no ma he kaa sɛ, “Mane atumfoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ, sɛ nnɛ hogyina papa a yɛayɔ ama yarefoɔ yi so ɔɔhwehwɛ yɛ nsɛm mu ahu nea ɔnam ne so ama beema yi ho atɔ no a, hedeɛ ho ne nnipa a hoya Israel nyinaa nhu sɛ ɔnam Nasareni Yesu Kristo a hobɔɔ no asennua mu a Nyankopɔn nyane no firii awufoɔ mu he dini so ne saa beema yi nyaa ayaresa.
Saa Yesu yi ne, boɔ a ho adansifoɔ poo no a wabɛyɛ tweaso ti boɔ he.
Nkwagyeɛ nni bi foforɔ mu, efiri sɛ dini foforɔ biaa nni soro anaa asaase so a bɛde ama nnipa sɛ bɛmfa so nye yɛ nkwa ka Yesu dini ho.” Na behuu sɛnea Petro ne Yohane kasa akokoɔduro so he, na behuu sɛ bɛyɛ nnipa a bensuaa nwoma na bɛyɛ mpapahwekwaa he, ɔyɛɛ bɛ nwanwa.
Na behuu sɛ na bɛne Yesu ne nanteeɛ.
Na bɛhwɛɛ nipa a bɛasa no yareɛ he sɛ ogyina Petro ne Yohane nkyɛne he, bɛanya hwee anka antia bɛ.
Na bɛhyɛɛ bɛ sɛ bemfiri dwa he mu mfiri adi, na betuu agyina.
Na bɛkaa sɛ, “Ɛɛne ne yɛbɛyɔ nnipa yi?
Na nsɛnkyerɛnne a ɔnam bɛ so aba he ada adi ya bɛ a bɛte Yerusalem nyinaa anim; na yentumi nnye ho akyinnye.
Na sɛ ɔbɛyɔ na ɔnkɔ so nterɛ nnipa he mu nti, homma yɛmmara bɛ sɛ bɛnnka dini yi ho asɛm nkyerɛ nipa biaa bio.” Nti bɛfrɛɛ bɛ hyɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛnnka asɛm na bɛnkyerɛkyerɛ Yesu dini mu baabiaa.
Nso Petro ne Yohane buaa bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ ɔtene Nyankopɔn anim sɛ yetie ho sene Nyankopɔn a, ho ankasa hommua.
Na yɛ mmom deɛ, nea yɛate na yɛahu he, yentumi nnyae ho asɛm ka da.” Na behunahunaa bɛ bio he, begyae bɛ esiane sɛ bɛannya bibiaa a bebegyina so atwe bɛ aso ɔnam nkurofoɔ he nti, efiri sɛ, na nkurofoɔ he nyinaa ɔɔhyɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam ya nea asi he ho.
Na beema a bɛnam anwanwakwane so saa no yadeɛ he adi boro mfie aduannan.
Asafo he mpaebɔ Begyae bɛ he, bɛkɔɔ bɛ mfɛfoɔ nkyɛne kɔkaa nea sɔfopanyini ne mpanyimfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ bɛ he kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Bɛtee yei he bɛde akoma korɔ maa bɛ nne so bɔɔ mpaeɛ sɛ, “Nyame Tumfoɔ, wo ne wobɔɔ soro ne asaase, po ne mu nnoɔma nyinaa, na wonam Honhom Kronkron so faa yɛ nana Dawid a ɔyɛ w’akoa so kaa sɛ: ‘Ɛɛne nti ne Amanamane yɛ gyegyeegye na nkurofoɔ susu ade hunu?
Asaase so ahemfo sɔre gyina, na atitire hyiaa faako sɔre tia Awurade ne ne Kristo he.’ Na Herode ne Pontio Pilato ne amanamane mufoɔ ne Israelfoɔ ka boom tiaa w’akoa kronkron Yesu a woasra no sɛ ɔmmɛyɔ nea wo nsa ne wo agyina ahyɛ ato hɔ sɛ ɔbɛba he.
Na afei, Awurade, hwɛ bɛ ahunahuna, na ma wo nkoa mfa akokoɔduro nyinaa nka w’asɛm, berɛ a wotene wo nsa sa yadeɛ, na wonam w’akoa kronkron Yesu dini so yɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne ne anwanwadeɛ yi.” Berɛ a bewiee mpaebɔ he, baabi a behyiaam he wosoeɛ, na Honhom Kronkron bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nyinaa mama na bɛde akokoɔduro kaa Nyankopɔn asɛm he.
Asafo mu anuadɔ Na afei bɛ a bɛgye diiɛ he mu bebree akoma ne bɛ kra yɛɛ baako, na bɛ mu biaa nka sɛ ne nnoɔma a ɔwɔ yɛ ɔno nkoaa ne dea, na mmom bɛ nnoɔma nyinaa yɛ kwasafodeɛ.
Asomafoɔ he de tumi kɛseɛ dii adanseɛ faa Awurade Yesu wusɔreɛ he ho, na adom kɛseɛ baa bɛ nyinaa bɛ so.
Bɛ mu biaa nni hɔ a na bibi hia no, efiri sɛ na bɛ a bɛwɔ nsaase anaa afie he nyinaa tɔno de nea benya he ba bɛhyɛ asomafoɔ he nsa ma bɛkyekyɛ ma biaa sɛnea n’ahiadeɛ teɛ.
Nti Yosef a asomafoɔ he too ne dini Barnaba, a asekyerɛ ne Futufoɔ, Lewini a ofiri Kipro, a ɔwɔ asaase bi he, tɔno de sika he bɛhyɛɛ asomafoɔ he nsa.
Torɔdie ho asotwee Na beema bi a ɔde Anania, ne ne yerɛ Safira nso tɔnoo bɛ asaase bi.
Na Anania yii sika a benyaeɛ he bi sieeɛ a na ne yerɛ nso nim ho bi, na bɛde nkaeɛ he bɛhyɛɛ asomafoɔ he nsa.
Petro bisaa sɛ, “Anania, ɛɛne nti ne Satan apirim w’akoma sɛ yi sika a wonyaeɛ firi asaase he tɔno he mu bi sie na bedi torɔ kyerɛ Honhom Kronkron?
Berɛ a asaase he ya wo nsam he, na ɔnyɛ wo dea?
Na wotɔnoeɛ he nso, na ɔnna so nyɛ wo dea anaa?
Mmɛ nti na wobɔɔ pɔ a ɔte saa w’akoma mu?
Nyankopɔn ne woadi torɔ akyerɛ no, na mmom ɔnyɛ nnipa.” Anania tee asɛm he, ɔhwee ase wuiɛ.
Na hu kɛseɛ bɔɔ bɛ a bɛteeɛ he nyinaa.
Na mmaranteɛ he sɔre de ntoma kyekyeree no, na bɛsoaa no firii adi kosiee no.
Afei bɛyɛ nnɔnhwere mmeɛnsa akyi he, ne yerɛ baeɛ a na onnim nea asi.
Petro bisaa no sɛ, “Ka kyerɛ me, hotɔnoo asaase he de gyee saa boɔ yi anaa?” Na obuaa sɛ, “Ɛɛ, saa ne yɛ tɔnoo no.” Na afei Petro bisaa no sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ho mmienu ayɔ ho adwene sɛ ho bɛsɔ Nyankopɔn Honhom ahwɛ yi?
Hwɛ, bɛ a bekosiee wo kunu he anammɔno ne ya pono ano he, saa ne bɛbɛsoa wo nso akɔ.” Amonom hɔaa ɔhwee Petro nane ase wuiɛ.
Na mmeranteɛ he baeɛ a behuu sɛ wawu he, bɛfaa no firi adi kosiee no ne kunu he nkyɛne.
Na hu kɛseɛ bɔɔ asafo he ne bɛ a bɛteeɛ nyinaa.
Anwanwadeɛ ahodoɔ Bio nso, Nyankopɔn nam asomafoɔ he so yɔɔ nsɛnkyerɛnne ne anwanwadeɛ bebree nnipa he mu, na na bɛ nyinaa de akoma koro ya Salomo abranaa he so.
Na nnipa a aka he mu biaa annya akokoɔduro amfa ne he ammɔ bɛ; nso nkurofoɔ de anidie kɛseɛ maa bɛ.
Na afei, afei, nea ɔkyɛne so ne sɛ mmeema ne mmaa pii a bɛagye Awurade adi he bɛkaa bɛ ho.
Na bɛde ayarefoɔ baa abɔntene bɛtotoo mpa ne kɛtɛ so sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a anyeyie koraa he, sɛ Petro ootwam a ne sunsum bɛtɔ bɛ mu bi so.
Afei nnipa pii firi nkuro a atwa Yerusalem ho ahyia he mu nso de ayarefoɔ ne bɛ a ahonhom fi ha bɛ baeɛ, na bɛsaa bɛ nyinaa yadeɛ.
Na sɔfo panyini he ne bɛ a bɛka ne ho nyinaa, Sadukifoɔ fekuo a na bɛya hɔ saa bere he sɔreeɛ, na ahoɔyea a ahyɛ bɛ ma nti, bɛkyee asomafoɔ he de bɛ guu afiase.
Na anadwo he, Awurade bɔfoɔ bi biee afiase apono he de bɛ firii adi kaa sɛ, “Honkɔ, na honkogyina asɔrefie hɔ, nkɔka nkwa yi ho nsɛm nyinaa nkyerɛ nkurofoɔ he.” Na bɛtee yei he, bɛkɔɔ asɔredane he mu ahemakye, na bɛkɔɔ so kyerɛkyerɛeɛ.
Na sɔfo panyini he ne bɛ a bɛka ne ho he beduruiɛ he, bɛfrɛɛ abadwakuo he ne Israel mpanyimfoɔ nyinaa behyiaeɛ, na bɛsoma ma bɛkɔɔ afiase hɔ sɛ bɛnkɔfa bɛ mmra.
Nso bere a awɛmfoɔ he duruu hɔ he, bɛanhu bɛ afiase hɔ.
Nti bɛsane kɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ, “Yɛahu sɛ bɛatoto afiase apono he nyinaa mu dendenndene a awɛmfoɔ he gyinagyina apono he ano, nso yebieɛ he yɛanhu biaa hɔ.” Na afei bere a asɔrefie hwɛfoɔ ne asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ he tee nsɛm yi he, bɛ adwene mu yɛɛ bɛ kesenenee; na na bennim baabi a nsɛm yi bɛkɔ akowie.
Afei nipa bi bɛbɔɔ bɛ amanneɛ sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Mmeema a hode bɛ guu afiase he ya asɔrefie hɔ, na begyinagyina hɔ ɔɔkyerɛkyerɛ nkurofoɔ he.” Petro dii wursɔreɛ ho adanseɛ Nti asɔrefie hwɛfoɔ he ne n’awɛmfoɔ kɔfaa bɛ baeɛ, nso bɛanyɔ bɛ gidigidi, efiri sɛ na besuro sɛ nkurofoɔ he besi bɛ aboɔ.
Afei bɛde bɛ begyinaa Yudafoɔ abadwakuo kɛseɛ a bɛfrɛ no Sanhedrin he anim.
Na sɔfo panyini he bisabisaa bɛ nsɛm na ɔkaa sɛ, “Yɛanhyɛ ho ketee sɛ honyina saa dini yi so nkyerɛkyerɛ?
Na afei ɔyɛɛ dɛ ne hode ho nkyerɛkyerɛ yi ahyeta Yerusalem nyinaa, na hoabɔ ho tim pɔ sɛ hode nipa yi mogyaa bebua yɛ atifi.” Petro ne asomafoɔ a bɛaka he buaa sɛ, “Ɔsɛ sɛ yetie Nyankopɔn mmom sene nnipa.
Yɛ agyanom Nyankopɔn nyanee Yesu a hosɛne no asennua so, na hokuu no he.
Saa nipa yi ne Nyankopɔn maa no so sɛ Safohene ne Agyenkwa kɔɔ ne nsa nifa so, sɛ ɔmma Israel nnya adwensakra ne bɔne fakyɛ.
Na yɛyɛ nsɛm he ho adansefoɔ, na Honhom Kronkron a Nyankopɔn de ama bɛ a betie no he nso di adanseɛ.” Berɛ a bɛtee yei he, ɔwɔɔ bɛ yie na bɛpɛɛ sɛ beku bɛ.
Nso Farisini bi a bɛfrɛ no Gamaliel a ɔyɛ mmarakyerɛni a nkurofoɔ he nyinaa de anidie ma no, sɔre gyinaa Sanhedrin he anim, na ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa mmeema he mfiri adi kakra.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Israel mmeema, honhwɛ ho ho yie nea hoayɔ ho adwene sɛ hode bɛyɔ nnipa yi ho.
Hwɛ, berɛ bi a atwam he Teuda sɔre kaa sɛ “Meyɛ dikanfoɔ titire bi”, na mmeema a bɛ dodoɔ bɛyɛ ahanan kɔkaa ne kuo he ho.
Nso bekuu no, na bɛ a betiee no nyinaa bɔhweteeɛ ma ne kuo he guiɛ.
Ɔno akyi he, Galileani bi a ɔde Yuda nso sɔree nna a bɛtwerɛtwerɛ dini he mu, na ɔtwee nnipa dii n’akyi.
Ɔno nso wuiɛ, na n’akyidifoɔ he nyinaa hweteeɛ.
Nti me deɛ, nea mewɔ ka fa nea asisi yi ho ne sɛ, hommfa ho ho nhyehyɛ bɛ nsɛm mu, na honyaa bɛ, efiri sɛ, sɛ agyinatuo anaa adwuma yi firi nnipa a obegu; nso sɛ ofiri Nyankopɔn a hontumi ntu bɛ ngu koraa.
Anyɛ saa ɔbɛyɛ sɛnea ho ne Nyankopɔn ankasa ɔɔko.
Bɛgyee ne nsusuiɛ he toom!” Na bɛfrɛɛ asomafoɔ he baeɛ, na betwaa bɛ mmaa.
Na bɛhyɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛmmɔ Yesu dini nka asɛm bio, na begyae bɛ.
Befirii Sanhedrin he anim kɔeɛ, na bɛ ani gyee sɛ Yesu dini nti bɛfata sɛ begu bɛ anim ase.
Na bɛkɔɔ so kyerɛkyerɛeɛ, kaa Kristo Yesu ho asɛmpa ya asɔrefie ne afie afie mu daa a bɛannyae.
Asafo he yii asomfo Na afei nna he mu a na asuafoɔ he ɔɔdɔɔso he, Yudafoɔ na beka Hela kasa a ɔno nti ne bɛfrɛ bɛ Helenifoɔ he nwiinwii tia Hebrifoɔ he, efiri sɛ na bebu bɛ ani gu Helenifoɔ akunafoɔ he daa daa aduane ma dwumadie so.
Nti dummienu he frɛɛ asuafokuo he ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ɔmfata sɛ yebegya Nyankopɔn asɛm hɔ akɔkyekyɛ aduane apono so.
Nti anuanom, ho ankasa honhwehwɛ ho mu mmeema nson a hobetumi adi bɛ ho adanse-pa, na Honhom ne nyansa ahyɛ bɛ ma, na yɛmfa saa dwumadie yi nhyɛ bɛ nsa, na yɛ nso yebetu yɛ ho asi hɔ ama mpaebɔ ne asɛm he nkyerɛkyerɛ.” Nea bɛkaeɛ he sɔɔ nnipakuo he nyinaa ani, na beyii Stefano a gyidie ne Honhom Kronkron ahyɛ no mma, ne Filipo, Prokoro, Nikanor, Timon, Parmena ne Nikolao a ofiri Antiokia a wasakra abɛyɛ Yudani he.
Bɛde bɛ begyinaa asomafoɔ he anim, na bɛde bɛ nsa guu bɛ so bɔɔ mpaeɛ maa bɛ.
Na Nyankopɔn asɛm kɔɔ so trɛeɛ, na asuafoɔ he kɔɔ so yɛɛ dodo ya Yerusalem, na Yudafoɔ som he mu asɔfoɔ mu pii gyee asɛm he diiɛ.
Afei Stefano a na adom ne tumi ahyɛ no ma he, yɔɔ anwanwadeɛ ne nsɛnkyerɛnne akɛseɛ nnipa he mu.
Nso nnipa bi a befiri nea bɛfrɛɛ no Ahofadiefoɔ Hyiadane he mu ne Kirenefoɔ ne Aleksandriafoɔ ne bɛ a befiri Kilikia ne Asia, sɔree sɛ bɛne Stefano oobedi anobaabaeɛ.
Nso bɛantumi annyina ne nyansa ne Honhom a ɔde kasaeɛ he ano.
Na betutu guu nnipa bi asum sɛ bɛnka sɛ, “Yɛate sɛ ɔɔka abususɛm atia Mose ne Nyankopɔn.” Na behwanyanee nnipa he ne mpanyimfoɔ he ne atwerɛfoɔ he maa bɛbaa no so mpofirem bɛkyee no kɔmaa Sanhedrin he.
Na bɛmaa adansekunumufoɔ bɛkaa sɛ, “Beema yi nnyae nsɛm a ɔka tia kronkronbea yi ne Mmara he; na yɛate sɛ ɔdɛ Yesu yi a ɔyɛ Nasareni he bedwiri bea yi agu fam na wasakra amanneɛ a Mose de maa yɛ he.” Berɛ a bɛ a bɛte Sanhedrin badwa he mu nyinaa hwɛɛ no dinn he, behuu sɛ n’anim te sɛ bɔfoɔ anim.
Bɛde Stefano kogyinaa badwa he anim Na sɔfo panyini he bisaa sɛ, “Nsɛm yi te saa anaa?” Na Stefano buaa sɛ: “Anuanom ne agyanom, hontie me.
Animuonyam Nyankopɔn he yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ yɛ nana Abraham, berɛ a na ɔya Mesopotamia ansa na ɔɔkɔtena Haran he, na ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, ‘Firi w’asaase so ne w’abusua mu na kɔ asaase a mɛkyerɛ wo he so.’ Nti firi Kaldeafoɔ asaase so kɔtena Haran.
Afei berɛ a ne papa wuiɛ akyi he, Nyankopɔn ma otu bɛtenaa asaase a hote so seesei he so.
Nso wamma no bi sɛ n’agyapadeɛ, wannya anammɔno baako mpo, na mmom Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ bɔ sɛ ɔde bɛma no sɛ agyapadeɛ, na ne wuo akyi he ɔde bɛma n’asefoɔ, nso saa berɛ he na onni ba.
Na Nyankopɔn kaa yei ho asɛm sɛ, n’asefoɔ bɛyɛ ahohoɔ binom mane mu, na nkurofoɔ he de bɛ ayɛ nkoa, ateetee bɛ mfie ahannan.
Nyankopɔn kaa sɛ, ‘Mebu mane a bɛde bɛ bɛyɛ nkoa he atɛne, na yeinom akyi he, bebefiri hɔ na bɛabɛsom me ha.’ Ɔmaa no twetiatwa apam nso; nti ɔwoo Isak, na da ɔtɔ so nwɔtwe he otwaa no twetia, na Isak woo Yakob, na Yakob woo mmusua dummienu he agyanom.
“Na saa agyanom he aniberee Yosef, na bɛtɔnoo no kɔɔ Misraim.
Nso na Nyankopɔn ka ne ho, na ɔgyee no firii n’ahohiahia nyinaa mu maa no adom ne nyansa wɔ Misraim hene Farao anim.
Na ɔpaa no sɛ ɔnhwɛ Misraim ne ne fie nyinaa so.
Na afei ɔbaa sɛ kɔm bi baa Misraim ne Kaana asaase nyinaa so, na yei de amaneɛ kɛseɛ baeɛ a na yɛ nananom nya aduane nni.
Na Yakob tee sɛ aduane ya Misraim he, ɔsomaa yɛ nananom berɛ a odi kane.
Na ne mprenu so he, Yosef yii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ ne nuanom, na Farao huu Yosef abusua.
Nti Yosef soma ma bɛkɔfaa ne papa Yakob ne n’abusua nyinaa firii hɔ baeɛ, nnipa a na bɛ dodoɔ yɛ aduɔson num.
Yakob kɔɔ Misraim.
Na ɔno ankasa wuiɛ, na yɛ agyanom nso wuwuu saa na bɛde bɛ kɔɔ Sekem kosiee bɛ adamena a Abraham de sika dwetɛ tɔ firii Hamor mma nkyɛne ya Sekem he mu.
“Na berɛ ɔɔyɛ aso ama bɔhyɛ a Nyankopɔn de maa Abraham he aba mu he, yɛ nkurofoɔ he dɔre yɛɛ bebree ya Misraim kosii sɛ hene foforɔ bedii adeɛ Misraim a na onnim Yosef.
Ɔno ne de anifire dii yɛ abusua na ɔhyɛɛ yɛ nananom sɛ bɛnto bɛ mmɔfra ngu ma benwuwu.
Saa berɛ heaa ne bɛwoo Mose, na ne ho ɔfɛ paa.
Na bɛtetee no bosome mmeɛnsa ne papa fie na begyae no hɔ he, Farao babaa faa no tetee no sɛ n’ankasa ba.
Na bɛkyerɛɛ Mose Misraim nyansa nyinaa.
Na ɔwɔ tumi ne kasa ne nnwuma mu.
“Na odii mfie aduannan he, ɔyɔɔ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛkɔ akɔhwehwɛ ne nuanom, Israelfoɔ he.
Na ohuu sɛ Misraimni bi ɔɔyɔ Israelni bi bɔne he, ɔgyee Israelni he ti, na okuu Misraimni he de yɛɛ aweretɔ maa Israelni a na ɔɔyɔ no bɔne he.
Osusuu sɛ ne nuanom behu sɛ Nyankopɔn nam ne so ɔɔgye bɛ, nso bɛanhu no saa.
Na adeɛ kyeeɛ he ɔkɔtoo Israelfoɔ binom sɛ bɛɛko, na ɔbɔɔ mmɔdene sɛ ɔbɛka bɛ abom bio ama asomdwie aba bɛ ntam, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Mmeema, ho yɛ anuanom.
Mmɛ nti ne hoyɔ ho ho bɔne yi?” Na nea ɔɔyɔ ne yɔnko bɔne he summ no kaa sɛ, “Hwane ne yii wo sɛ yɛ sodifoɔ ne temufoɔ?” Wopɛ sɛ woku me sɛ wokuu Misraimni he nnora he anaa?
Na Mose tee yei he, odwane kɔeɛ na ɔkɔyɛɛ hɔhoɔ Midian asaase so, na hɔ ne ɔwoo mma mmeema mmienu.
“Na mfie aduannan akyi he, bɔfoɔ bi yii ne ho kyerɛɛ no Sinai Bepɔ serɛ he so, nwura bi a ɔɔdɛre mu.
Mose huiɛ he, ɔyɛɛ no nwanwa.
Na ɔtwe pinii ho sɛ ɔɔkɔhwɛ he, Awurade kasaa sɛ: “Me ne wo agyanom Nyankopɔn, Abraham Nyankopɔn, Isak Nyankopɔn, ne Yakob Nyankopɔn.” Mose ho hyɛɛ aseɛ sɛ ɔɔpopo nti wannya akokoɔduro sɛ ɔɔkɔ so ahwɛ adekorɔ he bio.
Na Awurade ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Worɔ wo mpaboa, na baabi a wogyina he yɛ kronkron.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, maahu amaneɛ a me nkurofoɔ a bɛya Misraim he oohu; na maate bɛ apinisie, na maaba sɛ meebɛgye bɛ.
Afei bra, na mensoma wo nkɔ Misraim.” “Ɔyɛ saa Mose yi ne bɛpoo no berɛ a bɛkaa sɛ, Hwane ne yii wo sɛ yɛ sodifoɔ ne temufoɔ?” Ɔno ne afei deɛ Nyankopɔn nam bɔfoɔ a oyii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ no nwuram hɔ he so ɔɔsoma no sɛ sodifoɔ ne gyefoɔ he.
Oyii bɛ, na ɔyɔɔ anwanwadeɛ ne nsɛnkyerɛnne pii Misriam, Mmɛwa Po he mu ne serɛ he so mfie aduannan.
Saa Mose yi ne ka kyerɛɛ Israelfoɔ sɛ, ‘Nyankopɔn beyi diyifoɔ bi a ɔte sɛ me afiri ho nuanom mu ama ho.’ Mose yiaa ne na ɔka bɔfoɔ a ɔkasa kyerɛɛ no Bepɔ Sinai so he ho a ɔbaa asafo he mu ne yɛ nananom nkyɛne serɛ so he, na onyaa nkwa nsɛm kronkron a ɔde bɛma ho.
Yɛ nananom anyɛ setie ama no, na mmom bɛpoo no, na bebenya a na nka bɛ ya Misraim, na bɛka kyerɛɛ Aaron sɛ, “Yɛ abosom ma yɛ ma benni yɛ anim.
Na Mose yi a odii yɛ anim firi Misraim asaase so he, yennim nea ato no.” Nti ɔyɔɔ nantwie ba honyini bi, na bɛbɔɔ afɔdeɛ maa no.
Na bɛgyee bɛ ani bɛ nsa ano nnwuma ho.
Na Nyankopɔn yii n’ani firii bɛ so, na ogyae bɛ ma bɛsom soro asafo, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ adiyifoɔ he nwoma mu he sɛ: ‘O Israel fie, ɔyɛ me ne hode afɔrebɔdeɛ ne ayɛyɛdeɛ braa me serɛ so mfie adaduannan he?
Daabi, mmom hofaa Molok ntomadane ne ho bosom Refan nsoromma, ahonyini a hoyɔeɛ sɛ hobɛsom bɛ; nti meyi ho akɔ Babel akyi nohoa.’ “Yɛ nananom nyaa adanseɛ ntomadane he serɛ he so, sɛnea ɔhyɛɛ Mose berɛ a ɔɔkasa akyerɛ no sɛ ɔnyɔ no sɛ nhwɛsodeɛ a ohuiɛ he.
Na yɛ nananom nsa kaa saa ntomadane yi he, bɛne Yosua de baa amanamane a Nyankopɔn pamoo bɛ firii yɛ nananom anim he asaase so.
Na bɛkora noaa de besii Dawid a, onyaa Nyankopɔn anim adom na obisaa akwannya a ɔde besi tenabea ama Israel Nyankopɔn, he berɛ so.
Nso ɔyɛ Salomo ne sii fie maa no.
Na asɛm he ne sɛ, Sorosoroni he nte fie a bɛde nnipa nsa ayɔ mu, sɛnea diyifoɔ he kaa sɛ, ‘Soro yɛ m’ahennwa, na asaase yɛ me nane ntiasoɔ.
Mmɛ fie ne hobesi ama me, Awurade ne aka, anaa he ne me homebea?’ Ɔnyɛ me nsa ne yɔɔ nnoɔma yi nyinaa anaa?
“Nnipa a hoasene ho kɔno, ho a bentwaa ho akoma ne ho aso twetia, hoko tia Honhom Kronkron daa te sɛ ho agyanom yɔeɛ he.
Adiyifoɔ he mu hwane ne ho agyanom antaa no?
Bekuu bɛ a bɛhyɛɛ nkɔm faa Kronkronni he mmaeɛ ho, na afei hoayi no ama bɛaku no.
Hone honyaa mmara he sɛnea abɔfoɔ de maeɛ he, nso hoanni so.
Bɛtee yeinom he ɔwowɔɔ bɛ akoma mu na bɛ ani beree paa tia Stefano.
Nso esiane sɛ Honhom Kronkron ahyɛ ne ma nti, ɔhwɛɛ soro gyee huu Nyankopɔn animuonyam ne Yesu sɛ ogyina Nyankopɔn nsa nifa, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Mehu sɛ soro abie a Nipa Ba he gyina Nyankopɔn nsa nifa.” Na bɛteateam dendene, de bɛ nsa sisii bɛ aso, na bɛ nyinaa gyee twi kɔɔ no so.
Na bɛde no firii kuro he mu he, befirii aseɛ sii no aboɔ.
Na adansefoɔ he de bɛ ntaadeɛ ngugusoɔ guu abranteɛ bi a bɛfrɛ no Saulo nane ase.
Na begu so oosi no aboɔ he ɔsrɛɛ sɛ, “Awurade Yesu, gye me honhom.” Afei, obuu nkotodwe de nne kɛseɛ teaam sɛ, “Awurade, mmu bɔne yi ntia bɛ.” Na ɔkaa saa he ogyaam.
Bɛtaa agyidifoɔ Saulo nso penee kuu a na beeku Stefano he so.
Saa da he taa kɛseɛ bi baa asafo a ɔya Yerusalem he so; na bɛ nyinaa bɔ hwetee Yudea ne Samaria nyinaa.
Na mmeema nyamesurofoɔ bi faa Stefano kosiee no, na besuu no pii.
Nso Saulo firii aseɛ tuu n’ani sii asafo he so.
Owurawuraa afie mu kɔtwee mmaa ne mmeema de bɛ koguu afiase.
Na afei bɛ a bɛabɔ ahwete he kyinii asaase he so pae mu kaa asɛmpa he.
Filipo kɔɔ Samaria kuro he mu na ofirii aseɛ pae mu kaa Agyenkwa he ho asɛm kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Berɛ a nnipakuo he tieeɛ na behuu nsɛnkyerɛnne a Filipo ɔɔyɔ he, bɛde akoma korɔ tiee no.
Na nnipa pii wɔ ahonhom fi, na ahonhom fi he de nne kɛseɛ teateam firii bɛ mu firiiɛ.
Afei nso, mmubuafoɔ ne mpakye pii nyaa ayaresa.
Nti anigyeɛ kɛseɛ baa saa kuro he mu.
Afei na beema bi ya kuro he mu a bɛfrɛ no Simon, a na oyi nkonyaa ma Samaria mane he ho dwirii bɛ, na ɔka sɛ ɔyɛ nipa kɛseɛ.
Na bɛ nyinaa, firi nkumaa so kosi akɛseɛ so tie no ka sɛ, “Yei ne Nyankopɔn Tumi a bɛfrɛ no Kɛseɛ.” Na bɛyɛɛ dinn tie no efiri sɛ na ɔnam nkonyaa so ama bɛ ho adwiri bɛ akyɛre.
Na afei, berɛ a bɛgyee Filipo a na ɔɔka Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho asɛmpa ne Yesu Kristo dini he diiɛ he, ɔbɔɔ bɛ asu, mmaa ne mmeema nyinaa.
Mpo Simon nso gye diiɛ.
Na bɛbɔɔ no asu wieeɛ he, na ɔtaa ne Filipo nante.
Na nsɛnkyerɛnne ne ahoɔdenneɛ a ohuiɛ he yɛɛ no ahodwiri.
Na afei asomafoɔ a bɛya Yerusalem tee sɛ Samariafoɔ agye Nyankopɔn asɛm he, bɛsomaa Petro ne Yohane kɔɔ bɛ nkyɛne.
Bɛ mmienu he kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ maa bɛ sɛ bɛ benya Honhom Kronkron he efiri sɛ obesi saa bere he na Honhom he mmaa bɛ mu biaa so; na mmom asu kɛkɛ na na bɛabɔ no Awurade Yesu dini mu.
Na afei Petro ne Yohane de bɛ nsa guu bɛ so, na benyaa Honhom Kronkron he.
Berɛ a Simon huu sɛ asomafoɔ he nsa a bɛde guu binom so he maa Honhom baa bɛ so he, ɔyɔɔ sɛ ɔɔma bɛ sika.
Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Homma me nso saa tumi yi bi sɛ ɔbɛyɛ na nipa biaa a mede me nsa begu ne so he benya Honhom Kronkron he.” Nso Petro ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wo ne wo sika nyinaa nsɛe, efiri sɛ wodwene sɛ wobetumi de sika atɔ Nyankopɔn akyɛdeɛ!
Wonni agyapadeɛ anaa kyɛfa ya asɛm yi mu, efiri sɛ w’akoma ntene Nyankopɔn anim.
Sakra w’adwene ya saa bɔne a woayɔ yi ho, na srɛ Awurade sɛ, sɛ ɔbeyɛyie a ɔmfa bɔne a woasusu no w’akoma mu he nkyɛ wo.
Na maahu sɛ woyɛ anibereɛ paa, na amumuyɔ ahyɛ wo so.
Simon buaa sɛ, Honsrɛ Awurade mma me, sɛ na nea hoaka he mu biaa amma me so.” Afei Petro ne Yohane dii adanseɛ na bɛkaa Awurade asɛm wieeɛ he, bɛsane kɔɔ Yerusalem, na bɛkaa asɛm pa he Samaria Nkuraa pii ase.
Afei Awurade bɔfoɔ bi ka kyerɛɛ Filipo sɛ, “Sɔre na kɔ anaafoɔ fam hɔ kwane a ofiri Yerusalem kɔ Gaza he.” (Yei yɛ serɛ so kwane).
Nti ɔsɔre kɔeɛ.
Na hwɛ, Etiopiani panyini bi a odi mu paa di.
Na ɔyɛ Etiopiafoɔ hemaa Kandake Fotosanfoɔ.
Na waaba Yerusalem akɔsom na ɔte ne teaseɛnam mu ɔɔsane akɔ a ɔɔkenkane diyifoɔ Yesaia nwoma he.
Nti Honhom he ka kyerɛɛ Filipo sɛ, “Twe bɛne teaseɛnam yi.” Nti Filipo tuu mirika kɔɔ ho na ɔtee sɛ ɔɔkenkane diyifoɔ Yesaia nwoma he; na obisaa sɛ, “Wote nea wookane yi ase?” Na obuaa sɛ, “Sɛ bi ankyerɛ me a; ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na mate aseɛ?” Na ɔtoo nsa frɛɛ Filipo sɛ ɔmmra teaseɛnam he mu mmɛtena ne nkyɛne.
Twerɛsɛm mu nsɛm a na ɔɔkane he di: “Bɛde no baeɛ sɛ dwane a beebeku no, na sɛnea dwammaa tɔ mum nea otwitwa ne ho nwi anim he, wammie n’ano.
Berɛ a bɛbrɛɛ no ase he, bebuu no ntɛnkyea.
Hwane ne ɔbɛkyerɛ n’abusua?
Efiri sɛ bɛafa ne nkwa afiri asaase so kɔ.” Etiopiani panyini he bisaa Filipo sɛ, “Mepa wo kyɛw, hwane ne diyifoɔ yi ɔɔka ne ho asɛm yi?
Ɔno ankasa anaa nipa foforɔ?” Na Filipo biee n’ano, na ogyinaa saa twerɛsɛm heaa so kaa Yesu ho asɛm kyerɛɛ no.
Na bɛnam kwane so ɔɔkɔ he, beduruu nsuo bi ho.
Na Etiopiani he kaa sɛ, “Hwɛ, nsuo di!
Ɛɛne ne si me asubɔ ho kwane?” [ Na Filipo kaa sɛ, “Sɛ wode w’akoma nyinaa gye di a adeɛ biaa nsi wo kwane.” Na Etiopiani he kaa sɛ, “Megye di sɛ Yesu Kristo yɛ Nyankopɔn Ba.”] Na Filipo maa teaseɛnam he gyinaeɛ, na Filipo ne Etiopiani panyini he, siane kɔɔ nsuo he mu, na Filipo bɔɔ no asu.
Na berɛ a befiri nsuo he mu pieeɛ he, Awurade Honhom hwim Filipo kɔeɛ, na Etiopiani he anhu no bio, na ɔde anigyeɛ kɔɔ ne kwane.
Na Filipo kopiee Asdod, na ɔkɔfaa asaase he so toaa so pae mu kaa asɛmpa he kyerɛɛ nkuro he nyinaa kosii sɛ oduruu Kaesarea.
Saulo adwensakra Na Saulo a na ɔda so hunahuna Awurade asuafoɔ he na ɔpɛ sɛ okuku bɛ he kɔɔ sɔfo panyini he nkyɛne kɔkaa sɛ ɔmma no nkrataa a ɔde bɛkɔ Damasko hyia adane mu, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a obetumi akye biaa a obehu sɛ ɔnam gyidie Kwane He so, mmeema ne mmaa, de bɛ aba Yerusalem.
Afei ɔnam kwane he so ɔɔkɔ a ɔbene Damasko he, mpofiremuaa hann bi firi soro hyerɛn twaa ne ho hyiaeɛ.
Na ɔhwee fam, na ɔtee sɛ nne bi ɔɔka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Saulo, Saulo, mmɛ nti ne wotaa me?” Obisaa sɛ, “Wo ne hwane, owura?” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Me ne Yesu, nea wootaa no he.
Sɔre kɔ kuro he mu na bɛbɛka nea ɔsɛ sɛ woyɔ akyerɛ wo.” Na mmeema a bɛne no nam he gyinagyina hɔ a bentumi nkasa.
Nne he faa bɛ asum deɛ nso bɛanhu biaa.
Saulo sɔre firii fam, na n’ani gu so deɛ, nso na onhu hwee.
Nti bɛsosɔɔ ne nsa de no kɔɔ Damasko.
Na wanhu hwee nnansa, wannidi na wannom nso.
Na suani bi ya Damasko a bɛfrɛ no Anania, na Awurade ka kyerɛɛ no anisoadehunu mu sɛ, “Anania” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Awurade medi.” Awurade ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Sɔre na kɔ brɔno a bɛfrɛ no Tee he so, na kɔ Yuda fie kɔhwehwɛ beema bi a bɛfrɛ no Saulo, a ofiri Tarso he.
Na hwɛ, ɔɔbɔ mpaeɛ, na waahu beema bi a bɛfrɛ no Anania ya anisoadehunu mu sɛ waba de ne nsa abegu no so sɛnea obehu adeɛ bio” Nso Anania buaa sɛ, “Awurade maate beema yi ho asɛm afiri nnipa pii hɔ, sɛ ɔde bɔne bebree adi w’ahoteefoɔ a bɛya Yerusalem he.
Afei waanya tumi afiri asɔfoɔ mpanyini he nkyɛne sɛ ɔmfa bɛ a bɛbɔ wo dini he nyinaa ngu mpokyerɛ mu.” Na Awurade ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Si kwane so kɔ, efiri sɛ beema yi ne nea mayi sɛ ɔmfa me dini nkɔ amanamane ne ahene ne Israel mma nkyɛne.
Na m’ankasa mɛkyerɛ no amaneɛ a otwa sɛ ɔba no so ɔnam me dini nti.” Nti Anania kɔeɛ na ɔhyɛne fie he mu, na ɔde ne nsa guu no so kaa sɛ, “Me nua Saulo, Awurade Yesu a oyii ne ho adi kyerɛɛ wo kwane a na wonam so ɔɔba so he ne asoma me, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a wobehu adeɛ bio na Honhom Kronkron ahyɛ wo ma.” Na amonom hɔaa bibi a ɔte sɛ ntɛ fifiri n’ani so guu fam na ohuu adeɛ, na ɔsɔree ma bɛbɔɔ no asu, na odidii nyaa ahoɔdene.
Na odii nna kakra asuafoɔ a bɛya Damasko he nkyɛne.
Saulo kaa asɛm ya Damasko Na ntɛmaa ofirii aseɛ hyia adane mu kaa Yesu ho asɛm sɛ “Yesu ne Nyankopɔn Ba he.” Nso ɔyɛɛ bɛ a beetie no he nyinaa nwanwa, na bɛkaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ yei na ɔsɛe bɛ a bɛbɔ dini yi Yerusalem he?
Ɔnyɛ ɔno ne ɔde botaeɛ koro heaa baa ha sɛ ɔɔbɛkye bɛ de bɛ akɔma asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ he?” Nso Saulo kɔɔ so nyaa ahoɔdene, na ɔmaa Yudafoɔ a bɛya Damasko he ho dwirii bɛ berɛ a ɔde adanseɛ a mu da hɔ kyerɛeɛ sɛ yei ne Kristo he.
Na nna pii akyi he, Yudafoɔ he bɔɔ pɔ sɛ bebeku no.
Nso Saulo huu sɛ bɛabɔ ne ho pɔ.
Na bio nso na bɛwɛne apono he ano awia ne anadwo sɛ bebenya no aku no.
Nti n’asuafoɔ he faa no anadwo he de no sii kɛntɛne mu de no faa kwane bi a ɔda afasuo he mu, gyaagyaa no nkakrankakra sii fam.
Saulo kɔɔ Yerusalem, Kaesarea ne Tarso Oduruu Yerusalem he, ɔbɔɔ mmɔdene sɛ ɔde ne ho bɛbɔ asuafoɔ he; nso na bɛ nyinaa besuro no, efiri sɛ na bɛnnye nni sɛ ɔyɛ suani nɔkorem.
Nti Barnaba boaa no de no kɔɔ asomafoɔ he nkyɛne, na ɔkaa sɛnea ɔde akokoɔduro akasa Yesu dini mu Damasko he ho nsɛm nyinaa kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Na ɔne bɛ tenae, dii akɔneaba Yerusalem, kasaa Awurade dini mu akokoɔduro so.
Na ɔne Yudafoɔ a bɛka Hela kasa he kasa dii anobaabaeɛ.
Na bɛbɔɔ mmɔdene sɛ bebeku no.
Berɛ a agyidifoɔ he huu yei he, bɛde no baa Kaesarea; na bɛmaa no kɔɔ Tarso.
Saa berɛ heaa mu asafo a ɔyeya Yudea ne Galilea ne Samaria nyinaa nyaa asomdwie, na bɛyɛɛ nam.
Na bere a bɛde Awurade suro ne Honhom Kronkron he awerekyekyerɛ nanteeɛ he, bɛkɔɔ so dɔreeɛ.
Petro saa Aenea yadeɛ Afei bere a Petro ookyinikyini mmeammea he, okoduruu ahoteefoɔ a bɛte Lida he nso nkyɛne.
Hɔ ne ohuu beema bi a bɛfrɛ no Aenia a wabubu ada ne mpa so mfie nwɔtwe.
Na Petro ka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Aenia, Yesu Kristo asa wo yadeɛ.
Sɔre na woaa sɛ wo kɛtɛ.” Na ntɛmaa ɔsɔreeɛ.
Na bɛ a bɛtete Lida ne Saron asaasetam so nyinaa huu no, na bɛdane baa Awurade nkyɛne.
Tabita wunyaneeɛ Na suani bi ya Yopa a bɛfrɛ no Tabita, a Helafoɔ ka no Doka.
Na nnwuma pa ne adɔeɛ ahyɛ no ma.
Na nna he mu he, ɔbaa sɛ ɔyare wuiɛ.
Nti bedwaree no de no kɔtoo dane bi mu ya abrosane so.
Na afei na hɔ bɛne Yopa nti, berɛ a asuafoɔ he tee sɛ Petro ya saa kuro he mu he, bɛsomaa mmeema mmienu kɔɔ ne nkyɛne kɔsrɛɛ no sɛ, “Yɛsrɛ wo ntwentwɛne wo nane ase sɛ wobɛba yɛ nkyɛne.” Na Petro sɔre ne bɛ kɔeɛ.
Na oduruu hɔ he, bɛde no kɔɔ dane he mu abrosane he so; na akunafoɔ he nyinaa de suu baa ne nkyɛne de ntaadeɛ nhyɛaseɛ ne ntaadeɛ ngugusoɔ a Doka yɔeɛ berɛ a ɔya bɛ nkyɛne he bebree kyerɛeɛ.
Na Petro maa biaa pie kɔɔ abɔntene, na obuu nkotodwe bɔɔ mpaeɛ, na ɔdanee ne ho hwɛɛ amu he kaa sɛ, “Tabita, sɔre!” Obiee n’ani, na n’ani bɔɔ Petro so he, ɔsɔre tenaa ase.
Ɔtenee ne nsa na ɔmaa no so, na ɔfrɛɛ ahoteefoɔ ne akunafoɔ he de Doka maa bɛ a ɔya nkwa mu.
Asɛm yo trɛɛ Yopa mpɔtamu nyinaa sɛ wanyane afiri awufoɔ mu, na bebree begyee Awurade diiɛ.
Petro tenaa Yopa dii nna kakra Simon, nhomahyɛfoɔ no nkyɛne.
Petro ne Kornelio Na beema bi ya Kaesarea a bɛfrɛ no Konelio, a ɔyɛ Italia asrafodɔm ha so panyini.
Na ɔyɛ nipa a ɔwɔ ahofama na ɔne ne fiefoɔ nyinaa suro Nyankopɔn, na ɔyɛ nkurofoɔ adɔeɛ pii na ɔde adesrɛ to Nyankopɔn anim daa.
Bɛyɛ awia nnɔn mmeɛnsa berɛ mu he, ohuu Nyankopɔn bɔfoɔ pefee anisoadehunu mu sɛ waba ne nkyɛne na ɔɔfrɛɛ no sɛ, “Konelio.” Beema he hwɛɛ no dinn, na hu kaa no ma obisaa sɛ, “Awurade, ɛɛne a?” Obuaa sɛ, “Wo mpaebɔ ne w’adɔeɛ aforo soro ayɛ nkaeɛ Nyankopɔn anim.
Nti afei soma mmeema ma bɛnkɔ Yopa nkɔfrɛ Simon a bɛfrɛ no Petro he mmra.
Saa beema yi akɔsoeɛ nwomahyɛni bi a ɔde Simon a ne fie ya po he ano.” Berɛ a bɔfoɔ a ɔne no kasaeɛ he kɔeɛaa pɛ, ɔfrɛɛ ne fie nkoa mmienu ne sraani bi a ɔwɔ ahofama firii bɛ a bɛsom no daa he mu, na ɔkaa bibiaa kyerɛɛ bɛ somaa bɛ kɔɔ Yopa.
Adeɛ kyeeɛ a bɛnam kwane so ɔɔkɔ na bɛɛyɛ aduru kuro he mu he, Petro kɔɔ dane he atifi bɛyɛ awia dummienu berɛ mu kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ.
Afei kɔm dee no paa ma ɔpɛɛ sɛ odidi.
Berɛ a begu so ɔɔyɛ aduane he, onyaa anisoadehunu na ohuu sɛ soro abie na adeɛ bi a ɔte sɛ nwera ntoma kɛseɛ bi oosiane firi soro ɔɔba asaase so te sɛ nea nnipa binom kitakita anoano nnan he na beegyaagyaa mu.
Na ntɔteboa ne mmoa a bɛwea asaase so ne wiem nnomaa nyinaa bi yam.
Na ɔtee nne bi sɛ, “Petro, sɔre ku bi na di!” Nso Petro kaa sɛ, “Daabi da, Awurade, efiri sɛ mennii bibi a ho agu fi anaa ho nte biaa da.” Na nne he ka kyerɛɛ no ne mprenu so sɛ, “Mfrɛ nnoɔma a Nyankopɔn ate ho sɛ ho agu fi.” Yei baa ne mprɛnsa so, na hɔaa bɛfaa adeɛ a ɔte sɛ nwera he kɔɔ soro.
Afei berɛ a anisoadehunu he nti na Petro tim ayɛ no kesenenee he, hwɛ, na mmeema a Konelio somaa bɛ he abisabisa Simon fie kwane ma bɛabegyina pono he ano.
Na bɛfrɛ bisaa sɛ ebia Simon a bɛfrɛ no Petro he abɛsoeɛ hɔ.
Berɛ a Petro gu so ɔɔdwennwene anisoadehunu he ho he, Honhom he kaa sɛ, “Hwɛ, nnipa mmeɛnsa bi ɔɔhwehwɛ wo.
Wo deɛ, sɔre, si fam na wo ne bɛ nkɔ berɛ a wontwentwɛne wo nane ase, efiri sɛ me ne m’asoma bɛ.” Nti Petro sii fam kɔɔ mmeema he nkyɛne kɔkaa sɛ, “Hwɛ, mene nea hoohwehwɛ no he.
Ɛɛne nti ne ho baa ha?” Bɛkaa sɛ, “Bɔfoɔ kronkron bi de Nyankopɔn akwankyerɛ maa Konelio, asraafoɔ ha so hwɛfoɔ, teneneeni a osuro Nyankopɔn, a Yudafoɔ nyinaa bɔ no dini pa he sɛ ɔnsoma ma bɛmmɛfa wo mmra ne fie na ontie nea wowɔ ka.” Nti ɔde bɛ baa fie na ɔsom bɛ sɛ ahohoɔ.
Adeɛ kyeeɛ he ɔsɔre ne bɛ kɔeɛ, na agyidifoɔ binom a befiri Yopa ka bɛ ho.
Da a odi hɔ he, oduruu Kaesarea.
Na Konelio nso afrɛfrɛ n’abusuafoɔ ne ne nnamfonom nyinaa ɔɔtwɛne bɛ.
Berɛ a Petro piee hɔ he, Konelio kohyiaa no hwee ne nane ase sɔree no.
Nso Petro maa no so kaa sɛ, “Sɔre; me nso meyɛ nipa te sɛ woaa.” Na berɛ a ɔne no gu so ɔɔbɔ nkɔmmɔ he, ɔkɔɔ fie he mu kohuu sɛ nnipa bebree ahyiam, na ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Ho ankasa honim pefee sɛ mmara mma kwane sɛ Yudani ne abusua foforɔ munii bɛbɔ anaa ɔbɛbɛne no, nso Nyankopɔn akyerɛ me sɛ ɔnsɛ sɛ mefrɛ nipa biaa sɛ ne ho agu fi anaa ne ho nte.
Ne saa nti bere a bɛsoma bɛfrɛɛ me he, manyi ano koraa ne mebaeɛ.
Afei, mmɛ nti ne hosoma ma bɛfrɛɛ me.” Na Konelio kaa sɛ, “Nnannan di, saa berɛ yi muaa, na meya me fie awia nnɔn mmeɛnsa berɛ mu ɔɔbɔ mpaeɛ, na hwɛ, beema bi a ɔhyɛ ataadeɛ hyerɛnhyerɛn begyinaa m’anim.
Na ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Konelio Nyankopɔn atie wo mpaebɔ na w’adɔeɛ aduru n’anim.
Nti soma kɔ Yopa kɔfrɛ Simon a bɛfrɛ no Petro he.
Saa beema yi abɛsoeɛ Simon a ɔyɛ nwomahyɛni he fie po he ano.’ Nti ntɛmaa na mesoma ma bɛbaa wo nkyɛne, na woabɔ mmɔdene sɛ woaba.
Yei nti yɛ nyinaa ahyiam Nyankopɔn anim saa bere yi sɛ yeebetie nea Awurade ahyɛ wo sɛ ka nyinaa.” Na Petro biee n’ano kaa sɛ, “Nɔkwasɛm di, maahu sɛ Nyankopɔn nyɛ nyiyimu, na mmom mane biaa mu he, nipa a osuro no na ɔyɔ adetenenee he, ɔgye no tom.
Ɔde asɛm he kɔmaa Israel mma, na ɔkaa asomdwie a ɔnam Yesu Kristo so ba he ho asɛm pa kyerɛɛ bɛ, yei ne nnipa nyinaa wura.
Saa asɛm yi trɛɛ Yudea nyinaa, ofiri aseɛ Galilea berɛ a Yohane kaa asubɔ ho asɛm he akyi.
Yesu Nasareni he, Nyankopɔn de Honhom Kronkron ne tumi hyɛɛ no ma, na okyinikyinii asaase he so yɔɔ papa, na ɔsaa bɛ a Bronsam hyɛ bɛ so nyinaa yadeɛ, efiri sɛ na Nyankopɔn ka ne ho.
Yɛyɛ nnwuma a ɔyɔeɛ ya Yudea ne Yerusalem nyinaa ho adansefoɔ.
Bɛde no sɛnee asennua so kuu no.
Nso Nyankopɔn nyanee no da a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa na ɔmaa no kwane sɛ onyi ne ho adi nkyerɛ, ɔnyɛ nnipa nyinaa, na mmom bɛ a Nyankopɔn ayi bɛ sɛ adansefoɔ he, na ne wusɔreɛ akyi he bɛ ne no didiiɛ, na bɛnomeeɛ.
Ɔhyɛɛ yɛ sɛ yɛnka nkyerɛ mane he na yenni adanseɛ sɛ ɔno ne Nyankopɔn ayi no sɛ ateasefoɔ ne awufoɔ nyinaa temmufoɔ.
Adiyifoɔ he nyinaa dii ne ho adanseɛ sɛ biaa a ɔgye no di he benya bɔne fakyɛ ne dini mu.” Petro gu so ɔɔkasa he, Honhom Kronkron siane baa bɛ a bɛtee asɛm he nyinaa so.
Agyidifoɔ a bɛatwa bɛ twetia a na bɛ ne Petro nam he ho dwirii bɛ sɛ akyɛdeɛ a ɔyɛ Honhom Kronkron he asiane agu amanamane mufoɔ mpo so, efiri sɛ, bɛtee sɛ bɛɛka kasa foforɔ na beeyi Nyankopɔn ayɛ.
Na Petro bisaa sɛ, “Hwane ne betumi asi yeinom a bɛanya Honhom Kronkron sɛ yɛaa yi ho kwane sɛ yɛmfa nsuo mmɔ bɛ asu?” Nti ɔhyɛɛ ma bɛbɔɔ bɛ asu Yesu Kristo dini mu.
Afei bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ onni nna kakra bɛ nkyɛne.
Petro bɔɔ amanneɛ kyerɛɛ Yerusalem asɔre he Afei asomafoɔ he ne agyidifoɔ a bɛya Yudea he tee sɛ amanamane mufoɔ he nso agye Nyankopɔn asɛm.
Nti berɛ a Petro baa Yerusalem he, bɛ a bekura twetiatwa nhyehyɛeɛ mu he kasakasaeɛ sɛ, “Ɛɛne nti ne wokɔɔ bɛ a bentwaa bɛ twetia fie ne bɛ kodidiiɛ yi?” Na Petro hyɛɛ aseɛ kyerɛkyerɛɛ nsɛm he mu mmaako mmaako kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Na meya Yopa kuro mu ɔɔbɔ mpaeɛ, na afei bibi tɔɔ me so ma menyaa anisoadehunu bi, adeɛ bi a ɔte sɛ nwera ntoma kɛseɛ bi siane firii soro baa asaase so te sɛ nea nnipa binom kita anoano nnan he na beegyaagyaa mu, na ɔbɛnee me.
Mehwɛɛ mu he, mehuu asaase so ntɔteboa ne nkekaboa ne mmoa a bɛwea ne wiem nnomaa.
Afei metee sɛ nne bi dɛ, ‘Petro, sɔre ku bi na di.’ Na mekaa sɛ, ‘Daabi da, Awurade, efiri sɛ mennii bibiaa ho agu fi anaa ho nte da.’ Nso ne mprenu so he, nne he kasa firii soro sɛ, ‘Nea Nyankopɔn ate ho he, ɔnsɛ sɛ wofrɛ no sɛ ho agu fi.’ Yei sii mprɛnsa, na afei bɛtwee bibiaa sane kɔɔ soro.
Saa berɛ heaa, mmeema mmeɛnsa a bɛasoma bɛ firi Kaesarea sɛ bɛmmra me nkyɛne begyinaa fie a yɛte mu he aboboɔ ano.
Nti Honhom he ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ me ne bɛ nkɔ, menntwentwɛne me nane ase koraa.
Na anuanom nsia yi nso ne me kɔeɛ, na yɛhyɛne beema he fie.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ yɛ sɛ, ohuu bɔfoɔ sɛ ogyina ne fie a ɔɔka sɛ, ‘Soma nnipa kɔ Yopa ma bɛnkɔfrɛ Simon a bɛfrɛ no Petro he mmra, na ɔbɛka nea ɔbɛma bɛagye wo ne wo fiefoɔ nyinaa nkwa akyerɛ wo.’ Na bere a mefirii aseɛ sɛ meekasa he, Honhom Kronkron baa bɛ so sɛnea yɛ nso ɔbaa yɛ so mfitiaseɛ he.
Na mekae Awurade asɛm he, sɛnea na ɔtaa ka sɛ, ‘Yohane deɛ, ɔde nsuo ne bɔɔ asu, nso ho deɛ bɛde Honhom kronkron ne bɛbɔ ho asu.’ Nti sɛ Nyankopɔn maa bɛ akyɛdeɛ korɔ heaa sɛnea ɔmaa yɛ a yɛagye Awurade Yesu Kristo adi he a, mene hwane a metumi asi Nyankopɔn kwane?” Bɛtee yei he, bɛgye toom.
Na beyii Nyankopɔn ayɛ sɛ, “Hedeɛ Nyankopɔn ama amanamane mufoɔ nso anya adwensakra a ɔkɔ nkwa mu.” Amanamane mu asafo a odi kane Afei bɛ a ahohiahia a ɔnam Stefano so baeɛ he maa bɛbɔ hweteeɛ he kɔeɛaa kɔfaa Foinike ne Kipro ne Antiokia, nso bɛanka asɛm he ankyerɛ biaa sɛ Yudafoɔ nkoaa.
Na binom ya bɛ mu a bɛyɛ Kiprofoɔ ne Kirenefoɔ a bɛaba Antiokia.
Saa nnipa yi pae mu kaa Yesu ho asɛmpa kyerɛɛ nnipa a bɛka Hela kasa he.
Na Awurade nsa ya bɛ so, na nnipa pii bɛyɛɛ agyidifoɔ dane baa Awurade nkyɛne.
Bɛ ho asɛm duruu asafo a ɔya Yerusalem he nkyɛne, na bɛsomaa Barnaba kɔɔ Antiokia.
Berɛ a oduruu hɔ na ohuu Nyankopɔn adom he, odii ahurusie na ofiri aseɛ hyɛɛ bɛ nyinaa nkurane sɛ bɛnkɔ so mfa akoma a onhinhim ntena Awurade mu daa.
Na ɔyɛ nipa pa na Honhom Kronkron ne gyidie ayɛ no ma.
Na nnipadɔm gyee Awurade diiɛ.
Na afei Barnaba kɔɔ Tarso kɔhwehwɛɛ Saulo, na ohuu no he, ɔde no baa Antiokia.
Nti ɔbaa sɛ afe mũ he nyinaa he, bɛne asafo he hyia, na bɛkyerɛkyerɛɛ nnipadɔm pii, na Antiokia ne bedii kane frɛɛ asuafoɔ he Akristofoɔ.
Saa nna he mu he, adiyifoɔ firi Yerusalem baa Antiokia.
Bɛ mu baako a bɛfrɛ no Agabo sɔreeɛ, na ɔnam Honhom so hyɛɛ nkɔm sɛ kɔm kɛseɛ bi ɔɔba asaase nyinaa so, na nkɔmhyɛ yi baa mu Klaudio berɛ so.
Nti asuafoɔ he nyinaa bɔɔ bɛ adwene pɔ sɛ bɛde nnoɔma biaa bebetumi ayi bɛkɔ akɔsom agyidifoɔ a bɛya Yudea he, na bɛyɔɔ saa, somaa Barnaba ne Saulo ma bɛde kɔmaa mpanyimfoɔ he.
Bɛde Petro too afiase Saa berɛ he a mu ne hene Herode tuu n’ani sii nnipa a bɛya asafo he mu binom so dii bɛ ani.
Ɔmaa bɛde sekane kuu Yohane nua Yakobo.
Na ohuu sɛ nea wayɔ he asɔ Yudafoɔ he ani he, ɔkɔkyee Petro nso.
(Na saa bere he yɛ bere a bedi paanoo a mmɔreka nnim.)
Na ne nsa kaa no he, ɔde no too afiase de no hyɛɛ akuo nnan a asraafoɔ nnan ya mu biaa mu nsa sɛ bɛnwɛne no nnidisoɔ nnidisoɔ, a na wayɛ n’adwene sɛ, Twam Afahyɛ he akyi he, ɔde no bɛma nkurofoɔ he.
Berɛ a Petro da afiase he, asafo he bɔɔ mpaeɛ aniberɛ so kyerɛɛ Nyankopɔn maa no.
Saa anadwo heaa a Herode de Petro ɔɔbɛma nkurofoɔ he, na Petro da asraafoɔ mmienu ntam a nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn mmienu gu ne nsa, na awɛmfoɔ ya pono he ano ɔɔbɔ deduafie he ho bane.
Mpofiremuaa Awurade bɔfoɔ yii ne ho adi na hann bi hyerɛnn afiase dane he mu.
Ɔbɔɔ Petro nkyɛne mu nyanee no kaa sɛ, “Sɔre ntɛm.” Na ne nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn he firii ne nsa guu fam.
Bɔfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Bɔ w’abɔsoɔ na hyɛ wo mpaboa.” Na Petro yɔɔ saa.
Afei ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Fa wo ntoma he kyekyere wo ho na di m’akyi.” Petro pie dii n’akyi, na wanhu sɛ nea na bɔfoɔ he ɔɔboa no ama no ayɔ he yɛ asɛm paa, na ɔdwene sɛ ɔyɛ anisoadehunu.
Na betwaam awɛmfoɔ agyinaeɛ a odi kane ne nea ɔtɔ so mmienu koduruu dadeɛ pono a ɔkɔ kuro he mu he ano he, ɔno ankasa biee maa bɛ.
Na bepieeɛ he, bekosii tenpono baako so, na hɔaa bɔfoɔ he gyaa no hɔ kɔeɛ.
Na Petro ani baa ne ho so he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Afei ne mahu sɛ Awurade ankasa ne somaa ne bɔfoɔ beyii me firii Herode nsam ne nea na Yudafoɔ he ani da so sɛ bɛde bɛyɔ me nyinaa mu.” Asafo he anigyeɛ Na ohuu yei he, ntɛmaa ɔkɔɔ Yohane a na ɔsane de Marko he maame Maria fie.
Na nnipa pii ahyia hɔ ɔɔbɔ mpaeɛ.
Bere a ɔbɔɔ abɔntene pono he mu he, abaawa bi a bɛfrɛ no Rode baeɛ.
Na ɔtee Petro nne he, anigyeɛ nti, wammie pono he na mmom otuu mmirika kɔbɔɔ amaneɛ sɛ Petro gyina pono he akyi.
Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “W’adwene mu ka wo!” Nso ɔkɔɔ so kaa sɛ asɛm he yɛ nɔkorɛ.
Na bɛkaa sɛ, “ɔyɛ Petro samane.” Afei Petro kɔɔ soaa bɔɔ pono he mu, na bebiee no.
Behuu no he, bɛ ho dwirii bɛ.
Na ɔde ne nsa yɔɔ nsɛnkyerɛnee kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛnyɛ dinn.
Na ɔkyerɛɛ bɛ kwane a Awurade nam so yii no firii afiase hɔ.
Na ɔkaa bio nso sɛ, “Honkɔka yei nkyerɛ Yakobo ne agyidifoɔ he.” Na ofirii hɔ kɔɔ baabi foforɔ.
Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, nea na asi fa Petro ho he nti, asraafoɔ he ani so yɛɛ krakrakrakra.
Berɛ a Herode hwehwɛeɛ na wanhu Petro he, obisabisa awɛmfoɔ he nea osiiɛ, na ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa bɛ nkɔku bɛ.
Na Herode firii Yudea kɔɔ Kaesarea kodii nna kakra ya hɔ.
Herode wuo a oo’hu Afei nso Herode ani beree Tirofoɔ ne Sidonfoɔ so.
Nti bɛyɛɛ anokorɔ baa ne nkyɛne, na berɛ a bɛmaa Blasto a ɔhwɛ hene daberɛ so tee bɛ aseɛ he, befirii aseɛ srɛɛ hwehwɛɛ asomdwie, efiri sɛ na hene he asaase so na mane he nya bɛ aduane.
Na da a bɛahyɛ he duriiɛ he, Herode de ahentaadeɛ hyehyɛɛ ne ho, na ɔtenaa atemmuo adwa so firi aseɛ kasa kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Nkurofoɔ a bɛahyiam he nso firii aseɛ teateaam sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ nipa nne di, na mmom ɔyɛ nyame bi nne!” Hɔaa ne Awurade bɔfoɔ bɔɔ no, efiri sɛ wamfa animuonyam amma Nyankopɔn, na ɔdɔree mmoa wuiɛ.
Barnaba ne Saulo sane baa Antiokia Nso Awurade asɛm nyaa nkɔsoɔ na ɔtrɛɛe.
Na Barnaba ne Saulo wiee bɛ dwumadie he, bɛsane baa Yerusalem bɛfaa Yohane a bɛfrɛ no Marko he kaa bɛ ho sane baeɛ.
Bɛsomaa Barnaba ne Saulo Antiokia asafo he mu he, na adiyifoɔ ne akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ ya mu, Barnaba ne Simeon a bɛfrɛ no Niger he, ne Lukio a ofiri Kirene, ne Manaen a bɛtetee ɔne Herode a ɔyɛ mantam sodifoɔ he, ne Saulo.
Berɛ a bɛɛsom Awurade na bɛɛyɔ akɔmkyene he, Honhom Kronkron he kaa sɛ, “Honyi Barnaba ne Saulo mma me, na bɛnkɔ yɔ adwuma a mafrɛ bɛ sɛ bɛmmɛyɔ he.” Na bɛyɔɔ akɔmkyene wieeɛ a bɛbɔɔ mpaeɛ he, bɛde bɛ nsa guu bɛ so gyaa bɛ kwane.
Nti, saa mmeema yi a Honhom Kronkron asoma bɛ he kɔɔ Seleukia, na befirii hɔ de po so hyɛne kɔɔ Kipro.
Berɛ a beduru Salami he, befirii aseɛ bɔɔ Nyankopɔn asɛm he dawuro Yudafoɔ hyia adane mu.
Na Yohane boaa bɛ bɛ dwumadie mu.
Sergio Paulo ne Elima Berɛ a bɛfaa supɔ he so koduruu Pafo he, behyiaa Yudani beema bi a ɔyɛ nkonyaayifoɔ, diyifoɔ torɔfoɔ bi a bɛfrɛ no Bar-Yesu, na ɔya Amrado Sergio Paulo a ɔyɛ nyansani he nkyɛne.
Berɛ a bɛfrɛɛ Barnaba ne Saulo maa no he, amrado he hwehwɛɛ sɛ ɔbɛte Nyankopɔn asɛm.
Nso na nkonyaayifoɔ Elima (a Hela kasaa mu bɛfrɛ no Bar-Yesu) ya hɔ; ofirii aseɛ ne bɛ dii asie, pɛɛ sɛ ɔdane amrado he firi gyidie he ho.
Afei Saulo a na bɛsane frɛ no Paulo a na Honhom Kronkron ahyɛ no ma he hwɛɛ no gyee kaa sɛ, “Wo, beema a asisie ahyɛ wo ma, Bronsam ba, a wotane tenenee nyinaa, wonnyae sɛ wokyea Awurade kwane a ɔtene he?
Afei tie!
Awurade nsa ya me so, na w’ani befira, a wonhu awia hann kosi berɛ bi.” Amonom hɔaa Bar-Yesu ani so yɛɛ no kusuu na sum duruu no, na okyini hwehwɛɛ nnipa a bɛbɛsɔ ne nsa akyerɛ no kwane.
Afei berɛ a amrado he huu nea asi he, ɔgye diiɛ, efiri sɛ Awurade ho nkyerɛkyerɛ he yɛɛ no ahodwiri.
Afei mmeema he ne Paulo faa po so firii Pafo kɔɔ Perge a ɔya Pamfilia.
Na Yohane deɛ, ɔne bɛ dii ntete mu sane kɔɔ Yerusalem.
Nso bɛde bɛ firii Perge baa Antiokia a ɔya Pisidia, na bɛkɔɔ hyiadane mu homeda kɔtenaa ase.
Bɛkenkanee mmara ne adiyifoɔ he badwam wieeɛ he, hyiadane mu mpanyimfoɔ he somaa nnipa kɔɔ bɛ nkyɛne sɛ, “Anuanom, sɛ howɔ nkuranhyɛsɛm bi ma nnipa yi a, honka.” Nti Paulo sɔre nyam ne nsa kaa sɛ: “Ho Israelfoɔ ne ho a hosuro Nyankopɔn, hontie!
Israel mane yi, Nyankopɔn yii yɛ agyanom, na ɔmaa bɛ so berɛ a na bɛyɛ ahɔhoɔ Misraim asaase so he nam ne tumi so yii bɛ firii hɔ.
Na bɛyɛ mfie aduannan mu he, onyaa bɛ nneyɔeɛ ho aboterɛ serɛ he so.
Na ɔsɛee amane nson Kanaan asaase so akyi he, ɔkyekyɛɛ asaase he de maa bɛ sɛ bɛ agyapadeɛ; ne nyinaa sii bɛyɛ mfie ahanan aduonum mu.
Na yeinom akyi he, ɔmaa bɛ atemmufoɔ de besii diyifoɔ Samuel so.
Na ofiri ɔno so he, bebisaa hene, na Nyankopɔn de Kis ba Saulo, beema a ofiri Benyamin abusua mu, maa bɛ mfie aduannan.
Na oyii no firi hɔ, na ɔde Dawid bɛyɛɛ bɛ hene, na odii ne ho adanseɛ kaa sɛ, ‘Maahu Yisai ba Dawid, beema a ɔda m’akoma so, ɔno ne bɛyɔ nea mepɛ nyinaa.’ Saa beema yi aseni ne Yesu a Nyankopɔn yii no maa Israel sɛ Agyenkwa, sɛnea ne bɔhyɛ teɛ he.
Yohane a odii Yesu anim baeɛ he kaa asubɔ a ɔyɛ adwensakra ho nsɛnkyerɛnne ho asɛm badwam kyerɛɛ Israelfoɔ nyinaa.
Na berɛ a Yohane dwumadie ɔɔba awieeɛ he, ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Hosusu sɛ me ne Agyenkwa he anaa?
Ɔnnyɛ me ne no.
Nso, hwɛ, bi di m’akyi ɔɔba a memfata sɛ mesane ne nane ase mpaboa mpo.’ “Me nuanom, Abraham asefoɔ ne bɛ a besuro Nyankopɔn, yɛ ne bɛde nkwagyeɛ yi ho asɛm abra yɛ.
Na osiane sɛ bɛ a bɛtete Yerusalem ne bɛ sodifoɔ he anhu no na bɛante adiyifoɔ he nsɛm a bɛkenkanee no Homeda biaa he ase nti, bebuu no fɔ maa adiyifoɔ he nsɛm he baa mu.
Na bɛanhu hwee a ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔsɛ wuo deɛ, nso bɛkaa sɛ Pilato mma benku no.
Afei, berɛ a bɛyɔɔ nea bɛatwerɛ afa ne ho nyinaa wieeɛ he, beyii no firii asennua he so de no too adamena mu.
Nso Nyankopɔn nyanee no firii awufoɔ mu; na bɛ a bɛne no firi Galilea kɔɔ Yerusalem he huu no nna pii, na seesei bedi ne ho adanseɛ kyerɛ nkurofoɔ.
Ɔno nti, yɛɛka bɔhyɛ a bɛde maa nananom he ho asɛm akyerɛ ho, sɛ Nyankopɔn ama aba mu koraa ama yɛ a yɛyɛ bɛ mma he, efiri sɛ wanyane Yesu, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ ya Dwom a ɔtɔ so mmienu he mu sɛ, ‘Woyɛ me ba, nnɛ maayɛ w’Agya.’ Nea waka afa nyane a onyanee no firii awufoɔ mu a, ɔnsane nkɔ porɔeɛ mu he ne sɛ, ‘Mede bɔhyɛ kronkron a Dawid nyaeɛ he bɛ ma wo.’ Nti ɔno nso kaa no nnwom foforɔ mu sɛ, ‘Womma wo Kronkronni he honam mporɔ.’ Na Dawid deɛ, ɔyɔɔ Nyankopɔn pɛ a bɛada no adi he ya ɔno ankasa n’awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ mu, na owuiɛ, na besiee no ɔnoaa ne nananom nkyɛne, na ɔporɔeɛ; na nea Nyankopɔn ama no so he anhu porɔeɛ.
Nti me nuanom, honhu sɛ yɛnam nipa yi so ɔɔpae mu aka bɔne fakyɛ ho asɛm akyerɛ ho.
Na saa Yesu yi ne ɔnam ne so a nnipa a bɛgye no di nyinaa nya bɔne fakyɛ bɔne a bɛantumi amfa Mose mmara so ammu ho bem ho.
Nti honhwɛ na nea Adiyifoɔ he aka he amma ho so: ‘Ho a hobu Nyankopɔn asɛm animtia, honhwɛ ma ɔnyɛ ho nwanwa na honyera mfiri m’anim, efiri sɛ meeyɔ adwuma bi ho berɛ so, adwuma a sɛ bi ka ho asɛm nyinaa kyerɛ ho mpo a, honnye nni.’ ” Paulo ne Barnaba ɔɔkɔ he, nnipa hyɛɛ bɛ nkurane sɛ bɛnka saa nsɛm yiaa homeda a odi hɔ he.
Nti hyiadane he mu nhyiamu he baa awieeɛ he, Yudafoɔ he mu pii ne bɛ a bɛabɛdɔm Yudafoɔ som he na besuro Nyankopɔn he dii Paulo ne Barnaba akyi, na bɛkasa kyerɛɛ bɛ hyɛɛ bɛ nkurane sɛ bɛnkɔ so ntena Nyankopɔn adom mu.
Na homeda a odi hɔ he duruiɛ he, kuro mu he nyinaa hyiaa sɛ beebetie Awurade asɛm.
Na Yudafoɔ he huu nnipakuo he, ahoɔyea hyɛɛ bɛ ma.
Na bɛkaa abususɛm de bɔɔ nea Paulo kaeɛ he abira.
Na afei Paulo ne Barnaba kasaa akokoɔduro so sɛ, “Na ohia sɛ yɛka Nyankopɔn asɛm kyerɛ ho kane.
Na ɔnam sɛ hoapo asɛm he na hobu ho ho sɛ homfata daa nkwa he nti, yɛde asɛm he ɔɔkɔ Amanamane mufoɔ hɔ.
Na saa ne Awurade ahyɛ yɛ sɛ, ‘Mede wo asi hɔ sɛ Amanamane mufoɔ kanea, na ama wode nkwagyeɛ akoduru asaase ano nohoa.’ ” Berɛ a Amanamane mufoɔ tee yei he, bɛ ani gyeeɛ, na bɛhyɛɛ Awurade asɛm animuonyam, na dodoɔ a na Nyankopɔn ayi bɛ ama daa nkwa he bɛyɛɛ agyidifoɔ.
Taa de bɛ kɔɔ Ikonium Nti Nyankopɔn asɛm he trɛɛ pom hɔ nyinaa.
Na Yudafoɔ he hyɛɛ mmaa a bedi mu, ne mmeema atitire he kutupa ma bɛtaa Paulo ne Barnaba pamoo bɛ firi mpɔtamu hɔ.
Nti Paulo ne Barnaba proproo bɛ nane ase mfuturo sɛ ɔnyɛ nsɛnkyerɛnne ntia kuro mu hɔfoɔ, na bɛkɔɔ Ikonium.
Na anigyeɛ ne Honhom Kronkron hyɛɛ asuafoɔ he ma.
Paulo ne Barnaba kɔɔ Likaonia Saa asɛm korɔ heaa bi sii Ikonium.
Berɛ a bɛkɔɔ Yudafoɔ hyiadane mu he bɛkasa maa nnipakuo kɛseɛ bi a befiri Yudafoɔ ne Helafoɔ mu bɛyɛɛ agyidifoɔ.
Na Yudafoɔ a bɛannye anni he tutu guu amanamane mufoɔ he asom ma benyaa anuanom ho adwemmɔne.
Na bɛtenaa hɔ berɛ pii de akokoɔduro kasa maa Awurade, na Awurade ankasa dii n’adom ho asɛm he ho adanseɛ denam nsɛnkyerɛnne ne anwanwadeɛ ahodoɔ a ɔnam bɛ nsa so yɔeɛ he so.
Na kuro he mufoɔ he mu kyɛɛ mmienu, na binom kɔɔ Yudafoɔ he afa, na binom nso kɔɔ asomafoɔ he afa.
Na berɛ a Amanamane mufoɔ ne Yudafoɔ ne bɛ sodifoɔ he nyinaa yɛɛ sɛ bɛɛbɛhyɛ bɛ aniɔyea na bɛasi bɛ aboɔ he, asomafoɔ he teeɛ, na bedwane kɔɔ Likonia nkuro Listra ne Derbe, ne asaase a atwa ho ahyia so, na bɛkɔɔ so pae mu kaa asɛmpa he ya hɔ.
Na beema bi ya Listra a ɔte hɔ a ontumi nnyina ne nane so, efiri sɛ na ɔyɛ bubuani firi ne maame yam.
Otiee Paulo bere a na ɔɔkasa he.
Na Paulo hwɛɛ no gyee na ohuu sɛ ne gyidie betumi ama ne ho ayɛ no dene, ɔteaam kaa sɛ, “sɔre gyina hɔ kyirebenn.” Na beema he huri gyina firii aseɛ nanteɛ.
Na nnipakuo he huu nea Paulo ayɔ he, bɛteaam Likonia kasa mu sɛ, “abosom he ayɛ bɛ ho sɛ nnipa asane aba yɛ nkyɛne!” Bɛfrɛɛ Barnaba Seus, na Paulo nso bɛfrɛɛ no Hemes, efiri sɛ ɔno ne na ɔyɛ kasamafoɔ.
Na Seus a n’asɔredane ya kuro he anim he sɔfoɔ de anantwinyini ne nhwiren a bɛakyekyere baa kuro he pono ano pɛɛ sɛ ɔne nnipakuo he de bɛbɔ afɔdeɛ.
Na asomafoɔ Barnaba ne Paulo teeɛ he, besunsuanee bɛ ntaadeɛ mu tutuu mmirika kɔɔ nkurofoɔ he mu teaam sɛ, “Anuanom, ɛɛne nti ne ho ɔɔyɔ yei?
Yɛ nso yɛyɛ nnipa sɛ hoaa, na yɛka asɛmpa kyerɛ ho sɛ honnane mfiri ahuhudeɛ yi ho nkɔ Nyankopɔn a ɔte ase he nkyɛne; ɔno ne bɔɔ soro ne asaase ne po ne deɛ ɔya mu nyinaa.
Ɔno ne tete berɛ a atwam he, ogyae amanamane nyinaa maa bɛfaa bɛaa bɛ akwane so, nso ɔnam ne nnwuma pa so ma nsuo tɔ firi soro ma ho, ɔma nnɔbaeɛ ba ne berɛ mu, ɔma ho aduane ne anigyeɛ ma ho bo tɔ ho yam, na ɔnam so ada ne ho adi sɛ ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn.” Na nea bɛkaeɛ nyinaa akyi he, bɛka berɛɛ paa ansa na nnipakuo he oogyae afɔdeɛ a bɛpɛɛ sɛ bɛbɔ ama bɛ he bɔ.
Na Yudafoɔ bi firi Antiokia ne Ikonium baeɛ; na nnipakuo he baa bɛ afa.
Na besii Paulo aboɔ twee no firii kuro he mu susuu sɛ waawu.
Nso berɛ a asuafoɔ he twaa ne ho hyiaeɛ he, ɔsɔre kɔɔ kuro he mu.
Adeɛkyeeɛ he ɔne Barnaba kɔɔ Derbe.
Na bɛpae mu kaa asɛmpa he saa kuro he so, na benyaa asuafoɔ bebree he, bɛsane baa Listra, na bɛkɔɔ Ikonium ne Antiokia.
Hɔ ne bɛhyɛɛ akra he dene na bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nkuranee sɛ bɛntoa gyidie he so.
Na afei bɛkaa sɛ, “ɔsɛ sɛ yɛfa taa pii mu na yɛakɔ Nyankopɔn ahennie he mu.” Na beyii mpanyimfoɔ maa asafo biaa, na bɛde akɔmkyene bɔɔ mpaeɛ de bɛ hyɛɛ Awurade a bɛabenya ne mu gyidie he nsa.
Na betwaa mu Pisidia he, bɛbaa Pamfilia.
Bɛkaa asɛm he ya Perge he, bebeduruu Atalia.
Na befiri hɔ faa nsuo so kɔɔ Antiokia, baabi a asuafoɔ he de bɛ hyɛɛ Nyankopɔn adom ase maa adwuma a bɛakowie he.
Na bɛbaeɛ he, bɛfrɛɛ asafo he boaa ano, na bɛkaa nea Nyankopɔn de bɛ akɔyɛ nyinaa ne sɛnea wabie gyidie pono ama amanamane mufoɔ he.
Na bɛne asuafoɔ he nyinaa tenaa hɔ mmerɛ kakra.
Asomafoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ nhyiamu ya Yerusalem Afei nnipa binom baa Yudea a na bɛɛkyerɛkyerɛ sɛ, “Sɛ bɛantwa wo twetia sɛnea Mose mmara he ka he a, wontumi nya nkwa.” Na Paulo ne Barnaba ne bɛ dii anobaabaeɛ asɛm he ho wieeɛ he, beyii Paulo ne Barnaba ne nnipa binom kaa ho sɛ bɛnkɔ Yerusalem na bɛ ne asomafoɔ he ne mpanyimfoɔ he nkɔ booboo asɛm he ho.
Nti asafo he gyaa bɛ kwane he, bɛkɔfaa Foinike ne Samaria kaa adwensakra a amanamane mufoɔ he anya he ho asɛm, na bɛmaa anuanom he nyinaa ani gyee kɛse.
Na beduruu Yerusalem he, asafo he ne asomafoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ he gyee bɛ, na bɛkaa nea Nyankopɔn de bɛ ayɔ nyinaa kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Na Farisifoɔ he mu binom a bɛagye Nyankopɔn asɛm adi he sɔre kaa sɛ, “Ɔsɛ sɛ betwa bɛ twetia na bɛhyɛ bɛ sɛ benni Mose mmara so.” Na asomafoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ he behyiaa sɛ bɛɛbɛdwendwene asɛm yi ho.
Na bɛgyee ho akyinnye pii he, Petro sɔre ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Anuanom, ho ankasa honim sɛ mfitiaseɛ heaa ne Nyankopɔn yii me yɛ mu sɛ mene amanamane mufoɔ mfa m’anum asɛm so nte asɛmpa he na bɛnnye nni.
Na Nyankopɔn a onim akoma mu he maa bɛ Honhom Kronkron sɛnea ɔde maa yɛ heaa sɛ ɔnyɛ adansedie sɛ waagye bɛ atom.
Wamma nsonsonoeɛ amma yɛ ne bɛ ntam, na mmom ɔnam bɛ gyidie so tee bɛ akoma ho.
Afei mmɛ nti ne hosɔ Nyankopɔn hwɛ, sɛ hode konnua a yɛ nananom antumi ansoa to asuafoɔ he kɔno so?
Yɛgye di sɛ Awurade Yesu adom so mmom ne yɛnam nya nkwa, sɛ bɛ nso benya heaa.” Na nnipadɔm he nyinaa yɛɛ komm, na betiee Barnaba ne Paulo berɛ a bɛkaa nsɛnkyerɛnne ne anwanwadeɛ a Nyankopɔn nam bɛ so ayɔ ama amanamane mufoɔ ho asɛm.
Na bɛkasa wieeɛ he, Yakobo buaa sɛ, “Anuanom, hontie me.” Simon aka sɛnea kane Nyankopɔn kɔhwɛɛ amanamane he, sɛ ooyi mane bi afiri bɛ mu ama ne dini.
Adiyifoɔ he asɛm he si yei so, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Yei akyi he mɛsane abesi Dawid ntomadane a ahwe ase he bio, na masi nea bɛadwiri agu he bio, Na nnipa a aka he ne amanamane a bɛbɛbɔ me dini mu he nyinaa ahwehwɛ Awurade akyi kwane.
Awurade a ɔma behuu yeinom nyinaa firi wiase ahyɛaseɛ he ne ɔɔka.’ Nti m’asɛm a mewɔ ka ne sɛ mma yɛnha amanamane mufoɔ a bɛadane aba Nyankopɔn nkyɛne he; na yɛntwerɛ nkɔma bɛ sɛ, bɛntwe bɛ ho mfiri abosom afideɛ ne adwamammɔ ne mmoa a bɛanhwie bɛ mogyaa angu na bewuiɛ, ɔne mogyaa ho.
Na ofiri tete na Mose nyaa bɛ a bɛka ne ho asɛm nkuro nyinaa mu, na bɛkenkane no hyia adane mu homeda biaa nso.
Bɛde mane nwoma kɔma amanamane asafo he Afei asomafoɔ he ne mpanyimfoɔ he ne asafo mu he nyinaa hu sɛ ɔyɛ sɛ beyi bɛ mu binom ka Paulo ne Barnaba ho ma bɛkɔ Antiokia.
Bɛ a beyii bɛ he ne Yuda a bɛfrɛ no Barsaba ne Silas, mmeema a na bɛyɛ akannifoɔ anuanom he mu.
Na bɛde krataa maa bɛ a na mu nsɛm ne sɛ, “Anuanom, asomafoɔ ne mpanyimfoɔ he twerɛ krataa yi de kɔma agyidifoɔ a befiri amanamane a ɔya Antiokia ne Siria ne Kilikia.
Yɛkyea ho.
Esiane sɛ yɛate sɛ yɛ mu bi de nsɛm ɔɔteetee ho pɛ sɛ bɛsɛeɛ ho adwene berɛ a yɛmmaa bɛ akwankyerɛ biaa nti, yɛayɛ adwenkorɔ na ɔyɛ yɛ anigye sɛ yebeyi mmeema aka yɛ adɔfoɔ Barnaba ne Paulo ho aba ho nkyɛne, mmeema a bɛde bɛ kra ato hɔ, wuo mu oo nkwa mu oo, ama yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo.
Nti ne yɛasoma Yuda ne Silas, sɛ bɛmfa bɛ anum asɛm so nka asɛm korɔ heaa nkyerɛ ho.
Na ɔsɔ Honhom Kronkron he ne yɛ ankasa yɛ ani sɛ yɛmmfa adesoa foforɔ biaa nto ho so, gye sɛ yeinom a ohia yi, sɛ hontwe ho ho mfiri nnoɔma a bɛde abɔ afɔdeɛ ama abosom ne mogyaa ne mmoa a bɛanhwie bɛ mogyaa angu ne adwamammɔ ho.
Sɛ hotwe ho ho firi yeinom ho a, obesi ho yie.
Asomdwie nka ho.” Nti bɛsomaa bɛ kɔɔ Antiokia.
Bɛfrɛɛ asafo mma he boa ano, de krataa he maa bɛ.
Na bɛkenkane wieeɛ he, bedii ahurusie nkuranhyɛsɛm he ho.
Na Yuda ne Silas a na bɛ nso bɛyɛ adiyifoɔ he, kaa nsɛm pii de hyɛɛ bɛ nkurane na bɛhyɛɛ bɛ dene.
Na bɛtenaa hɔ kakra he, agyidifoɔ he gyaa bɛ kwane asomdwie mu ma bɛkɔɔ bɛ a bɛsomaa bɛ he hɔ.
(Nso Silas dwenee sɛ ɔyɛ sɛ ɔkɔ so tena hɔ.)
Na Paulo ne Barnaba kɔɔ so tenaa Antiokia, na bɛ ne nnipa foforɔ binom kyerɛkyerɛeɛ na bɛkaa Awurade asɛm.
Silas sii Barnaba ananmu Nna bi akyi he Paulo ka kyerɛɛ Barnaba sɛ, “Bra, na yɛnsane nkɔ na yɛnkɔsra agyidifoɔ a bɛya nkuro he mu a yɛkaa Awurade asɛm kyerɛɛ bɛ he na yɛnhwɛ sɛnea bɛ ho teɛ.” Barnaba pɛɛ sɛ bɛde Yohane a ɔsane de Marko he ka bɛ ho.
Nso Paulo yɔɔ n’adwene sɛ esiane sɛ ogyaa bɛ hɔ berɛ a beduruu Pamfilia na ɔne bɛ ankɔyɔ adwuma he nti, ɔnsɛ sɛ bɛde no ka bɛ ho kɔ.
Yei de akasakasaa a mu ɔdene baeɛ, na bedii mpaepaemu; Barnaba faa Marko kaa ne ho ma bɛfaa po so hyɛne de kɔɔ Kipro.
Paulo nso faa Silas, na berɛ a agyidifoɔ de Paulo hyɛɛ Awurade adom ase he, befirii hɔ kɔeɛ.
Na ɔkɔfaa Siria ne Kilikia hyehyɛɛ asafo ahodoɔ he dene.
Timoteo ka bɛ ho ya Listra Paulo kɔɔ Derbe ne Listra, baabi a na suani bi a bɛfrɛ no Timoteo a na ne maame yɛ Yudani na ne papa nso yɛ Helani ya.
Na agyidifoɔ a bɛya Listra ne Ikonium he kaa ne ho asɛm pa. Na Paulo pɛɛ sɛ Timoteo di n’akyi.
Na osiane Yudafoɔ a na bɛya hɔ he nti, ɔfaa no twaa no twetia, efiri sɛ na bɛ nyinaa nim sɛ ne papa yɛ Helani.
Afei berɛ a bɛnenam nkuro he so he bɛde mmara a asomafoɔ he ne mpanyimfoɔ a bɛya Yerusalem asi ho gyinaeɛ he maa bɛ sɛ benni so.
Nti asafo ahodoɔ he kɔɔ so yɛɛ dene gyidie mu na bɛkɔɔ so dɔree da biaa.
Paulo anisoadehunu ya Troa Afei bɛkɔfaa Frigia ne Galatia mpɔtamu efiri sɛ Honhom Kronkron he braa bɛ sɛ bɛnnka asɛm he Asia.
Na berɛ a beduruu Misia he, bɛyɛɛ bɛ adwene sɛ bɛbɛkɔ Bitinia, nso Honhom Kronkron ama bɛ kwane.
Nti betwaam Misia kɔɔ Troa.
Anadwo he Paulo nyaa anisoadehunu sɛ, Makedoniani bi gyina hɔ ɔɔserɛ no sɛ, “Bra Makedonia na bɛboa yɛ.” Na onyaa anisoadehunu heaa pɛ ne yesiim sɛ yɛɛkɔ Makedonia efiri sɛ yehuu sɛ Nyankopɔn ne wafrɛ yɛ sɛ yɛnkɔka asɛmpa he nkyerɛ bɛ.
Nti yɛfaa nsuo so firi Troa baa Samotrake tee, na adeɛ kyeeɛ he, yɛkɔɔ Neapoli.
Na yefirii hɔ he, yɛkɔɔ Filipi a ɔyɛ Roma atubrafoɔ kuro titire ya Makedonia mantam mu.
Yɛtenaa saa kuro he mu nna kakra.
Lidia adwensakra Homeda duruiɛ he, yepie faa kuro he pono ho kɔɔ asubɔntene bi ho, baabi a na yesusu sɛ yebenya baabi a bɛbɔ mpaeɛ.
Na yɛtenaa ase kasa kyerɛɛ mmaa a na bɛahyiam hɔ he.
Na baa bi a bɛfrɛ no Lidia a ɔtɔno ntoma kɔkɔɔ a ofiri Tiatira na ɔsom Nyankopɔn he tiee yɛ asɛm he.
Na Awurade biee n’akoma mu ma ɔyɛɛ aso maa nea Paulo kaeɛ he.
Afei berɛ a yɛbɔɔ ɔne ne fiefoɔ asu he, ɔde nkotosrɛ kaa sɛ, “Sɛ hoahu me sɛ nɔkwafoɔ ama Awurade a, hommɛtena me fie.” Na ɔkaeɛaa ma yɛkɔɔ ne fie.
Afenaa bi ayaresa Na dakoro bi, ɔbaa sɛ yɛɛkɔ baabi a bɛbɔ mpaeɛ he, yehyiaa afenaa bi a ɔwɔ akɔm honhom.
Na ɔka daakye nsɛm ma ne wuranom nya ne so mfasoɔ pii.
Na odii yɛ ne Paulo akyi teateaam sɛ, “Nnipa yi yɛ Sorosoro Nyankopɔn nkoa a bɛɛpae mu aka nkwagyekwane ho asɛm akyerɛ ho.” Ɔkɔɔ so yɔɔ saa nna pii.
Na ɔyɛɛ Paulo ahomte ma ɔdanee n’ani ka kyerɛɛ honhom he sɛ, “Mehyɛ wo Yesu Kristo dini mu sɛ firi ne mu firi” Na ofirii ne mu saa dɔno heaa.
Na ne wuranom huu sɛ nea bɛ ani da so a ɔbɛma bɛ mfasoɔ he ahwere bɛ he, bɛsosɔɔ Paulo ne Silas mu twee bɛ kɔɔ dwa so kɔmaa atumfoɔ he.
Na bɛde bɛ baa mane mpanyimfoɔ he anim he, bɛkaa sɛ, “Saa mmeema yi yɛ Yudafoɔ a bɛɛha yɛ kuro yi, na bɛɛkyerɛkyerɛ amanneɛ ahodoɔ bi a mmara mma yɛ a yɛyɛ Romafoɔ he kwane sɛ yedi so anaa yɛyɔ.” Na nnipakuo he nyinaa sɔre kɔɔ bɛ so; na berɛ a mane he mu mpanyimfoɔ he sunsuanee bɛ ntaadeɛ ngugusoɔ mu he, bɛhyɛɛ sɛ bɛmmɔ bɛ mmaa.
Na bɛbɔɔ bɛ mmaa pii wieeɛ he, bɛtwee bɛ koguu afiase na bɛhyɛɛ afiasehwɛfoɔ he sɛ ɔnhwɛ bɛ so yie.
Osiane sɛ bɛhyɛɛ no saa nti, ɔde bɛ koguu afiase dane a ɔhyɛ mfimfini paa he mu kyekyeree bɛ nane bɔɔ dua mu.
Afiasehwɛfoɔ he adwensakra Na anadwo dasuom he, Paulo ne Silas bɔɔ mpaeɛ too nnwom yii Nyankopɔn ayɛ, na nneduafoɔ he tiee bɛ.
Mpofiremuaa asaase wosoɔ kɛseɛ bi si maa afiase he fapem wosowosoeɛ.
Afei apono he nyinaa biebieɛ amonom hɔaa, na bɛ nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn he nyinaa sanesaneeɛ.
Berɛ a afiasehwɛfoɔ he sɔre firii nna mu a ohuu sɛ afiase apono he abiebie he, ɔtwee ne sekane sɛ nka oobeku ne ho, efiri sɛ na osusu sɛ nneduafoɔ he adwane.
Na Paulo de nne kɛseɛ teaam sɛ, “Nyɔ wo ho bɔne biaa, na yɛ nyinaa yɛya ha!” Na ɔkɔgyee kanea di mmirika bɔ wuraa hɔ, na ɔde ahopopoɔ hwee Paulo ne Silas anim.
Na ɔde bɛ baa abɔntene bisaa sɛ, “me wuranom, mennyɛ dɛ na manya daa nkwa?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Gye Awurade Yesu di, na ɔbɛgye wo ne wo fie nkwa.” Bɛkaa Awurade asɛm kyerɛɛ ɔne ne fiefoɔ nyinaa.
Na ɔde bɛ kɔɔ bea foforɔ bi saa anadwo heaa komiaa bɛ akuro he; na ntɛmaa bɛbɔɔ ɔne ne fiefoɔ nyinaa asu.
Ɔde bɛ baa fie hɔ, na ɔde aduane besisii bɛ anim, na ɔne ne fiefoɔ nyinaa dii ahurusie sɛ wabɛyɛ Nyankopɔn gyidini.
Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, mane he mu mpanyimfoɔ somaa awɛmfoɔ sɛ bɛnkɔka nkyerɛ afiasehwɛfoɔ he sɛ, “Gyae saa mmeema yi ma bɛnkɔ.” Na afiasehwɛfoɔ he kaa asɛm he kyerɛɛ Paulo, kaa sɛ, “Mane mpanyimfoɔ he asoma nnipa aba sɛ mennyae ho.
Nti afei hommɛsene nkɔ asomdwie mu.” Na Paulo buaa sɛ, “Bɛhwee yɛ badwam berɛ a yenni fɔ, nnipa a yɛyɛ Romafoɔ, na bɛde yɛ guu afiase, na afei deɛ beeyi yɛ kodɛɛ?
Daabi da, na mmom ma bɛ ankasa mmra mmeyi yɛ.” Awɛmfoɔ he kɔkaa nsɛm yi kyerɛɛ mpanyimfoɔ he.
Berɛ a bɛtee sɛ bɛyɛ Romafoɔ he, bɛbɔɔ hu.
Nti bɛba bɛpaa bɛ kyɛw.
Na beyii bɛ pieeɛ na bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ bemfiri kuro he mu nkɔ.
Befirii afiase he bɛkɔɔ Lidia fie.
Na berɛ a bɛhyɛɛ anuanom nkurane wieeɛ he, bɛkɔeɛ.
Sakasakayɛ baa Tesalonika Afei Paulo ne Silas kɔfaa Amfipoli ne Apolonia baa Tesalonika, baabi a na Yudafoɔ hyiadane bi ya he.
Na sɛnea Paulo taa yɛ he, ɔkɔɔ bɛ nkyɛne, na ɔde homeda mmeɛnsa ne bɛ susuu twerɛsɛm he ho, na ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ mu de adanseɛ ahodoɔ kyerɛɛ sɛ na ohia sɛ Kristo he hu amane na ɔsɔre fi awufoɔ mu, na ɔkaa sɛ, “Yei ne Kristo he, Yesu a meeka ne ho asɛm kyerɛ ho he.” Yei maa bɛ mu binom bɛyɛɛ agyidifoɔ, na bɛde bɛ ho bataa Paulo ne Silas ho, na Helafoɔ dɔm kɛseɛ bi a bɛsom Nyankopɔn ne mmaa atitire a bɛdɔɔso pii nso yɔɔ saa.
Na Yudafoɔ he ani bereeɛ, na bɛboaboa nsɛmmɔnefoɔ bi ano dwa so maa kuro he mu yɛɛ bagyabagya.
Na bɛto hyɛɛ Yason fie so hwehwɛɛ sɛ bɛde bɛ bɛbra bɛ a bɛɛyɔ basabasa he.
Berɛ a bɛanhu bɛ he, bɛtwee Yason ne agyidifoɔ binom kɔmaa kuro he mu atumfoɔ, na bɛteateaam sɛ, “Mmeema a bɛadane wiase ani he aba ha nso, na Yason agye bɛ aba ne fie.
Saa nnipa yi nyinaa sɔre tia Kaesare ahyɛdeɛ ka sɛ hene foforɔ bi ya hɔ a ɔde Yesu.” Berɛ a nnipa he ne kuro he mpanyimfoɔ tee yei he, bɛ ani bereeɛ, afei berɛ a bɛmaa Yason ne bɛ a bɛaka he dii agyinamu maa bɛ he, begyaa bɛ.
Paulo ne Silas kɔɔ Beroia Na ntɛmaa agyidifoɔ he maa Paulo ne Silas kɔɔ Beroia, na bekoduruiɛ he, bɛkɔɔ Yudafoɔ hyiadane mu.
Na yeinom gyee asɛm he sene bɛ a bɛya Tesalonika he, efiri sɛ bɛde bɛ adwene nyinaa gyee asɛm he, na da biaa na bɛhwehwɛ twerɛsɛm he mu yie hwɛ sɛ nsɛm he te saa anaa.
Na bɛ mu pii bɛgye diiɛ, ne Helafoɔ mmaa ne mmeema atitire a bɛdɔɔso pii nso yɔɔ saa.
Na Yudafoɔ a bɛya Tesalonika tee sɛ Paulo aka Nyankopɔn asɛm Beroia nso he, bɛbaa hɔ nso betu guu manfoɔ he asom, na bɛhwanyanee bɛ mu.
Na ntɛmaa agyidifoɔ he gyaa Paulo kwane koduruu po he ano nohoa, na Silas ne Timoteo deɛ bɛtenaa hɔ.
Bɛ a bekogyaa Paulo kwane he de no koduruu Atene.
Na ɔmaa bɛ nkra sɛ bɛnka nkyerɛ Silas ne Timoteo sɛ bɛmmra ne nkyɛne ntɛm so he, befirii hɔ kɔeɛ.
Paulo ne Yudafoɔ ne Helafoɔ nkɔmmɔbɔ Na Paulo gu so ɔɔtwɛne bɛ Atene na ohuu sɛ ahonyini ahyɛ kuro he so ma he, ɔyɛɛ no ahomte.
Nti ɔne Yudafoɔ ne nnipa a aka a bɛsom Nyankopɔn he susuu nsɛm ho hyiadane he mu, na da biaa na ɔkɔ bɛ a obenya bɛ he nso nkyɛne dwa so.
Nso Epikurofoɔ ne Stoafoɔ nyansapɛfoɔ bi ne no dii anobaabaeɛ, na binom kaa sɛ, “Mmɛ ne kasatentene wura yi pɛ sɛ ɔkyerɛ koraa yi?” Na binom nso kaa sɛ, “Gyama ɔka ananafoɔ abosom ho asɛm.” (Efiri sɛ, na ɔɔka Yesu ne wusɔreɛ he ho asɛmpa.)
Nti bɛkyee no de no kɔɔ Areopago asennibea bisaa no sɛ, “Wobetumi ama yɛahu nkyerɛkyerɛ foforɔ a wookyerɛkyerɛ yi mu?
Nea wooka he yɛ foforɔ yɛ asom.
Nti yɛpɛ sɛ yehu nea nsɛm yi kyerɛ.” Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, sɛ Atenefoɔ ne ahɔhoɔ a bɛabɛsoɛ hɔ he nya berɛ a, nea bɛde yɛaa ne sɛ bɛbɛka anaa bebetie asɛm foforɔ.
Afei Paulo sɔre gyinaa Areopago mfimfini, kaa sɛ, “Atene mmeema, maahu sɛ adeɛ nyinaa mu hopɛ nyamesom paa, efiri sɛ menenam kuro he mu na mehwɛɛ nnoɔma a hosom he, mehuu afɔrebokyia bi a bɛatwerɛ ho, ‘Yei yɛ Nyame Bi a Yennim No Dea.’ Nti nea hosom a honnim no he, ɔnoaa ne meeka ne ho asɛm akyerɛ ho yi.
Nyankopɔn a ɔyɔɔ wiase ne nea ɔya mu nyinaa, ɔno a ɔyɛ soro ne asaase Wura he ntena dane a bɛde nipa nsa asi mu, na bɛmfa nipa nsa nsom no, te sɛ nea ohia bibi, efiri sɛ ɔno mmom ne ma nnipa nyinaa nkwa, ahomee ne adeɛ nyinaa.
Na nipa baako mu ne oyii amane nyinaa firiiɛ sɛ bɛntena asaase nyinaa so, na waahyɛ mmerɛ ato hɔ, na ɔde hyeɛ atoto nnipa tenabea nso, na ama bɛapɛ Nyankopɔn akyi kwane, ahwehwɛ no anibereɛ so kosi sɛ bebehu no, nso nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ ɔne yɛ mu biaa ntam nware.
Na ɔnam ne so ne yɛwɔ nkwa, na yɛkeka yɛ ho na yɛte ase’; na ho mu anwensɛm atwerɛfoɔ bi mpo aka sɛ, ‘Yɛ nso yɛyɛ ne mma.’ Nti berɛ a yɛahu sɛ yɛyɛ Nyankopɔn asefoɔ yi, ɔnsɛ sɛ yesusu sɛ Nyankopɔn tebea te sɛ sikakɔkɔɔ anaa dwetɛ anaa boɔ, anaa adwenie bi a nipa de n’adwene adi anaa wabɔ ne tirim ayɔ.
Nyankopɔn buu n’ani guu mmerɛ a na bennim hwee he so, nso afei ɔɔka akyerɛ adasamma a bɛya mmaa nyinaa sɛ biaa nsakra n’adwene, efiri sɛ waayi da bi asi hɔ a wabɔ ne tim pɔ sɛ ɔnam beema bi a wayi no so bebu wiase atentenee mu, na wanyane no afiri awufoɔ mu de ayɔ nnyinasodeɛ ama nnipa nyinaa.” Na bɛtee awufoɔ sɔreɛ he ho asɛm he, binom dii fɛw, na binom nso kaa sɛ, “Yebetie yei ho asɛm afiri wo nkyɛne bio berɛ foforɔ nso.” Saa berɛ he Paulo gyaa bɛ hɔ kɔeɛ.
Nso mmeema bi de bɛ ho bɔɔ no bɛyɛɛ agyidifoɔ, bɛ mu binom ne Dionisio a ɔyɛ Areopago badwa he temmuafoɔ, ne baa bi a bɛfrɛ no Damari, ne afoforɔ a bɛka bɛ ho.
Paulo kɔɔ Korinto Yei akyi he, Paulo firii Atene kɔɔ Korinto.
Na ohuu Yudani bi a bɛfrɛ no Akwila, Pontoni bi a na ofiri Italia aba ne nkyɛne, ne ne yerɛ Priskila, efiri sɛ na Klaudio ahyɛ sɛ Yudafoɔ nyinaa mfiri Roma.
Nti ɔkɔɔ bɛ nkyɛne.
Na esiane sɛ na ɔne bɛ yɔ adwuma korɔ nti, ɔtenaa bɛ fie yɔɔ adwuma, efiri sɛ na bɛyɛ ntomadanyɔfoɔ.
Nso, homeda biaa, na ɔka asɛm hyiadane mu ma Yudafoɔ ne Helafoɔ gye di.
Afei berɛ a Silas ne Timoteo nyinaa firii Makedonia beduruiɛ he, Paulo de ne berɛ nyinaa pae mu kaa asɛm he, na odii Yudafoɔ adanseɛ kyerɛɛ sɛ Yesu ne Kristo he.
Berɛ a bɛ ne no dii asie na bɛkasa tiaa no he, ɔporoporoo ne ntaadeɛ mu mfuturo kaa sɛ, “Ho mogyaa mua hoaa ho atifi.
Me deɛ menni ho fɔ.
Ofiri nnɛ ɔɔkɔ yi meekɔ amanamane mufoɔ hɔ.” Afei ofirii hyiadane mu hɔ, na ɔkɔɔ beema bi a bɛfrɛ no Tito Yusto a ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn somfoɔ fie.
Na ne fie he ya hyiadane he nkyɛne pɛɛ.
Krispo a na ɔyɛ hyiadane he mu panyini ne ne fiefoɔ nyinaa gyee Awurade diiɛ.
Na Korintofoɔ he a betie Paulo he nso gye diiɛ na bɛbɔɔ bɛ asu.
Da koro anadwo bi, Awurade kaa no anisoadehunu mu kyerɛɛ Paulo sɛ, “Nsuro, kasa na mmua w’ano, efiri sɛ, meka wo ho, na biaa ntumi mfa ne nsa nka wo nyɔ wo bɔne biaa, na mewɔ nnipa pii ya kuro yi mu.” Ɔtenaa hɔ afe ne bosome nsia kyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ Nyankopɔn asɛm.
Afei berɛ a Galio yɛ Akaia amrado he, Yudafoɔ he yɛɛ baako sɔre tiaa Paulo de no kɔɔ atemmuo adwa he anim kɔkaa sɛ, “Saa nipa yi dane nkurofoɔ adwene ma bɛfa kwane foforɔ a ɔne mmara he bɔ abira so som Nyankopɔn.” Paulo yɛɛ sɛ ɔɔbɛkasa heaa, na Galio ka kyerɛɛ Yudafoɔ he sɛ, “Yudafoɔ, sɛ asɛm yi yɛ bɔne anaa ammumuyɔdeɛ bi a, nka mɛgye ho asɛm he atum.
Na mmom sɛ ɔyɛ nsɛm ne dini ne ho mmara ho akyinnyegyeɛ deɛ a, hedeɛ ho ankasa honhwɛ nka.
Mempɛ sɛ mɛyɛ nsɛm yi ho temufoɔ.” Na ɔpamoo bɛ firii atemmuo adwa he anim.
Nti bɛ nyinaa to hyɛɛ Sostene a ɔyɛ hyiadane mu panyini he so firii aseɛ hwee no atemmuo adwa he anim.
Nso Galio anyɛ yeinom ho hwee.
Paulo sane kɔɔ Antiokia Nso berɛ a Paulo dii nna kakra kaa ho hɔ he, ɔne agyidifoɔ he dii nkra na ɔde po so hyɛne firii hɔ kɔɔ Siria a na Priskila ne Akwila ka ne ho, na ɔbɔɔ ti kwa ya Kenkrea, efiri sɛ, na berɛ a ɔde asi hɔ sɛ ootua ne ho nnoɔma bi he aba awieeɛ.
Na beduruu Efeso he, ogyaa bɛ hɔ; na ɔno deɛ ɔkɔɔ hyiadane mu ne Yudafoɔ he kɔyɔɔ nsɛm bi ho mpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛmu.
Na bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔntena hɔ nkyɛre, nso wannye antom, na ɔne bɛ dii nkra ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Sɛ ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn pɛ a, mɛba ho nkyɛne bio.” Yei akyi he ofiri Efeso faa po so kɔeɛ.
Na oduruu Kaesarea he, ɔkɔɔ Yerusalem kɔkyeaa asafo he.
Na afei ɔkɔɔ Antiokia.
Berɛ a ɔtenaa hɔ kakra he, ofirii hɔ tutuu akwane faa Galatia ne Frigia nsaase so hyehyɛɛ asuafoɔ he nyinaa dene.
Apolo kɔɔ Efeso ne Korinto Afei Yudani bi a bɛfrɛ no Apolo a ofiri Aleksandria, baa Efeso.
Na Apolo yɛ bi a n’ano ate na onim twerɛsɛm mu paa nso.
Na bɛakyerɛkyerɛ no Awurade kwane so, na esiane sɛ na Honhom ahyɛ no ma nti, ɔkaa Yesu ho asɛm kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu pɛpɛɛpɛ, nso na Yohane asubɔ he nkoaa ne onim.
Na ɔhyɛɛ aseɛ sɛ ɔde akokoɔduro ɔɔkasa hyiadane he mu, nso berɛ a Priskila ne Akwila tiee no he, bɛfaa no kɔɔ nkyɛne baabi kyerɛkyerɛɛ no Nyankopɔn kwane he mu pɛpɛɛpɛ.
Afei esiane sɛ na ɔpɛ sɛ otware kɔ Akaia nti, agyidifoɔ he hyɛɛ ne nkurane, na bɛtwerɛɛ krataa kɔmaa asuafoɔ he srɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛnnye no fɛ so.
Nti berɛ a oduruu hɔ he, ɔboaa bɛ a bɛnam Nyankopɔn adom so agye adi he paa, ɔde nnamyɛ daa no adi pefee badwam sɛ Yudafoɔ he afom kwane, na ɔde Twerɛsɛm he kyerɛɛ sɛ Yesu ne Kristo he.
Paulo kɔɔ Efeso Ɔbaa sɛ berɛ a Apolo ya Korinto he, Paulo faa mpɔtamu hɔ baabi baa Efeso, bɛtoo asuafoɔ bi.
Na obisaa bɛ sɛ, “Berɛ a hogye diiɛ he honyaa Honhom Kronkron anaa?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Daabi, yɛntee da mpo sɛ Honhom Kronkron bi ya baabi.” Nti ɔkaa sɛ, “hedeɛ mmɛ asubɔ ne bɛbɔɔ ho?” Bebuaa sɛ, “Yohane asubɔ a.” Paulo kaa sɛ, “Yohane bɔɔ asu a ɔyɛ adwensakra ho nsɛnkyerɛnne, na ɔka kyerɛɛ nkurofoɔ he sɛ bennya deɛ odi n’akyi ɔɔba, a ɔne Yesu, he mu gyidie.” Na bɛtee yei he, bɛbɔɔ bɛ asu Awurade Yesu dini mu.
Na Paulo de ne nsa guu bɛ so he, Honhom Kronkron he baa bɛ so, na bɛkaa kasa hodoɔ hyɛɛ nkɔm.
Na bɛ dodoɔ yɛ du mmienu.
Paulo kɔɔ hyiadane he mu, de akokoɔduro kasaeɛ, na bosome mmeɛnsa ne ɔkasaeɛ, na ɔkaa Nyankopɔn ahennie ho asɛm a ɔtɔ asum.
Nso berɛ a binom prim bɛ akoma na bɛannye anni, na bɛkekaa gyidie Kwane He ho nsɛmmɔne nnipadɔm he anim he, ɔtwee ne ho yii asuafoɔ he firii bɛ mu, na daa na ɔka asɛm Tirano suadane he mu.
Yei toa so mfie mmienu, na bɛ a bɛte Asia mpɔtamu nyinaa, Yudafoɔ ne Helafoɔ nyinaa, tee Awurade asɛm.
Skewa mma nson ho asɛm Na Nyankopɔn nam Paulo so yɔɔ anwanwadeɛ soronko.
Na yei nti bɛde duku ne ntaadeɛ nsɛnanimu mpo ka ne honam na bɛde kogu ayarefoɔ so a bɛ yadeɛ he gyaeɛ, na ahonhommɔne nso he tutu firi bɛ mu.
Na Yudafoɔ a beekyinikyini tutu ahonhommɔne he mu binom nso bɔɔ mmɔdene sɛ bɛbɛbɔ Awurade dini agu bɛ a bɛwɔ ahonhommɔne he so sɛ, “Mehyɛ ho Yesu a Paulo kaa ne ho asɛm he dini mu sɛ hompie.” Na Yudani sɔfo panyini bi a ɔde Skewa wɔ mma nson bi a bɛyɔ saa.
Na honhommɔne he buaa sɛ, “Menim Yesu, menim Paulo, na ho nso, hoyɛ hefoɔ?” Na afei beema a honhommɔne ya ne mu he to hyɛɛ bɛ, so dii bɛ so, yɔɔ bɛ pasapasa, na bɛde adagya dwane firii fie hɔ kɔeɛ a na bɛapirapira.
Na Yudafoɔ ne Helafoɔ a bɛte Efeso tee yei he, hu kɛseɛ bɔɔ bɛ nyinaa, na bɛkɔɔ so kamfõõ Awurade Yesu dini.
Na bɛ a bɛbɛyɛɛ agyidifoɔ he mu pii kaa bɛ bɔne ne bɛ nneyɔeɛ kyerɛeɛ pefee.
Na bɛ a bedi asumansɛm he mu pii de bɛ nwoma ba bɛhye ma biaa huiɛ.
Na bebuu ne nyinaa ano huu sɛ ne boɔ yɛ nnwetɛbena apem aduonum.
Saa ara ne Awurade asɛm nam ahoɔdene so kɔɔ so trɛeɛ, na aseɛ timiiɛ.
Afei bewiee yeinom he, Paulo bɔɔ ne tim pɔ sɛ, sɛ ɔkɔfa Makedonia ne Akaia wie a, ɔbɛkɔ Yerusalem, na ɔkaa sɛ: “Sɛ meduru hɔ a, otwa sɛ mekɔ Roma nso.” Nti ɔsomaa n’aboɔfoɔ he mu mmienu, Timoteo ne Erasto, kɔɔ Makedonia, na ɔno ankasa deɛ, ɔtenaa Asia mantam he mu kyɛree kakra.
Demetrio sakasakayɔ Saa bere no sakasaka kɛseɛ bi sɔreeɛ a na ɔfa gyidie Kwane He ho.
Na dwetɛ dwumfoɔ bi a bɛfrɛ no Demetrio, nam Artemi abosom-adane a ɔde dwetɛ yɔ he so ma adwumfoɔ he nya mfasoɔ kɛseɛ; na ɔboaboaa bɛ a bɛyɔ nnoɔma a ɔtete saa ho adwuma he ano kaa sɛ: “Mmeema, honim yie sɛ adwuma yi ne ma yenya yɛ ho.
Afei nso, hoahu na hoate sɛnea ɔnyɛ Efeso nko na Paulo yi adane nnipakuo pii adwene ama bɛanya adwene foforɔ, na mmom ɔkame ayɛ sɛ Asia mantam mu nyinaa, na ɔka sɛ nea bɛde nsa ayɔ he nyɛ anyame.
Bio nso, ɔnyɛ yɛ adwuma a obenya dimmɔne he nkoaa ne asɛm he, na mmom bebebu bosombaa kɛseɛ Artemi asɔrefie nso adehunu, na n’animuonyam a Asia mantam ne asaase sɔfoɔ nyinaa de som no mpo, bɛbrɛ ase.” Berɛ a nkurofoɔ he tee yei he, bɛ bo fuiɛ.
Na bɛteateaam sɛ: “Efesofoɔ bosom Artemi yɛ kɛseɛ!” Nti kurom hɔ nyinaa bɛyɛɛ gyegyeegye, na bɛ nyinaa de koma koro bɔɔ twi kɔɔ adehwɛbea hɔ, na bɛkyee Gaio ne Aristarko a bɛyɛ Makedoniafoɔ ne Paulo akwantuo mu ahokafoɔ he.
Paulo deɛ, na ɔpɛ sɛ ɔkɔ nnipa he mu, nso asuafoɔ he amma no kwane.
Mpanyimfoɔ a bɛhwɛ afahyɛ ne agodie so he mu binom mpo a na bɛpɛ n’asɛm he soma bɛsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔmmfa ne ho nto asiane mu nkɔ adehwɛbea hɔ.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, sɛ binom teaam ka asɛm baako a, na afoforɔ nso aka asɛm foforɔ, na badwa he mu ayɛ bagyabagya, na bɛ mu dodoɔ heaa nnim nea nti a bɛabehyiam.
Nti bɛde Aleksandro firi nnipakuo he mu baeɛ, na Yudafoɔ he twee no baa anim, na Aleksandro nyam ne nsa pɛɛ sɛ oyi n’ano kyerɛ nkurofoɔ he.
Nso berɛ a behuu sɛ ɔyɛ Yudani he, bɛ nyinaa de nne koro teateaam bɛyɛ sɛ nnɔnhwere mmienu sɛ: “Efesofoɔ bosom Artemi yɛ kɛseɛ!” Afei kuro he twerɛfoɔ maa nnipa he yɛɛ komm, na ɔkaa sɛ: “Efeso mmeema, nipa hwane ne onnim sɛ Efesofoɔ kuro ne hwɛ Artemi kɛseɛ he ne honyini a ɔte firi soro baeɛ he asɔredane so?
Hedeɛ esiane sɛ bi ntumi nnye yeinom ho akyinnye nti, ɔfata sɛ hoyɛ komm na homfa ahoperɛ nyɔ bibiaa.
Efiri sɛ mmeema a hode bɛ aba yi nwiaa asɔredane mu nnoɔma, na bɛnkasa ntiaa yɛ bosombaa he.
Nti sɛ Demetrio ne adwumfoɔ a bɛka ne ho he wɔ bi ho asɛm a, nna a bedi asɛm ya hɔ, na amradofoɔ nso ya hɔ; sɛ bi wɔ asɛm tia ne yɔnko a, ɔmfa nkɔ ma badwa he.
Nso sɛ hoohwehwɛ bibi a ɔsene saa a, badwa a ɔya hɔ he ne ɔsɛ sɛ osi ho gyinaeɛ.
Na sɛ anhwɛ a, nea asi nnɛ yi bɛma bɛabɔ yɛ soboɔ sɛ yɛyɛ amammɔfoɔ, efiri sɛ yenni asɛm biaa bɛde bɛkyerɛkyerɛ basabasayɔ yi ase.” Na ɔkaa yei he, ɔmaa badwa he tuiɛ.
Paulo kɔɔ Makedonia ne Hela Na afei basabasa he ano berɛ ase he, Paulo soma ma bɛkɔfrɛɛ asuafoɔ he, na ɔhyɛɛ bɛ nkurane gyaa bɛ kwane he, ogyaa bɛ hɔ kɔɔ Makedonia.
Berɛ a ɔkɔfaa mpɔtamu hɔ na ɔhyɛɛ bɛ nkurane pii he, ɔbaa Hela, bedii bosome mmeɛnsa.
Na berɛ a ɔɔbɛkɔ Siria he Yudafoɔ he bɔɔ ne ho pɔ.
Ne saa nti ɔyɛɛ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛkɔ akɔfa Makedonia mmom ne akɔ.
Na bɛ a bɛka ne ho ne Beroiani Piro ba Sopater, Aristako ne Sekundo a bɛyɛ Tesalonikafoɔ, Derbeni Gaio, Timoteo, Asiafoɔ Tihiko ne Trofimo.
Yeinom dii yɛ anim kane kɔtwɛnee yɛ Troa.
Na Paanoo a Mmɔreka nnim Afahyɛ he akyi he, yɛtenaa hyɛne mu firii Filipi, na nnanum ntam he, yɛkɔtoo bɛ Troa.
Na yedii nnanson hɔ.
Paulo ne Troas asɔremma dii nkra Da a odi nnanwɔtwe kane he, berɛ a na yɛahyiam oobubu paanoo he, Paulo firi aseɛ sɛ ɔne bɛ ɔɔkasa, efiri sɛ na waayɛ n’adwene sɛ adeɛ kye a obefiri hɔ.
Nti ɔtoaa so kasaeɛ a kosii anadwo dasuom.
Nti na nkanea pii ya abrosane so dane a na yɛahyia mu he mu.
Paulo gu so ɔɔkasa he, abranteɛ bi a bɛfrɛ no Eutiko a na ɔte mpomaa mu faa mu daa hatee, na berɛ he mu he ofirii abrosane a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he so bɛhwee fam, na bɛmaa no so he, na waawu.
Nso Paulo siane kɔɔ fam kobutuu ne so, na ɔbamm no kaa sɛ, “Honhaehae, ne kra da so ya ne mu.” Afei Paulo foroo abrosane he, na ɔfaa paanoo diiɛ he, ɔtoa so ne bɛ dii nkɔmmɔ kɔpem ahemakye ansa na ɔɔkɔ.
Na bɛde abeemaa he baeɛ a na wasane anya nkwa.
Na bɛ werɛ kyekyere paa.
Paulo firii Troas kɔɔ Mileto Afei yedii kane kɔtenaa hyɛne mu kɔɔ Aso, baabi a na yɛayɔ adwene sɛ yɛbɛfa Paulo he, efiri sɛ berɛ a ɔka kyerɛɛ yɛ sɛ yɛnyɔ saa he, ɔno ankasa yɔɔ adwene sɛ ɔbɛnante akɔ.
Na ohyiaa yɛ Aso he, yɛfaa no tenaa yɛ kodoɔ he mu de no kɔɔ Mitelene.
Na yɛkaa kodoɔ he firii hɔ, na adeɛ kyeeɛ he yeduruu bea bi a na ɔne Kio di animhwɛ, na da a odi hɔ he yeduruu Samo, na adeɛ kyee bio he yɛbaa Mileto, efiri sɛ na Paulo asi gyinaeɛ sɛ onnyina Efeso, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ɔnseɛ berɛ Asia mpɔtamu, efiri sɛ na ne ho pere no sɛ, nka obetumi, akoduru Yerusalem da a bedi Pentekoste afahyɛ he.
Paulo ne Efeso mpanyimfoɔ dii nkra Na ɔya Mileto he ɔsoma nnipa kɔɔ Efeso kɔfrɛɛ asafo mu mpanyimfoɔ he.
Bɛbaeɛ he ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ: “Ho ankasa honim sɛnea me ne ho tenaa berɛ nyinaa ofiri daa odi kane a mebaa Asia, na mede ahobrɛaseɛ kɛseɛ ne nisuo pii, ne nsɔhwɛ a ɔtoo me ɔnam Yudafoɔ pɔ a bɛbɔeɛ so som Awurade.
Na mamfa nea mfasoɔ ya so a ɔsɛ sɛ meka kyerɛ ho biaa, ne Nyankopɔn asɛm a ɔsɛ sɛ mekyerɛkyerɛ ho badwam ne afie afie he ankame ho.
Na mmom medii Nyankopɔn fam adwensakra ne yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo mu gyidie ho adanseɛ kyerɛɛ Yudafoɔ ne Helafoɔ nyinaa.
Afei, hwɛ, ɔnam sɛ Honhom he hyɛ me nti meekɔ Yerusalem a mennim adeɛ a ɔbɛto me hɔ, ɔnoaa ne sɛ kuro biaa mu he Honhom Kronkron he di adanseɛ sɛ afiase da ne taa ɔɔtwɛne me.
Nso memmu me kra sɛ adehia sɛ wie a mewie me som ne adwuma a Awurade Yesu de ahyɛ me nsa sɛ menka asɛmpa a ɔfa Nyankopɔn adom he ho he.
“Na afei menim sɛ ho a me ne ho tenaeɛ na mebɔɔ ahennie he ho dawuro he mu biaa onhu me bio.
Nti meeka akyerɛ ho nnɛ da yi sɛ, menni ho mu biaa mogyaa ho fɔ, efiri sɛ mamfa Nyankopɔn nhyehyɛeɛ biaa ansie ho.
Honhwɛ ho ho so yie, na honhwɛ nnipa a Honhom Kronkron he de ho ayɛ bɛ so nhwɛsofoɔ he, na honhwɛ Nyankopɔn asafo a ɔde ɔnoaa ne Ba mogyaa atɔ he so.
Menim sɛ mekɔ akyi he, mpataku bɔne bɛhyɛne ho mu a bɛɛnyɛ nwankuo he brɛbrɛ.
Hoaa ho mu mmeema bɛsɔre akasa adane nɔkorɛ he de atwe asafo he adi bɛ akyi.
Nti honwɛne na honkae sɛ mfie mmeɛnsa di, awia ne anadwo, mannyae sɛ mede nisuo betu ho mu biaa fo.
Na afei mede ho hyɛ Nyankopɔn ne asɛm a ɔfa n’adom he ho, asɛm a obetumi ahyɛ ho dene na ama hoanya agyapadeɛ bɛ a bɛate bɛ ho nyinaa mu.
M’ani mmere biaa dwetɛ, sikakɔkɔɔ anaa bi ntoma.
Ho ankasa honim sɛ mede me nsa ayɔ adwuma ahwɛ me ho ne bɛ a bɛka me ho he.
Yei nyinaa mu he mede ayɔ nhwɛsoɔ ama ho sɛ ɔsɛ sɛ yɛyɔ adwuma de boa bɛ a bɛayɛ mmerɛ, na yɛkae Awurade Yesu nsɛm a ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Nhyira ya ma mu sene gyeɛ.’ ” Paulo kasa wieeɛ he, ɔne bɛ nyinaa buu nkotodwe bɔɔ mpaeɛ.
Na bɛ nyinaa suu pii.
Bɛyɔɔ Paulo atuu de bɛ nsa to ne nsa yam kyeakyea no, dii awerɛhoɔ ne titire ka a ɔkaa sɛ benhu no bio he ho.
Na afei bɛde no kɔɔ kodoɔ he ho.
Paulo kɔɔ Yerusalem Afei, yɛne bɛ tetee mu he, yɛfaa nsuo so kɔɔ tẽẽ koduru Ko.
Na adeɛ kyeeɛ he yɛkɔɔ Rode, na yefiri hɔ kɔɔ Patara.
Na berɛ a yehuu hyɛne bi a ɔɔkɔ Foinike he, yɛkɔforo kɔeɛ.
Afei yeduruu baabi a na yɛ ani tua Kipro he, yetwaam kɔɔ Siria berɛ a na yɛagya kuro he yɛ benkum so, na yekogyinaa Tiro, efiri sɛ hɔ ne na bebeyi kodoɔ he mu nnoɔma.
Yɛhwehwɛɛ asuafoɔ he, na yɛtenaa hɔ nnanson.
Honhom he ma bɛka kyerɛɛ Paulo sɛ, mma ɔnnkɔ Yerusalem.
Yɛ nna he soeɛ he, yefirii hɔ toaa yɛ akwantuo he so.
Na bɛ nyinaa bɛne bɛ ayerɛ ne bɛ mma kogyaa yɛ kwane kosii kurotia.
Na yebuu nkotodwe mpoano hɔ bɔɔ mpaeɛ na yɛ ne bɛ dii nkra.
Afei yɛkɔforoo kodoɔ he, na bɛsane kɔɔ fie.
Afei kwane a yetu firii Tiro he de yɛ koduruu Ptolemai, na yɛkyeakyea agyidifoɔ he na yɛtenaa bɛ nkyɛne da koro.
Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, yefirii hɔ kɔɔ Kaesarea; na yɛkɔɔ asɛmpakani Filipo a na ɔyɛ nnipa nson a asomafoɔ he de akunafoɔ aduanema ho dwumadie hyɛɛ bɛ nsa he mu baako fie, na yɛtenaa ne nkyɛne.
Na ɔwɔ mma mmaa nnan bi a bɛnwareeɛ a na bɛyɛ nkɔmhyɛfoɔ.
Na yedii nna kakra hɔ he, diyifoɔ bi a bɛfrɛ no Agabu firi Yudea baa hɔ.
Ɔbaa yɛ nkyɛne; na ɔfaa Paulo aboomu de kyekyeree ne nane ne ne nsa.
Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Nea Honhom Kronkron ɔɔka di, ‘Sei ne Yudafoɔ a bɛya Yerusalem bɛkyekyere aboomu yi wura, na bɛde no ama Amanamane mufoɔ.’ ” Yɛtee yei he, yɛ ne nkurofoɔ a bɛya hɔ he tuu Paulo fo sɛ ɔnnkɔ Yerusalem.
Nso obuaa sɛ, “Mmɛ ne hooyɔ yi, sɛ hode su ɔɔte me nsono mu yi?
Masiesie me ho sɛ ɔnyɛ kyekyere a bɛbɛkyekyere me nkoaa, na mmom, sɛ otwa sɛ mewu mpo a mewu ama Awurade Yesu dini ya Yerusalem.” Ɔnam sɛ na wawe ataaso sɛ ɔbɛkɔ nti, yɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Awurade pɛ ne nyɔ hɔ.” Na yɛanka bibiaa bio.
Na nna yi akyi he, yɛyɔɔ ahoboa siim kɔɔ Yerusalem.
Asuafoɔ a bɛya Kaesarea nso ne yɛ kɔeɛ de yɛ koduruu Kiproni Minason a na ɔyɛ asuafoɔ adikanfoɔ he mu bi fie.
Na yɛ ne no tenaeɛ.
Paulo kɔsraa Yakobo ya Yerusalem Berɛ a yeduruu Yerusalem he, anuanom de anigyeɛ gyee yɛ.
