Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, Paulo ne yɛ kɔsraa Yakobo, na yɛkɔtoo mpanyimfoɔ he nyinaa nso hɔ.
Na ɔkyea bɛ wieeɛ he, ofirii aseɛ kaa nea Nyankopɔn nam ne som adwuma he so ayɔ no Amanamane mufoɔ mu he nyinaa kyerɛɛ bɛ.
Na bɛtee yei he, bɛhyɛɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam.
Na afei bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Onua, woahu Yudafoɔ mpempem a bɛyɛ agyidifoɔ; na bɛ nyinaa bɛbɔ bɛ ho mmɔdene mmara he ho.
Nea bɛaka afa wo ho akyerɛ bɛ ne sɛ wokyerɛkyerɛ Yudafoɔ a bɛya Amanamane mu nyinaa sɛ bɛmmane mfiri Mose mmara he ho, na woka kyerɛ bɛ sɛ benntwa bɛ mma twetia na bennni amanneɛ he so.
Nti afei, ɛɛne ne yɛbɛyɔ afa saa asɛm yi ho?
Nea ɔbɛyɛ biaa bɛbɛte sɛ woaba ha.
Nti yɔ nea yɛbɛka akyerɛ wo yi: Yɛwɔ mmeema nnan bi a bɛahyɛ bɔ soronko sɛ beetua bɛ ho nnoɔma bi berɛ yi mu.
Ka saa mmeema yi ho, na homfa nhyehyɛeɛ a ɔfa ahodwira ho he mu, na afei tua sika a ɔsɛ sɛ betua yi beti he kyɛ bɛ.
Na yei bɛma biaa ahu sɛ wo ho asɛm a bɛteeɛ he nyɛ nɔkorɛ, na mmom wodi mmara he so na wo bɔ ho bane nso.
Na agyidifoɔ a befiri Amanamane mu he deɛ, yɛde gyinaeɛ a yɛasi he akɔ ma bɛ sɛ bɛntwe bɛ ho mfiri bibi a bɛde abɔ afɔdeɛ ama bosom ne mogyaa ne mmoa a bɛaku bɛ a bɛanhwie bɛ mogyaa angu, ne adwamammɔ ho.” Nti Paulo faa mmeema he.
Na adeɛ kyeeɛ a odwiraa ne ho he, ɔne bɛ kɔɔ asɔrefie hɔ kɔkyerɛɛ ahodwira nna he wie a bebewie he, na afei bɛbɔɔ biaa ti so afɔdeɛ.
Nnipakuo he kyee no Afei berɛ a nnanson a bɛayi asi hɔ ama ahodwira he ɔɔba awieeɛ he, na Yudafoɔ a befiri Asia huu no asɔrefie hɔ he, befirii aseɛ maa nnipa he yɛɛ gyegyeegye na bɛsosɔɔ ne mu teateaam sɛ, “Israel mmeema, hommɛboa yɛ!
Yei ne kyerɛkyerɛ nnipa nyinaa ya baabiaa de sɔre tia mane he ne Mmara ne bea yi, na nea ɔkyɛne ne nyinaa ne sɛ, ɔde Helafoɔ baa asɔrefie ha de beguu kronkronbea yi ho fi.” Na bɛadi kane ahu Efesoni Trofimo sɛ ɔka ne ho ya kuro he mu, na besusu sɛ Paulo de no baa asɔrefie hɔ.
Na kuro hɔ nyinaa yɛɛ gyegyeegye, na nnipa he nyinaa bɔɔ twi baeɛ.
Na bɛsosɔɔ Paulo mu twee no firii asɔrefie hɔ.
Na ntɛmaa bɛtotoo apono he mu.
Na berɛ a bɛɛhwehwɛ sɛ bebeku no he, asrafokuo so sahene he nyaa amanebɔ sɛ Yerusalem nyinaa ayɛ gyegyeegye; na ntɛmaa ɔfaa asraafoɔ ne bɛ mpanyimfoɔ kɔɔ bɛ so.
Berɛ a bɛ ani bɔɔ sahene he ne asraafoɔ he so he, begyae Paulo hweɛ.
Na sahene he bɛnee hɔ kɔsɔɔ ne mu hyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn mmienu ngu no.
Na ofirii aseɛ bisaa nipa ko a ɔyɛ ne nea wayɔ.
Nso nnipa he mu bi teaam kaa yei, na binom nso ateam aka asɛm foforɔ.
Nti berɛ a bɛantumi anhu asɛm he mu yie ɔnam sakasakayɛ he nti, ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa no mmra asraafoɔ asoeɛ hɔ.
Nso berɛ a oduruu dane-atwedeɛ he so he, osiane nnipakuo he basabasayɔ nti, asraafoɔ he maa no so.
Na nnipadɔm he kɔɔ so dii n’akyi teateaam sɛ, “Honyi no mfiri hɔ,” Paulo yii ne ho ano Na berɛ a bɛɛyɛ de no aduru asraafoɔ asoeɛ hɔ he, Paulo bisaa sahene he sɛ, “Mewɔ ho kwane sɛ meka asɛm bi kyerɛ ho anaa?” Obuaa sɛ, “Wobetumi aka Hela kasa?
Ɔnnyɛ wo ne Misraimni a nnansa yiaa wokɔfaa amammɔsɛm baeɛ a wode mmeema awudifoɔ mpemnan firii adi kɔɔ serɛ so he?” Paulo buaa sɛ, “Meyɛ Yudani a mefri Tarso a ɔya Kilikia, kuro a odi mu he mu.
Nti mesrɛ wo ma me kwane na me ne me manfoɔ he nkasa.” Berɛ a ɔmaa no kwane he, Paulo a na ogyina dane-atwedeɛ so he nyamm ne nsa kyerɛɛ nnipa he.
Afei berɛ a hɔ yɛɛ komm he, ɔde Hebri kasa ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ:
“Anuanom ne agyanom, hontie me na menyi nsɛm yi ano nkyerɛ ho.” Bɛtee sɛ ɔde Hebri kasa ne ɔɔkasa bɛ ho he, bɛyɛɛ dinn paa.
Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Meyɛ Yudani a bɛwoo me Tarso a ɔya Kilikia, nso bɛtetee me kuro yi mu, na metenaa Gamaliel nane ase suaa adeɛ.
Na ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ me nananom Mmara he pɛpɛɛpɛ, na mebɔɔ Nyamesom ho mmɔdene sɛnea ho nyinaa yɔ nnɛ yi.
Na metaa bɛ a bɛfa Yesu nkyerɛkyerɛɛ kwane so kosii sɛ mede binom mpo kɔɔ wuom.
Me kyekyee mmeema ne mmaa nyinaa ma bɛde bɛ guu afiase, sɔfopanyini ne mpanyimfoɔ badwa he nyinaa di me adanseɛ.
Megyegyee tumi-krataa firii bɛ hɔ de kɔmaa anuanom a bɛya Damasko.
Na mesiim sɛ meekɔ Damasko akɔkyekye nnipa a bɛya hɔ a bɛnam Yesu nkyerɛkyerɛɛ kwane so de bɛ aba Yerusalem ama bɛatwe bɛ aso.
“Na meekɔ a meeyɛ aduru Damasko, berɛ a na abɔ bɛyɛ awia dummienu he, mpofiremuaa, hann kɛseɛ bi hyerɛn firii soro twaa me ho hyiaeɛ, na metwa hwee fam, metee nne bi sɛ, ‘Saulo, Saulo, mmɛ nti na wotaa me?’ Mebuaa sɛ, ‘Wo ne hwane, owura?’ Na ɔka kyereɛ; me sɛ, ‘Ɔyɛ me Nasareni Yesu, a wotaa no he.’ Afei mmeema a bɛka me ho he huu hann he nso bɛante nne a na ɔne me ɔɔkasa he.
Na mekaa sɛ, “Owura, ɛɛne ne menyɔ?” Na Awurade ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Sɔre, kɔ Damasko na hɔ ne wobɛte bibiaa ɔsɛ sɛ woyɔ.” Na esiane sɛ na hann he hyerɛn kɛse paa nti, manhu hwee, na bɛ a me ne bɛ nam he sosɔɔ me nsa de me kɔɔ Damasko.
“Afei beema bi a bɛfrɛ no Anania a ɔyɛ nyamesuroni sɛnea Mmara he ɔɔhwehwɛ a Yudafoɔ a bɛtete hɔ nyinaa bɔ no dini pa he baa me nkyɛne, na obegyinaa me nkyɛne ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ “Onua Saulo, sane hu adeɛ!” Saa dɔno heaa mu, me sane huu adeɛ, na mehuu no.
Na afei ɔkaa sɛ, ‘Yɛ nananom Nyankopɔn ayi wo sɛ hu n’apɛdeɛ, na hu Teneneeni he na tie ɔno ankasa nne, efiri sɛ wobedi nea woahu na woate he ho adanseɛ akyerɛ nnipa nyinaa ama no.
Na afei mmɛ nti ne wootwentwɛne wo nane ase?
Sɔre, ma bɛmmɔ wo asu, nhohoro wo bɔne berɛ a wabɔ Awurade dini yi.’ “Nso berɛ a mesane baa Yerusalem a meebɔ mpaeɛ asɔrefie hɔ he, menyaa anisoadehunu.
Na mehuu Yesu sɛ ɔɔka akyerɛ me sɛ, ‘Ma wo ho nyɛ hare na firi Yerusalem ntɛm, efiri sɛ bɛmpene me ho adanseɛ a wodi he so.’ Na mekaa sɛ, ‘Awurade, bɛ ankasa benim pefee sɛ na mekye bɛ a bɛgye wo di he gu afiase hwe bɛ hyiadane ahodoɔ mu.
Na berɛ a beehwie wo danseni Stefano mogyaa agu he, na m’ankasa nso megyina hɔ bi a mepenee so, na mehwɛɛ bɛ a beeku no he ntaadeɛ ngugusoɔ so.’ Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, ‘Sɔre kɔ, efiri sɛ, mɛsoma wo akɔ Amanamane a ɔya akyirikyiri mu.’ ” Bɛkyee Paulo Na betiee no besii saa asɛm yi so, na bɛmaa bɛ nne so kaa sɛ, “Yi nipa yi firi asaase so, efiri sɛ ɔmfata sɛ ɔtena ase!” Na esiane sɛ na bɛɛteateam toto bɛ ntaadeɛ gu na beetu mfuturo gu mframa mu nti, sahene he hyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa no mmra asraafoɔ asoeɛ hɔ, na bentwa no mmaa mfa nhwehwɛ ne nsɛm mu, na ama wahu adeɛ pɔtee a nti bɛɛteateam gu no so saa he.
Na berɛ a bɛtwee Paulo mu a beebetwa no mmaa he, obisaa sraani panyini a ogyina hɔ he sɛ, “Nti mmara ma kwane sɛ hotwa Romani mmaa berɛ a hommuu no fɔ?” Sraani panyini he tee yei he, ɔkɔɔ sahene he nkyɛne kɔbɔɔ no amanneɛ sɛ, “Mmɛ ne wopɛ sɛ woyɔ yi?
Saa beema yi yɛ Romani” Nti sahene he baeɛ; bebisaa no sɛ, “Ka kyerɛ me, woyɛ Romani, anaa?” Na ɔkaa sɛ, “Ɛɛ!” Sahene he buaa sɛ, “Mede sika kɛseɛ paa ne tɔɔ Roma manbayɛ yi.” Na Paulo kaa sɛ, “Me mmom deɛ bɛwoo me toom.” Amonom hoaa bɛ a bɛɛbɛhwehwɛ ne nsɛm mu he firii ne nkyɛne kɔeɛ.
Na berɛ a sahene he huu sɛ ɔyɛ Romani na bɛakyekyere no he, osuroeɛ.
Bɛde Paulo kogyinaa asennibea Nti adeɛ kyeeɛ he, pɛɛ sɛ ohu adekorɔ pɔtee a nti Yudafoɔ he abɔ no so soboɔ he, ɔsanee no na ɔhyɛɛ asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ he ne Sanhedrin he nyinaa ma behyiaam.
Na ɔde Paulo begyinaa bɛ mfimfini.
Paulo hwɛɛ Sanhedrin badwa he gyee kaa sɛ, “Anuanom, mede ahonim pa abɔ me bra Nyankopɔn anim abesi nnɛ da yi.” Na sɔfo panyini Anania hyɛɛ bɛ a begyinagyina ne nkyɛne he sɛ bɛmmɔ no sotorɔ.
Na Paulo ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Nyankopɔn bɛbɔ wo, wo a wote sɛ fasuo a bɛaka ho fitaa.
Wotena ase bu me atɛne sɛnea Mmara he teɛ, na berɛ koro heaa nso woabu Mmara he so hyɛ sɛ bɛmmɔ me?” Bɛ a begyinagyina hɔ he kaa sɛ, “Nyankopɔn sɔfo panyini ne wo di no atɛm he?” Na Paulo kaa sɛ, “Anuanom, na mennim sɛ ɔyɛ sɔfo panyini.
Na bɛatwerɛ sɛ, ‘Nka wo mane sodifoɔ ho asɛmmɔne.’ ” Paulo huu sɛ nnipa he bi yɛ Sadukifoɔ na binom nso yɛ Farisifoɔ he, ɔteaa mu Sanhedrin badwa he mu sɛ, “Anuanom, meyɛ Farisini, Farisifoɔ ba.
Wusɔreɛ ho anidasoɔ ho nti ne beebu me atɛne yi.” Ɔkaa yei he, akasakasaa baa Farisifoɔ ne Sadukifoɔ he mu, na nnipa he mu kyɛeɛ.
(Sadukifoɔ he ka sɛ wusɔreɛ anaa abɔfoɔ anaa honhom nni hɔ, na Farisifoɔ he deɛ, bɛgye yeinom nyinaa di sɛ bɛya hɔ.)
Nti hɔ yɛɛ gyegyeegye, na atwerɛfoɔ a befiri Farisifoɔ kuo mu binom sɔre kasakasa dendenndene sɛ, “Yenhu mfomsoɔ biaa nipa yi ho, efiri sɛ ebia na honhom anaa bɔfoɔ bi ne akasa kyerɛ no.” Afei berɛ a akasakasaa he mu yɛɛ dene he, na sahene he suro sɛ bɛbɛtete Paulo mu asisinasini, nti ɔhyɛɛ asraafoɔ he sɛ bɛnkɔgye no mfiri bɛ nsa mu mfa no mmra asraafoɔ asoeɛ hɔ.
Saa anadwo he Awurade begyinaa ne nkyɛne kaa sɛ, “Nya akokoɔduro!
Sɛnea wo adi me ho adanseɛ Yerusalem he, saa ara nso ne otwa sɛ wodi me ho adanseɛ Roma nso.” Bɛbɔɔ Paulo ti so pɔ Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, Yudafoɔ he bɔɔ Paulo ti so pɔ kekaa bɛ ho ntam sɛ, bennidi na bɛnnom kosi sɛ bebeku no.
Nnipa bɛboro aduannan ne kɔɔ saa apam yi.
Bɛkɔɔ sɔfo panyini ne mpanyimfoɔ he hɔ kɔkaa sɛ, “Yɛaka ntam dendenndene sɛ, sɛ yenkuu Paulo a, yɛmfa aduane nka yɛ ano.
Nti afei, ho ne badwa he mma sahene nte sɛ ho pɛ sɛ ɔde no bra ho na hohwehwɛ n’asɛm he mu fann.
Na yɛ deɛ, yɛmma no nnuru ha mpo na yɛaku no.” Na Paulo wɔfaseɛ tee sɛ nkurofoɔ he akɔtɛ no; nti ɔkɔ kɔhyɛnee abane he mu koyii Paulo asotire.
Na Paulo frɛɛ asraafoɔ ha so mpanyimfoɔ he mu baako ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Fa abranteɛ yi kɔ safohene nkyɛne, na ɔwɔ asɛm bi ka kyerɛ no.” Na ɔfaa no de no kɔɔ safohene he nkyɛne kaa sɛ, “Deduani Paulo frɛɛ me, na ɔka kyerɛɛ me sɛ memfa abranteɛ yi mmra wo, na ɔwɔ asɛm bi ka kyerɛ wo.” Na safohene he sɔɔ ne nsa na ɔne no no kɔɔ kokoam baabi.
Na obisaa no sɛ, “Ɛɛne ne wowɔ ka kyerɛ me?” Obuaa sɛ, “Yudafoɔ he ayɔ adwene sɛ bɛbɛsrɛ wo na wode Paulo aba dwam kyena sɛnea bebebisa ne ho asɛm mu yie.
Nso ntie bɛ!
Na bɛ mu mmeema bɛboro aduannan ɔɔtɛ no, na bakeka bɛ ho ntam sɛ bennidi na bɛnnom gye sɛ bɛaku no ansa.
Seesei bɛayɛ krado, na bɛɛtwɛne sɛ wobɛma bɛ hõ kwane.” Na safohene he gyaa abranteɛ he kwane na ɔhyɛɛ no sɛ, “Nka nkyerɛ biaa sɛ woayi me asɛm yi ho asotire.” Bɛde Paulo kɔmaa Felike ya Kaesarea Afei ɔfrɛɛ asraafoɔ ha so mpanyimfoɔ he mu mmienu bi kaa sɛ, “Honsiesie asraafoɔ ahaanu, apɔnkɔsotefoɔ aduɔson, ne peakurafoɔ ahanu, anadwo nnɔnkron berɛ mu nkɔ Kaesarea.
Afei nso bensiesie mmoa na bɛmfa Paulo ntena so mfa no dwoodwoo nkɔma Amrado Felike.” Na ɔtwerɛɛ nwoma a mu asɛm ne sɛ: “Klaudio Lisia de krataa yi kyea Amrado pa Felike.
Beema yi a Yudafoɔ kɔfaa no sɛ nka bebeku no na me ne m’asraafoɔ kɔgyee no he, maate sɛ ɔyɛ Romani.
Na mepɛɛ sɛ nka mehu adekodeɛ a bɛde ɔɔbɔ no kwaadu he, na mede no kɔɔ bɛ badwam.
Na mehuu sɛ bɛ mmara ho nsemmisa nti ne bɛne no wɔ nkurobɔ, na bɛamfa bibi a ɔsɛ wuo anaa kyeɛ anto no so.
Nso bɛayi me asotire sɛ nnipa bi ɔɔtɛ beema he.
Nti meema bɛde no abra wo, na maahyɛ ne nkurobɔfoɔ he sɛ bɛmmɛka nea bɛwɔ fa ne ho w’anim.” Nti asraafoɔ he faa Paulo, sɛnea bɛhyɛɛ bɛ he, na bɛde no kɔɔ Antipatri anadwo he.
Na adeɛ kyeeɛ he, bɛmaa apɔnkɔsotefoɔ he ne no toaa so kɔeɛ, na asraafoɔ he sane baa abane he mu bio.
Na beduruu Kaesarea he, beyii nwoma he maa amrado he, na bɛde Paulo nso kogyinaa n’anim.
Na amrado he kenkane nwoma he wieeɛ he, obisaa mane korɔ a ofiri mu; na ɔtee sɛ ofiri Kilikia he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Wo nkurobɔfoɔ he ba a, na metie wo.” Na ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa no nsie Herode abane mu.
Tertulo bɔɔ somafoɔ he ho nkuro Nnanum akyi he, sɔfo panyini Anania ne mpanyimfoɔ bi ne Tertulo a ogyina badwa anim kasa he baeɛ.
Na bɛde Paulo ho nsɛm bɛtoo amrado he anim.
Berɛ a bɛfrɛɛ Paulo baeɛ he, Tertulo hyɛɛ aseɛ bɔɔ no kwaadu sɛ: Nimuonyamfoɔ Felike, esiane sɛ ɔnam wo so ne yenya asomdwie, na wo, ne wo nhunumu ama nsakraeɛ aba mane yi mu nti, yɛde aseda a ɔkyɛne so gye yeinom berɛ nyinaa ya baabiaa.
Nso sɛ ɔbɛyɔ na mennsɛe wo brɛ pii bio nti, mesrɛ wo sɛ firi w’anyamyɛ mu tie yɛ kakra.
Yɛahu beema yi sɛ busuyefoɔ a otutu gu Yudafoɔ nyinaa asom ma bɛte atua asaase nyinaa so, na ɔyɛ Nasarefoɔ kuo he mu panyini.
Na ɔnoaa nso ne bɔɔ ne ho mmɔdene sɛ obegu asɔrefie he ho fi ma yɛkyee no.
Na nka yebetumi abu no atene sɛ nea Mmara he teɛ.
Wo ankasa wobetumi abisabisa no ahu nea yɛde ɔɔbɔ no soboɔ yi nyinaa mu.
Yudafoɔ he nso de bɛ ho gyee mu bi sɛ, nsɛm yi te saa.
Paulo yii ne ho ano Felike anim Berɛ a amrado he maa Paulo kwane sɛ ɔnkasa he, obuaa sɛ, “Esiane sɛ menim yie sɛ woayɔ mane yi temmufoɔ mfie pii nti, ɔyɛ me anigyeɛ sɛ meeyi m’ano m’asɛm yi ho.
Sɛnea wobetumi anyɔ nhwehwemu ahu he, mekɔɔ Yerusalem kɔsomeeɛ he, onni mmoroo nnafua dummienu.
Ɔnyɛ adeɛ a behuu me sɛ me ne bi agye akyinnye ya asɔrefie hɔ anaa meehyɛ nnipakuo bi kutupa de basabasayɔ aba hyia adane anaa kuro he mu.
Na bentumi nso nya soboɔ a bɛɛbɔ me seeseiaa yi ho adanseɛ mma wo.
Nso megye nɔkwasɛm yi tom ya w’anim sɛ nea bɛfrɛ no fekusɛm yiaa ne Kwane a menam so som me nananom Nyankopɔn, efiri sɛ megye nea Mmara he ka na bɛatwerɛ Adiyifoɔ nwoma he mu he di.
Na mewɔ anidasoɔ ya Nyankopɔn mu, a bɛ nso bɛwɔ saa anidasoɔ heaa bi, sɛ berɛ bi bɛba a bɛ a bɛtene ne bɛ a bɛntene nyinaa bɛsɔre afiri awufoɔ mu.
Nti berɛ nyinaa mehwɛ hu sɛ menyɔ bɔne biaa ntiaa Nyankopɔn ne nnipa.
Nti mekokyinkyinii Amaneamane mu mfie kakra he, mesane baa Yerusalem de adɔeyɛdeɛ ne ayɛyɛdeɛ braa me mane.
Berɛ a meeyɔ yei he behuu me asɔrefie hɔ sɛ meedwira me ho, nso na nnipakuo anaa hooyɔ biaa nni hɔ.
Mmom, na Yudafoɔ bi a befiri Asia mantam he mu ne bɛya hɔ, na nka ɔsɛ sɛ bɛba w’anim na sɛ bɛwɔ bibi tia me a, bɛde ato dwa.
Anaa, ma mmeema yi ankasa nka bɔne a behuu sɛ meyɔeɛ berɛ a na megyina Sanhedrin he anim he.
Menkaa hwee gye asɛm baako yi a meteaa mu kaa sɛ, ‘Awufoɔ sɔreeɛ nti ne beebu me atɛne ho anim nnɛ yi!’ ” Nso esiane sɛ na Felike nim Kwane he ho asɛm yie nti, otuu nkurofoɔ he nsɛm he hyɛɛ da kaa sɛ, “Berɛ biaa sahene Lisia bɛba he, mebu nsɛm yi ho atɛne.” Na ɔhyɛɛ asraafoɔ ha so panyini he sɛ ɔnhwɛ Paulo so na bɛannha no, na bɛmmara ne ho nipa biaa a ɔbɛba abɛsra no.
Felike tuu asɛm he hyɛɛ mfie mmienu akyi Nna bi akyi he, Felike ne ne yerɛ Drusila a ɔyɛ Yudani he baeɛ, na ɔsoma ma bɛkɔfrɛɛ Paulo baeɛ, na betiee nea ɔwɔ ka fa Kristo Yesu mu gyidie ho.
Afei berɛ a Paulo kaa tenenee, ahohyɛsoɔ ne atemmuo a ɔbɛba ho asɛm he, hu kaa Felike ma ɔkaa sɛ, “Firi m’anim ha kɔ, na sɛ menya berɛ a mɛsane asoma abɛfrɛ wo.” Nso saa berɛ yi nyinaa na n’ani da so sɛ Paulo bɛma no sika.
Nti na ɔtaa soma kɔfrɛ no ne no bɛbɔ nkɔmmɔ.
Mfie mmienu akyi he, Porkio Festo bedii Felike adeɛ, na esiane sɛ na Felike pɛ sɛ onya Yudafoɔ he anim adom nti, ɔmaa Paulo kɔɔ soaa daa afiase.
Paulo de n’asɛm kɔdanee Kaesare Afei Festo baa ne mane a odi so amrado he mu.
Na nnansa akyi, ofiri Kaesarea kɔɔ Yerusalem.
Na asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ ne Yudafoɔ atitire he bɛkaa Paulo ho nsɛmmɔne kyerɛɛ no.
Na befirii aseɛ paa no kyɛw srɛɛ sɛ ɔnyɔ bɛ adom nsoma nkɔfrɛ beema he mmra Yerusalem.
Na bɛabɔ pɔ paa sɛ bɛbɛtɛ kwane ho aku no.
Nso Festo buaa sɛ bɛde Paulo ato afiase ya Kaesarea na ɔɔnnkyɛre biaa ɔnoaa nso bɛkɔ.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Nti homma bɛ a bɛya ho mu a bɛyɔ tumi he ne me nkɔ, na sɛ bibi a ɔmfa kwane mu ya beema he ho a, bɛabɔ no soboɔ.” Nti berɛ a odii bɛ nkyɛne bɛyɛ nnawɔtwe anaa dadu he, ɔsane kɔɔ Kaesarea, na adeɛ kyeeɛ he, ɔtenaa atemmuo adwa so hyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa Paulo mmra.
Berɛ a Paulo baeɛ he, Yudafoɔ a na befiri Yerusalem he betwaa ne ho hyiaeɛ, kaa nsɛm akɛseɛ bebree guu ne so a bɛantumi amfa ho adanseɛ biaa amma.
Paulo yii ne ho ano sɛ, “Menyɔɔ bɔne biaa a otia Yudafoɔ Mmara anaa asɔrefie he anaa Kaesare.” Afei esiane sɛ Festo pɛ sɛ onya Yudafoɔ he anim adom nti, obisaa Paulo sɛ, “Wopɛ sɛ wokɔ Yerusalem na bedi asɛm he m’anim anaa?” Na Paulo buaa sɛ, “Megyina Kaesare atemmuo adwa anim, na ha na ɔsɛ sɛ bedi m’asɛm.
Menyɛɛ Yudafoɔ bɔne biaa, sɛnea wo ankasa wonnim no pefee he.
Nso sɛ meyɛ bɔnefoɔ a maayɔ bibiaa a ɔsɛ sɛ mewu a, mennwane wuo he; nso sɛ nea bɛde ato me so yi mu biaa nnim a, biaa ntumi mfa me nnhyɛ bɛ nsa mfa mpata bɛ.
Mede asɛm he dane Kaesare.” Afei Festo ne abadwafoɔ he de bɛ ti sɛɛ ho he, Festo buaa sɛ, “Kaesare ne wode asɛm he akɔdane no nti, Kaesare hɔ ne wobɛkɔ.” Festo kaa Paulo ho asɛm kyerɛ Herode Agripa Nna bi akyi he, Hene Agrippa ne Berenike baa Kaesarea bɛkyeaa Festo.
Na esiane sɛ na bebedi nna kakra ya hɔ nti, Festo de Paulo asɛm he too hene he anim sɛ, “Beema bi ya ha a Felike gyae no afiase, na berɛ a meya Yerusalem he, asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ ne Yudafoɔ mpanyimfoɔ de ne ho asɛm baeɛ, srɛɛ sɛ memmu no fɔ.
Na mebuaa bɛ sɛ ɔnnyɛ Romafoɔ amanneɛ sɛ bebu bi fɔ ama bɛ a bɛabɔ no soboɔ berɛ a onii he nyaa ho kwane nyii ne ho ano bɛ anim.
Nti berɛ a bebehyia ha he, mantwentwɛne me nane ase koraa, na adeɛ kyeeɛaa na metenaa atemmuo adwa so hyɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa beema he mmra.
Ɔsɔre gyinaeɛ he, bɛ a bɛɛbɔ no soboɔ he antumi anka ne ho asɛmmɔne biaa sɛnea mesusuiɛ he.
Ɔne sɛ, bɛne no dii anobaabaeɛ faa bɛ ankasa bɛ som ne Yesu bi a owuiɛ a Paulo ka dendenndene sɛ ɔte ase he ho.
Afei na menhu nea menyɔ mfa anobaabaeɛ yi ho, nti mebisaa sɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔkɔ Yerusalem na bekodi asɛm he ya hɔ anaa.
Nso berɛ a Paulo srɛɛ sɛ bɛmfa no nkɔto afiase nkosi berɛ a Tumfoɔ he bebua asɛm he, mehyɛɛ sɛ bɛnhwɛ ne so nkosi sɛ mede no bɛkɔ akɔma Kaesare.” Na Agrippa ka kyerɛɛ Festo sɛ, “Mɛpɛ sɛ me ankasa metie beema he ano asɛm.” Ɔkaa sɛ, “Kyena wobɛte n’ano asɛm.” Bɛde Paulo kogyinaa Agripa anim Nti adeɛ kyeeɛ he Agrippa ne Benike baeɛ a na bɛahyehyɛ bɛ ho dɔsɔɔ, na bɛ ne asahene ne kuro he mu atitire he kɔɔ baabi a betie asɛm he, na Festo maa bɛde Paulo baeɛ.
Na Festo kaa sɛ, “Hene Agrippa ne nnipa a hoka yɛ ho ya ha nyinaa, beema a ho ani tua no yi yɛ bi a Yudafoɔ dɔm he srɛɛ me Yerusalem ne ha nso, teateaam sɛ ɔnsɛ sɛ ɔtena nkwa mu bio.
Nso mehuu sɛ ɔnyɔɔ bibiaa ɔfata sɛ owu.
Nti berɛ a ɔde asɛm he danee Tumfoɔ he, meyɔɔ m’adwene sɛ mede no bɛkɔ.
Nso mennim asɛm a mentwerɛ mfa ne ho nkɔma yɛ Wura.
Nti mede no baa ho anim, titire wo Hene Agrippa, na sɛ wohwehwɛ asɛm he mu wie a, manya bibi atwerɛ, efiri sɛ nyansa biaa nnim sɛ mede deduani bɛkɔ a menkyerɛ asɛm a bɛde ato no so he.”
Paulo yii n’ano ya Agripa anim Agrippa ka kyerɛɛ Paulo sɛ, “Wowɔ ho kwane sɛ woyi w’ano.” Na Paulo tenee ne nsa firi aseɛ yii ne ho ano sɛ, “Ɔyɛ me dɛ sɛ sommoɔ a Yudafoɔ de abɔ me nyinaa he, wo Hene Agrippa w’anim ne meebeyi m’ano nnɛ da yi, ne titire ne sɛ wonim amanneɛ nyinaa ne akyinnyegyeɛ a ɔya Yudafoɔ mu.
Ne saa nti mesrɛ wo, to wo bo ase na tie me.
“Yudafoɔ nyinaa nim me firi me mmabunuberɛ mu, asetena a mehyɛɛ aseɛ meaa mekuro mu ne Yerusalem.
Benim me firi mmerɛtentene, na bɛpɛ a bebetumi adi ho adanseɛ sɛ, mebɔɔ mebra sɛnea yɛ som mu amanneɛ teɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ sɛ Farisini.
Na seesei bɔhyɛ a Nyankopɔn de maa yɛ agyanom ho adanseɛ nti ne megyina atemmuo adwa anim yi; na yɛ mmusuakuo dummienu he som Nyankopɔn anibereɛ so, awia ne anadwo a bɛ ani da so sɛ bɛ nsa bɛka saa bɔhyɛ yi.
Nimuonyamfoɔ, saa anidasoɔ yi ho na Yudafoɔ abɔ me soboɔ yi.
“Mmɛ nti ne honnye nni sɛ Nyankopɔn nyane awufoɔ?
“Me nso, na medwene me mu sɛ ɔsɛ sɛ meyɔ nnoɔma pii de ko tia Nasareni Yesu dini, na saa pɛpɛɛpɛ ne meyɔeɛ Yerusalem, na menyaa tumi firii asɔfo mpanyimfoɔ he hɔ de ahoteefoɔ bebree guu afiase, na sɛ beeku bɛ a mefoa so.
Na metwee bɛ aso mprɛ pii hyia adane nyinaa mu sɛnea bɛbɛka bibi de apo bɛ gyidie.
Na esiane m’ani a na abere bɛ so paa nti, mekɔɔ nkuro foforɔ so mpo kɔtaa bɛ hɔ.
Paulo adwensakra ho asɛm “Berɛ a megu so ɔɔyɔ yie he mede tumi ne ahyɛdeɛ a menya firii asɔfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ hɔ he siim sɛ meekɔ Damasko.
Na oduruu awigyina he, me wura Nimuonyamfoɔ, mehuu hann bi a ano ɔdene sene awia sɛ ahyerɛn firi soro atwa me ne bɛ a bɛne me ɔɔkɔ he ho ahyia kwane he so.
Na berɛ a yɛ nyinaa hwehwee fam he, metee sɛ nne bi ka kyerɛɛ me Hebri kasa mu sɛ, ‘Saulo, Saulo, mmɛ nti ne wootaa me?
Sɛ woto boɔ bɔ dane a ɔba woaa wo so.’ Na mebisaa sɛ, ‘Ɔyɛ wo hwane, owura?’ Na Awurade ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, ‘Ɔyɛ me Yesu a wotaa no he.
Afei, sɔre gyina.
Na yei nti ne mama woahu me, sɛ meeyi wo sɛ somfoɔ ne adansefoɔ nea woahu ne nea mɛma woahu afa me ho nyinaa ho.
Na mɛgye wo nso afiri mmane yi ne Amanamane a meesoma wo akɔ bɛ nkyɛne he nsam, na woabie bɛ ani, adane bɛ afiri sum mu aba hann mu, na bɛafiri Satan tumi mu aba Nyankopɔn nkyɛne, na bɛanya bɔne fakyɛ ne agyapadeɛ bɛ a bɛnam me mu gyidie so ate bɛ ho mu.’ “Yei akyi he, Hene Agrippa, manyɔ anisoadeɛ a menya firii soro he ho asoɔdene, na mmom, medii kane kasa kyerɛɛ Damaskofoɔ.
Na afei mekɔɔ Yerusalem, ne Yudea mantam nyinaa mu, ne amanamane mufoɔ hɔ kɔkaa sɛ, sɛ bɛnsakra bɛ adwene na bɛmfa nnwuma a ɔkyerɛ adwensakra so nane mmra Nyankopɔn nkyɛne.
Yei nti ne Yudafoɔ kyee me asɔrefie hɔ pɛɛ sɛ beku me.
Nso mmoa a manya afiri Nyankopɔn nkyɛne nti ne makɔ so atena hɔ abesi nnɛ a megyina ha oodi adanseɛ akyerɛ nipasu ahodoɔ nyinaa yi, menkaa hwee, gye nsɛm a Adiyifoɔ he ne Mose kaeɛ sɛ ɔbɛba he, sɛ Kristo he behu amane, na esiane sɛ bɛadi kane anyane no afiri awufoɔ mu nti, wabɔ hann ho dawuro akyerɛ, nkurofoɔ yi ne Amanamane he.” Paulo tuu Agripa fo sɛ ɔnnye Kristo nni Afei berɛ a ɔɔka nsɛm yi de ayi n’ano he, Festo de nne kɛseɛ teaam sɛ, “Paulo, woobɔ dam!
Adesua pii ɔɔyɛ ama woabɔ dam!” Na Paulo kaa sɛ, “Ɔnyɛ dam ne meebɔ, Nimuonyamfoɔ Festo, na mmom meeka nsɛm a ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ na ɔtɔ asom.
Nɔkwasɛm di, hene a mede akokoɔduro ɔɔkasa akyerɛ no yi nim saa nsɛm yi mu yie, na menim sɛ nsɛm yi mu biaa nni hɔ a ahinta no, efiri sɛ ɔnyɛ adeɛ a bɛyɔɔ no kokoam.
Hene Agrippa, nti wogye Adiyifoɔ he di?
Menim sɛ wogye bɛ di.” Na Agrippa ka kyerɛɛ Paulo sɛ, “Nti wodwene sɛ wobetumi de berɛ tiaa yi ama me abɛyɛ Kristoni anaa?” Na Paulo buaa sɛ, “Sɛ menya a, nka berɛ tiaa bi oo, bere tentene bi oo, ɔnyɛ wo nkoa, na mmom nka Nyankopɔn nyɔ bɛ a beetie me nnɛ yi nyinaa nso sɛnea meteɛ yi, na mmom bengu ho mpokyerɛ sɛ me.” Na hene he ne amrado he ne Berenike ne mmeema a bɛne bɛ tete hɔ he sɔreeɛ.
Na berɛ a bɛɛkɔ he, asɛm a na bɛkaa ne sɛ, “Aa!
Nipa yi nyɔɔ bibiaa a ɔsɛ sɛ owu anaa begu no mpokyerɛ.” Afei nso Agrippa ka kyerɛɛ Festo sɛ, “Sɛ ɔnyɛ sɛ nipa yi de asɛm he akɔdane Kaesare a, nka bebetumi agyae.”
Paulo sii mu kɔɔ Roma Na afei besii gyinaeɛ wieeɛ sɛ yɛnkɔ Italia he, bɛde Paulo ne nneduafoɔ bi hyɛɛ panyini bi a ne dini de Yulio a ofiri Roma Tumfoɔ asraafoɔ kuo he mu nsa.
Yɛkɔtenaa Adramitio hyɛne bi a na ɔɔkɔ Asia fam he mu.
Na Makedoniani Aristarko a ofiri Tesalonika he ka yɛ ho.
Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, yekoduruu Sidon.
Yulio yii dɔ adi kyerɛɛ Paulo sɛ ɔmaa ne kwane maa no kɔsraa ne nnamfo sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a bɛbɛma no nnoɔma a ho hia no he.
Esiane sɛ yetuu hɔ he, na mframa ɔɔbɔ hyia yɛ nti, yɛka kɔɔ Kipro nifa fam.
Yɛnam po so kɔfaa Kilikia ne Pamfilia koduruu Mira a ɔya Likia mantam mu he mu.
Hɔ ne asraafoɔ panyini he huu hyɛne bi a ofiri Aleksandria ɔɔkɔ Italia.
Nti ɔde yɛ kɔtenaa mu.
Hyɛne he kɔɔ bɔkɔɔ ma yedii nna pii ya po he so.
Yɛbrɛeɛ ansa na yeeduru Kinido.
Esiane sɛ na mframa ɔɔbɔ hyia yɛ nti, yɛfaa Kreta anaafoɔ fam baabi a na hɔ dwo sanee Salmone ho.
Yɛka kɔɔ mpoano nkakrankakra kosii sɛ yebeduruu baabi a bɛfrɛ hɔ Hyɛne-Agyinaeɛ-Pa a ɔbɛne kuro Lasea.
Yedii nna pii po he so, na osiane sɛ na mmuadadie he mpo atwam, na saa berɛ he ɔɔkɔ afe he awieeɛ a po so fa ayɛ hu nti, yɛtenaa hɔ kyɛreeɛ.
Paulo tuu bɛ fo sɛ, “Anuanom, mehu sɛ, sɛ yɛtoa yɛ akwantuo yi so a, yebehu amane ama ebia hyɛne he mpo abɔ ama mu nnoɔma asɛe ama mu nnipa ahwere bɛ nkwa.” Nso asraafoɔ panyini he antie Paulo afutuo he, na mmom otiee nsɛm a hyɛnkafoɔ he ne hyɛne he wura kaeɛ he.
Osiane sɛ na hyɛngyinabea hɔ nyɛ mma bɛ sɛ bɛbɛtena hɔ awɔ berɛ mu he nti, nnipa he pii pɛɛ sɛ, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ yie a, nka hyɛne he betu afiri hɔ akɔ Foinike, a ɔyɛ hyɛngyinabea a ɔya Kreta a ɔda atifi ne anafoɔ ntam ya atɔeɛ fam, ɔyɛ baabi a bebetumi atena hɔ awɔberɛ mu.
Ahum tuu po he so Mframa a ano ɔdene bɔ firii anafoɔ fam.
Yei maa nnipa he susuu sɛ bebetumi atoa bɛ akwantuo he so sɛnea bɛahyehyɛ he.
Nti betuu sɛkyɛ he de hyɛne he faa Kreta mpoano.
Ankyɛre koraa ne mframa kɛseɛ bi a bɛfrɛ no “Atifi Apieɛ Mframa” bɔ firii supɔ he so.
Mframa he bɔ bunkam faa yɛ hyɛne he so twee no kɔɔ po he mu.
Yɛbɔɔ mmɔdene sɛ yɛbɛdane hyɛne he ani na anyɛ yie he, yegyae maa mframa he twee no kɔeɛ.
Yeduruu supɔ ketewa bi a bɛfrɛ no Klauda ho a na hɔ mframa ano nyɛ dene mpo he, yɛbrɛeɛ ansa na yeetumi atwe kodoɔ a ɔsɛne hyɛne he akyi he aba mu.
Hyɛne he mu adwumayɔfoɔ maa so baa hyɛne he mu, kyekyeree no dendenndene.
Osiane sɛ na besuro sɛ bɛbɛkɔ akotim anwea mu nti, beyiyii hyɛne dua he so ntoma maa mframa he bɔɔ hyɛne he kɔɔ faako a ɔpɛ.
Ahum he kɔɔ so tuu dendenndene kosii sɛ adeɛ kyeeɛ mpo, beyiyii hyɛne he mu nnoɔma he bi to guu po he mu.
Ne nnansa so he, bɛsesaa hyɛne he ho nnoɔma he bi to guiɛ.
Nna bebree twaa mu a na yenhu awia anaa nsoromma a na ahum he gu so ootu.
Yei maa yɛ anidasoɔ nyinaa saeɛ.
Paulo kyekyeree bɛ werɛ Nna bebree twaa mu a na biaa nnidiiɛ.
Afei Paulo ka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Anuanom, sɛ hotiee me na yɛantu amfiri Kreta a, nka ɔnyɛ ɔno ne sɛ yeehu amane yi.
Nso homma ho bo ntɔ ho yam, efiri sɛ, ho mu biaa oonwu na mmom hyɛne he ne bɛbɔ.
Nnora anadwo, Nyankopɔn a meyɛ ne deɛ a mesom no he bɔfoɔ baa me nkyɛne bɛka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, ‘Paulo, nsuro!
Nea obesi biaa wobeduru Kaesare anim ama wadi w’asɛm.
Bɛ a bɛka wo ho yi nso, Nyankopɔn adom nti, bibiaa ɔnyɔ bɛ.’ Anuanom, homma ho bo ntɔ ho yam, efiri sɛ, megye Nyankopɔn di na asɛm a waka akyerɛ me he bɛba mu pɛpɛɛpɛ.
Nso nea ɔbɛyɛ biaa, mframa bɛbɔ hyɛne he de yɛ akogu supɔ bi mpoano.” Ne nnawɔtwe mmienu anadwo he a na ahum he nti hyɛne he oodi akɔneaba ya Adria po so he, dasuom ne hyɛne he mu adwumayɔfoɔ huu sɛ yɛɛbɛne asaase.
Bɛtoo susuhoma huu sɛ nsuo he mu tentene yɛ anammɔno ha-aduonu; ɔyɛɛ kakra a besusu bio he, behuu sɛ ɔyɛ anammɔn aduɔkron.
Osiane sɛ na besuro sɛ anhwɛ a hyɛne he bɛpem abotane bi nti, bɛtoo asɛkyɛ nnan firii hyɛne he akyi, na bɛtwɛne sɛ adeɛ bɛkye.
Hyɛne he mu adwumayɔfoɔ pɛɛ sɛ bedwane firi hyɛne he mu.
Nti begyaa kodoɔ a na ɔsene hyɛne akyi he sii po he ani boapa yɛɛ sɛnea bɛɛkɔto sɛkyɛ ya hyɛne he anim.
Paulo ka kyerɛɛ asraafoɔ panyini he ne asraafoɔ a bɛka ne ho he sɛ, “Sɛ hyɛne yi mu adwumayɔfoɔ he dwane a, hobewuwu.” Yei nti, asraafoɔ he twaa homa a ɔkyekyere kodoɔ he mu he ma ɔkɔeɛ.
Adeɛ ɔɔyɛ akye he, Paulo srɛɛ bɛ nyinaa sɛ bennidi.
Nea ɔkaeɛ ne sɛ, “Nnawɔtwe mmienu di, ho mu biaa nni hwee.
Mesrɛ ho, biaa mfa bibi nka n’ano sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a hobenya ahoɔdene, na bibiaa ɔnyɔ ho mu biaa.” Paulo kasa wieeɛ he, ɔfaa paanoo bɔɔ mpaeɛ, daa Nyankopɔn ase bɛ nyinaa bɛ anim, na obuu bi diiɛ.
Amonom hɔaa nnipa he nyinaa bo tɔɔ bɛ yam ma befirii aseɛ didiiɛ.
(Na yɛ a na yɛya hyɛne he mu he dodoɔ yɛ nnipa ahanu ne aduɔson nsia.)
Biaa didi meeɛ he, hyɛne he mu adwumayɔfoɔ he too aburo a ɔya hyɛne he mu he guu po he mu maa hyɛne he mu yɛɛ hare.
Suhyɛn he bɔeɛ Adeɛ kyeeɛ he, hyɛne he mu adwumayɔfoɔ he anhu sɛ bɛaduru mpoano.
Behuu baabi a po he adidi akɔ asaase he mu a nsuo taa hɔ.
Nti bɛyɔɔ bɛ adwene sɛ bɛbɛka hyɛne he akogyina.
Yei nti betwitwaa hyɛne he asɛkyɛ ahoma mu maa asɛkyɛ he guu po mu.
Afei bɛsansanee homa a okita akyerɛkyerɛkwane he mu na afei besii ntoma a ɔya hyɛne he anim he sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a mframa betumi abɔ hyɛne he akɔ mpoano.
Nso hyɛne he kɔpemm anweatam bi ma otimiiɛ.
Hyɛne he anim tim dendenndene na n’akyi he nso, asorɔkye a na ɔɔbɔ no he maa obubuiɛ.
Asraafoɔ he yɛɛ bɛ adwene sɛ bebekuku nneduafoɔ he nyinaa sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a biaa oonnya kwane nnwane.
Nso osiane sɛ na asraafoɔ panyini he pɛ sɛ ɔgye Paulo nkwa he nti, wamma bɛ ho kwane.
Mmom, ɔhyɛɛ sɛ bɛ a bebetumi adware he mfiti aseɛ nnware nkɔ mpoano.
Bɛ a bɛaka he nso mu binom tetaree ntaaboo ne nnua asisinasini a abubu firi hyɛne he mu he so kɔɔ mpoano.
Saa kwane yi so ne yɛnam beduruu mpoano hɔ dwoodwoo.
Paulo ya Malta supɔ so Berɛ a yekoduruu dwodwo he, yehuu sɛ bɛfrɛ supɔ he Malta.
Na nnipa a bɛya hɔ he yɛ pɔtɔfoɔ; na bɛdaa ayamyɛ sononko adi kyerɛɛ yɛ.
Na nsuo a na ɔɔtɔ ne awɔ a na ɔyam nti, bɛsɔɔ gya maa yɛ de gyee yɛ nyinaa fɛ so.
Nso berɛ a Paulo boaboaa mmabaa bi ano a na ɔde oogu gya he mu he, ɔnam hyeɛ a na ofiri gya he mu ɔɔba nti, wɔ bi firii mmabaa he mu bɛto momanee ne nsa ho.
Berɛ a pɔtɔfoɔ he ani bɔɔ wɔ he so sɛ ɔsɛne ne nsa ho he, bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, “Akyinnye biaa nni hɔ sɛ nipa yi yɛ wudifoɔ, na ɔyam sɛ waafiri po he mu afiri dwoodwoo deɛ, nso aweretɔ nti, ɔmma sɛ obenya ne ti adidi mu.” Nso Paulo petee wɔ he too gya he mu a hwee anyɔ no.
Na bɛ deɛ, na bɛhwɛ kwane sɛ ɔɔbɛhonhono anaa oobetwa ahwe awu amonom hɔaa.
Berɛ a bɛtwɛne berɛ tentene a bɛanhu sɛ bɔne bi ato no he, bɛsesaa bɛ adwene firii aseɛ kaa sɛ ɔyɛ nyame.
Afei na supɔ he so kunyini a bɛfrɛ no Publio he wɔ nsaase ya mpɔtamu hɔ.
Na ɔgyee yɛ fɛ so de nnansa som yɛ hɔhoɔ fɛ so.
Nso ɔbaa sɛ na Publio papa da hɔ a abunu ne konkoriwa akye no, na Paulo kɔɔ ne nkyɛne kɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ de ne nsa guu ne so saa no yadeɛ.
Yei akyi he, supɔ he so nnipa a aka a bɛwɔ nyarewa nso firii aseɛ baa ne nkyɛne maa ɔsaa bɛ yadeɛ.
Na bɛ nso bɛde akyɛdeɛ pii dii yɛ ni, na berɛ a yeefiri hɔ akɔ he, bɛmaa yɛ nnoɔma pii a ho behia yɛ.
Paulo koduruu Roma Abosome mmeɛnsa akyi he, yɛforoo hyɛne bi a ofiri Aleksandria a obedii awɔberɛ supɔ he so a n’agyinahyɛdeɛ ne “Po so Abosom Ntaafoɔ”.
Na yekogyinaa Sirakuse dii hɔ nnansa, hɔ ne yefiri kontono koduruu Regio.
Na da a odi hɔ he, anaafoɔ mframa bi bɔeɛ, na ne nnanu so he yekoduruu Puteoli.
Yehuu agyidifoɔ bi ya hɔ, na bɛsrɛɛ yɛ sɛ yɛntena bɛ nkyɛne nnanson.
Na afei yɛkɔɔ Roma.
Na agyidifoɔ tee yɛ nka he, befirii hɔ behyiaa yɛ Apia Dwa so ne bea bi a bɛfrɛ hɔ Nsadane-Mmeɛnsa, na Paulo ani bɔɔ bɛ so pɛ na ɔdaa Nyankopɔn ase na otwaa n’akoma too ne yam.
Afei berɛ a yɛkɔɔ Roma he, bɛmaa Paulo kwane maa ɔno nkoaa kɔtenaeɛ, na na sraani a ɔwɛne no ka ne ho.
Paulo ne Yudafoɔ mpanimfoɔ nkɔmmɔbɔ Nso, nnansa akyi he, ɔfrɛfrɛɛ Yudafoɔ he mu atitire he ma bebehyiaeɛ.
Berɛ a behyiaeɛ he, ɔka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, “Anuanom, ɔyam sɛ menyɔɔ bibiaa a otia manfoɔ anaa yɛ nananom amanneɛ deɛ, nso bɛde me hyɛɛ Romafoɔ nsa sɛ deduani ya Yerusalem.
Na berɛ a bɛhwehwɛɛ asɛm he mu wieeɛ he, na bɛpɛ sɛ begyaa me efiri sɛ na menyɛɛ hwee a ɔsɛ wuo.
Na pene a Yudafoɔ he ampene so he nti, mede asɛm he kɔdane Kaesare, na ɔnyɛ sɛ ebia mewɔ bibi a mede ɔɔbɔ me mane soboɔ.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, asɛm yi ho nti ne mesrɛɛ sɛ mepɛ sɛ mehu ho ne ho kasa, efiri sɛ Israel anidasoɔ nti ne bɛagu me nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn yi.” Bɛka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Yennyaa wo ho krataa biaa mfirii Yudea, na anuanom a bɛaba he mu biaa mmɛbɔɔ amanneɛ, na bɛmmɛkaa wo ho nsɛmmɔne biaa.
Nso yesusuu sɛ, ɔyɛ sɛ yebetie w’adwene, efiri sɛ, nɔkwasɛm di, yenim sɛ bɛkasa tia saa fekuo yi baabiaa.” Paulo kaa asɛm ya Roma Bɛhyɛɛ da a bebehyia he wieeɛ he, nnipa pii baa baabi a na ɔda he.
Na ɔkɔkyerɛɛ asɛm he mu kyerɛɛ bɛ dii Nyankopɔn ahennie he ho adanseɛ, na ɔnam Mose mmara ne Adiyifoɔ he so kaa Yesu ho asɛm a ɔtɔ asom, firi anɔpa kosi anwummerɛ.
Na binom gyee nea ɔkaeɛ he diiɛ, binom nso annye anni.
Na osiane sɛ na bɛ adwene nhyia nti, befirii aseɛ sɛ bɛɛkɔ, na Paulo de asɛm yi kaa ho sɛ, “Honhom Kronkron faa diyifoɔ Yesaia so kaa no yei kyerɛɛ ho nananom sɛ: ‘Kɔ na kɔka kyerɛ mane yi sɛ: Te deɛ, hobɛte nso honte aseɛ na hwɛ deɛ hobɛhwɛ nso honhu, efiri sɛ mane yi akoma apirim, na bɛde bɛ aso tie kwa, na bɛakata bɛ ani, na bɛamfa bɛ ani anhu, amfa bɛ aso antie, na bɛamfa bɛ akoma ante aseɛ na bɛansakra amma mansa bɛ yadeɛ.’ Nti honhu sɛ bɛasoma nea Nyankopɔn nam so gye nkwa he kɔ Amanamane mu, na kwane biaa so, bebetie.” [Na ɔkaa yei nyinaa wieeɛ he, Yudafoɔ he firii hɔ kɔeɛ na bɛgyegyee akyinnye bɛ mu.]
Ɔtenaa hɔ mfie mmienu a na ɔnoaa hwɛ ne ho.
Na ɔgyee bɛ a bɛbaa ne nkyɛne nyinaa fɛ so, na ɔkaa Nyankopɔn ahennie ho asɛm de nnamyɛ kɛseɛ kyerɛkyerɛɛ bɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo ho nsɛm a bibiaa ansi ho kwane.
NNIANIMU Krataa a Paulo twerɛ kɔmaa Romafoɔ he, na ɔde oosiesie kwane ama ne nsrahwɛ a wahyehyɛ sɛ ɔbɛkɔ Roma he.
Ɔyɔɔ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛyɛ adwuma kakra Roma, na bɛaboa no ama watumi akɔ Spania.
Ɔtwerɛ krataa yi de kyerɛɛ ne nteaseɛ a ɔwɔ Kristosom gyidie ho, ne sɛdeɛ ɔsɛ sɛ ɔda adi Akristofoɔ abrabɔ mu.
Paulo kyeaa nnipa a bɛya Roma Asafo mu wieeɛ pɛ, na ɔmaa behuu ne mpaebɔ a ɔbɔ ma bɛ.
Ɔkaa ne botaeɛ a ɔde twerɛɛ Krataa he: “Efiri sɛ mu ne bɛayi Nyankopɔn tenenee adi firi gyidie mu kɔ gyidie mu, sɛdeɛ bɛatwerɛ sɛ: Deɛ ɔtene firi gyidie mu benya nkwa” .
Yei akyi he, Paulo firii aseɛ kyerɛkyerɛɛ ne botaeɛ he mu.
Nnipa nyinaa, meekyerɛ Yudafoɔ ne amanamane mufoɔ, hia sɛ bebegyina Nyankopɔn anim sɛdeɛ ɔfata, efiri sɛ bɛ nyinaa bɛhyɛ bɔne tumi ase.
Nnipa nam Yesu Kristo mu gyidie so betumi asiesie bɛ ne Nyankopɔn ntam.
Paulo toaa so kyerɛkyerɛɛ nkwa foforɔ a ɔnam Kristo mu ayɔnkofa a ɔka bɛ ne Nyankopɔn bɔ mu he mu.
Nyankopɔn Honhom ma gyidini tumi de ne ho firi bɔne ne wuo tumi ase ma asomdwie ba ɔne Nyankopɔn ntam.
Ofiri ti - he, Paulo kyerɛkyerɛɛ botaeɛ a Nyankopɔn mmara kita ne Nyankopɔn Honhom mu tumi a ɔya gyidini asetena mu.
Somafoɔ he toaa so kyerɛɛ sɛdeɛ Yudafoɔ ne amanamane mufoɔ ba Nyankopɔn nhyehyɛeɛ a ɔya hɔ ma adasa nyinaa he mu.
Owiee sɛ Yudafoɔ a bɛapo Yesu he, ka Nyankopɔn nhyehyɛeɛ a ɔnam so ɔɔma nnipa nyinaa aba n’adom a ɔya Yesu Kristo mu he ho.
Ɔgye di nso sɛ Yudafoɔ he ɔnkɔ soaa mpo Yesu daa.
Awieeɛ koraa he, Paulo kyerɛɛ sɛdeɛ ɔsɛ sɛ bɛtena ase, ne titire ne sɛ bɛbɛma dɔ ayɔ adwuma bɛ ne afoforɔ ntam.
Ɔfaa botaeɛ bi te sɛ som a bɛsom ma Nyankopɔn, Akristofoɔ asɛdeɛ a ɔfa amammuo ho, dwumadie ne nnipa afoforɔ ho ne nsɛm a ɔfa yɛ tiboa ho.
Paulo de ne nkyea nsɛm ne nsɛm a ɔde yi Nyankopɔn ayɛ ne wiee krataa he.
MU NSƐM Nnianimu ne nnyinasoɔ asɛm :- Hia a nnipa hia nkwagyeɛ :—: Nyankopɔn nkwagyeɛ kwane :—: Kristo mu abrabɔ foforɔ he :—: Nyankopɔn nhyehyɛeɛ a ɔya hɔ ma Israel :—: Kristoni abrabɔ :—: Awieeɛ ne nkyea :—:
Nkyea Paulo, Yesu Kristo akoa a bɛafrɛ no sɛ ɔmmɛyɛ somafoɔ na bɛayi no asi hɔ ama Nyankopɔn asɛmpa he a ɔnam n’adiyifoɔ so hyɛɛ ho bɔ siee twerɛnsɛm kronkron he mu he, asɛmpa a ɔfa Nyankopɔn Ba he ho, nea honam fam ɔyɛ Dawid aseni na bɛde tumi ayi no adi akyerɛ sɛ ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn Ba a ɔnam honhom ahoteɛ kronkron so awufoɔ sɔreeɛ mu; ɔno ne Yesu Kristo, yɛ Awurade.
Ɔno so ne yɛnam anya adom ne somafodwuma sɛ yɛde setie mu gyidie ɔɔbra Amanamane mufoɔ nyinaa ne dini nti, ho a bɛabɔ ho dini afrɛ ho ama Yesu Kristo he, ho nso hoka ho bi.
Me Paulo ne meetwerɛ krataa yi de abra ho, Nyankopɔn adɔfoɔ, a hoya Roma nyinaa, ho a bɛafrɛ ho sɛ hommɛyɛ ahoteefoɔ he: Adom ne asomdwie a ofiri yɛ Agya Nyankopɔn ne Awurade Yesu Kristo nka ho.
Aseda mpaebɔ Nea odi kane paa ne sɛ, menam Yesu Kristo so da me Nyankopɔn ase ma ho nyinaa, efiri sɛ bɛka ho gyidie ho asɛm wiase baabiaa.
Na Nyankopɔn a mede me honhom som no a mepae mu ka ne Ba he ho asɛmpa he, ɔno ne me danseni sɛ mennyae ho nkaeɛ wɔ me mpaebɔ mu, na mesrɛ sɛ Nyankopɔn pɛ a menya kwane aba ho nkyɛne.
Na m’ani agyina sɛ mehu ho sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a metumi ne ho akyɛ honhom adom akyɛdeɛ bi ama ahyɛ ho dene, ɔne sɛ yɛ nyinaa gyidie bɛhyehyɛ yɛ ho yɛ ho dene.
Anuanom agyidifoɔ, mepɛ sɛ hohu sɛ mpɛn pii ne maabɔ me tim pɔ sɛ mɛba ho nkyɛne (nso bibi asi me kwane), na ama matwa aba bi afiri ho hɔ sɛnea mayɔ no Amanamane a aka he hɔ.
Mede Helafoɔ ne Pɔtɔfoɔ nyinaa, anyansafoɔ ne adwenem harefoɔ nyinaa ka; saa nti ne me ho pere me sɛ mɛpaem aka asɛmpa he akyerɛ ho nso a hoya Roma.
Asɛmpa he mu tumi Na m’ani nwu asɛmpa he ho; efiri sɛ ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn tumi a ɔnam so gye biaa a ɔwɔ gyidie nkwa, Yudafoɔ ne bedi kane, na afei Helafoɔ nso.
Na asɛmpa he mu ne Nyankopɔn tenenee da adi firi gyidie mu kɔ gyidie mu; sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Nea ɔtene he nam gyidie so ne benya nkwa.” Nnipa nyinaa fobuo Na Nyankopɔn abufuo ayi adi atia bɛ a bɛde nnoɔma a ɔntene ne amumuyɔ berɛ nɔkorɛ he ase nyinaa.
Na nea bebetumi ahu afa Nyankopɔn ho he da adi pefee, efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn ayi no adi akyerɛ bɛ.
Ewom sɛ Nyankopɔn daa tumi ne ne nyamesu yɛ adeɛ a ani nhu deɛ, nso ofiri adebɔ mfitiaseɛ he, ne nnoɔma a wayɔ he ada no adi pefee, ama bɛde adwene ahu mu.
Nti benni anoyie biaa; efiri sɛ benim Nyankopɔn deɛ, nso bɛamfa anidie amma no sɛ Nyankopɔn na bɛanna no ase, nso nea bɛdwene he yɛ nsemhunu, na bɛ adwene hunu he yɛɛ sum.
Besusuu sɛ bɛwɔ nyansa, nso bɛdanee nkwaseafoɔ; na bɛsesaa Nyankopɔn a onwu da he animuonyam maa nipa a owu anaa nnomaa, ntɔteboa ne mmoa a bɛwea fam nsɛso.
Ne saa nti Nyankopɔn gyae bɛ maa bɛ akoma akɔnnɔ, na akɔnnɔ he de bɛ kɔɔ nnoɔma a ho nte ho, na nnoɔma a ho nte he maa bɛsɛe bɛ nipadua, efiri sɛ bɛde Nyankopɔn ho nɔkorɛ sesaa torɔ na bɛsomm abɔdeɛ sene sɛ bɛbɛsom Bɔadeɛ, ɔno ne nhyira nka no daa!
Amen.
Yei nti Nyankopɔn gyaa bɛ maa akɔnnɔ porɔeɛ.
Bɛ mmaa de bɛ honam fam nhyiamudie a ɔnam ne kwane so he sesaa nea ɔnnam ne kwane so, saa ara nso ne bɛ mmeema nso, gyaa nhyiamudie a ɔsɛ sɛ bɛ ne mmaa hyiam, maa benyaa akɔnnɔ maa bɛ yɔnko mmeema.
Mmeema ne mmeema bɔɔ aniwuo bra na benyaa bɛ bɔne he so akatua.
Na esiane sɛ bɛammu Nyankopɔn nti, Nyankopɔn gyae bɛ maa adwene a ɔmfata na bɛyɔɔ nnoɔma hunu a ɔnsɛ sɛ bɛyɔ koraa.
Na amumuyɔ: bɔne, anibereɛ ne nitane nyinaa bi hyɛɛ bɛ ma.
Bɔne bi te sɛ: ahoɔyeyaa, awudie, apereapereɛ, ntɔkwa, torɔ, nnaadaa ne nkontompo hyɛɛ bɛ ma, bɛyɛɛ nsekurofoɔ, nantitwitwafoɔ, Nyankopɔn atamfoɔ, akwadwofoɔ, basabasayɔfoɔ, ahohoahoafoɔ, bɔnepɛfoɔ, awofoɔ so atuatefoɔ, nkwaseafoɔ, nnipa a benni gyidie, akomadenfoɔ, atimuɔdenfoɔ.
Benim Nyankopɔn ahyɛdeɛ, sɛ bɛ a bɛyɔ saa bɔne yi nyinaa fata wuo, nso nyɛ ne yɔ nkoaa ne bɛyɔeɛ na mmom bɛfoaa bɛ a bɛyɔ saa nso so.
Nyankopɔn atemmuo a ɔtene Ne saa nti, adasamma nni anoyie biaa, sɛnea woteeɛ biaa, woobu bi atɛne he, na woobu woaa wo ho atɛne, efiri sɛ wo a woyɛ temmufoɔ he, woyɔ ade korɔ heaa.
Hoka sɛ, “Yenim sɛ Nyankopɔn atemmuo a ɔba bɛ a bɛyɔ saa he so he tene.” Nti, wo nipa, wosusu sɛ, sɛnea woteeɛ biaa, sɛ wobu bɛ a bɛyɔ saa he atɛne na wo nso woyɔ saa bi a, wobɛdwane Nyankopɔn atemmuo anaa?
Anaa wobu N’ayamyɛ pii a ɔno ne boasetɔ ne n’abodwokyɛre he animtia?
Wonnim sɛ Nyankopɔn ayamyɛ botae ne sɛ ɔde wo bɛkɔ adwensakram?
Nso w’akoma pirim ɔne sesa a wompɛ sɛ wosesa nti, wooboaboa Nyankopɔn abufuo ano ama wo ho ama abufuo da he, berɛ a Nyankopɔn atemmuo a ɔtene he beyi ne ho adi; efiri sɛ obetua biaa ka sɛnea biaa nnwuma teɛ: bɛ a bɛde ntoboaseɛ yɔ papa hwehwɛ animuonyam ne anidie ne nea ɔmporɔ he, ɔbɛma bɛ daa nkwa; nso bɛ a bedi ntuturasɛm; na bɛpo nɔkorɛ na bɛfa kwane a ɔntene so he, bebenya abufuo ne asotwe.
Na ahohiahia ne ahokyerɛ bɛba biaa a ɔyɔ bɔne so, Yudani kane, na afei Helani nso, nso animuonyam ne anidie ne asomdwie bɛba biaa a ɔyɔ papa so, Yudani kane, na afei Helani nso, efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn nyɛ nyiyimu.
Dodoɔ a benni mmara na bɛyɔɔ bɔne he, bɛbɛkwati mmara he nso ayera, na bɛ a bɛya mmara ase na bɛyɔɔ bɔne nyinaa bɛde mmara he bebu bɛ atɛne.
Na ɔnyɛ bɛ a betie mmara he ne bɛyɛ ateneneefoɔ Nyankopɔn ani so, na mmom bɛ a bɛyɛ mmara he yɔfoɔ nkoaa ne benya bembuo.
Sɛ Amanamane mufoɔ a benni mmara he, de bɛ awosuo yɔ deɛ mmara he hyɛ sɛ bɛnyɔ a, hedeɛ, ewom sɛ benni mmara he deɛ, nso nea bɛyɔ he yɛ mmara ma bɛ ankasa.
Bɛda no adi sɛ deɛ mmara he hyɛ sɛ bɛnyɔ he bɛatwerɛ no bɛ akomam, sɛnea bɛ ahonim nso di ho adanseɛ; na bɛ nsusuiɛ a ayɛ ntanta bɛtoto bɛ ano anaa obetwitwa agye bɛ da a Nyankopɔn a ɔnam Yesu Kristo so, bebu nnipa nyinaa kokoam nsusuiɛ atɛne sɛnea asɛmpa a maka he teɛ.
Yudafoɔ ne mmara he Nso sɛ wofrɛ wo ho Yudani, na wode wo ho to mmara he so, na wohoahoa wo ho Nyankopɔn mu, na wonim n’apɛdeɛ na wokyerɛ nea ɔyɛ, efiri sɛ bɛatete wo mmara he mu, na wogye di sɛ wokyerɛ anifirafoɔ kwane, woyɛ hann ma bɛ a bɛnam sum mu, wotene nkwaseafoɔ, woyɛ mmɔfra bɛ kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, wowɔ mmara he a nimdeɛ ne nɔkorɛ ahyɛ no ma; wo a afei deɛ, wokyerɛkyerɛ afoforɔ, wonkyerɛkyerɛ wo ho?
Wo a wokasa tia korɔnobɔ he, wommɔ korɔno?
Wo a wokasa tia adwammammɔ he, wommɔ adwamane?
Wo a wohoahoa wo ho mmara he mu, wommu mmara he so mfa mmu Nyankopɔn animtia?
Saa nti ne bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Wo nti bɛaka Nyankopɔn dini ho abususɛm Amanamane mu.” Na mmom sɛ wodi mmara he so a twetiatwa ho hia; nso sɛ wobu mmara he so a wo twetiatwa he dane bɛyɛ te sɛnea wontwaa twetia.
Nti sɛ bɛ a bentwaa twetia he di mmara he so a, twetia a bentwaeɛ he nti bemmu bɛ sɛ bɛ a bɛatwa bɛ twetia anaa?
Nti bɛ a honam fam bentwaa bɛ twetia na nso bedi mmara he so he bebu ho a bɛatwerɛ mmara he amma ho, na bɛatwa ho twetia nso hoto mmara he fɔ.
Ɔnyɛ honam fam nnoɔma ne ma bi yɛ Yudani, saa ara nso ne twetiatwa kann nso nna adi anisoɔ ne honam fam nnoɔma mu.
na mmom, sɛ bi yɛ Yudani mapa a, ɔyɛ no ne mu, na twetiatwa ankasa yɛ akoma mu asɛm; ɔyɛ honhom mu adeɛ, na mmom ɔnyɛ honam mu adeɛ.
Nea ɔyɛ Yudani mapa he, n’ayeyie firi Nyankopɔn hɔ, na mmom ommfiri nnipa hɔ.
Afei, mmɛ ne Yudani wɔ boro so?
Anaa mmɛ mfasoɔ ne ya twetiatwa so?
Ɔdɔɔso kwane hodoɔ bebree so, efiri sɛ nea odi kane he, Yudafoɔ he ne bɛde Nyankopɔn nsɛm hyɛɛ bɛ nsa.
Na sɛ bɛ mu binom annye anni ɛ?
Nti bɛgye a bɛannye anni he bɛsesa Nyankopɔn nɔkorɛdie he anaa?
Daabi da!
Ewom sɛ nnipa biaa nni nɔkorɛ, ma Nyankopɔn nyɛ nɔkwafoɔ, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ: “Sɛnea wobedi bem wo nsɛm mu.
Na woadi nkunim w’atemmuo mu.” Nti sɛ tene a yɛntene da Nyankopɔn tenenee adi a, mmɛ ne yɛbɛka?
Nti Nyankopɔn ntene sɛ obehwie n’abufuo agu yɛ so?
(Meka no nipa fam.)
Daabi da!
Saa deɛ a mmɛ kwane ne Nyankopɔn bɛfa so abu wiase atɛne?
Nso sɛ tene a mentene ma Nyankopɔn nɔkorɛdie bu so ma n’animuonyam da adi a, mmɛ nti ne bɛda so bu me sɛ debɔneyɛni?
Na ɛɛne nti ne yɛnka sɛ (sɛnea binom ka to yɛ so sɛ, yɛ dɛ), “Homma yɛnyɔ nnebɔne na nnepa aba?” Bɛ afobuo fata bɛ!
Nipa biaa ntene Nyankopɔn anim Hedeɛ asɛm he ne sɛ?
Nti yɛ Yudafoɔ he kyɛne bɛ a bɛaka he anaa?
Daabi, ɔnte saa koraa; efiri sɛ yɛadi kane aka sɛ, Yudafoɔ oo, Helafoɔ oo, biaa hyɛ bɔne tumi ase, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ: “Biaa nni hɔ a ɔtene, baako mpo nni hɔ; Biaa nni nteaseɛ, biaa nni hɔ a ɔhwehwɛ Nyankopɔn.
Biaa amane afiri kwanpa he so, bɛ nyinaa mfasoɔ nni bɛ so; biaa nni hɔ a ɔda ayamyɛ adi, biaa nni hɔ, baako mpo nni hɔ.” “Bɛ mene mu yɛ awufoɔ adakamena a ano abie; bɛde bɛ kɛtrɛma di torɔ.” “Nankatia borɔ ya bɛ ano.” “Duabɔ ne adenwono ahyɛ bɛ anum ma.” “Bɛ nane ɔhare mogyahwieguo ho; sɛeɛ ne awerɛhoɔ ya bɛ kwane so, na asomdwie kwane deɛ, bennim.” “Nyamesuro nni bɛ ani so.” Afei yenim sɛ, nea mmara he ka biaa, ɔkasa kyerɛ bɛ a bɛya mmara he ase, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ano biaa bɛka atom, na wiase nyinaa abu nkonta akyerɛ Nyankopɔn, efiri sɛ nipa biaa nni hɔ a obedi bem Nyankopɔn anim, sɛnea mmara he nnwuma teɛ, efiri sɛ yɛnam mmara he so ne yenya bɔne ho nimdeɛ.
Tenenee a ɔnam gyidie so ba Na afei, bɛakwati mmara he ayi Nyankopɔn tenenee adi, na mmara he ne adiyifoɔ he di ho adanseɛ, Nyankopɔn tenenee a ɔnam Yesu Kristo mu gyidie so ma bɛ a bɛgye di nyinaa.
Na nyiyimu nnim, efiri sɛ nnipa nyinaa ayɔ bɔne na yɛtɔ sini Nyankopɔn animuonyam ho; na afei ɔyɛ akyɛdeɛ kwa sɛ Nyankopɔn nam n’adom ne gyeɛ a ɔya Kristo Yesu mu he so abu nnipa bem.
Kristo ne Nyankopɔn de no asi hɔ sɛ ne mogyaa he nyɛ mpatadeɛ a nipa nam gyidie so ne nya mu kyɛfa; na Nyankopɔn de ayi ne tenenee adi sɛ nnebɔne a bɛyɔɔ no kane he, ɔnam ne boasetɔ so abu n’ani agu so; sɛnea ɔbɛyɔ a ɔbɛda n’ankasa ne tenenee adi saa berɛ yi mu, na berɛ a obu nipa a ɔwɔ Yesu mu gyidie bem he, ada adi sɛ ɔyɛ teneneeni mapa.
Afei mmɛ ne ahohoahoa yi?
Wɔayi afiri hɔ.
Mmɛ nhyehyɛeɛ so na ɔnam?
Mmara nnwuma so?
Daabi, na mmom ɔnam gyidie nhyehyɛeɛ so.
Na yesi no pi sɛ ɔnam gyidie so ne bebu bi bem, na mmom omfiri mmara nnwuma mu.
Anaa Nyankopɔn yɛ Yudafoɔ nkoaa bɛ Nyankopɔn?
Ɔnnyɛ Amanamane mufoɔ nso Nyankopɔn anaa?
Ampa, ɔyɛ Amanamane mufoɔ nso Nyankopɔn, efiri sɛ, Nyankopɔn yɛ baako; na ɔnam gyidie korɔ he a so ne bebu twetiatwafoɔ ne bɛ a bentwaa bɛ twetia bem.
Ɔsɛ sɛ yɛde saa gyidie he tu mmara he gu anaa?
Daabi da!
Na mmom, yɛma mmara he ase tim.
Abraham nhwɛsoɔ Ɔte saa a afei mmɛ ne yɛbɛka sɛ ɔyɛ mfasoɔ a Abraham a ɔyɛ yɛ honam fam agya-panyini he nyaeɛ?
Sɛ nnwuma mu ne bebuu Abraham bem a, nka ɔwɔ nea ɔde bɛhoahoa ne ho, nso ɔnyɛ Nyankopɔn anim.
Na mmɛ twerɛsɛm he ka?
“Abraham gyee Nyankopɔn diiɛ, na Nyankopɔn buu ne gyidie he sɛ tenenee maa no.” Na afei sɛ bi yɔ adwuma a, bemmu n’akatua sɛ akyɛdeɛ, na mmom bebu no sɛ adeɛ ɔfata no.
Nso bi a wannyɔ adwuma he gye nea obu debɔnyɛni bem he di a, obu saa gyidie he sɛ tenenee ma no.
Nti Dawid nso kasa faa nhyira a ɔba bɛ a Nyankopɔn kwati bɛ nnwuma bu bɛ bem he ho sɛ: “Nhyira ne bɛ a bɛde bɛ mmarato akyɛ bɛ, na bɛakata bɛ bɔne so; nhyira ne nipa a Awurade mmu ne bɔne ngu ne so.” Nti saa nhyira yi, kɔma bɛ a bɛatwa bɛ twetia nkoaa, anaa bɛ a bentwaa bɛ twetia nso ka ho?
Yɛpae mu ka sɛ, Gyidie ne bɛde buu Abraham sɛ ɔtene.
Mmɛ kwane so ne bɛde buu no saa?
Ɔyɛ berɛ a na bentwaa no twetia he anaa betwaa no twetia wieeɛ he a?
Ɔnnyɛ twetiatwa he akyi, na mmom yei siiɛ ansa na betwaa no twetia.
Onyaa twetiatwa he ho nsɛnkyerɛnne sɛ tenenee a ɔnam gyidie so nyaeɛ he ho nsɔano berɛ a na bentwaa no twetia.
Nyankopɔn yɔɔ yei nam so ama Abraham abɛyɛ bɛ a bentwaa bɛ twetia, na nso bɛgye Nyankopɔn di he nyinaa agya, na ne saa nti bɛabu bɛ nso sɛ ateneneefoɔ, saa ara nso ne ɔyɛ agya ma twetiafoɔ a, ɔnyɛ bɛ twetiatwa nkoaa, na mmom bɛnam yɛ agya Abraham a onyaa gyidie ansa na betwaa no twetia he anammɔno mu.
Nyankopɔn nhwɛsoɔ a ɔnam gyidie so Na bɔ a bɛhyɛɛ no sɛ obedi adeɛ wiase he annyɛ bɔhyɛ a ɔnam mmara so maa Abraham anaa n’asefoɔ na mmom ɔnam gyidie tenee so.
Sɛ mmara sodifoɔ he ne ɔsɛ sɛ bɛyɛ adedifoɔ a, hedeɛ na gyidie yɛ kwa na bɔhyɛ he nso nni mu; efiri sɛ mmara he twetwe Nyankopɔn abufuo ba; na sɛ mmara nni hɔ a, mmarato biaa nso nni hɔ.
Ne saa nti ogyina gyidie so, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a bɔhyɛ he begyina adom so na adi agyinamu ama n’asefoɔ nyinaa, ɔnnyɛ mmara sodifoɔ he nkoaa, na mmom bɛ a bekura Abraham gyidie he bi, efiri sɛ ɔyɛ yɛ nyinaa yɛ agya, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ “Maayɔ wo amane bebree bɛ agya,” Nyankopɔn a ɔgye no di he anim, nea ɔma awufoɔ nkwa, na ɔfrɛ adeɛ a onni hɔ ma no ba.
Berɛ a na anidasoɔ nni hɔ he, Abraham gyinaa anidasoɔ so gye dii sɛ ɔbɛyɛ amane bebree agya sɛnea bɛaka sɛ he, “Saa ara ne w’asefoɔ bɛyɛ bebree.” Ne gyidie anhinhim, mpo berɛ a ohuu sɛ ne nipadua ayɛ sɛnea awu (efiri sɛ na waadi mfeɛ ha), anaa berɛ a ohuu sɛ Sara yɛ bonyini he.
Na Nyankopɔn bɔhyɛ he ho deɛ wamma annyeannie biaa amma n’akwane mu, amma no annye akyinnye, na mmom ogyinaa pintinn gyidie mu na ɔhyɛɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam, onyaa awerɛhyɛmu paa sɛ Nyankopɔn betumi ayɔ nea w’ahyɛ ho bɔ he.
Gyidie a ɔnyaa yɛ nti “bebuu ne sɛ ɔtene.” Afei nsɛm a ɔka sɛ, “Nyankopɔn buu ne gyidie sɛ tenenee maa no” he, bɛantwerɛ amma ɔno nkoaa, na mmom bɛtwerɛ maa yɛ nso; na bɛabu yɛ a yɛgye nea ɔnyanee Yesu a ɔyɛ yɛ Awurade firii awufoɔ mu he di nso sɛ yɛ tene.
Yesus ne yɛ bɔne nti beyii no maa wuo na yɛ bembuo nti bɛyanee no he.
Bembuo so aba Afei ɔnam sɛ bɛabu yɛ bem gyidie mu nti, yɛnam yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo so anya asomdwie Nyankopɔn mu, ɔno so ne yɛnam anya saa adom a yegyina so yi; na yɛhoahoa yɛ ho anidasoɔ a yɛ wɔ no Nyankopɔn animuonyam mu.
Na ɔnyɛ yei nkoaa, na mmom yɛhoahoa yɛ ho ya yɛ amanehunu mu, yenim sɛ amanehunu de yɔkoduru ba, na yɔkoduru de subane pa ba, na subane pa de anidasoɔ ba, na anidasoɔ nni hwammɔ, efiri sɛ bɛnam Honhom Kronkron a bɛde ama yɛ he so ahwie Nyankopɔn dɔ agu yɛ akoma mu.
Na berɛ a yɛda so yɛ mmerɛ he, berɛ a ɔsɛ mu he Kristo wu maa nnebɔnyɛfoɔ.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, ɔbɛyɛ dene sɛ bi bewu ama deɛ ɔyɛ nipa tenenee mpo; na deɛ ɔyɛ nipa pa he deɛ, ebia nka bi besi ne bo sɛ obewu ama no.
Nso Nyankopɔn daa ne dɔ adi kyerɛɛ yɛ sɛ yɛda so yɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ he, Kristo wu maa yɛ.
Nea ɔka ho koraa ne sɛ, seesei bɛde ne mogyaa abu yɛ bem, bɛnam ne so bɛgye yɛ afiri Nyankopɔn abufuo mu.
Na sɛ berɛ a yɛyɛ Nyankopɔn atamfoɔ he, bɛnam ne Ba he wuo so apata yɛ ne Nyankopɔn ntam a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ ne bɛmfa ne nkwa so nnye yɛ.
Nso ɔnyɛ yei nkoaa, na mmom yɛnam yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo so hoahoa yɛ ho Nyankopɔn mu, seesei deɛ, yɛnam ne so anya mpata yi.
Adam ne Kristo Saa nti ɔnam nipa baako so ne bɔne baa wiase, na wuo nam bɔne so baeɛ, maa wuo trɛ kaa nnipa nyinaa, efiri sɛ nnipa nyinaa ayɔ bɔne; ansa na mmara he ɔɔba he na bɔne ya wiase, nso sɛ mmara nni hɔ a bemmu biaa fɔ bɔne ho.
Nso wuo faa nnipa nnommum firi Adam so kosii Mose so, mpo bɛ a bɛ bɔne nte sɛ Adam mmarato he, saa Adam yi yɛ nea na ɔɔba he ho nsɛso.
Na ɔnyɛ sɛdeɛ mmarato he teɛ ne adom akyɛdeɛ he nso teɛ, efiri sɛ baakofoɔ mmarato nti nnipa bebree awu a, Nyankopɔn Adom ne nipa baako a ɔno ne Yesu Kristo he mu adom akyɛdeɛ aboro so ama nnipa bebree akyɛne saa.
Na akyɛdeɛ a bɛde kyɛ kwa he nte sɛ nipa baako bɔne ho nsɛso he.
Na atemmuo a ɔnam mmarato baako so he de afobuo baeɛ, nso akyɛdeɛ a bɛde kyɛ kwa he, a odi mmarato bebree akyi he de bembuo ba.
Sɛ ɔnam baakofoɔ mmarato so maa wuo faa nnipa nnommum saa kwane yi so a, mprɛ meɛhe ne bɛ a benyaa adom ne tenenee akyɛdeɛ a ɔboro so he mmom ɔmmfa nipa baako, Yesu Kristo, so nya daa nkwa.
Nti sɛnea nipa baako mmarato de bebree kɔɔ afobuo mu he, saa ne ɔnam baakofoɔ tenenee so de bembuo ne nkwa bɛma nnipa nyinaa.
Sɛnea ɔnam baakofoɔ asoɔdene so maa nnipa bebree yɛɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ he, saa ara ne nipa baako setie bɛma nnipa bebree ayɛ ahoteefoɔ.
Nso mmara he baa sɛ mmarato bɛdɔɔso; nso sɛ bɔne dɔɔso a, adom broo so kyɛne saa.
Na sɛnea bɔne dii hene wuo mu he, adom so nam tenenee so adi hene afa yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo so kɔ daa nkwa mu.
Yesu mu ayɔnkofa ku bɔne Afei ɛɛne ne yɛnka?
Yɛnkɔ so nyɔ bɔne sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a adom bɛdɔɔso anaa?
Daabi da, ɔnsɛ sɛ yɛyɔ saa koraa!
Mmɛ nti ne ɔsɛ sɛ yɛ a yɛawu ama bɔne kɔ so tena bɔne mu?
Anaa honnim sɛ yɛ mu dodoɔ a bɛbɔɔ yɛ asu Kristo Yesu mu he, bɛbɔɔ yɛ asu kɔɔ ne wuom?
Nti besiee yɛ ne no ya asubɔ mu kɔɔ wuom, sɛ, sɛnea bɛde Agya he animuonyam nyanee Kristo firii awufoɔ mu he, saa ne ɔsɛ sɛ yɛ nso yɛnante nkwa foforɔ mu.
Nti sɛ yɛ ne no ayɛ baako ne wuo a ɔte sei mu a, yɛ ne no nso bɛyɛ baako ya wusɔreɛ a ɔte sɛ ne deɛ he mu.
Yenim sɛ bɛabɔ yɛ nipadua dada ne no asennua mu sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a bɔne nipadua he bɛsɛe, na yɛankɔ so anyɔ bɔne nkoa.
Na nea wawu he ade ne ho afiri bɔne ho.
Nso sɛ yɛ ne Kristo awu a, yɛgye di sɛ yɛ ne no bɛtena ase nso.
Yenim sɛ Kristo a bɛanyane no afiri awufuom he, onwu bio; efiri sɛ wuo ntumi mfa no nommum bio.
Wuo a owuiɛ he, owuu prɛko maa bɔne, maa nnipa nyinaa; nso ase a ɔte he, ɔte ma Nyankopɔn.
Nti ho nso ho mu ho ho sɛ hoawu ama bɔne ampa na hote ase ma Nyankopɔn, Kristo mu.
Nti, hommma bɔne mmfa ho nipadua a obewu yi nommum, sɛ hobɛyɛ setie ama honam akɔnnɔ.
Hommfa ho nipadua mma bɔne sɛ akodeɛ amumuyɔ kwane so, na mmom homfa ho ho ma Nyankopɔn sɛ bɛ a bɛagye bɛ afiri wuom aba nkwa mu, na homfa ho ho ma sɛ tenenee akodeɛ.
Na bɔne amfa ho nommum bio, efiri sɛ honni mmara ase, na mmom hoya adom ase.
Bɔne nkoa Afei mmɛ bio?
Yɛnyɔ bɔne efiri sɛ yenni mmara ase na mmom adom ase anaa?
Daabi da!
Honnim sɛ nea hode ho ho ma no na hotie no sɛ nkoa he, hoyɛ ne nkoa, sɛ bɔne a ɔkɔ wuom, anaa setie a ɔkɔ tenenee mu?
Nso yɛda Nyankopɔn ase sɛ, hoayɛ bɔne nkoa da, na hofiri akomam abɛyɛ setie ama nkyerɛkyerɛ a bɛde hyɛɛ ho nsa, na afei, berɛ a bɛagye ho afiri bɔne mu he, hoabɛyɛ tenenee nkoa.
Meeka no nipafam esiane ho honam mmerɛeɛ nti.
Sɛnea hode ho honam akwaa maa fi nkoa na hoyɔɔ amumuyɔ toaa amumuyɔ so he, nti saa mmerɛ yi deɛ homfa ho ho ma sɛ tenenee nkoa nkɔ ahoteɛ mu.
Berɛ a hoyɛ bɔne nkoa he, na hode ho ho tenenee ho.
Nti mmɛ mfasoɔ ne honyaa no nnoɔma a afei deɛ ho fɛre ho he mu?
Saa nnoɔma he awieeɛ ne wuo.
Nso afei a hoade ho ho afiri bɔne ho yi, ho abɛyɛ Nyankopɔn nkoa, mfasoɔ a honya ne ahoteɛ.
N’awieeɛ ne daa nkwa.
Na bɔne akatua a ne wuo, nso Nyankopɔn adom akyɛdeɛ ne daa nkwa a ɔya Awurade Kristo Yesu mu.
Awareɛ ho mfantoho Anuanom, honnim sɛ, meekasa akyerɛ bɛ a benim mmara he, sɛ mmara he kyekyere bi berɛ a onii he te ase?
Nti baa warefoɔ hyɛ ne kunu mmara ase berɛ a ne kunu he te ase; nso sɛ okunu he wu a, ɔde ne ho firi ne kunu mmara he ase.
Saa ne ɔteɛ, sɛ baa warefoɔ ne beema foforɔ te a, na ne kunu he nwuiɛ a, bɛbɛfrɛ no dwammanmɔfoɔ.
Nso sɛ ne kunu he wu a, baa he de ne ho firi saa mmara he ho; sɛ ɔware beema foforɔ a ɔnyɛ dwammanmɔfoɔ.
Annuanom, saa kwane he so ne honam Kristo nipadua so awu mmara he fam, saa nti, hohyɛ nipa foforɔ ase, nea benyanee no firi awufoɔ mu na ɔnam so ama yɛ aso aba ama Nyankopɔn.
Berɛ a na yɛte honam mu he, mmara he yɛnee yɛ bɔne akɔnnɔ he, na ɔyɔɔ adwuma yɛ nnipadua mu maa yɛsoo aba maa wuo.
Na afei deɛ, yɛade yɛ ho afiri mmara he mu, yɛawu afiri nea ɔfaa yɛ nommum he ase, na yɛnam Honhom he so ayɛ nkoa kwane foforɔ so, na ɔnyɛ kwane dadaa a ogyina atwerɛeɛ dadaa he so he.
Mmara he ne bɔne Ne saa nti mmɛ ne yɛnka?
Mmara he yɛ bɔne anaa?
Daabi da!
Nso, sɛ ɔnyɛ mmara he a, nka na menim bɔne.
Sɛ mmara he anka sɛ, “Mma w’ani mmere adeɛ” a, nka na mennim nea bɛfrɛ no anibereɛ.
Nso bɔne, nyaa kwane, de anibereɛ nyinaa hyɛɛ me mu; na sɛ mmara nni hɔ a, na bɔne nso awu.
Na mekwatii mmara he tenaa ase berɛ bi, nso berɛ a mmaransɛm he baeɛ he, bɔne nyaneɛ na mewuiɛ, na mmaransɛm korɔ he a ɔhyɛɛ nkwa ho bɔ he mmaa mehuu sɛ ɔyɛ wuo ma me.
Nso bɔne nam mmaransɛm he so nyaa akwannya, daadaa me na ɔnam so kuu me.
Nti mmara he yɛ kronkron, na mmaransɛm he yɛ kronkron, ɔtene na ɔyɛ papa nso.
Nti nea ɔyɛ papa he, adane wuo ama me anaa?
Daabi da!
Na mmom ɔyɛ bɔne a ɔnam nea ɔyɛ papa so de wuo di dwuma me mu, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ɔbɛda adi sɛ bɔne yɛ bɔne, na ɔnam mmaransɛm he so ama bɔneyɔ aboroso.
Ahutaeɛ mu apereapereɛ Na yenim sɛ mmara he yɛ honhom; nso meya honam mu a, bɛatɔno me ahyɛ bɔne nkoasom ase.
Mennte me ankasa me nneyɔeɛ ase, efiri sɛ mennyɔ nea mepɛ, nso meyɔ adeɛ pɔtee a metane.
Nti sɛ meyɔ adeɛ a mempɛ a, megye tom sɛ mmara he yɛ.
Nso afei ɔnnyɛ me ne meyɔ saa, na mmom bɔne a ɔte me mu he a. Na menim sɛ bibi papa biaa nte me mu, mekyerɛ, me honam mu.
Mewɔ pɛ pa sɛ mɛyɔ nea ɔyɛ, nso mentumi nyɔ, efiri sɛ menyɔ papa a mepɛ he, nso bɔne a mempɛ he ne meyɔ.
Nti sɛ nea mempɛ ne meyɔ deɛ a, hedeɛ ɔnyɛ me ne me yɔ bio, na mmom bɔne a ɔte me mu he a. Nti mehu sɛ ɔyɛ mmara sɛ berɛ a mepɛ sɛ meyɔ nea ɔyɛ he, bɔne bɛne me.
Na m’ani gye Nyankopɔn mmara a ɔte me mu he ho, nso mehu mmara foforɔ me honam akwaa mu a ɔne m’adwene mmara di asie, ɔma meyɔ bɔne a ɔya me nipadua mu he akoa.
Me, mmɔborɔwa!
Hwane ne bɛgye me afiri wuo nipadua yi mu?
Aseda mfa yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo so nka Nyankopɔn!
Nti afei, m’adwene mu he meyɛ akoa ma Nyankopɔn mmara, nso me honam mu he meyɛ bɔne akoa.
Honhom mu nkwa Nti afei afobuo biaa nni hɔ ma bɛ a bɛya Kristo Yesu mu, efiri sɛ Honhom mu nkwa mmara he ama ho faahodie Kristo Yesu mu afiri bɔne ne wuo mmara he mu.
Na Nyankopɔn ayɔ nea mmara he antumi anyɔ, ɔne sɛ ɔnam honam mmerɛyɛ nti ɔsomaa ɔnoaa ne Ba, honam subane mu maa no bɛyɛɛ nipa te sɛ yɛ nnipa adebɔneyɛfoɔ yi sɛ ɔne bɔne nni asie, na odii bɔne so nkunim honam mu, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a nnepa a mmara he hwehwɛ sɛ yɛyɔ he bɛba mu, ya yɛ a yɛnnante honam fam, na mmom yɛnante Honhom fam he abrabɔ mu; efiri sɛ bɛ a bɛbɔ bɛ bra sɛnea honam pɛ he de bɛ adwene si honam fam nnoɔma so, nso bɛ a bɛbɔ bɛ bra Honhom mu he de bɛ adwene si Honhom mu nnoɔma so.
Nea ɔde n’adwene si honam nnoɔma so he kɔ wuom, na nea ɔde n’adwene si honhom nnoɔma so he nya nkwa ne asomdwie.
Saa nti adwene a osi honam nnoɔma so he tane Nyankopɔn; ɔmmrɛ ne ho ase nhyɛ Nyankopɔn mmara ase, nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ ontumi nyɔ saa mpo, na bɛ a bɛya honam mu he ntumi nsɔ Nyankopɔn ani.
Nso honni honam mu; hoya Honhom mu, esiane Nyankopɔn Honhom a ɔte ho mu nti.
Biaa a onni Kristo Honhom he nyɛ Kristo dea.
Sɛ Kristo te ho mu a, ewom sɛ honam he awu deɛ, ɔnam bɔne nti, nso honhom he wɔ nkwa ɔnam tenenee nti.
Na afei sɛ nea ɔnyanee Yesu firii awufoɔ mu he Honhom te ho mu a, hedeɛ deɛ ɔnyanee Kristo firii awufoɔ mu he bɛma ho nnipadua a owu he nkwa ɔnam ne Honhom a ɔte ho mu he nti.
Nti, me nuanom, ɔnyɛ honam ne yɛde no ka na yɛatena ase sɛnea honam pɛ; na sɛ hotena ase sɛnea honam pɛ a, hobewu; nso sɛ hode Honhom he ku honam he a, hobɛtena ase.
Na dodoɔ a Nyankopɔn Honhom kyerɛ bɛ kwane he, bɛ ne bɛyɛ Nyankopɔn mma; Na sɛ hoannya akoayɛ honhom a ɔbɛma ho asane akɔ hu mu bio, na mmom hoanya abayɛ honhom.
Nti yetumi team sɛ, “Abba!
Agya!” Na ɔyɛ saa Honhom he ankasa ne yɛ honhom ne di adanseɛ sɛ yɛyɛ Nyankopɔn mma, na sɛ yɛyɛ mma a, hedeɛ yedi adeɛ nso, yɛyɛ Nyankopɔn adedifoɔ, na yɛ ne Kristo bom di adeɛ; nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, yɛ ne no hu amaneɛ a, saa ara nso ne bɛbɛhyɛ yɛne no animuonyam abom.
Daakye animuonyam Menim sɛ yentumi mfa wiase yi mu amanehunu ntoto animuonyam a bɛde bɛhyɛ yɛ daakye wiase he mu he ho.
Na abɔdeɛ he de anigyina ɔɔtwɛne Nyankopɔn mma ahoyie dendenndene; na bɛde abɔdeɛ he ahyɛ nnoɔma funu ase a ɔnyɛ ɔnoaa ne pɛ so, na mmom nea ɔde no hyɛɛ aseɛ he pɛ so, abɔdeɛ he anidasoɔ ne sɛ ɔbɛde ne ho afiri nkyekyereɛ ne porɔeɛ a bɛde no ahyɛ aseɛ he mu na obenya ahofadie ya Nyankopɔn mma animuonyam he mu.
Yenim sɛ abɔdeɛ he nyinaa asi apinie awoko yeyaa mu de besi nnɛ; na ɔnyɛ abɔdeɛ he nkoaa, na mmom yɛ nso a yɛanya aba a odi kane a ɔno ne Honhom he, yesi apinie yɛ mu dendenndene berɛ a yɛɛtwɛne sɛ bɛbɛgye yɛ ayɛ mma he, gyeɛ a bɛnam agyedeɛ so bɛgye yɛ afiri yɛ nnipadua mu he.
Na saa anidasoɔ yi mu ne bɛgyee yɛ nkwa.
Na hwane ne hwɛ nea ne nsa aka kwane?
Na sɛ nea yɛwɔ ho anidasoɔ he, yɛ nsa aka a, nka ɔnyɛ adeɛ sɛ yɛbɛkɔ so atwɛne sɛ ɔbɛba mu.
Nso sɛ yɛ ani da nea yɛ nsa nkaeɛ so a, yɛde ntoboaseɛ twɛne.
Saa ara nso ne Honhom he boa yɛ yɛ mmerɛyɛ mu; na yennim sɛnea ɔsɛ sɛ yɛbɔ mpaeɛ a ɔsɛ, nso Honhom he ankasa si apini a mu dɔ kyɛne nsɛm de di ma yɛ.
Na Nyankopɔn a, ɔhwehwɛ akoma mu pefee he, nim Honhom he adwene, efiri sɛ Honhom he di ma ahoteefoɔ he sɛnea Nyankopɔn pɛ.
Yenim sɛ bɛ a bɛdɔ Nyankopɔn he, bɛ a ɔnam ne pɛ so afrɛ bɛ he, ɔfa adeɛ nyinaa so di boa bɛ ma no wie bɛ yie.
Na bɛ a ohuu bɛ sieeɛ he, oyii bɛ too hɔ sɛ bɛnsɛ ne Ba he, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ne Ba he bɛyɛ abakane nnipa bebree mu.
Na bɛ a oyii bɛ sii hɔ he, ɔfrɛɛ bɛ nso; na bɛ a ɔfrɛɛ bɛ he, buu bɛ bem nso; na bɛ a obuu bɛ bem he, hyɛɛ bɛ animuonyam nso.
Nyankopɔn dɔ a ɔya Kristo Yesu mu Hedeɛ mmɛ ne yɛbɛka afa yeinom ho?
Sɛ Nyankopɔn ya yɛ afa a, hwane ne betumi ne yɛ adi asie?
Nea wamfa ɔno ankasa ne Ba ankame yɛ na ɔde no maa yɛ nyinaa he, ɔmmfa nnoɔma nyinaa nka ne (Ba he) ho mma yɛ kwa anaa?
Hwane ne bɛbɔ Nyankopɔn mma a waayi bɛ he kwaadu?
Nyankopɔn ne nea obu bi bem.
Hwane ne ɔsɛ sɛ obu atɛne?
Kristo Yesu ne nea obu atɛne, nea owuiɛ, na benyanee no, nea ɔte Nyankopɔn nsa nifa, nea odi ma yɛ nɔkorem he.
Hwane ne bɛte yɛ afiri Kristo dɔ ho?
Ahokyerɛ mu oo, ateetee mu oo, taa mu oo, kɔm mu oo, adagyada mu oo, amaneɛ mu oo, wuo mu oo; bibiaa nni hɔ a obetumi ate yɛ afiri Kristo dɔ ho.
Sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Wo nti beku yɛ daa; bebu yɛ sɛ dwane a bɛɛkɔ ku no.” Nso, yeinom nyinaa mu he yɛnam nea ɔdɔ yɛ he so adi nkunim.
Na megye di sɛ mpo wuo, anaa nkwa, anaa abɔfoɔ, anaa atumfoɔ, anaa nnoɔma a ɔya hɔ saa mmerɛ yi, anaa nnoɔma a ɔbɛba, anaa ahoɔdene, anaa nea ɔya soro, anaa nea ɔya bunum, asaase ase, anaa abɔdeɛ biaa, mpo betumi ntete yɛ mmfiri Nyankopɔn dɔ a ɔya yɛ Awurade Kristo Yesu mu he ho.
Yi a Nyankopɔn ayi Israel Meeka Kristo mu nɔkorɛ, meenni torɔ; Honhom Kronkron nam m’ahonim so di adanseɛ.
Medi awerɛhoɔ paa ne yeyaa m’akomam daa.
Nka mepɛ sɛ bɛde me ankasa yɛ abusudeɛ na beyi me firi Kristo mu, me mane mufoɔ a bɛyɛ me honam fam abusuafoɔ nti.
Bɛyɛ Israelfoɔ, na bɛ ne abayɛ, animuonyam, apam, ne mmara he som he, ɔne bɔhyɛ he nyinaa yɛ bɛ dea; bɛyɛ tete agyanom asefoɔ, na ofiri bɛ abusua mu ne Kristo he baa honam fam.
Nhyira nka Nyankopɔn a ɔyɛ adeɛ nyinaa sodifoɔ daa.
Amen.
Na ɔnyɛ sɛ ebia Nyankopɔn asɛm he adi hwammɔ.
Na ɔnyɛ bɛ a befiri Israel nyinaa ne bɛyɛ Israelfoɔ mapa, na nyɛ Abraham mma nyinaa ne bɛyɛ n’asefoɔ mapa; nso bɛatwerɛ sɛ “Wasefoɔ firi Isak mu ne bɛba.” Yei kyerɛ sɛ ɔnnyɛ honam fam mma ne yɛ Nyankopɔn mma, na mmom bɔhyɛ mma ne bebu bɛ sɛ n’asefoɔ ankasa.
Na sei ne bɔhyɛ he kaeɛ, “Berɛ sei mu mɛba, na Sara anya ba beema.” Na ɔnyɛ yei nkoaa; saa berɛ a Rebeka nso nam ne kunu, yɛ nana Isak so nyinsɛneeɛ he, bibi siiɛ.
Berɛ a na bennya nwoo bɛ mmaa bɛmmɛyɔɔ papa anaa bɔne bibiaa mu mpo he bɛka kyerɛɛ no (Rebeka) sɛ, “Panyini he bɛsom kumaa he.” Sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Medɔɔ Yakob, nso metanee Esau.” Hedeɛ mmɛ ne yɛbɛka?
Atɛntenenee nni Nyankopɔn fam?
Daabi da!
Efiri sɛ ɔka kyerɛɛ Mose sɛ, “Mehu nea mehu no mmɔbɔ mmɔbɔ, na me yam bɛhyehye me ama nea meyam bɛhyehye no ama no.” Ne saa nti onyina nipa pɛ anaa nhyɛ so, na mmom Nyankopɔn a ohu mmɔbɔ he so.
Na twerɛsɛm he ka kyerɛ Farao sɛ,” Maama wo so sɛ me botae a ɔkyerɛ me tumi he bɛda adi wɔ wo mu, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a bɛbɛbɔ me dini asaase nyinaa so.” Ne saa nti ohu biaa a waayi no mmɔbɔ, na opirim biaa ɔpɛ akoma.
Nyankopɔn abufuo ne n’ahummɔborɔ Hedeɛ wobebisa me sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne ɔda so hu mfomsoɔ?
Na hwane ne betumi asi Nyankopɔn pɛ kwane?” Nso ampa wone hwane, o!
Nipa dasani, sɛ wo ne Nyankopɔn yiyi nsɛm ano?
Nti nea bɛanwono no he betumi aka akyerɛ nea ɔnwonoo no he sɛ, “Mmɛ nti ne woyɔɔ me sei?” Nwonfoɔ nni tumi nɛteɛ so, sɛ ɔde nɛteɛ korɔ heaa bi bɛyɔ bibi a anidie yam na foforɔ so nea anidie nnim?
Na sɛ, Nyankopɔn pɛ sɛ ɔda n’abufuo adi na ɔma behu ne tumi, nso ɔde abodwokyɛre bebree kura abufuo adeɛ a ɔda hɔ ma ɔsɛe he mu a; na sɛ ɔnam saa kwane he so da n’animuonyam ahonya adi ma mmɔborɔhunu adeɛ a wasiesie ato hɔ dadaada ma animuonyam a— sɛ yɛ a ɔfrɛɛ yɛ yi nso yɛka ho a, na omfiri Yudafoɔ nkoaa mu na mmom Amanamane mufoɔ nso a, yɛbɛka sɛ?
Sɛnea Hosea mu nso ɔka sɛ, “Bɛ a na bɛnnyɛ me nkurofoɔ he mɛfrɛ bɛ ‘me nkurofoɔ,’ na nea ɔnnyɛ me dɔfo he mɛfrɛ no ‘medɔfo.’ ” “Na baabi a bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ, ‘Honnyɛ me nkurofoɔ,’ he hɔaa nso ne bɛbɛfrɛ bɛ Nyankopɔn Teasefoɔ he mma.” Na Yesaia teaa Israel ho sɛ, “Ewom sɛ na Israel mma te sɛ mpoano anwea, nso bɛ a bɛbɛka kakraa bi ne bɛbɛgye bɛ nkwa; efiri sɛ Awurade bedi n’asɛm asaase yi so awie atwa no tiaa.” Na sɛnea Yesaia kaa too hɔ he, “Sɛ Nyankopɔn a ɔya soro annya nkaeɛfoɔ amma yɛ a, nka yɛ ase hyee sɛ Sodom ama yɛayɛ sɛ Gomora.” Paulo mpaeɛ a ɔbɔ ma Israel Afei deɛ ɛɛne ne yɛbɛka?
Amanamane mufoɔ, a bɛanhwehwɛ tenenee he, bɛ nsa aka, ɔne sɛ, tenenee a ofiri gyidie mu; nso Israel a, bɛpere hwehwɛɛ tenenee a ogyina mmara so he, bɛ nsa anka.
Ɛɛne nti a?
Efiri sɛ ɔnyɛ gyidie so ne bɛde hwehwɛeɛ, na mmom bɛnam nnwuma so, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Hwɛ, meeto fapem bi Sion a ɔbɛto nnipa bebree sintidua, botane a ɔbɛma bɛahwe ase, na biaa a ɔbɛgye no adi biaa nsa onsi fam.”
Anuanom, m’akoma so adeɛ ne mpaeɛ a mebɔ kyerɛ Nyankopɔn ne sɛ ɔbɛgye me mane Israel nkwa.
Metumi adi adanseɛ sɛ bɛwɔ Nyankopɔn mu mmɔdemmɔ, nso benni nimdeɛ, efiri sɛ, benni tenenee a ofiri Nyankopɔn hɔ he ho nimdeɛ, esiane sɛ bɛpɛ sɛ bɛde bɛ ankasa bɛ tenenee si hɔ nti, bɛmfa bɛ ho nhyɛ Nyankopɔn tenenee mu.
Na Kristo mu ne mmara he nyinaa wie pɛyɛ, nti bɛnam ne so de tenenee ma nea ɔbɛgye adi biaa.
Nkwagyeɛ ya hɔ ma biaa Mose twerɛ faa tenenee a ofiri mmara he ho sɛ, “nipa a ɔyɔ saa nnoɔma yi benya nkwa.” Nso tenenee a ofiri gyidie mu he dɛ, “Nka no w’akomam sɛ, Hwane ne bɛforo akɔ soro?” (Ɔne sɛ, ɔde Kristo bɛba fam), anaa “Hwane besiane akɔ bunum” (ɔne sɛ ɔde Kristo befiri awufoɔ mu aba).
Nso ɛɛne ne ɔka?
Asɛm he bɛne wo, ɔya w’ano ne w’akomam (ɔne sɛ, gyidie asɛm a yɛpae mu ka); efiri sɛ, sɛ wode w’ano pae mu ka sɛ Yesu ne Awurade na wode w’akoma gye di sɛ Nyankopɔn anyane no afiri awufoɔ mu a, wobenya nkwa.
Na akoma ne bɛde gye di ma bebu bɛ bem, na ano ne bɛde pae mu ka nya nkwa.
Twerɛsɛm he dɛ, “Nea ɔgye no di biaa nsa onsi fam.” Na yei ho he, nsosonoeɛ biaa nni Yudani anaa Helani ntam; Awurade korɔ heaa ne di bɛ nyinaa bɛ so, ne yam yɛ ma bɛ a bɛbɔ ne dini nyinaa, efiri sɛ, “Nea ɔbɛbɔ Awurade dini biaa benya nkwa.” Nso ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na bi atumi abɔ nea ɔnnye no nni dini?
Na ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na bi agye nea ɔntee ne ho asɛm adi?
Na sɛ bi anka Awurade ho asɛm ankyerɛ bɛ a bɛbɛyɛdɛ ate?
Na sɛ bɛansoma asɛmpakafoɔ a, ɔbɛyɛdɛ na bi akɔka asɛm he?
Nti bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Hwɛ bɛ a bɛde asɛmpa he ba he bɛ nane ase ɔfɛ fa!” Nso nyɛ bɛ nyinaa ne bɛayɔ setie ama asɛmpa he; efiri sɛ Yesaia dɛ, “Awurade, hwane ne agye yɛ asɛm adi?” Nti gyidie firi nea yɛate mu ne ba, na nea yɛate nso firi Kristo asɛm he mu.
Nso meebisa sɛ, bɛntee koraa?
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ bɛate; efiri sɛ “Bɛapae mu aka no asaase nyinaa so, na bɛ nsɛm nso aduru wiase afanaa nyinaa.” Meebisa bio sɛ, nti Israel ante aseɛ?
Nea odi kane, Mose dɛ, “Mɛma ho atwe bɛ a bɛnyɛ mane he ho ninkunu; mɛma ho bo afu atia amane nkwaseafoɔ.” Hedeɛ, Yesaia nyaa akokoɔduro paa sɛ ɔkaa sɛ, “Bɛ a bɛanhwehwɛ me he, bɛahu me; Maayi me ho adi akyerɛ bɛ a bɛanhwehwɛ me.” Nso Israel ho deɛ ɔkaa sɛ, “Da nyinaa metrɛɛ me nsam maa mane asoɔdenfoɔ ne nyiyianofoɔ yi.”
Israel poɔ he nyɛ n’awieeɛ Afei meebisa sɛ, nti Nyankopɔn apo ne nkurofoɔ?
Daabi da!
M’ankasa meyɛ Israelni a meyɛ Abraham aseni a mefiri Benyamin abusuakuo mu.
Nyankopɔn mpoo ne nkurofoɔ a oyii bɛ sieeɛ he.
Wonnim deɛ twerɛsɛm he ka fa Elia ho, sɛnea ɔbɔɔ Isreal soboɔ kyerɛɛ Nyankopɔn?
“Awurade bɛaku w’adiyifoɔ, bɛabubu w’afɔrebokyia; me nkoaa ne maaka, na bɛɛhwehwɛ me aku me.” Na mmɛ mmuaeɛ ne Nyankopɔn de maa no?
“Makora nnipa mpem nson ama me ho a bɛ nkotodwe nkotoo Baal da.” Nti saa ne berɛ yi mu nso nnipa nkaeɛ bi ya hɔ a bɛnam adom so ayi bɛ.
Na sɛ ɔyɛ adom a, ɔnna so nyinaa nnwuma so, anyɛ saa a, hedeɛ na adom he nyɛ adom ankasa.
Afei mmɛ bio?
Israel nsa anka nea ɔɔhwehwɛ he.
Bɛ a bɛayi bɛ he deɛ bɛ nsa kaeɛ, nso bɛ a bɛaka he deɛ beprim bɛ akoma, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Nyankopɔn ama bɛ honhom a ɔtɔ nko, ani a onhu adeɛ ne aso a ɔnte asɛm, de besi nnɛ.” Na Dawid dɛ, “Ma bɛ adidipono nyɛ fidisum ne fidie, sintiduatoɔ ne akatua mma bɛ; ma bɛ ani nyɛ kusuu sɛnea benhu adeɛ, na ma bɛ akyi nkuntunu daa.” Amanamane nkwagyeɛ Nti meebisa sɛ, bɛasonti sɛ bɛbɛhwe ase?
Daabi da!
Nso ɔnam bɛ sintidua he so ama Amanamane mufoɔ anya nkwagyeɛ, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a Israel bɛtwe ninkunu.
Na afei sɛ bɛ sintiduatoɔ he kyerɛ wiase ahonya a, na sɛ bɛ nkoguo de ahonya maa Amanamane mufoɔ a, hedeɛ na gye a bɛbɛgye bɛ atom he bɛboro so!
Afei meekasa akyerɛ ho Amanamane mufoɔ.
Esiane sɛ meyɛ somafoɔ ma Amanamane mufoɔ nti, mehyɛ me som animuonyam sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a m’ankasa me nkurofoɔ bɛtwe ninkunu, na bɛagye binom.
Na sɛ bɛpo a bɛpoo bɛ he bɛyɛ wiase mpataa a, hedeɛ bɛ gyeɛ nso bɛyɛ nkwa a ofiri wuom!
Afei sɛ dua aba a odi kane a bɛde bɔɔ afɔdeɛ he yɛ kronkron a, aba mu he nyinaa nso yɛ kronkron; na sɛ ne nhini he yɛ kronkron a, ne mmane he nso nyinaa bɛyɛ kronkron.
Nso sɛ mmane he bi bu firii ho a, na wo, wuram ngodua, bɛde wo hyɛɛ ananem sɛ wobenya ahonya a ɔya ngodua nhini he mu bi a, nhoahoa wo ho mmane he ho.
Sɛ wohoahoa wo ho a, kae sɛ ɔnyɛ wo ne wokita nhini he mu, na mmom nhini he ne kita wo mu.
Saa nti wobɛka sɛ, “Mmane bi bubuiɛ sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a bɛde me besi ananem.” Ɛɛ, yei yɛ nɔkorɛ.
Gye a bɛannye anni nti ne betwaa bɛtweneeɛ, nso gyidie nkoaa so ne wobegyina.
Nti nyɛ ahantan, na mmom fa suro gyina pintinn.
Na sɛ Nyankopɔn ankora mmane he ankasa a, ebia wo nso ɔnkora wo.
Hyɛ Nyankopɔn ayamyɛ ne ne dene yɛ nso: ɔdene ma bɛ a bɛhwee ase, nso Nyankopɔn ayamyɛ ya hɔ ma wo, gye sɛ wo toa so n’ayamyɛ he mu; anyɛ saa a wo nso bebetwa wo atwene.
Na mpo Israel nso, sɛ bɛantoa so ampirim bɛ akoma annyeannie ho a, bɛde bɛ bɛhyɛ mu bio, efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn wɔ tumi sɛ ɔde bɛ hyɛ mu bio.
Sɛ wo mpo, betwaa wo firii wuram ngodua he ho, na bɛakwati wɔawosuo de wo atɛ ngodua pa he mu a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ ne ontumi mfa ne ngodua pa he ankasa mmane he ɔmmɛtɛ mu bio?
Bɛbɛgye Israel nyinaa nkwa Nti, anuanom, mepɛ sɛ hote saa ahintasɛm yi ase, na hoammu ho ho anyansafoɔ ho ankasa ho ani so: akomapirim bi aba Israelfoɔ bi so, kosi sɛ Amanamane mufoɔ bebree bɛba mu.
Ne saa nti bɛbɛgye Israelfoɔ nyinaa nkwa; sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Sion mu ne Gyefoɔ befiri aba; obetu amumuyɔ afiri Yakob.” “Na yei ne m’apam a me ne bɛ bɛpam, berɛ a meyi bɛ bɔne afiri hɔ.” Ɔfa asɛmpa he ho deɛ, ho nti bɛyɛ Nyankopɔn atamfoɔ; nso ɔfa yie he ho deɛ, bɛyɛ adɔfoɔ, bɛ nananom nti; efiri sɛ, Nyankopɔn ntwe n’akyɛdeɛ ne ne frɛ nsane da.
Sɛnea mmerɛ bi hoyɔɔ asoɔdene tiaa Nyankopɔn nso bɛ asoɔdene nti hoanya mmɔborɔhunu he, saa nso nti bɛayɛ asoɔdene a, ahummɔborɔ a hoanya nti, bɛ nso saa berɛ he bebenya mmɔborɔhunu.
Nyankopɔn ama bɛ asoɔdene aka bɛ ato afiase sɛ obehu bɛ mmɔbɔ.
O!
Nyankopɔn ahonya ne ne nyansa ɔne ne nimdeɛ a mu dɔ!
Yentumi nhu n’atemmuo ne n’akwane mu nwie da!
“Na hwane ne ahu Awurade adwene?
Anaa hwane ne ayɛ ne fotufoɔ?” “Anaa hwane ne ama no akyɛdeɛ, a ɔbɛgye akyɛdeɛ asi ananem?” Biaa nni hɔ efiri sɛ, nnoɔma nyinaa firi ne mu, na ɔnam ne so, na ɔyɛ ne dea.
Ɔno ne animuonyam nka no daa daa.
Amen.
Kristo mu nkwa foforɔ he Nti anuanom, megyina Nyankopɔn mmɔborɔhunu so ɔɔsrɛ ho sɛ, homfa ho nipadua nsi hɔ sɛ afɔdeɛ a ɔte ase, a ɔyɛ kronkron a ɔsɔ Nyankopɔn ani.
Yei ne nyamesom pa. Na homfa wiase nhyehyɛeɛ yi so, na mmom honsakra ho adwene na honyɛ foforɔ, na hoasɛ ahwɛ ahu nea Nyankopɔn pɛ a ɔyɛ na ɔsɔ ani na odi mu.
Na menam adom a bɛde ama me he so, meeka akyerɛ ho sɛ, ho mu biaa mmu ne ho ntra sɛnea ɔsɛ sɛ obu ne ho, na mmom, biaa nya anidahɔ adwene, sɛnea Nyankopɔn asusu gyidie ama ho he.
Na sɛnea honamdua baako wɔ akwaa bebree he, na biaa wɔ dwuma sonoko a odi he, saa nso ne yɛ a yɛdɔɔso yi, yɛyɛ nipadua baako Kristo mu, na yɛyeyɛ yɛ ho akwaa mmaako mmaako.
Yɛwɔ adom akyɛdeɛ a nsonsonoeɛ deda mu, sɛnea adom a bɛde adom yɛ he teɛ.
Sɛ ɔyɛ nkɔmhyɛ a, ma no mfata sɛnea bɛasusu ho gyidie; som adwuma a, ma no nsom; kyerɛkyerɛni a, ma no nkyerɛkyerɛ; fotufoɔ a, ma ontu fo; ɔma a, ma no mma no adɔeɛ mu; dikanfoɔ a, ma ɔmmɔ ne ho mmɔdene akannie mu; ahummɔborɔ a, ma ɔnyɔ no animteɛ mu.
Nɔkorɛ kristoni ahyɛnsodeɛ Hommma nyaatwom mfra dɔ mu; hontane nea ɔyɛ bɔne, honkura nea ɔyɛ papa mu; homfa nteaseɛ nnodɔ ho ho yie; homfa anidie mmɔho mma ho ho.
Honnyɛ mmɔdenmmɔ ho nyaa, honyɛ hye honhom mu, honsom Awurade!
Homma ho ani nnye anidasoɔ mu, honto ho boase amaneɛ mu, hontu ho ho nsi hɔ ma mpaebɔ.
Hommoa ahoteefoɔ ma bɛ nsa nka bɛ ahiadeɛ; homma ho ani nye ahɔhoyɛ ho.
Honhyira bɛ a bɛtaa ho; honhyira, na honnnome.
Ho ne bɛ a bɛ ani agye ani nnye mmom, ho ne bɛ a besu nso nsu mmom.
Ho ne nnipa nyinaa ntena asomdwie mu; honnnyɛ ahantan, na mmom ho ne ahobrɛaseɛfoɔ nante; honnyɛ ahomasoɔ.
Hommmfa bɔne ntua bɔne so ka, na mmom honwene nea odi mu nnipa nyinaa ani so.
Sɛ obetumi a, ho fam deɛ, ho ne nnipa nyinaa ntena asomdwiem.
Adɔfo, honnntotɔ ho ho ho ho werɛ, na mmom honnyae ma Nyankopɔn abufuo; efiri sɛ bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Awerɛtɔ yɛ me dea, meaa ne metua ka, Awurade ne ɔɔka.” Ne saa nti, sɛ kɔm de wo tamfoɔ a, ma no bibi nni; sɛ sukɔm de no a, ma no nsuo nom; na sɛ woyɔ saa a, wobɛhyɛ no aniwuo.
Mma bɔne nnni wo so, na mmom fa papa di bɔne so nim!
Hommrɛ ho ho ase ma tumidie Homma nnipa nyinaa mmrɛbrɛ bɛ ho ase nhyɛ mane mpanyimfoɔ tumi he ase; efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn ne ma nnipa tumi ma ɔde di dwuma, na Nyankopɔn ne de saa tumidie he sii hɔ.
Saa nti biaa a ɔte atua tumidie biaa so he te nea Nyankopɔn de no asi hɔ he so atua, na bɛ a bɛyɔ saa he bɛkɔ afobuo mu.
Efiri sɛ bɛ a bedi mpanyinnie he ho nyɛ hu mma bɛ a bɛbɔ bra pa, na mmom bɛho ohu ma bɛ a bɛyɔ bɔne.
Sɛ wompɛ sɛ wosuro tumfoɔ he a, hedeɛ yɔ nea ɔyɛ papa, na wobenya n’anim adom; efiri sɛ ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn somfoɔ ma wo yiedie.
Nso sɛ woyɔ bɔne a, ɔsɛ sɛ wosuro no, efiri sɛ tumidie he nni hɔ kwa, na mmom atumfoɔ he yɛ Nyankopɔn asomfoɔ a bɛtɔ were de abufuo ba deɛ ɔyɛ bɔne he so.
Ne saa nti ɔsɛ sɛ nipa brɛ ne ho ase, nyɛ abufuo nkoaa nti na mmom suro a osuro atumfoɔ he ɔnoaa n’ahonim nti.
Yei nti ne ɔsɛ sɛ wo tua toɔ nso, efiri sɛ atumfoɔ yi yɛ Nyankopɔn asomfoɔ, na mane he som ti ne bɛya hɔ.
Homfa nea ɔsɛ sɛ hode ma biaa ma no, hontua toɔ ma bɛ a ɔsɛ sɛ hotua toɔ ma bɛ, homfa akatua ma bɛ a akatua sɛ bɛ, hommu nea ɔfata buo, homfa anidie ma nea anidie sɛ no.
Honnodɔ ho ho ho ho Honnne biaa ka, gye sɛ dɔ a hode bɛdodɔ ho ho; na nea ɔdɔ foforɔ he awie mmara he so di, efiri sɛ mmaransɛm a ɔka sɛ, “Mmɔ adwamane; Nni awu; Mmɔ korɔno; Mma w’ani mmere” ne mmaransɛm foforɔ biaa, bɛde ne nyinaa abom asɛm baako yi mu, “Dɔ wo yɔnko sɛ wo ho.” Deɛ ɔdɔ ne yɔnko nyɔ no bɔne; nti dɔ ne ma mmara he nyinaa ba mu.
Adesrɛ a ohia Yeinom nyinaa akyi he, honim sɛnea berɛ he teɛ, sɛ saa berɛ yi ne ɔsɛ sɛ hosɔre firi ho nna mu; efiri sɛ nkwagyeɛ bɛne yɛ kyɛne berɛ a yɛbɛyɛɛ agyidifoɔ; anadwo akɔ n’anim, adekyeɛ abɛne.
Saa nti ho ma yɛnto sum nnwuma ngu na yɛmfa hann akodeɛ; homma yɛmmɔ bra a ɔfata hann mma, ɔnyɛ agobɔne ne nsaboro mu, nyɛ adwamammɔ ne akohwie mu, nyɛ ntɔkwakoo ne aniberebereɛ mu.
Na mmom, homfa Awurade Yesu Kristo nhyɛ (sɛ ataadeɛ), na homma kwane mma honam, akɔnnɔ nni ho so!.
Hommmu biaa atɛne Honnye nea ne gyidie ɔmmerɛ he na hommmu atɛne ya adwene nnaayɛ ho.
Binom gye di sɛ bɛwɔ ho kwane sɛ bedi nnoɔma nyinaa, na nea ɔmmerɛ he deɛ odi nhahama nkoaa.
Ɔnsɛ sɛ bɛ a bedi nnoɔma nyinaa he bebu bɛ a benni nnoɔma bi he animtia, na bɛ a benni nnoɔma bi he nso, ɔnsɛ sɛ bebu bɛ a bedi he atɛne; efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn agye saa nipa he.
Wo ne hwane sɛ wobebu bi akoa atɛne?
Ɔyɛ bɛ wura he ankasa ne bɛkyerɛ sɛ nea bɛayɔ he yɛ anaa ɔnyɛ; efiri sɛ nɔkorem he Awurade betumi ama bɛagyina Binom bu atɛne sɛ da bi di mu kyɛne bi, binom nso bu nna nyinaa pɛ.
Homma biaa nte ne ho ase sɛnea n’adwene kyerɛ no.
Bɛ a bebu da bi he, bɛde hyɛ Awurade animuonyam.
Na bɛ a bedi he nso, bedi hyɛ Awurade animuonyam, esiane sɛ bɛda Nyankopɔn ase; bɛ a benni he nso, di a benni he bɛde hyɛ Awurade animuonyam, na bɛda Nyankopɔn ase.
Na yɛnnte ase mma yɛ ho, saa so ne yenwu mma yɛ ho.
Sɛ yɛte ase a, yɛte ase ma Awurade, na sɛ yewu nso a, yewu ma Awurade; nti, sɛ yɛte ase oo, anaa sɛ yewu oo, yɛyɛ Awurade dea.
Na yei nti Kristo wuiɛ na ɔte ase bio, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ɔbɛyɛ awufoɔ ne ateasefoɔ nyinaa bɛ Awurade.
Mmɛ nti ne wobu wo ankasa wo nua atɛne?
Anaa wo, ɛɛne nti ne wobu wo nua animtia?
Na bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Awurade dɛ, sɛ mete ase yi, kotodwe nyinaa bɛkoto me, na kɛtrɛma nyinaa beyi Nyankopɔn ayɛ.” Ne saa nti, yemu biaa bebu n’ankasa akonta akyerɛ Nyankopɔn.
Honto biaa sintidua Afei hommma yemmu biaa atɛne, nso homma yɛnyɔ yɛadwene sɛ yɛmmfa akwansideɛ nto biaa kwane mu, saa ara nso ne yɛnnto biaa sintidua.
Menim na megye di Awurade Yesu mu sɛ bibi biaa nni hɔ a honnte ankasa; nso honnte mma nea ɔdwene sɛ honnte.
Sɛ aduane a wodi sɛe wo nua ahonim a, hedeɛ na ɔnyɛ dɔ mu ne woonante he.
Mma aduane a wodi he nto bi a Kristo wu maa no he sintidua.
Nti hommma bɛmmu ho papayɔ sɛ ɔyɛ bɔne; efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn ahennie he mfa adidie ne nom ho, na mmom ne nyinasoɔ ne tenenee ne asomdwie ne Honhom Kronkron mu anigyeɛ.
Na nea ɔsom Kristo saa kwane so he ɔno ne sɔ Nyankopɔn ani na nnipa gye no tom.
Nti homma yenni asomdwie ɔne nnoɔma a ɔma nkɔsoɔ akyi.
Aduane nti, honnsɛe Nyankopɔn adwuma.
Adeɛ nyinaa ho te deɛ, nso ɔnnyɛ sɛ aduane a wodi nti woma bi hwe ase; ɔyɛ sɛ wonnwe nam anaa wonnom nsa anaa sɛ wonnyɔ bibi a ɔbɛto wo nua sintidua.
Gyidie a wowɔ he, ma ɔnyɛ sɛnea w’ahonim teɛ Nyankopɔn anim.
Nhyira ne nea a ɔmma nea wasi ho gyinaeɛ he mmu ne fɔ.
Nso bɛ a bɛ adwene nsi bɛ pi he sɛ bedi a bedi fɔ, efiri sɛ bɛannyɔ no gyidie mu, na bibiaa a omfiri gyidie mu biaa yɛ bɔne.
Sɔ afoforɔ anni, ɔnyɛ wo ankasa Afei yɛ a yɛ ho ɔdene he ɔsɛ sɛ yɛboa bɛ a bɛyɛ mmerɛ he, na yɛansɔ yɛ ankasa yɛ ani.
Ɔsɛ sɛ yemmu biaa sɔ ne yɔnko ani a ne botae ne sɛ yɛbɛboa yɛ yɔnko ama no anyini honhom mu; efiri sɛ Kristo ammɛsɔ ɔnoaa ankasa ani; na mmom, sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Atɛm a bedii wo he abegu me so.” Efiri sɛ nea bɛtwerɛɛ no kane nna he mu he bɛtwerɛɛ sɛ ɔnyɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ mma yɛ, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ɔnam twerɛsɛm he so bɛma yɛ boasetɔ ne awerekyekyerɛ ama yɛaya anidasoɔ.
Boasetɔ ne awerekyekyerɛ Nyankopɔn he mma ho ntena asomdwie mu, sɛnea ɔfata Kristo Yesu, na hode anokorɔ ahyɛ Nyankopɔn a ɔyɛ yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo agya he animuonyam.
Asɛmpa a ɔyɛ Yudafoɔ ne Amanamane mufoɔ nyinaa deɛ Nti, honnye biaa mma ɔnhyɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam, sɛnea Kristo nso agye ho he.
Na meeka kyerɛ ho sɛ Kristo gyina Nyankopɔn nɔkorɛ so ayɛ akoa ama twetiatwafoɔ sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ɔbɛhyɛ bɔhyɛ a bɛde maa nananom he dene, na wɔama Amanamane mufoɔ ahyɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam ne mmɔborɔhunu nti.
Sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Nti mɛbɔ wo dini Amanamane mufoɔ mu, na mato wo dini ho ayeyie nnwomu”; na bio so ɔdɛ, “Amanamane mufoɔ, ho ne ne nkurofoɔ mma ho ani nye”; na bio, “Amanamane mufoɔ nyinaa, ho nyi Awurade ayɛ, na homma nnipa nyinaa nyi n’ayɛ”; na afei nso Yesaia kaa sɛ, “Yisai aseni bi bɛba, nea ɔbɛsɔre adi hene Amanamane mufoɔ so; ne mu ne Amanamane mufoɔ benya anidasoɔ.” Anidasoɔ Nyankopɔn ankasa nhyɛ ho ma anigyeɛ ne asomdwie nyinaa mu gye a hoogye adi ho, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a hobɛboro so anidasoɔ nyinaa mu Honhom Kronkron tumi mu.
Deɛ nti a Paulo de akokoɔduro ɔɔtwerɛ Me ankasa mewɔ awerɛhyɛmu ma ho, me nuanom, ho ankasa hoayɛ ma nnepa a ɔyɛ nyinaa mu, nimdeɛ nyinaa ahyɛ ho ma, na hotumi kyerɛkyerɛ ho ho.
Nso ne nyinaa mu he, deɛ ntia meetwerɛ ho penpen ya nsɛm yi bi ho, te sɛ deɛ mede ɔɔkae ho bio he ne adom a Nyankopɔn de adom me sɛ mɛnyɛ Kristo somfoɔ mma Amanamane mufoɔ sɛ Nyankopɔn asɛmpa he ho asɔfodwuma, na Amanamane mufoɔ afɔrebɔ ayɛ nea Honhom Kronkron ate ho a ɔsɔ ani.
Kristo Yesu mu deɛ, metumi hoahoa me ho Nyankopɔn adwuma a meyɔ ho.
Nti menhyɛ me ho nka asɛm biaa gye nea Kristo nam me so ayɔ ama Amanamane mufoɔ setie ya asɛm ne adwuma mu tumi a ɔyɔ anwanwadeɛ ne nsɛnkyerɛnne, Nyankopɔn Honhom tumi mu, sɛ maawie Kristo asɛmpa he ka firi Yerusalem de kosi Iliriko.
Nti mede ayɛ me botae sɛ mɛka asɛmpa he, nyɛ baabi a bɛabɔ Kristo dini dada, na manto bi fapem so, na mmom sɛnea bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Bɛ a bɛnkaa ne ho asɛm nkyerɛɛ bɛ he behu, na bɛ a bɛntee ne ho asɛm he bɛte aseɛ.” Paulo pɛɛ sɛ ɔbɛkɔ Roma Yei nti ne bɛasi kwane a mantumi amma ho nkyɛne.
Nso seesei deɛ, baabiaa nni hɔ a aka ma me a mɛkɔ mpɔtamu ha, ɔyɛ mepɛ, sɛnea mayɔ sɛ mfie bebree di, mɛba ho nkyɛne.
Da biaa a metu kwane akɔ Spania he, m’ani da so sɛ, mɛfa hɔ a, mehu ho anim, na sɛ megye m’ani kakra ho nkyɛne a, hoagya me kwane akɔ hɔ.
Nso saa berɛ yi deɛ, meekɔ Yerusalem akɔsom ahoteefoɔ he; na aasɔ Makedonia ne Akaia ani sɛ bɛde nea bɛwɔ he bi bɛma ahoteefoɔ a bɛya Yerusalem he mu ahiafoɔ.
Ɔsɔɔ bɛ ani sɛ bɛbɛyɔ saa, nɔkorɛ mu ɔfata; efiri sɛ, sɛ ɔnam bɛ so ama Amanamane mufoɔ he anya honhom fam nhyira a, otwa sɛ bɛ (Amanamane mufoɔ) nso bɛma bɛ (Yudafoɔ) honam fam nnoɔma de som bɛ bi.
Nti, sɛ mewie saa adeɛ yi a, na mede nea bɛagyegye he ma bɛ a, mɛfa ho nkyɛne akɔ Spania; na menim sɛ, sɛ meba ho nkyɛne a, mede Kristo mu nhyira a ɔboro so bɛbra ho.
Nso anuanom, megyina yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo ne Honhom he dɔ so, srɛ ho sɛ hommoa me, na homfa mpaebɔ nsrɛ Nyankopɔn aniberɛ so mma me, sɛ bɛbɛgye me afiri Yudeafoɔ a bɛnnye asɛmpa he nni he nsam, na me som a mɛsom Yerusalem he asɔ ahoteefoɔ he ani, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ɔnam Nyankopɔn pɛ so mede anigyeɛ bɛba ho nkyɛne na me ho adwo me ho nkyɛne.
Asomdwie Nyankopɔn he ne ho nyinaa ntena.
Amen.
Nkyea Afei medi yɛ nuabaa Foibe, somfoɔ a ɔya Kenkrea asafo mu ho adanse-pa kyerɛ ho, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a hobɛgye no Awurade mu sɛ anidie a ɔfata ahoteefoɔ, na hommoa no nea obebisa ho nyinaa ho, efiri sɛ waboa nnipa bebree a meaa nso meka ho bi.
Honkyea Priska ne Akwila, bɛ a bɛ ne meyɔ adwuma Kristo Yesu mu, na bekuu bɛ ho maa me, me nkwa ho, na meda bɛ ase, ɔnyɛ bɛ nkoa na mmom Amanamane mufoɔ asafo he nyinaa nso ka ho bi.
Honkyea asafo a ɔya bɛ fie he nso.
Honkyea me dɔfo Epaineto, a ɔyɛ Kristo mu abakane ya Asia he.
Honkyea Maria a, wayɔ adwuma dene paa ho mu he.
Honkyea Androniko ne Yunia, m’abusuafoɔ a na bɛka me ho afiase; bɛ a bedi mu asomafoɔ he mu, na bɛya Kristo mu ansa na meeba.
Honkyea Amplia a ɔyɛ me dɔfo Awurade mu.
Honkyea Urbano a ɔyɛ me yɔnko Kristo mu dwumayɔni, ne me dɔfoɔ Staki.
Honkyea Apele, a ɔsɔ ani Kristo mu.
Honkyea bɛ a befiri Aristobulo abusua mu.
Honkyea me busuani Herodion.
Honkyea Narkiso abusuafoɔ a bɛya Awurade mu.
Honkyea adwumayɔfoɔ a bɛya Awurade mu, Trifaina ne Trifosa.
Honkyea dɔfoɔ Persi a wayɔ adwuma dene Awurade mu.
Honkyea Rufo a, bɛayi no Awurade mu; na honkyea ne maame—a ɔyɛ me nso me maame.
Honkyea Asinkrito, Flegon, Herme, Patroba, Herma, ne anuanom a bɛka bɛ ho.
Honkyea Filologo, Yulia, Nereo ɔne ne nuabaa, ne Olimpa, ne ahoteefoɔ a bɛ ne bɛya hɔ he.
Honkyeakyea ho ho dɔ kwane so.
Kristo asafo he nyinaa kyea ho.
Nkyerɛkyerɛ a otwa toɔ Anuanom, mehyɛ ho nkurane sɛ, honhwɛ ho ho yie bɛ a bɛde mpaepaemu ne sintiduatoɔ, de ko tia nkyerɛkyerɛ a hoasua he; hontwe ho ho mfiri bɛ ho, efiri sɛ nnipa a bɛte saa he nsom yɛ Awurade Kristo, na mmom bɛsom bɛ a bɛ akɔnnɔ, na bɛde kɛtrɛma dɛ ne adɛfɛdɛfɛsɛm daadaa bɛ a bennim bɔne he akoma.
Nti ɔma m’ani gye ho ho, mepɛ sɛ honya nnepa ho nyansa, na honte ho ho mfiri bɔne ho koraa.
Asomdwie Nyankopɔn he bɛpɛkyɛ Satan ho nane ase ntɛm.
Yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo adom nka ho ho.
Timoteo, me yɔnko dwumayɔni, ne Lukio ne Yason ne Sosipatro a bɛyɛ m’abusuafoɔ kyea ho.
Me Tertio a meetwerɛ Paulo ano asɛm yi, me nso mekyea ho Awurade mu.
Gaio a ɔyɛ me ne asafo he nyinaa fiewura nso kyea ho.
Erasto, kurom ha sikakorafoɔ, ne yɛ nua beema Kwarto nso kyea ho.
