Ma w’ani mmara wo ho so ɔne wo nkyerɛkyerɛ so paa; toa so yeinom mu na wonam saa yɔ so bɛgye wo ne w’atiefoɔ nkwa.
Agyidifoɔ ho asodie Nkasa ntia panyini, na mmom tu no fo sɛ ɔyɛ w’agya, kasa kyerɛ mmaranteɛ sɛ wo nuanom, kasa kyerɛ mmaa mpanyimfoɔ sɛ wo nanom, kasa kyerɛ mmabaa sɛ wo nuammaanom ya ahoteɛ nyinaa mu.
Di akunafoɔ a benni aboafoɔ he ni, na ma bɛ ahiadeɛ nhia wo.
Sɛ kunani baa bi wɔ mma anaa nanaanom a, benni kane nsua nyamesom pa bɛ fie mu na bentua bibi mma bɛ awofoɔ; na yei ne sɔ Nyankopɔn ani.
Kunafoɔ baa a onni boafoɔ he de n’ani to Nyankopɔn so na okura nkotosrɛ ne mpaebɔ mu anadwo ne awia; na kunani baa a odi honam akɔnnɔ akyi he yɛ teaseawuo.
Yeinom ho ne hyɛ bɛ, na bɛannya dimmɔne biaa.
Na sɛ bi anhwɛ ɔnoaa ankasa n’abusuafoɔ, ne titire ne fiefoɔ a, waapa gyidie he, na deɛ ɔnnye nni mpo yɛ kyɛne no.
Ansa na bɛde kunafoɔ bi dini bɛka ho he, ɔsɛ sɛ waadi firi mfie aduosia ɔɔkɔ na ɔwɔ ɔno ankasa ne kunu; ɔsɛ sɛ bedi ne ho adanse-pa, sɛ ɔyɛ bi a watete mmɔfra, ayɔ ahɔhoyɛ, asom agyidifoɔ he ahobrɛaseɛ mu (ahohoro ahoteefoɔ he nane ase), aboa bɛ a bɛwɔ amaneɛ mu, na ɔde ne ho ama papayɔ adeɛ nyinaa mu.
Na akunafoɔ mmaa a benyiniiɛ deɛ, mfa bɛ nhyɛ mu bi; efiri sɛ bɛ akɔnnɔ twe bɛ firi Kristo ho a bɛbɛpɛ sɛ bɛbɛware, na bɛyɔ saa a, bebenya afobuo sɛ bɛabu bɛ bɔhyɛ so.
Ɔno akyi he, besua aniha, kyinkyini afie mu, na bɛnyɛ aniha nkoaa, na mmom bedi nsekuro a bɛnenam terɛterɛ keka nsɛm a ɔnsɛ sɛ bɛka.
Nti mepɛ sɛ akunafoɔ a benyiniiɛ he wareware, wowo mma, na bɛhwɛ bɛ fie, na yɛamma tamfoɔ he kwane amma wanka yɛ ho asɛm bɔne.
Na binom asane akodi Satan akyi dada.
Sɛ gyidini baa bi wɔ abusuafoɔ a bɛyɛ akunafoɔ a, ma ɔmmoa bɛ; mma ɔmfa nto asafo he so, na asafo he atumi aboa akunafoɔ a benni mmoa he.
Ma bɛmfa anidie a odi mu mma asafo mpanyimfoɔ a bedi asafo he so yie he, titire ne bɛ a bɛka asɛmpa na bɛkyerɛkyerɛ; na atwerɛ he ka sɛ, “Nkata nantwie a ɔɔpore aburo ano,” na “Paani akatua sɛ no.” Nnye kwaadu a otia panyini biaa ntom gye sɛ ogyina adansefoɔ mmienu anaa mmeɛnsa anum asɛm so.
Adesrɛ ne afotuo Na bɛ a bɛkɔ so tena bɔne mu he deɛ, yi bɛ atene nnipa nyinaa anim na ama bɛ a bɛaka he nso bɛasuro.
Nyankopɔn ne Kristo Yesu ne abɔfoɔ a bɛayi bɛ he anim ne meebɔ wo kɔkɔ sɛ di saa nkyerɛkyerɛ yi so a wonhwɛ nnipa anim, na womfa ntɛnkyea nni dwuma biaa.
Mpre wo ho mfa wo nsa ngu biaa so, na nyɔ afoforɔ bɔne bi; ma wo ho nte.
Nnom nsuo nkoaa bio, na wo yafunu ne mmerɛ a wotaa yɛ he nti, nom nsa kakraa bi nso!
Nnipa binom bɔne da adi pefee de bɛ ɔɔkɔ atemmuo mu binom nso bɔne di bɛ akyi.
Saa nso ne nnwuma pa nso da adi pefee; na sɛ anyɛ saa mpo a onhinta afebɔɔ.
Ma bɛ a bɛhyɛ nkoasom ase nhu bɛ wuranom sɛ bɛ sɛ anidie mapa, na amma bi ankasa antia Nyankopɔn dini ne nkyerɛkyerɛ he.
Na mma bɛ a bɛwɔ awuranom gyidifoɔ mmmu bɛ animtia sɛ bɛyɛ anuanom nti, na mmom bɛnsom bɛ yie, efiri sɛ bɛ a bɛsom bɛ he yɛ agyidifoɔ ne adɔfoɔ.
Yeinom ne kyerɛkyerɛ, na tu ho fo.
Nkontompo nkyerɛkyerɛ Biaa a ɔkyerɛkyerɛ bibi foforɔ a ɔne Awurade Yesu Kristo nsɛmpa ne ne nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɔyɛ nyamesompa he bɔ abira he, ɔyɛ nipa a ahomasoɔ ahyɛ no ma, onnim hwee, n’asɛm yɛ twintwann, na ɔgye asɛm biaa ho akyinnye ma no de ahoɔyeya, mpaepaemu, nantitwitwa, nnipa ho adwemmɔne, ne ntɔkwapɛ ba bɛ a porɔeɛ asɛe bɛ adwene a nɔkorɛ asapare bɛ na bɛdwene sɛ nyamesom pa yɛ adeɛ a bɛde pɛ mfasoɔ he mu.
Adufudepɛ Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, nyamesompa, ɔne sɔ a bi ɔɔma n’ani asɔ nea ɔwɔ he, yɛ adenya kɛseɛ, efiri sɛ yɛamfa hwee amma wiase, na yentumi mfa hwee mfiri mu nkɔ; na sɛ yɛwɔ nea yebedi ne nea yɛbɛhyɛ a, yɛmma ɔnsom bo mma yɛ.
Na bɛ a bɛɛpɛ bɛ ho anya he hwe sɔhwɛ, fidie ne nkwasea akɔnnɔ mu a ɔde yawdie ba, a ɔnyɛ mma nnipa na ɔtwe bɛ kɔ sɛeɛ ne yera mu.
Na bɔne ahodoɔ nyinaa bi farebae ne sikaniberɛ a, binom adi akyire ayera kwane na bɛde yea pii awowɔ bɛ ho.
Adesrɛ bi Na wo, Nyankopɔn nnipa deɛ, po yeinom nyinaa; hwehwɛ tenenee, nyamesom-pa, gyidie, dɔ, yokoduru ne dwoɔ akyi kwane.
Ko gyidie ko pa he, sɔ daa nkwa a bɛfrɛ wo baa mu, berɛ a wogye too mu kwane pa so adansefoɔ bebree anim, he mu dene.
Meetu wo fo Nyankopɔn a ɔma nnoɔma nyinaa nkwa ne Kristo Yesu a ɔpaee mu kaa no yie, dii ho adanseɛ Pontio Pilato anim he, sɛ: hwɛ ahyɛdeɛ he so, mma dɛm anaa asɛm bi mmma ho kosi Awurade Yesu Kristo ahoyie so.
Ɔno Nyankopɔn ne bɛkyerɛ berɛ a ɔsɛ mu ne ahotɔ tumfoɔ korɔ he, ahene mu Hene ne awuranom mu Awurade.
Ɔno nkoaa ne wɔ anwuda tebea na ɔte hann a bi ntumi nkɔ ho, nea biaa nhu no da na biaa ntumi nhu no; ɔno ne anidie ne daa tumidie wɔ no.
Amen.
Otu adefoɔ fo Nnipa a bɛanya bɛ ho wiase yi mu he, hyɛ bɛ sɛ mma bɛnnwene akokurokosɛm, saa nso ne bɛmmfa bɛ ho nto ahonyadeɛ a onni hɔ daa so, na mmom bɛmfa bɛ ho nto Nyankopɔn a ɔma yɛ nea yɛpɛ nyinaa ma ɔdɔɔso he so.
Ɔsɛ sɛ bɛyɔ papa, na bennya bɛ ho nnwuma pa fam; bɛ nsɛm ngo na bɛnkyɛ adeɛ fɛ so, na saa yɔ mu ne bɛhyehyɛ fapem pa ama bɛ ho daakye, na bɛanya nkwa a ɔyɛ nkwa mapa.
Awieeɛ ne nhyira Timoteo, bɔ nea bɛde ahyɛ wo nsa he ho bane.
Kwati nsɛmhuhuo ɔne nea bɛfrɛ no nimdeɛ nso ɔnte saa; binom akeka yei amane afiri gyidie botae he ho.
Adom nka wo!
NNIANIMU Krataa a ɔtɔ so mmienu a Paulo twerɛ kɔmaa Timoteo he yɛ afotuo a ɔde maa n’abɔfra Timoteo a ɔsane yɛ ne boafoɔ he.
Asɛm titire a ɔya mu ne boasetɔ.
Otu Timoteo fo sane hyɛ no dene sɛdeɛ ɔbɛkɔ so adi Yesu Kristo ho adanseɛ nɔkorɛ mu, na wakura nɔkorɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɔfa Asɛmpa he ne Apam Dada he ho mu.
Ɔka sɛ, Timoteo nyɔ n’asɛdeɛ sɛ kyerɛkyerɛni ne sɛmpakani ya taa ne amanehunu mu.
Ade titire a ɔbɔɔ Timoteo kɔkɔ ho ne “nkwasea akyinnye ne bibi a onnim ho akyinnye” a ɔmfa bibi pa biaa mma, na mmom ɔsɛe bɛ a betie no he.
Ne nyinaa mu ne twerɛfoɔ he kae Timoteo he ankasa n’abrabɔ ne ne botaeɛ nhwɛsoɔ—ne gyidie, n’aboterɛ, ne dɔ, ne boasetɔ, n’amanehunu ya taa mu.
MU NSƐM Nsɛm a odi kane :- Ayeyie ne afotusɛm :—: Afotuo ne kɔkɔbɔ :—: Paulo tebea a Paulo ya mu :- Awieeɛ :-
Nkyea Me, Paulo a ɔnam Nyankopɔn pɛ so yɛ Kristo Yesu somafoɔ, sɛdeɛ nkwa a ɔya Kristo Yesu mu bɔhyɛ he teɛ he, twerɛ krataa yi de kɔma Timoteo, me dɔba: Adom, mmɔborɔhunu ne asomdwie a ofiri Agya Nyankopɔn ne yɛ Awurade Kristo Yesu nkyɛne nka wo.
Meda Nyankopɔn a mede ahonim pa som no sɛdeɛ me nananom someeɛ he ase, berɛ a mekae wo me mpaebɔ mu, anadwo ne awia.
Mekae nisuo a woteeɛ berɛ a na yeedi mpaepaemu he a, m’ani gyina awia ne anadwo sɛ mehu wo, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a anigyeɛ bɛhyɛ me ma.
Mekae wo nɔkorɛ gyidie he, gyidie a wo nana Lois nyaeɛ, na wo maame Eunike nso nyaa bi a megye di sɛ agye nhini ya wo nso wo mu he.
Afotuo ahodoɔ Yei nti, meekae wo sɛ kanyane Nyankopɔn akyɛdeɛ a ɔnam me nsa a mede guu wo so ba wo mu he; efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn amma yɛ hu honhom, na mmom ahoɔdene ne dɔ ne adwenemteɛ honhom ne ɔde mmaa yɛ.
Nti mma w’ani nwu yɛ Awurade ho adansedie ne me, a meyɛ deduani he ho, na mmom hu asɛmpa he ho amaneɛ bi sɛdeɛ Nyankopɔn tumi teɛ he, nea ɔgyee yɛ na ɔde frɛ kronkron frɛɛ yɛ, ɔnyɛ yɛ nnwuma nti, na mmom ɔnam ɔnoaa ne tirimpɔ ne n’adom a ɔde mmaeɛ Kristo Yesu mu firi mmeresantene.
Na afei ɔnam yɛ Agyenkwa Yesu Kristo ahoyie he so ada no adi.
Ɔno ne wasɛe wuo tumi, na ɔnam asɛmpa he so ayi nkwa ne adeɛ a ɔmporɔ adi pefee.
Saa asɛmpa yi nti ne bɛayi me sɛ sɛnkafoɔ ne somafoɔ ne kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, ɔno nti ne mehu saa amaneɛ yi nso.
Nso m’ani nwu ho, efiri sɛ menim nea maagye no adi, na menim sɛ obetumi akora nea mede ahyɛ ne nsa akosi Da he.
Sɔ asɛmpa a wotee no me nkyɛne, gyidie ne dɔ a ɔya Yesu Kristo mu, he mu yie.
Adepa a ɔde ahyɛ wo nsa he, fa Honhom Kronkron a ɔte yɛ mu he sɔ mu yie.
Figelo, Hermogene, Onesiforo Wonim sɛ bɛ a bɛya Asia nyinaa adane afiri me nkyɛne, bɛ mu bi ne Figelo ne Hermogene.
Awurade nhu Onesiforo fie mmɔbɔ, efiri sɛ na ɔtaa ma me ho tɔ me, na n’ani nwu me nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn ho; ɔbaa Roma he, ɔbɔɔ mmɔdene hwehwɛɛ me, na ohuu me.
Awurade Yesu Kristo mma honya Nyankopɔn hɔ mmɔborɔhunu Da he!
Na som a ɔsom Efeso he woaa wonim.
Yesu Kristo sraani nɔkwafoɔ Afei wo, me ba, ɔnam adom a bɛde adom wo Yesu Kristo mu nti, yɛ nam.
Na deɛ wote firii m’anum adansefoɔ bebree anim he, ɔnoaa ne fa hyɛ nnipa anokwafoɔ a bebetumi akyerɛkyerɛ binom nso nsa.
Wo nso mia w’ani hu amane sɛ Yesu Kristo sraani pa. Sraani biaa nni hɔ a ɔkɔ sa de asetena mu nsɛm bebare ne ho, sraani he botaeɛ ne sɛ ɔbɛsɔ ne panyini ani.
Na sɛ bi di akansie mu kane a, bɛmfa nkunim abotire mmɔ no gye sɛ osii akane he sɛnea ho mmara he teɛ.
Ɔsɛ sɛ kuani a wɔayɔ adwuma dene he ne di kane di nnɔbae he bi.
Dwene nea meka yi ho, na Awurade bɛma wo nnoɔma nyinaa ho nteaseɛ.
Kae Yesu Kristo a ɔsɔre firii awufoɔ mu a ɔyɛ Dawid aseni he, sɛdeɛ m’asɛmpa a meka he teɛ; ɔno nti mu ne meehu amane, na meda mpokyerem sɛ debɔnyɛni.
Nso Nyankopɔn asɛm deɛ bɛnkyekyeree no.
Yei nti meto me bo nnoɔma nyinaa mu, sɛnea ɔbɛyɔ a bɛ a bɛayi bɛ he nso bebenya Kristo Yesu mu nkwagyeɛ, daa animuonyam mu.
Asɛnnua ne abotire Nɔkwasɛm di: sɛ yɛne no awu a, yɛne no bɛsɔre nso; sɛ yegyina pintinn a, yɛ ne no bedi hene nso; sɛ yɛpo no a ɔno nso bɛpo yɛ; sɛ yɛnyɛ nɔkwafoɔ a, ɔno deɛ ɔyɛ nɔkwafoɔ efiri sɛ ontumi mpa ne ho akyi.
Dwumayɔni a ɔsɔ Nyankopɔn ani Kɔ so kae bɛ saa nsɛm yi, na di bɛ adanseɛ Nyankopɔn anim, na bɛannye nsɛm ho akyinnye hunu a mfasoɔ nni so a ɔsɛe atiefoɔ adwene.
Bɔ mmɔdene sɛ wobɛ sɔ Nyankopɔn ani na obehu wo sɛ dwumayɔni a n’ani nwu bibiaa ho, na ɔkyerɛ nɔkwasɛm mu pɛpɛɛpɛ.
Yi wo ho firi nsɛmhuhuo a ho nte ho, efiri sɛ, ɔbɛma nipa akɔ n’anim amumuyɔ mu, na bɛ asɛm bɛterɛ sɛ yare bɔne.
Bemu bi ne Himeneo ne Fileto, a bɛamane afiri nɔkorɛ he ho ka sɛ wusɔreɛ he aba dada, na bɛnam so ɔɔdane binom gyidie abutu, sɛ yei nyina mu he Nyankopɔn fapem da soaa gyina hɔ pintinn a ho ntwerɛeɛ ne sɛ: “Awurade nim ne deɛ,” ɔne, “ma nea ɔbɔ Awurade dini biaa ntwe ne ho mfiri amumuyɔ ho.” Na fikɛseɛ biaa mu he ɔnyɛ sika ne dwetɛ nnoɔma nkoaa ne ya hɔ, na mmom nnua ne nnɛteɛ deɛ nso ya hɔ bi, na bebu bi, bi nso bemmu no.
Na sɛ bi te ne ho firi yeinom ho a, ɔbɛyɛ nea bebu, na bɛate ho a, owura he de yɛ bibi a, ɔbɛyɛ yie, na bɛasiesie de ayɔ adwuma pa biaa.
Nti dwane firi mmabunu berɛ mu akɔnnɔ ho na hwehwɛ tenenee, gyidie, dɔ ne asomdwie, wo ne bɛ a befiri akoma a mu te mu frɛ Awurade he.
Na nkwasea-akyinnye a bɛmfa nsua hwee deɛ, nkɔ ho koraa, efiri sɛ, sɛnea wonim he, ɔde ntɔkwa ba.
Na ɔnsɛ Awurade akoa bi sɛ ɔyɛ ntɔkwapɛfoɔ, na mmom, ɔsɛ sɛ ɔdwo ma nnipa nyinaa, ohu nkyerɛkyerɛ, ɔhyɛ ne ho so bɔne ho, na ɔde dwoɔ tenetene bɛ a bɛ ne no nyɛ adwene asɛm mu, sɛ ebia Nyankopɔn bɛma bɛ adwensakra ahu nɔkorɛ he, na ama bɛanni aba bɛ ho so ya bronsam fidie a ɔde akye bɛ sɛ bɛnyɛ n’apɛdeɛ he mu.
Amanehunu berɛ Nso hu yei sɛ, nna a odi akyire he, mmerɛ a mu ɔdene bɛba; efiri sɛ nnipa bɛyɛ ahopɛfoɔ, sikapɛfoɔ, ahohoahoafoɔ, ahantanfoɔ, abususɛnkafoɔ, awofoɔ ho asoɔdenfoɔ, boniayɛfoɔ, bɛ a benni nyamesuro, nnipa a benni tema, apamsɛefoɔ, nsekubɔfoɔ, nnipa a bɛnhyɛ bɛ akɔnnɔ so, nnipa a bɛyɛ werɛmfoɔ, nnipa a bɛmpɛ papa, afatwafoɔ, akakabenfoɔ, nnipa a bɛyɛ ahomasoɔ kɛseɛ, nnipa a bɛdɔ anigyedeɛ sene Nyankopɔn; bɛde nyamesompa adura bɛ anim nso bɛamfa tumi a ɔyam he nni dwuma.
Twe wo ho mfiri saa nnipa yi ho.
Na yeinom mu bi ne bɛ a bɛkɔ afie mu na bɛfa mmaa adwenemharefoɔ na bɔne ahyɛ bɛ ma, na akɔnnɔ ahodoɔ afa bɛ nommum, bɛ a betie nkyerɛkyerɛ daa nso benhu nɔkorɛ he da.
Sɛnea Yane ne Yambrɛ ko tiaa Mose he, saa ara ne yeinom nso ne nɔkorɛ he di asie.
Bɛyɛ nnipa a bɛ adwene aporɔ na bɛ gyidie nyɛ papa.
Nso bennya nkɔsoɔ, efiri sɛ sɛnea bɛyɔeɛ he, bɛ gyimii bɛda adi nnipa nyinaa anim, sɛnea nnipa mmienu he deɛ daa adi he.
Paulo amanehunu Afei wo ankasa woahu me nkyerɛkyerɛ, me bra, me botaeɛ, me gyidie, me boasetɔ, me dɔ, m’abodwokyɛre, taa a bɛtaa me, ne amanehunu a mefaa mu Antiokia, Ikonium ne Listra.
Saa taa yi ne megyinaa mu!
Nso Awurade gyee me firi ne nyinaa mu.
Ampa, bɛ a bɛpɛ sɛ bɛde nyamesom pa tena Kristo Yesu mu nyinaa, bɛbɛtaa bɛ.
Na nnipa bɔne sisifoɔ deɛ bɛkɔ bɛ anim bɔne mu, bɛbɛdaadaa binom na binom adaadaa bɛ nso.
Na wo deɛ kɔ so tena nea woasua na woagye adi he mu, na hu sɛ wosua firii yɛ nkyɛne ne sɛnea wofiri wo mmɔfrase nim atwerɛ kronkron he a, obetumi ama woahu nyansa afa Kristo Yesu mu akɔ nkwagyeɛ mu.
Atwerɛ nyinaa firi Nyankopɔn homee mu na ɔyɛ ma nkyerɛkyerɛ, atenyie, atenetene ne tenenee mu nteteɛ, na Nyankopɔn nipa nam so ayɛ pɛ a bɛasiesie no koraa ama nnwuma pa nyinaa.
Adesrɛ bi Afei mehyɛ wo Nyankopɔn ne Kristo Yesu a obebu ateasefoɔ ne awufoɔ atɛne n’ahoyie ne n’ahennie mu he anim sɛ: pae mu ka asɛmpa he, gyina mu berɛ pa ne berɛ bɔne mu; yi atene, ka anim, tu fo, abodwokyɛre ne nkyerɛkyerɛ nyinaa mu.
Na berɛ bi bɛba a nnipa ontie nkyerɛkyerɛ pa a ɔyɛ he, nso esiane sɛ bɛasom yɛ bɛ hene nti, bɛbɛboaboa akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ ano sɛnea bɛ a bɛ akɔnnɔ teɛ, na bebeyi bɛ aso afiri nɔkorɛ ho, na bɛatie anansesɛm.
Na wo deɛ ma w’ani nna hɔ berɛ biaa, mia w’ani hu amane, yɔ sɛmpakafoɔ adwuma, yɛ wo som adwuma nyinaa.
Na me deɛ, berɛ he anya aduru sɛ behwie me agu sɛ hwiesa, na me ntetemudie berɛ aso.
Maakõ kõ pa he, maawie mmirika he tu, maakura gyidie he mu.
Afei nea aka a ɔsɛ sɛ me nsa ka ne tenenee abotire a Awurade, temufoɔ a ɔtene he de bɛma me Da he, ɔnyɛ me nko na mmom bɛ a bɛdɔ n’ahoyie nyinaa nso.
Paulo ani gyina Timoteo Bɔ mmɔdene bra me nkyɛne ntɛm.
Na Dema deɛ, ɔdɔ nnɛ wiase nti, waagya me hɔ kɔ Tesalonika; Kreske kɔ Galatia, Tito nso kɔ Dalmatia.
Luka nkoaa ne ya me nkyɛne.
Fa Marko ka wo ho bra, efiri sɛ ne ho hia me som adwuma mu paa.
Tihiko deɛ, masoma no Efeso.
Sɛ wooba a, fa m’ataadeɛ duruduru a megyaa no Karpo nkyɛne ya Troa ne me nwoma he bra me, ne titire he kokwanwoma he.
Tomfoɔ Aleksandro Aleksandro, kɔɔbere dwumfoɔ he, yɛɛ me bɔne bebree.
Awurade betua no ka sɛnea ne nwuma teɛ.
Wo nso, hwɛ yie ne ho, efiri sɛ osii yɛ asɛm he ho kwane bebree.
Gyeɛ a bɛgye Paulo Me nyiano nea odi kane he mu he, biaa annyina m’akyi, biaa põõ me.
Mempɛ sɛ bɛde ho asodie bɛto bɛ so.
Nso Awurade gyinaa m’akyi na ɔmaa me ahoɔdene, de kaa asɛmpa he nyinaa sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a amanamane mufoɔ nyinaa bɛte.
Nti oyii me firii gyata anum.
Ampa, Awurade beyi me afiri bɔne nyinaa mu, na wagye me akɔ ne soro ahennie mu.
Ɔno ne animuonyam nka no daadaa.
Amen.
Gye a bɛgyee Paulo Mekyea Priska ne Akwila ne Onesiforo fiefoɔ.
Erasto deɛ, ɔkaa Korinto, ne megyaa Trofimo ya Mileto a na ɔyare.
Bɔ mmɔdene bra ansa na awɔ berɛ aba.
Eubulo ne Pude ne Lino ne Klaudia ne anuanom nyinaa kyeakyea wo.
Awurade ne wo honhom ntena.
Adom nka wo!
NNIANIMU Tito yɛ bi a na ɔnyɛ Yudani na ɔbɛyɛɛ Kristoni.
Ɔbɛyɛɛ Paulo yɔnko dwumayɔni ne boafoɔ ya n’asɛnka akwantuo dwumadie mu.
Paulo twerɛɛ krataa yi de kɔmaa Tito a na ɔyɛ ne boafoɔ.
Na Tito yɛ aberanteɛ a na ɔya Kreta.
Ɔno ne deɛ Paulo gyaa no akyire sɛ ɔnhwɛ asafo a ɔya hɔ he so.
Nnoɔma ahodoɔ mmeɛnsa a ohia ne ɔkaa ho asɛm ya krataa yi mu.
Deɛ odi kane he, ɔkae Tito su korɔ a ɔsɛ sɛ asafo mu akannifoɔ he yi no adi, esiane abrabɔ bɔne a na Kretafoɔ bebree ɔɔbɔ he nti.
Deɛ odi hɔ yɛ afotuo a ɔde maa Tito sɛdeɛ obesi akyerɛkyerɛ nnipakuo ahodoɔ ya asafo he mu: Mmeema mpanyimfoɔ, mmaa mpanyimfoɔ (a bɛ nso ɔsɛ sɛ bɛkyerɛkyerɛ mmaa nkumaa he), mmeranteɛ ne nkoa.
Deɛ otwa toɔ he, otuu Tito fo fa Kristoni abrabɔ ho, sɛ ɔbɛfa asomdwie ne ayɔnkofa, na wakwati tane, akyinnye ne mpaepaemu asafo he mu.
MU NSƐM Nsɛm a odi kane :- Asafo he mu mpanyimfoɔ :- Nnipakuo ahodoɔ a bɛya asafo he mu asɛdeɛ :- Afotuo ne kɔkɔbɔ :- Awieeɛ :-
Nkyea Me, Paulo, Nyankopɔn akoa ne Yesu Kristo somafoɔ ma bɛ a Nyankopɔn ayi bɛ gyidie ne nyamesom pa ho nɔkorɛ he nimdeɛ mu, daa nkwa ho anidasoɔ a Nyankopɔn a onni torɔ, hyɛɛ ho bɔ too hɔ ansa na adebɔ ɔɔbɛhyɛ aseɛ— na berɛ a ɔsɛ mu he, oyii n’asɛm adi, asɛnka a bɛnam yɛ Agyenkwa Nyankopɔn hyɛ so de ahyɛ me nsa he mu; twerɛ krataa yi de kɔma Tito a ɔyɛ me ba kann gyidie korɔ heaa mu: Adom ne asomdwie a ofiri Agya Nyankopɔn ne Kristo Yesu a ɔyɛ yɛ Agyenkwa nka wo!
Tito ya Kreta Yei nti ne megyaa wo Kreta, sɛ wobɛtoto nnoɔma a ohia sɛ bɛyɔ nyinaa yie, na woayi kuro biaa mu asafo mpayimfoɔ sɛdeɛ me kyerɛɛ wo sɛ: Yi nipa a ne ho nni asɛm biaa, na ɔyɛ yerɛ baako kunu, na ne mma yɛ agyidifoɔ a bɛmmɔ akohwibra, na bɛnnyɛ asoɔdene nso.
Na ɔsɛ sɛ asafo mu hwɛfoɔ yɛ bi a biaa onnya ne ho asɛm nka sɛ Nyankopɔn fie so hwɛsofoɔ.
Ɔnsɛ sɛ ɔyɛ ahomasoɔ, bi a ne bo fu ntɛm, bi a ɔyɛ nsadweam, bi a ɔyɛ pupopupo anaa bi a ɔde adufudeɛ pɛ mfasoɔ; na mmom ɔsɛ sɛ asafo hwɛfoɔ yɛ bi a ɔpɛ ahɔhoyɛ, ɔpɛ papayɔ, n’adwene mu da hɔ, ɔtene, ne ho te, na ɔwɔ ahohyɛsoɔ.
Ɔsɛ sɛ okura asɛm a ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ a ne nyinasoɔ ne nkyerɛkyerɛ pa he mu yie, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a obetumi de nkyerɛkyerɛ a odi mu atu fo na ɔde ayi bɛ a bɛkasa tia nɔkorɛ he atɛne nso.
Kreta asafo mu agyegyefoɔ Nnipa bebree nso ya hɔ a bɛte atua, bɛyɛ kasahunufoɔ na bɛyɛ nnaadaafoɔ, ne titire ne bɛ a befiri twetiatwafoɔ mu he; esiane sɛ bɛkyerɛkyerɛ nea onni ho kwane sɛ bɛkyerɛkyerɛ, de ɔɔpɛ mfasoɔ hunu de ɔɔdane anuanom adwene ani afiri nɔkorɛ he ho nti, ɔsɛ sɛ wosi bɛ kwane na bɛankyerɛkyerɛ.
Ɔyɛ bɛaa bɛ nipa baako a ofiri bɛ mu, bɛ ankasa bɛ diyifoɔ, ne kaa sɛ, “Kretafoɔ yɛ atorɔfoɔ daa, nkekaboa bɔne, akwadwofoɔ adidifoɔ.” Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ atorofoɔ Saa adansedie yi yɛ nɔkorɛ.
Ne saa nti yi bɛ atɛne dendene, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bebekura nɔkorɛ gyidie he mu, na bɛantie Yudafoɔ anansesɛm anaa bɛ a bɛpo nɔkorɛ he ahyɛdeɛ.
Nipa ɔtene he nnoɔma nyinaa ho te ma no, nso deɛ ɔntene na ɔnnye nni he deɛ, bibiaa ho nte mma no na mmom n’adwene ne n’ahonim nyinaa ho agu fi.
Nnipa a bɛte saa he ka sɛ benim Nyankopɔn, nso bɛde bɛ nneyɔeɛ po no.
Bɛyɛ Nyankopɔn akyiwadeɛ, asoɔdenfoɔ, bɛnyɛ ma adwuma pa biaa.
Nso wo Tito deɛ, ɔsɛ sɛ wokyerɛkyerɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ a odi mu.
Kasa kyerɛ nkokora sɛ bɛnnyɔ bibi mma ɔntraso, bɛma bɛ anim nyɛ duru, na bɛmfa nyansa, dɔ ne boasetɔ nyɛ dene gyidie he mu.
Saa ara nso ne mmerewafoɔ he nso, kasa kyerɛ bɛ sɛ bɛma buo nna adi bɛ abrabɔ mu, bennni nsekuro na bɛmma nsa nso mfa bɛ nommum; ɔsɛ sɛ bɛkyerɛkyerɛ nea ɔyɛ, na bɛatete mmabaa ama bɛadɔ bɛ kununom ne bɛ mma, na bɛadwene adwene pa, ahyɛ bɛ ho so, ayɔ bɛ fie nnwuma yie; benya ayamyɛ, ahoteɛ mu, na bɛmmrɛbrɛ bɛ ho ase mma bɛ kununom, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a nnipa onya asɛmmɔne bi nka mfa Nyankopɔn asɛm he ho.
Saa ara ne tu mmeranteɛ nso fo sɛ, bɛnhyɛ bɛ ho so.
Na bibiaa mu he, yi wo ho adi sɛ nnwuma pa nhwɛsoɔ, nkyerɛkyerɛ mu yi pɛyɛ, animuduro, asɛmpa a ɔyɛ a bennya ho asɛm bi nka adi, na deɛ ɔne yɛ anya he afɛre, efiri sɛ onni yɛ ho bɔne biaa ka.
Kasakyerɛ nkoa sɛ bɛmmrɛbrɛ bɛ ho ase ma bɛ wuranom na bɛasɔ bɛ wuranom ani adeɛ nyinaa mu; bennyiyi bɛ wuranom nsɛm ano, bennwia adeɛ mfiri bɛ wuranom fotoɔ mu, na mmom benni nɔkorɛ turodoo ade nyinaa mu, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bebeyi Nyankopɔn a ɔyɛ yɛ Agyenkwa he nkyerɛkyerɛ ayɛ.
Na Nyankopɔn adom a ɔde nkwagyeɛ ma nnipa nyinaa he ada adi, na ɔkyerɛkyerɛ yɛ sɛ yɛmpo fi nnoɔma nyinaa ne wiase akɔnnɔ, na yɛmfa adwenemteɛ, ahoteɛ ne nyamesom pa mmɔ yɛ bra saa mmerɛ yi mu, mmerɛ a yɛɛtwɛne yɛ Nyankopɔn kɛseɛ ne yɛ Agyenkwa Yesu Kristo ahotɔ anidasoɔ ne n’animuonyam ahoyie.
Ɔno ne de ne ho maeɛ ɔnam yɛ nti sɛ ɔbɛgye yɛ afiri amumuyɔ nyinaa mu na wate yɛ ho afa yɛ ayɛ ɔno ankasa ne nkurofoɔ a bɛbɔ mmɔdene nwuma pa mu.
Pae mu ka saa nsɛm yi; kɔ so tu fo na ka anim sɛdeɛ bɛama wo tumi sɛ yɔ he.
Mma biaa mmmu wo animtia.
Akristofoɔ abrabɔ Kae Kreta asafo he sɛ bɛmmerɛ bɛ ho ase nhyɛ bɛ a bedi bɛ so ne tumidie ahodoɔ ase, bɛnyɛ setie, nsiesie bɛ ho ma nnwuma pa nyinaa, bɛnnka biaa ho asɛmmɔne, bɛnnyɛ ntɔkwapɛfoɔ, ɔsɛ sɛ bɛ dwo na bɛde anidie ma nnipa biaa, efiri sɛ, berɛ bi a atwam a na yɛ nso yennim nyansa, na yɛyɛ asoɔdenfoɔ, na yɛamane afiri kwane pa he so, na yɛyɛ nkoa ma akɔnnɔ ahodoɔ ne anigyedeɛ he, yɛde nitane ne ahoɔyeya ne bɔɔ yɛ bra, a na yɛ ho yɛ ahi, tentanee yɛ ho yɛ ho.
Nso berɛ a yɛ Agyenkwa Nyankopɔn nnepa ne n’ayamyɛ daa adi he, ɔgyee yɛ, ɔnyɛ tenenee nnwuma bi a yɛayɔ nti, na mmom ɔnam ne mmɔborɔhunu so faa nsuo adwareɛ a ɔnam awofoforɔ ne foforɔyɛ a ofiri Honhom Kronkron so ne gyee yɛ.
Saa Honhom yi ne ɔnam yɛ Agyenkwa Yesu Kristo so ahwie agu yɛ so pii, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a, yɛnam n’adom so benya bembuo na yɛabɛyɛ adedifoɔ daa nkwa anidasoɔ he mu.
Ɔyɛ nɔkwasɛm paa.
Na yeinom ne mehwɛ sɛ wohyɛ mu kena, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bɛ a bɛabɛgye Nyankopɔn adi he bɛhwɛ yei sɛ bɛde bɛ ho bɛma nnwuma pa; yeinom ne yɛ paa na ɔyɛ mfasodeɛ ma nnipa.
Twe wo ho firi akyinnye hunu, ananasɛm, akasakasaa ne ntɔkwa a ɔfa mmara he ho, efiri sɛ, mfasoɔ nni so na ɔyɛ nnoɔma hunu.
Nipa a ɔde mpaepaemu ba a woakasa akyerɛ no baako ne ne mprenu so, na wantie he, wo ne no nya twaka biaa, efiri sɛ, wonim sɛ, saa nipa he yɛ debɔnyɛni a wayera kwane, na waabu ne ho fɔ.
Asɛm a otwa toɔ ne nhyira Sɛ mesoma Artema anaa Tihiko ba wo nkyɛne a, bɔ mmɔdene sɛ wobɛba me hɔ Nikopoli, efiri sɛ hɔ ne maabɔ me tim pɔ sɛ medi awɔ mmerɛ he.
Bɔ mmɔdene sɛ wobegya mmaranimfoɔ Sena ɔne Apolo kwane a bibiaa onhia bɛ.
Na ma yɛ nkurofoɔ nsua sɛ bebetu bɛ ho asi hɔ ama nnwuma pa na bɛde aboa nnoɔma a ohia paa, na bɛanyɛ nnipa a mfasoɔ nni bɛ so.
Bɛ a bɛka me ho nyinaa kyea wo.
Kyea bɛ a bɛdɔ yɛ gyidie he mu nyinaa.
Adom nka ho nyinaa!
NNIANIMU Filemon yɛ Kristoni a na ɔwɔ dini paa.
Ɔno ne na ɔyɛ akoa bi a na bɛfrɛ no Onesimo wura, na ɔbɛyɛ sɛ na ɔyɛ Kolose asafo he mu nipa.
Ɔbaa sɛ na akoa yi adwane afiri ne wura nkyɛne, na kwane bi so he, ɔne Paulo a saa berɛ he na ɔda afiase he kɔhyiaeɛ.
Ɔnam Paulo so maa Onesimo bɛyɛɛ Kristoni.
Krataa a Paulo twerɛ kɔmaa Filemon he yɛ adesrɛ a ɔde pɛɛ n’akoa a ɔɔsoma no ne nkyɛne saa berɛ he nkabom.
Ɔhwehwɛɛ sɛ, Filemon nnye no ntom sɛ akoa a bɛde ne bɔne akyɛ no ama nkabom ne asomdwie aba ɔne ne wura ntam nkoaa, na mmom sɛ nua Kristoni mapa nso.
MU NSƐM Nsɛm a odi kane - Filemon ayeyie - Paulo srɛ ma Onesimo - Awieeɛ -
Nkyea Paulo, Kristo Yesu deduani, ne yɛ nua Timoteo, twerɛ krataa yi de kɔma yɛ dɔfoɔ ne yɛ yɔnko dwumayɔni Filemon, ne yɛ nuabaa Afia, ne Arkipus a ɔyɛ yɛ yɔnko sraani, ne asafo a ohyia wo fie he: Adom ne asomdwie a ofiri yɛ Agya Nyankopɔn ne Awurade Yesu Kristo nka ho.
Filemon dɔ ne ne gyidie Berɛ biaa a mɛkae wo me mpaebɔ mu he, meda me Nyankopɔn ase daa, efiri sɛ, mete wo dɔ a wode dɔ ahoteefoɔ he nyinaa ne wo gyidie a wo wɔ no Awurade Yesu mu he.
Na mebɔ mpaeɛ sɛ wo gyidie mu ayɔnkofa he bɛma nnoɔma pa a ɔsɛ sɛ yɛyɔ no Kristo mu nyinaa ho nimdeɛ a mu dɔ ada adi.
Nɔkwasɛm di, me nua, ɔnam wo dɔ so ama manya anigye ne awerɛkyekyerɛ, efiri sɛ, woama ahoteefoɔ he, bɛ akoma atɔ bɛ yam.
Paulo di maa Onesimo Yei nti, owom sɛ mewɔ akokoɔduro Kristo mu sɛ metumi ahyɛ wo ama woayɔ nea ɔsɛ sɛ woyɔ deɛ, nso dɔ nti, me Paulo ankasa a meyɛ asafopanyini, na seeseiaa mesane yɛ Kristo Yesu deduani he, srɛ wo— ama m’abɔfra Onesimo a mabɛyɛ n’agya m’afiase mpokyerɛ yi mu.
(Mmerɛ bi a atwam he na ne so nni mfasoɔ ma wo, nso seesei deɛ, nɔkorɛ di, ne so aba mfasoɔ ama wo ɔne me).
Meesoma no ama no asane aba wo nkyɛne bio, ɔyɛ nipa a ɔda m’akoma so paa.
Na nka mepɛ sɛ ɔtena me nkyɛne, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a nka obesi w’anane mu asom me saa berɛ yi a ɔnam asɛmpa he nti, meya mpokyerɛ mu.
Nso mempɛ sɛ mefiri wo akyi yɔ bibiaa na anyɛ sɛ wo papayɔ he firi hyɛ mu, na mmom afiri woankasa wo pɛ mu.
Ebia yei nti ne ɔtwee ne ho firii wo nkyɛne mmerɛ kakra yi, na ɔnam so ama wanya no bio afebɔɔ.
Wonya no sɛ akoa bio na mmom deɛ ɔsene saa; sɛ ɔmmɛyɛ nua dɔfo, titire ya me fam, nso ɔbɛyɔ ne ɔboro so saa ama wo honam fam, na afei Awurade mu nso.
Nti sɛ wobu me sɛ wo yɔnko dwumayɔni deɛ a, gye no fɛ so sɛdeɛ nka wobɛgye me he.
Sɛ waafom wo kwane bi so a, anaa sɛ ɔde wo ka bi a, bu gu me so, na me ankasa metua.
Meaa Paulo ne mede me nsa ɔɔtwerɛ saa krataa yi sɛ metua ka biaa.
Onhia mpo sɛ mɛkae wo sɛ wode me ka, mpo wo nipadua ho ka.
Oo me nua, ampa, ma menya mfasoɔ mfiri wo hɔ Awurade mu!
Ma m’akoma ntɔ me yam Kristo mu.
Meetwerɛ saa krataa yi abra wo yi, mewɔ ahotɔsoɔ sɛ wobetie, na menim sɛ wobɛyɔ akyɛne nea meesrɛ wo yi mpo.
Na yei akyi he siesie ahɔhodane ma me, efiri sɛ mewɔ anidasoɔ sɛ ho mpaebɔ nti ho nsa bɛka me bio.
Nkradie ne nhyira Me yɔnko deduani Kristo mu, Epafra, ɔne Marko, Aristarkus, Demas ne Luka a bɛyɛ me yɔnko adwumayɔfoɔ kyea wo.
Awurade Yesu Kristo adom nka ho honhom ho.
NNIANIMU Krataa a bɛde kɔmaa Hebrifoɔ he yɛ deɛ bɛtwerɛ kɔmaa Kristofoɔ nnipakuo bi a na begu so ɔɔtaa bɛ.
Deɛ na ohu ne sɛ, na bɛɛyɛ apa aba ya kristosom gyidie mu.
Twerɛfoɔ he hyɛ bɛ nkurane, deɛ odi kane, ya bɛ gyidie a ɔkyerɛ sɛ Yesu Kristo ne Nyankopɔn adiyie kann a otwa toɔ.
Ɔɔyɔ yei he, osii nɔkwasɛm ahodoɔ mmeɛnsa so dua: Deɛ odi kane, Yesu yɛ Nyankopɔn Ba he a ɔnam amanehunu mu sua sɛ ɔbɛyɛ setie ama Agya he nɔkorɛ mu.
Ɔnam sɛ ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn Ba he nti, ɔyɛ kɛseɛ sene Apam Dada mu adiyifoɔ, abɔfoɔ, ne Mose nso.
Deɛ ɔtɔ so mmienu ne sɛ, Nyankopɔn ayi Yesu akyerɛ sɛ ɔnyɛ daa sɔfo a ɔkyɛne Apam Dada mu asɔfoɔ he mu biaa.
Deɛ ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa ne sɛ, gyidini nam Yesu so nya gyeɛ firi bɔne, hu ne wuo mu.
Ɔnam sɛ Yesu yɛ Sɔfo Panyini nti, otumi ma nkwagyeɛ trodoo a ne mfonyini ya Hebrifoɔ som amaneɛ ne mmoa afɔrebɔ mu.
Ɔnam mfatoho a ɔyɔ faa nnipa bi a bɛgyee dini ya Israel abakɔsɛm mu srɛ n’akenkanfoɔ sɛdeɛ bɛbɛkɔ soaa atena ase nɔkorɛdie mu.
Ti mu he, ɔsrɛ bɛ sɛ bɛnkɔ so ntena ase nɔkorɛdie mu nkosi awieeɛ na bɛnhwɛ Yesu.
Afei nso, bemmia bɛ ani nhu amane ya taa biaa a ɔbɛba bɛ so he mu.
Deɛ ɔde wie nwoma yi yɛ afotusɛm bi ne kɔkɔbɔ.
MU NSƐM Nsɛm a odi kane: Kristo yɛ Nyankopɔn adiyie a otwa toɔ :- Kristo korɔn kyɛne abɔfoɔ :—: Kristo korɔn kyɛne Mose ne Yosua :—: Kristo kɛseyɛ ya ne sɔfodie mu :—: Kristo kɛseyɛ ya n’apam mu :—: Kristo kɛseyɛ ya n’afɔrebɔ mu :—: Gyidie ne adeɛ ohia titire :—: Sɛ yɛɛsɔ Nyankopɔn ani :- Mpaebɔ a otwa toɔ :- Nsɛm a otwa toɔ :-
Nyankopɔn nam ne Ba he so akasa Tete mmerɛ mu he, Nyankopɔn nam mmerɛ ahodoɔ ne akwane ahodoɔ so faa adiyifoɔ he so kasa kyerɛɛ yɛ nananom, na nna a odi akyire yi mu deɛ, ɔnam ne Ba a waayi no asi hɔ sɛ nnoɔma nyinaa so diadeɛ, na ɔnam ne so bɔɔ nnoɔma nyinaa he so, akasa akyerɛ yɛ.
Ɔno ankasa ne da Nyankopɔn animuonyam a ɔhyerɛn he adi na ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn su nsɛso pɛpɛɛpɛ, na ɔnam n’asɛm a tumi yam so kita nnoɔma nyinaa mu.
Na odwiraa yɛ bɔne wieeɛ he, ɔkɔtenaa deɛ ɔwɔ tumi boro tumi nyinaa so, na ɔya soro soro he nifa.
Ɔno ne korɔn kyɛne abɔfoɔ he, sɛdeɛ ne dini kunyini a wanya he kyɛne bɛ deɛ koraa he.
Ba he di mu kyɛne abɔfoɔ Na abɔfoɔ he mu hwane ne Nyankopɔn ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wone me Ba; nnɛ ne mayi wo sononko’”?
Anaa bio, “Mɛyɛ n’Agya, na wayɛ me ba”?
Afei nso, berɛ a na ɔno ankasa de ne Ba a ɔkyɛne so he ɔɔba wiase he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Ma Nyankopɔn abɔfoɔ nyinaa nsɔre no.” Na abɔfoɔ he deɛ, nea ɔka faa bɛ ho ne sɛ, “Ɔyɔ n’abɔfoɔ sɛ mframa, na n’asomfoɔ he nso sɛ gyaframa.” Na Ba he deɛ, nea ɔka faa ne ho ne sɛ, “O Nyankopɔn, w’ahennie tim hɔ daa, na w’ahennie poma yɛ tenenee poma.
Wodɔ tenenee na wotane amumuyɔ; nti Nyankopɔn, wo Nyankopɔn, asra wo ngo ahosane ngo a ɔboro wo mfɛfoɔ deɛ so.” Na afei nso, “Mfitiaseɛ he, Awurade, wotoo asaase fapem, na soro yɛ wo nsa ano adwuma; Yeinom bɛyera, nso wo deɛ wotim hɔ daa; ne nyinaa bɛpa sɛ ataadeɛ; wobɛbobɔ bɛ sɛ ntoma, na bɛbɛsesa.
Nso wo deɛ wote sɛ nea woteaa, na wo mfie to ontwa da.” Na abɔfoɔ he mu hwane na waaka akyerɛ no da sɛ, “Tena me nifa so kosi sɛ mede w’atamfoɔ bɛyɛ wo nane ase ntiasoɔ”?
Nti abɔfoɔ nyinaa nyɛ honhom a bɛsom Nyankopɔn a wasoma bɛ sɛ bɛnsom nkwagyeɛ diadefoɔ anaa?
Ahwɛyie ho kɔkɔbɔ Yei nti, ɔsɛ sɛ yɛsɔ nnoɔma a yɛate he mu dene paa, na yɛamfiri ho da.
Na sɛ asɛm a ɔnam abɔfoɔ so baeɛ he dii mu, na mmarato ne asoɔdene biaa nyaa so akatua, sɛnea atɛntenenee teɛ a, sɛ yɛpo nkwagyeɛ kɛseɛ yi a, nti yebetumi adwane afiri atemmuo mu anaa?
Saa asɛm yi ne Awurade firii aseɛ kaeɛ he.
Na bɛ a bɛteeɛ he hyɛɛ mu kena maa yɛ, berɛ a Nyankopɔn nso de nsɛnkyerɛnne ne anwanwadeɛ ne tumideɛyɔ bebree, ne Honhom Kronkron akyɛdeɛ a ɔkyekyɛeɛ sɛdeɛ ne pɛ teɛ he dii ho adanseɛ bi.
Nkwagyeɛ mu dikanfoɔ Na ɔnyɛ abɔfoɔ ne Nyankopɔn de wiase a ɔɔba a yɛɛka ho asɛm he hyɛɛ bɛ ase.
Yei nti ne twerɛsɛm he di adanseɛ baabi sɛ, “Nipa ne hwane a wodwene ne ho, anaa dasani ne hwane a w’ani ku ne ho?
Woyɔɔ no sɛ bi a aka kakra bi na ɔne abɔfoɔ ayɛ pɛ; wode animuonyam ne anidie abɔ no abotire, na wode nnoɔma nyinaa nso ahyɛ ne nane ase.” Na afei, ɔde nnoɔma nyinaa ɔɔhyɛ ne nane ase he, Nyankopɔn annyae bibiaa hɔ a wamfa anhyɛ ne tumi ase.
Owom sɛ yennya nhuu sɛ ɔde nnoɔma nyinaa ahyɛ ne nane ase deɛ, na mmom, yehu Yesu a, ne tebea baa fam kakra sene abɔfoɔ berɛ tiaa bi mu, na seesei deɛ bɛde animuonyam ne anidie abɔ no abotire he, efiri sɛ ohuu wuo mu amane, na ɔnam Nyankopɔn adom so awu ama nnipa nyinaa.
Na ɔsɔɔ Nyankopɔn a nnoɔma nyinaa yɛ ne dea na ɔnam ne so baeɛ he ani sɛ ɔde mma bebree bɛba animuonyam mu, mmerɛ a bɛ nkwagyeɛ safohene he nam amanehunu mu bewie pɛyɛ.
Na deɛ ɔte bi ho ne bɛ a bɛate bɛ ho he nyinaa wɔ abɔseɛ korɔ.
Ne saa nti Yesu amfɛre sɛ ɔbɛfrɛ bɛ sɛ ne nuanom, nti ɔkaa sɛ, “Mɛpae mu abɔ wo dini akyerɛ me nuanom, asafo mu ne meyi wo ayɛ.” Na bio nso, ɔkaa sɛ, “Mede me werɛ bɛhyɛ ne mu.” Na afei nso, Hwɛ me di, na mma a Nyankopɔn de bɛ maa me he nso di.” Nti sɛ mma he anya honam ne mogyaa korɔ he bi he, saa ne ɔno nso faa mu bi, sɛ ɔnam wuo so betu deɛ ɔwɔ wuo tumi a ɔne Bronsam he agu, na wagye bɛ a bɛte ase a wuo ho hu nti bɛyɛ nkoa he nyinaa.
Na ɔyɛ nɔkwasɛm paa sɛ ɔnyɛ abɔfoɔ ne ɔbaa sɛ ɔɔbɛgye bɛ, na mmom Abraham asefoɔ.
Nti na ɔsɛ sɛ ɔsɛ ne nuanom ade nyinaa mu, na wayɛ mmɔborɔhunu ne sɔfo panyini trodoo, Nyankopɔn fam nnoɔma mu, na wayɛ mane he bɔne ho mpatadeɛ.
Esiane sɛ ɔno ankasa huu amane, na bɛsɔɔ no hwɛeɛ nti, otumi boa bɛ a bɛsɔ bɛ hwɛ nyinaa.
Kristo sene Mose Nti, me nuanom ahoteefoɔ a ho nso hoanya soro frɛ he, honhu sɛ Yesu ne yɛ yɛ gyidie he mu Somafoɔ ne Sɔfo panyini.
Odii nɔkorɛ maa deɛ ɔfrɛɛ no he, sɛdeɛ Mose nso “dii nɔkorɛ Nyankopɔn fie nyinaa mu he.” Nso Yesu wɔ animuonyam pii sene Mose, sɛdeɛ nipa a osi fie he wɔ anidie bebree sene fie he.
(Efiri sɛ, fie biaa, nipa ne si, na deɛ ɔyɔ ade nyinaa ne Nyankopɔn).
Na Mose deɛ, odii nɔkorɛ Nyankopɔn fie nyinaa so sɛ somfo, na odii adanseɛ faa nsɛm a Nyankopɔn bɛka no akyire he ho.
Nso Kristo deɛ, odii nɔkorɛ Nyankopɔn fie nyinaa so sɛ ba, na sɛ yɛsɔ nnamyɛ a yɛde kasa ne anidasoɔ a yɛde hoahoa yɛ ho he mu pintinn kosi awieeɛ a, ɔno ne ma yɛyɛ ne fiefoɔ.
Annyeannie ho kɔkɔbɔ Nti sɛnea Honhom Kronkron ka he, “Nnɛ, sɛ hote ne nne a, hommpirim ho akoma sɛ atuateɛ mmerɛ he, sɛ nsɔhwɛ mmerɛ he mu serɛ he so, baabi a ho nananom sɔɔ mehwɛeɛ he, na behuu me nnwuma mfie aduannan.
Yei maa me bo fuu saa awoɔntoatoasoɔ he, na mekaa sɛ, ‘Bɛfom bɛ akomam daa, nso bɛ deɛ, na benhuu m’akwane.’ Sɛdeɛ m’abufuo mu mekaa ntam sɛ ‘Bɛnnhyɛne me home mu da.’ ” Anuanom, honhwɛ yie, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bɔne ne annyeannie akoma ɔntwe ho mfiri teasefoɔ Nyankopɔn he nkyɛne.
Nso hontutu ho ho fo, da biaa a bɛ bɔ dini sɛ “Nnɛ,” na bɔne a ɔyɛ nnaadaa biaa amma ho mu na amma biaa ampirim n’akoma.
Nso gye sɛ yɛsɔ ahotɔsoɔ a yedii kane nyaeɛ he mu pintinn kosi awieeɛ, ansa na yɛanya kyɛfa Yesu mu ankasa.
Sɛdeɛ bɛkaa sɛ, “Nnɛ, sɛ hote ne nne a, hommpirim ho akoma sɛ berɛ a bɛhyɛɛ me abufuo he.” Na hefoɔ ne bɛtee asɛm he nso bɛhyɛɛ no abufuo he?
Ɔnyɛ bɛ a Mose dii bɛ anim de bɛfirii Misraim he nyinaa?
Bio nso, hefoɔ ne ne bofuu bɛ mfie aduannan he?
Ɔnyɛ bɛ a bɛyɔɔ bɔne, na bɛ afunu totɔɔ serɛ he so he anaa?
Na ɔnyɛ asoɔdenfoɔ he ho ne ɔkaa ntam sɛ bɛnhyɛne n’ahomegyeɛ mu he?
Nti yɛahu sɛ annyeannie nti ne bɛantumi anhyɛne n’ahomegyeɛ mu.
Home a Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ ho bɔ he Nti, esiane sɛ bɔhyɛ da so ya hɔ sɛ yebetumi ahyɛne n’ahomegyeɛ mu nti, homma yɛnhwɛ yie sɛ ho mu bi ɔnntɔ ho sini daakye; na bɛaka asɛmpa he akyerɛ yɛ sɛnea bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ heaa; nso bɛannya mfasoɔ asɛm a bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ he mu, efiri sɛ bɛ a bɛteeɛ he amfa gyidie annye.
Na yɛ a yɛagye adi he nya n’ahomegyeɛ he mu kyɛfa, sɛdeɛ Nyankopɔn aka he, “Sɛnea m’abufuo mu mekaa ntam sɛ, ‘Bennya m’ahomegyeɛ mu kyɛfa,’ ” nso owiee ne nnwuma he ansa na ɔɔto wiase fapem.
Na mmom baabi he na ɔɔka da a ɔtɔ so nson he ho asɛm sɛ, “Na da a ɔtɔ so nson he Nyankopɔn home firii ne nnwuma nyinaa mu.” Ɔsane kaa no ha nso sɛ, “Bennya m’ahomegyeɛ mu kyɛfa da.” Afei esiane sɛ ɔda so abie kwane ama binom sɛ bennya n’ahomegyeɛ mu kyɛfa na nso asoɔdene amma bɛ a bedii kane nyaa asɛmpa he bɛannya n’ahomegyeɛ mu kyɛfa nti, ɔsane hyɛɛ da foforɔ berɛ a ɔkaa berɛ tentenntene akyi ya David dwom mu sɛ, “Nnɛ”, he; sɛnea bɛaka dada sɛ, “Nnɛ, sɛ hote ne nne a, hommpirim ho akoma.” Na sɛ Yosua maa bɛ ahomegyeɛ a, nka Nyankopɔn ɔɔnka da foforɔ bi ho asɛm.
Ne saa nti, homedadie bi da soaa ya hɔ ma Nyankopɔn nkurofoɔ; na bɛ a bɛhyɛne Nyankopɔn ahomegyeɛ mu he home firi bɛ nnwuma ho sɛdeɛ Nyankopɔn nso yɔeɛ he.
Nti homma yɛmmɔ mmɔdene nhyɛne saa ahomegyeɛ he mu bi, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a biaa ɔnyɔ asoɔdene korɔ heaa bi nhwe ase sɛdeɛ bɛyɔeɛ he.
Nɔkwasɛm di, nkwa na ahoɔdene ya Nyankopɔn asɛm mu, ano ɔnam sene sekane anofanu biaa, otumi hwire bibiaa mu koduru sɛ ɔpaepae kra firi honhom ho, akwaa firi kyim ho; na otumi bu adwene ne akoma mu nsusuiɛ atɛne.
Na abɔdeɛ biaa ntumi nhinta no, ne nyinaa da adagya na so abie a ɔda deɛ yɛ nyinaa bebu nkonta akyerɛ no he anim pefee.
Yesu a ɔyɛ yɛ sɔfopanyini Esiane sɛ yɛwɔ sɔfopanyini kɛseɛ a waforo akɔ soro, Yesu a ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn Ba he nti, homma yɛnsɔ yɛ gyidie asɛm a yɛpae mu ka he mu, efiri sɛ, sɔfopanyini a yɛwɔ he ɔnyɛ nea onni tema mma yɛ ya yɛ mmerɛyɛ mu, na ɔyɛ nea bɛasɔ no ahwɛ akwane nyinaa mu sɛ yɛ, na ne nyinaa mu he wannyɔ bɔne da.
Saa deɛ a homma yɛmfa akokoɔduro mmra adom ahennwa he anim, na yɛanya mmɔborɔhunu ne adom a ɔbɛboa yɛ berɛ a ɔsɛ mu.
Na sɔfopanyini biaa a beyi no firi nnipa mu he, bɛhyɛ no sɔfo ma ɔyɔ Nyankopɔn som adwuma ma nnipa na ɔde bɔne ho ayɛyɛdeɛ ne afɔrebɔdeɛ ama.
Esiane sɛ mmerɛyɛ atwa ɔno nso ho ahyia nti, otumi ne bɛ a bennim ne bɛ a bɛafom kwane he di no bɔkɔɔ; ne saa nti ɔsɛ sɛ ɔbɔ ɔno ankasa ne bɔne ho afɔreɛ ne nnipa he nyinaa deɛ nso.
Na bi mfa saa anidie he mma ne ho, gye sɛ deɛ Nyankopɔn afrɛ no te sɛ nea ɔfrɛɛ Aaron he.
Saa nso ne Kristo amfa anidie ama ne ho sɛ sɔfopanyini, na mmom deɛ ɔfrɛɛ no he ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ, “Wo ne me Ba, Nnɛ maayi wo kwane sononko so”; sɛdeɛ ɔka no baabi foforɔ sɛ, “Woyɛ sɔfo daa, ya Melkisedek asɔfoyɛ kwane so.” Berɛ a Yesu ya honam mu he, ɔde nteamu ne nisuo ne nkotosrɛ mpaebɔ kɔɔ deɛ obetumi agye no afiri wuom he anim, na ne nyamesuro nti otiee no.
Ɔyam sɛ na ɔyɛ Ba he deɛ, nso osuaa amaneɛ a ohuiɛ he mu setie, na owiee pɛyɛ he, ɔbɛyɛɛ daa nkwa farebae maa bɛ a bɛyɛ setie ma no he nyinaa, mmerɛ a Nyankopɔn yii no ma no bɛyɛɛ sɔfopanyini ya Melkisedek asɔfoyɛ kwane so.
Akyirisane ho kɔkɔbɔ Yɛwɔ nsɛm pii ka fa yei ho, nso ɔnam sɛ ho yɛ nyaa nteaseɛ mu nti ɔdene ma yɛ sɛ yɛbɛkyerɛkyerɛ mu.
Ɔyam sɛ ɔsɛ sɛ nka saa mmerɛ yi ho tumi kyerɛkyerɛ afoforɔ, nso ho da soaa hia sɛ bɛkyerɛkyerɛ ho Nyankopɔn nsɛm mu mfitiasesɛm he.
Ho hia nofosuo, na ɔnyɛ aduane a mu ɔdene; efiri sɛ nipa biaa a nofosuo yɛ n’aduane he nyiniiɛ, ne ho nkokwaa tenenee asɛm he mu.
Na mmom bɛde aduane a mu oduru ma nipa a wayini, deɛ bɛatete no a n’adwene ma no tumi hu papa ne bɔne ntam nsonsonoeɛ.
Nti afei, homma yɛmfa Kristo ho mfitiasesɛm he nto nkyɛne, na yɛmpere nkɔ nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɔfata bɛ a bɛ anyini Kristo mu he, na yɛansane anto fapem a ɔfa yeinom ho bio: nnwuma funu ho adwensakra ne Nyankopɔn mu gyidie, nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɔfa asubɔ hodoɔ ho, nsa a bɛde gu nkurofoɔ so, awufoɔ sɔreeɛ, ne daa atemmuo ho.
Na sɛ Nyankopɔn ma kwane a, saa nnoɔma yi ne yɛbɛyɔ.
Na ontumi mma sɛ, bɛ a bɛahu hann he, na bɛaka soro ahennie akyɛdeɛ he ahwɛ, na bɛanya kyɛfa Honhom Kronkron mu, na bɛaka Nyankopɔn asɛm he ho nnepa ahwɛ ne wiase a ɔɔba he mu tumi, na afei bɛafiri (nɔkorɛ he) ho, esiane sɛ bɛ ankasa bɛbɔ Nyankopɔn Ba he asennua mu bio na bebu no animtia he, bɛbɛma bɛ nso bɛaba adwensakram bio.
Asaase a nsuo tɔ gu so daa, na ɔsõ aba ma bɛ a bɛyɔ so adwuma he, nya nhyira firi Nyankopɔn hɔ.
Na mmom sɛ ofifiri nkasɛe ne hwerɛmo a, onni mfasoɔ biaa na ɔbɛne nnome ho; n’awieeɛ ne sɛ bɛde bɛbɛhye no.
Adɔfonom, ɔyam sɛ yɛkasa saa kwane yi so deɛ, nso yɛwɔ awerɛhyɛmu sɛ ho fam deɛ nnoɔma pa bi ya hɔ ma ho, nnoɔma a ɔma nkwagyeɛ.
Nyankopɔn nyɛ deɛ ɔntene; na ommu n’ani ngu nwuma pa a ho yɔ ne dɔ a ɔno nti ho da no adi ya ahoteefoɔ som ho, na hogu so yɔ he ho.
Na yɛpɛ sɛ ho mu biaa da mmɔdemmɔ korɔ he adi sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a hobenya anidasoɔ mu ahotɔsoɔ akosi awieeɛ, na hoannyɛ nyaa, na mmom hoasua bɛ a bɛnam gyidie ne aboterɛ so nyaa bɔhyɛ he.
Nyankopɔn bɔhyɛ a ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ Mmerɛ a Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ Abraham bɔ he, esiane sɛ na bi nni hɔ a ɔsõ sene ɔno Nyankopɔn a ɔde no bɛka ntam nti, ɔno Nyankopɔn ankasa kaa ne ho ntam, ɔkaa sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ di mehyira wo na mama wo ase atrɛ.” Nti Abraham de ntoboaseɛ twene saa he, bɔhyɛ he baa mu maa no.
Ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ sɛ nipa biaa de deɛ ɔsõ kyɛne no ne ka ntam, na ntam hyɛ asɛm biaa mu dene na otwa akyingyegyeɛ biaa so.
Ɔno nti ne mmerɛ a Nyankopɔn yɔɔ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛkyerɛ bɔhyɛ he ho diadeɛ he pefee ne botaeɛ a ɔnsesa he, ɔde ntam ne dii agyinamu, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a ɔnam nnoɔma mmienu a ɔnsesa so, sɛ Nyankopɔn ntumi nni torɔ, na yɛ a yɛadwane abɛtoa no he benya nkuranhyɛ a mu ɔdene na yɛasɔ anidasoɔ a ɔda yɛ anim he mu.
Yɛwɔ saa anidasoɔ a otim hɔ pintinn sɛ kra sɛkyɛ, anidasoɔ a ɔhyɛne mu de kosii ntwamutam he mu, baabi a yɛ nti Yesu adi kane ahyɛne hɔ na wayɛ sɔfopanyini ya daa Sɔfopanyini Melkisedek asɔfoyɛ kwane so.
Melkisedek kwane so asɔfoyɛ Na saa Melkisedek yi, Salem hene, Sorosoro Nyankopɔn sɔfo he, berɛ a Abraham dii ahemfo he so nkunim a ɔɔsane aba he, okohyiaa Abraham hyiraa no; ɔno ne Abraham maa no nnoɔma nyinaa so ntotosoɔ du du.
Melkisedek dini he asekyerɛ a odi kane ne sɛ, “tenenee hene”; afei nso ɔyɛ Salem hene a ne nkyerɛaseɛ ne “asomdwie hene.” Twerɛsɛm he anka bibiaa amfa n’agya, ne na, anaa n’awoɔntoatoasoɔ ho, saa nso ne wɔanka bibiaa amfa n’ ahyɛaseɛ ne n’awieeɛ ho, yei ma bɛde no toto Nyankopɔn Ba he ho, na ɔkɔ so di sɔfo daa.
Hwɛ di a odi mu!
Abraham mpo a ɔyɛ nanapanyini he maa no asadeɛ he so ntotosoɔ du du.
Ɔyam sɛ Lewi asefoɔ he yɛ Abraham asefoɔ he bi deɛ, nso ɔnam sɛ benyaa sɔfodwuma he nti mmara he maa bɛ kwane sɛ bɛnnye ntotosoɔ du du mfiri nkorɔfoɔ, mekyerɛ, bɛ nuanom hɔ.
Nso saa beema yi a omfiri Lewi abusua he mu he gyee ntotosoɔ du du firii Abraham a ne nsa kaa bɔhyɛ he hɔ; na ohyiraa Abraham.
Akyinnye biaa nni hɔ sɛ nipa kɛseɛ he ne hyira deɛ ɔyɛ kumaa he.
Lewi asefoɔ he fam deɛ, ɔyɛ nnipa a bewu ne bɛgye ntotosoɔ du du he; nso Melkisedek fam deɛ, ɔyɛ deɛ a bedi ne ho adanseɛ sɛ ɔte ase daa he ne gye ntotosoɔ dudu he.
Mpo bi bɛka sɛ Lewi ankasa a ɔgye ntotosoɔ du du he nam Abraham so tua ntotosoɔ du du, efiri sɛ, Lewi a ɔbɛyɛɛ Abraham aseni he, berɛ a Abraham hyiaa Melkisedek he, na ɔya Abraham asenem a benya nwoo no.
Sɔfo foforɔ a ɔsɛ Melkisedek Na afei sɛ pɛyɛ nam Lewifoɔ sɔfodwuma so (ɔnam sɛ bɛ sɔfodwuma so ne nkurofoɔ he nyaa mmara he) a, mmɛ hia ne ohia sɛ bɛkwati Aaron abusua he yi sɔfo foforɔ bi ya Melkisedek asɔfoyɛ kwane so.
Na sɛ nsakraeɛ ba sɔfodwuma he mu a, hedeɛ na ɔsɛ sɛ nsakraeɛ ba mmara he mu nso.
Na afei deɛ, nea bɛɛka yei fa ne ho he firi abusua foforɔ bi a mu nipa biaa mfirii mu mmɛyɔɔ afɔrebokyia so adwuma da.
Na ɔda hɔ pefee sɛ yɛ Awurade he firi Yuda abusua mu, na saa abusua he deɛ Mose anka sɔfodie ho hwee amfa bɛ ho.
Yei da adi pefee sɛ, berɛ a sɔfo foforɔ sɔre ya Melkisedek asɔfoyɛ kwane so he, bɛamfa honam ahyɛdeɛ mmara so, na mmom bɛnam nkwa a ɔnsɛeɛ ahoɔdene so yɔɔ no sɔfo.
Na bɛadi ne ho adanseɛ sɛ, “Wo yɛ sɔfo daa, te sɛ Melkisedek asɔfoyɛ.” Na kwane bi so he, beyii mmara dadaa he sii nkyɛne, efiri sɛ na ɔmerɛ, na na onni mu nso (efiri sɛ mmara he amma bibiaa anwie pɛyɛ); na mmom, anidasoɔ a ɔyɛ kyɛne yei so na yɛnam bɛne Nyankopɔn.
Na Nyankopɔn ankwati ntanka anyɔ yei.
Lewifoɔ he deɛ bɛkwatii ntanka yɛɛ asɔfoɔ, nso Yesu deɛ, deɛ ɔka faa ne ho ne sɛ, “Awurade aka ntam na ɔnsesa n’adwene, ‘Woyɛ sɔfo daa,’ ” yei ma apam a Yesu adi mu agyinamu yɛ papa kyɛne kane apam he.
Bio nso, na ohia sɛ nnipa pii toatoa so yɛ asɔfoɔ, esiane sɛ wuo amma bɛantoa so anni sɔfo he daa nti; nso Yesu deɛ ɔnam sɛ ɔte hɔ daa nti, odi sɔfo afebɔɔ.
Ne saa nti berɛ biaa obetumi agye bɛ a bɛnam ne so ba Nyankopɔn nkyɛne he, efiri sɛ ɔte ase daa sɛ obedi ama bɛ.
Nti na ohia sɛ yenya sɔfo panyini a ɔte saa, ne ho te, ne ho nni asɛm, nkekaeɛ nni ne ho, bɛate ne ho afiri nnebɔnyɛfoɔ ho, na bɛama no so mmorosoɔ.
Na Yesu deɛ ɔnte sɛ asɔfoɔ mpayimfoɔ a bɛaka he, bɛ deɛ ohia sɛ bɛbɔ afɔreɛ daa, deɛ odi kane, bɛbɔ bɛ a bɛ bɔne ho afɔdeɛ, na afei mane he nso bɔne ho afɔdeɛ; nso ɔno deɛ, ɔbɔɔ afɔreɛ he prɛko pɛ mmerɛ a ɔde ne ho maeɛ he.
Na mmara he hyɛ nnipa a bɛyɛ mmerɛ asɔfoɔ, na mmom, asɔfodie a ntanka ka ho a ɔbaa mmara he akyi he hyɛ Ba a ɔyɛ pɛ he sɔfo panyini afebɔɔ.
Apam a odi mu ntamgyinafoɔ Na afei yɛ asɛm a yɛɛka he titire paa ne sɛ, yɛwɔ saa sɔfo panyini yi a ɔte deɛ ɔte Tumi kɛseɛ he ahennwa nifa so ya soro, a ɔyɔ kronkronbea ne ntomadane a owie pɛyɛ a ɔnnyɛ nipa ne yɔeɛ, na mmom ɔyɛ Awurade he ankasa ne yɔeɛ he mu adwuma.
Na bɛ de sɔfo panyini biaa si hɔ sɛ ɔmfa ayɛyɛdeɛ ne afɔrebɔdeɛ mmra afɔrebokyia so; ne saa nti ohia sɛ ɔno nso nya bibi bɔ afɔreɛ.
Na afei, sɛ nka ɔya asaase yi so a, nka ɔnyɛ sɔfo koraa, esiane sɛ asɔfoɔ bebree ya hɔ daa a bɛbɔ afɔreɛ sɛnea mmara he ka he.
Saa asɔfoɔ he som kronkronbea a ɔyɛ soro deɛ he nhwɛsoɔ ne ne mfonyini; efiri sɛ berɛ a Mose oobesi ntomadane he, Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ no sɛ, “Hwɛ sɛ wobɛyɔ bibiaa sɛdeɛ mfonyini a mede kyerɛɛ wo ya mmepɔ he so he teɛ he.” Nso Yesu deɛ, waanya asɔfodwuma a ɔkyɛne so koraa, ne saa nti ɔyɛ ntamgyinafoɔ mma apam a ɔkyɛne so he, deɛ ɔnam bɔhyɛ a ɔkyɛne so he so baeɛ he.
Apam foforɔ bɔhyɛ Na sɛ apam a odi kane he ho nni asɛm a, nka ho ankohia sɛ apam a ɔtɔ so mmienu he bɛba.
Nyankopɔn nyaa bɛ ho mfomsoɔ mmerɛ a ɔkaa sɛ: “Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ nna bi ɔɔba, Awurade ne ɔɔka, sɛ me ne Israel fie ne Yuda fie bɛpam apam foforɔ a ɔnte sɛ apam a me ne bɛ nananom pameɛ he, da he a mesɔɔ bɛ nsa yii bɛ firii Misraim asaase so he; efiri sɛ bɛantena m’apam he mu, ne saa nti na memfa bɛ ho koraa, Awurade ne ɔɔka.
Apam a me ne Israel fie bɛpam di, Awurade dɛ nna he akyi he: Mede me mmara bɛhyɛ bɛ adwenem, na matwerɛ no bɛ akoma so, na mɛyɛ bɛ Nyankopɔn, na bɛbɛ yɛ me mane.
Na bɛnkyerɛkyerɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho, saa nso ne bɛnnka nkyerɛ bɛ ho bɛ ho sɛ, ‘Ɔsɛ sɛ wo hu Awurade,’ efiri sɛ bɛ nyinaa behu me, ofiri bɛ mu kumaa paa so de kosi kɛseɛ paa so.
Na mehu bɛ mmɔbɔ bɛ ammumuyɔ ho, na menkae bɛ bɔne bio.” Na ɔɔka “apam foforɔ,” bi ho asɛm he, na ɔɔma kane deɛ he atwam.
Na deɛ atwam na ɔɔyɛ dadaa he, ɔnkyɛre biaa ɔbɛyera afiri hɔ.
Asaase ne soro kronkronbea he Na afei kane apam he wɔ nhyehyɛeɛ ya hɔ ma som ne asaase so kronkronbea.
Na besii ntomadane he mu pie, mekyerɛ deɛ bedi kane wuram ansa na bɛawura nea ɔtɔ so mmienu he mu.
Saa dane yi mu ne na kaneadua, didi-pono ne Kyerɛ-paanoo he ya; hɔ ne bɛfrɛ no Kronkronbea he.
Twamtam a ɔtɔ so mmienu he akyi ne ntomadane a bɛfrɛ no Kronkron mu Kronkron he ya.
Mu ne sikakɔkɔɔ aduhwamhyeɛ bokyea ne apam adaka a bɛde sikakɔkɔɔ adura ho nyinaa, mu ne sika kuruwaa a mana yam ne Aaron poma a ɔfefɛeɛ ne apam aboɔpono he ya; so ne animuonyam Kerubim he kata mpata adwa he so.
Saa nnoɔma yi deɛ yentumi nka ho asɛm nkɔ akyiri seesei.
Sɛ bewie saa nnoɔma yi siesie a, asɔfo he kɔ ntomadane a odi kane he mu daa kɔyɔ bɛsom adwuma; Na deɛ ɔtɔ so mmienu he deɛ, sɔfo panyini he nkoaa ne afe biaa ɔkɔ hɔ prɛko, berɛ a ɔde mogyaa kɔbɔ afɔreɛ, ɔnam ɔnoaa ne mfomsoɔ ne mane he deɛ nti.
Nti Honhom Kronkron da no adi pefee sɛ mmerɛ tentene a na ntomadane a odi kane he da so si hɔ he, na bennya nyii kwane a ɔkɔ kronkronbea he adi.
Na ɔyɛ mfatoho de ma yɛ nnɛ mmerɛ yi.
Saa nhyehyɛeɛ mu he bɛde ayɛyɛdeɛ ne afɔdeɛ nso mma a ontumi mma deɛ ɔsom he nni mu n’ahonim fam, na mmom, ɔyɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɔfa aduane ne anonneɛ ne asubɔ hodoɔ ho, nhyehyɛeɛ a ɔfa nipadua he ho nkoaa kosi sɛ mmerɛ bɛbɛba a bɛtoto nnoɔma nyinaa yie.
Kristo asɔfodie a odi mu Nso Kristo deɛ, berɛ a ɔbaa sɛ nnoɔma pa a aba he ho sɔfo panyini he, na afei ɔnam ntomadane a ɔkyɛne so na odi mu he mu he (nyɛ deɛ bɛde nsa ayɔ, meekyerɛ sɛ nyɛ adebɔ yi mu), ɔhyɛnee Kronkron mu Kronkron hɔ prɛko pɛ.
Kristo amfa mmirekyie ne anantwie mogyaa, na mmom ɔde ɔno ankasa ne mogyaa ne nyaa daa gyeɛ maa yɛ.
Na sɛ mmirekyie ne anantwinyini mogyaa ne nantwibedeɛ mma nso mogyaa a bɛde petee bɛ a na bɛ ho agu fi ho maa bɛ honam ho teeɛ a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ ne Kristo a ɔnam daa honhom so de ne ho bɔɔ afɔdeɛ, a ho nni dɛm maa Nyankopɔn he mogyaa ontumi nte ho ahonim ho mfiri nnwuma funu nyinaa mu ma ho nkɔsom Nyankopɔn a ɔte ase he?
Kristo yɛ Apam foforɔ ntamgyinafoɔ Sɛ saa deɛ a, Kristo yɛ apam foforɔ ho ntamgyinafoɔ, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bɛ a bɛafrɛ bɛ he benya daa agyapadeɛ a bɛahyɛ ho bɔ he, efiri sɛ wuo a owuiɛ he agye bɛ afiri apam a odi kane he mmarato ase.
Ansa na bi nsamanseɛ betumi adi dwuma he, na nea ɔhyɛeɛ he awu, efiri sɛ wuo akyi ne bɛ de nsamanseɛ di dwuma, mprɛ dodoɔ a nea ɔhyɛeɛ he te ase he deɛ ne nsamanseɛ he ntumi nni dwuma.
Yei nti woankwati mogyaa amfa apam a odi kane he ansi hɔ, efiri sɛ mmerɛ a Mose kaa ahyɛdeɛ biaa ne ahyɛdeɛ ho asɛm kyerɛɛ mane he, sɛdeɛ mmara he teɛ he, ɔfaa nantwie mma ne mmirekyie mogyaa, ne nsuo ne ntoma kɔkɔɔ a sommɛ bɔ ano na ɔde petee nwoma heaa ne mane he nyinaa so, kaa sɛ, “Yei ne apam he mogyaa a Nyankopɔn ahyɛ ama ho.” Na saa kwane heaa so ne ɔde mogyaa he petee ntomadane ne nnoɔma a bɛde yɔ som adwuma he nyinaa ho.
Nɔkwasɛm, bɛde mogyaa te bibiaa ho sɛdeɛ mmara he teɛ he, na sɛ mogyaa angu a bɔne fakyɛ nni hɔ.
Kristo afɔrebɔ yi bɔne hɔ Nti ohia sɛ soro nnoɔma he ho nhwɛsoɔ he, bɛde saa amanneɛ yi te ho, nso soro nnoɔma he ankasa hia afɔreɛ a odi mu kyɛne yeinom.
Na Kristo anhyɛne kronkronbea a bɛde nsa ayɔ a ɔyɛ kronkronbea kann he ho nhwɛsoɔ he mu, na mmom ɔhyɛnee soro ankasa sɛ afei ookoyi ne ho adi Nyankopɔn anim ama yɛ.
Saa ara nso ne wanhyɛne hɔ sɛ ɔde ne ho bɛbɔ afɔdeɛ mprɛ pii, sɛdeɛ sɔfo panyini hyɛne kronkronbea hɔ de mogyaa a ɔnyɛ ɔno ankasa ne mogyaa kɔ bɔ afɔdeɛ afe biaa he; efiri sɛ nka obehu amane da biaa firi wiase ahyɛaseɛ.
Nso sɛdeɛ ɔteɛ yi deɛ, waayi ne ho adi prɛko ama biaa kosi wiase awieeɛ sɛ ɔde ɔno ankasa ne ho bɛbɔ afɔreɛ ayi bɔne hɔ.
Na sɛdeɛ ɔda hɔ sɛ nipa bewu prɛko, na wuo he akyi atemmuo ya hɔ he, saa nso ne Kristo a ɔde ne ho bɔɔ afɔreɛ prɛko sɛ ɔbɛsoa nnipa bebree bɔne prɛko he, beyi ne ho adi ne mprenu so a, ɔmmɛyɔ bɔne ho adwuma, na mmom ɔɔbɛgye bɛ a bɛhwɛ no kwane dendenndene he nkwa.
Kristo afɔreprɛko a ɔbɔ maa biaa Na esiane sɛ mmara he kura nnoɔma pa a ɔɔba he nsɛsoɔ na mmom onni nnoɔma he ankasa nti, ontumi mfa saa daa daa afɔreɛ a bɛbɔ no afe biaa he so mma bɛ a bɛde bɛ ho to so he nwie pɛyɛ.
Sɛ asɔrefoɔ he afɔreɛ a bɛbɔeɛ he tumi popaa bɛ bɔne na ɔtee bɛ ahonim ho ampa, nti nka bɛannyae afɔrebɔ anaa?
Nso saa afɔrebɔ henom ma bɛkae bɔne afe biaa, efiri sɛ, anantwie ne mmirekyie mogyaa ntumi nyi bɔne hɔ.
Nti, berɛ a Kristo baa wiase he, ɔkaa sɛ, “Woampɛ afɔrebɔ ne ayɛyɛdeɛ, na mmom nipadua ne woasiesie ama me; hyeɛ afɔreɛ ne bɔne afɔreɛ ansɔ w’ani Na afei mekaa sɛ, ‘Nyankopɔn, hwɛ, maaba sɛ meebɛyɔ deɛ wopɛ, O me Nyankopɔn’ (sɛdeɛ bɛatwerɛ me ho asɛm nwoma mmobɔeɛ he mu).” Mmerɛ a odii kane kaa sɛ, “Afɔrebɔ ne ayɛyɛdeɛ anaa hyeɛ afɔreɛ ne bɔne afɔreɛ ansɔ w’ani he” (ɔnam mmara he so na bɛde yeinom ma), na ɔka kaa ho sɛ, “Hwɛ, maaba sɛ meebɛyɔ deɛ wopɛ.” Oyii deɛ odi kane he hɔ, na ɔde deɛ ɔtɔ so mmienu he besii hɔ.
Na ɔnam Nyankopɔn pɛ so ne yɛ ho ate ɔnam Yesu Kristo nipadua a ɔde bɔɔ afɔre-prɛko he nti.
Na sɔfo biaa gyina hɔ sɛ ɔyɔ ne som adwuma da biaa, na ɔtaa bɔ afɔreɛ korɔ heaa a ontumi nyi bɔne hɔ.
Nso mmerɛ a Kristo bɔɔ afɔreɛ baako maa bɔne afebɔɔ he, “ɔtenaa Nyankopɔn nifa so,” na ɔɔtwɛne “kosi sɛ bɛde n’atamfoɔ bɛyɛ ne nane ase ntiasoɔ.” Na ɔnam afɔreɛ baako pɛ so ama bɛ a bɛate bɛ ho nyinaa awie pɛyɛ afebɔɔ.
Na Honhom Kronkron so di adanseɛ Twerɛsɛm he mu sɛ, “Yei ne apam a me ne bɛ bɛpam he Awurade dɛ: nna he akyi he Mede me mmara bɛhyɛ bɛ akomam, na mɛtwerɛ no bɛ adwenem,” na ɔsane ka kaa ho sɛ, “Menkae bɛ bɔne ne bɛ mmarato bio.” Baabiaa a yeinom ho fakyɛ ya he, bɔne ho afɔrebɔ nni hɔ bio.
Nyankopɔn anim korɔ kwane Nti, me nuanom, esiane sɛ yɛnam Yesu mogyaa so anya awerɛhyɛmu a yɛde bɛhyɛne kronkronbea hɔ, na ɔnam kwane foforɔ a nkwa yam so abie ntomadane he ama yɛ yi (mekyerɛ ɔnam ne honam so), na yɛwɔ Nyankopɔn fie so sɔfopanyini yi nti, homma yɛmfa akoma a mu yɛ fann a gyidie mu ahotɔsoɔ ahyɛ no ma, akoma a bɛapete ho ate ho afiri ahonim bɔne ho ne yɛ nipadua a bɛde nsuo a ho te adware he ntwe mmɛne no.
Homma yɛnhimhim na mmom yenkura yɛ anidasoɔ asɛm a yɛka he mu dene, efiri sɛ deɛ waahyɛ bɔ he yɛ nɔkwafoɔ.
Na homma yɛnhwɛ sɛ yɛbɛkanyane yɛ ho yɛ ho na yɛadodɔ yɛ ho yɛ ho; na yɛmfa nnwuma pa nsom yɛ ho yɛ ho, hommma yennyae yɛ ho yɛ ho nhyiamu, sɛdeɛ binom agyae bɛ ho bɛ ho nhyiamu he, na mmom homma yɛnhyehyɛ yɛ ho yɛ ho nkurane, ne titire mmerɛ a yehu sɛ Da he abɛne.
Na sɛ yɛboapa kɔ so yɔ bɔne mmerɛ a yɛanya nɔkorɛ he ho nimdeɛ a, bɔne ho afɔrebɔ foforɔ biaa nni hɔ bio, na mmom atemmuo a ohu akwanhwɛ, ne abufuo gya a ɔbɛhye Nyankopɔn atamfoɔ pasaa he ne ya hɔ ma yɛ.
Nipa biaa a ɔto Mose mmara he gyina adansefoɔ mmienu anaa mmeɛnsa adanseɛ wu berɛ a onnya mmɔborɔhunu biaa.
Mmɛ asotwe koraa ne ɔboro so a hosusu sɛ ɔfata sɛ bɛde bɛtwe bɛ a bɛde Nyankopɔn Ba he anim atwitwi fam na bɛabu apam mogyaa a bɛde tee bɛ ho he animtia, na bɛasopa adom Honhom he?
Na yenim deɛ ɔkaa sɛ “Mene metɔ werɛ, metua ka.” Na ɔkaa bio sɛ, “Awurade bebu ne mane atɛne.” Nti ohu ma bi sɛ ɔbɛtɔ Nyankopɔn teasefoɔ he abufuom.
Nso honkae kane nna he a hohuu hann he, sɛ hode animia gyinaeɛ, kõ dendene amanehunu mu, maa bɛbɔɔ ho adapaa na bɛtaa ho badwam, na da bi nso ho ne bɛ a bɛfaa saa tebea he mu he nyaa ayɔnkofa.
Na honyaa tema maa nneduafoɔ, na hode anigyeɛ penee so maa bɛfom ho agyapadeɛ, efiri sɛ honim sɛ ho ankasa howɔ agyapadeɛ a odi mu, na ɔbɛtena hɔ daa.
Nti honnto ho nnamyɛ a ɔma akatua kɛseɛ he ntwene; efiri sɛ ho hia boasetɔ, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a sɛ hoyɔ deɛ Nyankopɔn pɛ wie a, ho nsa bɛka deɛ wahyɛ ho bɔ he.
Na “aka kakraa bi, deɛ ɔɔba he bɛba, na ɔnkyɛre koraa; Na deɛ ɔtene he firi gyidie mu benya nkwa, na me kra ani nsɔ deɛ ɔtwe ne ho sane akyi he.” Nso yɛ deɛ, yɛnnka bɛ a bɛtwe bɛ ho sane akyi na bɛayera he ho, na mmom yɛka bɛ a bɛwɔ gyidie na bɛanya nkwa he ho.
Gyidie asekyerɛ Na afei, gyidie ne nnoɔma a yɛ ani da so ho awerɛhyemu a osi pi, ne nnoɔma a yenhu ho adansegyeɛ.
Ɔnam yei so ne maa bedii tetefoɔ he ho adanseɛ.
Gyidie ne ma yɛ te aseɛ sɛ Nyankopɔn nam n’asɛm so ne bɔɔ nnoɔma nyinaa, na nnoɔma yehu yi firi deɛ onni hɔ mu ne baeɛ.
Habel, Henok ne Noah ho nhwɛsoɔ Gyidie ne Habel de bɔɔ afɔreɛ maa Nyankopɔn a na ɔsɔ ani kyɛnee Kain deɛ he.
Ɔnam yei so maa bebuu Habel sɛ ɔtene, na Nyankopɔn dii n’afɔreɛ he ho adanseɛ.
Ɔyam sɛ Habel awu deɛ, nso ɔnam ne gyidie he so da so kasa kyerɛ yɛ.
Gyidie nti ne Nyankopɔn faa Henok kɔeɛ a wanhu wuo; na “bɛanhu no bio, efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn faa no kɔeɛ.” Na ansa na ɔɔbɛfa no akɔ he, bedii ne ho adanseɛ sɛ “ɔsɔ Nyankopɔn ani.” Na sɛ gyidie nni hɔ a, biaa ntumi nsɔ Nyankopɔn ani, efiri sɛ ɔsɛ sɛ deɛ ɔba ne nkyɛne biaa gye di sɛ ɔya hɔ na ɔyɛ bɛ a bɛhwehwɛ n’akyi kwane he katuafoɔ.
Gyidie so ne Noah, mmerɛ a Nyankopɔn bɔɔ no kɔkɔ faa nnoɔma a obesi ho he, ɔde anidie gyee kɔkɔbɔ he too mu na ɔyɔɔ adaka de gyee ne fiefoɔ nkwa; Noah nam saa so buu wiase fɔ, na ɔnam ne gyidie so bɛyɛɛ tenenee adedifoɔ.
Abraham gyidie Gyidie nti ne bɛfrɛɛ Abraham sɛ ontu nkɔ baabi a daakye bɛde bɛ ma no sɛ n’agyapadeɛ he, ɔyɔɔ setie kɔeɛ berɛ a na onnim baabi a na ɔɔkɔ he.
Abraham nam gyidie so tenaa asaase a bɛahyɛ no ho bɔ he so sɛ hɔhoɔ, tenaa ntomadane mu, sɛdeɛ Isak ne Yakob nso yɔeɛ he, a bɛ nso bɛka ne ho sɛ bɔhyɛ korɔ heaa ho adedifoɔ.
Na ɔɔtwɛne kuro a ɔwɔ fapem a ne kyekyerefoɔ ne ne yɔfoɔ ne Nyankopɔn.
Sara Gyidie nti Sara tumi nyinsɛneeɛ, mpo berɛ a na n’awoɔ atwam, efiri sɛ obuu deɛ na wahyɛ no awoɔ ho bɔ he nɔkwafoɔ.
Nti ɔnam nipa baako a na ɔte sɛ deɛ waawu he so ne maa nipa, “na bɛdɔɔso sɛ soro nsoromma ne mpoano anwea a bentumi nkane mpo” baeɛ.
Yeinom nyinaa wuu gyidie mu a bɛ nsa anka bɔhyɛ he, na mmom behuu no akyirikyiri gye tomm, kaa sɛ, bɛyɛ ahɔhoɔ ne amanfrafoɔ asaase yi so, efiri sɛ bɛ a bɛkaa saa he daa no adi pefee sɛ bɛ ani da bɛ ankasa bɛ mane so.
Sɛ na bɛ akoma da kuro a befirii mu baeɛ he so a, nka bɛwɔ akwannya sɛ bɛbɛsane akɔ hɔ.
Na afei, bɛ ani gyinaa mane papa bi, mekyerɛ, soro mane he.
Ne saa nti ɔnyɛ Nyankopɔn aniwuo sɛ bɛbɛfrɛ no bɛ Nyankopɔn; nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, wasiesie kuro bi ama bɛ.
Gyidie nti ne Abraham, mmerɛ a bɛsɔɔ no hwɛeɛ he, ɔde Isak maeɛ.
Ɔno a onyaa bɔhyɛ he yɔɔ krado sɛ ɔde ne ba koro he bɛbɔ afɔreɛ, ɔno ho ne bɛkaa sɛ, “Ɔnam Isak so ne wobenya w’asefoɔ.” Osusuu sɛ Nyankopɔn betumi anyane no afiri awufoɔ mu mpo.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, sɛ wofa nea osiiɛ he kasabebuom a, wobetumi aka sɛ, ne nsa kaa Isak bio firii wuom.
Isak, Yakob ne Yosef Gyidie nti ne Isak hyiraa Yakob ne Esau ya nnoɔma a ɔbɛba daakye ho.
Afei ɔnam gyidie so ne Yakob, mmerɛ a na ɔda awusu mpo he, ohyiraa Yosef mmammeema he mu biaa.
Yakob de ne ho tweree ne poma, na ɔkoto sɔree Nyankopɔn.
Bio nso, ɔnam gyidie nti, ne Yosef, mmerɛ a ne nna ɔɔba awieeɛ he, ɔkaa nkorɔeɛ a Israelfoɔ betu akɔ he ho asɛm, na ɔhyɛɛ ne nnompe sie ho nsamanseɛ nso.
Mose gyidie Afei gyidie nti ne bɛwoo Mose he n’awofoɔ de no siee bosome mmeɛnsa n’awoɔ akyi, efiri sɛ, behuu sɛ abɔfra he ho ɔfɛ; na bɛansuro mmara a na hene he ahyɛ he.
Gyidie nti ne Mose nyiniiɛ he, wampɛ sɛ bɛbɛfrɛ no Farao babaa ba, na mmom ɔpɛɛ sɛ ɔne Nyankopɔn mane behu amaneɛ kyɛne sɛ ɔbɛte bɔne mu dɛ mmerɛ tiaa bi.
Obuu amaneɛ a Kristo nti obehu he kyɛnee Misraim ahonyadeɛ, efiri sɛ na ɔɔhwɛ akatua a ɔda n’anim he kwane.
Gyidie nti ne ofirii Misraim he wansuro hene he abufuo, na omiaa n’ani te sɛ deɛ wahu Nyankopɔn a benhu no he.
Gyidie nti ne odii Twam ne mogya-peteɛ afahyɛ he, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a deɛ ɔsɛe mmakane he ɔmfa ne nsa nka Israel mmakane he.
Israel akofofoɔ binom nso gyidie Gyidie nti ne mane he faa Mmɛwa Po he mu te sɛ bɛnam asaase pɛsɛɛ so, nso Misraimfoɔ he yɔɔ sɛ bɛɛfa mu he, Po he faa bɛ nyinaa.
Gyidie nti ne Yeriko afasuo he bubu guu fam mmerɛ a Israelfoɔ twaa ho hyiaa nna nson he.
Ɔnam dwamanfoɔ Rahab gyidie so ne maa no gyee akwansrafoɔ he asomdwie mu a ne saa nti bɛ anku, na mmom bekuu asoɔdenfoɔ he.
Na mmɛ ne menka bio?
Efiri sɛ mmerɛ ɔmma kwane mma me nka Gideon, Barak, Samson, Yefta, Dawid ne Samuel ne adiyifoɔ he ho asɛm— yeinom ne nam gyidie so dii ahennie so nkunim, hwɛɛ sɛ atɛntenenee bɛyɔ adwuma, bɛ nsa kaa bɔhyɛ, mmua gyata ano, dum gya a ɔɔdɛre, dwane sekane ano, nyaa ahoɔdene berɛ a bɛyɛɛ mmerɛ mu, yɛɛ nam kõ mu, kaa amanfrafoɔ dɔm guiɛ.
Nnanom nsa kaa bɛ awufoɔ a bɛasɔre.
Bɛyɛɛ bebree ayakayakadeɛ, nso bɛampene sɛ bɛbɛgye bɛ, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a bebenya wusɔreɛ a odi mu.
Bedii binom ho fɛw na bɛbɔɔ bɛ mmaa, na mpo bɛde nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn guu binom de bɛ too afiase.
Besii bɛ aboɔ kuu bɛ, bɛde asradaa paee bɛ mu mmienu, bɛde sekane kuu bɛ; na bɛakɔneabadie nyinaa mu he, ntaadeɛ a na bɛhyɛ nyinaa yɛ nnwane ne mmirekyie nwoma, ohiaa bɛ, bɛ ho hiahia bɛ na bedii bɛ ani.
Na bɛyɛɛ sɛ nnipa a na wiase so nni mfasoɔ mma bɛ.
Nti bekyinkyinnii serɛ ne mmepɔ so, ne abodane mu asaase mu monku mu.
Nso yei nyinaa mu he, ɔyam sɛ bɛ gyidie nyaa adanse-pa deɛ, nso bɛ nsa anka bɔhyɛ he, esiane sɛ na Nyankopɔn asiesie bibi a ɔyɛ kyɛne so asie amma yɛ, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a bɛnkwati yɛ nyɛ bɛ pɛ.
Yesu nhwɛsoɔ Saa nti yɛ nso, esiane sɛ adansefoɔ bebree atwa yɛ ho ahyia yi, homma yɛnto adesoa ne bɔne biaa a ɔkyekyere yɛ na ɔtwe yɛ he ngu, na yɛmfa animia ntu akansie a ɔda yɛ anim he mu mmirika, nhwɛ, Yesu a ɔyɛ yɛ gyidie farebae na ɔno nso ne ma no wie pɛyɛ, ɔno ne hwɛɛ anigyeɛ a ɔda n’anim he na ɔde boasetɔ huu asennua he ho amaneɛ, na obuu n’ani guu ho aniwuo so.
Ne saa nti, waagye n’adwa Nyankopɔn ahennie he nifa.
Na honhwɛ deɛ ɔde boasetɔ faa nnebɔnyɛfoɔ nitane a bɛde tiaa no he mu, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a hoommerɛ anaa hoompa aba, ho akomam.
Ampa, apereapereɛ a ho ne bɔne oodi yi, onnya nkoduru sɛ hode ho mogyaa betwa so koraa.
Na ho werɛ afiri afutusɛm a bɛde maa ho ɔnam sɛ ho yɛ mma nti he anaa?
Ɔne sɛ, “Me ba, mmu wo ani ngu Awurade asotwe so, anaa ɔtwe w’aso a mma waba mu mmu; efiri sɛ bɛ a Awurade dɔ bɛ he ne ɔtwe bɛ aso, na ɔtea ne ba biaa a ɔgye no.” Honya atenetene a bɛtenetene ho he mu boasetɔ, efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn yɛ ho sɛ mma.
Na ba deɛ ɔya he ne n’agya ntenetene no?
Sɛ hoanya atenetene a mma nyinaa fa mu he bi a, hedeɛ na honnyɛ mma mmara kwane so sɛ ɔno ankasa ne mma nɔkorem.
Afei nso, yɛwɔ honam fam awofoɔ a bɛtenetene yɛ, na yɛde buo ma bɛ.
Sɛ saa deɛ a, nti ɔnsɛ sɛ yɛbrɛ yɛ ho ase mpo kyɛne saa hyɛ honhom nyinaa Agya he ase na yɛanya nkwa anaa?
Na yɛ honam fam awofoɔ he deɛ, bɛtenetene yɛ mmerɛ tiaa bi mu sɛnea ɔsɔ bɛ ani, nso ɔno deɛ, yɛ yiedie nti ne ɔtenetene yɛ, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a yɛbɛ yɛ kronkron sɛdeɛ ɔno nso yɛ kronkron he.
Na seeseiaa deɛ atenetene biaa nyɛ anigyeɛ, na mmom ɔyɛ haw, nso akyire yi ɔsõ asomdwie aba a ɔyɛ tenenee ma bɛ a bɛfa saa nteteɛ he mu.
Nti homma ho nsa a mu ago he so na honhyɛ ho nkotodwe a ayɛ mmerɛ he mu dene, na homma ho akwane ntene, na adeɛ biaa a abubu he amfiri ne nyinasoɔ so, na mmom anya ayaresa.
Kɔkɔbɔ a otia bɛ a bɛpo Nyankopɔn adom Honhwehwɛ asomdwie ho ne nnipa nyinaa ntam, ɔne kronkronyɛ a deɛ ɔkwati biaa ntumi nhu Awurade he.
Honhwɛ yie na Nyankopɔn adom he ammɔ biaa; na nhini biaa a nwonwono yam amfifiri ho mu na ammɛyɛ haw amma ho, na angu nnipa bebree ho fi.
Honhwɛ yie sɛ ho mu bi ɔnnyɛ sɛ Esau, dwamamfoɔ ne huhuni a aduane baako nti ɔtɔnoo ne mpanyinnie.
Honnim sɛ akyire yi, ɔyam sɛ ɔde nisuo hwehwɛɛ nhyira he deɛ, nso bɛpoo no, efiri sɛ wanhwehwɛ adwensakra akyi kwane.
Na ɔnyɛ mmepɔ a bɛde nsa ka he ho, ne gya a ɔɔhye ne mununkum kusuu ne sum ne mframa a ɔɔbɔ huu, ne mmɛne nnyegyeɛ ne nsɛm nne a bɛ a bɛteeɛ he srɛɛ sɛ ɔmmfa asɛm bi nka bɛ ho bio he ho ne hoaba; efiri sɛ, ahyɛdeɛ a bɛde maa bɛ he mu yɛɛ duru maa bɛ, ɔne sɛ, “Sɛ aboa mpo ho kɔka mmepɔ he a, bensi no aboɔ ma onwu.” Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, ɔnam sɛ na ohu paa he nti, Mose kaa sɛ, “Mebɔ hu na me ho popo.” Na mmom, ho deɛ hoaba Sion Bepɔ so ne Nyankopɔn teasefoɔ he kuro, soro Yerusalem, ne abɔfoɔ bebree nhyiamu, ne mmakane a bɛatwerɛ bɛ dini soro ahennie mu nhyiamu ase ne Nyankopɔn a ɔyɛ nnipa nyinaa temufoɔ, ne ahoteefoɔ ahonhom a bɛayɛ no pɛ, na ho aba Yesu hɔ, apam foforɔ he ho ntamgyinafoɔ, ne mogyaa a bɛapete a ɔkasa yie kyɛne Habel mogyaa he.
Honhwɛ yie na hoampo deɛ ɔɔkasa he; na sɛ bɛ a bɛpoo kɔkɔbɔ a bɛte firii asaase yi so he antumi annwane a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ ne yɛ a yɛate kɔkɔbɔ a ofiri soro he betumi adwane?
Saa mmerɛ he ne nne wosoo asaase; nso afei deɛ waahyɛ bɔ sɛ, “Mesane awoso asaase bio, ɔnyɛ asaase nkoaa na mmom soro nso ka ho.” Saa asɛm a ɔka sɛ, “Mɛwoso no bio”, he kyerɛ sɛ obeyi nnoɔma a ɔwosoeɛ he afiri hɔ, ɔne sɛ, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a deɛ bentumi nwoso he bɛtena hɔ daa.
Nti esiane sɛ yɛanya ahennie a ɔnwoso yi, homma yɛmfa aseda mmra mfa so nsom Nyankopɔn sɛdeɛ ɔsɔ n’ani anidie ne ahodasoɔ mu, efiri sɛ, yɛ Nyankopɔn te sɛ gya a ɔdɛre.
Som a ɔsɔ Nyankopɔn ani Homma nuadɔ ntena hɔ daa.
Hommmu ho ani ngu ahɔhoyɛ so.
Na binom nam ahɔhoyɛ so yɔɔ abɔfoɔ papa a na bennim sɛ bɛyɛ abɔfoɔ mpo.
Honkae bɛ a bɛda afiase, te sɛ deɛ ho ne bɛ ne da hɔ ɔne bɛ a bɛyɔ bɛ ayakayakadeɛ te sɛ deɛ ho ne bɛ ne ohu amaneɛ.
Homma nnipa nyinaa nni awareɛ nni, na honngu awareɛ mpa ho fi; efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn bebu adwamammɔfoɔ ne awaresɛefoɔ atɛne.
Hommma sikaniberɛ mmma ho abrabɔ mu, na homma ho ani nsɔ deɛ ho wɔ; efiri sɛ waaka sɛ, “Mennyae ho na mempo ho.” Ne saa nti, yebetumi de akokoɔduro aka sɛ, “Nyankopɔn ne me boafoɔ; Mensuro.
Ɛɛne ne nipa betumi de ayɔ me?” Honkae ho mpayimfoɔ, bɛ a bɛkaa Nyankopɔn asɛm he kyerɛɛ ho; honhwɛ sɛdeɛ bɛ abrabɔ wieeɛ, na honsua bɛ gyidie.
Sɛnea Yesu Kristo teɛ nnora he, ɔte saa nnɛ, na ɔbɛyɛ saa ara daa.
Hommma nkyerɛkyerɛ ahodoɔ ne nsɛm foforɔ mmfa ho nkyinkyini, na ɔyɛ sɛ bɛ de adom hyɛ akoma dene, na ɔnyɛ nnuane a bɛ a bediiɛ he nni ho mfasoɔ biaa.
Yɛwɔ afɔrebokyia bi a bɛ a bɛyɔ som adwuma ntomadane he mu he nni ho kwane sɛ bedi so bibi.
Na mmoa a sɔfo panyini he de bɛ mogyaa bɔɔ bɔne ho afɔreɛ he bɛhye bɛ nsrabane he akyi.
Saa nti ne Yesu nso huu amane kuro he akyi sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a ɔde ɔno ankasa ne mogyaa bɛte mane he ho.
Saa deɛ a, homma yɛnkɔ ne nkyɛne kuro he akyi na yɛasoa n’ahohorabɔ a ohuu mu amaneɛ he; efiri sɛ yenni kuro a ɔtena hɔ daa ya ha yi, na mmom nea ɔɔba he na yɛɛhwɛ no kwane dendene.
Nti homma yɛmfa ne so mmɔ aseda afɔreɛ ma Nyankopɔn, ɔne sɛ, aba a ofiri anofafaa a ɔbɔ ne dini mu.
Hommmu ho ani ngu papayɔ ne adekyɛ so, efiri sɛ, saa afɔreɛ he sɔ Nyankopɔn ani.
Homfa buo ne ahobrɛaseɛ ma ho mpayimfoɔ, efiri sɛ bɛwɛne ho kra sɛ bɛ a bebu ho akonta.
Homma bɛmfa anigye nyɔ na ɔnyɛ ahomeguo so, sɛ bɛde ahomeguo a, ɔnyɛ mfasoɔ biaa mma ho.
Hommɔ mpaeɛ ma yɛ; efiri sɛ yɛwɔ ahotɔsoɔ sɛ yɛwɔ ahonim a ho te, yɛasiesie yɛ ho sɛ yebedi nɔkorɛ nnoɔma nyinaa mu.
Metu ho fo sɛ honyɔ saa adeɛ yi anibereɛ so, na ama bɛde asane abɛka ho ho animuanimu yiaa.
Nhyirasɛm Na asomdwie Nyankopɔn a ɔnam daa apam he mogyaa so, ayi nnwane he hwɛfoɔ kɛseɛ a ɔne yɛ Awurade Yesu afiri awufoɔ mu he, mma ho nni mu nnoɔma nyinaa mu na hoayɔ nea ɔpɛ, deɛ ɔyɔ ho mu adwuma he mfa Yesu Kristo so, sɛdeɛ ɔsɔ n’ani.
Ɔno ne animuonyam nka no daa daa.
Amen.
Afotusɛm a otwatoɔ ne nkyea Anuanom, metu ho fo sɛ honkura m’afotusɛm he mu, efiri sɛ m’atwerɛ no tiaa bi ne abra ho.
Mepɛ sɛ hohu sɛ bɛagyae yenua Timoteo; na sɛ ɔba mmerɛ pa mu a me ne no bɛba abehu ho.
Honkyea ho mpayimfoɔ ne ahoteefoɔ he nyinaa ma me.
Bɛ a befiri Italia he kyea ho.
Adom nka ho nyinaa.
Amen.
NNIANIMU Krataa a ofiri Yakobo hɔ he yɛ Nyamesompa ho nhyehyɛeɛ ahodoɔ bi.
Ɔtwerɛ kɔmaa “Nyankopɔn nkurofoɔ a bɛabɔ ahwete asaase so nyinaa”.
Twerɛfoɔ he nam kasakoa a mu da hɔ so kyerɛ nyansa akwankyerɛ a ɔfa Kristosom su ne nneyɔeɛ ho.
Ɔkasa fa ahonya ne hia, sɔhwɛ, subane pa, adwen-hunu a benya tia afoforɔ, gyidie ne nnwuma, sɛdeɛ bɛde kɛtrɛma yɔ adwuma, nyansa, ntɔkwapɛ, ahantan ne ahobrɛaseɛ, atemmuo a bɛde bu afoforɔ, ahohoahoa, ntoboaseɛ ne mpaebɔ ho.
Afei nso twerɛfoɔ he ka bibi fa nyamesompa ho, a ɔno ne sɛ “bi bɛdwene nyanka ne akunafoɔ ho, bɛ ahohiahia mmerɛ mu, na ɔbɛte ne ho afiri wiase nkekaeɛ ho” .
Afei nso, otu fo sɛ ɔnam sɛ biaa nnim adekyeɛ mu nsɛm nti, ɔnsɛ sɛ biaa de kyena hoahoa ne ho .
Krataa he si hia a ohia sɛ bɛde nnwuma bata gyidie ho, ne deɛ ɔsɛ sɛ ɔyɔ adwuma Kristosom mu so dua paa.
MU NSƐM Nsɛm a odi kane : Kristoni ne sɔhwɛ :- Hia ne ahonya :- Amaneɛ ne sɔhwɛ :- Setie yɛ adepa :- Nyiyimu ho kɔkɔbɔ :- Gyidie ne nnwuma :- Kristoni ne ne kɛtrɛma :- Kristoni ne wiase :—: Nhyehyɛeɛ ahodoɔ :-
Nkyea Yakobo, Nyankopɔn ne Awurade Yesu Kristo akoa, twerɛ krataa yi de kɔma abusuakuo dummienu a bɛabɔ ahwete he de nkyea mma bɛ nyinaa.
Kristoni ne Sɔhwɛ Me nuanom, sɛ hohyia sɔhwɛ ahodoɔ biaa a, hommu no anigyeɛ, efiri sɛ honim sɛ, ho gyidie he sɔhwɛ yɛ boasetɔ ho adwuma.
Na homma boasetɔ nwie n’adwuma, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ho bewie honhom mu nyini na ho ayɛ pɛ, a bibiaa ɔnka.
Nyansa a ofiri Nyankopɔn Sɛ ho mu bi hia nyansa a, ma no mmisa Nyankopɔn a ɔma nnipa nyinaa adeɛ kwa na ahohora biaa nni mu he, na ɔde bɛma nipa korɔ he.
Na mmom ɔsɛ sɛ obisa no gyidie mu, a n’adwene ɔnyɛ no ntanta, efiri sɛ nea n’adwene yɛ no ntanta he te sɛ po asorɔkye a mframa bɔ no di akɔneaba.
Na mma saa nipa he nsusu sɛ obenya Awurade hɔ bibiaa; efiri sɛ, nipa a n’adwene yɛ no ntanta he hinhim n’akwane nyinaa mu.
Hia ne ahonya Ɔsɛ sɛ gyidini a ɔyɛ hiani he ma n’ani gye, efiri sɛ, ɔwɔ honhom mu ahonyadeɛ, na defoɔ a ɔnyɛ gyidini he mma ne werɛ nho, efiri sɛ, ɔbetwam akɔ sɛ wiram nhwiren.
Na sɛdeɛ awia de ne hyeɛ pie, na ɔhye wira mma ne nhwiren te tɔ, ma nhwiren he ahoɔfɛ sɛe he, saa ne defoɔ nso betwam akɔ berɛ a ogu so ɔɔyɔ ne nnwuma he.
Amaneɛ ne sɔhwɛ Nhyira ne nipa a ɔto ne bo ase sɔhwɛ mu.
Na sɛ otumi gyina sɔhwɛ berɛ he mu a, obenya nkwa abotire a Awurade ahyɛ bɔ sɛ ɔde bɛma bɛ a bɛdɔ no he.
Sɛ sɔhwɛ ba bi so a, mma onii he nka sɛ, “Nyankopɔn asɔ me ahwɛ”, efiri sɛ bi ntumi mfa bɔne nsɔ Nyankopɔn nhwɛ, na ɔno nso nsɔ bi nhwɛ.
Na mmom bi akɔnnɔ ne gyegye no, daadaa no na ɔsɔ onii he hwɛ; na sɛ saa akɔnnɔ he nyinsɛne a, ɔwo bɔne, na sɛ bɔne he nso nyini a, ɔwo wuo.
Me nuanom adɔfo, hommma bɛnnaadaa ho.
Akyɛdeɛ pa ne nnoɔma a ɔyɛ pɛ nyinaa firi soro, ofiri hann Agya he hɔ ne ba.
Ɔno ne nsakraeɛ anaa adanedaneɛ sunsum biaa nni ne mu.
Ɔnam n’asɛm a ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ so ne woo yɛ, sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ a ɔno ankasa ne pɛ bɛba mu, na yɛabɛyɛ sɛ n’abɔdeɛ mu aba a odi kane.
Asɛm he tie ne ne yɔ Anuanom adɔfo, honhu yei sɛ: Ɔsɛ sɛ nipa biaa yɔ krado wɛne n’aso tie asɛm; ɔnsɛ sɛ ɔpere ne ho kasa; saa nso ne ɔnsɛ sɛ ɔpere ne ho fa abufuo; efiri sɛ, abufuo nna Nyankopɔn tenenee mma.
Nti honto fi ne bɔne nyinaa ngu, na homfa ahobrɛaseɛ nye Nyankopɔn asɛm a bɛadua ne ho mu a obetumi agye ho kra nkwa he.
Honyɛ asɛm he yɔfoɔ, na mmom honnyɛ atiefoɔ kɛkɛ, nnaadaa ho ho.
Na sɛ bi tie asɛm he kɛkɛ na wamfa anni dwuma a, ɔte sɛ nipa a ɔhwɛ n’ anim ahwehwɛ mu; na sɛ ɔhwɛ n’anim na ofiri hɔ kɔ a, hɔaa na ne werɛ afiri sɛdeɛ na ɔteɛ he.
Nso deɛ ɔhwɛ mmara a ɔyɛ pɛ mu he, mmara a ɔma ahofadie he tena ne mu, ɔnyɛ tiefoɔ werɛfirefoɔ na mmom ɔyɛ deɛ otie na ɔyɔ, bebehyira no deɛ ɔyɔ nyinaa mu.
Sɛ bi dwene sɛ ɔyɛ nyamesomni, na woanto ne kɛtrɛma nnareka na mmom ɔdaadaa n’akoma a, na ne nyamesom he yɛ kwa.
Nyamesom a ho te na nkekaeɛ nni mu a Agya Nyankopɔn ani sɔ di: Sɛ bi bɛdwene nyanka ne akunafoɔ ho, bɛ ahohiahia mmerɛ mu, na ɔbɛte ne ho afiri wiase nkekaeɛ ho.
Nyiyimu ho kɔkɔbɔ Me nuanom a hoyɛ yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo a ɔyɛ animuonyam wura he mu agyidifoɔ he, ɔnsɛ sɛ honyɔ nyinyimu.
Sɛ nipa bi a ɔhyɛ sikakɔkɔɔ nkaa ne ataade-pa ba ho nhyiamu ase, na sɛ hiani bi nso a ɔnhyɛ ataade-pa nso ba hɔ a, na sɛ hohu deɛ ɔhyɛ ataade pa he na hoka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Mepa wo kyɛw, bɛtena ha,” na mmom hiani he deɛ hoka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Gyina hɔ,” anaa, “Tena me nane ase fam ha,” a na honyɔɔ nyiyimu ho mu anaa, na homfaa adwemmɔne mmu atɛne anaa?
Anuanom adɔfo, hontie!
Nyankopɔn nyii bɛ a wiasefoɔ bu bɛ sɛ ahiafoɔ he sɛ bɛnyɛ gyidie mu adefoɔ ne ahennie a ɔhyɛɛ ho bɔ ma bɛ a bɛdɔ no he ho adedifoɔ?
Nso hoabu saafoɔ he animtia.
Ɔnyɛ wiasefoɔ adefoɔ ne bɛhyɛ ho so he?
Ɔnyɛ bɛ ne bɛtwe ho kɔ asennibea he anaa?
Ɔnyɛ bɛ ne bɛka dini pa a bɛde frɛ ho he ho nsɛmmɔne he?
Sɛ hodi twerɛsɛm he mu adehye-mmara a ɔne sɛ, “Ɔsɛ sɛ wodɔ wo yɔnko sɛ wo ho” he so a, hoyɔ no yie.
Na mmom sɛ hoyɛ nyiyimu a, hoayɔ bɔne na mmara he bu ho atɛne sɛ hoyɛ mmaratofoɔ.
Na sɛ bi di mmara mũ he nyinaa so na ɔto baako a, waadi mmara he nyinaa ho fɔ, efiri sɛ, deɛ ɔkaa sɛ, “Nsɛe awareɛ” heaa nso ne kaa sɛ, “Nni awu.” Saa nti, nea ɔnsɛe awareɛ na nso odi awu he, yɛ mmara he tofoɔ.
Sɛ ɔte saa deɛ a, homma ho kasaa ne ho dwumadie nyɛ nea ɔfata nnipa a bɛde adehyedie mmara he bebu ho atɛne; efiri sɛ, atemmuo berɛ he, Nyankopɔn onhu biaa a wanhu afoforɔ mmɔbɔ he mmɔbɔ, nso mmɔborɔhunu di atemmuo so nkunim.
Gyidie a nnwuma nni mu he awu Anuanom, mmɛ mfasoɔ ne ya so sɛ bi bɛka sɛ ɔwɔ gyidie na onni nnwuma?
Saa nipa he gyidie betumi agye no nkwa anaa?
Sɛ wo nuabeema anaa wo nuabaa bi da adagya na onya n’ano aduane a, na ho mu baako ka kyerɛ no sɛ, “Fa asomdwie kɔ; wo ho nyɛ wo hye, na didi mee,” na woama no deɛ ohia honam fam a, mmɛ mfasoɔ ne ya so?
Saa ara ne gyidie nkoaa ya hɔ na onni dwuma a, na waawu.
Nso bi bɛka sɛ, “Wowɔ gyidie, na me nso mewɔ nnwuma.” Kyerɛ me wo gyidie a nwuma nka ho, na mede me nnwuma bɛkyerɛ wo me gyidie.
Wogyidi sɛ Nyankopɔn yɛ baako; woyɛ no yie.
Mpo ahonhommɔne nso gye saa di, na bɛ ho popo.
O!
nipa hunu, nti wopɛ sɛ bi ne nna no adi nkyerɛ wo sɛ gyidie a nnwuma nka ho he awu anaa?
Ɔnnyɛ nnwuma mu ne bebuu yɛ nana Abraham bem mmerɛ a ɔde ne ba Isak maeɛ ya afɔrebokyia so he anaa?
Woahu sɛ ne gyidie ne ne nnwuma nyinaa bom yɔɔ adwuma, na gyidie nam nnwuma so wiee pɛyɛ.
Na ɔnam so maa twerɛsɛm he baa mu sɛ, “Abraham gyee Nyankopɔn diiɛ, na Nyankopɔn buu ne gyidie he sɛ tenenee maa no,” na bɛfrɛɛ no Nyankopɔn adamfo.
Woahu sɛ ɔnam nnwuma nso so ma bebu bi bem, na ɔnyɛ gyidie nkoaa so.
Ɔnyɛ dwamamfoɔ Rahab nnwuma so ne bɛnam buu no bem, berɛ a ɔnam akwansrafoɔ a ɔgyee bɛ na ɔmaa bɛfaa kwane foforɔ so kɔeɛ he anaa?
Na sɛdeɛ nipadua a honhom nni mu he awu he, saa ara ne gyidie a nnwuma nni mu nso awu.
Kɛtrɛma dwodwoɔ Anuanom, hommpere ho ho nyɛ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ, efiri sɛ sɛnea honim he, bebebu yɛ a yɛyɛ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he atɛne a mu ɔdene; na yɛ nyinaa yɔ mfomsoɔ bebree.
Nipa biaa a ɔnyɔ mfomsoɔ kasa mu he yɛ pɛ, na otumi to nipadua he nyinaa nnareka.
Sɛ yɛde nnareka to pɔnkɔ ano ma no yɔ setie ma yɛ a, yetumi ka aboa he kɔ faako a yɛpɛ.
Hwɛ hyɛne nso, ɔnam ne kɛseɛ nti mframa a mu ɔdene ne tumi pia no, nso bɛde bibi ketewa bi ne ka no ma deɛ hyɛnkafoɔ he pɛ sɛ ɔkɔ biaa odi so.
Saa ne kɛtrɛma nso teɛ, ɔyɛ honam akwaa a osua deɛ, nso ɔhoahoa ne ho nnoɔma akɛseɛ ho.
Hwɛ kwaeɛ kɛseɛ a gya ketewa bi tumi hye ne nyinaa!
Na kɛtrɛma te sɛ gya; ɔyɛ nipadua akwaa a ɔte sɛ kuro a amumuyɔ ahyɛ mu ma, efiri sɛ, ɔde nkekaeɛ ba nipadua he nyinaa ho, na ɔde gya to asetena kwane nyinaa mu, na amanehunu kuro he mu ne ɔsɔ gya he.
Na dasani tumi hyɛ ntɔteboa ne ntakraboa, mmoa a bɛwea ne bɛ a bɛya po mu nyinaa so.
Nipa tumi yɔ yei nyinaa nso kɛtrɛma deɛ, ontumi nnya ho ahohyɛsoɔ, kɛtrɛma yɛ ade bɔne a ɔyɛ werɛmfoɔ a awuduro ahyɛ no ma.
Ɔno ne bɛde hyira Awurade ne Agya he, na ɔnoaa nso ne bɛde dome nnipa a bɛayɔ bɛ sɛ Nyankopɔn nsɛso.
Ano korɔ heaa mu ne nhyira ne nnome firi ba.
Me nuanom, ɔnsɛ sɛ ɔba saa.
Nti nsuo korɔgyee ne nsuo a ahono betumi afiri nsuo aniwa korɔ mu aba anaa?
Me nuanom, sɛnea borɔdoma ntumi nso ngo aba he, na bobe nso ntumi nso borɔdoma aba he, saa ara nso ne asuti a ɔyɛ nkyenenkyene ntumi mma nsu pa. Nyansa ahodoɔ mmienu Ho mu hwane ne yɛ nyansafoɔ ne nimdefoɔ?
Ma no mfa n’abrabɔ pa nkyerɛ sɛ ɔdwo, na ofiri nyansa mu ne yɔ ne nnwuma.
Nso sɛ ahoɔyeya dendenndene ne pɛsɛmenkomenya ya ho akoma mu a, honnhoahoa ho ho na honnni torɔ ntia nɔkorɛ he nso.
Saa nyansa yi mfiri soro, na mmom, ɔyɛ wiase nyansa a mfasoɔ biaa nni mu na ofiri ahonhommɔne.
Na baabi a anibereɛ ne pɛsɛmenkomenya ya he, hɔ nso ne basabasa ne bɔne nyinaa bi ya.
Na nyansa a ofiri soro he deɛ, deɛ odi kane ne sɛ, ho te, na afei ɔpɛ asomdwie, ɔdwo, ɔwɔ asoɔmmerɛ, ɔwɔ nteaseɛ; ahummɔborɔ ne aba pa ahyɛ no ma, a ɔnyɛ nyiyimu anaa nyaatwom kwane biaa so.
Na begu tenenee aba asomdwie mu ma bɛ a bɛpɛ asomdwie.
Wiase Adamfofa Hefa ne kõ ne apereapereɛ a ɔya ho mu yi firi ba?
Omfiri ho akɔnnɔ a ɔne honam akwaa di ako ya ho mu he?
Hopɛ bibi nso honnya; nti ho di awu.
Ho anibere bibi nso honnya; nti hodi akõ ne apereapereɛ.
Honnya, efiri sɛ hommisa.
Hobisa nso ho nsa nka, efiri sɛ hobisa no kwammɔne so, sɛdeɛ hode bedi ho honam akɔnnɔ ho dwuma.
Ei awaresɛefoɔ!
Honnim sɛ wiase yi adamfofa yɛ tane a bɛ tane Nyankopɔn anaa?
Biaa a ɔpɛ sɛ ɔyɛ wiase adamfo yɛ Nyankopɔn tamfoɔ.
Anaa hosusu sɛ twerɛsɛm he ka no kwa sɛ, “Nyankopɔn twe honhom a ɔde adua yɛ mu he ho ninkunu?” Nso adom a ɔde ma he dɔɔso; nti ɔka sɛ, “Nyankopɔn si ahantafoɔ kwane, na ɔdom ahobrɛaseɛfoɔ.” Ne saa nti hommrɛ ho ho ase nhyɛ Nyankopɔn ase.
Honnsi bronsam kwane, na ɔbɛdwane afiri ho nkyɛne.
Hommɛne Nyankopɔn na ɔno nso bɛtwe abɛne ho.
Honhohoro ho nsa, na homma ho akoma mu nte, ho nnebɔnyɛfoɔ a ho adwene yɛ ntanta.
Hontwa adwo na hommɔ bena na honsu.
Homma ho anigyeɛ nnane benabɔ na ho ahosɛpɛ nso nane aboobodie.
Hommrɛ ho ho ase Awurade anim, na ɔbɛma ho so.
Atenyie ho kɔkɔbɔ Anuanom, honnnka nsɛmmɔne ntia ho ho.
Nipa biaa a ɔka asɛmmɔne tia bi he anaa obu bi atɛne he, ɔka asɛmmɔne tia mmara he na obu mmara he atɛne; nso sɛ wobu mmara he atɛne a, wonyɛ mmara he sodifoɔ, na mmom, woyɛ temmufoɔ.
Na Nyankopɔn ne yɛ mmarahyɛfoɔ ne temmufoɔ a obetumi agye nkwa na obetumi asɛe nso.
Na wo ne hwane a wobu bi atɛne?
Mfa kyena nhoahoa wo ho Mhõõ, afei ho nso ɛ!
Ho a hoka sɛ, “Nnɛ anaa kyena yɛbɛkɔ kuro yei anaa foforɔ so na yɛadi afe hɔ, adi dwa na yɛapɛ sika,” nso honnnim adekyeeɛ mu nsɛm.
Honnim nea obesi ho nkwa ho?
Hote sɛ huhuo a ɔya hɔ mmerɛ tiaa bi na ɔyera.
Nea ɔsɛ sɛ ho ka mmom ne sɛ, “Sɛ ɔyɛ Awurade pɛ a, yɛbɛtena ase ayɔ yei anaa yei.” Nso sɛdeɛ ɔteɛ yi, ho hoahoa ho ho ahantan kwane so; saa ahohoahoa he nyinaa yɛ bɔne.
Nti nipa biaa a onim deɛ ɔyɛ na wannyɔ he, ɔyɛ bɔne mma no.
Ahonyafoɔ a bɛhyɛ binom so ho kɔkɔbɔ Afei ho adefoɔ, honnyina yie, ɔnam amanehunu a ɔɔba ho so nti honsu na hommɔ bena.
Ho ahonyadeɛ he aporɔ, na nnwenweboa awe ho ntoma ne ho ntaadeɛ.
Ho sikakɔkɔɔ ne dwetɛ awe naakyee, na ne naakyee he bedi adanseɛ atia ho, na obɛhye ho honam sɛ gya.
Hoahyehyɛ agyapadeɛ ama nna a odi akyire yi.
Hontie!
Apaafoɔ a bɛyɔɔ ho afuom adwuma a hosisii bɛ faa bɛ akatua he ɔɔteam gu ho so, na Awurade a ɔya soro he aso ate atwafoɔ a betwaa ho nnɔbae he nteamu.
Hode asetena pa ne ahohwie atena asaase yi so; hoama ho akoma adɔre sradeɛ ama kũ da.
Hoabu teneneeni fɔ na hoaku no a onsi ho kwane.
Amanehunu mu aboterɛ Nti adɔfonom, honto ho bo ase nkosi sɛ Awurade bɛba.
Kuani a ɔhwɛ ne nnɔbae a ofiri asaase mu ba kwane he nya ntoboaseɛ kosi sɛ obenya sukane ne berempɔnsuo.
Saa na ɔsɛ sɛ ho nso hoto ho bo ase.
Honhyɛ ho akoma dene, efiri sɛ Awurade maeɛ he abɛne.
Adɔfonom, honngu ahome ntietia ho ho ho ho, na bɛammu ho atɛne.
Honhwɛ, temmufoɔ he gyina aboboɔ he ano!
Adɔfonom, homma adiyifoɔ a bɛkasaa Awurade dini mu he nyɛ nhwɛsoɔ ma ho ya amanehunu ne boasetɔ ho.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, yebu bɛ a behuu amane, too bɛ bo ase ya amanehunu mu he sɛ bɛwɔ anigyeɛ amapa.
Hoate Hiob amanehunu mu boasetɔ ho asɛm, na hoahu Awurade botae, sɛdeɛ ɔyɛ ayamyefoɔ ne mmɔborɔhunufoɔ he.
Ne nyinaa mu he, adɔfonom, honnka soro anaa asaase ntam, anaa ntam foforɔ biaa, na mmom, homma ho ɛɛ, nyɛ ɛɛ, na ho Daabi nso nyɛ daabi, na hoankɔ afobuom.
Gyidie mpaebɔ Bi ya ho mu a ohu amane anaa?
Homma no mmɔ mpaeɛ.
Bi ani agye anaa?
Homma no nto ayeyie nnwom.
Bi ya ho mmu a ɔyare anaa?
Homma no mfrɛ asafo he mu mpayimfoɔ na bɛmmɔ mpaeɛ mma no, na bɛnsra no ngo Awurade dini mu.
Na gyidie mpaebɔ bɛgye yarefoɔ he nkwa, na Awurade bɛmma no so; na sɛ woayɔ bɔne bi a, ɔde bɛkyɛ no.
Ne saa nti honkeka ho mfomsoɔ nkyerɛkyerɛ ho ho ho ho, na hommɔ mpaeɛ ma ho ho ho ho, na hoanya ayaresa.
Teneneeni mpaebɔ a mu ɔdene tumi yɔ nnoɔma bebree.
Na Elia yɛ nipa te sɛ yɛaa, nso ɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ dendene sɛ nsuo ntɔ, na mfie mmeɛnsa ne bosome nsia nsuo antɔ asaase yi so.
Na afei, ɔbɔɔ mpaeɛ bio, na soro maa nsuo na asaase nso sõõ n’aba.
Anuanom, sɛ ho mu bi mmane firi nɔkorɛ he ho na foforɔ de no sane ba kwanpa he so a, ɔsɛ sɛ hohu sɛ bi a ɔdane debɔnyɛni firi ne kwammɔne so he bɛgye debɔnyɛni he kra afiri wuom na ɔbɛkata bɔne bebree so.
NNIANIMU Petro krataa a odi kane he, ɔtwerɛ kɔmaa Akristofoɔ a ɔfrɛɛ bɛ sɛ “nnipa a Nyankopɔn ayi bɛ,” na bɛabɔ ahwete ya Asia Kumaa atifi fam.
Ne botaeɛ titire ne sɛ, ɔbɛhyɛ n’akenkanfoɔ nkurane, bɛ a berɛ he mu, esiane bɛ gyidie nti behuu amane ya taa mu.
Twerɛfoɔ he kae n’akenkanfoɔ he sɛ, asɛmpa a ɔfa Yesu Kristo a, ne wuo, ne wusɔreɛ mu ne bɔhyɛ a ɔfa ne mmaeɛ ho ma bɛ anidasoɔ he ho.
Esiane yeinom nyinaa nti bennya boasetɔ nnye ntom, mfa amanehunu mu.
Bennya awerɛhyɛmu sɛ ɔyɛ deɛ bɛde ɔsɔ bɛ gyidie mapa ahwɛ, na bebenya akatua “da a Yesu Kristo beyi ne ho adi he” .
Deɛ twerɛfoɔ he de ka ne nkuranhyɛ ya haw berɛ mu ho ne sɛ, otuu bɛ fo sɛdeɛ bɛbɛtena ase sɛ Kristo nkurofoɔ.
MU NSƐM Nsɛm a odi kane :- Nyankopɔn nkwagyeɛ ho nkaeɛ :- Kronkronyɛ ho afotuo :—: Kristoni asɛdeɛ amanehunu berɛ mu :—: Kristoni ahobrɛaseɛ ne som :- Awieeɛ :-
Me Petro, Yesu Kristo somafoɔ, twerɛ saa krataa yi de kɔma Nyankopɔn nnipa a bɛayi bɛ a bɛahwete sɛ ahɔhoɔ kɔ Ponto, Galatia, Kapadokia, Asia ne Bitinia amantam mu he.
Ɔnam Agya Nyankopɔn botaeɛ so ne beyii ho, na ɔnam ne Honhom so tee ho ho sɛ honyɔ setie mma Yesu Kristo na ɔnam so ama ne mogyaa he ate ho ho.
Adom ne asomdwie mmorosoɔ nka ho.
Anidasoɔ a ɔya nkwa mu Nhyira nka yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo Nyankopɔn; saa Nyankopon yi ne yɛ n’Agya nso.
Esiane n’ahummɔborɔ pii nti, ɔnam nyane a onyanee Yesu Kristo firii wuo mu he so maa yɛ nkwa foforɔ.
Yei ama yɛanya anidasoɔ a atim, ne agyapadeɛ a ɔmporɔ a ho nni dɛm, na ɔmpa a bɛde asie soro ama ho.
Na Nyankopɔn bɛfa ne tumi he so ahwɛ sɛ honam gyidie so benya nkwagyeɛ a bɛasiesie sɛ bebeyi no adi berɛ a odi akyire he mu.
Ɔyam sɛ, ebia seesei ɔbɛba sɛ, esiane haw pii a hobɛfa mu he nti, ho werɛ bɛho deɛ, nso homma ho ani nnye saa asɛm yi ho, na ama bɛahu sɛ ho gyidie he yɛ kann, na ɔsombo kyɛne sikakɔkɔɔ mpo.
Sikakɔkɔɔ a betumi sɛe no he mpo, bɛde gya sɔ hwɛ, nti ho gyidie a ɔsom bo kyɛne sikakɔkɔɔ he, ɔsɛ sɛ bɛsɔ hwɛ hu sɛ, obetumi agyina anaa.
Ɔno akyi ansa na da a Yesu Kristo bɛba he, hoanya animuonyam.
Ɔyam sɛ honhu Yesu seesei yi deɛ, nso hodɔ no.
Honhuu no da, nso hogye no di, na ho ho siane ho anigyeɛ a onni kabea a animuonyam yam, sɛ honya ho gyidie akatua a ɔyɛ ho kra nkwagyeɛ he.
Saa nkwagyeɛ yi ne adiyifoɔ a bɛhyɛɛ adom a hobenya he ho nkɔm he de mmɔdemmɔ hwehwɛɛ mu pɛɛpɛɛ mu yie.
Bɛhwehwɛɛ berɛ korɔ ne berɛ ahodoɔ a Kristo honhom a ɔya bɛ mu dii kane daa no adi faa n’amanehunu ne akyire animuonyam a ɔbɛba he ho.
Nyankopɔn daa no adi kyerɛɛ saa adiyifoɔ he sɛ, ɔnyɛ bɛ ho ne bɛsomeeɛ na mmom ho ne bɛde nnoɔma a asie na bɛɛka ho asɛm he ɔɔsom ho.
Na akyire yiaa bɛada Asɛmpa he adi akyerɛ yɛ nyinaa.
Saa Honhom Kronkron he a bɛsoma no firii soro he tumi so ne bɛnam kasa kyerɛɛ bɛ; saa tumi heaa so ne bɛnam kasa kyerɛɛ yɛ nso.
Yeinom yɛ nnoɔma bi a abɔfoɔ mpo pɛɛ sɛ behu mu.
Abrabɔ kronkron Nti honsi ho adwene pi, na homma ho ani nna hɔ.
Honnyina yie, na homma ho ani nna adom a bɛde bɛma ho Yesu Kristo ba a ɔbɛba he mu he so.
Sɛ hoyɛ asoɔmmerɛ mma yi, ɔnsɛ sɛ homma akɔnnɔ abrabɔ a odii ho so berɛ a na honnim Nyankopɔn he di ho so bio, na mmom, ɔsɛ sɛ hoyɛ kronkron bibiaa a hoyɔ mu sɛnea Nyankopɔn a ɔfrɛɛ ho he yɛ kronkron he, na bɛatwerɛ sɛ, “Ɔsɛ sɛ hoyɛ kronkron, efiri sɛ, meyɛ kronkron.” Na sɛ hofrɛ deɛ ɔnhwɛ nnipa anim, na obu atɛne sɛdeɛ biaa adwuma teɛ he sɛ Agya a, homfa suro mmɔ ho bra ho ahɔhobea tenabea yi mu.
Sɛ honim sɛ bɛamfa nnoɔma a ɔporɔ, te sɛ dwetɛ anaa sikakɔkɔɔ ne gyee ho firii ho abrabɔ hunu a ho nya firii ho agyanom nkyɛne he mu, na mmom, bɛde Kristo a ɔte sɛ adwammaa a onni dɛm ne nkekaeɛ he mogyaa a ne boɔ ɔdene he ne gyee ho.
Ansa na Nyankopɔn bɔɔ wiase he, na waayi no dada, na ho nti ne nna a odi akyire yi he, wada no adi.
Ɔnam ne so ne hogyee Nyankopɔn a onyanee no firii awufoɔ mu na ɔmaa no animuonyam he diiɛ.
Ɔnam so ama ho gyidie ne ho anidasoɔ atim Nyankopɔn mu.
Afei a hoayɔ setie ama nɔkorɛ he de adwira ho kra ho ama hoanya nuadɔ a nyaatwom nni mu he, homfiri ho akoma nyinaa mu nnodɔ ho ho.
Na bɛamfiri aba a ɔporɔ mu, na mmom befiri nea ɔmporɔ mu, ɔne sɛ bɛnam Nyankopɔn asɛm a ɔte ase na ɔbɛtena hɔ he so ne awo bɛ foforɔ.
Sɛnea Twerɛsɛm he ka sɛ, “Nnipa nyinaa te sɛ serɛ; na bɛ animuonyam te sɛ nhwiren.
Serɛ he wu ma ne nhwiren he pre gu, nso Awurade asɛm he ya hɔ daa nyinaa.” Yei ne Asɛmpa he a bɛaka akyerɛ ho he.
Boɔ a Nkwa wɔ mu ne Mane Kronkron Hontwe ho ho mfiri bɔne nyinaa, nnaadaa nyinaa, nyaatwom, anibereɛ ne sɛ hooka nsɛm de agu nnipa ho fi, ho.
Honyɛ sɛ nkokoa a bɛɛpre honhom mu nofosuo kronkron anom na sɛ honom a, hoanyini akɔ nkwagyeɛ mu, efiri sɛ hoaka Awurade ayamyɛ he ahwɛ.
Hommra Awurade a ɔyɛ boɔ a nkwa yam he nkyɛne.
Ɔno ne nnipa poo no, na Nyankopɔn ani so deɛ ɔyɛ nea wayi no, na ɔsom bo he.
Ho nso hote sɛ aboɔ a nkwa yam a bɛnam so oosi honhom mu dane a ɔbɛyɛ asɔfokuo Kronkron a bɛnam Yesu Kristo so bɛbɔ honhom mu afɔdeɛ a ɔsɔ Nyankopɔn ani ya mu.
Na ɔya atwerɛ he mu sɛ: Hwɛ, mede tweaso tiboɔ a bɛayi he na ne boɔ ɔdene ato Sion, na deɛ ɔgye no di he ani onnwu.
Saa boɔ yi ho wɔ mfasoɔ yie ma ho a hogye di, na bɛ a bɛnnye nni he deɛ asɛm he abam sɛ: “Boɔ a abantofoɔ apo he, abɛyɛ tweasotiboɔ,” ne sintiboɔ ne sintiduatoɔ botane ama bɛ.
Bɛne besonti, efiri sɛ bɛanyɛ setie amma asɛm he.
Ɔno nti na beyii bɛ maeɛ.
Na ho deɛ, hoyɛ abusua a bɛayi ho, sɛ adehyeɛ asɔfokuo, mane kronkron, Nyankopɔn ankasa nkurofoɔ a bɛayi ho sɛ honka n’anwanwadwuma he ho asɛm.
Ɔno na ɔfrɛɛ ho firi sum mu baa ɔno ankasa hann nwanwasono he mu.
Nna bi a atwam he, na honnyɛ Nyankopɔn nkurofoɔ, nso afei, hoyɛ ne nkurofoɔ; nna bi a atwam he na honnim Nyankopɔn mmɔborɔhunu he, nso sɛsei deɛ, hoanya ne mmɔborɔhunu he.
Hontena ase sɛ Nyankopɔn nkoa Adɔfonom, mekasa kyerɛ ho sɛ ahɔhoɔ ne amamfrafoɔ a hoya wiase.
Hontwe ho ho mfiri honam akɔnnɔ a ɔne kra he di asie he ho.
Hommɔ bra pa ya amanamane mufoɔ a hofra bɛ mu he mu, na sɛ bɛka ho ho nsɛm sɛ hoyɛ nnebɔnyɛfoɔ a, bɛahu ho papa a hoayɔ he nso nam so ahyɛ Nyankopɔn animuonyam, “nsrada” he.
