Hommrɛ ho ho ase Awurade dini mu mma nnipa nhyehyɛeɛ nyinaa, sɛ ɔyɛ hempɔno anaa amradofoɔ a hempɔno he asoma bɛ sɛ bɛntwe nnebɔnyɛfoɔ aso, na bɛnkamfo bɛ a bɛyɛ papa he.
Na yei ne deɛ Nyankopɔn pɛ, sɛ hode papayɔ si nnipa a benni adwene he nkwaseasɛm ano.
Hontena ase sɛ nnipa a bɛde bɛ ho, na bɛmfa bɛ ahofadie he nyɔ bɔne biaa nso.
Na hontena ase sɛ Nyankopɔn nkoa.
Homfa anidie mma nnipa nyinaa.
Honnɔ anuanom agyidifoɔ.
Honsuro Nyankopɔn, na homfa anidie mma hempɔno.
Ho, nkoa nso, hommrɛ ho ho ase mma ho wuranom, na honnni bɛ a bɛ yam yɛ na bɛ tim ɔmmrɛ nkoaa ni, na mmom honni bɛ a bɛ tim ɔdene nso ni.
Nipa a ɔsɔ Nyankopɔn ani ne dea ɔnam Nyankopɔn ho ahonim nti, ɔde awerɛhoɔ hu amane a nka ɔnsɛ sɛ ohu, na ne nyina mu he, ogyina pintinn.
Na sɛ hoyɔ bɔne na bɛhwe ho, na honya ho boasetɔ a, mmɛ mfasoɔ ne hobenya?
Na mmom sɛ hoyɔ papa na hohu amane na honya ho boasetɔ a, Nyankopɔn behyira ho.
Na yei nti ne Nyankopɔn frɛɛ ho, efiri sɛ, Kristo he ankasa huu amanneɛ maa ho de saa nhwɛso he gya ho, sɛnea hobedi n’anammɔno akyi.
Ɔno na wanyɛ bɔne, na bɛanhu nnaadaa biaa nso n’anum.
Bedidii no atɛm he, wammua bɛ.
Ohuu amane he, wampoopoo n’ani, na mmom ɔde n’asɛm hyɛɛ deɛ obu atɛntenenee he nsa.
Kristo he ankasa soaa yɛ bɔne ya ne honam mu kɔɔ asennua he so sɛnea yebewu ama bɔne, na yɛatena ase tenenee mu.
Ne mmaa ntampeɛ mu ne hoanya ayaresa.
Na hote sɛ nwane a bɛayera nso afei deɛ, hoasane abedi ho kra Hwɛfoɔ ne Wɛmfoɔ he akyi.
Yerenom ne Kununom Saa nso ne ho, ayerenom, ɔsɛ sɛ hobrɛ ho ho ase ma ho kununom sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a sɛ bɛ mu bi nnye asɛm he nni a, ho subane pa he bɛtwetwe no ama no agye asɛm he adi, sɛ bebehu bɛbɛhwɛ ho abrabɔ a hoobɔ no tenenee ne nyamesuro mu he.
Hommma ho ahoɔfɛ nyɛ nnipa ani so deɛ te sɛ ti a hoayɔ no kyɛnkyerɛnn, anaa sika kaawa a hohyɛ anaa ntoma papa a hofira, na mmom homma ɔnyɛ akoma a hode dwoɔ ne honhom a ɔyɛ dinn asiesie no.
Ɔno ne sɔ Nyankopɔn ani.
Saa kwane yi so ne mmaa agyidifoɔ a bɛtenaa ase tete he a na bɛwɔ anidasoɔ Nyankopɔn mu he nam brɛɛ bɛ ho ase maa bɛ kununom, de kyerɛɛ bɛ ahoɔfɛ.
Sara yɔɔ saa.
Ɔyɔɔ setie maa Abraham, na ɔfrɛɛ no “Me wura.” Sɛ hoyɔ papa na hommma bibiaa mmɔ ho hu a, hedeɛ na seesei hoyɛ ne mmamaa.
Saa ne ho, kununom nso, ɔsɛ sɛ hodwene ho yerɛnom ho ya ho asetena mu.
Homfa anidie mma bɛ, na honhu sɛ bɛyɛ mmerɛ kyɛne ho, na afei nso honhu sɛ bɛne ho yɛ adedifoɔ, na bibi ansi ho mpaebɔ kwane.
N’awieeɛ ne sɛ, ho nyinaa hontena ase asomdwie mu.
Honnya tema mma ho ho ho ho.
Honnodɔ ho ho ho ho, na honyɛ ahummɔborɔ, na hommrɛ ho ho ase.
Hommfa bɔne ntua bɔne so ka, na hommfa yea nso ntua yea so ka.
Na mmom daa, honhyirahyira, efiri sɛ, ɔno ne bɛma ho anya nhyira.
Na deɛ ɔdɔ nkwa na ɔpɛ sɛ ohu nna pa he, ma no nyi ne kɛtrɛma mfiri bɔne mu, ne n’ano na anka nnaadaasɛm.
Ma no nkyiri bɔne na ɔnyɔ papa, ma no nhwehwɛ asomdwie na onni akyire.
Efiri sɛ Awurade ani ya bɛ a bɛtene so, na n’aso abie ama bɛ mpaebɔ, na bɛ a bɛyɔ bɔne deɛ, Awurade ani kyiri bɛ.
Sɛ wobɔ tenenee ho mmɔdene a, hwane ne betumi aha ho?
Na sɛ tenenee nti hohu amane mpo a, hoyɛ nhyira.
Honnsuro nnipa, na hommma hwee nnha ho.
Na mmom homfa anidie mma Kristo sɛ Awurade na honsom no ho akoma.
Honsiesie ho ho sɛ, berɛ biaa a bi bebisa gyidi a howɔ ya ho mu he ho asɛm he, hobɛkyerɛ no aseɛ dwoɔ ne anidie kwane so.
Honkura ahonim pa mu na bɛ a bɛka ho Kristo mu abrabɔ pa ho nsɛmmɔne he ani awu asɛm a bɛka tia ho he ho.
Na sɛ hohu amane papa ho na sɛ ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn pɛ sɛ ɔba saa a, ɔyɛ sene sɛ hohu amane ɔnam bɔne a hoayɔ nti.
Na Kristo nso huu bɔne ho amane prɛko; ɔno a ɔtene he wu maa abɔnefoɔ, na ɔde ho akɔ Nyankopɔn nkyɛne; ɔno na bekuu no honam mu nso, ɔnam Honhom he so sɔreeɛ, na ɔkɔkaa Asɛmpa he kyerɛɛ ahonhom a bɛdeda afiase a tete he bɛyɛɛ asoɔdenfoɔ, berɛ a Nyankopɔn abodwokyɛre twɛneeɛ, Noa nna a bɛɛyɔ adaka he mu.
Yei mu ne akra kakraa bi a bɛyɛ nwɔtwe nyaa nkwa nsuo no mu.
Ɔno na afei ne nsɛso a ɔno ne asubɔ he, gye ho nso nkwa, a ɔnyɛ honam ho fi yi mu, na mmom ɔyɛ ahonim pa ho adebisa a Yesu Kristo wusɔreɛ nti yɛnam so yɛ Nyankopɔn deɛ.
Saa Yesu yi ne kɔɔ soro na ɔte Nyankopɔn nifa, na bɛde abɔfoɔ ne bɛ a tumidie ahyɛ n’ase.
Fieahwɛfoɔ pa ya Nyankopɔn adom mu Esiane sɛ Kristo huu amane ne honam mu nti, ho nso homfa adwene korɔ heaa bi mfa nhyɛ ho ho dene.
Efiri sɛ, biaa a ohu amane honam mu he ne bɔne nni bibiaa yɔ.
Efiri seesei ɔɔkɔ he, ho nna a aka ya asaase so ha he, ɔsɛ sɛ Nyankopɔn ne di ho abrabɔ so, na mmom ɔnyɛ nipa akɔnnɔ.
Yɛ asetena berɛ a atwa mu he, yɛsɛe berɛ yɔɔ anyeaniefoɔ apɛdeɛ, sɛ yɛnantee ahohwie, akɔnnɔ, nsaboro, agobɔne, didimeeɛ ne abosonsom a bɛkyiri mu.
Seesei ɔyɛ anyeaniefoɔ he nwanwa sɛ ho ne bɛ mmɔ mu mmu ahuhubra bio, ɔno nti, bɛka ho ho nsɛmmɔne.
Nso bebebu bɛ ho nkonta akyerɛ Nyankopɔn a wasiesie ne ho bu ateasefoɔ ne awufoɔ atɛne he.
Saa nti ne bɛkaa Asɛmpa he kyerɛɛ awufoɔ, sɛdeɛ bebebu bɛ atɛne sɛ ateasefoɔ a bɛya honam mu, na bɛatena ase honhom mu sɛ Nyankopɔn.
Nnoɔma nyinaa awieeɛ abɛne.
Saa nti homma ho adwene mu nna hɔ, na ho ani nna hɔ mma mpaeɛ.
Ne titire koraa he, honnodɔ ho ho yie, efiri sɛ, dɔ kata bɔne nyinaa so.
Honyɔ ahɔhoyɛ a anwiinwii biaa nni mu.
Honhom mu adom a biaa anya he, onnyina so mfa nsom afoforɔ sɛ Nyankopɔn adom ahodoɔ he ho fie ahwɛfoɔ pa. Sɛ bi ɔɔka asɛm a ɔnka Nyankopɔn asɛm.
Biaa a ɔsom he, mfa ahoɔdene a Nyankopɔn de ma no he nsom sɛnea bibiaa mu, bɛbɛfa Yesu Kristo so ahyɛ Nyankopɔn a animuonyam ne tumi wɔ no daadaa he animuonyam.
Amen!
Amaneɛ a Kristo nti Behu Anuanom, hommma amanehunu a hoohu he nyɛ ho nwowa te sɛ nea hontee ho asɛm da.
Na mmom, homma ho ani nnye sɛ ho ne Kristo oohu amane sɛnea ho ani bɛgye na ho adi ahurusie da a n’animuonyam bɛda adi he.
Nhyira nka ho sɛ Kristo dini nti bɛya ho, efiri sɛ animuonyam honhom a ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn honhom he ya ho so.
Nso ɔnsɛ sɛ ho mu biaa hu amane sɛ wudifoɔ anaa korɔmfoɔ anaa dwotwafoɔ anaa sɛmpɛfoɔ.
Na sɛ hohu amane ya ho Kristosom ho a, hommma ho ani nwu na mmom, honna Nyankopɔn ase sɛ Kristo dini bata ho ho.
Na berɛ aduru sɛ bebu atɛne, na Nyankopɔn nkurofoɔ ne bebedi kane abu bɛ atɛne.
Na sɛ befiti aseɛ ya yɛ so a, mmɛ kwane so ne ɔbɛfa akɔ bɛ a bɛnnye Asɛmpa a ofiri Nyankopɔn nkyɛne he nni he nkyɛne?
Na sɛ, “ɔdene sɛ bɛbɛgye nipa pa nkwa a, hedeɛ bɛ a bɛnnye asɛm he nni ne nnebɔnyɛfoɔ he deɛ, mmɛ ne bɛba bɛ so?” Saa nti, bɛ a behu amane sɛnea Nyankopɔn ahyehyɛ he, ɔsɛ sɛ bɛde bɛ ho ma Bɔadeɛ nɔkwafoɔ he na bɛkɔ so yɛ papa.
Nyankopɔn nnwankuo so hwɛ Me a meyɛ asafo panyini he, metu asafo he mu mpanyimfoɔ fo sɛ, meyɛ Kristo amanehunu he ho dansefoɔ nti n’animuonyam a ɔbɛba he bɛka me.
Honyɛne nnwankuo a Nyankopɔn de bɛ ahyɛ ho nsa he, na honnyɔ no nhyɛ so, na mmom honyɔ no dɔ mu, sɛdeɛ Nyankopɔn pɛ; ɔnyɛ adufudepɛ nti, na mmom akoma pa mu.
Honnhyɛ bɛ a bɛde bɛ ahyɛ ho nsa he so, na mmom honyɛ nhwɛso pa mma nnwankuo he.
Na sɛ Dwanhwɛfoɔ panyini he ba a, bɛbɛma ho animuonyam ahenkyɛ a ɔnnsɛe da.
Saa ne ɔsɛ sɛ mmabunu, hobrɛ ho ho ase ma mpanyimfoɔ.
Ho nyinaa mfa ahobrɛaseɛ nkatanim mmɔ ho asene na honsom ho ho ho ho efiri sɛ, “Nyankopɔn si ahantanfoɔ kwane na ɔdom ahobrɛaseɛfoɔ.” Nti hommrɛ ho ho ase nhyɛ Nyankopɔn nsa a tumi ya mu he ase sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ɔbɛma ho so berɛ a ɔsɛ mu.
Homfa ho dadwene ne ho haw nyinaa nto ne so, efiri sɛ, ɔdwene ho ho.
Honsi sɔhwɛfoɔ he kwane Homma ho ani nna hɔ, na honwɛne, efiri sɛ, ho tamfoɔ bronsam he nam sɛ gyata a ɔɔbobom hwehwɛ nea obenya no amene.
Homfa gyidie nnyina hɔ pintinn nsi no kwane efiri sɛ, honim sɛ amanehunu korɔ heaa ne bɛde ato ho nuanom agyidifoɔ a bɛya wiase afanaa nyinaa so sɛ otwa sɛ behu.
Na adom nyinaa Nyankopɔn a wafrɛ ho aba ne daa animuonyam he mu Kristo mu he, ɔnoaa ne sɛ ho hu amane kakra, obesiesie ho pɛ; ɔbɛma ho ase atim.
Ɔbɛhyɛ ho dene; ɔbɛma ho anya nnyinasoɔ.
Ɔno ne tumi yɛ no deɛ daa daa.
Amen.
Nkradie ne nkyea Me nua gyidini Silwano ne boaa me ma metwerɛɛ saa krataa tiaa yi.
Mepɛ sɛ mehyɛ ho nkurane na medi adanseɛ sɛ, yei yɛ Nyankopɔn adom trodoo.
Honnyina mu pintinn.
Asafo a Nyankopɔn ayi no Babel he ne me ba Marko kyea ho.
Homfa dɔ nkyeakyea ho ho ho ho Kristo mu.
Asomdwie nka ho a hoya Kristo mu he nyinaa.
NNIANIMU Petro twerɛɛ krataa a ɔtɔ so mmienu he kɔmaa Akristofoɔ a na bɛdɔɔso a bedi kane a bɛbɔ hwete kɔɔ maa nyinaa he.
Ne botaeɛ titire paa ne sɛ ɔbɛko atia atorɔ nkyerɛkyerɛ ne abrabɔ bɔne a ofiri mu ba he.
Behu amaneɛ yi ho mmuaeɛ ya kura a bebekura Nyankopɔn ne Awurade Yesu Kristo nɔkorɛ nimdeɛ mu.
Yesu Kristo nɔkorɛ ho nimdeɛ yɛ nea bɛate firi nnipa bi a bɛ ankasa behuiɛ na betiee Yesu anum nkyerɛkyerɛ he.
Adeɛ titire a ɔha twerɛfoɔ he ne sɛ, binom kyerɛkyerɛ sɛ Yesu ɔnsane mma bio.
Ɔka sɛ deɛ ɔda adi pefee ya kyɛre a Kristo akyɛre ya ne mmaeɛ ho ne sɛ, “Nyankopɔn mpɛ sɛ nipa biaa bɛsɛe na mmom ɔpɛ sɛ biaa sakra firi ne bɔne ho.” MU NSƐM Nsɛm a odi kane :- Kristoni frɛ he :- Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ atorɔfoɔ :- Kristo mmaeɛ a otwa toɔ :-
Nkyea Simon Petro, Yesu Kristo akoa a ɔsane yɛ ne somafoɔ twerɛ krataa yi de kɔma bɛ a esiane yɛ Nyankopɔn ne yɛ Agyenkwa Yesu Kristo tenenee nti, bɛanya gyidie a ɔte sɛ yɛ deɛ heaa.
Adom ne asomdwie nnɔɔso mma ho, Nyankopɔn ne yɛ Awurade Yesu ho nimdeɛ mu.
Kristoni frɛ ne ne yie he Na Nyankopɔn nam ne tumi so akyɛ yɛ nnoɔma a ɔfa nkwa ne nyamesom-pa ho nyinaa, nea ɔnam ɔno ankasa ne ho nimdeɛ so afrɛ yɛ aba ɔnoaa n’animuonyam ne ne mmaninyɛ mu.
Yeinom so ne ɔnam ama ne bɔhyɛ akɛseɛakɛseɛ a ɔsombo he aba mu ama yɛ, na honam yeinom so adwane akɔnnɔ mu porɔeɛ a ɔya wiase; na hoanya Nyankopɔn su he bi.
Ne saa nti, hommɔ mmɔdene mfa nneyɔeɛ a ho te nka ho gyidie ho; na homfa nimdeɛ nka nneyɔeɛ pa ho; na homfa ahohyɛsoɔ nka nimdeɛ ho; na homfa boasetɔ nka ahohyɛsoɔ ho; na homfa nyamesom pa nka boasetɔ ho; na homfa nuadɔ nka nyamesom pa ho; na homfa dɔ mapa nka nuadɔ ho.
Na sɛ yeinom ya ho mu na ɔdɔɔso a, ɔmmma honyɛ mmerɛ anaa nnipa a bɛnso aba yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo fam.
Na deɛ onni yeinom he, ɔte sɛ nifirani a ontumi nhu adeɛ a ne werɛ afiri sɛ bɛahohoro ne bɔne dadaa he.
Nti me nuanom, homfa mmɔdemmɔ nsi frɛ a bɛafrɛ ho ne yi a bɛayi ho he pi; na sɛ hoyɔ saa a, honnsonti da.
Sɛ hofa saa kwane yi so a, hobenya akwannya kɛseɛ paa a hode bɛkɔ yɛ Awurade ne yɛ Agyenkwa Yesu Kristo ahennie a otim hɔ daa he mu.
Ne saa nti, daa mekaekae ho saa asɛm yi a honim na atim nɔkorɛ a hoagye adi he mu he.
Nso megye di sɛ, ohia sɛ mmerɛ tentene a mete ase yi, mebɔ ho nkaeɛ kanyane ho saa asɛm yi ho.
Menim sɛ ɔnnkyɛre biaa na matoa nananom nseɛdo sɛnea yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo daa no adi kyerɛɛ me he.
Nso mɛbɔ mmɔdene na me wuo akyi he, hoatumi akae yeinom da biaa.
Kristo animuonyam hyerɛn ho adansedie Ɔnyɛ anansesɛm a bɛanwene ne yɛto kyerɛɛ ho berɛ a yɛkaa yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo tumi ne ne ba he ho asɛm kyerɛɛ ho he, na mmom yɛde yɛ ani kann huiɛ n’animuonyam, na ɔno ho ne yedii adanseɛ kyerɛɛ ho.
Na berɛ a onyaa anidie ne animuonyam firi Agya Nyankopɔn hɔ na nne bi firi animuonyam kɛseɛ mu kaa sɛ, “Yei ne me dɔ Ba a ɔsɔ m’ani he,” yɛ ankasa yɛtee nne he sɛ ofiri soro ɔɔba berɛ a na yɛne no ya bepɔ kronkron he so he.
Yei ahyɛ adiyifoɔ ne nkɔmhyɛsɛm he mu dene ama yɛ.
Ɔsɛ sɛ hotie no yie, efiri sɛ, ɔte sɛ kanea a ɔhyerɛn sum mu kosi sɛ adeɛ bɛkye ama anɔpa nsoromma ahyerɛn ho akoma mu.
Na deɛ odi kane koraa he, honhu sɛ adiyisɛm biaa nni hɔ a nipa dasani betumi de ɔnoaa n’adwene akyerɛ aseɛ, efiri sɛ adiyisɛm biaa nni hɔ a ofiri nipa nyansa mu ne baeɛ, na mmom Honhom Kronkron he ne nam nnipa he so kaa asɛm a ofiri Nyankopɔn nkyɛne.
Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ atorɔfoɔ ne bɛ asotwe Nso, atorɔ adiyifoɔ sɔree bɛ mu, sɛdeɛ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ atorɔfoɔ bɛsɔre ho nso ho mu, awiawia bɛ ho abɛkyerɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ bɔne a nɔkorɛ nni mu, na bɛapo owura he a ɔgyee bɛ he sɛ bɛ Awurade, na ɔnam so ama sɛeɛ aba bɛ so prɛko pɛ he.
Nnipa bebree bɛfa akohwibra so; na esiane nea bɛyɔ he nti, nnipa bɛkasa atia nɔkorɛ kwane he.
Saa atorɔ adiyifoɔ yi nam bɛ adufudepɛ so bɛka nnaadaasɛm akyerɛ ho de apɛ ho ho mfasoɔ.
Na bɛ deɛ bɛ atemmuo a ɔya hɔ firi teteete he ntwentwɛne ase, saa nso ne bɛ sɛefoɔ he nso gyina bɛ aboboa ano pɛɛ.
Nyankopɔn amfa abɔfoɔ a bɛyɔɔ bɔne he ho ankyɛ bɛ.
Ɔtoo beguu Asamando amanehunu bunu mu, guu bɛ nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn, na hɔ ne bɛɛtwɛne atemmuo da he.
Na sɛ Nyankopɔn amma kane wiase he amfa ne ho anni, na mmom Noa a ɔyɛ tenenee sɛnkafoɔ ne nnipa nson a bɛka ne ho ne ɔgyee bɛ, na ɔde nsuhyiri bɛkataa amumuyɔfoɔ wiase he so; na afei nso, sɛ ɔhyee Sodom ne Gomora nkuro ma no danee nsõ, na ɔde sɛeɛ buu bɛ fɔ hyee bɛ ase de bɛ yɔɔ nhwɛsoɔ maa bɛ a akyire yi bɛbɛyɛ amumuyɔdeɛ, na ɔgyee Lot a ɔyɛ teneneeni he firii nnipa nnebɔnyɛfoɔ bɛde akohwibra haa no he nsam (na saa teneneeni he te saa nnipa nnebɔnyɛfoɔ he mu na afideɛ a na saa nnipa he yɔ no adekyeɛ ne adesaeɛ he ha no yie) a, hedeɛ na Awurade nim kwane a ɔbɛfa so agye n’akyidifoɔ afiri haw mu, na wama bɛatwe bɛ a bɛntene aso de akosi atemmuo da he, ne titire he, bɛ a bedi bɛ honam akɔnnɔ akyi na bebu Nyankopɔn tumi he animtia.
Saa atorɔ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ yi yɛ aniɔdenfoɔ ne ahopɛfoɔ, bensuro sɛ bɛbɛkasa atia animuonyamfoɔ henom.
Na abɔfoɔ a bɛwɔ ahoɔdene ne tumi sene saa atorɔ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ yi mpo nka nsɛmmɔne mmu bɛ atɛne Awurade anim.
Na yeinom deɛ, bɛte sɛ mmoa a benni adwene a bɛ su ne sɛ bɛawo bɛ sɛ bɛnkye bɛ nsɛe bɛ.
Bɛka deɛ bennim ho nsɛmmɔne, bɛbɛfa bɛaa bɛ sɛeɛ kwane so akɔ sɛeɛ mu, na bebenya bɛ nnebɔne so akatua.
Nea bebu no anigyeɛ ne daa akohwie asetena, bɛyɛ nkekaeɛ ne dɛm, na nea bɛ ani gye hoaa ne sɛ bɛde atorɔ nkyerɛkyerɛ bɛdaada ho berɛ a bɛ ne ho bom didi he.
Bɛwɔ ani a awaresɛeɛ ahyɛ no ma a ontumi nkwati bɔne.
Bɛdaadaa nnipa a bɛyɛ mmerɛ kɔ bɔne mu.
Bɛwɔ akoma a anibereɛ ahyɛ no ma.
Bɛyɛ nnomee mma.
Bɛamane afiri kwane pa he so nti bɛayera.
Bɛafa kwane a Beor ba Bileam a ɔpɛ ne mfasoɔ kwammɔne so, na bɛkaa n’anim ne bɔne he ho.
N’afunumu de nipa nne kasaeɛ de sii diyifoɔ he abɔdamsɛm he ho kwane.
Yeinom yɛ mmura a nsuo nni mu, bosuo a mframa bɔ huu de kɔ, bɛne bɛde sum kabii asie bɛ.
Na bɛkeka akokurokosɛm a mfasoɔ biaa nni so, na bɛnam honam akɔnnɔ ne ahohwie so to bɛ a afei ne bɛatete bɛ ho afiri nnebɔnyɛfoɔ ho he mmradɛ.
Atorɔ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ he hyɛ bɛ bɔ sɛ bɛbɛma bɛ ahofadie, nso bɛ ankasa deɛ bɛyɛ porɔeɛ nkoa efiri sɛ nipa biaa yɛ akoa ma bibiaa a odi ne so.
Na sɛ nipa sua yɛ Awurade ne yɛ Agyenkwa Yesu Kristo ho nsɛm, na ɔnam so dwane firi wiase yi mu akwammɔne so, na akyire yi ɔkɔ bɔne mu bio ma ɔdane bɔne akoa a, hedeɛ na tebea a ɔyam seesei he aseɛ koraa sene kane deɛ he.
Sɛ saa nipa he nnim Kristo koraa a, nka ɔyɛ ma no sene sɛ obesua ne ho nsɛm na afei ɔbɛdane bɛ akyi akyerɛ mmara kronkron a ɔde maa no he.
Nea ɔbaa bɛ so he kyerɛ sɛ, saa bɛ yi yɛ nɔkorɛ: Kramane sane kɔ ne feɛ ho bio, na “prako a bɛadware no he nso kɔyantam ne ho atɛkyɛ mu.”
Awurade mmaeɛ ho bɔhyɛ Adɔfonom, yei ne krataa a ɔtɔ so mmienu a matwerɛ abra ho.
Metwerɛɛ ne mmienu nyinaa sɛ mede ɔɔbɛkae ho, de akanyane ho adwene, na hoakae nsɛm a adiyifoɔ kronkron he kaeɛ mmerɛ bi a atwam he ne mmara a efiri Awurade ne Agyenkwa a bɛde faa ho asomafoɔ so maa ho he.
Nea odi kane he, ɔsɛ sɛ hote aseɛ sɛ, nna a odi akyire he mu he, afedifoɔ a bedi bɛaa bɛ honam akɔnnɔ akyi de fɛwdie bɛba, abɛka sɛ, “Ɔhyɛɛ ho bɔ sɛ ɔbɛba.
Wanka saa?
Na afei ɔya he?
Yɛ nananom awuwu dadaada, nso bibiaa te sɛ nea ɔte firii adebɔ mfitiaseɛ!” Bɛboapa bu bɛ ani gu nɔkorɛ he so, ɔne sɛ, ofiri tete na Nyankopɔn kasaeɛ na bɛbɔɔ soro ne asaase, bɛbɔɔ asaase firi nsuo mu na bɛde nsuo ne yɔeɛ na bɛde nsuhyiri nso ne sɛee kane wiase he.
Nso soro ne asaase a ɔya hɔ seesei yi deɛ, bɛnam Nyankopɔn asɛm heaa so ɔɔkora ama gya asɛe no.
Bɛɛkora ama da a bebebu nnebɔnyɛfoɔ atɛne na bɛasɛe bɛ he.
Na, adɔfonom, hommma ho ani mpa nɔkwasɛm yi so sɛ, Awurade ani so he, da koro te sɛ mfie apem, na mfie apem nso te sɛ da koro.
Awurade ntwentwɛne ne nane ase ne bɔ a wahyɛ ho sɛnea binom dwene he.
Na nea ɔteɛ ne sɛ, ɔwɔ ho ho boasetɔ, efiri sɛ, ɔmpɛ sɛ biaa bɛyera, na mmom ɔpɛ sɛ biaa nya adwensakra.
Na Awurade da he bɛba mpofirem te sɛ korɔmfoɔ ɔɔba he.
Saa da he, soro bɛbobom dendene na ayera, na wiem nnoɔma bɛhye na asɛe, na bɛapa asaase ne so nnwuma nyinaa nso ho ntoma.
Sɛ saa kwane yi so ne bɛbɛfa asɛe ade nyinaa deɛ a, hedeɛ abɛ nnipa ne ɔsɛ sɛ hoyɛ ya abrabɔ kronkron ne nyamesom pa mu, berɛ a hootwɛne na hoopɛ sɛ Nyankopɔn da he ba ntɛm yi?
Ɔno mu ne soro bɛsɔ gya asɛe, na wiem mfitiasedeɛ anane ahye.
Nso sɛnea ne bɔhyɛ teɛ he, yɛɛtwɛne soro foforɔ ne asaase foforɔ a tenenee ahyɛ mu ma he.
Afotuo a odi akyire ne awieeɛ Nti, adɔfonom, hogu so ɔɔtwɛne da he yi, hommɔ mmɔdene sɛ hobɛyɛ nnipa kronkron a mfomsoɔ biaa nni ho ho ya Nyankopɔn anim na ho ne no atena asomdwie mu.
Na honkae sɛ Awurade boasetɔ he kyerɛ nkwagyeɛ te sɛ nea yɛ nua Paulo nam nyansa a Nyankopɔn de maa no he so twerɛɛ ho he, sɛdeɛ ɔfa so twerɛ ne nkrataa nyinaa he, na saa nsɛm yiaa so nso ne ogyina twerɛeɛ.
Nsɛm bi a mu ɔdene ya ne nkrataa he mu a bɛ a bensuaa adeɛ na bɛ ase ntimiiɛ ntumi nkyerɛ aseɛ yie, sɛnea Twerɛsɛm a aka he nso bɛnkyerɛ aseɛ yie ma ɔde sɛeɛ bra bɛ he.
Nso, adɔfonom, ho deɛ honim yei dada.
Honhwɛ ho ho so yie, na bɛ a benni mmara so annaadaa ho ama hoamfiri ho tim a hoatim he mu anhwe ase.
Na honyini ya yɛ Awurade ne Agyenkwa Yesu Kristo adom ne nimdeɛ mu.
Ɔno ne animuonyam nka no seesei ne daa.
Amen.
NNIANIMU Yohane krataa a odi kane he wɔ botaeɛ mmienu: Nkuranhyɛ a ɔhyɛ n’akenkanfoɔ sɛdeɛ ɔbɛyɛ na bɛatena ase ya Nyankopɔn ne ne ba Yesu Kristo ayɔnkofa mu.
Ɔsane bɔ yɛ kɔkɔ fa atorɔ nkyerɛkyerɛ a obetumi asɛe saa ayɔnkofa yi ho.
Saa nkyerɛkyerɛ yi nnyinasoɔ ne sɛ, wiase mu nkitahodie de bɔne ba.
Yei nti Yesu a ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn Ba he ntumi mma honam mu.
Nkyerɛkyerɛ yi kɔ soaa ka sɛ, nkwagyeɛ ne sɛ bi beyi ne ho afiri wiase asetena mu nsɛm ho.
Ɔka nso sɛ, nkwagyeɛ mfa abrabɔ pa anaa dɔ a yɛde dɔ yɛ mfɛfoɔ ho.
Deɛ twerɛfoɔ yi ka no pefee de tia saa nkyerɛkyerɛ yi, ka sɛ, Yesu Kristo aba honam mu sɛ nipa ankasa.
Osi so dua nso sɛ, biaa a ɔgye Yesu he na ɔdɔ Nyankopɔn he, ɔsɛ sɛ ɔdɔ ne yɔnko nso.
MU NSƐM Nsɛm a odi kane :- Hann ne sum :—: Nyankopɔn mma ne Bronsam mma :- Nɔkorɛ ne Torɔ :- Dɔ asɛdeɛ :- Nkunimdie gyidie :-
Nea na ɔya hɔ firi mfitiaseɛ, nea yɛate, nea yɛde yɛ ani ahu, nea yɛhwɛɛ no yie na yɛde yɛ nsa kaeɛ a ɔfa nkwa asɛm he ho he, ampa, nkwa he daa ne ho adi kyerɛɛ yɛ, na yɛahu a yeedi ho adanseɛ, na yɛɛka daa nkwa a ɔya Agya he nkyɛne a bɛdaa no adi kyerɛɛ yɛ he ho asɛm akyerɛ ho, nea yɛahu na yɛate he ne yɛɛka akyerɛ ho nso, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ho ne yɛ benya ayɔnkofa.
Bio nso saa ayɔnkofa yi ya yɛne Agya he ne ne Ba Yesu Kristo ntam.
Yɛɛtwerɛ yei sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a yɛ anigyeɛ bewie pɛyɛ.
Hann mu asetena ne bɔneka Afei, yei ne asɛm a yɛate afiri ne Ba he nkyɛne a yɛɛbɔ ho amanneɛ: Nyankopɔn yɛ hann a sum nni ne mu koraa.
Na sɛ afei yɛka sɛ yɛne no wɔ ayɔnkofa na saa berɛ koro heaa mu yɛnante sum mu a, na yeedi torɔ na yɛnnante nɔkorɛ he mu.
Na sɛ yɛnante hann he mu sɛnea ɔno nso nante mu he a, hedeɛ na yɛ ne yɛ ho yɛ ho wɔ ayɔnkofa, na ne Ba Yesu he mogyaa te yɛ ho firi bɔne nyinaa ho.
Sɛ yɛka sɛ yenni bɔne a, na yɛdaadaa yɛ ho, na nɔkorɛ he nni yɛ mu.
Na sɛ yɛka yɛ bɔne kyerɛ Nyankopɔn a, ɔyɛ nɔkwafoɔ ne teneneeni sɛ ɔde yɛ bɔne bɛkyɛ yɛ, na wate yɛ ho afiri nea ɔntene nyinaa ho.
Sɛ yɛka sɛ yɛnyɔɔ bɔne a, yɛma Nyankopɔn yɛ torɔfoɔ, na n’asɛm he nni yɛ mu.
Wiase Agyenkwa Me mma nkumaa, meetwerɛ yei abra ho na aboa ho ama hoanyɔ bɔne; na sɛ bi yɔ bɔne a, yɛwɔ kamafoɔ bi ya Agya he nkyɛne, ɔno ne Yesu Kristo teneneeni he.
Na Kristo he ankasa ne yɛ yɛ bɔne ho mpatadeɛ, na ɔnyɛ yɛ bɔne nkoaa, na mmom wiase nyinaa bɔne nso.
Adeɛ paa a ɔkyerɛ sɛ yennim Nyankopɔn ne sɛ, yebedi ne mmara so.
Sɛ bi ka sɛ, “Menim no,” na nso onni ne mmara so a, saa nipa he yɛ torɔfoɔ a nɔkorɛ he nni ne mu.
Na biaa a odi Nyankopɔn asɛm so he, ɔno mu ne Nyankopɔn dɔ he awie pɛyɛ.
Yei ne ma yenya ahotɔsoɔ sɛ yɛte ne mu.
Ɔsɛ sɛ biaa a ɔka sɛ ɔte ne mu he bɔ ne bra sɛ ɔnoaa pɛpɛɛpɛ.
Mmara foforɔ Adɔfonom, mmara a meetwerɛ abra ho yi nyɛ asɛm foforɔ.
Ɔyɛ mmara dadaa a hoate firi mfitiaseɛ heaa.
Mmara dadaa he yɛ adeɛ a hoate ho asɛm dada.
Nso, kwane bi so he, mmara a meetwerɛ abra ho yi yɛ foforɔ, na mu nɔkorɛ he da adi ya Kristo mu.
Sum he ootwam na hann trodoo he ahyɛ aseɛ ɔɔhyerɛn.
Biaa a ɔka sɛ ɔya hann he mu, nso ɔtane ne nua he da so ya sum mu.
Biaa a ɔdɔ ne nua he te hann mu, na bibiaa nni saa nipa he mu a ɔto bi sintidua.
Nso biaa a ɔtane ne nua he te sum mu.
Na ɔnam sum mu a onnim baabi a ɔɔkɔ, efiri sɛ, sum he afira n’ani.
Mma nkumaa, meetwerɛ ho krataa yi, efiri sɛ, ne dini nti, bɛde ho bɔne akyɛ ho.
Agyanom, meetwerɛ abra ho, efiri sɛ, honim nea ɔte ase firi mfitiaseɛ he.
Mmabunu, meetwerɛ abra ho, efiri sɛ, hoadi Bronsam so.
Mmɔfra nkumaa, meetwerɛ abra ho, efiri sɛ, honim Agya he.
Agyanom, meetwerɛ abra ho, efiri sɛ, honim nea ɔte ase firi mfitiaseɛ he.
Mmabunu, meetwerɛ abrɛ ho, efiri sɛ, howɔ nwentaasoɔ.
Nyankopɔn asɛm he te ho mu na hoadi bɔnefoɔ he so nkunim.
Wiase dɔ ne Nyankopɔn dɔ Honnnɔ wiase anaa bibiaa a ɔyɛ wiase deɛ.
Biaa a ɔdɔ wiase he, Agya he dɔ nni ne mu.
Na bibiaa a ɔyɛ wiase su, te sɛ, honam akɔnnɔ, ani akɔnnɔ, ne asetena mu ahoahoa, mfiri Agya he, na mmom ofiri wiase.
Na wiase ne n’akɔnnɔ ootwam, nso nea ɔyɔ Nyankopɔn apɛdeɛ he tena hɔ daa.
Nea ɔko tia Kristo Me mma nkumaa, awieeɛ he abɛne.
Bɛka kyerɛɛ ho sɛ Kristo-kotiafoɔ he bɛba, nso seesei, nnipa bebree aba a bɛko tia Kristo.
Yei nti yɛahu sɛ ampa awieeɛ he abɛne.
Nɔkwasɛm ne sɛ, befiri yɛ mu ne kɔeɛ deɛ, nso na benni yɛ afa, na sɛ bɛya yɛ afa a, nka bɛne yɛ tenaa hɔ.
Nso begyaa yɛ hɔ sɛnea bebehu no pefee sɛ benni yɛ afa.
Na ho deɛ, hoanya ngosra firi Kronkronni he hɔ, nti ho nyinaa howɔ nimdeɛ.
Ɔnyɛ sɛ honnim nɔkorɛ he nti ne meetwerɛ saa krataa yi, na mmom honim, na honim nso sɛ, torɔ biaa mfiri nɔkorɛ mu mma.
Afei, hwane ne torɔfoɔ he?
Torɔfoɔ he ne nea ɔka sɛ Yesu nyɛ Kristo he.
Ɔno ne Kristo-kotiafoɔ he.
Saa nipa he ne nea ɔpo Agya he ne Ba he nyinaa.
Na nea ɔpo Ba he po Agya he nso; nea ɔgye Ba he, gye Agya he nso.
Homma asɛm a hote no mfitiaseɛ he ntena ho mu.
Sɛ asɛm a hotee no mfitiaseɛ he tena ho mu a, ɔno ne hobɛtena Ba he ne Agya he mu.
Na yei ne wahyɛ yɛ ho bɔ he, nkwa a onni awieeɛ he.
Meetwerɛ ho afa bɛ a bɛpɛ sɛ bɛdaadaa ho he ho.
Na ho deɛ, ngosra a honyaa no ne nsa mu he te ho mu, nti onhia ho sɛ bi kyerɛkyerɛ ho; na mmom nea ngosra heaa kyerɛkyerɛ ho afa adeɛ nyinaa ho he, hontena deɛ wasra ho ngo he mu.
Na nea wakyerɛkyerɛ ho he yɛ nɔkorɛ, na ɔnyɛ torɔ!
Na afei, me mma nkumaa, hontena ne mu sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a sɛ oyi ne ho adi a, yebenya akokoɔduro na yɛmfa aniwuo nkohinta da a ɔbɛba he.
Nyankopɔn mma Sɛ honim sɛ ɔyɛ teneneeni a, honhu sɛ biaa a ɔyɔ ade tenenee he, Nyankopɔn ne awo no.
Nyankopɔn Dɔ Honhwɛ dɔ mmorosoɔ a Agya he de adɔ yɛ, sɛ bɛmfrɛ yɛ Nyankopɔn mma.
Na yɛyɛ ne mma nso.
Deɛ nti a wiase nnim yɛ he ne sɛ onnim no.
Me nuanom, seesei yɛyɛ ne mma nso nea daakye yɛbɛyɛ he nya nnaa adi.
Nso yenim sɛ, sɛ oyi ne ho adi a, yɛbɛyɛ te sɛ ɔno, efiri sɛ, yebehu no sɛnea ɔteɛ ankasa.
Na biaa a ɔwɔ saa anidasoɔ yi ne mu he te ne ho, sɛnea ɔno nso ho te he.
Biaa a ɔyɛ bɔne he to Nyankopɔn mmara, efiri sɛ, bɔne yɛ mmarato.
Honim sɛ ɔbaa sɛ oobeyi bɔne afiri hɔ, ɔno deɛ, bɔne biaa nni ne mu.
Nti nea ɔte ne mu he nkɔ so nyɔ bɔne.
Na biaa a ɔkɔ so yɔ bɔne he nhuu no, na onnim no.
Hommma bi nnaadaa ho, mma nkumaa.
Nea ɔyɔ nea ɔtene he yɛ teneneeni sɛnea ɔno nso yɛ teneneeni he.
Nea ɔkɔ so yɔ bɔne he yɛ Bronsam deɛ, efiri sɛ, Bronsam firi mfitiaseɛ pɛɛ ne yɔɔ bɔne.
Yei nti ne Nyankopɔn Ba he baeɛ: Ɔbaa sɛ ɔɔbɛsɛe Bronsam nnwuma.
Biaa a ɔyɛ Nyankopɔn ba he ntena bɔne mu, efiri sɛ, Nyankopɔn su ya ne mu na ɔnam sɛ Nyankopɔn awo no nti, ontumi ntena bɔne mu.
Nsosonoeɛ a ɔda Nyankopɔn mma ne Bronsam mma ntam ne sɛ, biaa a ɔnyɔ deɛ ɔtene anaa ɔnnɔ ne nua he mfiri Nyankopɔn.
Honnodɔ ho ho ho ho Na yei ne nsɛm a hoate firi mfitiaseɛ, sɛ honnodɔ ho ho ho ho.
Ɔnsɛ sɛ yɛyɔ sɛ Kain a na ɔyɛ Bronsam deɛ nti, okuu ɔno ankasa ne nua.
Na ɛɛne nti ne Kain kuu no?
Ɔyɔɔ saa efiri sɛ, ɔnoaa ne nnwuma a ɔyɔeɛ he, na ɔyɛ bɔne.
Nso ne nua he deɛ, ɔyɔɔ deɛ ɔtene.
Nti anuanom, sɛ wiasefoɔ tane ho a, hommma ɔnnyɛ ho nwanwa.
Yenim sɛ yɛatwam afiri wuo mu aba nkwa mu, efiri sɛ, yɛdɔ anuanom.
Nea onni dɔ he te wuo mu.
Nipa biaa a ɔtane ne nua he yɛ wudini, na honim nso sɛ wudini biaa nni daa nkwa ya ne mu.
Yei ne ma yehu sɛnea dɔ teɛ, sɛ ɔno de ne nkwa too hɔ maa yɛ.
Ɔsɛ sɛ yɛ nso yɛde yɛ nkwa to hɔ ma yɛ nuanom.
Sɛ bi yɛ defoɔ na ohu sɛ ne nua hia bibi, na wanhu ne mmɔbɔ a, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ na watumi aka sɛ ɔdɔ Nyankopɔn n’akoma mu?
Me mma nkumaa, hommma yɛmmfa ano anaa kɛtrɛma kɛkɛ nnɔ, na mmom homma yɛdɔ nna adi nneyɔeɛ ne nɔkorɛ mu.
Yei ne bɛma yɛahu sɛ yefiri nɔkorɛ he mu, na ama yɛ akoma atɔ yɛ yam Nyankopɔn anim, ya bibiaa a yɛ akoma bu yɛ fɔ mu, efiri sɛ, Nyankopɔn so sene yɛ akoma, na onim adeɛ nyinaa.
Nti anuanom adɔfo, sɛ yɛ akoma ammu yɛ fɔ a, hedeɛ na yɛde akokoɔduro kɔ Nyankopɔn anim.
Bibiaa a yebisa no he, yɛ nsa ka efiri sɛ, yedi ne mmara so na yɛyɔ nea ɔsɔ n’ani.
Na yei ne n’ahyɛdeɛ, sɛ yɛnnye ne Ba Yesu Kristo dini he nni, na yɛnnodɔ yɛ ho yɛ ho, sɛnea ɔhyɛɛ yɛ he.
Biaa a odi Nyankopɔn ahyɛdeɛ so he te Nyankopɔn mu, na Nyankopɔn nso te ne mu.
Na yei ne ma yehu sɛ Nyankopɔn te yɛ mu.
Na deɛ yɛde hu sɛ ɔte yɛ mu ne Honhom a ɔde ama yɛ he.
Honsɔ ahonhom he nhwɛ Adɔfo, honnye ahonhom nyinaa nnni, na mmom honsɔ ahonhom he nhwɛ sɛ befiri Nyankopɔn anaa; efiri sɛ, atorɔ adiyifoɔ bebree aba wiase.
Kwane a hobefa so ahu Nyankopɔn honhom di: Honhom biaa a ɔpae mu ka sɛ Yesu Kristo aba honam mu he firi Nyankopɔn.
Na honhom a ɔnka saa mfa Yesu ho he mfiri Nyankopɔn.
Saa honhom he yɛ Kristo-kotiafoɔ a hotee sɛ ɔbɛba he, na afei wanya aba wiase he.
Mma nkumaa, hoyɛ Nyankopɔn deɛ, na hoadi bɛ so nkunim, efiri sɛ, deɛ ɔya ho mu he wɔ tumi sene deɛ ɔya wiase mu.
Bɛkasa sɛ wiasefoɔ; wiase tie bɛ efiri sɛ, bɛyɛ wiase deɛ.
Nso yɛ deɛ, yefiri Nyankopɔn.
Biaa a onim Nyankopɔn he tie yɛ.
Na biaa a onnim Nyankopɔn he ntie yɛ.
Yei mu ne yehu nɔkorɛ honhom ne atorɔ honhom.
Nyankopɔn yɛ dɔ Anuanom, homma yɛnnodɔ yɛ ho yɛ ho, efiri sɛ, dɔ firi Nyankopɔn.
Nipa biaa a ɔwɔ dɔ he yɛ Nyankopɔn ba na onim Nyankopɔn nso.
Na nipa biaa a onni dɔ he nnim Nyankopɔn; efiri sɛ, Nyankopɔn yɛ dɔ.
Kwane a Nyankopɔn nam so daa ne dɔ adi kyerɛɛ yɛ ne sɛ: Ɔsomaa ne Ba koro he baa wiase, sɛnea yɛbɛfa ne so anya nkwa.
Yei mu ne dɔ he ya, ɔnyɛ sɛ yɛ ne yɛdɔɔ Nyankopɔn, na mmom ɔno ne dɔɔ yɛ na ɔnam so somaa ne Ba sɛ ɔmmɛyɛ yɛ bɔne ho mpatadeɛ.
Adɔfonom, sɛ saa ne Nyankopɔn dɔ yɛ deɛ a, hedeɛ ɔsɛ sɛ yɛ nso yɛdodɔ yɛ ho yɛ ho.
Biaa nhuu Nyankopɔn da.
Sɛ yɛdodɔ yɛ ho yɛ ho a, na Nyankopɔn te yɛ mu, na ne dɔ he awie pɛyɛ yɛ mu nso.
Nea ɔma yehu sɛ yɛte Nyankopɔn mu, na ɔno nso te yɛ mu ne sɛ, waama yɛ ne Honhom.
Yɛahu, na yedi adanseɛ sɛ Agya he somaa ne Ba ma ɔbɛyɛɛ wiase Agyenkwa.
Biaa a ɔpae mu ka sɛ Yesu yɛ Nyankopɔn Ba he Nyankopɔn te ne mu, na ɔno nso te Nyankopɔn mu.
Na yɛ ankasa yenim na yɛgye Nyankopɔn dɔ a ɔde dɔ yɛ he di.
Nyankopɔn yɛ dɔ, na biaa a ɔte dɔ mu he te Nyankopɔn mu na Nyankopɔn nso te ne mu.
Saa kwane yi so ne dɔ wie pɛyɛ yɛ mu, na ama yɛatumi akasa akokoɔduro mu atemmuda he, efiri sɛ sɛnea ɔteɛ he, saa nso ne yɛteɛ wiase yi mu.
Hu biaa nni dɔ mu, na mmom dɔ a odi mu he pam hu nyinaa, efiri sɛ, hu ne atemmuo ne nam, na deɛ osuro atemmuo he nwie pɛyɛ ya dɔ mu.
Yɛdɔ, efiri sɛ, Nyankopɔn ne dii kane dɔɔ yɛ.
Sɛ bi ka sɛ, “Medɔ Nyankopɔn” na ɔtane ne nua a, ɔyɛ torɔfoɔ, efiri sɛ, bi ntumi nnɔ Nyankopɔn a onhuu no, berɛ a ɔtane ne nua a ohu no he.
Yei ne ahyɛdeɛ a yɛanya no ne nkyɛne: nea ɔdɔ Nyankopɔn he, ɔsɛ sɛ ɔdɔ ne nua nso.
Gyidie di wiase so nkonim Nea ɔgye di sɛ Yesu ne Kristo he, Nyankopɔn ne awo no.
Biaa nni hɔ a ɔdɔ bi na ɔnnɔ saa nipa he ba nso.
Sɛ yɛdɔ Nyankopɔn na yedi n’ahyɛdeɛ so a, ɔnoaa ne yɛde hu sɛ yɛdɔ Nyankopɔn mma.
Dɔ a yɛdɔ Nyankopɔn he, kyerɛ di a yedi ne mmara so.
Na ne mmara he nso so di nyɛ adesoa mma yɛ, efiri sɛ, biaa a Nyankopɔn awo no di wiase so nkunim, na ɔnam yɛ gyidie so ama yɛadi wiase so nkunim.
Hwane ne betumi adi wiase so nkunim ka dea ɔgye di sɛ Yesu yɛ Nyankopɔn Ba he ho?
Nyankopɔn Ba he ho adansedie Yesu Kristo ne deɛ a ɔnam nsuo ne mogyaa so baeɛ.
Ɔnyɛ nsuo nkoaa so ne ɔnam baeɛ na mmom nsuo ne mogyaa so.
Na ɔyɛ Honhom he ne di ho adanseɛ.
Na Honhom he ne nɔkorɛ he.
Adansefoɔ mmeɛnsa ne di adanseɛ, Honhom, nsuo ne mogyaa.
Saa adansefoɔ yi adwene hyia.
Sɛ yɛgye nnipa adanseɛ di a adanseɛ a Nyankopɔn di he kyɛne no.
Na Nyankopɔn adanseɛ he ne adanseɛ a wadi afa ne Ba he ho.
Nti biaa a ɔgye Nyankopɔn Ba he di he wɔ saa adanseɛ yi ya n’akoma mu.
Na nea ɔnnye Nyankopɔn nni he ama Nyankopɔn ayɛ torɔfoɔ, efiri sɛ, wannye adanseɛ a Nyankopɔn di faa ne Ba he ho he anni.
Yei ne adanseɛ he: Nyankopɔn ama yɛ nkwa a onni awieeɛ; na saa nkwa he ya ne Ba he mu.
Biaa a ɔwɔ Ba he wɔ saa nkwa he, na biaa a onni Ba he nni nkwa he.
Meetwerɛ yei abra ho, ho a hogye Nyankopɔn ba he dini di he, na ama hoahu sɛ howɔ nkwa a onni awieeɛ.
Na nnam a yɛde kɔ ne nkyɛne ne sɛ, yɛsrɛ bibiaa sɛdeɛ ɔpɛ a, ootie yɛ.
Na sɛ yenim sɛ otie yɛ abisadeɛ a, hedeɛ, yenim sɛ nnoɔma a yɛasrɛ no ne nkyɛne he, yɛ nsa bɛka.
Sɛ bi hu sɛ ne nua ayɔ bɔne bi a ɔmfa no nkɔ wuo mu a, ɔmmɔ Nyankopɔn a ɔbɛma no nkwa he mpaeɛ mma no.
Yei ka bɛ a bɛ bɔne mfa bɛ nkɔ wuo mu he ho.
Bɔne bi ya hɔ a ɔde nipa kɔ wuo mu na ɔno ho deɛ, menka sɛ hommɔ ho mpaeɛ nkyerɛ Nyankopɔn.
Deɛ ɔntene nyinaa yɛ bɔne, na bɔne bi ya hɔ a ɔnkɔ wuo mu.
Yenim sɛ Nyankopɔn ba biaa ntena bɔne mu, efiri sɛ, nea Nyankopɔn awo no he hwɛ ne ho so yie, na bɔnefoɔ he ntumi mfa ne nsa nka no.
Yenim sɛ wiase nyinaa hyɛ bɔnefoɔ he tumi ase, nso yɛ deɛ yɛyɛ Nyankopɔn nkurofoɔ.
Na yenim sɛ Nyankopɔn Ba he aba, na waama yɛ nteaseɛ ama yɛahu Nyankopɔn trodoo he.
Yɛ abrabɔ ya Nyankopɔn trodoo he ne ne Ba Yesu Kristo he mu.
Yei ne Nyankopɔn trodoo he ne nkwa a onni awieeɛ he.
Me mma nkumaa, hontwe ho ho mfiri ahonyini ho.
NNIANIMU Nipa a ɔtwerɛɛ Yohane nwoma a ɔtɔ so mmienu he, bɛfrɛ no “Asafo Panyini.” Ɔde kɔmaa “Awuraa dɔfo bi ne ne mma” (obetumi akyerɛ sɛ asafo bi ne mu nnipa).
Asɛm tia a ɔya mu yɛ dɔ a bɛde bɛdɔ bɛ ho ne kɔkɔbɔ adesrɛ a ɔfa atorɔ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ ne bɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ ho.
MU NSƐM Ahyɛaseɛ nkyerɛkyeremu - Dɔ ne adeɛ a odi kane - Torɔ nkyerɛkyerɛ ho kɔkɔbɔ - Awieeɛ -
Nkyea Me, Asafo Panyini, twerɛ krataa yi de kɔma Awuraa a bɛayi no ne ne mma a medɔ bɛ nɔkorɛ he mu.
Ɔnyɛ me nkoaa, na mmom bɛ a benim nɔkorɛ he nyinaa nso dɔ ho, ɔnam nɔkorɛ he a ɔte yɛ mu na ɔbɛtena yɛ mu akosi daa daa he nti: Adom, mmɔborɔhunu ne asomdwie mfiri Agya Nyankopɔn ne Awurade Yesu Kristo, Agya he Ba he, nkyɛne mmra yɛ so nɔkorɛ ne dɔ mu.
Nɔkorɛ ne dɔ M’ani agye kɛse sɛ mahu sɛ wo mma he bi nam nɔkorɛ he mu sɛnea Agya he ahyɛ yɛ heaa.
Nti afei, Awuraa, meeka akyerɛ wo sɛ, yɛnnodɔ yɛ ho yɛ ho.
Yei nyɛ mmara foforɔ a meehyɛ ama wo, na mmom ɔyɛ mmara a yenya firii mfitiaseɛ heaa.
Na dɔ a meeka ho asɛm yi di: Sɛ yɛbɛnante sɛdeɛ ahyɛdeɛ he teɛ.
Yei ne ahyɛdeɛ a hote firii mfitiaseɛ he sɛ, honnante dɔ mu.
Na nnaadaafoɔ bebree aba wiase, nipa a bɛmpae mu nka sɛ Yesu Kristo baa honam mu.
Nipa biaa a ɔte saa he yɛ daadaafoɔ he ne nea ɔko tia Kristo he.
Honhwɛ ho ho so yie na hoanhwere nea hoayɔ ho adwuma, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ a hobenya ho akatua nyinaa.
Nipa biaa a ɔfom na ɔntena Kristo nkyerɛkyerɛ he mu he, onnim Nyankopɔn.
Na nea ɔtena nkyerɛkyerɛ he mu he, ɔno mmom ne nea onim Agya he ne ne Ba he.
Sɛ bi ba ho nkyɛne na wamfa saa nkyerɛkyerɛ yi ammra ho a, honnnye no nkɔ ho fie, na honnkyea no nka sɛ, “Asomdwie nka wo,” efiri sɛ, biaa a ɔde Nyankopɔn asomdwie bɛma no he nso de ne ho bata bɔne a saa nipa he yɔ he ho.
Awieeɛ Ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ sɛ, mewɔ nsɛm pii ka kyerɛ ho, nso memfa krataa ne twerɛdua so nka.
Na mmom, mewɔ anidasoɔ sɛ mɛba ne ho atena ase akasa, na yɛ anigyeɛ awie pɛyɛ.
Wo nuabaa a bɛayi no he mma he kyea wo.
NNIANIMU Deɛ ɔtwerɛɛ Yohane nwoma a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he, bɛfrɛ no “Asafo Panyini”.
Ɔde kɔmaa asafo mu panyini bi a bɛfrɛ no Gaio.
Twerɛfoɔ he yii Gaio ayɛ esiane mmoa a ɔde boa Akristofoɔ, na ɔbɔ no kɔkɔ nnipa bi a ne dini ne Diotrefe ho.
MU NSƐM Ahyɛaseɛ nkyerɛkyeremu - Asafo Panyini he yii Gaio ayɛ - Diotrefe afobuo - Diometrio ayeyie - Awieeɛ -
Nkyea ne ayeyie Me, Asafo Panyini, metwerɛ krataa yi de kɔma dɔfo Gaio a medɔ no nɔkorɛ mu.
Me dɔfo pa, mebɔ mpaeɛ sɛ adeɛ nyinaa mu, onsi wo yie, na nya ahoɔdene sɛnea asi wo kra yie he.
Berɛ a anuanom bi baeɛ na bebedii wo nɔkorɛdie ho adanseɛ sɛnea wonam nɔkorɛ he mu he, m’ani gyee paa.
Bibiaa nyɛ me anigye nkyɛne sɛ mɛte sɛ me mma he nam nɔkorem.
Me dɔfo pa, wodi nɔkorɛ yie adwuma a woyɔ ma anuanom, ahɔhoɔ mpo.
Bɛadi wo dɔ he ho adanseɛ asafo he anim.
Mesrɛ wo, ma nea wode begya bɛ kwane he nyɛ adeɛ a ɔbɛsɔ Nyankopɔn ani, efiri sɛ, Kristo dini mu ne bɛnam, na bɛnhwehwɛ mmoa biaa mfiri bɛ a bɛnyɛ agyidifoɔ he nkyɛne.
Ɔsɛ sɛ yɛ Akristofoɔ mmom ne yɛboa saa nnipa he sɛnea yɛ ne bɛ bɛyɛ nɔkorɛ he ho adwuma ayɔnkofoɔ.
Diotrefe ne Demetrio Metwerɛɛ krataa bi kɔmaa asafo he, nso Diotrefe a ɔpɛ sɛ odi kane bɛ mu he antie nea mekaeɛ he, efiri sɛ, ɔnnye me mpanyinnie ntom.
Yei nti sɛ meba a, mede bibiaa a wayɔ he ho asɛm bɛto ho anim pefee, nsɛmmɔne a ɔka fa me ho nyinaa.
Ɔmma no nso hɔaa, na mmom sɛ anuanom he ba a, ɔnnye bɛ, na bɛ a bɛpɛ sɛ bɛgye bɛ he nso, ɔbɔ mmɔdene sɛ obesi bɛ kwane na watu bɛ afiri asafo he mu.
Me dɔfo, nhwɛ bɔne nsua, na mmom hwɛ papa sua.
Biaa a ɔyɛ papa he yɛ Nyankopɔn deɛ.
Na biaa a ɔyɛ bɔne he nso nhuu Nyankopɔn.
Demetrio deɛ, nnipa nyinaa ne nɔkorɛ he ankasa di ne ho adanse-pa. Na yɛ nso yedi ne ho adanse-pa na honim sɛ nea yɛka he yɛ nɔkorɛ.
Awieeɛ Nka mewɔ nsɛm bebree ka kyerɛ ho nso memfa krataa ne twerɛdua so nka.
Na mewɔ anidasoɔ sɛ ɔnkyɛre biaa mehu ho ne ho atena ase akasa.
Asomdwie nka ho.
Ho nnamfonom nyinaa kyeakyea ho.
Bobɔ nnamfonom nyinaa dini mmaako mmaako kyeakyea bɛ.
NNIANIMU Yuda krataa a ɔtwerɛeɛ he yɛ kɔkɔ a ɔbɔ fa atorɔ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ a bɛfrɛ bɛ ho sɛ agyidifoɔ he ho.
Nsɛm a ɔya nwoma tia yi mu ne deɛ ɔya Petro nwoma a ɔtɔ so mmienu mu he sɛ.
Twerɛfoɔ he hyɛ n’akenkanfoɔ nkurane sɛ, “bɛnko nkɔ bɛ anim ya gyidie a Nyankopɔn de ama ne nkurofoɔ prɛko he mu.” MU NSƐM Ahyɛaseɛ nkyerɛkyeremu - Torɔ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ subane, bɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ ne bɛ sɛeɛ - Gyidie kura ho afotuo - Nhyira nsɛm -
Nkyea Yesu Kristo akoa Yuda a ɔyɛ Yakobo nua twerɛ krataa yi de kɔma bɛ a bɛafrɛ bɛ a Agya Nyankopɔn dɔ bɛ na bɛakora bɛ ama Yesu Kristo he.
Mmɔborɔhunu, asomdwie ne dɔ nnɔɔso mma ho.
Kristofoɔ gyidie ho pere Adɔfonom, berɛ a meebɔ mmɔdene atwerɛ ho afa nkwagyeɛ a yɛ nyinaa te mu he ho he, mehuu sɛ ohia sɛ metwerɛ de fa hia ohia sɛ hoyere ho ho gyina gyidie a Nyankopɔn de ahyɛ ahoteefoɔ nsa prɛko he ho.
Na nnipa bi awiawia bɛ ho aba mu a befiri tete atwerɛ bɛ ho asɛm ato hɔ ama saa atemmuo yi, amumuyɔfoɔ a bɛde akohwibra bu Nyankopɔn adom he animtia, na bɛpo Owura korɔ a ɔne Awurade Yesu Kristo he.
Torɔ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ atemmuo Ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ sɛ honim yei dada, nso mepɛ sɛ mekae ho adwene fa gyeɛ a Awurade gyee Israelfoɔ firii Misraim asaase so prɛko na akyire yi he, ɔsɛee bɛ a bɛannye asɛm he anni he.
Na abɔfoɔ a bɛtraa bɛ tumi, na begyaa bɛ atenaeɛ he, bɛde daa nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn agugu bɛ ya sum kabii mu a Nyankopɔn de bɛ asie ɔɔtwɛne da kɛseɛ he atemmuo.
Saa ara ne Sodom ne Gomora ne nkuro a atwa bɛ ho ahyia a bɛyɔɔ sɛ yeinom, de bɛ ho maa adwamammɔfoɔ, na bekodii honam akɔnnɔ akyi a na ɔnyɛ ne kwane so, na bɛde daa gya twee bɛ aso de ayɔ nsɛnnahɔ ama yɛ.
Saa nnipa he nam saa kwane korɔ heaa so sosoo daeɛ ma bɛyɔɔ bɔne tiaa bɛ nipadua.
Bemmu tumidie, na bɛkasa tiaa animuonyamfoɔ.
Nso berɛ a bɔfo-panyini Mikael ne bronsam ɔɔpere Mose amu so a akasakasaa sii bɛ ntam he mpo, bɔfoɔ Mikael anyɔ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛka asɛmmɔne abu no atɛne, na mmom asɛm a ɔkaeɛaa ne sɛ, “Awurade nka w’anim!” Nso saa nnipa yi ka nea bennim he ho nsɛmmɔne, na deɛ befiri bɛ nnipa su mu nim sɛ mmoa a benni adwene he nso nim he, ɔno mu ne begu bɛ ho fi.
Mmusuo nka bɛ!
Efiri sɛ, kwane a Kain faa so heaa so ne bɛnam, na mfasoɔ nti, bɛde bɛ ho ahyɛ mfomsoɔ a Bileam yɔeɛ he bi ase.
Bɛayɔ dɔm sɛnea Kora yɔɔ dɔm he nam so ma bɛasɛe bɛ sɛ ɔno.
Yeinom yɛ ho dɔ adidie mu nkekaeɛ, bɛne ho bom oodidi, bɛmfɛre adeɛ, bɛyɛne bɛ ho; bɛte sɛ mununkum a nsuo nni mu a mframa twetwe kyinkyini, anaa nnua a so nhahane apere a onni aba, na awu mprenu a ne nhini atutu.
Bɛ aniwuo da adi te sɛ po asorɔkye a opu ahuro fi gu, bɛte sɛ nsoromma a okyinkyini a Nyankopɔn de bɛ asie sum kabii mu afebɔɔ.
Yeinom ho ne Henok nso a ɔtɔ Adam so nson awoɔ ntoatoasoɔ mu hyɛɛ saa nnipa yi ho nkɔm teteete sɛ, “Hwɛ, Awurade ne n’abɔfoɔ kronkron mpempem bɛba, na bɛabebu ho nyinaa atɛne na bɛabu nnebɔnyɛfoɔ nyinaa atɛne bɛ bɔne a bɛayɔ ne nsɛm a ano ɔdene a bɛaka atia Nyankopɔn he ho.” Yeinom yɛ anwiinwiifoɔ, yɔnaafoɔ a bedi bɛaa bɛ akɔnnɔ akyi, na bɛyɛ anumdwafoɔ a mfasoɔ nti, bɛdɛfɛdɛfɛ nnipa.
Kɔkɔbɔ ne afutuo ahodoɔ Adɔfonom, honkae nsɛm a tete he asomafoɔ he ka too hɔ faa Awurade Yesu Kristo ho, bɛkaa sɛ, “Sɛ awieeɛ he duru a, fɛwdifoɔ bɛba a, bebedi bɛaa bɛ amumuyɔ akɔnnɔ akyi.” Yeinom ne nnipa a bɛnam bɛ akɔnnɔ so de mpaepaemu ba he.
Na benni Honhom he.
Nti adɔfonom, metu ho fo sɛ, honkɔ so nyini ho gyidie kronkron mu, hommɔ mpaeɛ Honhom Kronkron he tumi mu, na honkɔ so ntena Nyankopɔn dɔ mu berɛ a hootwɛne yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo mmɔborɔhunu mu ama wama ho nkwa a onni awieeɛ he.
Na akyinnyegyefoɔ nso, honhu bɛ mmɔbɔ berɛ a hoontwe bɛ afiri gya mu agye bɛ nkwa, homfa suro nhu binom mmɔbɔ, na hontane nipasu a ɔte sɛ ataadeɛ a nkekaeɛ akeka mu he nso.
Nhyira nsɛm Na nea obetumi asɔ ho mu na hoansonti, na ɔde ho asi n’animuonyam anim sɛ nnipa a benni dɛm ahosane mu he, Nyankopɔn koro a ɔnam yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo so yɛ yɛ Agyenkwa he, ɔno ne animuonyam ne kɛseyɛ ne ahoɔdene ne tumi nka no mmerɛ santene, seesei ne daa nyinaa.
Amen.
NNIANIMU Bɛtwerɛɛ Yohane adiyisɛm he berɛ a na Akristofoɔ ɔɔfa taa mu esiane gyidie a na bekura sɛ Yesu Kristo ne Awurade he nti.
Deɛ na ohia twerɛfoɔ he titire ne sɛ ɔbɛma n’akenkanfoɔ anya anidasoɔ ne nkuranhyɛ a bebetumi de atena ase nɔkorɛdie mu ya taa berɛ he mu.
Krataa he fa kɛseɛ he yɛ adiyie ne anisoadehunu a ɔtoatoa so na bɛnam nsɛnkyerɛnne so kasa a Akristofoɔ a na bɛya hɔ saa berɛ he te aseɛ, na berɛ korɔ heaa nso ayɛ ahintasɛm ama afoforɔ.
Bɛnam anisoadehunu ahodoɔ so ka nwoma he botaeɛ mprɛ bebree ya akwane ahodoɔ so.
Ne nyinaa kyerɛ nteaseɛ a ɔya botaeɛ ahodoɔ a ɔya krataa he mu.
Ɔyam sɛ adwenkyerɛ ahodoɔ ne ya hɔ fa nkyerɛaseɛ ho deɛ, nso botaeɛ pɔtee he mu da hɔ pefee sɛ: Nyankopɔn nam Kristo a ɔyɛ Awurade he so bedi atamfoɔ he so koraa, a Satan nso ka ho bi.
Afei, ɔde nhyira a ɔyɛ soro foforɔ ne asaase foforɔ bɛma nnipa a bedi nɔkorɛ ma no he.
Yei bɛyɛ bɛ akatua berɛ a saa nkonimdie yi beduru he.
MU NSƐM Nsɛm a odi kane :- Anisoadehunu a odi kane ne krataa a ɔde kɔmaa asafo ahodoɔ nson he :—: Nwoma a ɔwɔ nsɔano nson :—: Ntotorobɛnto nson he :—: Tweaseɛ kɛseɛ he ne mmoa mmienu he :—: Anisoadehunu ahodoɔ :—: Nyankopɔn abufuo a ogu kuruwa nson mu :- Babel sɛeɛ ne aboa he, ne diyifoɔ torɔfoɔ ne Bronsam nkoguo :—: Atemmuo a odi akyire :- Soro foforɔ, asaase foforɔ ne Yerusalem foforɔ he :—: Awieeɛ :-
Nnianimu ne nkyea Saa nwoma yi fa Yesu Kristo adiyisɛm a Nyankopɔn de maa no sɛ ɔnkyerɛ ne nkoa nnoɔma a otwa sɛ ɔba ntɛm.
Kristo somaa ne bɔfoɔ kɔɔ ne n’akoa Yohane nkyɛne kɔdaa asɛm yi adi kyerɛɛ no.
Na Yohane dii adanseɛ faa Nyankopɔn asɛm ne Yesu Kristo ne nea ohuiɛ nyinaa ho.
Nhyira ne nipa a ɔkenkane saa nwoma yi, ne bɛ a betie adiyisɛm he na bedi so sɛnea bɛatwerɛ no saa nwoma yi mu he, efiri sɛ berɛ he abɛne.
Nsɛm a Yohane de kɔmaa asafo ahodoɔ nson a na bɛya Asia he di: Adom mmra ho so.
Afei nso, asomdwie a ofiri nea ɔya hɔ, seesei, na ɔya hɔ firi tetentredee, na ɔya hɔ daa he, ne ahonhom nson a ɔya n’ahennwa anim, ne Yesu Kristo a ɔyɛ danseni nɔkwafoɔ ne wusɔreɛ mu dikanfoɔ ne asaase so ahene sodifoɔ he nkyɛne nka ho.
Ɔno a ɔdɔ yɛ, na ɔnam ne mogyaa he so agye yɛ afiri yɛ bɔne mu he ayɔ yɛ ahemmane ne asɔfoɔ ama ne Nyankopɔn a ɔyɛ n’agya.
Ɔno ne animuonyam ne tumi nka no daa daa.
Amen!
Hwɛ!
Ɔnam mununkum mu ɔɔba; ani nyinaa behu no, na bɛ a bɛwɔɔ no pea he nso behu no bi.
Na ɔno nti asaase so nnipa nyinaa bɛbɔ bena.
Ampa, saa ne ɔbɛyɔ.
Amen!
“Mene ahyɛaseɛ ne awieeɛ,” Awurade Nyankopɔn ne ɔɔka, ɔno ne ya hɔ seesei na ɔya hɔ firi tetentredee na ɔya hɔ daa, ade nyinaa so tumfoɔ, he.
Kristo ho anisoadehunu Me, Yohane, ho nua a me ne ho bom Yesu mu hunu amane n’ahennie ne ne boasetɔ mu, na meya supɔ Patmo so, esiane Nyankopɔn asɛm ne Yesu adanseɛ nti.
Awurade da he, na meya Honhom mu, na metee nne dendene bi ya m’akyi a ɔte sɛ totorobɛnto.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Twerɛ bibiaa a wohu gu nwoma mu, na fa nwoma he kɔma asafo ahodoɔ nson yi: Deɛ ɔya Efeso, Smirna, Pergamo, Tiatira, Sardi, Filadelfia ne Laodikea.” Afei, medanee m’ani pɛɛ sɛ mehu nea ɔɔkasa akyerɛ me he, mehuu sikakɔkɔɔ nkaneadua nson.
Na bi a ɔte sɛ nipa ba he hyɛ ataadeɛ yuu a osi ne nane ase a sikakɔkɔɔ aboomu bɔ ne koko gyina nkaneadua nson he mfimfini.
Na ne tinwi yɛ fitaa te sɛ asaawafufuo, te sɛ akaadoo, na n’ani dɛre sɛ gyaframa.
Na ne nane ase hyerɛn sɛ yaawa fɛɛfɛ a adɔ ya fononoo mu, na afei bɛatwi ho na ne nne woro so te sɛ nsuo ɔɔworo dendene.
Na okita nsoromma nson ne nsa nifa mu, na nkrantɛ anofanu nnamnnam firi n’anum baeɛ.
Na n’anim hyerɛn sɛ awia a ɔɔhyerɛn dendene.
Mehuu no he, mekɔhwee ne nane ase yɛɛ te sɛ wufoɔ.
Na ɔde ne nsa nifa too me so kaa sɛ, “Nsuro!
Mene Kannifoɔ ne Kyidifoɔ.
Mene teasefoɔ he!
Mewuiɛ, na hwɛ, mete ase daa daa.
Mekita Wuo ne asamando nsafoa.
Nti afei twerɛ nnoɔma a wohu; nea wohu no seesei ne nea ɔbɛba akyire he.
Nsoromma nson a wohu no me nsa nifa mu ne sika nkaneadua he nkyerɛaseɛ a ɔyɛ ahintasɛm he di: Nsoromma nson he yɛ asafo nson he abɔfoɔ, na nkaneadua nson he nso yɛ asafo nson he.”
Krataa a ɔtwerɛ kɔmaa Efeso asafo “Twerɛ krataa kɔma Efeso asafo mu bɔfoɔ he, na ka kyerɛ no sɛ: Yei ne nsɛm a ofiri nea a okita nsoromma nson ne nsa nifa mu a, ɔnante sika nkaneadua nson he ntam he nkyɛne.
“Menim wo nnwuma.
Menim nsiyɛ a wode ayɔ adwuma ne boasetɔ a wowɔ.
Menim sɛ wonnye nnebɔnyɛfoɔ, na afei woasɔ bɛ a bɛfrɛ bɛ ho asomafoɔ nso bɛnyɛ bi he ahwɛ, na woahu sɛ bɛyɛ atorɔfoɔ.
Wowɔ boasetɔ na me dini nti, woahu amane bebree, na ne nyinaa mu he, wompaa aba.
Nso mewɔ nsɛm bi tia wo: Wonnɔ me sɛnea kane he na wodɔ me he.
Kae baabi a wofiri hwee ase.
Sakra w’adwene firi bɔne ho na yɔ sɛnea kane he na woyɔ he.
Sɛ woansakra amfiri wo bɔne ho a, mɛba wo nkyɛne abeyi wo kaneadua he afiri ne sibrɛ.
“Nso adepa a mahu ne wo ho ne sɛ, wokyiri Nikolaifoɔ nwuma he, na saa ne me nso mekyiri.
Nea ɔwɔ aso he ntie nea Honhom he ka kyerɛ asafo ahodoɔ he.
Bɛ a bɛadi nkunim he, mɛma bɛ akwanya na bɛadi nkwa dua a ɔya Nyankopɔn turo he mu aba he.’ Krataa a ɔtwerɛ kɔmaa Smirna asafo he “Twerɛ krataa yi kɔma Smirna asafo mu bɔfoɔ he sɛ: ‘Saa asɛm yi firi kannifoɔ ne kyidifoɔ he nkyɛne.
Ɔno ne wuiɛ, na ɔte ase bio he.
“Menim amaneɛ a wohu maa Awurade na menim wo hia nso, nso woyɛ defoɔ honhom mu.
Menim nsɛm a bɛ a bɛka sɛ bɛyɛ Yudafoɔ, nso bɛnyɛ Yudafoɔ he ka tia wo.
Bɛyɛ Satan apamfoɔ.
Nsuro haw a ɔɔbɛto wo he.
Tie, bɛde ho mu bi bɛto afiase na Bronsam nam so asɔ ho ahwɛ.
Na ho haw he bedi dadu.
Di nɔkorɛ ma me kosi wuo mu mpo, na mɛma wo nkwa abotire.
“Ma nea ɔwɔ aso he ntie nea Honhom he ka kyerɛ asafo he.
Deɛ odi nkunim he, wuprenu he ɔnka no da.’ Krataa a ɔtwerɛ kɔmaa Pergamo asafo he “Twerɛ krataa yi kɔma bɔfoɔ a ɔya Pergamo asafo mu sɛ: Saa krataa yi firi nea ɔwɔ nkrantɛ anofanu a ɔnam he nkyɛne.
“Menim sɛ faako a wote he, hɔ ne Satan ahennwa si, nso wokuraa me dini mu, na woampa me gyidie, nna a bekuu me danseni nɔkwafoɔ Antipa a na ɔne ho ya hɔ, deɛ a Satan te he.
Nso nsɛm kakra a mewɔ tia wo ne sɛ, nnipa bi ya wo mu a bedi Bileam nkyerɛkyerɛ akyi.
Saa Bileam he ne kyerɛɛ Balak ma ɔmaa Israelfoɔ dii abosom so nnuane, kyerɛɛ bɛ adwamammɔ, nam so ma bɛyɔɔ bɔne he.
Saa ara nso ne wowɔ nnipa bi ka wo ho a bedi Nikolaifoɔ nkyerɛkyerɛ akyi.
“Sakra w’adwene firi wo bɔne ho.
Anyɛ saa a, ɔɔnkyɛre biaa mɛba wo nkyɛne de nkrantɛ a ofiri m’anum he abɛko atia saa nnipa he.
“Ma nea ɔwɔ aso he ntie nea Honhom he ka kyerɛ asafo ahodoɔ he.
“Na nea odi nkunim he, mɛma no mana a ahinta he bi.
Afei mɛma no boɔ fitaa a bɛatwerɛ dini foforɔ so a biaa nnim, gye nipa a bɛde bɛma no he nko.” Krataa a ɔtwerɛ kɔmaa Tiatira asafo he “Twerɛ krataa kɔma bɔfoɔ a ɔya Tiatira asafo mu sɛ: Yei ne asɛm a ofiri Nyankopɔn Ba a n’ani dɛre sɛ gyaframa a ne nane ase hyerɛn sɛ yaawa he nkyɛne.
“Menim wo nnwuma.
Menim wo dɔ, wo gyidie, wo som ne wo boasetɔ.
Menim sɛ wooyɔ adwuma sene kane he.
Nso nea mewɔ nsɛm bi tia wo: Wososɔɔ baa bi a ne dini de Isebel, a ɔfrɛ ne ho diyifoɔ he so.
Saa baa yi kyerɛkyerɛ, na odi m’asomfoɔ anim ma bɛbɔ adwamane di abosom-nnuane.
Memaa no berɛ sɛ ɔnsakra mfiri ne bɔne mu nso wansakra amfiri n’adwamammɔ mu.
Yei nti, mede no bɛto ahohiahia mpa so na ɔne bɛ a bɛsɛe awareɛ he ahu amane a ano ɔdene yie, gye sɛ ebia bɛsesa firi ne nnwuma he ho.
Afei, meku n’akyidifoɔ he, na asafo he nyinaa behu sɛ mene deɛ ɔhwehwɛ adwene ne akoma mu.
Metua ho mu biaa ka sɛnea ne nwuma teɛ.
Nso ho a hoya Tiatira a honni saa nkyerɛkyerɛ bɔne he akyi he, na honnsua nea afoforɔ frɛ no Satan asumansɛm he deɛ, meeka makyerɛ ho sɛ, memmfa adesoa biaa nto ho so.
Na honsɔ nea howɔ he mu dene nkosi sɛ mɛba.
“Deɛ odi nkunim na ɔkɔ so yɔ nea mepɛ kosi awieeɛ he, mɛma no amane so tumi, na ɔde dadeɛ poma paa ne bɛyɛne bɛ, na wabobɔ bɛ sɛ nwomfoɔ nkukuo, te sɛ tumi korɔ heaa a menya firi m’Agya hɔ he.
Afei mede adekyeeɛ nsoromma bɛma no.
Nea ɔwɔ aso he ntie nea Honhom he ka kyerɛ asafo ahodoɔ he.
Krataa a ɔtwerɛ kɔmaa Sardi asafo he “Twerɛ krataa kɔma Sardi asafo he mu bɔfoɔ sɛ: “Yei ne nsɛm a ofiri nea ɔwɔ Nyankopɔn ahonhom nson ne nsoromma nson he nkyɛne.
“Menim wo nnwuma; wowɔ dini sɛ wote ase deɛ, nso woawu.
Nti nyane na kanyane nea aka wo nkyɛne he na anwu koraa, na menhuu wo nnwuma sɛ ɔyɛ pɛ me Nyankopɔn anim.
Kae nea wonyaeɛ na woteeɛ he, di so na sakra w’adwene firi wo bɔne ho.
Sɛ woanwɛne a, mɛba wo so te sɛ korɔmfoɔ, na wonhu dɔnhwere korɔ a mɛba wo nkyɛne.
“Nso ho mu kakraa bi a bɛya Sardi he mfaa wiase nkekaeɛ nkekaa bɛ ntaadeɛ mu.
Na bɛ ne me bɛnante berɛ a bɛhyɛ ntaade fitaa, efiri sɛ, bɛfata sɛ bɛyɔ saa.
Na deɛ odi nkunim he bɛbɛhyɛ no ataade-fitaa, na mempopa ne dini mfiri nkwa nwoma he mu.
Mɛbɔ ne dini ahyɛ no animuonyam m’Agya ne n’abɔfoɔ anim.
Nea ɔwɔ aso he ntie nea Honhom he ka kyerɛ asafo ahodoɔ he.
Krataa a ɔtwerɛ kɔmaa Filadelfia asafo he “Twerɛ krataa kɔma Filadelfia asafo he mu bɔfoɔ he sɛ: Yei ne asɛm a ofiri nea ɔyɛ kronkron, a ɔyɛ nɔkwafoɔ a okita Dawid safoa a sɛ obie a, bi ntumi nto mu, na ɔto mu nso a, bi ntumi mmie, he nkyɛne.
“Menim wo nnwuma.
Hwɛ, mede pono bi a mabie a bi ntumi ntom asi w’anim.
Menim sɛ wowɔ tumi ketewa bi deɛ, nso woadi me nkyerɛkyerɛ he so na woampa me dini.
Hwɛ!
Mɛma bɛ a befiri Satan hyiadane mu, a bedi torɔ ka sɛ bɛyɛ Yudafoɔ, nso bɛnyɛ bi he abɛkoto wo nane ase, na bɛ nyinaa ahu sɛ medɔ wo.
Esiane sɛ woadi m’ahyɛdeɛ so boasetɔ mu nti, sɛ haw a ɔɔba wiase nyinaa abɛsɔ asaase so nnipa nyinaa ahwɛ he ba a, mɛgye wo afiri mu.
Ɔnkyɛre biaa mɛba.
Sɔ nea wowɔ he mu dene, na bi annye wo nkunim abotire he.
Nea obedi nkunim he, mɛma no ayɛ me Nyankopɔn asɔredane he fapem titire, na ommfiri mu bio da.
Mɛtwerɛ me Nyankopɔn dini ne me Nyankopɔn kuro dini a ɔyɛ Yerusalem foforɔ a obefiri soro me Nyankopɔn nkyɛne aba he agu ne ho.
Bio, mɛtwerɛ me dini foforɔ agu ne ho.
Nea ɔwɔ aso he ntie nea Honhom he ka kyerɛ asafo ahodoɔ he.
Krataa a ɔtwerɛ kɔmaa Laodikea asafo he “Twerɛ krataa kɔma Laodikea asafo mu bɔfoɔ he sɛ: Yei ne asɛm a ofiri Amen a ɔyɛ danseni nɔkwafoɔ a ɔyɛ bibiaa a Nyankopɔn bɔeɛ he abɔseɛ nkyɛne.
“Menim wo nnwuma.
Wo a wonyɛ nwunu, wo nso a wonyɛ hye.
Sɛ woyɛ nwunu anaa hye a, nka ɔyɛ!
Nso esiane sɛ woyɛ botrobodwo na wonyɛ hye, wo so a wonyɛ nwunu nti, mɛfe wo afiri m’anum.
Woka sɛ, ‘Meyɛ defoɔ na maanya me ho, na mewɔ nea ohia me nyinaa.’ Nso wonnim hia a ahia wo ne mmɔbɔ a woyɛ.
Woyɛ hiani.
Woda adagya, na w’ani nso afira.
Nti metu wo fo sɛ tɔ sikakɔkɔɔ a bɛabere ho gya mu, firi me nkyɛne sɛnea ɔbɛma woayɛ defoɔ.
Afei tɔ ntaadeɛ fitaa hyɛ fa kata w’adagya a ama w’anim agu ase he so.
Afei tɔ aniduro sra w’ani so sɛnea wobehu adeɛ.
Mekɔ so twe bɛ a medɔ bɛ he nyinaa aso.
Nti bɔ mmɔdene na sakra w’adwene.
Hwɛ!
Megyina pono he akyi ɔɔbɔ mu, sɛ bi te me nne na obie pono he a, mɛba mu na me ne no abedidi na ɔno nso ne me adidi.
Mɛma nkunimdifoɔ he atena m’ahennwa he so sɛnea madi nkunim nti mete m’Agya ahennwa so seesei he.
Ma nea ɔwɔ aso he ntie nea Honhom he ka kyerɛ asafo ahodoɔ he.”
Soro pono a Bɛabie Yei akyi he, mehwɛeɛ, na hwɛ, mehuu soro pono sɛ abie.
Na nne bi teaam sɛ totorobɛnto a mate sɛ bi akasa akyerɛ me pɛn he; na ɔkaa sɛ, “Bra soro ha, na mɛkyerɛ wo nea ɔbɛba yei akyi.” Prɛko pɛ!
Na meya honhom mu.
Na hwɛ, na bɛde ahennwa bi asi soro a bi te so.
Na nea ɔte he anim hyerɛn te sɛ ahwehwɛboɔ ne bogyanamboɔ.
Na nyankontɔno a ɔte sɛ ahabamonoboɔ atwa ahennwa he ho ahyia.
Na ahennwa aduonu nnan atwa ahennwa he ho ahyia a mpanyimfoɔ aduonu nnan tete so a bɛhyehyɛ ntaadeɛ fitaa na sikakɔkɔɔ abotire bobɔ bɛ ti.
Na anyinam ne nne ahodoɔ ne apranaa boboom firi ahennwa he mu.
Na nkanea nson a bɛasosɔ a ɔɔdɛre ya ahennwa he anim.
Na yeinom ne Nyankopɔn ahonhom nson.
Na bibi te sɛ ahwehwɛ po a ɔyɛ krɔgyee sɛ ahwehwɛ da ahennwa he anim.
Na ateasefoɔ nnan a ani tuatua bɛ anim ne bɛ akyi atwa ahennwa he ho ahyia.
Na teasefoɔ a odi kane he te sɛ gyata; nea ɔtɔ so mmienu he te sɛ nantwie ba; nea ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he anim te sɛ nipa; na nea ɔtɔ so nnan he te sɛ kɔdeɛ a ootu.
Na ateasefoɔ nnan he mu biaa wɔ ntabane nsia a ani tuatua akyire ne animu nyinaa.
Anadwo ne awia nyinaa bɛto nnwom sɛ, “Kronkron, Kronkron, Kronkron ne Awurade Nyankopɔn Tumfoɔ a na ɔya hɔ tetentredee, na seesei nso ɔya hɔ, na ɔya hɔ daa.” Saa ateasefoɔ nnan he to nnwom de hyɛ nea ɔte ahennwa he so a ɔte hɔ daa daa he animuonyam de ma no anidie da no ase.
Sɛ bɛyɔ saa a, mpanyimfoɔ aduonu nnan he butubutu nea ɔte ahennwa he so he anim sɔre nea ɔte hɔ daa daa he.
Betu bɛ ahenkyɛ gu ahennwa he anim ka sɛ, “Yɛ Awurade ne Nyankopɔn; wofata sɛ wonya animuonyam, anidie ne tumi, efiri sɛ, wo ne wobɔɔ nnoɔma nyinaa, na wo pɛ mu nti na bɛya hɔ, ne bɛbɔeɛ.”
Nwoma he ne Adwammaa he Na mehuu nwoma bi ya deɛ ɔte ahennwa so he nsa nifa mu.
Na bɛatwerɛ mu ne akyire nyinaa a na bɛde nsɔano nson asosɔ ano.
Na mehuu bɔfoɔ hoɔdenfoɔ bi a ɔde nne kɛseɛ kaa sɛ, “Hwane ne fata sɛ ɔte nsɔano he ano na obie nwoma he mu?” Na bɛannya biaa a ɔya soro anaa asaase so, anaa asaase ase a otumi biee nwoma he mu na ohwɛɛ mu.
Mesuu paa efiri sɛ, bɛannya biaa a ɔfata sɛ obie nwoma he mu na ɔhwɛ mu.
Afei mpanyimfoɔ he mu baako ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Nsu.
Hwɛ!
Yuda abusuakuo mu Gyata a ɔyɛ Dawid aseni he adi nkunim, na ɔno ne betumi ate nsɔano nson he ano na wabie nwoma he mu.” Afei mehuu adwamaa bi sɛ ogyina ahennwa he mfimfini a ateasefoɔ nnan he ne mpanyimfoɔ he atwa ne ho ahyia.
Wohwɛ a, na ɔte sɛ nea bɛaku no.
Na ɔwɔ mmɛne nson ne ani nson a ogyina hɔ ma Nyankopɔn ahonhom nson a bɛasoma bɛ aba wiase he.
Adwamaa he kɔgyee nwoma he firii nea ɔte ahennwa so he nsa nifa mu.
Ɔyɔɔ saa he, ateasefoɔ nnan he ne mpanyimfoɔ aduonu nnan he butubutuu adwamaa he anim.
Na bɛ mu biaa kita sankuo ne sika ayowa a aduhwam, a ɔyɛ ahoteefoɔ mpaebɔ, ahyɛ no ma.
Bɛtoo nnwom foforɔ bi sɛ, “Wofata sɛ wofa nwoma he, na wote nsɔano he ano, efiri sɛ, bekuu wo, na bɛde wo mogyaa atɔ nnipa afiri abusua, kasa, mane ne nkurofoɔ ahodoɔ mu ama Nyankopɔn.
Woama bɛayɛ ahemmane ne asɔfoɔ ama yɛ Nyankopɔn, na bebedi asaase so ahene.” Bio mehwɛeɛ, na metee abɔfoɔ mpempem buburugyaa nka.
Na bɛatwa ahennwa he ne ateasefoɔ nnan he ne mpanyimfoɔ he ho ahyia a na bɛɛto nnwom dendene sɛ, “Adwamaa a bekuu no he fata sɛ ɔgye tumi, ahonya, nyansa ne ahoɔdene ne anidie ne animuonyam ne nhyira!” Na metee sɛ abɔdeɛ a ɔya soro, asaase so, asaase ase, po mu ne dea ɔya wiase nyinaa ɔɔto nnwom sɛ, “Nhyira ne anidie ne animuonyam ne tumi nka nea ɔte ahennwa he so ne adwamaa he daa daa!” Ateasefoɔ nnan he gyee so sɛ, “Amen!” Na mpanyimfoɔ he butubutuiɛ, na bɛkoto sɔreeɛ.
Nsɔano nson he Afei mehuu sɛ adwamaa he ate nsɔano nson he mu nea odi kane he ano, na metee sɛ ateasefoɔ nnan he mu baako de nne a ɔte sɛ apranaa ɔɔka sɛ, “Bra!” Afei mehwɛeɛ, na hwɛ, na pɔnkɔ fitaa bi di.
Na deɛ ɔte ne so he kita agyane, na bɛmaa no ahenkyɛ.
Ofiri adi sɛ nkunimdifoɔ a ookodi nkunim bio.
Na ɔtee nsɔano a ɔto so mmienu he ano, na metee sɛ teasefoɔ a ɔtɔ so mmienu he ɔɔka sɛ, “Bra!” Afei pɔnkɔ foforɔ bi a ɔyɛ kɔkɔɔ pie baeɛ.
Bɛmaa nea ɔte ne so he tumi sɛ ɔmfa kõ mmra asaase so, na nnipa nkuku bɛ ho.
Bɛmaa no nkrantɛ kɛseɛ bi.
Na ɔtee nsɔano a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he ano, na metee sɛ teasefoɔ a ɔtɔ so mmeɛnsa he ɔɔka sɛ, “Bra!” Mehwɛeɛ, na hwɛ, pɔnkɔ tuntum bi di.
Na nea ɔte ne so he kita nsania ya ne nsam.
Metee bibi te sɛ nne bi firi ateasefoɔ nnan he nkyɛne.
Na nne he kaa sɛ, “Ayuo susukora yɛ paani da koro akatua, na aburo susukora mmeɛnsa nso yɛ paani da koro akatua.
Nso, nsɛe ngo he ne nsa he!” Afei adwamaa he tee nsɔano a ɔtɔ so nnan he ano, na metee sɛ teasefoɔ a ɔtɔ so nnan he ɔɔka sɛ, “Bra!” Mehwɛeɛ na hwɛ, pɔnkɔ nsõnsõ bi di.
Bɛtoo ne sotefoɔ he dini sɛ Wuo.
Na Asamando nso di n’akyi pɛɛ.
Bɛmaa bɛ asaase nkyemu nnan mu baako so tumi sɛ bɛmfa afena ne kɔm ne wuo ne asaase so nkekaboa nkuku bɛ.
Afei ɔtee nsɔano a ɔto so num he ano.
Na mehuu bɛ a Nyankopɔn asɛm ne bɛ adanseɛ a bediiɛ nti bɛakuku bɛ he akra, afɔrebokyia he ase.
Bɛde nne a ano ɔdene kaa sɛ, “O Awurade Tumfoɔ, kronkronni ne nɔkwafoɔ!
Wobɛtwentwɛne wo nane ase akosi da bɛ na woabu atɛne atua nnipa a bɛya asaase so ka yɛ mogyaa ho?” Bɛmaa bɛ mu biaa ataade tentene fitaa, na bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛntwɛne kakra nkosi sɛ bɛ mfɛfoɔ asomfo ne bɛ nuanom a bebekuku bɛ sɛnea bekuu bɛ he bɛba abɛka bɛ ho ama bɛ dodoɔ awie pɛyɛ.
Na mehuu sɛ ɔtee nsɔano a ɔtɔ so nsia he ano.
Na asaasewosoɔ a ano ɔdene ba maa awia yɛɛ tumm sɛ birisie, na bosome yɛɛ kɔɔ sɛ mogyaa.
Na nsoromma tete firi soro bɛhwee asaase so te sɛ borɔdoma a mframa kɛseɛ woso no tete n’aba bunu gu fam.
Afei soro yeraeɛ te sɛ nwoma a bɛabobɔ, na mmepɔ, ne nsupɔ firii baabi a na bɛyeya.
Na asaase so ahemfo ne nnipa akɛseɛ ne asafohene ne adefoɔ ne ahoɔdenfoɔ ne nkoa ne adehyeɛ nyinaa hintahintaa abodane ne mmepɔ mu abotane mu.
Na bɛka kyerɛɛ mmepɔ ne abotane he sɛ, “Honkata yɛ so na homfa yɛ nsie sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a nea ɔte ahennwa he so he ani onhu yɛ na yemfiri Adwamaa he abufuo ano, efiri sɛ n’abufuo da kɛseɛ he aduru; na hwane ne betumi agyina ano?”
Israel nnipa mpemha aduanan nnan he Yei akyi he, mehuu abɔfoɔ nnan sɛ, begyinagyina asaase ntweasoɔ nnan he so a, bɛɛtwe mframa nnan a ɔya asaase so he ɔɔsane akyi sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a, mframa biaa ɔmmɔ asaase ne po ne dua biaa so.
Na mehuu bɔfoɔ foforɔ a ofiri awia apieɛ ɔɔba a okita Nyankopɔn teasefoɔ he nsɔano.
Ɔteaam frɛɛ abɔfoɔ nnan he a na Nyankopɔn ama bɛ tumi sɛ bɛnsɛe asaase ne po he.
Bɔfoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Honnsɛe asaase ne po anaa nnua kosi sɛ yɛbɛhyɛ Nyankopɔn nkoa he nso bɛ moma so.” Na bɛkyerɛɛ me bɛ a bɛahyɛ bɛ nsõ he dodoɔ.
Na bɛ nyinaa bɛ dodoɔ yɛ mpemha aduannan nnan a, befiri Israel mmusuakuo nyinaa mu.
Yuda abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Ruben abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Gad abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu Aser abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Naftali abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Manase abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Simeon abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Lewi abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Isakar abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Sebulon abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Yosef abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Benyamin abusuakuo mu nnipa a bɛhyɛɛ bɛ nso he dodoɔ yɛ mpem dummienu.
Yei akyi he, mehwɛeɛ, na mehuu nnipakuo a biaa ntumi nkane bɛ dodoɔ a befiri amane ne mmusuakuo ne nkurofoɔ ne kasa nyinaa mu a begyinagyina ahennwa he ne Adwamaa he anim a bɛhyehyɛ ntaadeɛ fitaa kitakita berɛɛ.
Bɛteaam dendene sɛ, “Nkwagyeɛ firi yɛ Nyankopɔn a ɔte ahennwa he so ne Adwamaa he hɔ.” Na abɔfoɔ he atwa ahennwa he ne mpanyimfoɔ he ne ateasefoɔ nnan he ho ahyia.
Afei bebutubutuu ahennwa he anim, sɔree Nyankopɔn kaa sɛ, “Amen!
Nhyira ne animuonyam ne nyansa ne aseda ne anidie ne tumi ne ahoɔdene yɛ Nyankopɔn dea daa daa!
Amen!” Nkwagyeɛ a ɔnam adwammaa he so ba Afei mpanyimfoɔ he mu baako bisaa me sɛ, “Hefoɔ ne bɛhyehyɛ ntaadeɛ fitaa yi, na befiri he?” Mebuaa sɛ “Owura, wo ne wonim.” Ɔka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Yeinom ne bɛ a bɛafiri taa mu, na bɛde Adwamaa he mogyaa ahohoro bɛ ntaadeɛ ama ayɛ fitaa.
Na yei nti ne begyina Nyankopɔn ahennwa anim a bɛɛsom awia ne anadwo ne hyiadane mu yi.
Nea ɔbɛtena ahennwa he so he bɛbɔ bɛ ho bane.
Kɔm ɔnne bɛ bio.
Awia anaa ahuhuro biaa ɔnnhye bɛ bio, efiri sɛ, Adwamaa he a ɔya ahennwa he mfinimfini he bɛyɛ bɛ dwanhwɛfoɔ de bɛ akɔ nkwa asuti ho.
Na Nyankopɔn bɛpopa bɛ aniwa mu nisuo nyinaa.”
Nsɔano a ɔtɔ so nson Berɛ a ɔtee nsɔano a ɔto so nson he ano he, soro nyinaa tam dinn bɛyɛ dɔnhwere fa.
Afei mehuu abɔfoɔ nson a begyinagyina Nyankopɔn anim.
Bɛmaa bɛ ntotorobɛnto nson.
Bɔfoɔ foforɔ a na okita sikakɔkɔɔ aduhwam adaka begyinaa afɔrebokyia he ho.
Bɛmaa no aduhwam bebree sɛ ɔmfa mmɔ mpaeɛ nka Nyankopɔn nkurofoɔ he deɛ ho na ɔmmɔ sikakɔkɔɔ afɔrebokyia a osi ahennwa he anim he so afɔdeɛ.
Aduhwam he hua ne Nyankopɔn nkurofoɔ mpaeɛ firi bɔfoɔ he nsam kɔɔ Nyankopɔn anim.
Afei bɔfoɔ he faa aduhwam adaka he de gya a ofiri afɔrebokyia he so hyɛɛ no ma too twenee asaase so.
Na apranaa ne nne ahoroɔ ne anyinam ne asaasewosoɔ baeɛ.
Na abɔfoɔ nson a bekitakita ntotorobɛnto nson he siesiee bɛ ho sɛ bɛɛbɛhyɛne.
Bɔfoɔ a odi kane he hyɛne ne totorobɛnto he.
Na asukɔtwea ne gya a ɔne mogyaa adi afra tɔ guu asaase so.
Asaase nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako hyeeɛ.
Nnua nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako hyeeɛ, na nwura mono nyinaa nso hyeeɛ.
Afei bɔfoɔ a ɔtɔ so mmienu he hyɛnee ne totorobɛnto he.
Na bɛtoo bibi a ɔte sɛ bepɔ kɛseɛ a ɔɔdɛre too po mu.
Po he nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako danee mogyaa.
Na abɔdeɛ a bɛwɔ nkwa a bɛya po mu he, bemu nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako wuwuiɛ maa ahyɛne mu nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako nso sɛeɛ.
Afei bɔfoɔ a ɔto so mmeɛnsa he hyɛnee ne totorobɛnto he.
Na nsoromma kɛseɛ bi a ɔɔdɛre sɛ gyatanaa te firii soro bɛhwee nsuo nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako mu.
Nsoromma he dini de Nwononwono.
Nsuo he nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako yɛɛ nwono, na nnipa a bɛnomeeɛ he mu bebree wuwuiɛ, efiri sɛ, na ayɛ nwono.
Afei bɔfoɔ a ɔto so nnan he hyɛnee ne totorobɛnto he.
Na bɛbɔɔ awia nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako ne bosome nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako, ne nsoromma nkyekyem mmeɛnsa mu baako, na biaa nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako he duduruu sum, na adekyeɛ mu nkyekyem mmeɛnsa mu baako anhyerɛn, na anadwo nso saa.
Na mehuu kɔdeɛ bi sɛ a watu nam sorosoro, na metee sɛ ɔɔteam sɛ, “Bɛ a bɛte asaase so he nnue; honnue, honnue ɔnam totorobɛnto a aka a abɔfoɔ mmeɛnsa he ɔɔbɛhyɛne he nti.”
Afei bɔfoɔ a ɔto so nnum he hyɛnee ne totorobɛnto he, na mehuu nsoromma bi sɛ ofiri soro abɛhwe asaase so.
Bɛmaa no amena donkodonko he ano safoa.
Nsoromma he biee amena donkodonko he, na wusie kumoo firi mu sɛ fononoo kɛseɛ bi, na wusie he maa awia hann ne mframa a ɔya hɔ he yɛɛ tumm.
Ntutummɛ firii wusie he mu baa asaase so, na bɛmaa bɛ tumi a ɔte sɛ asaase so naanantwi tumi.
Afei bɛka kyerɛɛ bɛ sɛ bɛnsɛe serɛ anaa nnua anaa afideɛ biaa.
Na mmom nnipa a Nyankopɔn ahyɛnsodeɛ he bi nni bɛ moma so he deɛ, betumi ha bɛ.
Na bɛamma ntutummɛ he kwane sɛ bekuku saa nnipa he, na mmom bɛnha bɛ abosome nnum.
Bɛka bɛ a, bɛ ano yeyaa he te sɛ naanantwi ano yeyaa.
Saa bosome num he mu he, saa nnipa he bɛpere wuo, nso bennya.
Bɛbɛpɛ sɛ bewu, nso wuo bedwane afiri bɛ nkyɛne.
Ntutummɛ he te sɛ apɔnkɔ a bɛasiesie bɛ ama ko.
Bɛwɔ bibi te sɛ sikakɔkɔɔ ahenkyɛ hyɛ bɛ ti.
Na bɛ anim te sɛ nnipa anim.
Bɛ tinwi te sɛ mmaa tinwi, na bɛ sẽ nso te sɛ gyata sẽ.
Bɛde bibi te sɛ dadeɛ nkataboɔ akatakata bɛ bo.
Na bɛ ntabane yɛ dede te sɛ apɔnkɔ pii a bɛɛtwe nteaseɛnam akɔ ko.
Bɛwɔ dua a ne nwowɔeɛ te sɛ naanantwi.
Na bɛ dua he ne maa bɛ tumi a bɛde ha nnipa bosome num he.
Bɛwɔ hene a odi bɛ so a ɔno ne bɔfoɔ a ɔhwɛ amena donkodonko he so.
Ne dini ya Hebri kasa mu ne Abadon; na Hela kasa mu nso ɔde Apolion (a n’asekyerɛ ne “Sɛefoɔ”).
Haw baako atwam.
Yei akyi he, haw mmienu bi bɛba.
Afei bɔfoɔ a ɔtɔ so nsia he hyɛne ne totorobɛnto he, na metee nne bi firii sikakɔkɔɔ afɔrebokyia a osi Nyankopɔn anim he mmɛne he mu.
Nne he ka kyerɛɛ bɔfoɔ a ɔto so nsia a okita totorobɛnto he sɛ, “Sansane abɔfoɔ nnan a bɛakyekyere bɛ asubɔntene Eufrate ho he.” Besansanee abɔfoɔ nnan he a bɛasiesie bɛ ama saa dɔnhwere yi, saa da yi, saa bosome yi ne saa afe yi sɛ benkuku adasamma mu nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako.
Na metee sɛ dɔm a bɛtete apɔnkɔ so he ano si mpem du ahodoɔ mpem aduonu.
Na m’anisoadehunu he mu he, mehuu apɔnkɔ he ne bɛ akafoɔ.
Na bɛ nkataboɔ he ahosu te sɛ gya, tumm te sɛ afasebiri, na ɔte sɛ sɔfe nso.
Na apɔnkɔ he ti te sɛ gyata ti a gya, wusie ne sɔfe firi bɛ anum.
Saa haw ahodoɔ mmeɛnsa he a ɔyɛ gya, wusie ne sɔfe he a ofiri apɔnkɔ he anum baeɛ he kuu adasamma nkyekyɛmu mmeɛnsa mu baako, efiri sɛ, na apɔnkɔ he tumi nyinaa firi bɛ anum ne bɛ dua.
Bɛ dua te sɛ awɔ a bɛwɔ ti a ɔno ne na bɛde pirepira nnipa.
Adasamma a bɛkaeɛ he a haw he anku bɛ he antwe bɛ ho amfiri bɛ nnwuma ho.
Bɛannyae ahohommɔne ne ahoni ne sika ne dwetɛ ne ayowa ne aboɔ ne nnua a onhu adeɛ na ɔnte asɛm na ontumi nnante he som.
Saa nso ne bɛansakra bɛ adwene amfiri bɛ awudie, bɛ adutoɔ, bɛ adwamammɔ ne bɛ korɔnobɔ ho.
Bɔfoɔ he ne Nwoma ketewa he Afei mehuu bɔfoɔ tumfoɔ bi a ofiri soro oosiane ba fam.
Na ɔhyɛ mununkum mu a nyankontɔno bɔ ne ti.
Na n’anim te sɛ awia, na ne nane te sɛ gya fadum.
Na nwoma ketewa bi kita no a wabie mu.
Ɔde ne nane nifa sii po so a na benkum he nso si asaase so.
Ɔteaam maa ne nne woroo so sɛ gyata.
Ɔfrɛeɛ he, apranaa nson he woroo so gyee so.
Bɛka saa pɛ, na mepɛ sɛ metwerɛ.
Nso metee nne bi firi soro a ɔkaa sɛ, “Ma nsɛm a apranaa nson he kaeɛ he nka wo tim.
Ntwerɛ!” Hɔaa, bɔfoɔ a mehuu sɛ ogyina hɔ a ne nane baako si po so na baako nso si asaase so he maa ne nsa nifa so kɔɔ soro, na ɔde deɛ ɔte hɔ daa daa a ɔbɔɔ soro ne asaase ne po ne nea ɔya mu nyinaa he dini kaa ntam.
Bɔfoɔ he kaa sɛ, “Bɛntwentwɛne bɛ nana ase bio.
Na sɛ bɔfoɔ a ɔto so nson he hyɛ ne totorobɛnto he a, ne Nyankopɔn bewie n’ahintasɛm mu nhyehyɛeɛ he, sɛnea ɔka kyerɛɛ n’asomfoɔ a bɛyɛ adiyifoɔ he.” Bɔfoɔ he nwoma Afei nne a metee sɛ ofiri soro he kasa kyerɛɛ me bio sɛ, “Kɔ na kɔgye nwoma a bɛabie mu a okita bɔfoɔ a ogyina po ne asaase so he.” Mekɔɔ bɔfoɔ he nkyɛne kɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ ɔmfa nwoma ketewa he mma me.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Gye na we.
Ɔbɛkeka wo yam, nso w’anum deɛ, ɔbɛyɛ dɛ te sɛ woɔ.” Megyee nwoma ketewa he firii ne nsam weeɛ, na ɔyɛɛ dɛ te sɛ woɔ ya m’anum.
Nso memeneeɛ he akyi, ɔkekaa me yam.
Afei bɛka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Ɔsɛ sɛ woka nkurofoɔ ne amane ne kasa ne ahemfo bebree ho adiyisɛm bio.”
Adansefoɔ mmienu he Afei bɛmaa me susudua bi a ɔte sɛ poma, na bɛka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Sɔre na susu Nyankopɔn asɔredane he ne afɔrebokyia he na kane bɛ a bɛɛsom asɔredane he mu he.
Nso mfa asɔredane he mfikyiri nka ho, efiri sɛ, bɛde hɔ ama amanamane mufoɔ, na bebetiatia kuro kronkron he so abosome aduannan mmienu.
Mɛsoma m’adansefoɔ mmienu a befirafira ayitoma, na bɛaka adiyisɛm nna apem ahanu ne aduosia.” Yeinom ne ngodua mmienu he ne kaneadua mmienu a osisi asaase a ɔya Awurade anim he so he.
Gya firi bɛ anum bekuku atamfoɔ biaa a bɛpɛ sɛ bɛha bɛ he.
Ɔno nti, biaa a ɔpɛ sɛ ɔha bɛ he, bebeku no.
Yeinom wɔ tumi sɛ bɛto soro mu, na nsuo ɔnntɔ ya nna a bɛde hyɛ nkɔm he mu, na bɛwɔ tumi ya nsuo so sɛ bɛma ɔdane mogyaa na bɛde haw nyinaa bi ha asaase berɛ dodoɔ biaa bɛ pɛ.
Na sɛ bɛka bɛ asɛm he wie a, aboa a obefiri amena donkodonko he mu apie he ne bɛ bɛko.
Obedi bɛ so aku bɛ.
Na bɛ afunu bɛdeda kuro kɛseɛ he abɔntene so, kuro a honhom mu bɛfrɛ no Sodom ne Misraim, baabi a bɛbɔɔ bɛ Awurade nso asennua mu he Na nnipa a befiri amane so ne mmusuakuo ne kasa hodoɔ ne amane bi so bɛhwɛ bɛ afunu he nnansa ne fa, na bɛmma kwane mma bensie bɛ.
Asaase so nnipa ani bɛgye sɛ saa nnipa mmienu he awuwu.
Bɛbɛgye bɛ ani na bɛakyɛ bɛ ho akyɛdeɛ, efiri sɛ, saa adiyifoɔ mmienu he ne bɛde haw bɛtoo asaase sofoɔ so.
Na nnansa ne fa akyi he, honhom a ofiri Nyankopɔn bewuraa bɛ mu na bɛsɔre gyinaeɛ.
Na hu kɛseɛ kãã biaa a ohuu bɛ.
Afei nne a ano ɔdene firi soro bɛkaa sɛ, “Homforo mmra soro ha.” Na berɛ a na bɛ atamfoɔ ɔɔhwɛ bɛ he, bɛfaa mununkum mu kɔɔ soro.
Saa mmerɛ heaa, asaase wosoo dendenndene, kuro he nkyekyɛmu du mu baako sɛeɛ, na nnipa mpemnson wuwuiɛ ɔnam asaasewosoɔ he nti.
Nnipa a bɛaka he bɔɔ hu na bɛkamfoo Nyankopɔn a ɔya soro he kɛseyɛ.
Haw a ɔtɔ so mmienu he atwam, nso, hwɛ, ɔnkyɛre na haw a ɔto so mmeɛnsa nso aba.
Totorobɛnto a ɔto so nson Afei bɔfoɔ a ɔto so nson he hyɛne ne totorobɛnto he, na nne dendene bi firi soro kaa sɛ, “Wiase ahennie ayɛ yɛ Awurade ne ne Kristo he dea, na obedi hene daa daa.” Afei mpanyimfoɔ aduonu nnan a bɛte bɛ ahennwa so Nyankopɔn anim he de bɛ anim butubutuu fam, sɔree Nyankopɔn, kaa sɛ: Yɛda wo ase, Awurade Nyankopɔn a woyɛ adeɛ nyinaa so Tumfoɔ a na woya hɔ firi tetentredee, na woya hɔ nnɛ nso, sɛ woafa wo tumi kɛseɛ, na woadi hene.
Na amanamane he bo fuiɛ, na w’abufuo ne awufoɔ berɛ he aduru sɛ wobebu atɛne, na woama wo nkoa, adiyifoɔ ne ahoteefoɔ ne bɛ a besuro wo dini, nketewa ne akɛseɛ nyinaa, he akatua, na woasɛe bɛ a bɛasɛe asaase he.
Afei Nyankopɔn asɔredane a ɔya soro he bieeɛ ma behuu adaka a apam he ya mu he asɔredane he mu.
Afei anyinam ne apranaa paepaeɛ, na asaase wosoeɛ, na asukɔtwea pii nso baeɛ.
Baa he ne tweaseɛ he Afei nsɛnkyerɛnne kɛseɛ bi daa ne ho adi soro.
Baa bi pieeɛ a na ofira awia a bosome ya ne nane ase, na nsoromma dummienu ahenkyɛ hyɛ no.
Na ɔnyem a ɔɔbɛwo, na awoyeya nti, na oosu.
Afei nsɛnkyerɛnne kɛseɛ foforɔ bi daa ne ho adi soro.
Wɔ kɔkɔɔ kakraka bi pieeɛ a na ne ti yɛ nson a na ɔwɔ mmɛne du; na ahemmotire bobɔ ne ti he biaa so.
Ɔde ne dua twee nsoromma a ɔya soro he mu nkyemu mmeɛnsa mu baako too guu fam.
Na ogyinaa baa a ɔɔwo he anim sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a ɔwo abɔfra he to hɔaa pɛ, ɔbɛfa abɔfra he awe.
Afei baa he woo abeemaa a ɔde dadeɛ poma bedi amane nyinaa so.
Nso behwim abɔfra he kɔɔ Nyankopɔn ne n’ahennwa ho.
Baa he dwane kɔɔ serɛ so baabi a Nyankopɔn asiesie ama no a bɛbɛhwɛ no hɔ nnafua apem ahanu ne aduosia mu.
Mikael dii wɔ he so nkunim Afei ko sii soro hɔ.
Mikael ne n’abɔfoɔ ko tiaa tweaseɛ kɛseɛ he, na wɔ kɛseɛ he nso ne n’abɔfoɔ ko tia bɛ.
Nso bedii bɛ so nkunim na bɛamma ɔne n’abɔfoɔ antena soro bio.
Bɛtoo tweaseɛ kɛseɛ he tweneeɛ.
Ɔno ne wɔ dadaa he a bɛfrɛ no Bronsam ne Satan he, ɔno ne daadaa wiase nyinaa he.
Na bɛtoo no twenee asaase so a na n’abɔfoɔ nyinaa ka ne ho.
Afei metee nne dendene bi soro a ɔkaa sɛ, “Afei Nyankopɔn nkwagyeɛ, ne tumi, n’ahennie ne ne Kristo he tumi he aba, efiri sɛ, bɛapam nea ogyina Nyankopɔn anim toto yɛ nuanom ano awia ne anadwo he afiri soro.
Nso bɛnam Adwamaa he mogyaa so ne bɛ adanseɛ asɛm adi no so nkunim, na bɛannɔ bɛ kra, mpo de kosii wuo mu.
Nti ho a hote soro homma ho ani nnye.
Afei asaase ne po nnue!
Efiri sɛ, Bronsam he atoa ho, na ne bo afu efiri sɛ, onim sɛ, ne mmerɛ a aka sua!” Tweaseɛ he tuu sa bio asaase so Mmerɛ a tweaseɛ he huu sɛ bɛato no atwene asaase so he, ɔtaa baa a wawo abeemaa he.
Nso bɛmaa baa he kɔdeɛ ntabane akɛseɛ mmienu sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a obetumi atu akɔ serɛ so baabi a hɔ yɛ ne tenaberɛ, dea bɛbɛhwɛ no mfie mmeɛnsa ne fa sɛnea wɔ he oonni n’akyi bio.
Afei wɔ he puu n’anum nsuo te sɛ asubɔntene guu baa he akyi, sɛ nka ɔmfa no.
Nso asaase boaa baa he.
Obiee n’anum nom nsuo a tweaseɛ he pu guu hɔ he nyinaa.
Na tweaseɛ he bo fuu baa he, na okotuu n’asefoɔ nkaeɛ a bedi Nyankopɔn ahyɛdeɛ so na bekura Yesu adanseɛ he so sa.
Na okogyinaa mpoano anwea so.
Aboa a odi kane he Afei mehuu sɛ aboa bi apie po he mu ɔɔba.
Na ɔwɔ mmɛne du ne tire nson a, na ahemmotire du bobɔ ne mmɛne he so a abusudini bobɔ tire he ho.
Aboa a mehuu no he, na ɔte sɛ sebɔ a ne nane te sɛ sisire, na n’ano nso te sɛ gyata ano.
Na tweaseɛ he de ɔno ankasa ne tumi ne n’ahennwa ne ne tumi kɛseɛ maa aboa he.
Na mehuu ne ti he mu baako a ɔte sɛ deɛ bɛatwa ama ɔɔyɛ awu, nso bɛsaa ne pirakuro he, na aboa he ho yɛɛ wiasefoɔ nyinaa nwanwa maa bedii n’akyi.
Nnipa nyinaa som tweaseɛ he efiri sɛ, ɔde ne tumi nyinaa ama aboa he.
Bɛsom aboa he nso kaa sɛ, “Hwane ne te sɛ aboa he?
Na hwane ne betumi ne no ako?” Bɛmaa aboa he kwane ma ɔkaa nsɛm akɛseɛ ne abususɛm, na bɛmaa no kwane ma onyaa tumi bosome aduannan mmienu.
Na obiee n’ano kaa abususɛm tiaa Nyankopɔn, sɛ ɔbɛka ne dini ne ne ntomadane ne bɛ a bɛtete soro he ho abususɛm.
Bɛmaa no kwane maa ɔne ahoteefoɔ koeɛ sɛ obedi bɛ so.
Na bɛmaa no mmusuakuo ne nkurofoɔ ne kasa hodoɔ ne amane nyinaa so tumi.
Na bɛ a bɛte asaase so nyinaa bɛkoto no, meekyerɛ bɛ a bɛamfiri wiase ahyɛaseɛ antwerɛ bɛ dini Adwammaa a bekuu no he nkwa nwoma mu he.
Sɛ bi wɔ aso a, ma no ntie.
Biaa a ɔsɛ sɛ bɛkye no he, bɛbɛkye no.
Biaa a ɔsɛ sɛ beku no nkrantɛ ano he, bebeku no.
Yei mu ne ahoteefoɔ boasetɔ ne gyidie ho hia.
Afei mehuu aboa foforɔ a oopie afiri asaase mu.
Na ɔwɔ mmɛne mmienu te sɛ adwamaa, nso na ɔkasa te sɛ wɔ.
Na ɔwɔ aboa a odi kane he ahoɔdenneɛ nyinaa ya n’anim, na ɔmaa asaase ne bɛ a bɛtete so koto aboa a odi kane a bɛasa ne wuopira he.
Aboa a ɔto so mmienu yi yɔɔ anwanwadeɛ akɛseɛ bebree.
Ɔmaa gya firii soro baa asaase so a nnipa nyinaa huiɛ.
Na ɔnam anwanwadeɛ a bɛmaa no ho kwane maa no yɔeɛ ya aboa a odi kane he anim he so daadaa nnipa a bɛte asaase so nyinaa.
Aboa he ka kyerɛɛ wiase nnipa nyinaa sɛ, bensi honyini mma aboa a bɛde nkrantɛ piraa no na nso n’apirakuro he awu na ɔte ase bio he.
Bɛmaa aboa a ɔto so mmienu he kwane ma ɔhomee nkwa guu aboa a odi kane honyini he mu, sɛnea ɔbɛyɛ a honyini he betumi akasa, na waku biaa a ɔnsom no he.
Afei aboa he hyɛɛ nnipa nyinaa, nketewa ne akɛseɛ, adefoɔ ne ahiafoɔ, bɛ a bɛde bɛ ho ne nkoa sɛ bɛnhyɛ bɛ nsa nifa ho ne bɛ moma so agyinaeɛ.
Biaa nni ho kwane sɛ ɔtɔ anaa ɔtɔno gye sɛ bɛde aboa he dini anaa ne dini akonta ntwerɛeɛ he hyɛ ne ho agyinaeɛ.
Yei hia ma nimdeɛ.
Biaa a ɔwɔ nimdeɛ he betumi ahu nsɛnkyerɛnne a ogyina hɔ ma aboa he ase, efiri sɛ, nsɛnkyerɛnne he gyina hɔ ma nipa dini.
Ne nsɛnkyerɛnne yɛ ahansia aduosia nsia.
Adwammaa he ne ne nkurɔfoɔ Afei mehwɛeɛ, na hwɛ, mehuu Adwamaa he sɛ ogyina Sion Bepɔ so.
Na nnipa mpemha aduannan nnan ka ne ho a bɛatwerɛ ne dini ne n’agya dini bɛ moma so.
Na metee nne bi firi soro te sɛ nsuworoeɛ a ano ɔdene, na ɔte sɛ apranaa nso.
Nne a meteeɛ he te sɛ nnwom a sankubɔfoɔ bi ɔɔbɔ no ne sankuo so.
Na bɛtoo dwom foforɔ bi, ahennwa ne ateasefoɔ nnan ne mpanyimfoɔ he anim, na biaa antumi ansua dwom he, gye nnipa mpem ha aduannan nnan a bɛagye bɛ afiri asaase so he nko.
Yeinom ne nnipa a bɛamfa adwamammɔ angu bɛ ho fi, na bɛyɛ mmabunu.
Baabiaa a Adwamaa he bɛkɔ he, na bedi n’akyi.
Bɛagye bɛ nkwa afiri nnipa mu, na bɛne nnipa a bedi kane a bɛde bɛ ama Nyankopɔn ne Adwamaa he.
Na bɛante torɔsɛm biaa amfiri bɛ anum; na dɛm biaa nni bɛ ho.
Abɔfoɔ mmeɛnsa he Afei mehuu bɔfoɔ foforɔ bi sɛ watu nam soro soro a ɔɔkɔka Asɛmpa a ontwam da he akyerɛ asaase so nnipa a amane ne mmusuakuo ne kasa ne nkurofoɔ nyinaa ka ho.
Ɔde nne kɛseɛ teaam sɛ, “Honsuro Nyankopɔn na honkamfo ne kɛseyɛ, efiri sɛ, berɛ he aduru sɛ obu adasamma atɛne.
Honsom nea ɔbɔɔ soro, asaase, po ne nsuti he!” Bɔfoɔ a ɔto so mmienu dii akyire kaa sɛ, “Wahwe ase!
Babilon kɛseɛ ahwe ase, efiri sɛ waama amanamane nyinaa anom n’adwamammɔ nsa dendene he bi.” Bɔfoɔ a ɔto so mmeɛnsa dii bɛ akyi teaam kaa sɛ, “Biaa a ɔsom aboa he ne ne sɛso honyini a na ɔma bɛhyɛ ne nsa ho anaa ne moma so agyinaeɛ he ankasa bɛnom Nyankopɔn abufuo nsa korɔgyee a bɛahwie agu n’abufuo kuruwa mu he bi.
Bɛ a bɛbɛyɔ saa he nyinaa, bɛbɛhyɛ no aniɔyeyaa gya ne sɔfe mu, abɔfoɔ ne Adwamaa he anim.
Na gya he wusie a ɔhyɛ bɛ aniɔyeyaa he foro kɔ soro daa daa.
Na bɛ a bɛsomm aboa he ne ne sɛso honyini he onnya home biaa, awia anaa anadwo.” Yei nti ne ɔsɛ sɛ Nyankopɔn nkurofoɔ ne bɛ a bedi Nyankopɔn mmara so na bɛgye Yesu di he nya boasetɔ he.
Afei metee nne bi firi soro a ɔkaa sɛ, “Twerɛ yei: Honhom he dɛ, Nhyira ne awufoɔ a bewu Awurade mu firi seesei ɔɔkɔ yi, ampa, bɛbɛhome afiri bɛ brɛ he mu; na bɛ nnwuma di bɛ akyi.” Na mehwɛeɛ, na hwɛ, mununkum fitaa bi a na abɔdeɛ bi a na ɔte so he te sɛ nipa a sikakɔkɔɔ abotire bɔ ne ti na okita kantankrankyi nnamnnam bi di.
Na bɔfoɔ foforɔ bi firii asɔredane he mu pieeɛ, teaam kyerɛɛ nea ɔte mununkum he so he sɛ, “Fa wo kantankrankyi he twa, efiri sɛ, twaberɛ he aduru; asaase he aso aba a ɔsɛ sɛ betwa!” Nti nea ɔte mununkum so he hwimm ne kantankrankyi asaase so ma otwaa asaase so nnɔbae.
Afei mehuu bɔfoɔ foforɔ bi a ofiri soro asɔredane mu apie a ɔno nso kita kantankrankyi nnamnnam bi.
Bɔfoɔ foforɔ bi a ɔno nso hwɛ gya so firi afɔrebokyia he mu pieeɛ.
Ɔteaa bɔfoɔ a okita kantankrankyi nnamnnam he sɛ, “Fa wo kantankrankyi nnamnnam he twitwa asaase so bobe aba akuoakuo he, efiri sɛ, n’aba he abere.” Nti bɔfoɔ he himm ne kantankrankyi he asaase so de twitwaa bobe aba he na ɔde koguu Nyankopɔn abufuo nsa-kyi-amena kɛseɛ he mu.
Na betiatiaa nsa-kyi-amena he so kuro he akyi, na mogyaa firii nsa-kyi-amena he mu taa hɔ foro koduru bɛyɛ sɛ apɔnkɔ nnareka ho, na ɔtenee kɔɔ bɛyɛ nkwansini ha aduowɔtwe nnan.
Abɔfoɔ a bekitakita haw mmusuo a otwa toɔ he Na mehuu nsɛnkyerɛnne foforɔ bi a ɔsõ na ɔyɛ nwanwa ya soro.
Na abɔfoɔ nson kitakita haw nson a ɔyɛ haw a otwa toɔ, efiri sɛ, ɔno ne kyerɛ Nyankopɔn abufuo a otwa toɔ.
Afei mehuu bibi te sɛ ahwehwɛ po a bɛde gya afra mu, ne bɛ a bɛadi aboa he ne ne honyini ne n’akontahyɛdeɛ he so nkunim.
Na begyinagyina ahwehwɛ po he ho a bekitakita Nyankopɔn nsankuo.
Na bɛɛto Nyankopɔn akoa Mose nnwom ne Adwamaa he nnwom sɛ, Awurade Nyankopɔn, adeɛ nyinaa so tumfoɔ, wo nnwuma yɛ akɛseɛ na ɔyɛ nwanwa.
O!
meresantene hene, w’akwane tene na ɔyɛ nɔkorɛ.
Awurade, hwane na oonsuro wo na ɔɔnhyɛ wo dini animuonyam?
Efiri sɛ wo nkoaa ne woyɛ kronkron, na amane nyinaa bɛba abɛkoto w’anim, efiri sɛ w’atɛne tenenee ada adi.
Na yeinom akyi he, mehuu sɛ asɔredane a ɔyɛ adanseɛ ntomadane a ɔya soro he abie.
Abɔfoɔ nson a bɛmaa bɛ tumi sɛ bɛmfa haw nson mmra he pie firii asɔredane he mu a na bɛhyehyɛ ntaadeɛ fitaa a sikakɔkɔɔ aboomu bɔ bɛ mu.
Afei ateasefoɔ nnan he mu baako maa abɔfoɔ nson he sikakɔkɔɔ nkuruwaa nson a, Nyankopɔn a ɔte ase daa daa he abufuo ahyɛ no ma.
Wusie a ofiri Nyankopɔn animuonyam ne ne tumi mu he hyɛɛ asɔredane he ma.
Na biaa antumi ankɔ asɔredane he mu kosii sɛ haw nson a abɔfoɔ nson he de baeɛ he to twaeɛ.
Nyankopɔn abufuo nkuruwa nson he Afei metee nne kɛseɛ bi a ofiri asɔredane he mu a ɔka kyerɛɛ abɔfoɔ nson he sɛ, “Kɔ na kohwie Nyankopɔn abufuo nson a ɔya nkuruwaa nson mu he gu asaase so.” Bɔfoɔ a odi kane he kohwiee nea ɔya ne kuruwa he mu guu asaase so.
Akuro a ohu na ɔyeya tutuu bɛ a bɛde aboa he ahyɛ bɛ ho agyinaeɛ he ne bɛ a bɛsomm ne sɛso honyini he nso.
Bɔfoɔ a ɔto so mmienu he hwiee nea ɔya ne kuruwa he mu guu po mu.
Afei nsuo he danee te sɛ awufoɔ mogyaa, na abɔdeɛ biaa a nkwa yam ya po he mu he wuiɛ.
Bɔfoɔ a ɔto so mmeɛnsa he hwiee nea ɔya ne kuruwa he mu guu nsubɔntene mu maa nsuo he nyinaa danee mogyaa.
Metee sɛ bɔfoɔ a ɔhwɛ nsuo so he ɔɔka sɛ, “O Kronkronni a wotene, na woya hɔ, na woya ha firi tetentredee, w’atɛne a wobuiɛ he yɛ atɛntenenee.
Na bɛahwie Nyankopɔn ahoteefoɔ ne adiyifoɔ mogyaa agu, nti woama bɛ mogyaa sɛ bɛ nom.
Nea ɔfata bɛaa ne beenya yi.” Na metee sɛ nne bi firi afɔrebokyia he mu a ɔdɛ: Ɛɛ!
Awurade Nyankopɔn, adeɛ nyinaa so tumfoɔ, w’atemmuo yɛ nɔkorɛ ne tenenee.
Afei bɔfoɔ a ɔto so nnan he hwiee nea ɔya ne kuruwa he mu guu awia so na bɛmaa awia tumi sɛ ɔmfa ne hyeɛ yaayaa he nhye nnipa.
Awia he hyeɛ yaayaa he hyee nnipa ma bɛkaa Nyankopɔn a ɔwɔ saa haw yi nyinaa so tumi he dini he ho abususɛm.
Nso bɛannu bɛ ho anhyɛ no animuonyam.
Afei bɔfoɔ a ɔto so num he hwiee nea ɔya ne kuruwa he mu guu aboa he ahennwa he so.
Sum duruu aboa he ahemmane mu, na osiane yeya nti, nnipa wee bɛ kɛtrɛma, na esiane saa yeyaa he ne akuro a otutuu bɛ he nti, bɛdomee soro Nyankopɔn.
Nso bɛansakra bɛ adwene amfiri bɛ bɔne ho.
Bɔfoɔ a ɔto so nsia he hwiee nea ɔya ne kuruwa he mu guu asubɔntene Eufrate mu.
Nsuo he weweeɛ na ɔdanee kwane maa ahene a befiri awia apieeɛ.
Afei mehuu ahohommɔne mmeɛnsa bi a na bɛte sɛ atwerɛ a na befifiri tweaseɛ he ne aboa he ne atorɔ diyifoɔ he anum.
Bɛyɛ ahohommɔne a bɛyɔ anwanwadeɛ.
Saa ahohom mmeɛnsa yi kɔɔ ahene a bɛya asaase so nyinaa nkyɛne kɔka bɛ nyinaa boa ano ma Tumfoɔ Nyankopɔn da kɛseɛ he mu ko he.
(“Hontie!
Hwɛ, meeba te sɛ korɔmfoɔ.
Nhyira ne nea ɔwɛne na ɔhwɛ ne ntaadeɛ so sɛnea ɔɔnnante adagya, ngu ne ho anim ase badwam!”) Na bɛboaboaa ahene he ano kɔɔ baabi a Hebri kasa mu bɛfrɛ hɔ Armagedon.
Afei bɔfoɔ a ɔto so nson he hwiee nea ɔya ne kuruwa he mu guu mframa mu.
Na nne dendene bi firi ahennwa a ɔya asɔredane he mu kaa sɛ, “Bɛawie.” Na anyinam tete maa apranaa paepaeɛ, na asaasewosoɔ kɛseɛ bi a ohu paa a ofiri berɛ a nnipa baa asaase so bi nsii saa da, baeɛ.
Yei ne asaasewosoɔ nyinaa mu nea ano ɔdene paa.
Kuro kɛseɛ he mu paee mmeɛnsa, na amane nyinaa nkuro akɛseɛ sɛesɛee.
Nyankopɔn kaee Babel kɛseɛ he maa ɔnom nsa a ano ɔdene he, firii ne kuruwa ano.
Nsupɔ ne mmepɔ nyinaa yeraeɛ.
Na asukɔtwea akɛseɛ a ɔte sɛ nkariboɔ ha firi soro guguu nnipa so, na asukɔtwea he haw nti, nnipa kaa Nyankopɔn ho abususɛm efiri sɛ na haw he so kɛse paa.
Dwamamfoɔ kɛseɛ he ne aboa he Afei abɔfoɔ nson he mu baako a okita nkuruwaa nson he ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Bra na menkyerɛ wo dwamanfoɔ kɛseɛ a ɔte nsuo pii so he atemmuo.
Ɔno ne wiase ahemfo ne no abɔ adwamane, na n’adwamammɔ nsa he aboroboro bɛ a bɛtete asaase so he.” Honhom he faa me maa bɔfoɔ he de me kɔɔ serɛ so.
Hɔ ne mehuu baa bi sɛ ɔte aboa kɔkɔɔ bi a abususɛm dini ahyɛ no mã so.
Na aboa he wɔ ti nson ne mmɛne du.
Na baa he hyɛ ataadeɛ a n’ahosuo yɛ afasebiri ne kɔkɔɔ, afei nso ɔde sikakɔkɔɔ aboɔ ne nhwene pa ahyehyɛ ne ho.
Na okita sika kuruwa a afideɛ ne adwamammɔ ho nnoɔma ayɛ no ma tɔ.
Na bɛatwerɛ dini bi ya ne moma so a ne nkyerɛaseɛ yɛ ahintasɛm: “Babel kɛseɛ he, asaase so adwamanfoɔ ne akyiwadeɛ na.” Na mehuu sɛ ahoteefoɔ ne Yesu akyidifoɔ a bekuu bɛ he mogyaa aboro baa he.
Mehu no he, ɔyɛɛ me nwanwa paa.
Bɔfoɔ he bisaa me sɛ, “Mmɛ nti na ɔyɛ wo nwanwa?
Mɛkyerɛ wo baa he ne aboa a ɔsõ no a ɔwɔ tire nson ne mmɛne du he ho ahintasɛm he.
Aboa a wohuu no he, na ɔte ase nso ɔnte ase bio.
Oobefiri amena donkodonko he mu aba ama bɛasɛe no.
Nnipa a bɛte asaase so a bɛantwerɛ bɛ dini angu ateasefoɔ nwoma he mu ansa na bɛɛbɔ wiase he, sɛ wohu aboa he a, ɔbɛyɛ bɛ nwanwa, efiri sɛ mmerɛ bi na ɔte asɛ, nso seesei deɛ, ɔnte ase na ɔbɛsane aba.
“Yei ho ne nimdeɛ ne nteaseɛ ho hia.
Ti nson he gyina hɔ ma mmepɔ nson a baa he tena so he.
Bɛyɛ ahemfo nson nso, bɛ mu nnum awu, na bɛ mu baako da so di hene, na baako a ɔka bɛ ho he mmaeɛ.
Na sɛ ɔba a, ɔsɛ sɛ ɔtwɛne kakra bi.
Aboa he a nka na ɔte ase he na afei deɛ ɔnte ase he yɛ hene a ɔto so nwɔtwe a ɔka nson a bedi kane he ho a ɔɔkɔ ne sɛeɛ mu.
“Na mmɛne du a wohuiɛ he yɛ ahemfo du a bennyaa ahennie, nso bɛne aboa he benya tumi sɛ ahemfo dɔnhwere baako.
Yeinom wɔ adwene korɔ, na bɛde bɛ tumi ne bɛ ahoɔdene bɛma aboa he.
Bɛbɛko atia Adwamaa he ne n’akyidifoɔ, agyidifoɔ a bɛafrɛ bɛ he ne no bedi bɛ so, efiri sɛ, ɔyɛ Awurade mu Awurade ne Ahemfo mu Hene.” Bɔfoɔ he nso ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Nsuo a wohuiɛ a dwamanfoɔ he te so he yɛ nkuro ne nkurofoɔ akuoakuo ne amane ne kasa ahodoɔ.
Mmɛne du ne aboa he a wohuiɛ he bɛtane dwamanfoɔ he.
Bɛbɛfa bibiaa a ɔya ne ho ama wada adagya.
Bɛbɛwe ne nam na bɛde gya ahye no, efiri sɛ, Nyankopɔn de ahyɛ bɛ akoma mu sɛ bɛbɛyɔ adwene korɔ de bɛ ahennie ama aboa he na wadi hene akosi sɛ Nyankopɔn asɛm he bɛba mu.
Afei baa a wohuu no he yɛ kuro kɛseɛ a odi asaase so ahemfo so hene he.”
Babel ahweaseɛ Yei akyi he, mehuu bɔfoɔ foforɔ sɛ ofiri soro ɔɔba fam.
Na ɔwɔ tumi kɛseɛ na n’animuonyam hyerɛn asaase so nyinaa.
Ɔteaam dendenndene sɛ, “Wahwe ase!
Babel kɛseɛ ahwe ase, na adane ahonhommɔne tenaberɛ ne ahonhom fi nyinaa nso atenaeɛ.
Nnomaa fi a bekyiri bɛ nyinaa te ne mu.
