Efiri sɛ, amanamane nyinaa anom n’adwamammɔ nsa dendene he bi, na asaase so ahemfo ne no abɔ adwamane, na asaase so adwadifoɔ anya bɛ ho ɔnam n’akɔnnɔbɔne ntrasoɔ nti.” Afei metee nne foforɔ firii soro sɛ, “Me mane, homfiri ne mu, na hoanyɔ ne nneyɔeɛ bɔne he bi, na hoannya ne haw he bi; efiri sɛ, ne nneyɔeɛ bɔne atoatoa abeduru soro, na Nyankopɔn kae n’akwammɔne he.
Sɛnea ɔyɔɔ ho he, honyɔ no saa pɛpɛɛpɛ; nea ɔyɔɔ ho biaa he, hontua no so ka mprenu.
Nsa a ɔde maa ho he, honhyɛ no bi a ano ɔdene mmɔho mmienu.
Homma onhu amane na ne werɛ nho ɔnam animuonyam ne n’ahonya a ɔpɛ maa ne ho he nti, efiri sɛ, daa ɔka sɛ, ‘Mete ha sɛ hemaa.
Menyɛ kunafoɔ, me werɛ ɔnho da!’ Esiane yei nti, n’amanehunu bɛba ne so da bi, yadeɛ, awerɛhoɔ ne kɔm, na bɛde gya ahye no; efiri sɛ Awurade Nyankopɔn a obu no atɛne he yɛ hoɔdenfoɔ.” Sɛ asaase so ahemfo a bɛne no bɔɔ adwamane, dii dɛ he hu ne hyeɛ wusie a, bebesu, atwa agyaadwoɔ.
N’amanehunu he hu a ɔyɛ nti, bebegyina akyirikyiri asu sɛ, “Due!
Due!
O!
kuro kɛseɛ, O Babel, kuro a ɔwɔ tumi.
Hwɛ!
dɔnhwere baako pɛ mu, na w’atemmuo aba.” Adwadifoɔ a bɛya asaase so nso su no efiri sɛ, biaa ntɔ bɛ nnoɔma bio.
Biaa ntɔ sikakɔkɔɔ ne dwetɛ, ne aboɔdeneboɔ ne nhwene pa, ne nwera pa ne ntoma afasebiri ne serekye ne ntoma kɔkɔɔ, ne nnua a ohwam nyinaa ne asommɛne adwinnie nyinaa, ne adwinnie a bɛde nnua a ɔwɔ dini ayɔ, ne yaawa ne dadeɛ ne abohemmaa, ne pɛprɛ ne mmorɔngo, ne nnuhwam ne kurobo, ne hwamfufuo ne nsa ne ngo, ne siam muhumuhu ne ayuo, ne nyɛmmoa bi te sɛ nnwane ne apɔnkɔ ne nteaseɛnam ne nnipadua ne nnipa akra bio.
Na aduaba a wo kra kɔno dɔ he afiri wo nkyɛne, na nnepa ne animuonyanneɛ nyinaa afiri wo ho ayera, na wonhu bio koraa.” Nnoɔma yi ho adwadifoɔ a kuro he nti bɛanya adeɛ he, begyinagyina akyirikyiri n’ayayadeɛ he suro nti, na bɛasu na bɛagyam sɛ, “Due!
Due!
O!
kuro kɛseɛ a ofira nwera pa ne ntoma afasebiri ne ntoma kɔkɔɔ na ɔde sika ne aboɔdenboɔ ne nhwene pa abobɔ mu, efiri sɛ, dɔnhwere pɛ mu, na saa ahonya dodoɔ yi asa.” Nsuomhyɛnkafoɔ, ne hyɛne he mu nnipa, ne hyɛne he mu adwadifoɔ, ne bɛ a bɛka ho a benya bɛ ano aduane firi hyɛne adwumayɔ mu he nyinaa gyinaa akyirikyiri na behuu ne hyeɛ wusie he, bɛteaam sɛ: Abɛ kuro ne te sɛ kuro kɛseɛ yi?” Na bɛde mfuturo guu bɛ atifi, na bɛde sũ ne gyam teaa mu sɛ: Due!
Due!
Kuro kɛseɛ yi a n’aboɔdenneɛ nti bɛ a bɛya hyɛne mu ya po so nyinaa anyinya bɛ ho ya mu, hwɛ!
Dɔnhwere baako pɛ mu na bɛayɛ no pasaa.
Soro ne ho ahoteefoɔ ne asomafoɔ ne adiyifoɔ, ɔno nti homma ho ani nnye ya ne ho, efiri sɛ Nyankopɔn abu no atɛne ama ho.
Afei bɔfoɔ hoɔdenfoɔ bi faa boɔ a ne kɛseɛ bɛyɛ sɛ ayuyammoɔ to twenee po mu kaa sɛ, “Saa ahoɔdene yiaa ne bɛde bɛto Babilon kɛse he atwene fam a bennhu no bio.
Bɛnnte sankubɔfoɔ ne nwomtofoɔ, atɛntɛbɛnbɔfoɔ ne totorobɛntohyɛnfoɔ nka bio mfiri ho mu.
Bennhu dwumfoɔ biaa ya wo mu bio.
Na bɛnte ayuyammoɔ biaa nka ho mu bio.
Kanea hann onhyerɛn ya ho mu bio.
Na bɛnnte ayefokunu ne ayeforɔ nne ya ho mu bio.
W’adwadifoɔ yɛ wiase mu nnipa titire.
Na bɛde wo ntafowayie adaadaa amane nyinaa.
Na ɔno mu ne behuu adiyifoɔ ne ahoteefoɔ ne bɛ a bɛaku bɛ asaase so he nyinaa mogyaa.”
Sorofoɔ dii ahurisie Yei akyi he, metee bibi a ɔte sɛ nnipakuo bebree nne firii soro sɛ: “Haleluya!
Nkwagyeɛ ne animuonyam ne tumi yɛ yɛ Nyankopɔn dea efiri sɛ, n’atemmuo yɛ nɔkorɛ na ɔtene sɛ obuu dwamanfoɔ kɛseɛ a ɔde n’adwamammɔ asɛe asaase he atɛne, na ɔtɔɔ ne nkoa mogyaa so werɛ ne nsa mu.” Na afei bɛteaam bio sɛ, “Haleluya!
Na wusie a ofiri ne mu he kɔ soro daa daa.” Mpanyimfoɔ aduonu nnan ne ateasefoɔ nnan he butubutu Nyankopɔn a ɔte n’ahennwa so he anim somm no.
Na bɛteaam sɛ, “Amen, Haleluya!” Afei nne bi firi ahennwa he so baa sɛ, “Honkamfo yɛ Nyankopɔn, ho a hoyɛ ne nkoa, ne ho a hosuro no nyinaa, akɛseɛ ne nkumaa!” Afei metee nne bi te sɛ nnipadɔm nne, ne nsuo nworosoɔ ne apranaa a ɔɔpaepae a ɔɔteam sɛ, “Haleluya!
Yɛ Tumfoɔ Awurade Nyankopɔn di hene.
Homma yɛ ho nsɛpɛ yɛ na yɛ ani nnye na yɛnhyɛ no animuonyam, efiri sɛ, dwammaa he ayefohyia aduru, na ne yerɛ asiesie ne ho.
Bɛde nwera pa a ani hyerɛn na ani te maa no sɛ ɔnhyɛ.” Nwera pa he ne ahoteefoɔ tenenee adeyɔ.
Afei bɔfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Twerɛ sɛ, Nhyira nka bɛ a bɛato nsa afrɛ bɛ dwammaa he ayefohyia apontoɔ ase.” Na ɔka kaa ho sɛ, “Yei yɛ Nyankopɔn asɛm turodoo.” Afei mebutuu ne nane ase sɔree no.
Nso ɔka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Nyɔ saa, efiri sɛ, meyɛ akoa te sɛ wo ne wo nuanom a bedi Yesu ho adanseɛ heaa, Nyankopɔn mmom ne koto sɔre no!
Na Yesu adanseɛ ne yɛ adiyie honhom he.” Gyefoɔ he ho anisoadehunu kɛseɛ Afei mehuu sɛ soro abie a pɔnkɔ fitaa ya hɔ.
Na nea ɔte ne so he dini de “Ɔseadeɛyɔ ne Nɔkwafoɔ,” na tenenee ne ogyina so bu atɛne ko ne ko nso.
N’ani te sɛ gya a ɔɔdɛre, na na ɔbɔ ahemmotire bebree.
Na bɛatwerɛ ne dini bi a biaa nnim gye sɛ ɔno nkoaa.
Na bɛde n’ataadeɛ a ɔhyɛ he anu mogyaa mu.
Dini a bɛde frɛ no ne “Nyankopɔn Asɛm.” Soro asraafoɔ a bɛhyehyɛ nwera fitaa a ani te a bɛtete pɔnkɔ fitaa so dii n’akyi.
Afei nkrantɛ nnamnnam a ɔde bedi amane so firi n’anum baeɛ.
Ɔde dadeɛ poma ne bedi bɛ so.
Obetiatia Nyankopɔn a ɔyɛ adeɛ nyinaa so tumfoɔ he abufuo a ɔdene he nsa-kyi-amena he so.
Na bɛatwerɛ dini “Ahene mu Hene ne awuranom mu Awurade” agu n’ataadeɛ mu ne ne nane ho.
Bedii aboa he ne n’asraafoɔ he so nkunim Afei mehuu bɔfoɔ bi a ogyina awia mu.
Ɔteaam guu nnomaa a bɛnam wiem nyinaa so sɛ, “Hommra mmehyiam Nyankopɔn apontoɔ kɛseɛ he ase.
Hommedi ahemfo nam ne asafohene nam ne atumfoɔ nam ne apɔnkɔ ne bɛ a bɛtete bɛ so nam ne adehyeɛ ne nkoa ne akɛseɛ ne nkumaa nyinaa nam.” Afei mehuu aboa he ne asaase so ahemfo ne bɛ asraafoɔ a bɛaboa bɛ ano ɔɔkɔko atia nea ɔte pɔnkɔ he so he ne ne dɔm.
Bɛkyee aboa he ne ne diyifoɔ torɔfoɔ a ɔyɔɔ anwanwadeɛ n’anim he de no too afiase.
Saa anwanwadeɛ he so ne ɔnam daadaa bɛ a bɛde aboa he ahyɛ bɛ agyinaeɛ ne bɛ a bɛsom aboa he honyini he.
Bɛtoo aboa he ne diyifoɔ torɔfoɔ he anikann guu gya tadeɛ a sɔfe ɔɔdɛre mu he mu.
Bɛde nkrantɛ a ofiri pɔnkɔkafoɔ he anum kukuu bɛ asraafoɔ, na nnomaa he dii bɛ nam meeɛ.
Mfie apem he Afei mehuu bɔfoɔ bi sɛ ofiri soro ɔɔba fam a na okita amena donkodonko he ano safoa ne nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn kɛseɛ bi.
Ɔkyee wɔ kɛseɛ dadaa a ɔno ne Bronsam ne Satan he kyekyeree no maa odii mfie apem.
Bɔfoɔ he too no twenee amena donkodonko he mu too mu safoa bram akyire na wantumi annaadaa amane bio kosi sɛ mfie apem he betwam.
Nso mfie apem he akyi he bebegyaa no kakra.
Afei mehuu nhennwa bi ne bɛ a bɛtete so a na bɛama bɛ tumi sɛ bemmu atɛne.
Na mesane huu bɛ a Yesu adanseɛ ne Nyankopɔn asɛm nti betwitwaa bɛ ti he kra, ne bɛ a bɛankoto aboa he anaa ne honyini na bɛannye agyinaeɛ he ammɔ bɛ moma ne bɛ nsa so he.
Na benyaa nkwa bio, na bɛne Kristo dii hene mfie apem.
(Na awufoɔ nkaeɛ he deɛ, bɛannya nkwa bio kosii sɛ mfie apem he twaa mu.)
Yei ne wusɔreɛ a odi kane he.
Nhyira ne bɛ a bɛate bɛ ho ama Awurade a benya kyɛfa sɔreeɛ a odi kane he mu.
Saa nkurofoɔ he deɛ, wuprenu he nni bɛ so tumi, na mmom bɛbɛyɛ Nyankopɔn ne Kristo asɔfoɔ, na bɛne no bedi ahene mfie apem.
Mfie apem he akyi he, bebesane Satan afiri afiase hɔ; na ɔbɛkɔ akɔdaadaa amane a bɛya wiase nyinaa, Gog ne Magog, akɔboaboa nnipa a bɛ dodoɔ te sɛ mpoano anwea de bɛ akɔ sa.
Betuu sa faa asaase so nyina kotwaa kuro a Nyankopɔn dɔ no he, na n’ahoteefoɔ tete mu he ho hyiaeɛ.
Nso gya firi soro bɛhyee bɛ.
Na bɛtoo Bronsam a ɔdaadaa bɛ he too gya ne sɔfe tadeɛ a bɛde aboa he ne diyifoɔ torɔfoɔ he ato mu he mu.
Na bɛbɛyɛ bɛ ayayadeɛ awia ne anadwo daa daa.
Bebuu awufoɔ atɛne Afei mehuu ahennwa kɛseɛ fitaa bi ne nea ɔte ahennwa he so a asaase ne soro dwane firii n’anim, na bɛanya baabiaa amma bɛ.
Na mehuu awufoɔ akɛseɛ ne nketewa sɛ begyinagyina ahennwa he anim.
Bebiebiee nwoma bebree mu, na bebiee nwoma foforɔ bi a ɔyɛ nkwa nwoma he mu.
Bebuu awufoɔ he atɛne, sɛnea bɛ nnwuma teɛ, ne sɛnea bɛatwerɛ ya nwoma ahoroɔ he mu he.
Afei po nso yii n’awufoɔ maeɛ.
Wuo ne Asamando nso yii bɛ awufoɔ maeɛ.
Na bebuu bɛ nyinaa atɛne sɛnea bɛ nnwuma teɛ.
Na bɛtoo Wuo ne Asamando guu gya tadeɛ he mu.
Saa gya tadeɛ yi ne wuprenu he.
Na biaa a bɛantwerɛ ne dini nkwa nwoma he mu he, bɛtoo no twenee gya tadeɛ he mu.
Soro foforɔ ne asaase foforɔ Afei mehuu soro foforɔ ne asaase foforɔ, na kane soro ne kane asaase he nni hɔ bio, na po nso nni hɔ bio.
Na mehuu Kuro Kronkron a ɔyɛ Yerusalem foforɔ sɛ osiane afiri soro afiri Nyankopɔn nkyɛne ɔɔba fam, a bɛasiesie ne ho sɛ ayeforɔ a bɛahyehyɛ no ama ne kunu.
Na metee nne dendene bi firi ahennwa he so sɛ: “Hwɛ!
Nyankopɔn ntomadane ya nnipa mu.
Ɔne bɛ bɛtena na bɛayɛ ne mane.
Na Nyankopɔn he ankasa ne bɛ bɛtena Na ɔbɛpepa bɛ aniwa mu nisuo nyinaa.
Na wuo nni hɔ bio; na awerɛhoɔ ne su ne yeyaa biaa nni hɔ bio, efiri sɛ, kane nnoɔma he atwam.” Afei nea ɔte ahennwa he so he kaa sɛ, “Hwɛ!
Meeyɔ nnoɔma nyinaa foforɔ!” Ɔka kyerɛɛ me nso sɛ, “Twerɛ yei, efiri sɛ, saa nsɛm yi yɛ nɔkorɛ, na wobetumi de wo ho ato so.” Na ɔkɔɔ so kaa sɛ, “Bɛawie!
Mene Ahyɛaseɛ ne Awieeɛ, kyerɛ sɛ, mfitiaseɛ ne awieeɛ he.
Biaa a sukɔm de no he, mɛma no nsuo a ofiri nkwa asuti mu anom kwa.
Biaa a obedi nkunim he benya yei afiri me nkyɛne.
Mɛyɛ ne Nyankopɔn na ɔno nso ayɛ me ba.
Nso ahufoɔ ne bɛ a bɛnnye nni ne akyiwadeyɔfoɔ ne awudifoɔ ne adwamanfoɔ ne adutofoɔ ne abosonsomfoɔ ne atorɔfoɔ nyinaa benya bɛ kyɛfa ya tadeɛ a gya ne sɔfe ɔɔdɛre mu he.
Yei ne wuprenu he.” Yerusalem foforɔ he Abɔfoɔ nson a bekitakita nkuruwaa nson a haw nson a otwa toɔ he ahyɛ no ma he mu baako baa me nkyɛne bɛkaa sɛ, “Bra, na mɛkyerɛ wo Ayeforɔ a ɔyɛ Dwammaa he yerɛ he.” Na ɔde me nam honhom mu kɔɔ bepɔ kɛseɛ tentene bi atifi.
Ɔkyerɛɛ me Yerusalem, Kuro Kronkron a ofiri soro, Nyankopɔn hɔ ɔɔba fam, a ɔɔhyerɛn Nyankopɔn animuonyam mu.
Na kuro he hyerɛn sɛ aboɔdenboɔ, sɛ ahwehwɛboɔ a mu te sɛ ahwehwɛ.
Na ne fasuo he wɔ ahoɔdene na ɔware yie, na ɔwɔ pono dummienu gu ano a, abɔfoɔ dummienu na bɛhwɛ apono he so.
Apono he so ne bɛatwerɛ Israel mmusuakuo dummienu he mu nnipa dini.
Na apono mmeɛnsa ya apieɛ; mmeɛnsa ya anafoɔ; mmeɛnsa ya atifi na mmeɛnsa nso ya atɔeɛ.
Besii kuro he afasuo sii aboɔ dummienu a bɛatwerɛ Dwammaa he asomafoɔ dummienu he dini ya so he so.
Bɔfoɔ a ɔkasa kyerɛɛ me he wɔ sikakɔkɔɔ poma susudua a bɛde besusu kuro he, n’apono ne ne fasuo.
Na kuro he yɛ ahinanan, ne tentene ne ne tɛtrɛtɛ yɛ pɛ.
Bɔfoɔ he de ne susudua he susu kuro he.
Na ne tentene yɛ nkwansini apem ahanum na ne tɛtrɛtɛ, ne tentene ne sorokɔ nyinaa yɛ pɛ.
Bɔfoɔ he susuu afasuo he nso a na ne sorokɔ yɛ basafa ha aduannan nnan sɛnea na saa berɛ he nsusuiɛ a bɔfoɔ he nam so kaeɛ he teɛ.
Ahwehwɛboɔ ne ɔde too afasuo he.
Na kuro he deɛ, sikakɔkɔɔ mapa a ɔyɛ hyerɛnn te sɛ ahwehwɛ na bɛde toeɛ.
Bɛde aboɔdenboɔ ahodoɔ a ɔfɛ ne hyehyɛɛ kuro he fapem.
Fapem a odi kane he yɛ ahwehwɛboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so mmienu he yɛ hoaboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so mmeɛnsa he yɛ mununkumboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so nnan he yɛ ahabamonoboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so num he yɛ tɔnboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so nsia he yɛ bogyanamboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so nson he yɛ sikabereboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so nwɔtwe he yɛ apopobibireboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so nkron he yɛ akrateboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so du he yɛ dɛnkyɛmmoɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so dubaako he yɛ wusieboɔ.
Fapem a ɔto so dummienu he yɛ beredumboɔ.
Na bɛde nhwene pa dummienu ne yɔɔ apono dummienu he.
Apono he mu biaa, bɛde ahwene pa baako ne yɔeɛ.
Na kuro he abɔntene kɛseɛ yɛ sika mapa, kronkron a ɔte sɛ ahwehwɛ.
Na manhu asɔredane ya kuro he mu baabiaa, efiri sɛ, na Awurade Nyankopɔn, ade nyinaa so tumfoɔ, ne Adwammaa he ne yɛ n’asɔredane.
Na kuro he nhia awia anaa bosome hann, efiri sɛ, na Nyankopɔn animuonyam hyerɛn mu, na kuro he kanea ne Dwammaa he.
Ne hann he bɛhyerɛn asaase so amane nyinaa so, na asaase so amane sodifoɔ de bɛ animuonyam bɛba mu.
Bɛntoto kuro he apono mu koraa awia, efiri sɛ adeɛ nsa hɔ da.
Bɛde amane he animuonyam ne anidie bɛba kuro he mu.
Nso bibiaa a ho nte nkɔ kuro he mu.
Saa ara ne bi a ɔyɛ aniwudeɛ anaa odi atorɔ nkɔ mu.
Bɛ a bɛatwerɛ bɛ dini ahyɛ Dwammaa he nkwa nwoma he mu he nkoaa na bɛbɛkɔ kuro he mu.
Nkwa asubɔntene ne nkwa dua hee Afei bɔfoɔ he kyerɛɛ me nkwa asubɔntene a ani te krɔgyee sɛ ahwehwɛ a ofiri Nyankopɔn ne Dwammaa he ahennwa so a, ɔtene fa kuro he abɔntene mfinimfini.
Na nkwa dua a ɔsõ aba ahodoɔ dummienu sisi Asubɔntene he afanu nyinaa, na ɔsoso n’aba bosome biaa.
Na dua he ahahane ne bɛde sa amane yadeɛ.
Bibiaa a ɔhyɛ Nyankopɔn nnome ase he nkɔ kuro he mu.
Bebehu Nyankopɔn ne Dwammaa he ahennwa ya kuro he mu na ne nkoa bɛsom no.
Bebehu n’anim na bɛbɛtwerɛ ne dini agu bɛ moma so.
Adeɛ ɔnnsa hɔ bio na nkanea anaa awia ho nhia, efiri sɛ, Awurade Nyankopɔn bɛyɛ bɛ hann na bebedi ahene daa daa.
Afei bɔfoɔ he ka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Saa nsɛm yi yɛ nɔkorɛ a wode wo ho to so a, ɔyɛ.
Na Awurade Nyankopɔn a ɔnam adiyifoɔ so kasaeɛ he somaa ne bɔfoɔ sɛ ɔmmɛkyerɛ ne nkoa adeɛ a ɔbɛba nnansa yiaa he.
Hwɛ!
Ɔnkyɛre koraa mɛba.” Nhyira nka bɛ a betie adiyisɛm a ɔya saa nwoma yi mu he!
Na me, Yohane, mene mehuu nnoɔma yi na meteeɛ.
Na meteeɛ na mehuiɛ he, mehwee ase sɛ meekoto asɔre bɔfoɔ a ɔkyerɛɛ me nnoɔma yi.
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ me sɛ: Nyɔ saa, meyɛ akoa te sɛ wo ne wo nuanom adiyifoɔ, ne bɛ a bedi nwoma yi mu nsɛm mu he soaa pɛ.
Nyankopɔn nkoaa ne koto no sɔre no!
Na ɔka kyerɛɛ me sɛ, “Nsɔ nwoma yi mu adiyisɛm he ano, efiri sɛ berɛ he abɛne sɛ nea bɛtwerɛ ya mu nyinaa ba mu.
Ee!
Deɛ ɔyɔ bɔne he nkɔso nyɔ bɔne ara, na nea ɔyɔ fi he nyɔ fi ara.
Na deɛ ɔtene he nkɔso ntene ara, na deɛ ɔyɛ kronkron he nkɔso nyɛ kronkron ara.” “Hwɛ!
Ɔnkyɛre koraa mɛba!
Na mekita m’akatua sɛ mede bra biaa sɛnea n’adwuma teɛ.
Mene Alpha ne Omega, kannifoɔ ne kyidifoɔ, mfitiaseɛ ne awieeɛ he.” Nhyira nka bɛ a bɛahoro bɛ ntaadeɛ na afiri, na bɛ a bɛwɔ ho kwane sɛ bedi nkwa dua he aba na bɛfa kuro he pono he mu.
Na kuro he akyi ne nkramane ne adutofoɔ ne adwamanfoɔ ne awudifoɔ ne abosonsomfoɔ ne bɛ a bɛpɛ torɔ na bedi he nyinaa ya.
“Me, Yesu, ne masoma me bɔfoɔ sɛ ɔmmɛbɔ ho saa nwoma yi nyinaa ho amanneɛ ya asafo mu.
Mene Dawid nhini ne n’aseni, mene anɔpa nsoromma a ɔhyerɛn he.” Honhom he ne ayeforɔ he dɛ, “Bra!” Na biaa a ɔte saa asɛm yi nso ka sɛ, “Bra!” Na deɛ sukɔm de no he mmra; na nea ɔpɛ he nso mmɛgye nkwa nsuo he kwa.
Awieeɛ Me, Yohane, mebɔ biaa a ɔte saa adiyisɛm a ɔya nwoma yi mu kɔkɔ sɛ: Sɛ bi de bi ka ho a, Nyankopɔn de asotwe bɛka haw a bɛatwerɛ no saa nwoma yi mu he ho de ama no.
Na sɛ bi nso yi bi firi adiyisɛm a ɔya saa nwoma yi mu he mu a, Nyankopɔn beyi ne kyɛfa a obenya afiri nkwa dua he aba he ne kuro Kronkron a bɛakyerɛkyerɛ mu nwoma yi mu he.
Nea odi nwoma yi ho adanseɛ he ka sɛ, “Nɔkorɛ!
Ɔnkyɛre koraa mɛba!” Ɔmmra mu saa.
Awurade Yesu, bra!
Yɛ Awurade Yesu Kristo adom nka ho nyinaa.
Amen.
